vimalakalāśrayābhinavasṛṣṭimahā jananī bharitatanuśca pañcamukhaguptarucirjanakaḥ । tadubhayayāmalasphuritabhāvavisargamayaṃ hṛdayamanuttarāmṛtakulaṃ mama sasphuratāt ।। naumi citpratibhāṃ devīṃ parāṃ bhairavayoginīm । mātṛmānaprameyāṃśaśūlāmbujakṛtāspadām ।।
naumi devīṃ śarīrasthāṃ nṛtyato bhairavākṛte । prāvṛṇmeghaghanavyomavidyullekhāvilāsinīm ।। dīptajyotiśchaṭāpluṣṭabhedabandhatrayaṃ sphurat । stājjñānaśūlaṃ satpakṣavipakṣotkartanakṣamam ।।
svātantryaśaktiḥ kramasaṃsisṛkṣā kramātmatā ceti vibhorvibhūtiḥ । tadeva devītrayamantarāstāmanuttaraṃ me prathayatsvarūpam ।। taddevatāvibhavabhāvimahāmarīcicakreśvarāyitanijasthitireka eva । devīsuto gaṇapatiḥ sphuradindukāntiḥ samyaksamucchalayatānmama saṃvidabdhim ।।
rāgāruṇāṃ granthibilāvakīrṇa yo jālamātānavitānavṛtti । kalombhitaṃ bāhyapathe cakāra stānme sa macchandavibhuḥ prasannaḥ ।। traiyambakābhihitasantatitāmraparṇīsanmauktikaprakarakāntiviśeṣabhājaḥ । pūrve jayanti guravo guruśāstrasindhukallolakelikalanāmalakarṇadhārāḥ ।।
jayati gurureka eva śrīśrīkaṇṭho bhuvi prathitaḥ । tadaparamūrtirbhagavān maheśvaro bhūtirājaśca ।। śrīsomānandabodhaśrīmadutpalaviniḥsṛtāḥ । jayanti saṃvidāmodasandarbhā dikprasarpiṇaḥ ।।
tadāsvādabharāveśabṛṃhitāṃ matiṣaṭpadīm । gurorlakṣmaṇaguptasya nādasaṃmohinīṃ numaḥ ।। yaḥ pūrṇānandaviśrāntasarvaśāstrārthapāragaḥ । sa śrīcukhulako diśyādiṣṭaṃ me gururuttamaḥ ।।
jayatājjagaduddhṛtikṣamo asau bhagavatyā saha śaṃbhunātha ekaḥ । yadudīritaśāsanāṃśubhirme prakaṭo ayaṃ gahano api śāstramārgaḥ ।। santi paddhatayaścitrāḥ srotobhedeṣu bhūyasā । anuttaraṣaḍardhārthakrame tvekāpi nekṣyate ।।
ityahaṃ bahuśaḥ sadbhiḥ śiṣyasabrahmacāribhiḥ । arthito racaye spaṣṭāṃ pūrṇārthā prakriyāmimām ।। śrībhaṭṭanāthacaraṇābjayugāttathā śrībhaṭṭārikāṃghriyugalādgurusantatiryā । bodhānyapāśaviṣanuttadupāsanotthabodhojjvalo abhinavagupta idaṃ karoti ।।
na tadastīha yanna śrī-mālinīvijayottare । devadevena nirdiṣṭaṃ svaśabdenātha liṅgataḥ ।। daśāṣṭādaśavasvaṣṭabhinnaṃ yacchāsanaṃ vibhoḥ । tatsāraṃ trikaśāstraṃ hi tatsāraṃ mālinīmatam ।।
ato atrāntargataṃ sarva saṃpradāyojjhitairbudhaiḥ । adṛṣṭa prakaṭīkurmo gurunāthājñayā vayam ।। abhinavaguptasya kṛtiḥ seyaṃ yasyoditā gurubhirākhyā । trinayanacaraṇasaroruhacintanalabdhaprasiddhiriti ।।
śrīśambhunāthabhāskaracaraṇanipātaprabhāpagatasaṃkocam । abhinavaguptahṛdambujametadvicinuta maheśapūjanahetoḥ ।। iha tāvatsamasteṣu śāstreṣu parigīyate । ajñānaṃ saṃsṛterheturjñānaṃ mokṣaikakāraṇam ।।
malamajñānamicchanti saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam । iti proktaṃ tathā va śrīmalinīvijayottare ।। viśeṣaṇena buddhisthe saṃsārottarakālike । saṃbhāvanāṃ nirasyaitadabhāve mokṣamabravīt ।।
ajñānamiti na jñānābhāvaścātiprasaṅgataḥ । sa hi loṣṭādike apyasti na ca tasyāsti saṃsṛtiḥ ।। ato jñeyasya tattvasya sāmastyenāprathātmakam । jñānameva tadajñānaṃ śivasūtreṣu bhāṣitam ।।
caitanyamātmā jñānaṃ ca bandha ityatra sūtrayoḥ । saṃśleṣetarayogāśyāmayamarthaḥ pradarśitaḥ ।। caitanyamiti bhāvāntaḥ śabdaḥ svātantryamātrakam । anākṣipraviśeṣaṃ sadāha sūtre purātane ।।
dvitīyena tu sūtreṇa kriyāṃ vā karaṇaṃ ca vā । bruvatā tasya cinmātrarūpasya dvaitamucyate ।। dvaitaprathā tadajñānaṃ tucchatvādbandha ucyate । tata eva samucchedyamityāvṛttyānirūpitam ।।
svatantrātmātiriktastu tuccho a tuccho api kaścana । na mokṣo nāma tannāsya pṛthaṅnāmāpi gṛhyate ।। yattu jñeyasatattvasya pūrṇapūrṇaprathātmakam । taduttarottaraṃ jñānaṃ tattatsaṃsāraśāntidam ।।
rāgādyakaluṣo asmyantaḥśūnyo ahaṃ kartṛtojjhitaḥ । itthaṃ samāsavyāsābhyāṃ jñānaṃ muñcati tāvataḥ ।। tasmānmukto apyavacchedādavacchedāntarasthiteḥ । amukta eva muktastu sarvāvacchedavarjitaḥ ।।
yattu jñeyasatattvasya jñānaṃ sarvātmanojjhitam । avacchedairna tatkutrāpyajñānaṃ satyamuktidam ।। jñānājñānasvarūpaṃ yaduktaṃ pratyekamapyadaḥ । dvidhā pauruṣabauddhatvabhidoktaṃ śivaśāsane ।।
tatra puṃso yadajñānaṃ malākhyaṃ tajjamapyaya । svapūrṇacitkriyārūpaśivatāvaraṇātmakam ।। saṃkocidṛkkriyārūpaṃ tatpaśoravikalpitam । tadajñānaṃ na budghyaṃśo adhyavasāyādyabhāvataḥ ।।
ahamitthamidaṃ vedmītyevamadhyavasāyinī । ṣaṭkañcukābilāṇūtthapratibimbanato yadā ।। dhīrjāyate tadā tādṛgjñānamajñānaśabditam । bauddhaṃ tasya ca tatpauṃsnaṃ poṣaṇīyaṃ ca poṣṭṛca ।।
kṣīṇe tu paśusaṃskāre puṃsaḥ prāptaparasthiteḥ । vikasvaraṃ tadvijñānaṃ pauruṣaṃ nirvikalpakam ।। vikasvarāvikalpātmajñānaucityena yāvasā । tadbauddhaṃ yasya tatpauṃsnaṃ prāgvatpoṣyaṃ ca poṣṭṛ ca ।।
tatra dīkṣādinā pauṃsnamajñānaṃ dhvaṃsi yadyapi । tathāpi taccharīrānte tajjñānaṃ vyajyate sphuṭam ।। bauddhajñānena tu yadā bauddhamajñānajṛmbhitam । vilīyate tadā jīvanmuktiḥ karatale sthitā ।।
dīkṣāpi bauddhavijñānapūrvā satyaṃ vimocikā । tena tatrāpi bauddhasya jñānasyāsti pradhānatā ।। jñānājñānāgataṃ caitaddvitvaṃ svāyambhuve rurau । mataṅgādau kṛtaṃ śrīmatkheṭapālādidaiśikaiḥ ।।
tathāvidhāvasāyātmabauddhavijñānasampade । śāstrameva pradhānaṃ yajjñeyatattvapradarśakam ।। dīkṣayā galite apyantarajñāne pauruṣātmani । dhīgatasyānivṛttatvādvikalpo api hi saṃbhaveta ।।
dehasadbhāvaparyantamātmabhāvo yato dhiyi । dehānte api na mokṣaḥ syātpauruṣājñānahānitaḥ ।। bauddhājñānanivṛttau tu vikalponmūlanāddhruvam । tadaiva mokṣa ityuktaṃ dhātrā śrīmanniśāṭane ।।
vikalpayuktacitastu piṇḍapātācchivaṃ brajet । itarastu tadaiveti śāstrasyātra pradhānataḥ ।। jñeyasya hi paraṃ tattvaṃ yaḥ prakāśātmakaḥ śivaḥ । nahyaprakāśarūpasya prākāśyaṃ vastutāpi vā ।।
avastutāpi bhāvānāṃ camatkāraikagocarā । yatkuḍyasadṛśī neyaṃ dhīravastvetadityapi ।। prakāśo nāma yaścāyaṃ sarvatraiva prakāśate । anapahnavanīyatvāt kiṃ tasminmānakalpanaiḥ ।।
pramāṇānyapi vastūnāṃ jīvitaṃ yāni tanvate । teṣāmapi paro jīvaḥ sa eva parameśvaraḥ ।। sarvāpahnavahevākadharmāpyevaṃ hi vartate । jñānamātmārthamityetanneti māṃ prati bhāsate ।।
apahnutau sādhane vā vastūnāmādyamīdṛśam । yattatra ke pramāṇānāmupapattyupayogite ।। [ missing]।। kāmike tata evoktaṃ hetuvādavivarjitam ।
tasya devātidevasya parāpekṣā na vidyate ।। parasya tadapekṣatvātsvatantro ayamataḥ sthitaḥ । anapekṣasya vaśino deśakālākṛtikramāḥ ।। niyatā neti sa vibhurnityo viśvākṛtiḥ śivaḥ ।
vibhutvātsarvago nityabhāvādādyantavarjitaḥ ।। viśvākṛtitvāccidacittadvaicitryāvabhāsakaḥ । tato asya bahurūpatvamuktaṃ dīkṣottarādike ।। bhuvanaṃ vigraho jyotiḥ khaṃ śabdo mantra eva ca ।
bindunādādisaṃbhinnaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ śiva ucyate ।। yo yadātmakatāniṣṭhastadbhāvaṃ sa prapadyate । vyomādiśabdavijñānātparo mokṣo na saṃśayaḥ ।। viśvākṛtitve devasya tadetaccopalakṣaṇam ।
anavacchinnatārūḍhāvavacchedalaye asya ca ।। uktaṃ ca kāmike devaḥ sarvākṛtirnirākṛtiḥ । jaladarpaṇavattena sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ carācaram ।। na cāsya vimutādyo ayaṃ dharmo anyonyaṃ vibhidyate ।
eka evāsya dharmo asau sarvākṣepeṇa vartate ।। tena svātantryaśaktyaiva yukta ityāñjaso vidhiḥ । bahuśaktitvamapyasya tacchaktyaivāviyuktatā ।। śaktiśca nāma bhāvasya svaṃ rūpaṃ mātṛkalpitam ।
tenādvayaḥ sa evāpi śaktimatparikalpane ।। mātṛklṛpte hi devasya tatra tatra vapuṣyalam । ko bhedo vastuto vahnerdagdhṛpaktṛtvayoriva ।। na vāsau paramārthena na kiṃcidbhāsanādṛte ।
nahyasti kiṃcittacchaktitadvadbhedo api vāstavaḥ ।। svaśaktyudrekajanakaṃ tādātmyādvastuno hi yat । śaktistadapi devyevaṃ bhāntyapyanyasvarūpiṇī ।। śivaścāluptavibhavastathā sṛṣṭo avabhāsate ।
svasaṃvinmātṛmakure svātantryādbhāvanādiṣu ।। tasmādyena mukhenaiṣa bhātyanaṃśo api tattathā । śaktirityeṣa vastveva śaktitadvatkramaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।। śrīmatkiraṇaśāstre ca tatpraśnottarapūrvakam ।
anubhāvo vikalpo api mānaso na manaḥ śive ।। avijñāya śivaṃ dīkṣā kathamityatra cottaram । kṣudhādyanubhavo naiva vikalpo nahi mānasaḥ ।। rasādyanadhyakṣatve api rūpādeva yathā tarum ।
vikalpo vetti tadvattu nādabindvādinā śivam ।। bahuśaktitvamasyoktaṃ śivasya yadato mahān । kalātattvapurārṇāṇupadādirbhedavistaraḥ ।। sṛṣṭisthititirodhānasaṃhārānugrahādi ca ।
turyamityapi devasya bahuśaktitvajṛmbhitam ।। jāgratsvapnasuṣuptānyatadatītāni yānyapi । tānyapyamuṣya nāthasya svātantryalaharībharaḥ ।। mahāmantreśamantreśamantrāḥ śivapurogamāḥ ।
akalau sakalaśceti śivasyaiva vibhūtayaḥ ।। tattvagrāmasya sarvasya dharmaḥ syādanapāyavān । ātmaiva hi svabhāvātmetyuktaṃ śrītriśiromate ।। hṛdisthaṃ sarvadehasthaṃ svabhāvasthaṃ susūkṣmakam ।
sāmūhyaṃ caiva tattvānāṃ grāmaśabdena kīrtitam ।। ātmaiva dharma ityuktaḥ śivāmṛtapariplutaḥ । prakāśāvasthitaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvābhāvādimadhyataḥ ।। svasthāne vartanaṃ jñeyaṃ draṣṭṛtvaṃ vigatāvṛti ।
viviktavastukathitaśuddhavijñānanirmalaḥ ।। grāmadharmavṛttiruktastasya sarvaṃ prasiddhyati । ūrdhva tyaktvādho viśetsa rāmastho madhyadeśagaḥ ।। gatiḥ sthānaṃ svapnajāgradunmeṣaṇanimeṣaṇe ।
dhāvanaṃ plavanaṃ caiva āyāsaḥ śaktivedanam ।। buddhibhedāstathā bhāvāḥ saṃjñāḥ karmāṇyanekaśaḥ । eṣa rāmo vyāpako atra śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। kalmaṣakṣīṇamanasā smṛtimātranirodhanāt ।
dhyāyate paramaṃ dhyeyaṃ gamāgamapade sthitam ।। paraṃ śivaṃ tu vrajati bhairavākhyaṃ japādapi । tatsvarūpaṃ japaḥ prokto bhāvābhāvapadacyutaḥ ।। tadatrāpi tadīyena svātantryeṇopakalpitaḥ ।
dūrāsannādiko bhedaścitsvātantryavyapekṣayā ।। evaṃ svātantryapūrṇatvādatidurghaṭakāryayam । kena nāma na rūpeṇa bhāsate parameśvaraḥ ।। nirāvaraṇamābhāti bhātyābṛtanijātmakaḥ ।
āvṛtānāvṛto bhāti bahudhā bhedasaṃgamāt ।। iti śaktitrayaṃ nāthe svātantryāparanāmakam । icchādibhirabhikhyābhirgurubhiḥ prakaṭīkṛtam ।। devo hyanvarthaśāstroktaiḥ śabdaiḥ samupadiśyate ।
mahābhairavadevo ayaṃ patiryaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ ।। viśvaṃ bibharti pūraṇadhāraṇayogena tena ca śriyate । savimarśatayā rava rūpataśca saṃsārabhīruhitakṛcca ।। saṃsārabhītijanitādravātparāmarśato api hṛdi jātaḥ ।
prakaṭībhūtaṃ bhavabhayavimarśanaṃ śaktipātato yena ।। nakṣatraprerakakālatattvasaṃśoṣakāriṇo ye ca । kālagrāsasamādhānarasikamanaḥsu teṣu ca prakaṭaḥ ।। saṃkocipaśujanabhiye yāsāṃ ravaṇaṃ svakaraṇadevīnām ।
antarbahiścaturvidhakhecaryādikagaṇasyāpi ।। tasya svāmī saṃsāravṛttivighaṭanamahābhīmaḥ । bhairava iti gurubhirimairanvarthaiḥ saṃstutaḥ śāstre ।। heyopādeyakathāvirahe svānandaghanatayocchalanam ।
krīḍā sarvotkarṣeṇavartanecchā tathā svatantratvam ।। vyavaharaṇamabhinne api svātmani bhedena saṃjalpaḥ । nikhilāvabhāsanācca dyotanamasya stutiryataḥ sakalam ।। tatpravaṇamātmalābhātprabhṛti samaste api kartavye ।
bodhātmakaḥ samastakriyāmayo dṛkkriyāguṇaśca gatiḥ ।। iti nirvacanaiḥ śivatanuśāstre gurubhiḥ smṛto devaḥ । śāsanarodhanapālanapācanayogātsa sarvamupakurute । tena patiḥ śreyomaya eva śivo nāśivaṃ kimapi tatra ।।
īdṛgrūpaṃ kiyadapi rudropendrādiṣu sphuredyena । tenāvacchedanude paramamahatpadaviśeṣaṇamupāttam ।। iti yajjñeyasatattvaṃ darśyate tacchivājñayā । mayā svasaṃvitsattarkapatiśāstratrikakramāt ।।
tasya śaktaya evaitāstisro bhānti parādikāḥ । sṛṣṭau sthitau laye turye tenaitā dvādaśoditāḥ ।। tāvānpūrṇasvabhāvo asau paramaḥ śiva ucyate । tenātropāsakāḥ sākṣāttatraiva pariniṣṭhitāḥ ।।
tāsāmapi ca bhedāṃśanyūnādhikyādiyojanam । tatsvātantryabalādeva śāstreṣu paribhāṣitam ।। ekavīro yāmalo atha triśaktiścaturātmakaḥ । pañcamūrtiḥ ṣaḍātmāyaṃ saptako aṣṭakabhūṣitaḥ ।।
navātmā daśadikchaktirekādaśakalātmakaḥ । dvādaśāramahācakranāyako bhairavastviti ।। evaṃ yāvatsahasrāre niḥsaṃkhyāre api vā prabhuḥ । viśvacakre maheśāno viśvaśaktirvijṛmbhate ।।
teṣāmapi ca cakrāṇā svavargānugamātmanā । aikyena cakrago bhedastatra tatra nirūpitaḥ ।। catuṣṣaḍdvirdvigaṇanāyogāttraiśirase mate । ṣaṭcakreśvaratā nāthasyoktā citranijākṛteḥ ।।
nāmāni cakradevīnāṃ tatra kṛtyavibhedataḥ । saumyaraudrākṛtidhyānayogīnyanvarthakalpanāt ।। ekasya saṃvinnāthasya hyāntarī pratibhā tanuḥ । saumyaṃ vānyanmitaṃ saṃvidūrmicakramupāsyate ।।
asya syātpuṣṭirityeṣā saṃviddevī tathoditāt । dhyānātsaṃjalpasaṃmiśrād vyāpārāccāpi bāhyataḥ ।। sphuṭībhūtā satī bhāti tasya tādṛkphalapradā । puṣṭiḥ śuṣkasya sarasībhāvo jalamataḥ sitam ।।
anugamya tato dhyānaṃ tatpradhānaṃ pratanyate । ye ca svabhāvato varṇā rasaniḥṣyandino yathā ।। dantyauṣṭhyadantyaprāyāste kaiścidvarṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ saha । taṃ bījabhāvamāgatya saṃvidaṃ sphuṭayanti tām ।।
puṣṭiṃ kuru rasenainamāpyāyaya tarāmiti । saṃjalpo api vikalpātmā kiṃ tāmeva na pūrayet ।। amṛteyamidaṃ kṣīramidaṃ sarpirbalāvaham । tenāsya bījaṃ puṣṇīyāmityenāṃ pūrayetkriyām ।।
tasmādviśveśvaro bodhabhairavaḥ samupāsyate । avacchedānavacchidbhyāṃ bhogamokṣārthibhirjanaiḥ ।। ye apyanyadevatābhaktā ityato gururādiśat । ye bodhādvyatiriktaṃ hi kiṃcidyājyatayā viduḥ ।।
te api vedyaṃ viviñcānā bodhābhedena manvate । tenāvicchinnatāmarśarūpāhantāprathātmanaḥ ।। svayaṃ-prathasya na vidhiḥ sṛṣṭyātmāsya ca pūrvagaḥ । vedyā hi devatāsṛṣṭiḥ śakterhetoḥ samutthitā ।।
ahaṃrūpā tu saṃvittirnityā svaprathanātmikā । vidhirniyogastryaṃśā ca bhāvanā codanātmikā ।। tadekasiddhā indrādyā vidhipūrvā hi devatāḥ । ahaṃbodhastu na tathā te tu saṃvedyarūpatām ।।
unmagnāmeva paśyantastaṃ vidanto api no viduḥ । taduktaṃ na vidurmāṃ tu tattvenātaścalanti te ।। calanaṃ tu vyavacchinnarūpatāpattireva yā । devāndevayajo yāntītyādi tena nyarūpyata ।।
nimajjya vedyatāṃ ye tu tatra saṃvinmayīṃ sthitim । viduste hyanavacchinnaṃ tadbhaktā api yānti mām ।। sarvatrātra hyahaṃśabdo bodhamātraikavācakaḥ । sa bhoktṛprabhuśabdābhyāṃ yājyayaṣṭṭatayoditaḥ ।।
yājamānī saṃvideva yājyā nānyeti coditam । na tvākṛtiḥ kuto apyanyā devatā na hi socitā ।। vidhiśca noktaḥ ko apyatra mantrādi vṛttidhāma vā । so ayamātmānamāvṛtya sthito jaḍapadaṃ gataḥ ।।
āvṛtānāvṛtātmā tu devādisthāvarāntagaḥ । jaḍājaḍasyāpyetasya dvairūpyasyāsti citratā ।। tasya svatantrabhāvo hi kiṃ kiṃ yanna vicintayet । taduktaṃ triśiraḥśāstre saṃbuddha iti vetti yaḥ ।।
jñeyabhāvo hi ciddharmastacchāyācchādayenna tām ।। । tenājaḍasya bhāgasya pudgalāṇvādisaṃjñinaḥ । anāvaraṇabhāgāṃśe vaicitryaṃ bahudhā sthitam ।। saṃvidrūpe na bhedo asti vāstavo yadyapi dhruve ।
tathāpyāvṛtinirhāsatāratamyātsa lakṣyate ।। tadvistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ śaktipātavinirṇaye । samāpya paratāṃ sthaulyaprasaṃge carcayiṣyate ।। ataḥ kaṃcitpramātāraṃ prati prathayate vibhuḥ ।
pūrṇameva nijaṃ rūpaṃ kaṃcidaṃśāṃśikākramāt ।। viśvabhāvaikabhāvātmasvarūpaprathanaṃ hi yat । aṇūnāṃ tatparaṃ jñānaṃ tadanyadaparaṃ bahu ।। tacca sākṣādupāyena tadupāyādināpi ca ।
prathamānaṃ vicitrābhirbhaṃgībhiriha bhidyate ।। tatrāpi svaparadvāradvāritvātsarvaśoṃśaśaḥ । vyavadhānāvyavadhinā bhūyānbhedaḥ pravartate ।। jñānasya cābhyupāyo yo na tadajñānamucyate ।
jñānameva tu tatsūkṣmaṃ paraṃ tvicchātmakaṃ matam ।। upāyopeyabhāvastu jñānasya sthaulyaviśramaḥ । eṣaiva ca kriyāśaktirbandhamokṣaikakāraṇam ।। tatrādye svaparāmarśe nirvikalpaikadhāmani ।
yatsphuretprakaṭaṃ sākṣāttadicchākhyaṃ prakīrtitam ।। yathā visphuritadṛśāmanusandhiṃ vināpyalam । bhāti bhāvaḥ sphuṭastadvatkeṣāmapi śivātmatā ।। bhūyo bhūyo vikalpāṃśaniścayakramacarcanāt ।
yatparāmarśamabhyeti jñānopāyaṃ tu tadviduḥ ।। yattu tatkalpanāklṛptabahirbhūtārthasādhanam । kriyopāyaṃ tadāmnātaṃ bhedo nātrāpavargagaḥ ।। yato nānyā kriyā nāma jñānameva hi tattathā ।
rūḍheryogāntatāṃ prāptamiti śrīgamaśāsane ।। yogo nānyaḥ kriyā nānyā tattvārūḍhā hi yā matiḥ । svacittavāsanāśāntau sā kriyetyabhidhīyate ।। svacitte vāsanāḥ karmamalamāyāprasūtayaḥ ।
tāsāṃ śāntinimittaṃ yā matiḥ saṃvitsvabhāvikā ।। sā dehārambhibāhyasthatattvabrātādhiśāyinī । kriyā saiva ca yogaḥ syāttattvānāṃ cillayīkṛtau ।। loke api kila gacchāmītyevamantaḥ sphuraiva yā ।
sā dehaṃ deśamakṣāṃścāpyāviśantī gatikriyā ।। tasmātkriyāpi yā nāma jñānameva hi sā tataḥ । jñānameva vimokṣāya yuktaṃ caitadudāhṛtam ।। mokṣo hi nāma naivānyaḥ svarūpaprathanaṃ hi saḥ ।
svarūpaṃ cātmanaḥ saṃvinnānyattatra tu yāḥ punaḥ ।। kriyādikāḥ śaktayastāḥ saṃvidrūpādhikā nahi । asaṃvidrūpatāyogāddharmiṇaścānirūpaṇāt ।। parameśvaraśāstre hi na ca kāṇādadṛṣṭivat ।
śaktīnāṃ dharmarūpāṇāmāśrayaḥ ko api kathyate ।। tataśca dṛkkriyecchādyā bhinnāścecchaktayastathā । ekaḥ śiva itīyaṃ vāgvastuśūnyaiva jāyate ।। tasmātsaṃvittvamevaitatsvātantryaṃ yattadapyalam ।
vivicyamānaṃ bahvīṣu paryavasyati śaktiṣu ।। yataścātmaprathā mokṣastannehāśaṅkyamīdṛśam । nāvaśyaṃ kāraṇātkārya tajjñānyapi na mucyate ।। yato jñānena mokṣasya yā hetuphalatoditā ।
na sā mukhyā tato nāyaṃ prasaṃga iti niścitam ।। evaṃ jñānasvabhāvaiva kriyā sthūlatvamātmani । yato vahati tenāsyāṃ citratā dṛśyatāṃ kila ।। kriyopāye abhyupāyānāṃ grāhyabāhyavibhedinām ।
bhedopabhedavaividhyānniḥsaṃkhyatvamavāntarāt ।। anena caitatpradhvastaṃ yatkecana śaśaṅkire । upāyabhedānmokṣe api bhedaḥ syāditi sūrayaḥ ।। malatacchaktividhvaṃsatirobhūcyutimadhyataḥ ।
hetubhede api no bhinnā ghaṭadhvaṃsādivṛttivat ।। tadetattrividhatvaṃ hi śāstre śrīpūrvanāmani । ādeśi parameśitrā samāveśavinirṇaye ।। akiṃciccintakasyaiva guruṇā pratibodhataḥ ।
utpadyate ya āveśaḥ śāmbhavo asāvidīritaḥ ।। uccārarahitaṃ vastu cetasaiva vicintayan । yaṃ samāveśamāpnoti śāktaḥ so atrābhidhīyate ।। uccārakaraṇadhyānavarṇasthānaprakalpanaiḥ ।
yo bhavetsa samāveśaḥ samyagāṇava ucyate ।। akiṃciccintakasyeti vikalpānupayogitā । tayā ca jhaṭiti jñeyasamāpattirnirūpyate ।। sā kathaṃ bhavatītyāha guruṇātigarīyasā ।
jñeyābhimukhabodhena drākprarūḍhatvaśālinā ।। tṛtīyārthe tasi vyākhyā vā vaiyadhikaraṇyataḥ । āveśaścāsvatantrasya svatadrūpanimajjanāt ।। paratadrūpatā śambhorādyācchaktyavibhāginaḥ ।
tenāyamatra vākyārtho vijñeyaṃ pronmiṣatsvayam ।। vināpi niścayena drāk mātṛdarpaṇabimbitam । mātāramadharīkurvat svāṃ vibhūtiṃ pradarśayat ।। āste hṛdayanairmalyātiśaye tāratamyataḥ ।
jñeyaṃ dvidhā ca cinmātraṃ jaḍaṃ cādyaṃ ca kalpitam ।। itarattu tathā satyaṃ tadvibhāgo ayamīdṛśaḥ । jaḍena yaḥ samāveśaḥ sapraticchandakākṛtiḥ ।। caitanyena samāveśastādātmyaṃ nāparaṃ kila ।
tenāvikalpā saṃvittirbhāvanādyanapekṣiṇī ।। śivatādātmyamāpannā samāveśo atra śāṃbhavaḥ । tatprasādātpunaḥ paścādbhāvino atra viniścayāḥ ।। santu tādātmyamāpannā na tu teṣāmupāyatā ।
vikalpāpekṣayā mānamavikalpamiti bruvan ।। pratyukta eva siddhaṃ hi vikalpenānugamyate । gṛhītamiti suspaṣṭā niścayasya yataḥ prathā ।। gṛhṇāmītyavikalpaikyabalāttu pratipadyate ।
avikalpātmasaṃvittau yā sphurattaiva vastunaḥ ।। sā siddhirna vikalpāttu vastvapekṣāvivarjitāt । kevalaṃ saṃvidaḥ so ayaṃ nairmalyetaraviśramaḥ ।। yadvikalpānapekṣatvasāpekṣatve nijātmani ।
niśīthe api maṇijñānī vidyutkālapradarśitān ।। tāṃstānviśeṣāṃścinute ratnānāṃ bhūyasāmapi । nairmalyaṃ saṃvidaścedaṃ pūrvābhyāsavaśādatho ।। aniyantreśvarecchāta ityetaccarcayiṣyate ।
pañcāśadvidhatā cāsya samāveśasya varṇitā ।। tattvaṣaṭtriṃśakaitatsthasphuṭabhedābhisandhitaḥ । etattattvāntare yatpuṃvidyāśaktyātmakaṃ trayam ।। ambhodhikāṣṭhājvalanasaṃkhyairbhedairyataḥ kramāt ।
puṃvidyāśaktisaṃjñaṃ yattatsarvavyāpakaṃ yataḥ ।। avyāpakebhyastenedaṃ bhedena gaṇitaṃ kila । aśuddhiśuddhyamānatvaśuddhitastu mitho api tat ।। bhūtānyadhyakṣasiddhāni kāryahetvanumeyataḥ ।
tattvavargātpṛthagbhūtasamākhyānyata eva hi ।। sarvapratītisadbhāvagocaraṃ bhūtameva hi । viduścatuṣṭaye cātra sāvakāśe tadāsthitim ।। rudraśaktisamāveśaḥ pañcadhā nanu carcyate ।
ko avakāśo bhavettatra bhautāveśādivarṇane ।। prasaṃgādetaditicetsamādhiḥ saṃbhavannayam । nāsmākaṃ mānasāvarjī loko bhinnaruciryataḥ ।। ucyate dvaitaśāstreṣu parameśādvibheditā ।
bhūtādīnāṃ yathā sātra na tathā dvayavarjite ।। yāvānṣaṭtriṃśakaḥ so ayaṃ yadanyadapi kiṃcana । etāvatī mahādevī rudraśaktiranargalā ।। tata eva dvitīye asminnadhikāre nyarūpyata ।
dharāderviśvarūpatvaṃ pāñcadaśyādibhedataḥ ।। tasmādyathā purasthe arthe guṇādyaṃśāṃśikāmukhāt । niraṃśabhāvasaṃbodhastathaivātrāpi budhyatām ।। ata evāvikalpatvadhrauvyaprābhavavaibhavaiḥ ।
anyairvā śaktirūpatvāddharmaiḥ svasamavāyibhiḥ ।। sarvaśo apyatha vāṃśena taṃ vibhuṃ parameśvaram । upāsate vikalpaughasaṃskārādye śrutotthitāt ।। te tattatsvavikalpāntaḥsphurattaddharmapāṭavāt ।
dharmiṇaṃ pūrṇadharmaughamabhedenādhiśerate ।। ūcivānata eva śrīvidyādhipatirādarāt । tvatsvarūpamavikalpamakṣajā kalpane na viṣayīkaroti cet । antarullikhitacitrasaṃvido no bhaveyuranubhūtayaḥ sphuṭāḥ ।।
taduktaṃ śrīmataṅgādau svaśaktikiraṇātmakam । atha patyuradhiṣṭhānamityādyuktaṃ viśeṣaṇaiḥ ।। tasyāṃ divi sudīptātmā niṣkampo acalamūrtimān । kāṣṭhā saiva parā sūkṣmā sarvadikkāmṛtātmikā ।।
pradhvastāvaraṇā śāntā vastumātrātilālasā । ādyantoparatā sādhvī mūrtitvenopacaryate ।। tathopacārasyātraitannimitaṃ saprayojanam । tanmukhā sphuṭatā dharmiṇyāśu tanmayatāsthitiḥ ।।
ta eva dharmāḥ śaktyākhyāstaistairucitarūpakaiḥ । ākāraiḥ paryupāsyante tanmayībhāvasiddhaye ।। tatra kācitpunaḥ śaktiranantā vā mitāśca vā । ākṣipeddhavatāsattvanyāyāddūrāntikatvataḥ ।।
tena pūrṇasvabhāvatvaṃ prakāśatvaṃ cidātmatā । bhairavatvaṃ viśvaśaktīrākṣipedvyāpakatvataḥ ।। sadāśivādayastūrdhvavyāptyabhāvādadhojuṣaḥ । śaktīḥ samākṣipeyustadupāsāntikadūrataḥ ।।
itthaṃ-bhāve ca śāktākhyo vaikalpikapathakramaḥ । iha tūkto yatastasmāt pratiyogyavikalpakam ।। avikalpapathārūḍho yena yena pathā viśet । dharāsadāśivāntena tena tena śivībhavet ।।
nirmale hṛdaye prāgryasphuradbhūmyaṃśabhāsini । prakāśe tanmukhenaiva saṃvitparaśivātmatā ।। evaṃ parecchāśaktyaṃśasadupāyamimaṃ viduḥ । śāmbhavākhyaṃ samāveśaṃ sumatyantenivāsinaḥ ।।
śākto atha bhaṇyate cetodhī-manohaṃkṛti sphuṭam । savikalpatayā māyāmayamicchādi vastutaḥ ।। abhimānena saṃkalpādhyavasāyakrameṇa yaḥ । śāktaḥ sa māyopāyo api tadante nirvikalpakaḥ ।।
paśorvai yāvikalpā bhūrdaśā sā śāmbhavī param । apūrṇā mātṛdaurātmyāttadapāye vikasvarā ।। evaṃ vaikalpikī bhūmiḥ śākte kartṛtvavedane । yasyāṃ sphuṭe paraṃ tvasyāṃ saṃkocaḥ pūrvanītitaḥ ।।
tathā saṃkocasaṃbhāravilāyanaparasya tu । sā yatheṣṭāntarābhāsakāriṇī śaktirujjvalā ।। nanu vaikalpikī kiṃ dhīrāṇave nāsti tatra sā । anyopāyātra tūccārarahitatvaṃ nyarūpayat ।।
uccāraśabdenātroktā bahvantena tadādayaḥ । śaktyupāye na santyete bhedābhedau hi śaktitā ।। aṇurnāma sphuṭo bhedastadupāya ihāṇavaḥ । vikalpaniścayātmaiva paryante nirvikalpakaḥ ।।
nanu dhī-mānasāhaṃkṛtpumāṃso vyāpnuyuḥ śivam । nādhovartitayā tena kathitaṃ kathamīdṛśam ।। ucyate vastuto asmākaṃ śiva eva tathāvidhaḥ । svarūpagopanaṃ kṛtvā svaprakāśaḥ punastathā ।।
dvaitaśāstre mataṅgādau cāpyetatsunirūpitam । adhovyāptuḥ śivasyaiva sa prakāśo vyavasthitaḥ ।। yena buddhi-manobhūmāvapi bhāti paraṃ padam ।। dvāvapyetau samāveśau nirvikalpārṇavaṃ prati ।
prayāta eva tadrūḍhiṃ vinā naiva hi kiṃcana ।। saṃvittiphalabhiccātra na prakalpyetyato abravīt । kalpanāyāśca mukhyatvamatraiva kila sūcitam ।। vikalpāpekṣayā yo api prāmāṇyaṃ prāha tanmate ।
tadvikalpakramopāttanirvikalpapramāṇatā ।। ratnatattvamavidvānprāṅniścayopāyacarcanāt । anupāyāvikalpāptau ratnajña iti bhaṇyate ।। abhedopāyamatroktaṃ śāmbhavaṃ śāktamucyate ।
bhedābhedātmakopāyaṃ bhedopāyaṃ tadāṇavam ।। ante jñāne atra sopāye samastaḥ karmavistaraḥ । prasphuṭenaiva rūpeṇa bhāvī so antarbhaviṣyati ।। kriyā hi nāma vijñānānnānyadvastu kramātmatām ।
upāyavaśataḥ prāptaṃ tatkriyeti puroditam ।। samyagjñānaṃ ca muktyekakāraṇaṃ svaparasthitam । yato hi kalpanāmātraṃ svaparādivibhūtayaḥ ।। tulye kālpanikatve ca yadaikyasphuraṇātmakaḥ ।
guruḥ sa tāvadekātmā siddho muktaśca bhaṇyate ।। yāvānasya hi saṃtāno gurustāvatsa kīrtitaḥ । samyagjñānamayaśceti svātmanā mucyate tataḥ ।। tata eva svasaṃtānaṃ jñānī tārayatītyadaḥ ।
yuktyāgamābhyāṃ saṃsiddhaṃ tāvāneko yato muniḥ ।। tenātra ye codayanti nanu jñānādvimuktatā । dīkṣādikā kriyā ceyaṃ sā kathaṃ muktaye bhavet ।। jñānātmā seti cejjñānaṃ yatrasthaṃ taṃ vimocayet ।
anyasya mocane vāpi bhavetkiṃ nāsamañjasam । iti te mūlataḥ kṣiptā yattvatrānyaiḥ samarthitam ।। malo nāma kila dravyaṃ cakṣuḥsthapaṭalādivat । tadvihantrī kriyā dīkṣā tvañjanādikakarmavat ।।
tatpurastānniṣetsyāmo yuktyāgamavigarhitam । malamāyākarmaṇāṃ ca darśayiṣyāmahe sthitim ।। evaṃ śaktitrayopāyaṃ yajjñānaṃ tatra paścimam । mūlaṃ taduttaraṃ madhyamuttarottaramādimam ।।
tato api paramaṃ jñānamupāyādivivarjitam । ānandaśaktiviśrāntamanuttaramihocyate ।। tatsvaprakāśaṃ vijñānaṃ vidyāvidyeśvarādibhiḥ । api durlabhasadbhāvaṃ śrīsiddhātantra ucyate ।।
mālinyāṃ sūcitaṃ caitatpaṭale aṣṭādaśe sphuṭam । na caitadaprasannena śaṃkareṇeti vākyataḥ ।। ityanenaiva pāṭhena mālinīvijayottare । iti jñānacatuṣkaṃ yatsiddhimuktimahodayam ।
tanmayā tantryate tantrālokanāmnyatra śāsane ।। tatreha yadyadantarvā bahirvā parimṛśyate । anudghāṭitarūpaṃ tatpūrvameva prakāśate ।। tathānudghāṭitākārā nirvācyenātmanā prathā ।
saṃśayaḥ kutracidrūpe niścite sati nānyathā ।। etatkimiti mukhye asminnetadaṃśaḥ suniścitaḥ । saṃśayo astitvanāstyādidharmānudghāṭitātmakaḥ ।। kimityetasya śabdasya nādhiko arthaḥ prakāśate ।
kiṃ tvanunmudritākāraṃ vastvevābhidadhātyayam ।। sthāṇurvā puruṣo veti na mukhyo astyeṣa saṃśayaḥ । bhūyaḥsthadharmajāteṣu niścayotpāda eva hi ।। āmarśanīyadvairūpyānudghāṭanavaśātpunaḥ ।
saṃśayaḥ sa kimityaṃśe vikalpastvanyathā sphuṭaḥ ।। tenānudghāṭitātmatvabhāvaprathanameva yat । prathamaṃ sa ihoddeśaḥ praśnaḥ saṃśaya eva ca ।। tathānudghāṭitākārabhāvaprasaravartmanā ।
prasarantī svasaṃvittiḥ praṣṭrī śiṣyātmatāṃ gatā ।। tathāntaraparāmarśaniścayātmatirohiteḥ । prasarānantarodbhūtasaṃhārodayabhāgapi ।। yāvatyeva bhavedbāhyaprasare prasphuṭātmani ।
anunmīlitarūpā sā praṣṭrī tāvati bhaṇyate ।। svayamevaṃ vibodhaśca tathā praśnottarātmakaḥ । guruśiṣyapade apyeṣa dehabhedo hyatāttvikaḥ ।। bodho hi bodharūpatvādantarnānākṛtīḥ sthitāḥ ।
bahirābhāsayatyeva drāksāmānyaviśeṣataḥ ।। srakṣyamāṇaviśeṣāṃśākāṃkṣāyogyasya kasyacit । dharmasya sṛṣṭiḥ sāmānyasṛṣṭiḥ sā saṃśayātmikā ।। srakṣyamāṇo viśeṣāṃśo yadā tūparamettadā ।
nirṇayo mātṛrucito nānyathā kalpakoṭibhiḥ ।। tasyātha vastunaḥ svātmavīryākramaṇapāṭavāt । unmudraṇaṃ tayākṛtyā lakṣaṇottaranirṇayāḥ ।। nirṇītatāvaddharmāṃśapṛṣṭhapātitayā punaḥ ।
bhūyo bhūyaḥ samuddeśalakṣaṇātmaparīkṣaṇam ।। dṛṣṭānumānaupamyāptavacanādiṣu sarvataḥ । uddeśalakṣaṇāvekṣātritayaṃ prāṇināṃ sphuret ।। nirvikalpitamuddeśo vikalpo lakṣaṇaṃ punaḥ ।
parīkṣaṇaṃ tathādhyakṣe vikalpānāṃ paramparā ।। nago ayamiti coddeśo dhūmitvādagnimāniti । lakṣyaṃ vyāptyādivijñānajālaṃ tvatra parīkṣaṇam ।। uddeśo ayamiti prācyo gotulyo gavayābhidhaḥ ।
iti vā lakṣaṇaṃ śeṣaḥ parīkṣopamitau bhavet ।। svaḥkāma īdṛguddeśo yajetetyasya lakṣaṇam । agniṣṭomādinetyeṣā parīkṣā śeṣavartinī ।। vikalpasrakṣyamāṇānyarucitāṃśasahiṣṇunaḥ ।
vastuno yā tathātvena sṛṣṭiḥ soddeśasaṃjñitā ।। tadaiva saṃviccinute yāvataḥ srakṣyamāṇatā । yato hyakālakalitā saṃdhatte sārvakālikam ।। srakṣyamāṇasya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prāksṛṣṭāṃśasya saṃhṛtiḥ ।
anūdyamāne dharme sā saṃvillakṣaṇamucyate ।। tatpṛṣṭhapātibhūyoṃśasṛṣṭisaṃhāraviśramāḥ । parīkṣā kathyate mātṛrucitā kalpitāvadhiḥ ।। prākpaśyantyatha madhyānyā vaikharī ceti tā imāḥ ।
parā parāparā devī caramā tvaparātmikā ।। icchādi śaktitritayamidameva nigadyate । etatprāṇita evāyaṃ vyavahāraḥ pratāyate ।। etatpraśnottarātmatve pārameśvaraśāsane ।
parasaṃbandharūpatvamabhisaṃbandhapañcake ।। yathoktaṃ ratnamālāyāṃ sarvaḥ parakalātmakaḥ । mahānavāntaro divyo miśro anyo anyastu pañcamaḥ ।। bhinnayoḥ praṣṭṛtadvaktroścaikātmyaṃ yatsa ucyate ।
saṃbandhaḥ paratā cāsya pūrṇaikātmyaprathāmayī ।। anenaiva nayena syātsaṃbandhāntaramapyalam । śāstravācyaṃ phalādīnāṃ paripūrṇatvayogataḥ ।। itthaṃ saṃvidiyaṃ devī svabhāvādeva sarvadā ।
uddeśāditrayaprāṇā sarvaśāstrasvarūpiṇī ।। tatrocyate puroddeśaḥ pūrvajānujabhedavān । vijñānabhidgatopāyaḥ paropāyastṛtīyakaḥ ।। śāktopāyo naropāyaḥ kālopāyo atha saptamaḥ ।
cakrodayo atha deśādhvā tattvādhvā tattvabhedanam ।। kalādyadhvādhvopayogaḥ śaktipātatirohitī । dīkṣopakramaṇaṃ dīkṣā sāmayī pautrike vidhau ।। prameyaprakriyā sūkṣmā dīkṣā sadyaḥsamutkramaḥ ।
tulādīkṣātha pārokṣī liṅgoddhāro abhiṣecanam ।। antyeṣṭiḥ śrāddhaklṛptiśca śeṣavṛttinirūpaṇam । liṅgārcā bahubhitparvapavitrādi nimittajam ।। rahasyacaryā mantraugho maṇḍalaṃ mudrikāvidhiḥ ।
ekīkāraḥ svasvarūpe praveśaḥ śāstramelanam ।। āyātikathanaṃ śāstropādeyatvanirūpaṇam । iti saptādhikāmenāṃ triṃśataṃ yaḥ sadā budhaḥ ।। āhnikānāṃ samabhyasyet sa sākṣādbhairavo bhavet ।
saptatriṃśatsu saṃpūrṇabodho yadbhairavo bhavet ।। kiṃ citramaṇavo apyasya dṛśā bhairavatāmiyuḥ । ityeṣa pūrvajoddeśaḥ kathyate tvanujo adhunā ।। vijñānabhitprakaraṇe bharvasyoddeśanaṃ kramāt ।
dvitīyasminprakaraṇe gatopāyatvabheditā ।। viśvacitpratibinbatvaṃ parāmarśodayakramaḥ । mantrādyabhinnarūpatvaṃ paropāye vivicyate ।। vikalpasaṃskriyā tarkatattvaṃ gurusatattvakam ।
yogāṅgānupayogitvaṃ kalpitārcādyanādaraḥ ।। saṃviccakrodayo mantravīrya japyādi vāstavam । niṣedhavidhitulyatvaṃ śāktopāye atra carcyate ।। buddhidhyānaṃ prāṇatattvasamuccāraścidātmatā ।
uccāraḥ paratattvāntaḥpraveśapathalakṣaṇam ।। karaṇaṃ varṇatattvaṃ cetyāṇave tu nirūpyate । cāramānamahorātrasaṃkrāntyādivikalpanam ।। saṃhāracitratā varṇodayaḥ kālādhvakalpane ।
cakrabhinmantravidyābhidetaccakrodaye bhavet ।। parimāṇaṃ purāṇāṃ ca saṃgrahastattvayojanam । etaddeśādhvanirdeśe dvayaṃ tattvādhvanirṇaye ।। kāryakāraṇabhāvaśca tattvakramanirūpaṇam ।
vastudharmastattvavidhirjāgradādinirūpaṇam ।। pramātṛbheda ityetat tattvabhede vicāryate । kalāsvarūpamekatripañcādyaistattvakalpanam ।। varṇabhedakramaḥ sarvādhāraśaktinirūpaṇam ।
kalādyadhvavicārāntaretāvatpravivicyate ।। abhedabhāvanākampahāsau tvadhvopayojane । saṃkhyādhikyaṃ malādīnāṃ tattvaṃ śaktivicitratā ।। anapekṣitvasiddhiśca tirobhāvavicitratā ।
śaktipātaparīkṣāyāmetāvānvācyasaṃgrahaḥ ।। tirobhāvavyapagamo jñānena paripūrṇatā । utkrāntyanupayogitvaṃ dīkṣopakramaṇe sthitam ।। śiṣyaucityaparīkṣādau sthānabhitsthānakalpanam ।
sāmānyanyāsabhedo arghapātraṃ caitatprayojanam ।। dravyayogyatvamarcā ca bahirdvārārcanaṃ kramāt । praveśo diksvarūpaṃ ca dehaprāṇādiśodhanam ।। viśeṣanyāsavaicitryaṃ saviśeṣārghabhājanam ।
dehapūjā prāṇabuddhicitsvadhvanyāsapūjane ।। anyaśāstragaṇotkarṣaḥ pūjā cakrasya sarvataḥ । kṣetragrahaḥ pañcagavyaṃ pūjanaṃ bhūgaṇeśayoḥ ।। astrārcā vahnikāryaṃ cāpyadhivāsanamagnigam ।
tarpaṇaṃ carusaṃsiddhirdantakāṣṭhāntasaṃskriyā ।। śivahastavidhiścāpi śayyāklṛptivicāraṇam । svapnasya sāmayaṃ karma samayāśceti saṃgrahaḥ ।। samayitvavidhāvasminsyātpañcadaśa āhnike ।
maṇḍalātmānusandhānaṃ nivedyapaśuvistaraḥ ।। agnitṛptiḥ svasvabhāvadīpanaṃ śiṣyadehagaḥ । adhvanyāsavidhiḥ śodhyaśodhakādivicitratā ।। dīkṣābhedaḥ paro nyāso mantrasattāprayojanam ।
bhedo yojanikādeśca ṣoḍaśe syādihāhnike ।। sūtraklṛptistattvaśuddhiḥ pāśadāho atha yojanam । adhvabhedastathetyevaṃ kathitaṃ pautrike vidhau ।। jananādivihīnatvaṃ mantrabhedo atha susphuṭaḥ ।
iti saṃkṣiptadīkṣākhye syādaṣṭādaśa āhnike ।। kalāvekṣā kṛpāṇyādinyāsaścāraḥ śarīragaḥ । brahmavidyāvidhiścaivamuktaṃ sadyaḥsamutkrame ।। adhikāraparīkṣāntaḥsaṃskāro atha tulāvidhiḥ ।
ityetadvācyasarvasvaṃ syādviṃśatitamāhnike ।। mṛtajīvadvidhirjālo padeśaḥ saṃskriyāgaṇaḥ । balābalavicāraścetyekaviṃśāhnike vidhiḥ ।। śravaṇaṃ cābhyanujñānaṃ śodhanaṃ pātakacyutiḥ ।
śaṅkāccheda iti spaṣṭaṃ vācyaṃ liṅgoddhṛtikrame ।। parīkṣācāryakaraṇaṃ tadvrataṃ haraṇaṃ mateḥ । tadvibhāgaḥ sādhakatvamabhiṣekavidhau tviyat ।। adhikāryatha saṃskārastatprayojanamityadaḥ ।
caturviṃśe antyayāgākhye vaktavyaṃ paricarcyate ।। prayojanaṃ bhogamokṣadānenātra vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ । pañcaviṃśāhnike śrāddhaprakāśe vastusaṃgrahaḥ ।। prayojanaṃ śeṣavṛtternityārcā sthaṇḍile parā ।
liṅgasvarūpaṃ bahudhā cākṣasūtranirūpaṇam ।। pūjābheda iti vācyaṃ liṅgārcāsaṃprakāśane । naimittikavibhāgastatprayojanavidhistataḥ ।। parvabhedāstadviśeṣaścakracarcā tadarcanam ।
gurvādyantadinādyarcāprayojananirūpaṇam ।। mṛteḥ parīkṣā yogīśīmelakādividhistathā । vyākhyāvidhiḥ śrutavidhirgurupūjāvidhistviyat ।। naimittikaprakāśākhye apyaṣṭāviṃśāhnike sthitam ।
adhikāryātmano bhedaḥ siddhapatnīkulakramaḥ ।। arcāvidhirdautavidhī rahasyopaniṣatkramaḥ । dīkṣābhiṣekau bodhaścetyekonatriṃśa āhnike ।। mantrasvarūpaṃ tadvīryamiti triṃśe nirūpitam ।
śūlābjabhedo vyomaśasvastikādinirūpaṇam ।। vistareṇābhidhātavyamityekatriṃśa āhnike । guṇapradhānatābhedāḥ svarūpaṃ vīryacarcanam ।। kalābheda iti proktaṃ mudrāṇāṃ saṃprakāśane ।
dvātriṃśatattvādīśākhyātprabhṛti prasphuṭo yataḥ ।। na bhedo asti tato noktamuddeśāntaramatra tat । mukhyatvena ca vedyatvādadhikārāntarakramaḥ ।। ityuddeśavidhiḥ proktaḥ sukhasaṃgrahahetave ।
athāsya lakṣaṇāvekṣe nirūpyete yathākramam ।। ātmā saṃvitprakāśasthitiranavayavā saṃvidityāttaśaktivrātaṃ tasya svarūpaṃ sa ca nija mahasaśchādanādbaddharūpaḥ । ātmajyotiḥsvabhāvaprakaṭanavidhinā tasya mokṣaḥ sa cāyaṃ citrākārasya citraḥ prakaṭita iha yatsaṃgraheṇārtha eṣaḥ ।। mithyājñānaṃ timiramasamān dṛṣṭidoṣānprasūte tatsadbhāvādvimalamapi tadbhāti mālinyadhāma ।
yattu prekṣyaṃ dṛśi parigataṃ taimirīṃ doṣamudrāṃ dūraṃ runddhetprabhavatu kathaṃ tatra mālinyaśaṅkā ।। bhāvavrāta? haṭhājjanasya hṛdayānyākramya yannartayan bhaṅgībhirvividhābhirātmahṛdayaṃ pracchādya saṃkrīḍase । yastvāmāha jaḍaṃ jaḍaḥ sahṛdayaṃmanyatvaduḥśikṣito manye amuṣya jaḍātmatā stutipadaṃ tvatsāmyasaṃbhāvanāt ।। iha galitamalāḥ parāvarajñāḥ śivasadbhāvamayā adhikriyante ।
guravaḥ pravicāraṇe yatastadviphalā dveṣakalaṃkahāniyācñā ।। e tantrāloke abhinavaracite amutra vijñānasattābhedodgāraprakaṭanapaṭāvāhnike asminsamāptiḥ । yattatrādyaṃ padamaviratānuttarajñaptirūpaṃ । tannirṇetuṃ prakaraṇamidamārabhe ahaṃ dvitīyam ।।
anupāyaṃ hi yadrūpaṃ ko artho deśanayātra vai । sakṛtsyāddeśanā paścādanupāyatvamucyayate ।। anupāyamidaṃ tattvamityupāyaṃ vinā kutaḥ । svayaṃ tu teṣāṃ tattādṛk kiṃ brūmaḥ kila tānprati ।।
yaccaturdhoditaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānasya vibhorasau । svabhāva eva mantavyaḥ sa hi nityodito vibhuḥ ।। etāvadbhirasaṃkhyātaiḥ svabhāvairyatprakāśate । ke apyaṃśāṃśikayā tena viśantyanye niraṃśataḥ ।।
tatrāpi cābhyupāyādisāpekṣānyatvayogataḥ । upāyasyāpi no vāryā tadanyatvādvicitratā ।। tatra ye nirmalātmāno bhairavīyāṃ svasaṃvidam । nirupāyāmupāsīnāstadvidhiḥ praṇigadyate ।।
tatra tāvatkriyāyogo nābhyupāyatvamarhati । sa hi tasmātsamudbhūtaḥ pratyuta pravibhāvyate ।। jñaptāvupāya eva syāditi cejjñaptirucyate । prakāśatvaṃ svaprakāśe tacca tatrānyataḥ katham ।।
saṃvittattvaṃ svaprakāśamityasminkaṃ nu yuktibhiḥ । tadabhāve bhavedviśvaṃ jaḍatvādaprakāśakam ।। yāvānupāyo bāhyaḥ syādāntaro vāpi kaścana । sa sarvastanmukhaprekṣī tatropāyatvabhākkatham ।।
tyajāvadhānāni nanu kva nāma dhatse avadhānaṃ vicinu svayaṃ tat । pūrṇe avadhānaṃ na hi nāma yuktaṃ nāpūrṇamabhyeti ca satyabhāvam ।। tenāvadhānaprāṇasya bhāvanādeḥ pare pathi । bhairavīye kathaṃkāraṃ bhavetsākṣādupāyatā ।।
ye api sākṣādupāyena tadrūpaṃ praviviñcate । nūnaṃ te sūryasaṃvittyai khadyotādhitsavo jaḍāḥ ।। kiṃ ca yāvadidaṃ bāhyamāntaropāyasaṃmatam । tatprakāśātmatāmātraṃ śivasyaiva nijaṃ vapuḥ ।।
nīlaṃ pītaṃ sukhamiti prakāśaḥ kevalaḥ śivaḥ । amuṣminparamādvaite prakāśātmani ko aparaḥ ।। upāyopeyabhāvaḥ syātprakāśaḥ kevalaṃ hi saḥ ।। idaṃ dvaitama ayaṃ bheda idamadvaitamityapi ।
prakāśavapurevāyaṃ bhāsate parameśvaraḥ ।। asyāṃ bhūmau sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bandho mokṣaścitarjaḍaḥ । ghaṭakumbhavadekārthāḥ śabdāste apyekameva ca ।। praśāśe hyaprakāśāṃśaḥ kathaṃ nāma prakāśatām ।
prakāśamāne tasminvā taddvaitāstasya lopitāḥ ।। aprakāśe atha tasminvā vastutā kathamucyate । na prakāśaviśeṣatvamata evopapadyate ।। ata ekaprakāśo ayamiti vāde atra susthite ।
dūrādāvāritāḥ satyaṃ vibhinnajñānavādinaḥ ।। prakāśamātramuditamaprakāśaniṣedhanāt । ekaśabdasya na tvarthaḥ saṃkhyā cidvyaktibhedabhāk ।। naiṣa śaktirmahādevī na paratrāśrito yataḥ ।
na caiṣa śaktimāndevo na kasyāpyāśrayo yataḥ ।। naiṣa dhyeyo dhyātrabhāvānna dhyātā dhyeyavarjanāt । na pūjyaḥ pūjakābhāvātpūjyābhāvānna pūjakaḥ ।। na mantro na ca mantryo asau na ca mantrayitā prabhuḥ ।
na dīkṣā dīkṣako vāpi na dīkṣāvānmaheśvaraḥ ।। sthānāsananirodhārghasaṃghānāvāhanādikam । visarjanāntaṃ nāstyatra kartṛkarmakriyojjhite ।। na sanna cāsatsadasanna ca tannobhayojjhitam ।
durvijñeyā hi sāvasthā kimapyetadanuttaram ।। ayamityavabhāso hi yo bhāvo avacchidātmakaḥ । sa eva ghaṭavalloke saṃstathā naiṣa bhairavaḥ ।। asattvaṃ cāprakāśatvaṃ na kutrāpyupayogitā ।
viśvasya jīvitaṃ satyaṃ prakāśaikātmakaśca saḥ ।। ābhyāmeva tu hetubhyāṃ na dvyātmā na dvayojjhitaḥ । sarvātmanā hi bhātyeṣa kena rūpeṇa mantryatām ।। śrīmattriśirasi proktaṃ parajñānasvarūpakam ।
śaktyā garbhāntarvartinyā śaktigarbha paraṃ padam ।। na bhāvo nāpyabhāvo na dvayaṃ vācāmagocarāt । akathyapadavīrūḍhaṃ śaktisthaṃ śaktivarjitam ।। iti ye rūḍhasaṃvittiparamārthapavitritāḥ ।
anuttarapathe rūḍhāste abhyupāyāniyantritāḥ ।। teṣāmidaṃ samābhāti sarvato bhāvamaṇḍalam । puraḥsthameva saṃvittibhairavāgnivilāpitam ।। eteṣāṃ sukhaduḥkhāṃśaśaṃkātaṃkavikalpanāḥ ।
nirvikalpaparāveśamātraśeṣatvamāgatāḥ ।। eṣāṃ na mantro na dhyānaṃ na pūjā nāpi kalpanā । na samayyādikācāryaparyantaḥ ko api viśramaḥ ।। samastayantraṇātantratroṭanāṭaṃkadharmiṇaḥ ।
nānugrahātparaṃ kiṃciccheṣavṛttau prayojanam ।। svaṃ kartavyaṃ kimapi kalayaṃlloka eṣa prayatnānno pārārthyaṃ prati ghaṭayate kāṃcana svapravṛttim । yastu dhvastākhilabhavamalo bhairavībhāvapūrṇaḥ kṛtyaṃ tasya sphuṭamidamiyallokakartavyamātram ।। taṃ ye paśyanti tādrūpyakrameṇāmalasaṃvidaḥ ।
te api tadrūpiṇastāvatyevāsyānugrahātmatā ।। etattattvaparijñānaṃ mukhyaṃ yāgādi kathyate । dīkṣāntaṃ vibhunā śrīmatsiddhayogīśvarīmate ।। sthaṇḍilāduttaraṃ tūraṃ tūrāduttarataḥ paṭaḥ ।
paṭāddhyānaṃ tato dhyeyaṃ tataḥ syāddhāraṇottarā ।। tato api yogajaṃ rūpaṃ tato api jñānamuttaram । jñānena hi mahāsiddho bhavedyogīśvarastviti ।। so api svātantryadhāmnā cedapyanirmalasaṃvidām ।
anugrahaṃ cikīrṣustadbhāvinaṃ vidhimāśrayet ।। anugrāhyānusāreṇa vicitraḥ sa ca kathyate । parāparādyupāyaughasaṃkīrṇatvavibhedataḥ ।। tadarthameva cāsyāpi parameśvararūpiṇaḥ ।
tadabhyupāyaśāstrādiśravaṇādhyayanādaraḥ ।। nahi tasya svatantrasya kāpi kutrāpi khaṇḍanā । nānirmalacitaḥ puṃso anugrahastvanupāyakaḥ ।। śrīmadūrmimahāśāstre siddhasaṃtānarūpake ।
idamuktaṃ tathā śrīmatsomānandādidaiśikaiḥ ।। gurorvākyādyuktipracayaracanonmārjanavaśāt samāśvāsācchāstraṃ prati samuditādvāpi kathitāt । vilīne śaṃkābhre tdṛdayagaganodbhāsimahasaḥ prabhoḥ sūryasyeva spṛśata caraṇāndhvāntajayinaḥ ।। idamanuttaradhāmavivecakaṃ vigalitaupayikaṃ kṛtamāhnikam ।।
atha paraupayikaṃ praṇigadyate padamanuttarameva maheśituḥ ।। prakāśamātraṃ yatproktaṃ bhairavīyaṃ paraṃ mahaḥ । tatra svatantratāmātramadhikaṃ pravivicyate ।। yaḥ prakāśaḥ sa sarvasya prakāśatvaṃ prayacchati ।
na ca tadvyatirekyasti viśvaṃ sadvāvabhāsate ।। ato asau parameśānaḥ svātmavyomanyanargalaḥ । iyataḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārāḍambarasya pradarśakaḥ ।। nirmale makure yadvadbhānti bhūmijalādayaḥ ।
amiśrāstadvadekasmiṃścinnāthe viśvavṛttayaḥ ।। sadṛśaṃ bhāti nayanadarpaṇāmbaravāriṣu । tathā hi nirmale rūpe rūpamevāvabhāsate ।। pracchannarāgiṇī kāntapratibimbitasundaram ।
darpaṇaṃ kucakumbhābhyāṃ spṛśantyapi na tṛpyati ।। na hi sparśo asya vimalo rūpameva tathā yataḥ । nairmalyaṃ cātiniviḍasajātīyaikasaṃgatiḥ ।। svasminnabhedādbhinnasya darśanakṣamataiva yā ।
atyaktasvaprakāśasya nairmalyaṃ tadgurūditam ।। nairmalyaṃ mukhyamekasya saṃvinnāthasya sarvataḥ । aṃśāṃśikātaḥ kvāpyanyadvimalaṃ tattadicchayā ।। bhāvānāṃ yatpratīghāti vapurmāyātmakaṃ hi tat ।
teṣāmevāsti sadvidyāmayaṃ tvapratighātakam ।। tadevamubhayākāramavabhāsaṃ prakāśayan । vibhāti varado bimbapratibimbadṛśākhile ।। yastvāha netratejāṃsi svacchātpratiphalantyalam ।
viparyasya svakaṃ vaktraṃ gṛhṇantīti sa pṛcchyate ।। dehādanyatra yattejastadadhiṣṭhāturātmanaḥ । tenaiva tejasā jñatve ko arthaḥ syāddarpaṇena tu ।। viparyastaistu tejobhirgrāhakātmatvamāgataiḥ ।
rūpaṃ dṛśyeta vadane nije na makurāntare ।। svamukhe sparśavaccaitadrūpaṃ bhāyānmametyalam । na tvasya spṛśyabhinnasya vedyaikāntasvarūpiṇaḥ ।। rūpasaṃsthānamātraṃ tatsparśagandharasādibhiḥ ।
nyagbhūtaireva tadyuktaṃ vastu tatpratibimbitam ।। nyagbhāvo grāhyatābhāvāttadabhāvo apramāṇataḥ । sa cārthasaṃgamābhāvātso apyādarśe anavasthiteḥ ।। ata eva gurutvādirdharmo naitasya lakṣyate ।
nahyādarśe saṃsthito asau taddṛṣṭau sa upāyakaḥ ।। tasmāttu naiṣa bhedena yadbhāti tata ucyate । ādhārastatra tūpāyā dīpadṛksaṃvidaḥ kramāt ।। dīpacakṣurvibodhānāṃ kāṭhinyābhāvataḥ param ।
sarvataścāpi nairmalyānna vibhādarśavatpṛthak ।। etacca devadevena darśitaṃ bodhavṛddhaye । mūḍhānāṃ vastu bhavati tato apyanyatra nāpyalam ।। pratīghāti svatantraṃ no na sthāyyasthāyi cāpi na ।
svacchasyaivaiṣa kasyāpi mahimeti kṛpālunā ।। na deśoṃ no rūpaṃ na ca samayayogo na parimā na cānyonyāsaṃgo na ca tadapahānirna ghanatā । na cāvastutvaṃ syānna ca kimapi sāraṃ nijamiti dhruvaṃ mohaḥ śāmyediti niradiśaddarpaṇavidhiḥ ।। itthaṃ pradarśite amutra pratibimbanavartmani ।
śabdasya pratibimbaṃ yat pratiśrutketi bhaṇyate ।। na cāsau śabdajaḥ śabda āgacchattvena saṃśravāt । tenaiva vaktrā dūrasthaiḥ śabdasyāśravaṇādapi ।। piṭhirādipidhānāṃśaviśiṣṭachidrasaṃgatau ।
citratvāccāsya śabdasya pratibimbaṃ mukhādivat ।। idamanyasya vedyasya rūpamityavabhāsate । yathādarśe tathā kenāpyuktamākarṇaye tviti ।। niyamādbimbasāṃmukhyaṃ pratibimbasya yattataḥ ।
tanmadhyagāḥ pramātāraḥ śṛṇvanti pratiśabdakam ।। mukhyagrahaṃ tvapi vinā pratibimbagraho bhavet । svapaścātsthaṃ priyaṃ paśyeṭṭaṅkitaṃ mukure vapuḥ ।। sāṃmukhyaṃ cocyate tādṛgdarpaṇābhedasaṃsthiteḥ ।।
ataḥ kūpādipiṭhirākāśe tatpratibimbitam । vaktrākāśaṃ saśabdaṃ sadbhāti tatparavaktavat ।। yathā cādarśapāścātyabhāgastho vetti no mukham । tathā tathāvidhākāśapaścātstho vetti na dhvanim ।।
śabdo na cānabhivyaktaḥ pratibimbati taddhruvam । abhivyaktiśrutī tasya samakālaṃ dvitīyake ।। kṣaṇe tu pratibimbatvaṃ śrutiśca samakālikā । tulyakālaṃ hi no hastatacchāyārūpaniścayaḥ ।।
itthaṃ pradarśite amutra pratibimbasatattvake । prakṛtaṃ brūmahe tatra pratibimbanamarhati ।। śabdo nabhasi sānande sparśadhāmani sundaraḥ । sparśo anyo api dṛḍhāghātaśūlaśītādikodbhavaḥ ।
parasthaḥ pratibimbatvātsvadehoddhūlanākaraḥ ।। na caiṣa mukhyastatkāryapāramparyāprakāśanāt ।। evaṃ ghrāṇāntare gandho raso dantodake sphuṭaḥ ।। yathā ca rūpaṃ pratibimbitaṃ dṛśorna cakṣuṣānyena vinā hi lakṣyate ।
tathā rasasparśanasaurabhādikaṃ na lakṣyate akṣeṇa vinā sthitaṃ tvapi ।। na cāntare sparśanadhāmani sthitaṃ bahiḥspṛśonyākṣadhiyaḥ sa gocaraḥ ।। ato antikasthasvakatādṛgindriyaprayojanāntaḥkaraṇairyadā kṛtā । tadā tadāttaṃ pratibimbamindriye svakāṃ kriyāṃ sūyata eva tādṛśīm ।।
na tu smṛtānmānasagocarādṛtā bhavetkriyā sā kila vartamānataḥ । ataḥ sthitaḥ sparśavarastadindriye samāgataḥ sanviditastathākriyaḥ ।। asaṃbhave bāhyagatasya tādṛśaḥ sva eva tasminpratibimbitastathā । karoti tāṃ sparśavaraḥ sukhātmikāṃ sa cāpi kasyāmapi nāḍisaṃtatau ।।
tena saṃvittimakure viśvamātmānamarpayat । nāthasya vadate amuṣya vimalāṃ viśvarūpatām ।। yathā ca gandharūpaspṛgrasādyāḥ pratibimbitāḥ । tadādhāroparāgeṇa bhānti khaṅge mukhādivat ।।
tathā viśvamidaṃ bodhe pratibimbitamāśrayet । prakāśatvasvatantratvaprabhṛtiṃ dharmavistaram ।। yathā ca sarvataḥ svacche sphaṭike sarvato bhavet । pratibimbaṃ tathā bodhe sarvataḥ svacchatājuṣi ।।
atyantasvacchatā sā yatsvākṛtyanavabhāsanam । ataḥ svacchatamo bodho na ratnaṃ tvākṛtigrahāt ।। pratibimbaṃ ca bimbena bāhyasthena samarpyate । tasyaiva pratibimbatve kiṃ bimbamavaśiṣyatām ।।
yadvāpi kāraṇaṃ kiṃcidbimbatvenābhiṣicyate । tadapi pratibimbatvameti bodhe anyathā tvasat ।। itthametatsvasaṃvittidṛḍhanyāyāstrarakṣitam । sāmrājyameva viśvatra pratibimbasya jṛmbhate ।।
nanu bimbasya virahe pratibimbaṃ kathaṃ bhavet । kiṃ kurmo dṛśyate taddhi nanu tadbimbamucyatām ।। naivaṃ tallakṣaṇābhāvādbimbaṃ kila kimucyate । anyāmiśraṃ svatantraṃ sadbhāsamānaṃ mukhaṃ yathā ।।
svarūpānapahānena pararūpasadṛkṣatām । pratibimbātmatāmāhuḥ khaḍgādarśatalādivat ।। uktaṃ ca sati bāhye api dhīrekānekavedanāt । anekasadṛśākārā na tvaneketi saugataiḥ ।।
nanvitthaṃ pratibimbasya lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ taducyate । anyavyāmiśraṇāyogāttadbhedāśakyabhāsanam । pratibimbamiti prāhurdarpaṇe vadanaṃ yathā ।। bodhamiśramidaṃ bodhādbhedenāśakyabhāsanam ।
paratattvādi bodhe kiṃ pratibimbaṃ na bhaṇyate ।। lakṣaṇasya vyavasthaiṣākasmāccedbimbamucyatām । prājñā vastuni yujyante na tu sāmayike dhvanau ।। nanu na pratibimbasya vinā bimbaṃ bhavetsthitiḥ ।
kiṃ tataḥ pratibimbe hi bimbaṃ tādātmyavṛtti na ।। ataśca lakṣaṇasyāsya proktasya tadasaṃbhave । na hānirhetumātre tu praśno ayaṃ paryavasyati ।। tatrāpi ca nimittākhye nopādāne kathaṃcana ।
nimittakāraṇānāṃ ca kadācitkvāpi saṃbhavaḥ ।। ata eva purovartinyāloke smaraṇādinā । nimittena ghanenāstu saṃkrāntadayitākṛtiḥ ।। anyathā saṃvidārūḍhā kāntā vicchedayoginī ।
kasmādbhāti na vai saṃvid vicchedaṃ purato gatā ।। ata evāntaraṃ kiṃciddhīsaṃjñaṃ bhavatu sphuṭam । yatrāsya vicchidā bhānaṃ saṃkalpasvapnadarśane ।। ato nimittaṃ devasya śaktayaḥ santu tādṛśe ।
itthaṃ viśvamidaṃ nāthe bhairavīyacidambare । pratibimbamalaṃ svacche na khalvanyaprasādataḥ ।। ananyāpekṣitā yāsya viśvātmatvaṃ prati prabhoḥ । tāṃ parāṃ pratibhāṃ devīṃ saṃgirante hyanuttarām ।।
akulasyāsya devasya kulaprathanaśālinī । kaulikī sā parā śaktiraviyukto yayā prabhuḥ ।। tayoryadyāmalaṃ rūpaṃ sa saṃghaṭṭa iti smṛtaḥ । ānandaśaktiḥ saivoktā yato viśvaṃ visṛjyate ।।
parāparātparaṃ tattvaṃ saiṣā devī nigadyate । tatsāraṃ tacca hṛdayaṃ sa visargaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ ।। devīyāmalaśāstre sā kathitā kālakarṣiṇī । mahāḍāmarake yāge śrīparā mastake tathā ।।
śrīpūrvaśāstre sā mātṛsadbhāvatvena varṇitā । saṃghaṭṭe asmiṃścidātmatvādyattatpratyavamarśanam ।। icchāśaktiraghorāṇāṃ śaktīnāṃ sā parā prabhuḥ । saiva prakṣubdharūpā cedīśitrī saṃprajāyate ।।
tadā ghorāḥ parā devyo jātāḥ śaivādhvadaiśikāḥ । svātmapratyavamarśo yaḥ prāgabhūdekavīrakaḥ ।। jñātavyaviśvonmeṣātmā jñānaśaktitayā sthitaḥ । iyaṃ parāparā devī ghorāṃ yā mātṛmaṇḍalīm ।।
sṛjatyavirataṃ śuddhāśuddhamārgaikadīpikām । jñeyāṃśaḥ pronmiṣankṣobhaṃ yadaiti balavattvataḥ ।। ūnatābhāsanaṃ saṃvinmātratve jāyate tadā । rūḍhaṃ tajjñeyavargasya sthitiprārambha ucyate ।।
rūḍhireṣā vibodhābdheścitrākāraparigrahaḥ । idaṃ tadbījasaṃdarbhabījaṃ cinvanti yoginaḥ ।। icchāśaktirdvirūpoktā kṣubhitākṣubhitā ca yā । iṣyamāṇaṃ hi sā vastudvairūpyeṇātmani śrayet ।।
aciradyutibhāsinyā śaktyā jvalanarūpayā । iṣyamāṇasamāpattiḥ sthairyeṇātha dharātmanā ।। unmeṣaśaktāvastyetajjñeyaṃ yadyapi bhūyasā । tathāpi vibhavasthānaṃ sā na tu prācyajanmabhūḥ ।।
icchāśakterataḥ prāhuścātūrūpyaṃ parāmṛtam । kṣobhāntarasyāsadbhāvānnedaṃ bījaṃ ca kasyacit ।। prakṣobhakatvaṃ bījatvaṃ kṣobhādhāraśca yonitā । kṣobhakaṃ saṃvido rūpaṃ kṣubhyati kṣobhayatyapi ।।
kṣobhaḥ syājjñeyadharmatvaṃ kṣobhaṇā tadbahiṣkṛtiḥ । antaḥsthaviśvābhinnaikabījāṃśavisisṛkṣutā ।। kṣobho atadicche tattvecchābhāsanaṃ kṣobhaṇāṃ viduḥ । yadaikyāpattimāsādya tadicchā kṛtinī bhavet ।।
kṣobhādhāramimaṃ prāhuḥ śrīsomānandaputrakāḥ । saṃvidāmīṣaṇādīnāmanudbhinnaviśeṣakam ।। yajjñeyamātraṃ tadbījaṃ yadyogādbījatā svare । tasya bījasya saivoktā visisṛkṣā ya udbhavaḥ ।
yato grāhyamidaṃ bhāsyadbhinnakalpaṃ cidātmanaḥ ।। eṣa kṣobhaḥ kṣobhaṇā tu tūṣṇīṃbhūtānyamātṛgam । haṭhādyadaudāsīnyāṃśacyāvanaṃ saṃvido balāt ।। jātāpi visisṛkṣāsau yadvimarśāntaraikyataḥ ।
kṛtārthā jāyate kṣobhādhāro atraitatprakīrtitam ।। tatastadāntaraṃ jñeyaṃ bhinnakalpatvamicchati । viśvabījādataḥ sarva bāhyaṃ bimbaṃ vivartsyati ।। kṣobhyakṣobhakabhāvasya satattvaṃ darśitaṃ mayā ।
śrīmanmaheśvareṇoktaṃ guruṇā yatprasādataḥ ।। prakṛtaṃ brūmahe nedaṃ bījaṃ varṇacatuṣṭayam । nāpi yoniryato naitatkṣobhādhāratvamṛcchati ।। ātmanyeva ca viśrāntyā tatproktamamṛtātmakam ।
itthaṃ prāguditaṃ yattatpañcakaṃ tatparasparam ।। ucchaladvividhākāramanyonyavyatimiśraṇāt । yo anuttaraḥ paraḥ spando yaścānandaḥ samucchalan ।। tāvicchonmeṣasaṃghaṭṭādgacchato ativicitratām ।
anuttarānandacitī icchāśaktau niyojite ।। trikoṇamiti tatprāhurvisargāmodasundaram । anuttarānandaśaktī tatra rūḍhimupāgate ।। trikoṇadvitvayogena vrajataḥ ṣaḍarasthitim ।
ta evonmeṣayoge api punastanmayatāṃ gate ।। kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭaṃ rūpamabhivyaṅktaḥ parasparam । icchonmeṣagataḥ kṣobho yaḥ proktastadgaterapi ।। te eva śaktī tādrūpyabhāginyau nānyathāsthite ।
nanvanuttaratānandau svātmanā bhedavarjitau ।। kathametāvatīmenāṃ vaicitrīṃ svātmani śritau । śṛṇu tāvadayaṃ saṃvinnātho aparimitātmakaḥ ।। anantaśaktivaicitryalayodayakaleśvaraḥ ।
asthāsyadekarūpeṇa vapuṣā cenmaheśvaraḥ ।। maheśvaratvaṃ saṃvittvaṃ tadatyakṣyaddhaṭādivat । paricchinnaprakāśatvaṃ jaḍasya kila lakṣaṇam ।। jaḍādvilakṣaṇo bodho yato na parimīyate ।
tena bodhamahasindhorullāsinyaḥ svaśaktayaḥ ।। āśrayantyūrmaya iva svātmasaṃghaṭṭacitratām । svātmasaṃghaṭṭavaicitryaṃ śaktīnāṃ yatparasparam ।। etadeva paraṃ prāhuḥ kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭaṃ vapuḥ ।
asmiṃścaturdaśe dhāmni sphuṭībhūtatriśaktike ।। triśūlatvamataḥ prāha śāstā śrīpūrvaśāsane । nirañjanamidaṃ coktaṃ gurubhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।। śaktimānañjyate yasmānna śaktirjātu kenacit ।
icchā jñānaṃ kriyā ceti yatpṛthakpṛthagañjyate ।। tadeva śaktimatsvaiḥ svairiṣyamāṇādikaiḥ sphuṭam । etattritayamaikyena yadā tu prasphurettadā ।। na kenacidupādheyaṃ svasvavipratiṣedhataḥ ।
lolībhūtamataḥ śaktitritayaṃ tattriśūlakam । yasminnāśu samāveśādbhavedyogī nirañjanaḥ ।। itthaṃ parāmṛtapadādārabhyāṣṭakamīdṛśam । brāhmyādirūpasaṃbhedādyātyaṣṭāṣṭakatāṃ sphuṭam ।।
atrānuttaraśaktiḥ sā svaṃ vapuḥ prakaṭasthitam । kurvantyapi jñeyakalākāluṣyādvindurūpiṇī ।। uditāyāṃ kriyāśaktau somasūryāgnidhāmani । avibhāgaḥ prakāśo yaḥ sa binduḥ paramo hi naḥ ।।
tattvarakṣāvidhāne ca taduktaṃ parameśinā । hṛtpadmamaṇḍalāntaḥstho naraśaktiśivātmakaḥ ।। boddhavyo layabhedena vindurvimalatārakaḥ । yo asau nādātmakaḥ śabdaḥ sarvaprāṇiṣvavasthitaḥ ।।
adha ūrdhvavibhāgena niṣkriyeṇāvatiṣṭhate । hlādataikṣṇyādi vaicitryaṃ sitaraktādikaṃ ca yat ।। svayaṃ tannirapekṣo asau prakāśo gururāha ca । yanna sūryo na vā somo nāgnirbhāsayate api ca ।।
na cārkasomavahnīnāṃ tatprakāśādvinā mahaḥ । kimapyasti nijaṃ kiṃ tu saṃviditthaṃ prakāśate ।। svasvātantryaprabhāvodyadvicitropādhisaṃgataḥ । prakāśo yāti taikṣṇyādimavāntaravicitratām ।।
durdarśano api gharmāṃśuḥ patitaḥ pāthasāṃ pathi । netrānandatvamabhyeti paśyopādheḥ prabhāvitām ।। sūryādiṣu prakāśo asāvupādhikaluṣīkṛtaḥ । saṃvitprakāśaṃ māheśamata eva hyapekṣate ।।
prakāśamātraṃ suvyaktaṃ sūrya ityucyate sphuṭam । prakāśyavastusārāṃśavarṣi tatsoma ucyate ।। sūrya pramāṇamityāhuḥ somaṃ meyaṃ pracakṣate । anyonyamaviyuktau tau svatantrāvapyubhau sthitau ।।
bhoktṛbhogyobhayātmaitadanyonyonmukhatāṃ gatam । tato jvalanacidrūpaṃ citrabhānuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। yo ayaṃ vahneḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ pramāturidameva tat । saṃvideva tu vijñeyatādātmyādanapekṣiṇī ।।
svatantratvātpramātoktā vicitro jñeyabhedataḥ । somāṃśadāhyavastūtthavaicitryābhāsabṛṃhitaḥ ।। tata evāgniruditaścitrabhānurmaheśinā । jñeyādyupāyasaṃghātanirapekṣaiva saṃvidaḥ ।।
sthitirmātāhamasmīti jñātā śāstrajñavadyataḥ । ajña eva yato jñātānubhavātmā na rūpataḥ ।। na tu sā jñātṛtā yasyāṃ śuddhajñeyādyapekṣate । tasyāṃ daśāyāṃ jñātṛtvamucyate yogyatāvaśāt ।।
mānataiva tu sā prācyapramātṛparikalpitā । ucchalantyapi saṃvittiḥ kālakramavivarjanāt ।। uditaiva satī pūrṇā mātṛmeyādirūpiṇī । pākādistu kriyā kālaparicchedātkramocitā ।।
matāntyakṣaṇavandhyāpi na pākatvaṃ prapadyate । itthaṃ prakāśatattvasya somasūryāgnitā sthitā ।। api mukhyaṃ tatprakāśamātratvaṃ na vyapohyate । eṣāṃ yatprathamaṃ rūpaṃ hrasvaṃ tatsūrya ucyate ।।
kṣobhānandavaśāddīrghaviśrāntyā soma ucyate । yattatparaṃ plutaṃ nāma somānandātparaṃ sthitam ।। prakāśarūpaṃ tatprāhurāgneyaṃ śāstrakovidāḥ । atra prakāśamātraṃ yatsthite dhāmatraye sati ।।
uktaṃ vindutayā śāstre śivavindurasau mataḥ । makārādanya evāyaṃ tacchāyāmātradhṛdyathā ।। ralahāḥ ṣaṇṭhavaisargavarṇarūpatvasaṃsthitāḥ । ikāra eva rephāṃśacchāyayānyo yathā svaraḥ ।।
tathaiva mahaleśādaḥ so anyo dvedhāsvaro api san । asyāntarvisisṛkṣāsau yā proktā kaulikī parā ।। saiva kṣobhavaśādeti visargātmakatāṃ dhruvam । uktaṃ ca triśiraḥśāstre kalāvyāptyantacarcane ।।
kalā saptadaśī tasmādamṛtākārarūpiṇī । parāparasvasvarūpabindugatyā visarpitā ।। prakāśyaṃ sarvavastūnāṃ visargarahitā tu sā । śaktikuṇḍalikā caiva prāṇakuṇḍalikā tathā ।।
visargaprāntadeśe tu parā kuṇḍalinīti ca । śivavyometi paramaṃ brahmātmasthānamucyate ।। visargamātraṃ nāthasya sṛṣṭisaṃhāravibhramāḥ । svātmanaḥ svātmani svātmakṣepo vaisargikī sthitiḥ ।।
visarga evamutsṛṣṭa āśyānatvamupāgataḥ । haṃsaḥ prāṇo vyañjanaṃ ca sparśaśca paribhāṣyate ।। anuttaraṃ paraṃ dhāma tadevākulamucyate । visargastasya nāthasya kaulikī śaktirucyate ।।
visargatā ca saivāsyā yadānandodayakramāt । spaṣṭībhūtakriyāśaktiparyantā procchalatsthitiḥ ।। visarga eva tāvānyadākṣiptaitāvadātmakaḥ । iyadrūpaṃ sāgarasya yadanantormisaṃtatiḥ ।।
ata eva visargo ayamavyaktahakalātmakaḥ । kāmatattvamiti śrīmatkulaguhvara ucyate ।। yattadakṣaramavyakta kāntākaṇṭhe vyavasthitam । dhvanirūpamanicchaṃ tu dhyānadhāraṇavarjitam ।।
tatra cittaṃ samādhāya vaśayedyugapajjagat । ata eva visargasya haṃse yadvatsphuṭā sthitiḥ ।। tadvatsānuttarādīnāṃ kādisāntatayā sthitiḥ । anuttarātkavargasya sūtiḥ pañcātmanaḥ sphuṭam ।।
pañcaśaktyātmatovaśa ekaikatra yathā sphuṭaḥ । icchāśakteḥ svasvarūpasaṃsthāyā ekarūpataḥ ।। cavargaḥ pañcaśaktyātmā kramaprasphuṭatātmakaḥ । yā tūktā jñeyakāluṣyabhākkṣipracarayogataḥ ।।
dvirūpāyāstato jātaṃ ṭa-tādyaṃ vargayugmakam । unmeṣātpādivargastu yato viśvaṃ samāpyate ।। jñeyarūpamidaṃ pañcaviṃśatyantaṃ yataḥ sphuṭam । jñeyatvātsphuṭataḥ proktametāvatsparśarūpakam ।।
icchāśaktiśca yā dvedhā kṣubhitākṣubhitatvataḥ । sā vijātīyaśaktyaṃśapronmukhī yāti yātmatām ।। saiva śīghrataropāttajñeyakāluṣyarūṣitā । vijātīyonmukhatvena ratvaṃ latvaṃ ca gacchati ।।
tadvadunmeṣaśaktirdvirūpā vaijātyaśaktigā । vakāratvaṃ prapadyeta sṛṣṭisārapravarṣakam ।। icchaivānuttarānandayātā śīghratvayogataḥ । vāyurityucyate vahnirbhāsanātsthairyato dharā ।।
idaṃ catuṣkamantaḥsthamata eva nigadyate । icchādyantargatatvena svasamāptau ca saṃsthiteḥ ।। sajātīyakaśaktīnāmicchādyānāṃ ca yojanam । kṣobhātmakamidaṃ prāhuḥ kṣobhākṣobhātmanāmapi ।।
anuttarasya sājātye bhavettu dvitayī gatiḥ । anuttaraṃ yattatraikaṃ taccedānandasūtaye ।। prabhaviṣyati tadyoge yogaḥ kṣobhātmakaḥ sphuṭaḥ । atrāpyanuttaraṃ dhāma dvitīyamapi sūtaye ।।
na paryāptaṃ tadā kṣobhaṃ vinaivānuttarātmatā । icchā yā karmaṇā hīnā yā caiṣṭavyena rūṣitā ।। śīghrasthairyaprabhinnena tridhā bhāvamupāgatā । anunmiṣitamunmīlatpronmīlitamiti sthitam ।।
iṣyamāṇaṃ tridhaitasyāṃ tādrūpyasyāparicyuteḥ । tadeva svoṣmaṇā svātmasvātantryapreraṇātmanā ।। bahirbhāvya sphuṭaṃ kṣiptaṃ śa-ṣa-satritayaṃ sthitam । tata eva sakāre asminsphuṭaṃ viśvaṃ prakāśate ।।
amṛtaṃ ca paraṃ dhāma yoginastatpracakṣate । kṣobhādyantavirāmeṣu tadeva ca parāmṛtam ।। sītkārasukhasadbhāvasamāveśasamādhiṣu । tadeva brahma paramamavibhaktaṃ pracakṣate ।।
uvāca bhagavāneva tacchrīmatkulaguhkare । śaktiśaktimadaikātmyalabdhānvarthābhidhānake ।। kākacañcupuṭākāraṃ dhyānadhāraṇavarjitam । viṣatattvamanackākhyaṃ tava snehātprakāśitam ।।
kāmasya pūrṇatā tattvaṃ saṃghaṭṭe pravibhāvyate । viṣasya cāmṛtaṃ tattvaṃ chādyatve aṇoścyute sati ।। vyāptrī śaktirviṣaṃ yasmādavyāptuśchādayenmahaḥ । nirañjanaṃ paraṃ dhāma tattvaṃ tasya tu sāñjanam ।।
kriyāśaktyātmakaṃ viśvamayaṃ tasmātsphuredyataḥ । icchā kāmo viṣaṃ jñānaṃ kriyā devī nirañjanam ।। etattrayasamāveśaḥ śivo bhairava ucyate । atra rūḍhiṃ sadā kuryāditi no guravo jaguḥ ।।
viṣatattve saṃpraviśya na bhūtaṃ na viṣaṃ na ca । grahaḥ kevala evāhamiti bhāvanayā sphuret ।। nanvatra ṣaṇṭhavarṇebhyo janmoktaṃ tena ṣaṇṭhatā । kathaṃ syāditi cedbrūmo nātra ṣaṇṭhasya sotṛtā ।।
tathāhi tatragā yāsāvicchāśaktirudīritā । saiva sūte svakartavyamantaḥsthaṃ sveṣṭarūpakam ।। yattvatra rūṣaṇāhetureṣitavyaṃ sthitaṃ tataḥ । bhāgānna prasavastajjaṃ kāluṣyaṃ tadvapuśca tat ।।
jñeyārūṣaṇayā yuktaṃ samudāyātmakaṃ viduḥ । ṣaṇṭhaṃ kṣobhakatākṣobhadhāmatvābhāvayogataḥ ।। etadvarṇacatuṣkasya svoṣmaṇābhāsanāvaśāt । ūṣmeti kathitaṃ nāma bhairaveṇāmalātmanā ।।
kādi-hāntamidaṃ prahuḥ kṣobhādhāratayā budhāḥ । yonirūpeṇa tasyāpi yoge kṣobhāntaraṃ vrajet ।। tannidarśanayogena pañcāśattamavarṇatā । pañcaviṃśakasaṃjñeyaprāgvadbhūmisusaṃsthitam ।।
catuṣkaṃ ca catuṣkaṃ ca bhedābhedagataṃ kramāt । ādyaṃ catuṣkaṃ saṃvitterbhedasaṃdhānakovidam ।। bhedasyābhedarūḍhyekaheturanyaccatuṣṭayam । itthaṃ yadvarṇajātaṃ tatsarva svaramayaṃ purā ।।
vyaktiyogādvyañjanaṃ tatsvaraprāṇaṃ yataḥ kila । svarāṇāṃ ṣaṭkameveha mūlaṃ syādvarṇasaṃtatau ।। ṣaḍdevatāstu tā eva ye mukhyāḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ । saurāṇāmeva raśmīnāmantaścāndrakalā yataḥ ।।
ato atra dīrghatritayaṃ sphuṭaṃ cāndramasaṃ vapuḥ । candraśca nāma naivānyo bhogyaṃ bhoktuśca nāparam ।। bhoktaiva bhogyabhāvena dvaividhyātsaṃvyavasthitaḥ । ghaṭasya na hi bhogyatvaṃ svaṃ vapurmātṛgaṃ hi tat ।।
ato mātari yā rūḍhiḥ sāsya bhogyatvamucyate । anuttaraṃ parāmṛśyaparāmarśakabhāvataḥ ।। saṃghaṭṭarūpatāṃ prāptaṃ bhogyamicchādikaṃ tathā । anuttarānandabhuvāmicchādye bhogyatāṃ gate ।।
saṃdhyakṣarāṇāmudayo bhoktṛrūpaṃ ca kathyate । anuttarānandamayo devo bhoktaiva kathyate ।। icchādikaṃ bhogyameva tata evāsya śaktitā । bhogyaṃ bhoktari līnaṃ ced bhoktā tadvastutaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।।
ataḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ trikaṃ sāraṃ cidiṣyunmeṣaṇātmakam । tadeva tritayaṃ prāhurbhairavasya paraṃ mahaḥ ।। tattrikaṃ parameśasya pūrṇā śaktiḥ pragīyate । tenākṣiptaṃ yato viśvamato asminsamupāsite ।।
viśvaśaktāvavacchedavandhye jātamupāsanam । ityeṣa mahimaitāvāniti tāvanna śakyate ।। aparicchinnaśakteḥ kaḥ kuryācchaktiparicchidām । tasmādanuttaro devaḥ svācchandyānuttaratvataḥ ।।
visargaśaktiyuktatvātsaṃpanno viśvarūpakaḥ । evaṃ pañcāśadāmarśapūrṇaśaktirmaheśvaraḥ ।। vimarśātmaika evānyāḥ śaktayo atraiva niṣṭhitāḥ । ekāśītipadā devī hyatrāntarbhāvayiṣyate ।।
ekāmarśasvabhāvatve śabdarāśiḥ sa bhairavaḥ । āmṛśyacchāyayā yogātsaiva śaktiśca mātṛkā ।। sā śabdarāśisaṃghaṭṭādbhinnayonistu mālinī । prāgvannavatayāmarśātpṛthagvargasvarūpiṇī ।।
ekaikāmarśarūḍhau tu saiva pañcāśadātmikā । itthaṃ nādānuvedhena parāmarśasvabhāvakaḥ ।। śivo mātāpitṛtvena kartā viśvatra saṃsthitaḥ । visarga eva śākto ayaṃ śivabindutayā punaḥ ।।
garbhīkṛtānantaviśvaḥ śrayate anuttarātmatām । aparicchinnaviśvāntaḥsāre svātmani yaḥ prabhoḥ ।। parāmarśaḥ sa evokto dvayasaṃpattilakṣaṇaḥ । anuttaravisargātmaśivaśaktyadvayātmani ।।
parāmarśo nirbharatvādahamityucyate vibhoḥ । anuttarādyā prasṛtirhāntā śaktisvarūpiṇī ।। pratyāhṛtāśeṣaviśvānuttare sā nilīyate । tadidaṃ viśvamantaḥsthaṃ śaktau sānuttare pare ।।
tattasyāmiti yatsatyaṃ vibhunā saṃpuṭīkṛtiḥ । tena śrītrīśikāśāstre śakteḥ saṃpuṭitākṛtiḥ ।। saṃvittau bhāti yadviśvaṃ tatrāpi khalu saṃvidā । tadetattritayaṃ dvandvayogātsaṃghātatāṃ gatam ।।
ekameva paraṃ rūpaṃ bhairavasyāhamātmakam । visargaśaktiryā śaṃbhoḥ setthaṃ sarvatra vartate ।। tata evasamasto ayamānandarasavibhramaḥ । tathāhi madhure gīte sparśe vā candanādike ।।
mādhyasthyavigame yāsau hṛdaye spandamānatā । ānandaśaktiḥ saivoktā yataḥ sahṛdayo janaḥ ।। pūrva visṛjyasakalaṃ kartavyaṃ śūnyatānale । cittaviśrāntisaṃjño ayamāṇavastadanantaram ।।
dṛṣṭaśrutāditadvastupronmukhatvaṃ svasaṃvidi । cittasaṃbodhanāmoktaḥ śāktollāsabharātmakaḥ ।। tatronmukhatvatadvastusaṃghaṭṭādvastuno hṛdi । rūḍheḥ pūrṇatayāveśānmitacittalayācchive ।।
prāgvadbhaviṣyadaunmukhyasaṃbhāvyamitatālayāt । cittapralayanāmāsau visargaḥ śāmbhavaḥ paraḥ ।। tattvarakṣāvidhāne ato visargatraidhamucyate । hṛtpadmakośamadhyasthastayoḥ saṃghaṭṭa iṣyate ।।
visargo antaḥ sa ca proktaścittaviśrāntilakṣaṇaḥ । dvitīyaḥ sa visargastu cittasaṃbodhalakṣaṇaḥ ।। ekībhūtaṃ vibhātyatra jagadetaccarācaram । grāhyagrāhakabhedo vai kiṃcidatreṣyate yadā ।।
tadāsau sakalaḥ prokto niṣkalaḥ śivayogataḥ । grāhyagrāhakavicchittisaṃpūrṇagrahaṇātmakaḥ ।। tṛtīyaḥ sa visargastu cittapralayalakṣaṇaḥ । ekībhāvātmakaḥ sūkṣmo vijñānātmātmanirvṛtaḥ ।।
nirūpito ayamarthaḥ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate । sātra kuṇḍalinī bījaṃ jīvabhūtā cidātmikā ।। tajjaṃ dhruvecchonmeṣākhyaṃ trikaṃ varṇāstataḥ punaḥ । ā ityavarṇādityādiyāvadvaisargikī kalā ।।
kakārādisakārāntā visargātpañcadhā sa ca । bahiścāntaśca hṛdaye nāde atha parame pade ।। bindurātmani mūrdhāntaṃ hṛdayādvyāpako hi saḥ । ādimāntyavihīnāstu mantrāḥ syuḥ śaradabhravat ।।
gurorlakṣaṇametāvadādimāntyaṃ ca vedayet । pūjyaḥ so ahamiva jñānī bhairavo devatātmakaḥ ।। ślokagāthādi yatkiṃcidādimāntyayutaṃ tataḥ । tasmādvidaṃstathā sarvaṃ mantratvenaiva paśyati ।।
visargaśaktirviśvasya kāraṇaṃ ca nirūpitā । aitareyākhyavedānte parameśena vistarāt ।। yallohitaṃ tadagniryadvīryaṃ sūryenduvigraham । a iti brahma paramaṃ tatsaṃghaṭṭodayātmakam ।।
tasyāpi ca paraṃ vīrya pañcabhūtakalātmakam । bhogyatvenānnarūpaṃ ca śabdasparśarasātmakam ।। śabdo api madhuro yasmādvīryopacayakārakaḥ । taddhi vīryaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ visisṛkṣātmakaṃ matam ।।
tadbalaṃ ca tadojaśca te prāṇāḥ sā ca kāntatā । tasmādvīryātprajāstāśca vīrya karmasu kathyate ।। yajñādikeṣu tadvṛṣṭau sauṣadhīṣvatha tāḥ punaḥ । vīrye tacca prajāsvevaṃ visarge viśvarūpatā ।।
śabdarāśiḥ sa evokto mātṛkā sāca kīrtitā । kṣobhyakṣobhakatāveśānmālinīṃ tāṃ pracakṣate ।। bījayonisamāpattivisargodayasundarā । mālinī hi parā śaktirnirṇītā viśvarūpiṇī ।।
eṣā vastuta ekaiva parā kālasya karṣiṇī । śaktimadbhedayogena yāmalatvaṃ prapadyate ।। tasya pratyavamarśo yaḥ paripūrṇo ahamātmakaḥ । sa svātmani svatantratvādvibhāgamavabhāsayet ।।
vibhāgābhāsane cāsya tridhā vapurudāhṛtam । paśyantī madhyamā sthūlā vaikharītyabhiśabditam ।। tāsāmapi tridhā rūpaṃ sthūlasūkṣmaparatvataḥ । tatra yā svarasandarbhasubhagā nādarūpiṇī ।।
sā sthūlā khalu paśyantī varṇādyapravibhāgataḥ । avibhāgaikarūpatvaṃ mādhuryaṃ śaktirucyate ।। sthānavāyvādigharṣotthā sphuṭataiva ca pāruṣī । tadasyāṃ nādarūpāyāṃ saṃvitsavidhavṛttitaḥ ।।
sājātyāntarma[ttama] yībhūtirjhagityevopalabhyate । yeṣāṃ na tanmayībhūtiste dehādinimajjanam ।। avidanto magnasaṃvinmānāstvahṛdayā iti । yattucarmāvanaddhādi kiṃcittatraiṣa yo dhvaniḥ ।।
sa sphuṭāsphuṭarūpatvānmadhyamā sthūlarūpiṇī । madhyāyāścāvibhāgāṃśasadbhāva iti raktatā ।। avibhāgasvaramayī yatra syāttatsurañjakam । avibhāgo hi nirvṛtyai dṛśyatāṃ tālapāṭhataḥ ।।
kilāvyaktadhvanau tasminvādane parituṣyati । yā tu sphuṭānāṃ varṇānāmutpattau kāraṇaṃ bhavet ।। sā sthūlā vaikharī yasyāḥ kāryaṃ vākyādi bhūyasā । asminsthūlatraye yattadanusandhānamādivat ।।
pṛthakpṛthaktattritayaṃ sūkṣmamityabhiśabdyate । ṣaḍjaṃ karomi madhuraṃ vādayāmi bruve vacaḥ ।। pṛthagevānusandhānatrayaṃ saṃvedyate kila । etasyāpi trayasyādyaṃ yadrupamanupādhimat ।।
tatparaṃ tritayaṃ tatra śivaḥ paracidātmakaḥ । vibhāgābhāsanāyāṃ ca mukhyāstisro atra śaktayaḥ ।। anuttarā parecchā ca parāparatayā sthitā । unmeṣaśaktirjñānākhyā tvapareti nigadyate ।।
kṣobharūpātpunastāsāmuktāḥ ṣaṭ saṃvido amalāḥ । āsāmeva samāveśātkriyāśaktitayoditāt ।। saṃvido dvādaśa proktā yāsu sarvaṃ samāpyate । etāvaddevadevasya mukhyaṃ tacchakticakrakam ।।
etāvatā devadevaḥ pūrṇaśaktiḥ sa bhairavaḥ । parāmarśātmakatvena visargākṣepayogataḥ ।। iyattākalanājjñānāttāḥ proktāḥ kālikāḥ kvacit । śrīsāraśāstre cāpyuktaṃ madhya ekākṣarāṃ parām ।।
pūjayedbhairavātmākhyāṃ yoginīdvādaśāvṛtām । tābhya eva catuḥṣaṣṭiparyantaṃ śakticakrakam ।। ekārataḥ samārabhya sahasrāraṃ pravartate । tāsāṃ ca kṛtyabhedena nāmāni bahudhāgame ।।
upāsāśca dvayādvaitavyāmiśrākārayogataḥ । śrīmattraiśirame tacca kathitaṃ vistarādbahu ।। iha no likhitaṃ vyāsabhayāccānupayogataḥ । tā eva nirmalāḥ śuddhā aghorāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
ghoraghoratarāṇāṃ tu sotṛtvācca tadātmikāḥ । sṛṣṭau sthitau ca saṃhāre tadupādhitrayātyaye ।। tāsāmeva sthitaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā pravibhajyate । upādhyatītaṃ yadrūpaṃ taddvidhā guravo jaguḥ ।।
anullāsādupādhīnāṃ yadvā praśamayogataḥ । praśamaśca dvidhā śāntyā haṭhapākakrameṇa tu ।। alaṃ grāsarasākhyena satataṃ jvalanātmanā । haṭhapākapraśamanaṃ yattṛtīyaṃ tadeva ca ।
upadeśāya yujyeta bhedendhanavidāhakam ।। nijabodhajaṭharahutabhuji bhāvāḥ sarve samarpitā haṭhataḥ । vijahati bhedavibhāgaṃ nijaśaktyā taṃ samindhānāḥ ।। haṭhapākena bhāvānāṃ rūpe bhinne vilāpite ।
aśnantyamṛtasādbhūtaṃ viśvaṃ saṃvittidevatāḥ ।। tāstṛptāḥ svātmanaḥ pūrṇa hṛdayaikāntaśāyinam । cidvyomabhairavaṃ devamabhedenādhiśerate ।। evaṃ kṛtyakriyāveśānnāmopāsābahutvataḥ ।
āsāṃ bahuvidhaṃ rūpamabhede apyavabhāsate ।। āsāmeva ca devīnāmāvāpodvāpayogataḥ । ekadvitricatuṣpañcaṣaṭsaptāṣṭanavottaraiḥ ।। rudrārkānyakalāsenāprabhṛtirbhedavistaraḥ ।
alamanyena bahunā prakṛte atha niyujyate ।। saṃvidātmani viśvo ayaṃ bhāvavargaḥ prapañcavān । pratibimbatayā bhāti yasya viśveśvaro hi saḥ ।। evamātmani yasyedṛgavikalpaḥ sadodayaḥ ।
parāmarśaḥ sa evāsau śāṃbhavopāyamudritaḥ ।। pūrṇāhantāparāmarśo yo asyāyaṃ pravivecitaḥ । mantramudrākriyopāsāstadanyā nātra kāścana ।। bhūyobhūyaḥ samāveśaṃ nirvikalpamimaṃ śritaḥ ।
abhyeti bhairavībhāvaṃ jīvanmuktyaparābhidham ।। ita eva prabhṛtyeṣā jīvanmuktirvicāryate । yatra sūtraṇayāpīyamupāyopeyakalpanā ।। prāktane tvāhnike kācidbhedasya kalanāpi no ।
tenānupāye tasminko mucyate vā kathaṃ kutaḥ ।। nirvikalpe parāmarśe śāmbhavopāyanāmani । pañcāśadbhedatāṃ pūrvasūtritāṃ yojayedbudhaḥ ।। dharāmevāvikalpena svātmani pratibimbitām ।
paśyanbhairavatāṃ yāti jalādiṣvapyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। yāvadante paraṃ tattvaṃ samastāvaraṇordhvagam । vyāpi svatantraṃ sarvajñaṃ yacchivaṃ parikalpitam ।। tadapyakalpitodārasaṃviddarpaṇabimbitam ।
paśyanvikalpavikalo bhairavībhavati svayam ।। yathā raktaṃ puraḥ paśyannirvikalpakasaṃvidā । tattaddvāraniraṃśaikaghaṭasaṃvittisusthitaḥ ।। tadvaddharādikaikaikasaṃghātasamudāyataḥ ।
parāmṛśansvamātmānaṃ pūrṇa evāvabhāsate ।। matta evoditamidaṃ mayyeva pratibimbitam । madabhinnamidaṃ ceti tridhopāyaḥ sa śāmbhavaḥ ।। sṛṣṭeḥ sthiteḥ saṃhṛteśca tadetatsūtraṇaṃ kṛtam ।
yatra sthitaṃ yataśceti tadāha spandaśāsane ।। etāvataiva hyaiśvarya saṃvidaḥ khyāpitaṃ param । viśvātmakatvaṃ cetyanyallakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ nu kathyatām ।। svātmanyeva cidākāśe viśvamasmyavabhāsayan ।
sraṣṭā viśvātmaka iti prathayā bhairavātmatā ।। ṣaḍadhvajātaṃ nikhilaṃ mayyeva pratibimbitam । sthitikartāhamasmīti sphuṭeyaṃ viśvarūpatā ।। sadoditamahābodhajvālājaṭilatātmani ।
viśvaṃ dravati mayyetaditi paśyanpraśāmyati ।। anantacitrasadgarbhasaṃsārasvapnasadmanaḥ । ploṣakaḥ śiva evāhamityullāsī hutāśanaḥ ।। jagatsarvaṃ mattaḥ prabhavati vibhedena bahudhā tathāpyetadrūḍhaṃ mayi vigalite tvatra na paraḥ ।
taditthaṃ yaḥ sṛṣṭisthitivilayabhekīkṛtivaśādanaṃśaṃ paśyetsa sphurati hi turīyaṃ padabhitaḥ ।। tadasminparamopāye śāmbhavādvaitaśālini । ke apyeva yānti viśvāsaṃ pasmeśena bhāvitāḥ ।। snānaṃ vrataṃ dehaśuddhirdhāraṇā mantrayojanā ।
adhvaklṛptiryāgavidhirhomajapyasamādhayaḥ ।। ityādikalpanā kāpi nātra bhedena yujyate । parānugrahakāritvamatrasthasya sphuṭaṃ sthitam ।। yadi tādṛganugrāhyo daiśikasyopasarpati ।
athāsau tādṛśo na syādbhavabhaktyā ca bhāvitaḥ ।। taṃ cārādhayate bhāvitādṛśānugraheritaḥ । tadā vicitraṃ dīkṣādividhiṃ śikṣeta koviṃdaḥ ।। bhāvinyo api hyupāsāstā straivāyānti niṣṭhitim ।
etanmayatvaṃ paramaṃ prāpyaṃ nirvarṇyateśivam ।। iti kathitamidaṃ suvistaraṃ paramaṃ śāmbhavamātmavedanam ।। atha śāktamupāyamaṇḍalaṃ kathayāmaḥ paramātmasaṃvide ।। anantarāhnikokte asminsvabhāve pārameśvare ।
pravivikṣurvikalpasya kuryātsaṃskāramañjasā ।। vikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sūte vikalpaṃ svātmasaṃskṛtam । svatulyaṃ so api so apyanyaṃ so apyanyaṃ sadṛśātmakam ।। caturṣveva vikalpeṣu yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kramādasau ।
asphuṭaḥ sphuṭatābhāvī prasphuṭansphuṭitātmakaḥ ।। tataḥ sphuṭataro yāvadante sphuṭatamo bhavet । asphuṭādau vikalpe ca bhedo apyastyāntarālikaḥ ।। tataḥ sphuṭatamodāratādrūpyaparivṛṃhitā ।
saṃvidabhyeti vimalāmavikalpasvarūpatām ।। ataśca bhairavīyaṃ yattejaḥ saṃvitsvabhāvakam । bhūyo bhūyo vimṛśatāṃ jāyate tatsphuṭātmatā ।। nanu saṃvitparāmraṣṭrī parāmarśamayī svataḥ ।
parāmṛśyā kathaṃ tāthārūpyasṛṣṭau tu sā jaḍā ।। ucyate svātmasaṃvittiḥ svabhāvādeva nirbharā । nāsyāmapāsyaṃ nādheyaṃ kiṃcidityuditaṃ purā ।। kiṃ tu durghaṭakāritvātsvācchandyānnirmalādasau ।
svātmapracchādanakrīḍāpaṇḍitaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। anāvṛtte svarūpe api yadātmācchādanaṃ vibhoḥ । saiva māyā yato bheda etāvānviśvavṛttikaḥ ।। tathābhāsanamevāsya dvaitamuktaṃ maheśituḥ ।
taddvayāpāsanenāyaṃ parāmarśo abhidhīyate ।। durbhedapādapasyāsya mūlaṃ kṛntanti kovidāḥ । dhārārūḍhena sattarkakuṭhāreṇeti niścayaḥ ।। tāmenāṃ bhāvanāmāhuḥ sarvakāmadughāṃ budhāḥ ।
sphuṭayedvastu yāpetaṃ manosthapadādapi ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre tatproktaṃ tarko yogāṅgamuttamam । heyādyālocanāttasmāttatra yatnaḥ praśasyate ।। mārge cetaḥ sthirībhūtaṃ heye api viṣayecchayā ।
prerya tena nayettāvadyāvatpadamanāmayam ।। mārgo atra mokṣopāyaḥ sa heyaḥ śāstrāntaroditaḥ । viṣiṇoti nibadhnāti yecchā niyatisaṃgatam ।। rāgatattvaṃ tayoktaṃ yat tena tatrānurajyate ।
yathā sāmrājyasaṃbhogaṃ dṛṣṭvādṛṣṭvāthabādhame ।। bhoge rajyeta durbuddhistadvanmokṣe api rāgataḥ । sa evāṃśaka ityuktaḥ svabhāvākhyaḥ sa tu sphuṭam ।। siddhyaṅgamiti mokṣāya pratyūha iti kovidāḥ ।
śivaśāsanamāhātmyaṃ vidannapyata eva hi ।। vaiṣṇavādhyeṣu rajyeta mūḍho rāgeṇa rañjitaḥ । yatastāvati sā tasya vāmākhyā śaktiraiśvarī ।। pāñcarātrikavairiñcasaugatādervijṛmbhate ।
dṛṣṭāḥ sāmrājyasaṃbhogaṃ nindantaḥ ke api vāliśāḥ ।। na tu saṃtoṣataḥ sveṣu bhogeṣvāśīḥpravartanāt । evaṃcidbhairavāveśanindātatparamānasāḥ ।। bhavantyatisughorābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ pātitā yataḥ ।
tena śāṃbhavamāhātmyaṃ jānanyaḥ śāsanāntare ।। āśvasto nottarītavyaṃ tena bhedamahārṇavāt । śrīkāmikāyāṃ proktaṃ ca pāśaprakaraṇe sphuṭam ।। vedasāṃkhyapurāṇajñāḥ pāñcarātraparāyaṇāḥ ।
ye kecidṛṣayo dhīrāḥ śāstrāntaraparāyaṇāḥ ।। bauddhārhatādyāḥ sarve te vidyārāgeṇa rañjitāḥ । māyāpāśena baddhatvācchivadīkṣāṃ na vindate ।। rāgaśabdena ca proktaṃ rāgatattvaṃ niyāmakam ।
māyīye tacca taṃ tasmiñchāstre niyamayediti ।। mokṣo api vaiṣṇavāderyaḥ svasaṃkalpena bhāvitaḥ । paraprakṛtisāyujyaṃ yadvāpyānandarūpatā ।। viśuddhacittamātraṃ vā dīpavatsaṃtatikṣayaḥ ।
sa savedyāpavedyātmapralayākalatāmayaḥ ।। taṃ prāpyāpi ciraṃ kālaṃ tadgogābhogabhuktataḥ । tattattvapralayānte tu tadūrdhvāṃ sṛṣṭimāgataḥ ।। mantratvameti saṃbodhādananteśena kalpitāt ।
etaccāgre taniṣyāma ityāstāṃ tāvadatra tat ।। tenājñajanatāklṛptapravādairyo viḍambitaḥ । asadgurau rūḍhacitsa māyāpāśena rañjitaḥ ।। so api sattarkayogena nīyate sadguruṃ prati ।
sattarkaḥ śuddhavidyaiva sā cecchā parameśituḥ ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ sa yiyāsuḥ śivecchayā । bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati ।। śaktipātastu tatraiṣa kramikaḥ saṃpravartate ।
sthitvā yo asadgurau śāstrāntare vā satpathaṃ śritaḥ ।। guruśāstragate sattve asattve cātra vibhedakam । śaktipātasya vaicitryaṃ purastātpravivicyate ।। uktaṃ svacchandaśāstre tat vaiṣṇavādyānpravādinaḥ ।
sarvānbhramayate māyā sāmokṣe mokṣalipsayā ।। yastu rūḍho api tatrodyatparāmarśaviśāradaḥ । sa śuddhavidyāmāhātmyācchaktipātapavitritaḥ ।। ārohatyeva sanmārgaṃ pratyūhaparivarjitaḥ ।
sa tāvatkasyacittarkaḥ svata eva pravartate ।। sa ca sāṃsiddhikaḥ śāstre proktaḥ svapratyayātmakaḥ । kiraṇāyāṃ yadapyuktaṃ gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ ।। tatrottarottaraṃ mukhyaṃ pūrvapūrva upāyakaḥ ।
yasya svato ayaṃ sattarkaḥ sarvatraivādhikāravān ।। abhiṣiktaḥ svasaṃvittidevībhirdīkṣitaśca saḥ । sa eva sarvācāryāṇāṃ madhye mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। tatsaṃnidhāne nānyeṣu kalpiteṣvadhikāritā ।
sa samastaṃ ca śāstrārthaṃ sattarkādeva manyate ।। śuddhavidyā hi tannāsti satyaṃ yadyanna bhāsayet । sarvaśāstrārthavettṛtvamakasmāccāsya jāyate ।। iti śrīpūvavākye tad akasmāditi-śabdataḥ ।
lokāprasiddho yo hetuḥ so akasmāditi kathyate ।। sa caiṣa parameśānaśuddhavidyāvijṛmbhatam । asya bhodāśca bahavo nirbhittiḥ sahabhittikaḥ ।। sarvago aṃśagataḥ so api mukhyāmukhyāṃśaniṣṭhitaḥ ।
bhittiḥ paropajīvitvaṃ parā prajñātha tatkṛtiḥ ।। adṛṣṭamaṇḍalo apyevaṃ yaḥ kaścidvetti tattvataḥ । sa siddhibhāgbhavennityaṃ sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ ।। evaṃ yo vetti tattvena tasya nirvāṇagāminī ।
dīkṣā bhavediti proktaṃ tacchrītriṃśakaśāsane ।। akalpito gururjñayaḥ sāṃsiddhika iti smṛtaḥ । yastu tadrūpabhāgātmabhāvanātaḥ paraṃ vinā ।। śāstravitsa guruḥ śāstre prokto akalpitakalpakaḥ ।
tasyāpi bhedā utkṛṣṭamadhyamandādyupāyataḥ ।। bhāvanāto atha vā dhyānājjapātsvapnādvratāddhuteḥ । prāpnotyakalpitodāramabhiṣekaṃ mahāmatiḥ ।। śrīmadvājasanīye śrīvīre śrībrahmayāmale ।
śrīsiddhāyāmidaṃ dhātrā proktamanyatra ca sphuṭam ।। tasya svecchāpravṛttatvātkāraṇānantateṣyate । kadācidbhaktiyogena karmaṇā vidyayāpi vā ।। jñānadharmopadeśena mantrairvā dīkṣayāpi vā ।
evamādyairanekaiśca prakāraiḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। saṃsāriṇo anugṛhṇāti viśvasya jagataḥ patiḥ । mātṛmaṇḍalasaṃbodhātsaṃskārāttapasaḥ priye ।। dhyānādyogājjapājjñānānmantrārādhanāto vratāt ।
saṃprāpyaṃ kulasāmānyaṃ jñānaṃ kaulikasiddhidam ।। tattvajñānātmakaṃ sādhyaṃ yatra yatraiva dṛśyate । sa eva hi gurustatra hetujālaṃ prakalpyatām ।। tattvajñānādṛte nānyallakṣaṇaṃ brahmayāmale ।
tatraiva coktaṃ sevāyāṃ kṛtāyāmavikalpataḥ ।। sādhakasya na cetsiddhiḥ kiṃ kāryamiti codite । ātmīyamasya saṃjñānakrameṇa svātmadīkṣaṇam ।। sasphuratvaprasiddhyarthaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ prasiddhyati ।
anena svātmavijñānaṃ sasphuratvaprasādhakam ।। uktaṃ mukhyatayācāryo bhavedyadi na sasphuraḥ । tatraiva ca punaḥ śrīmadraktārādhanakarmaṇi ।। vidhiṃ proktaṃ sadā kurvanmāsenācārya ucyate ।
pakṣeṇa sādhako ardhārdhātputrakaḥ samayī tathā ।। dīkṣayejjapayogena raktādevī kramādyataḥ । guroralābhe proktasya vidhimetaṃ samācaret ।। mate ca pustakādvidyādhyayane doṣa īdṛśaḥ ।
ukto yastena taddoṣābhāve asau na niṣiddhatā ।। mantradravyādiguptatve phalaṃ kimiti codite । pustakādhītavidyā ye dīkṣāsamayavarjitāḥ ।। tāmasāḥ parahiṃsādi vaśyādi ca carantyalam ।
na ca tattvaṃ vidustena doṣabhāja iti sphuṭam ।। pūrvaṃ padayugaṃ vācyamanyonyaṃ hetuhetumat । yastu śāstraṃ vinā naiti śuddhavidyākhyasaṃvidam ।। guroḥ sa śāstramanvicchustaduktaṃ kramamācaret ।
yena kenāpyupāyena gurumārādhya bhaktitaḥ ।। taddīkṣākramayogena śāstrārthaṃ vettyasau tataḥ । abhiṣekaṃ samāsādya yo bhavetsa tu kalpitaḥ ।। sannapyaśeṣapāśaughavinivartanakovidaḥ ।
yo yathākramayogena kasmiṃścicchāstravastuni ।। ākasmikaṃ brajedbodhaṃ kalpitākalpito hi saḥ । tasya yo akalpito bhāgaḥ sa tu śreṣṭhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। utkarṣaḥ śuddhavidyāṃśatāratamyakṛto yataḥ ।
yathā bhedenādisiddhācchivānmuktaśivā hyadhaḥ ।। tathā sāṃsiddhikajñānādāhṛtajñānino adhamāḥ । tatsaṃnidhau nādhikārasteṣāṃ muktaśivātmavat ।। kiṃ tu tūṣṇīṃ-sthitiryadvā kṛtyaṃ tadanuvartanam ।
yastvakalpitarūpo api saṃvādadṛḍhatākṛte ।। anyato labdhasaṃskāraḥ sa sākṣādbhairavo guruḥ । yataḥ śāstrakramāttajjñaguruprajñānuśīlanāt ।। ātmapratyayitaṃ jñānaṃ pūrṇatvādbhairavāyate ।
tena śrīkiraṇoktaṃ yadgurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ ।। tripratyayamidaṃ jñānamiti yacca niśāṭane । tatsaṃghātaviparyāsavigrahairbhāsate tathā ।। karaṇasya vicitratvādvicitrāmeva tāṃ chidam ।
kartuṃ vāsīṃ ca ṭaṅkaṃ ca krakacaṃ cāpi gṛhṇate ।। tāvacca chedanaṃ hyekaṃ tathaivādyābhisaṃdhitaḥ । itthameva mitau vācyaṃ karaṇasya svakaṃ vapuḥ ।। na svatantraṃ svato mānaṃ kuryādadhigamaṃ haṭhāt ।
pramātrāśvāsaparyanto yato adhigama ucyate ।। āśvāsaśca vicitro asau śaktipātavaśāttathā । pramite api pramāṇānāmavakāśo astyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā samāśliṣya ciraṃ saṃcarvya cetasā ।
priyā yaiḥ parituṣyeta kiṃ brūmaḥ kila tānprati ।। itthaṃ ca mānasaṃplutyāmapi nādhigate gatiḥ । na vyarthatā nānavasthā nānyonyāśrayatāpi ca ।। evaṃ yogāṅgamiyati tarka eva na cāparam ।
antarantaḥ parāmarśapāṭavātiśayāya saḥ ।। ahiṃsā satyamasteyabrahmacaryāparigrahāḥ । iti pañca yamāḥ sākṣātsaṃvittau nopayoginaḥ ।। tapaḥprabhṛtayo ye ca niyamā yattathāsanam ।
prāṇāyāmāśca ye sarvametadbāhyavijṛmbhitam ।। śrīmadvīrāvalau coktaṃ bodhamātre śivātmake । cittapralayabandhena pralīne śaśibhāskare ।। prāpte ca dvādaśe bhāge jīvāditye svabodhake ।
mokṣaḥ sa eva kathitaḥ prāṇāyāmo nirarthakaḥ ।। prāṇāyāmo na kartavyaḥ śarīraṃ yena pīḍyate । rahasyaṃ vetti yo yatra sa muktaḥ sa ca mocakaḥ ।। pratyāhāraśca nāmāyamarthebhyo akṣadhiyāṃ hi yaḥ ।
anibaddhasya bandhasya tadantaḥ kila kīlanam ।। cittasya viṣaye kvāpi bandhanaṃ dhāraṇātmakam । tatsadṛgjñānasaṃtāno dhyānamastamitā param ।। yadā tu jñeyatādātmyameva saṃvidi jāyate ।
grāhyagrahaṇatādvaitaśūnyateyaṃ samāhitiḥ ।। tadeṣā dhāraṇādhyānasamādhitritayī parām । saṃvidaṃ prati no kaṃcidupayogaṃ samaśnute ।। yogāṅgatā yamādestu samādhyantasya varṇyate ।
svapūrvapūrvopāyatvādantyatarkopayogataḥ ।। antaḥ saṃvidi rūḍhaṃ hi taddvārā prāṇadehayoḥ । buddhau vārpyaṃ tadabhyāsānnaiṣa nyāyastu saṃvidi ।। atha vāsmaddṛśi prāṇadhīdehāderapi sphuṭam ।
sarvātmakatvāttatrastho apyabhyāso anyavyapohanam ।। deha utplutisaṃpātadharmojjigamiṣārasāt । utplāvyate tadvipakṣapātāśaṅkāvyapohanāt ।। guruvākyaparāmarśasadṛśe svavimarśane ।
prabuddhe tadvipakṣāṇāṃ vyudāsaḥ pāṭhacintane ।। nahyasya guruṇā śakyaṃ svaṃ jñānaṃ śabda eva vā । dhiyi ropayituṃ tena svaprabodhakramo dhruvam ।। ata eva svapnakāle śrute tatrāpi vastuni ।
tādātmyabhāvanāyogo na phalāya na bhaṇyate ।। saṃketānādare śabdaniṣṭhamāmarśanaṃ paṭhiḥ । tadādare tadarthastu cinteti paricarcyatām ।। tadadvayāyāṃ saṃvittāvabhyāso anupayogavān ।
kevalaṃ dvaitamālinyaśaṅkānirmūlanāya saḥ ।। dvaitaśaṅkāśca tarkeṇa tarkyanta iti varṇitam । tattarkasādhanāyāstu yamāderapyupāyatā ।। uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśastre ca na dvaitaṃ nāpi cādvayam ।
liṅgapūjādikaṃ sarvamityupakramya śaṃbhunā ।। vihitaṃ sarvamevātra pratiṣiddhamathāpi vā । prāṇāyāmādikairaṅgairyogāḥ syuḥ kṛttrimā yataḥ ।। tattenākṛtakasyāsya kalāṃ nārghanti ṣoḍaśīm ।
kiṃ tvetadatra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate ।। tattve cetaḥ sthiraṃ kāryaṃ tacca yasya yathāstviti । evaṃ dvaitaparāmarśanāśāya parameśvaraḥ ।। kvacitsvabhāvamamalamāmṛśannaniśaṃ sthitaḥ ।
yaḥ svabhāvaparāmarśa indriyārthādyupāyataḥ ।। vinaiva tanmukho anyo vā svātantryāttadvikalpanam । tacca svacchasvatantrātmaratnanirbhāsini sphuṭam ।। bhāvaughe bhedasaṃdhātṛ svātmano naiśamucyate ।
tadeva tu samastārthanirbharātmaikagocaram ।। śuddhavidyātmakaṃ sarvamevedamahamityalam । idaṃ vikalpanaṃ śuddhavidyārūpaṃ sphuṭātmakam ।। pratihantīha māyīyaṃ vikalpaṃ bhedabhāvakam ।
śuddhavidyāparāmarśo yaḥ sa eva tvanekadhā ।। snānaśuddhyarcanāhomadhyānajapyādiyogataḥ । viśvametatsvasaṃvittirasanirbharitaṃ rasāt ।। āviśya śuddho nikhilaṃ tarpayedadhvamaṇlam ।
ullāsibodhahutabhugdagdhaviśvendhanodite ।। sitabhasmani dehasya majjanaṃ snānamucyate । itthaṃ ca vihitasnānastarpitānantadevataḥ ।। tato api dehārambhīṇi tattvāni pariśodhayet ।
śivātmakeṣvapyeteṣu buddhiryā vyatirekiṇī ।। saivāśuddhiḥ parākhyātā śuddhistaddhīvimardanam । evaṃ svadehaṃ bodhaikapātraṃ galitabhedakam ।। paśyansaṃvittimātratve svatantre tiṣṭhati prabhuḥ ।
yatkiṃcinmānasāhlādi yatra kvāpīndriyasthitau ।। yojyate brahmasaddhāmni pūjopakaraṇaṃ hi tat । pūjā nāma vibhinnasya bhāvaughasyāpi saṃgatiḥ ।। svatantravimalānantabhairavīyacidātmanā ।
tathāhi saṃvideveyamantarbāhyobhayātmanā ।। svātantryādvartamānaiva parāmarśasvarūpiṇī । sa ca dvādaśadhā tatra sarvamantarbhavedyataḥ ।। sūrya eva hi somātmā sa ca viśvamayaḥ sthitaḥ ।
kalādvādaśakātmaiva tatsaṃvitparamārthataḥ ।। sā ca mātari vijñāne māne karaṇagocare । meye caturvidhaṃ bhāti rūpamāśritya sarvadā ।। śuddhasaṃvinmayī prācye jñāne śabdanarūpiṇī ।
karaṇe grahaṇākārā yataḥ śrīyogasaṃcare ।। ye cakṣurmaṇḍale śvete pratyakṣe parameśvari । ṣoḍaśāraṃ dvādaśāraṃ tatrasthaṃ cakramuttamam ।। prativāraṇavadrakte tadbahirye taducyate ।
dvitīyaṃ madhyage ye te kṛṣṇaśvete ca maṇḍale ।। tadantarye sthite śuddhe bhinnāñjanasamaprabhe । caturdale tu te jñeye agnīṣomātmake priye ।। mithunatve sthite ye ca cakre dve parameśvari ।
saṃmīlanonmīlanaṃ te anyonyaṃ vidadhātake ।। yathā yoniśca liṅgaṃ ca saṃyogātsravato amṛtam । tathāmṛtāgnisaṃyogāddravataste na saṃśayaḥ ।। taccakrapīḍanādrātrau jyotirbhātyarkasomagam ।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā paramāṃ jyotsnāṃ kālajñānaṃ pravartate ।। sahasrāraṃ bhaveccakraṃ tābhyāmupari saṃsthitam । tataścakrātsamudbhūtaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।। tatrasthāṃ muñcate dhārāṃ somo hyagnipradīpitaḥ ।
sṛjatītthaṃ jagatsarvamātmanyātmanyanantakam ।। ṣoḍaśadvādaśārābhyāmaṣṭāreṣvatha sarvaśaḥ । evaṃ krameṇa sarvatra cakreṣvamṛtamuttamam ।। somaḥ sravati yāvacca pañcānāṃ cakrapaddhatiḥ ।
tatpunaḥ pibati prītyā haṃso haṃsa iti sphuran ।। sakṛdyasya tu saṃśrutyā puṇyapāpairna lipyate । pañcāre savikāro atha bhūtvā somasrutāmṛtāt ।। dhāvati trirasārāṇi guhyacakrāṇyasau vibhuḥ ।
yato jātaṃ jagallīnaṃ yatra ca svakalīlayā ।। tatrānandaśca sarvasya brahmacārī ca tatparaḥ । tatra siddhiśca muktiśca samaṃ saṃprāpyate dvayam ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ punaryāti yāvadbrahmātmakaṃ padam ।
agnīṣomau samau tatra sṛjyete cātmanātmani ।। tatrasthastāpitaḥ somo dvedhā jaṅghe vyavasthitaḥ । adhastaṃ pātayedagniramṛtaṃ sravati kṣaṇāt ।। gulphajānvādiṣu vyaktaṃ kuṭilārkapradīpitā ।
sā śaktistāpitā bhūyaḥ pañcārādikramaṃ sṛjet ।। evaṃ śrotre api vijñeyaṃ yāvatpādāntagocaram । pādāṅguṣṭhātsamārabhya yāvadbrahmāṇḍadarśanam ।। ityajānannaiva yogī jānanviśvaprabhurbhavet ।
jvalannivāsau brahmādyairdṛśyate parameśvaraḥ ।। atra tātparyataḥ proktamakṣe kramacatuṣṭayam । ekaikatra yatastena dvādaśātmakatoditā ।। na vyākhyātaṃ tu nirbhajya yato atisarahasyakam ।
meye api devī tiṣṭhantī māsarāśyādirūpiṇī ।। ata eṣā sthitā saṃvidantarbāhyobhayātmanā । svayaṃ nirbhāsya tatrānyadbhāsayantīva bhāsate ।। tataśca prāgiyaṃ śuddhā tathābhāsanasotsukā ।
sṛṣṭiṃ kalayate devī tannāmnāgama ucyate ।। tathā bhāsitavastvaṃśarañjanāṃ sā bahirmukhī । svavṛtticakreṇa samaṃ tato api kalayantyalam ।। sthitireṣaiva bhāvasya tāmantarmukhatārasāt ।
saṃjihīrṣuḥ sthiternāśaṃ kalayantī nirucyate ।। tato api saṃhārarase pūrṇe vighnakarīṃ svayam । śaṅkāṃ yamātmikāṃ bhāge sūte saṃharate api ca ।। saṃhṛtya śaṅkāṃ śaṅkyārthavarjaṃ vā bhāvamaṇḍale ।
saṃhṛtiṃ kalayatyeva svātmavahnau vilāpanāt ।। vilāpanātmikāṃ tāṃ ca bhāvasaṃhṛtimātmani । āmṛśatyeva yenaiṣā mayā grastamiti sphuret ।। saṃhāryopādhiretasyāḥ svasvabhāvo hi saṃvidaḥ ।
nirupādhini saṃśuddhe saṃvidrūpeṣastamīyate ।। vilāpite api bhāvaughe kaṃcidbhāvaṃ tadaiva sā । āśyānayedya evāste śaṅkā saṃskārarūpakaḥ ।। śubhāśubhatayā so ayaṃ soṣyate phalasaṃpadam ।
pūrvaṃ hi bhogātpaścādvā śaṅkeyaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate ।। anyadāśyānitamapi tadaiva drāvayediyam । prāyaścittādikarmabhyo brahmahatyādikarmavat ।। rodhanāddrāvaṇādrūpamitthaṃ kalayate citiḥ ।
