tadapi drāvayedeva tadapyāśyānayedatha ।। itthaṃ bhogye api saṃbhukte sati tatkaraṇānyapi । saṃharantī kalayate dvādaśaivāhamātmani ।। karmabuddhyakṣavargo hi buddhyanto dvādaśātmakaḥ ।
prakāśakatvātsūryātmā bhinne vastuni jṛmbhate ।। ahaṃkārastu karaṇamabhimānaikasādhanam । avicchinnaparāmarśī līyate tena tatra saḥ ।। yathāhi khaṅgapāśādeḥ karaṇasya vibhedinaḥ ।
abhedini svahastādau layastadvadayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। tenendriyaughamārtaṇḍamaṇḍalaṃ kalayetsvayam । saṃviddevī svatantratvātkalpite ahaṃkṛtātmani ।। sa eva paramādityaḥ pūrṇakalpastrayodaśaḥ ।
karaṇatvātprayātyeva kartari pralayaṃ sphuṭam ।। kartā ca dvividhaḥ proktaḥ kalpitākalpitātmakaḥ । kalpito dehabuddhyādivyavacchedena carcitaḥ ।। kālāgnirudrasaṃjñāsya śāstreṣu paribhāṣitā ।
kālo vyavacchittadyukto vahnirbhoktā yataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। saṃsārāklṛptiklṛptibhyāṃ rodhanāddrāvaṇātprabhuḥ । anivṛttapaśūbhāvastatrāhaṃkṛtpralīyate ।। so api kalpitavṛttitvādviśvābhedaikaśālini ।
vikāsini mahākāle līyate ahamidaṃmaye ।। etasyāṃ svātmasaṃvittāvidaṃ sarvamahaṃ vibhuḥ । iti pravikasadrūpā saṃvittiravabhāsate ।। tato antaḥsthitasarvātmabhāvabhogoparāgiṇī ।
paripūrṇāpi saṃvittirakule dhāmni līyate ।। pramātṛvargo mānaughaḥ pramāśca bahudhā sthitāḥ । meyaugha iti yatsarvamatra cinmātrameva tat ।। iyatīṃ rūpavaicitrīmāśrayantyāḥ svasaṃvidaḥ ।
svācchandyamanapekṣaṃ yatsā parā parameśvarī ।। imāḥ prāguktakalanāstadvijṛmbhocyate yataḥ । kṣepo jñānaṃ ca saṃkhyānaṃ gatirnāda iti kramāt ।। svātmano bhedanaṃ kṣepo bheditasyāvikalpanam ।
jñānaṃ vikalpaḥ saṃkhyānamanyato vyatibhedanāt ।। gatiḥ svarūpārohitvaṃ pratibimbavadeva yat । nādaḥ svātmaparāmarśaśeṣatā tadvilopanāt ।। iti pañcavidhāmenāṃ kalanāṃ kurvatī parā ।
devī kālī tathā kālakarṣiṇī ceti kathyate ।। mātṛsadbhāvasaṃjñāsyāstenoktā yatpramātṛṣu । etāvadantasaṃvittau pramātṛtvaṃ sphuṭībhavet ।। vāmeśvarīti-śabdena proktā śrīniśisaṃcare ।
itthaṃ dvādaśadhā saṃvittiṣṭhantī viśvamātṛṣu ।। ekaiveti na ko apyasyāḥ kramasya niyamaḥ kvacit । kramābhāvānna yugapattadabhāvātkramo api na ।। kramākramakathātītaṃ saṃvittattvaṃ sunirmalam ।
tadasyāḥ saṃvido devyā yatra kvāpi pravartanam ।। tatra tādātmyayogena pūjā pūrṇaiva vartate । parāmarśasvabhāvatvādetasyā yaḥ svayaṃ dhvaniḥ ।। sadoditaḥ sa evoktaḥ paramaṃ hṛdayaṃ mahat ।
hṛdaye svavimarśo asau drāvitāśeṣaviśvakaḥ ।। bhāvagrahādiparyantabhāvī sāmānyasaṃjñakaḥ । spandaḥ sa kathyate śāstre svātmanyucchalanātmakaḥ ।। kiṃciccalanametāvadananyasphuraṇaṃ hi yat ।
ūrmireṣā vibodhābdherna saṃvidanayā vinā ।। nistaraṅgataraṅgādivṛttireva hi sindhutā । sārametatsamastasya yaccitsāraṃ jaḍaṃ jagat ।। tadadhīnapratiṣṭhatvāttatsāraṃ hṛdayaṃ mahat ।
tathā hi sadidaṃ brahmamūlaṃ māyāṇḍasaṃjñitam ।। icchājñānakriyārohaṃ vinā naiva saducyate । tacchaktitritayārohādbhairavīye cidātmani ।। visṛjyate hi tattasmādbahirvātha visṛjyate ।
evaṃ sadrūpataivaiṣāṃ satāṃ śaktitrayātmatām ।। visargaṃ parabodhena samākṣipyaiva vartate । tatsadeva bahīrūpaṃ prāgbodhāgnivilāpitam ।। antarnadatparāmarśaśeṣībhūtaṃ tato apyalam ।
khātmatvameva saṃprāptaṃ śaktitritayagocarāt ।। vedanātmakatāmetya saṃhārātmani līyate । idaṃ saṃhārahṛdayaṃ prācyaṃ sṛṣṭau ca hṛnmatam ।। etadrūpaparāmarśamakṛtrimamanābilam ।
ahamityāhureṣaiva prakāśasya prakāśatā ।। etadvīryaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ hṛdayātmakam । vinānena jaḍāste syurjīvā iva vinā hṛdā ।। akṛtrimaitaddhṛdayārūḍho yatkiṃcidācaret ।
prāṇyādvā mṛśate vāpi sa sarvo asya japo mataḥ ।। yadeva svecchayā sṛṣṭisvābhāvyādbahirantarā । nirmīyate tadevāsya dhyānaṃ syātpāramārthikam ।। nirākāre hi ciddhāmni viśvākṛtimaye sati ।
phalārthināṃ kācideva dhyeyatvenākṛtiḥ sthitā ।। yathā hyabhedātpūrṇe api bhāve jalamupāharan । anyākṛtyapahānena ghaṭamarthayate rasāt ।। tathaiva parameśānaniyatipravijṛmbhaṇāt ।
kācidevākṛtiḥ kāṃcit sūte phalavikalpanām ।। yastu saṃpūrṇahṛdayo na phalaṃ nāma vāñchati । tasya viśvākṛtirdevī sā cāvacchedavarjanāt ।। kule yogina udriktabhairavīyaparāsavāt ।
ghūrṇitasya sthitirdehe mudrā yā kācideva sā ।। antarindhanasaṃbhāramanapekṣyaiva nityaśaḥ । jājvalītyakhilākṣaughaprasṛtograśikhaḥ śikhī ।। bodhāgnau tādṛśe bhāvā viśantastasya sanmahaḥ ।
udrecayanto gacchanti homakarmanimittatām ।। yaṃ kaṃcitparameśānaśaktipātapavitritam । purobhāvya svayaṃ tiṣṭheduktavaddīkṣitastu saḥ ।। japyādau homaparyante yadyapyekaikakarmaṇi ।
udeti rūḍhiḥ paramā tathāpītthaṃ nirūpitam ।। yathāhi tatra tatrāśvaḥ samanimnonnatādiṣu । citre deśe vāhyamāno yātīcchāmātrakalpitām ।। tathā saṃvidvicitrābhiḥ śāntaghoratarādibhiḥ ।
bhaṅgībhirabhito dvaitaṃ tyājitā bhairavāyate ।। yathā puraḥsthe mukure nijaṃ vaktraṃ vibhāvayan । bhūyo bhūyastadekātma vaktraṃ vetti nijātmanaḥ ।। tathā vikalpamukure dhyānapūjārcanātmani ।
ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ paśyannacirāttanmayībhavet ।। tanmayībhavanaṃ nāma prāptiḥ sānuttarātmani । pūrṇatvasya parā kāṣṭhā setyatra na phalāntaram ।। phalaṃ sarvamapūrṇatve tatra tatra prakalpitam ।
akalpite hi pūrṇatve phalamanyatkimucyatām ।। eṣa yāgavidhiḥ ko api kasyāpi hṛdi vartate । yasya prasīdecciccakraṃ drāgapaścimajanmanaḥ ।। atra yāge gato rūḍhiṃ kaivalyamadhigacchati ।
lokairālokyamāno hi dehabandhavidhau sthitaḥ ।। atra nāthaḥ samācāraṃ paṭale aṣṭādaśe abhyadhāt । nātra śuddhirna cāśuddhirna bhakṣyādivicāraṇam ।। na dvaitaṃ nāpi cādvaitaṃ liṅgapūjādikaṃ na ca ।
na cāpi tatparityāgo niṣparigrahatāpi vā ।। saparigrahatā vāpi jaṭābhasmādisaṃgrahaḥ । tattyāgo na vratādīnāṃ caraṇācaraṇaṃ ca yat ।। kṣetrādisaṃpraveśaśca samayādiprapālanam ।
parasvarūpaliṅgādi nāmagotrādikaṃ ca yat ।। nāsminvidhīyate kiṃcinna cāpi pratiṣidhyate । vihitaṃ sarvamevātra pratiṣiddhamathāpi ca ।। kiṃ tvetadatra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate ।
tattve cetaḥ sthirīkāryaṃ suprasannena yoginā ।। tacca yasya yathaiva syātsa tathaiva samācaret । tattve niścalacittastu bhuñjāno viṣayānapi ।। na saṃspṛśyeta doṣaiḥ sa padmapatramivāmbhasā ।
viṣāpahārimantrādisaṃnaddho bhakṣayannapi ।। viṣaṃ na muhyate tena tadvadyogī mahāmatiḥ । aśuddhaṃ hi kathaṃ nāma dehādyaṃ pāñcabhautikam ।। prakāśatātirikte kiṃ śuddhyaśuddhī hi vastunaḥ ।
aśuddhasya ca bhāvasya śuddhiḥ syāttādṛśaiva kim ।। anyonyāśrayavaiyarthyānavasthā itthamatra hi । pṛthivī jalataḥ śuddhyejjalaṃ dharaṇitastathā ।। anyonyāśrayatā seyamaśuddhatve apyayaṃ kramaḥ ।
aśuddhājjalataḥ śuddhyeddhareti vyarthatā bhavet ।। vāyuto vāriṇo vāyostejasastasya vānyataḥ । bahurūpādikā mantrāḥ pāvanātteṣu śuddhatā ।। mantrāḥ svabhāvataḥ śuddhā yadi te api na kiṃ tathā ।
śivātmatā teṣu śuddhiryadi tatrāpi sā na kim ।। śivātmatvāparijñānaṃ na mantreṣu dharādivat । te tena śuddhā iti cettajjñaptistarhi śuddhatā ।। yoginaṃ prati sā cāsti bhāveṣviti viśuddhatā ।
nanu codanayā śuddhyaśuddhyādikaviniścayaḥ ।। itthamastu tathāpyeṣā codanaiva śivoditā । kā syātsatīti cedetadanyatra pravitānitam ।। vaidikyā bādhiteyaṃ cedviparītaṃ na kiṃ bhavet ।
samyakcenmanyase bādho viśiṣṭaviṣayatvataḥ ।। apavādena kartavyaḥ sāmānyavihite vidhau । śuddhyaśuddhī ca sāmānyavihite tattvabodhini ।। puṃsi te bādhite eva tathā cātreti varṇitam ।
nārthavādādiśaṅkā ca vākye māheśvare bhavet ।। abuddhipūrvaṃ hi tathā saṃsthite satataṃ bhavet । vyomādirūpe nigame śaṅkā mithyārthatāṃ prati ।। anavacchinnavijñānavaiśvarūpyasunirbharaḥ ।
śāstrātmanā sthito devo mithyātvaṃ kvāpi nārhati ।। icchāvānbhāvarūpeṇa yathā tiṣṭhāsurīśvaraḥ । tatsvarūpābhidhānena tiṣṭhāsuḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ ।। arthavādo api yatrānyavidhyādimukhamīkṣate ।
tatrāstvasatyaḥ svātantrye sa eva tu vidhāyakaḥ ।। vidhivākyāntare gacchannaṅgabhāvamathāpi vā । na nirarthakaṃ evāyaṃ saṃnidhergajaḍādivat ।। svārthapratyāyanaṃ cāsya svasaṃvittyaiva bhāsate ।
tadapahnavanaṃ kartuṃ śakyaṃ vidhiniṣedhayoḥ ।। yuktiścātrāsti vākyeṣu svasaṃviccāpyabādhitā । yā samagrārthamāṇikyatattvaniścayakāriṇī ।। mṛtadehe atha dehotthe yā cāśuddhiḥ prakīrtitā ।
anyatra neti buddhyantāmaśuddhaṃ saṃvidaścyutam ।। saṃvittādātmyamāpannaṃ sarvaṃ śuddhamataḥ sthitam । śrīmadvīrāvalau coktaṃ śuddhyaśuddhinirūpaṇe ।। sarveṣāṃ vāhako jīvo nāsti kiṃcidajīvakam ।
yatkiṃcijjīvarahitamaśuddhaṃ tadvijānata ।। tasmādyatsaṃvido nātidūre tacchudvimāvahet । avikalpena bhāvena munayo api tathābhavan ।। lokasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ tu tattattvaṃ taiḥ pragopitam ।
bahiḥ satsvapi bhāveṣu śuddhyaśuddhī na nīlavat ।। pramātṛdharma evāyaṃ cidaikyānaikyavedanāt । yadi vā vastudharmo api mātrapekṣānibandhanaḥ ।। sautrāmaṇyāṃ surā hotuḥ śuddhānyasya viparyayaḥ ।
anena codanānāṃ ca svavākyairapi bādhanam ।। kvacitsaṃdarśitaṃ brahmahatyāvidhiniṣedhavat । bhakṣyādividhayo apyenaṃ nyāyamāśritya carcitāḥ ।। sarvajñānottarādau ca bhāṣate sma maheśvaraḥ ।
nararṣidevadruhiṇaviṣṇurudrādyudīritam ।। uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyāt pūrvapūrvaprabādhakam । na śaivaṃ vaiṣṇavairvākyairbādhanīyaṃ kadācana ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ brahmasaṃbhūtairnetyādi paricarcayet ।
bādhate yo vaiparītyātsamūḍhaḥ pāpabhāgbhavet ।। tasmānmukhyatayā skanda lokadharmānna cācaret । nānyaśāstrasamuddiṣṭaṃ srotasyuktaṃ nije caret ।। yato yadyapi devena vedādyapi nirūpitam ।
tathāpi kila saṃkocabhāvābhāvavikalpataḥ ।। saṃkocatāratamyena pāśavaṃ jñānamīritam । vikāsatāratamyena patijñānaṃ tu bādhakam ।। idaṃ dvaitamidaṃ neti parasparaniṣedhataḥ ।
māyīyabhedaklṛptaṃ tatsyādakālpanike katham ।। uktaṃ bhargaśikhāyāṃ ca mṛtyukālakalādikam । dvaitādvaitavikalpotthaṃ grasate kṛtadhīriti ।। siddhānte liṅgapūjoktā viśvādhvamayatāvide ।
kulādiṣu niṣiddhāsau dehe viśvātmatāvide ।। iha sarvātmake kasmāttadvidhipratiṣedhane । niyamānupraveśena tādātmyapratipattaye ।। jaṭādi kaule tyāgo asya sukhopāyopadeśataḥ ।
vratacaryā ca mantrārthatādātmyapratipattaye ।। tanniṣedhastu mantrārthasārvātmyapratipattaye । kṣetrapīṭhopapīṭheṣu praveśo vighnaśāntaye ।। mantrādyārādhakasyātha tallābhāyopadiśyate ।
kṣetrādigamanābhāvavidhistu svātmanastathā ।। vaiśvarūpyeṇa pūrṇatvaṃ jñātumityapi varṇitam । samayācārasadbhāvaḥ pālyatvenopadiśyate ।। bhedaprāṇatayā tattattyāgāttattvaviśuddhaye ।
samayādiniṣedhastu mataśāstreṣu kathyate ।। nirmaryādaṃ svasaṃbodhaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ buddhyatāmiti । parakīyamidaṃ rūpaṃ dhyeyametattu me nijam ।। jvālādiliṅgaṃ cānyasya kapālādi tu me nijam ।
ādiśabdāttapaścaryāvelātithyādi kathyate ।। nāma śaktiśivādyantametasya mama nānyathā । gotraṃ ca gurusaṃtāno maṭhikākulaśabditaḥ ।। śrīsaṃtatistryambakākhyā tadardhāmardasaṃjñitā ।
itthamardhacatasro atra maṭhikāḥ śāṃkare krame ।। yugakrameṇa kūrmādyā mīnāntā siddhasaṃtatiḥ । ādiśabdena ca gharaṃ pallī pīṭhopapīṭhakam ।। mudrā chummeti teṣāṃ ca vidhānaṃ svaparasthitam ।
tādātmyapratipattyai hi svaṃ saṃtānaṃ samāśrayet ।। bhuñjīta pūjayeccakraṃ parasaṃtāninā nahi । etacca mataśāstreṣu niṣiddhaṃ khaṇḍanā yataḥ ।। akhaṇḍe api pare tattve bhedenānena jāyate ।
evaṃ kṣetrapraveśādi saṃtānaniyamāntataḥ ।। nāsminvidhīyate taddhi sākṣānnaupayikaṃ śive । na tasya ca niṣodho ya nna tattattvasya khaṇḍanam ।। viśvātmano hi nāthasya svasminrūpe vikalpitau ।
vidhirniṣedho vā śaktau na svarūpasya khaṇḍane ।। paratattvapraveśe tu yameva nikaṭaṃ yadā । upāyaṃ vetti sa grāhyastadā tyājyo atha vā kvacit ।। na yantraṇātra kāryeti proktaṃ śrītrikaśāsane ।
samatā sarvadevānāmovallīmantravarṇayoḥ ।। āgamanāṃ gatīnāṃ ca sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ । sa hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvaṃ śivatattvaṃ prapaśyati ।। yo hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvamātmatattvaṃ prapadyate ।
ketakīkusumasaurabhe bhṛśaṃ bhṛṅga eva rasiko na makṣikā । bhairavīyaparamādvayārcane ko api rajyati maheśacoditaḥ ।। asmiṃśca yoge viśrāntiṃ kurvatāṃ bhavaḍambaraḥ । himānīva mahāgrīṣme svayameva vilīyate ।।
alaṃ vātiprasaṅgena bhūyasātiprapañcite । yogyo abhinavagupto asminko api yāgavidhau budhaḥ ।। ityanuttarapadapravikāse śāktamaupayikamadya viviktam ।। āṇavena vidhinā paradhāma prepsatāmatha nirūpyata etat ।।
vikalpasyaiva saṃskāre jāte niṣpratiyogini । abhīṣṭe vastuni prāptirniścitā bhogamokṣayoḥ ।। vikalpaḥ kasyacitsvātmasvātantryādeva susthiraḥ । upāyāntarasāpekṣyaviyogenaiva jāyate ।।
kasyacittu vikalpo asau svātmasaṃskaraṇaṃ prati । upāyāntarasāpekṣastatroktaḥ pūrvako vidhiḥ ।। vikalpo nāma cinmātrasvabhāvo yadyapi sthitaḥ । tathāpi niścayātmāsāvaṇoḥ svātantryayojakaḥ ।।
niścayo bahudhā caiṣa tatropāyāśca bhedinaḥ । aṇuśabdena te coktā dūrāntikavibhedataḥ ।। tatra buddhau tathā prāṇe dehe cāpi pramātari । apāramārthike apyasmin paramārthaḥ prakāśate ।।
yataḥ prakāśāccinmātrāt prāṇādyavyatirekavat । tasyaiva tu svatantratvāddviguṇaṃ jaḍacidvapuḥ ।। uktaṃ traiśirase caitaddevyai candrārdhamaulinā । jīvaḥ śaktiḥ śivasyaiva sarvatraiva sthitāpi sā ।।
svarūpapratyaye rūḍhā jñānasyonmīlanātparā । tasya cidrūpatāṃ satyāṃ svātantryollāsakalpanāt ।। paśyañjaḍātmatābhāgaṃ tirodhāyādvayo bhavet । tatra svātantryadṛṣṭyā vā darpaṇe mukhabimbavat ।।
viśuddhaṃ nijacaitanyaṃ niścinotyatadātmakam । buddhiprāṇādito bhinnaṃ caitanyaṃ niścitaṃ balāt ।। satyatastadabhinnaṃ syāttasyānyonyavibhedataḥ । viśvarūpāvibheditvaṃ śuddhatvādeva jāyate ।।
niṣṭhitaikasphuranmūrtermūrtyantaravirodhataḥ । antaḥ saṃvidi satsarvaṃ yadyapyaparathā dhiyi ।। prāṇe dehe athavā kasmātsaṃkrāmetkena vā katham । tathāpi nirvikalpe asminvikalpo nāsti taṃ vinā ।।
dṛṣṭe apyadṛṣṭakalpatvaṃ vikalpena tu niścayaḥ । buddhiprāṇaśarīreṣu pārameśvaryamañjasā ।। vikalpyaṃ śūnyarūpe na pramātari vikalpanam । buddhirdhyānamayī tatra prāṇa uccāraṇātmakaḥ ।।
uccāraṇaṃ ca prāṇādyā vyānāntāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ । ādyā tu prāṇanābhikhyāparoccārātmikā bhavet ।। śarīrasyākṣaviṣayaitatpiṇḍatvena saṃsthitiḥ । tatra dhyānamayaṃ tāvadanuttaramihocyate ।।
yaḥ prakāśaḥ svatantro ayaṃ citsvabhāvo hṛdi sthitaḥ । sarvatattvamayaḥ proktametacca triśiromate ।। kadalīsaṃpuṭākāraṃ sabāhyābhyantarāntaram । īkṣate hṛdayāntaḥsthaṃ tatpuṣpamiva tattvavit ।।
somasūryāgnisaṃghaṭṭaṃ tatra dhyāyedananyadhīḥ । taddhyānāraṇisaṃkṣobhānmahābhairavahavyabhuk ।। hṛdayākhye mahākuṇḍe jājvalan sphītatāṃ vrajet । tasya śaktimataḥ sphītaśakterbhairavatejasaḥ ।।
mātṛmānaprameyākhyaṃ dhāmābhedena bhāvayet । vahnyarkasomaśaktīnāṃ tadeva tritayaṃ bhavet ।। parā parāparā ceyamaparā ca sadoditā । sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāraistāsāṃ pratyekatastridhā ।।
caturthaṃ cānavacchinnaṃ rūpamāsāmakalpitam । evaṃ dvādaśa tā devyaḥ sūryabimbavadāsthitāḥ ।। ekaikamāsāṃ vahnyarkasomatacchāntibhāsanam । etadānuttaraṃ cakraṃ hṛdayāccakṣurādibhiḥ ।।
vyomabhirniḥsaratyeva tattadviṣayagocare । taccakrabhābhistatrārthe sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt ।। somasūryāgnibhāsātma rūpaṃ samavatiṣṭhate । evaṃ śabdādiviṣaye śrotrādivyomavartmanā ।।
cakreṇānena patatā tādātmyaṃ paribhāvayet । anena kramayogena yatra yatra patatyadaḥ ।। cakraṃ sarvātmakaṃ tattatsārvabhaumamahīśavat । itthaṃ viśvādhvapaṭalamayatnenaiva līyate ।।
bhairavīyamahācakre saṃvittiparivārite । tataḥ saṃskāramātreṇa viśvasyāpi parikṣaye ।। svātmocchalattayā bhrāmyaccakraṃ saṃcintayenmahat । tatastaddāhyavilayāt tatsaṃskāraparikṣayāt ।।
praśāmyadbhāvayeccakraṃ tataḥ śāntaṃ tataḥ śamam । anena dhyānayogena viśvaṃ cakre vilīyate ।। tatsaṃvidi tataḥ saṃvidvilīnārthaiva bhāsate । citsvābhāvyāt tato bhūyaḥ sṛṣṭiryaccinmaheśvarī ।।
evaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ viśvaṃ svasaṃvidi vilāpayan । visṛjaṃśca tato bhūyaḥ śaśvadbhairavatāṃ vrajet ।। evaṃ triśūlāt prabhṛti catuṣpañcārakakramāt । pañcāśadaraparyantaṃ cakraṃ yogī vibhāvayet ।।
catuṣṣaṣṭiśatāraṃ vā sahasrāramathāpi vā । asaṃkhyārasahasraṃ vā cakraṃ dhyāyedananyadhīḥ ।। saṃvinnāthasya mahato devasyollāsisaṃvidaḥ । naivāsti kācitkalanā viśvaśaktermaheśituḥ ।।
śaktayo asya jagat kṛtsnaṃ śaktimāṃstu maheśvaraḥ । iti māṅgalaśāstre tu śrīśrīkaṇṭho nyarūpayat ।। ityetat prathamopāyarūpaṃ dhyānaṃ nyarūpayat । śrīśaṃbhunātho me tuṣṭastasmai śrīsumatiprabhuḥ ।।
anayaiva diśānyāni dhyānānyapi samāśrayet । anuttaropāyadhurāṃ yānyāyānti kramaṃ vinā ।। atha prāṇasya yā vṛttiḥ prāṇanādyā nirūpitā । tadupāyatayā brūmo anuttarapravikāsanam ।।
nijānande pramātraṃśamātre hṛdi purā sthitaḥ । śūnyatāmātraviśrānternirānandaṃ vibhāvayet ।। prāṇodaye prameye tu parānandaṃ vibhāvayet । tatrānantaprameyāṃśapūraṇāpānanirvṛtaḥ ।।
parānandagatastiṣṭhedapānaśaśiśobhitaḥ । tato anantasphuranmeyasaṃghaṭṭaikāntanirvṛtaḥ ।। samānabhūmimāgatya brahmānandamayo bhavet । tato api mānameyaughakalanāgrāsatatparaḥ ।।
udānavahnau viśrānto mahānandaṃ vibhāvayat । tatra viśrāntimabhyetya śāmyatyasminmahārciṣi ।। nirupādhirmahāvyāptirvyānākhyopādhivarjitā । tadā khalu cidānando yo jaḍānupabṛṃhitaḥ ।।
nahyatra saṃsthitiḥ kāpi vibhaktā jaḍarūpiṇaḥ । yatra ko api vyavacchedo nāsti yadviśvataḥ sphurat ।। yadanāhatasaṃvitti paramāmṛtabṛṃhitam । yatrāsti bhāvanādīnāṃ na mukhyā kāpi saṃgatiḥ ।।
tadeva jagadānandamasmabhyaṃ śaṃbhurūcivān । tatra viśrāntirādheyā hṛdayoccārayogataḥ ।। yā tatra samyagviśrāntiḥ sānuttaramayī sthitiḥ । ityetaddhṛdayādyekasvabhāve api svadhāmani ।।
ṣaṭprāṇoccārajaṃ rūpamatha vyāptyā taducyate । prāṇadaṇḍaprayogena pūrvāparasamīkṛteḥ ।। catuṣkikāmbujālambilambikāsaudhamāśrayet । triśūlabhūmiṃ krāntvāto nāḍitritayasaṅgatām ।।
icchājñānakriyāśaktisamatve praviśet sudhīḥ । ekāṃ vikāsinīṃ bhūyastvasaṃkocāṃ vikasvarām ।। śrayedbhrūbindunādāntaśaktisopānamālikām । tatrordhvakuṇḍalībhūmau spandanodarasundaraḥ ।।
visargastatra viśrāmyenmatsyodaradaśājuṣi । rāsabhī vaḍavā yadvatsvadhāmānandamandiram ।। vikāsasaṃkocamayaṃ praviśya hṛdi hṛṣyati । tadvanmuhurlīnasṛṣṭabhāvavrātasunirbharām ।।
śrayedvikāsasaṃkocarūḍhabhairavayāmalām । ekīkṛtamahāmūlaśūlavaisargike hṛdi ।। parasminneti viśrāntiṃ sarvāpūraṇayogataḥ । atra tatpūrṇavṛttyaiva viśvāveśamayaṃ sthitam ।।
prakāśasyātmaviśrāntāvahamityeva dṛśyatām । anuttaravimarśe prāgvyāpārādivivarjite ।। cidvimarśaparāhaṃkṛt prathamollāsinī sphuret । tata udyogasaktena sa dvādaśakalātmanā ।।
sūryeṇābhāsayedbhāvaṃ pūrayedatha carcayet । athenduḥ ṣoḍaśakalo visargagrāsamantharaḥ ।। saṃjīvanyamṛtaṃ bodhavahnau visṛjati sphuran । icchājñānakriyāśaktisūkṣmarandhrasrugagragam ।।
tadevama[tada]mṛtaṃ divyaṃ saṃviddevīṣu tarpakam । visargāmṛtametāvad bodhākhye hutabhojini ।। visṛṣṭaṃ cedbhavetsarvaṃ hutaṃ ṣoḍhādhvamaṇḍalam । yato anuttaranāthasya visargaḥ kulanāyikā ।
tatkṣobhaḥ kādihāntaṃ tatprasarastattvapaddhatiḥ ।। aṃa iti kuleśvaryā sahito hi kuleśitā । paro visargaviśleṣastanmayaṃ viśvamucyate ।। vitprāṇaguṇadehāntarbahirdravyamayīmimām ।
arcayejjuhuyāddhyāyeditthaṃ saṃjīvanīṃ kalām ।। ānandanāḍīyugalaspandanāvahitau sthitaḥ । enāṃ visarganiḥṣyandasaudhabhūmiṃ prapadyate ।। śākte kṣobhe kulāveśe sarvanāḍyagragocare ।
vyāptau sarvātmasaṃkoce hṛdayaṃ praviśetsudhīḥ ।। somasūryakalājālaparasparanigharṣataḥ । agnīṣomātmake dhāmni visargānanda unmiṣet ।। alaṃ rahasyakathayā guptametatsvabhāvataḥ ।
yoginīhṛdayaṃ tatra viśrāntaḥ syātkṛtī budhaḥ ।। hānādānatiraskāravṛttau rūḍhimupāgataḥ । abhedavṛttitaḥ paśyedviśvaṃ citicamatkṛteḥ ।। arthakriyārthitādainyaṃ tyaktvā bāhyāntarātmani ।
kharūpe nirvṛtiṃ prāpya phullāṃ nādadaśāṃ śrayet ।। vaktramantastayā samyak saṃvidaḥ pravikāsayet । saṃvidakṣamaruccakraṃ jñeyābhinnaṃ tato bhavet ।। tajjñeyaṃ saṃvidākhyena vahninā pravilīyate ।
vilīnaṃ tat trikoṇe asmiñśaktivahnau vilīyate ।। tatra saṃvedanodārabindusattāsunirvṛtaḥ । saṃhārabījaviśrānto yogī paramayo bhavet ।। antarbāhye dvaye vāpi sāmānyetarasundaraḥ ।
saṃvitspandastriśaktyātmā saṃkocapravikāsavān ।। asaṃkocavikāso api tadābhāsanatastathā । antarlakṣyo bahirdṛṣṭiḥ paramaṃ padamaśnute ।। tataḥ svātantryanirmeye vicitrārthakriyākṛti ।
vimarśanaṃ viśeṣākhyaḥ spanda aunmukhyasaṃjñitaḥ ।। tatra viśrāntimāgacchedyadvīryaṃ mantramaṇḍale । śāntyādisiddhayastattadrūpatādātmyato yataḥ ।। divyo yaścākṣasaṃgho ayaṃ bodhasvātantryasaṃjñakaḥ ।
so animīlita evaitat kuryātsvātmamayaṃ jagat ।। mahāsāhasasaṃyogavilīnākhilavṛttikaḥ । puñjībhūte svaraśmyoghe nirbharībhūya tiṣṭhati ।। akiciccintakastatra spaṣṭadṛgyāti saṃvidam ।
yadvisphuliṅgāḥ saṃsārabhasmadāhaikahetavaḥ ।। taduktaṃ parameśena triśirobhairavāgame । śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi mantrabhūmyāṃ praveśanam ।। madhyanāḍyordhvagamanaṃ taddharmaprāptilakṣaṇam ।
visargāntapadātītaṃ prāntakoṭinirūpitam ।। adhaḥpravāhasaṃrodhādūrdhvakṣepavivarjanāt । mahāprakāśamudayajñānavyaktipradāyakam ।। anubhūya pare dhāmni mātrāvṛttyā puraṃ viśet ।
nistaraṅgāvatīrṇā sā vṛttirekā śivātmikā ।। catuṣṣaḍdvirdviguṇitacakraṣaṭkasamujjvalā । tatsthaṃ [tstho] vicārayet khaṃ khaṃ khasthaṃ khasthena saṃviśet ।। khaṃ khaṃ tyaktvā khamāruhya khasthaṃ khaṃ coccarediti ।
khamadhyāsyādhikāreṇa padasthāścinmarīcayaḥ ।। bhāvayedbhāvamantaḥsthaṃ bhāvastho bhāvaniḥspṛhaḥ । bhāvābhāvagatī ruddhvā bhāvābhāvāvarodhadṛk ।। ātmāṇukulamūlāni śaktirbhūtiścitī ratiḥ ।
śaktitrayaṃ draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ tadvivarjitam ।। etatkhaṃ daśadhā proktamuccāroccāralakṣaṇam । dhāmasthaṃ dhāmamadhyasthaṃ dhāmodarapuṭīkṛtam ।। dhāmnā tu bodhayeddhāma dhāma dhāmāntagaṃ kuru ।
taddhāma dhāmagatyā tu bhedyaṃ dhāmāntamāntaram ।। bhedopabhedabhedena bhedaḥ kāryastu madhyataḥ । iti praveśopāyo ayamāṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। śrīmaheśvaranāthena yo hṛtsthena mamoditaḥ ।
śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ śrīmān rāvo daśātmakaḥ ।। sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paro hṛdyaḥ kaṇṭhyastālavya eva ca । sarvataśca vibhuryo asau vibhutvapadadāyakaḥ ।। jitarāvo mahāyogī saṃkrāmetparadehagaḥ ।
parāṃ ca vindati vyāptiṃ pratyahaṃ hyabhyaseta tam ।। tāvadyāvadarāve sā rāvāllīyeta rāviṇī । atra bhāvanayā dehagatopāyaiḥ pare pathi ।। vivikṣoḥ pūrṇatāsparśātprāgānandaḥ prajāyate ।
tato api vidyudāpātasadṛśe dehavarjite ।। dhāmni kṣaṇaṃ samāveśādudbhavaḥ prasphuṭaṃ plutiḥ । jalapāṃsuvadabhyastasaṃviddehaikyahānitaḥ ।। svabalākramaṇāddehaśaithilyāt kampamāpnuyāt ।
galite dehatādātmyaniścaye antarbhukhatvataḥ ।। nidrāyate purā yāvanna rūḍhaḥ saṃvidātmani । tataḥ satyapade rūḍho viśvātmatvena saṃvidam ।। saṃvidan ghūrṇate ghūrṇirmahāvyāptiryataḥ smṛtā ।
ātmanyanātmābhimatau satyāmeva hyanātmani ।। ātmābhimāno dehādau bandho muktistu tallayaḥ । ādāvanātmanyātmatve līne labdhe nijātmani ।। ātmanyanātmatānāśe mahāvyāptiḥ pravartate ।
ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nindrā ghūrṇiśca pañcakam ।। ityuktamata eva śrīmālinīvijayottare । pradarśite asminnānandaprabhṛtau pañcake yadā ।। yogī viśettadā tattaccakreśatvaṃ haṭhādvrajet ।
yathā sarveśinā bodhenākrāntāpi tanuḥ kvacit ।। kiṃcitkartuṃ prabhavati cakṣuṣā rūpasaṃvidam । tathaiva cakre kutrāpi praveśātko api saṃbhavet ।। ānandacakraṃ vahnyaśri kanda udbhava ucyate ।
kampo hṛttālu nidrā ca ghūrṇiḥ syādūrdhvakuṇḍalī ।। etacca sphuṭamevoktaṃ śrīmantraiśirase mate । evaṃ pradarśitoccāraviśrāntihṛdayaṃ param ।। yattadavyaktaliṅgaṃ nṛśivaśaktyavibhāgavat ।
atra viśvamidaṃ līnamatrāntaḥsthaṃ ca gamyate ।। idaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ pūrṇaśaktibhairavasaṃvidaḥ । dehagādhvasamunmeṣe samāveśastu yaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।। ahantācchāditonmeṣibhāvedaṃbhāvayuk sa ca ।
vyaktāvyaktamidaṃ liṅgaṃ mantravīryaṃ parāparam ।। naraśaktisamunmeṣi śivarūpādvibheditam । yannyakkṛtaśivāhantāsamāveśaṃ vibhedavat ।। viśeṣaspandarūpaṃ tad vyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ cidātmakam ।
vyaktātsiddhiprasavo vyaktāvyaktāddvayaṃ vimokṣaśca । avyaktādbalamādyaṃ parasya nānuttare tviyaṃ carcā ।। ātmākhyaṃ yadvyaktaṃ naraliṅgaṃ tatra viśvamarpayataḥ । vyaktāvyaktaṃ tasmādgalite tasmiṃstadavyaktam ।।
tenātmaliṅgametat parame śivaśaktyaṇusvabhāvamaye । avyakte viśrāmyati nānuttaradhāmagā tviyaṃ carcā ।। ekasya spandanasyaiṣā traidhaṃ bhedavyavasthitiḥ । atra liṅge sadā tiṣṭhet pūjāviśrāntitatparaḥ ।।
yoginīhṛdayaṃ liṅgamidamānandasundaram । bījayonisamāpattyā sūte kāmapi saṃvidam ।। atra prayāsavirahātsarvo asau devatāgaṇaḥ । ānandapūrṇe dhāmnyāste nityoditacidātmakaḥ ।।
atra bhairavanāthasya sasaṃkocavikāsikā । bhāsate durghaṭā śaktirasaṃkocavikāsinaḥ ।। etalliṅgasamāpattivisargānandadhārayā । siktaṃ tadeva sadviśvaṃ śaśvannavanavāyate ।।
anuttare abhyupāyo atra tādrūpyādeva varṇitaḥ । jvaliteṣvapi dīpeṣu gharmāṃśuḥ kiṃ na bhāsate ।। artheṣu tadbhogavidhau tadutthe duḥkhe sukhe vā galitābhiśaṅkam । anāviśanto api nimagnacittā jānanti vṛttikṣayasaukhyamantaḥ ।।
satyevātmani citsvabhāvamahasi svānte tathopaktiyāṃ tasmai kurvati tatpracāravivaśe satyakṣavarge api ca । satsvartheṣu sukhādiṣu sphuṭataraṃ yadbhedavandhyodayaṃ yogī tiṣṭhati pūrṇaraśmivibhavastattattvamācīyatām ।। ityuccāravidhiḥ proktaḥ karaṇaṃ pravivicyate । taccetthaṃ triśiraḥśāstre parameśena bhāṣitam ।।
grāhyagrāhakacidvyāptityāgākṣepaniveśanaiḥ । karaṇaṃ saptadhā prāhurabhyāsaṃ bodhapūrvakam ।। tadvyāptipūrvamākṣepe karaṇaṃ svapratiṣṭhatā । guruvaktrācca boddhavyaṃ karaṇaṃ yadyapi sphuṭam ।।
tathāpyāgamarakṣārthaṃ tadagre varṇayiṣyate । ukto ya eṣa uccārastatra yo asau sphuran sthitaḥ ।। avyaktānukṛtiprāyo dhvanirvarṇaḥ sa kathyate । sṛṣṭisaṃhārabījaṃ ca tasya mukhyaṃ vapurviduḥ ।।
tadabhyāsavaśādyāti kramādyogī cidātmatām । tathā hyanacke sācke vā kādau sānte punaḥpunaḥ ।। smṛte proccārite vāpi sā sā saṃvitprasūyāte । bāhyārthasamayāpekṣā ghaṭādyā dhvanayo api ye ।।
te apyarthabhāvanāṃ kuryurmanorājyavadātmani । taduktaṃ parameśena bhairavo vyāpako akhile ।। iti bhairavaśabdasya saṃtatoccāraṇācchivaḥ । śrīmattraiśirase apyuktaṃ mantroddhārasya pūrvataḥ ।।
smṛtiśca smaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhāveṣu vastutaḥ । mantrasvarūpaṃ tadbhāvyasvarūpāpattiyojakam ।। smṛtiḥ svarūpajanikā sarvabhāveṣu rañjikā । anekākārarūpeṇa sarvatrāvasthitena tu ।।
svasvabhāvasya saṃprāptiḥ saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ । vyaktiniṣṭhā tato viddhi sattā sā kīrtitā parā ।। kiṃ punaḥ samayāpekṣāṃ vinā ye bījapiṇḍakāḥ । saṃvidaṃ spandapantyete neyuḥ saṃvidupāyatām ।।
vācyābhāvādudāsīnasaṃvitspandātsvadhāmataḥ । prāṇollāsanirodhābhyāṃ bījapiṇḍeṣu pūrṇatā ।। sukhasītkārasatsamyaksāmyaprathamasaṃvidaḥ । saṃvedanaṃ hi prathamaṃ sparśo anuttarasaṃvidaḥ ।।
hṛtkaṇṭhyoṣṭhyatridhāmāntarnitarāṃ pravikāsini । caturdaśaḥ praveśo ya ekīkṛtatadātmakaḥ ।। tato visargoccārāṃśe dvādaśāntapathāvubhau । hṛdayena sahaikadhyaṃ nayate japatatparaḥ ।।
kandahṛtkaṇṭhatālvagrakauṇḍilīprakriyāntataḥ । ānandamadhyanāḍyantaḥ spandanaṃ bījamāvahet ।। saṃhārabījaṃ khaṃ hṛtsthamoṣṭhyaṃ phullaṃ svamūrdhani । tejastryaśraṃ tālukaṇṭhe bindurūrdhvapade sthitaḥ ।।
ityenayā budho yuktyā varṇajapyaparāyaṇaḥ । anuttaraṃ paraṃ dhāma praviśedacirāt sudhīḥ ।। varṇaśabdena nīlādi yadvā dīkṣottare yathā । saṃhāranragnimaruto rudrabinduyutānsmaret ।।
hṛdaye tanmayo lakṣyaṃ paśyetsaptadinādatha । visphuliṅgāgnivannīlapītaraktādicitritam ।। jājvalīti hṛdambhoje bījadīpaprabodhitam । dīpavajjvalito bindurbhāsate vighanārkavat ।।
svayaṃbhāsātmanānena tādātmyaṃ yātyananyadhīḥ । śivena hematāṃ yadvattāmraṃ sūtena vedhitam ।। upalakṣaṇametacca sarvamantreṣu lakṣayet । yadyatsaṃkalpasaṃbhūtaṃ varṇajālaṃ hi bhautikam ।।
tat saṃvidādhikyavaśādabhautikamiva sthitam । atastathāvidhe rūpe rūḍho rohati saṃvidi ।। anācchāditarūpāyāmanupādhau prasannadhīḥ । nīle pīte sukhe duḥkhe saṃvidrūpamakhaṇḍitam ।।
gurubhirbhāṣitaṃ tasmādupāyeṣu vicitratā । uccārakaraṇadhyānavarṇairebhiḥ pradarśitaḥ ।। anuttarapadaprāptāvabhyupāyavidhikramaḥ । akiṃciccintanaṃ vīryaṃ bhāvanāyāṃ ca sā punaḥ ।।
dhyāne tadapi coccāre karaṇe so api taddhvanau । sa sthānakalpane bāhyamiti kramamupāśrayet ।। laṅghanena paro yogī mandabuddhiḥ krameṇa tu । vīryaṃ vinā yathā ṣaṇṭhastasyāpyastyatha vā balam ।
mṛtadeha iveyaṃ syādbāhyāntaḥparikalpanā ।। ityāṇave anuttaratābhyupāyaḥ prokto nayaḥ spaṣṭapathena bāhyaḥ ।। sthānaprakalpākhyatayā sphuṭastu bāhyo abhyupāyaḥ pravivicyate atha ।। sthānabhedastridhā proktaḥ prāṇe dehe bahistathā ।
prāṇaśca pañcadhā dehe dvidhā bāhyāntaratvataḥ ।। maṇḍalaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pātramakṣasūtraṃ sapustakam । liṅgaṃ tūraṃ paṭaḥ pustaṃ pratimā mūrtireva ca ।। ityekādaśadhā bāhyaṃ punastadbahudhā bhavet ।
tatra prāṇāśrayaṃ tāvadvidhānamupadiśyate ।। adhvā samasta evāyaṃ ṣaḍvidho apyativistṛtaḥ । yo vakṣyate sa ekatra prāṇe tāvatpratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। adhvanaḥ kalanaṃ yattatkramākramatayā sthitam ।
kramākramau hi citraikakalanā bhāvagocare ।। kramākramātmā kālaśca paraḥ saṃvidi vartate । kālī nāma parā śaktiḥ saiva devasya gīyate ।। saiva saṃvidbahiḥ svātmagarbhībhūtau kramākramau ।
sphuṭayantī prarohaṇa prāṇavṛttiriti sthitā ।। saṃvinmātraṃ hi yacchuddhaṃ prakāśaparamārthakam । tanmeyamātmanaḥ projjhya viviktaṃ bhāsate nabhaḥ ।। tadeva śūnyarūpatvaṃ saṃvidaḥ parigīyate ।
neti neti vimarśena yogināṃ sā parā daśā ।। sa eva khātmā meye asminbhedite svīkriyonmukhaḥ । patansamucchalattvena prāṇaspandormisaṃjñitaḥ ।। tenāhuḥ kila saṃvitprākprāṇe pariṇatā tathā ।
antaḥkaraṇatattvasya vāyurāśrayatāṃ gataḥ ।। iyaṃ sā prāṇanāśaktirāntarodyogadohadā । spandaḥ sphurattā viśrāntirjīvo hṛtpratibhā matā ।। sā prāṇavṛttiḥ prāṇādyai rūpaiḥ pañcabhirātmasāt ।
dehaṃ yatkurute saṃvitpūrṇastenaiṣa bhāsate ।। prāṇanāvṛttitādātmyasaṃvitkhacitadehajām । ceṣṭāṃ paśyantyato mugdhā nāstyanyaditi manvate ।। tāmeva bālamūrkhastrīprāyaveditṛsaṃśritām ।
matiṃ pramāṇīkurvantaścārvākāstattvadarśinaḥ ।। teṣāṃ tathā bhāvanā caddārḍhyameti nirantaram । taddehabhaṅge suptāḥ syurātādṛgvāsanākṣayāt ।। tadvāsanākṣaye tveṣāmakṣīṇaṃ vāsanāntaram ।
buddhaṃ kutaścitsaṃsūte vicitrāṃ phalasampadam ।। adārḍhyaśaṅkanātprācyavāsanātādavasthyataḥ । anyakartavyaśaithilyātsaṃbhāvyānuśayatvataḥ ।। atadrūḍhānyajanatākartavyaparilopanāt ।
nāstikyavāsanāmāhuḥ pāpātpāpīyasīmimām ।। alamaprastutenātha prakṛtaṃ pravivicyate । yāvānsamasta evāyamadhvā prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। dvidhā ca so adhvā kriyayā mūrtyā ca pravibhajyate ।
prāṇa eva śikhā śrīmattriśirasyuditā hi sā ।। baddhā yāgādikāle tuṃ niṣkalatvācchivātmikā । yato ahorātramadhye asyāścaturviṃśatidhā gatiḥ ।। prāṇavikṣeparandhrākhyaśataiścitraphalapradā ।
kṣapā śaśī tathāpāno nāda ekatra tiṣṭhati ।। jīvādityo na codgacchettuṭyardhaṃ sāndhyamīdṛśam । ūrdhvavaktro raviścandro adhomukho vahnirantare ।। mādhyāhnikī mokṣadā syādvyomamadhyasthito raviḥ ।
anastamitasāro hi jantucakraprabodhakaḥ ।। binduḥ prāṇo hyahaścaiva ravirekatra tiṣṭhati । mahāsandhyā tṛtīyā tu supraśāntātmikā sthitā ।। evaṃ baddhā śikhā yatra tattatphalaniyojikā ।
ataḥ saṃvidi sarvo ayamadhvā viśramya tiṣṭhati ।। amūrtāyāḥ sarvagatvānniṣkriyāyāśca saṃvidaḥ । mūrtikriyābhāsanaṃ yatsa evādhvā maheśituḥ ।। adhvā krameṇa yātavye pade saṃprāptikāraṇam ।
dvaitināṃ bhogyabhāvāttu prabuddhānāṃ yato adyate ।। iha sarvatra śabdānāmanvarthaṃ carcayedyataḥ । uktaṃ śrīmanniśācāre saṃjñātra trividhā matā ।। naimittikī prasiddhā ca tathānyā pāribhāṣikī ।
pūrvatve vā pradhānaṃ syāttatrāntarbhāvayettataḥ ।। ato adhvaśabdasyokteyaṃ niruktirnoditāpi cet । kvacitsvabuddhyā sāpyūhyā kiyallekhyaṃ hi pustake ।। tatra kriyābhāsanaṃ yatso adhvā kālāhva ucyate ।
varṇamantrapadābhikhyamatrāste adhvatrayaṃ sphuṭam ।। yastu mūrtyavabhāsāṃśaḥ sa deśādhvā nigadyate । kalātattvapurābhikhyamantarbhūtamiha trayam ।। trikadvaye atra pratyekaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ paraṃ vapuḥ ।
yato asti tena sarvo ayamadhvā ṣaḍvidha ucyate ।। ṣaḍvidhādadhvanaḥ prācyaṃ yadetattritayaṃ punaḥ । eṣa eva sa kālādhvā prāṇe spaṣṭaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। tattavamadhyasthitātkālādanyo ayaṃ kāla ucyate ।
eṣa kālo hi devasya viśvābhāsanakāriṇī ।। kriyāśaktiḥ samastānāṃ tattvānāṃ ca paraṃ vapuḥ । etadīśvaratattvaṃ tacchivasya vapurucyate ।। udriktābhogakāryātmaviśvaikātmyamidaṃ yataḥ ।
etadīśvararūpatvaṃ paramātmani yatkila ।। tatpramātari māyīye kālatattvaṃ nigadyate । śivādiśuddhavidyāntaṃ yacchivasya svakaṃ vapuḥ ।। tadeva puṃso māyādirāgāntaṃ kañcukībhavet ।
anāśritaṃ yato māyā kalāvidye sadāśivaḥ ।। īśvaraḥ kālaniyatī sadvidyā rāga ucyate । anāśritaḥ śūnyamātā buddhimātā sadāśivaḥ ।। īśvaraḥ prāṇamātā ca vidyā dehapramātṛtā ।
anāśrayo hi śūnyatvaṃ jñānameva hi buddhitā ।। viśvātmatā ca prāṇatvaṃ dehe vedyaikatānatā । tena prāṇapathe viśvākalaneyaṃ virājate ।। yena rūpeṇa tadvacmaḥ sadbhistadavadhīyatām ।
dvādaśāntāvadhāvasmindehe yadyapi sarvataḥ ।। otaprotātmakaḥ prāṇastathāpītthaṃ na susphuṭaḥ । yatno jīvanamātrātmā tatparaśca dvidhā mataḥ ।। saṃvedyaścāpyasaṃvedyo dvidhetthaṃ bhidyate punaḥ ।
sphuṭāsphuṭatvāddvaividhyaṃ pratyekaṃ paribhāvayet ।। saṃvedyajīvanābhikhyaprayatnaspandasundaraḥ । prāṇaḥ kandātprabhṛtyeva tathāpyatra na susphuṭaḥ ।। kandādhārātprabhṛtyeva vyavasthā tena kathyate ।
svacchandaśāstre nāḍīnāṃ vāyvādhāratayā sphuṭam ।। tatrāpi tu prayatno asau na saṃvedyatayā sthitaḥ । vedyayatnāttu hṛdayātprāṇacāro vibhajyate ।। prabhoḥ śivasya yā śaktirvāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrikā ।
satadanyatamāvātmaprāṇau yatnavidhāyinau ।। prabhuśaktiḥ kvacinmukhyā yathāṅgamarudīraṇe । ātmaśaktiḥ kvacitkandasaṃkocaspandane yathā ।। prāṇaśaktiḥ kvacitprāṇacāre hārde yathā sphuṭam ।
trayaṃ dvayaṃ vā mukhyaṃ syādyogināmavadhāninām ।। avadhānādadṛṣṭāṃśādbalavattvādatheraṇāt । viparyayo api prāṇātmaśaktīnāṃ mukhyatāṃ prati ।। vāmā saṃsāriṇāmīśā prabhuśaktirvidhāyinī ।
jyeṣṭhā tu suprabuddhānāṃ bubhutsūnāṃ ca raudrikā ।। vāmā saṃsāravamanā jyeṣṭhā śivamayī yataḥ । drāvayitrī rujāṃ raudrī roddhrī cākhilakarmaṇām ।। sṛṣṭyāditattvamajñātvā na mukto nāpi mocayet ।
uktaṃ ca śrīyogacāre mokṣaḥ sarvaprakāśanāt ।। utpattisthitisaṃhārān ye na jānanti yoginaḥ । na muktāste tadajñānabandhanaikādhivāsitāḥ ।। sṛṣṭyādayaśca te sarve kālādhīnā na saṃśayaḥ ।
sa ca prāṇātmakastasmāduccāraḥ kathyate sphuṭaḥ ।। hṛdayātprāṇacāraśca nāsikyadvādaśāntataḥ । ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulo jantoḥ sarvasya svāṅgulakramāt ।। kṣodiṣṭhe vā mahiṣṭhe vā dehe tādṛśa eva hi ।
vīryamojo balaṃ spandaḥ prāṇacāraḥ samaṃ tataḥ ।। ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule cāre yadgamāgamayugmakam । nālikātithimāsābdatatsaṅghro atra sphuṭaṃ sthitaḥ ।। tuṭiḥ sapādāṅgulayukprāṇastāḥ ṣoḍaśocchvasan ।
niḥśvasaṃścātra caṣakaḥ sapañcāṃśe aṅgule aṅgule ।। śvāsapraśvāsayornālī proktāhorātra ucyate । navāṅgulāmbudhituṭau praharāste abdhayo dinam ।। nirgame antarniśenendū tayoḥ saṃdhye tuṭerdale ।
ketuḥ sūrye vidhau rāhurbhaumādervārabhāginaḥ ।। praharadvayamanyeṣāṃ grahāṇāmudayo antarā । siddhirdavīyasī mokṣo abhicāraḥ pāralaukikī ।। aihikī dūranaikaṭyātiśayā praharāṣṭake ।
madhyāhnamadhyaniśayorabhijinmokṣabhogadā ।। nakṣatrāṇāṃ tadanyeṣāmudayo madhyataḥ kramāt । nāgā lokeśamūrtīśā gaṇeśā jalatattvataḥ ।। pradhānāntaṃ nāyakāśca vidyātattvādhināyakāḥ ।
sakalādyāśca kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyaparyantā bhairavāstathā ।। śaktayaḥ pārameśvaryo vāmaśā vīranāyakāḥ । aṣṭāvaṣṭau ye ya itthaṃ vyāpyavyāpakatājuṣaḥ ।। sthūlasūkṣmāḥ kramātteṣāmudayaḥ praharāṣṭake ।
dine krūrāṇi saumyāni rātrau karmāṇyasaṃśayam ।। krūratā saumyatā vābhisandherapi nirūpitā । dinarātrikṣaye muktiḥ sā vyāptidhyānayogataḥ ।। te coktāḥ parameśena śrīmadvīrāvalīkule ।
sitāsitau dīrghahrasvau dharmādharmau dinakṣape ।। kṣīyete yadi taddīkṣā vyāptyā dhyānena yogataḥ । ahorātraḥ prāṇacāre kathito māsa ucyate ।। dinaṃ kṛṣṇo niśā śuklaḥ pakṣau karmasu pūrvavat ।
yāḥ ṣoḍaśoktāstithayastāsu ye pūrvapaścime ।। tayostu viśramo ardhe ardhe tithyaḥ pañcadaśetarāḥ । sapāde dvyaṅgule tithyā ahorātro vibhajyate ।। prakāśaviśramavaśāttāveva hi dinakṣape ।
saṃvitpratikṣaṇaṃ yasmātprakāśānandayoginī ।। tau klṛptau yāvati tayā tāvatyeva dinakṣape । yāvatyeva hi saṃvittiruditoditasusphuṭā ।। tāvāneva kṣaṇaḥ kalpo nimeṣo vā tadastvapi ।
yāvānevodayo vittervedyaikagrahatatparaḥ ।। tāvadevāstamayanaṃ veditṛsvātmacarvaṇam । vedye ca bahirantarvā dvaye vātha dvayojjhite ।। sarvathā tanmayībhūtirdinaṃ vettṛsthatā niśā ।
veditā vedyaviśrānto vettā tvantarmukhasthitiḥ ।। purā vicārayanpaścātsattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ । jāgradveditṛtā svapno vettṛbhāvaḥ purātanaḥ ।। paraḥ suptaṃ kṣaye rātridinayosturyamadvayam ।
kadācidvastuviśrāntisāmyenātmani carvaṇam ।। vedyavedakasāmyaṃ tat sā rātridinatulyatā । vedye viśrāntiradhikā dinadairghyāya tatra tu ।। nyūnā syātsvātmaviśrāntirviparīte viparyayaḥ ।
svātmautsukye prabuddhe hi vedyaviśrāntiralpikā ।। itthameva divārātrinyūnādhikyakramaṃ vadet । yathā deheṣvahorātranyūnādhikyādi no samam ।। tathā pureṣvapītyevaṃ tadviśeṣeṇa noditam ।
śrītraiyambakasantānavitatāmbarabhāskaraḥ ।। dinarātrikramaṃ me śrīśaṃbhuritthamapaprathat । śrīsantānagurustvāha sthānaṃ buddhāprabuddhayoḥ ।। hṛda ārabhya yattena rātrindivavibhājanam ।
tadasatsitapakṣe antaḥ praveśollāsabhāgini ।। abuddhasthānamevaitaddinatvena kathaṃ bhavet । alaṃ vānena nedaṃ vā mama prāṅmatamatsaraḥ ।। heye tu darśite śiṣyāḥ satpathaikāntadarśinaḥ ।
vyākhyātaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo ya statra prāṇagataḥ śaśī ।। āpyāyanātmanaikaikāṃ kalāṃ pratitithi tyajet । dvādaśāntasamīpe tu yāsau pañcadaśī tuṭiḥ ।। sāmāvasyātra sa kṣīṇaścandraḥ prāṇārkamāviśet ।
uktaṃ śrīkāmikāyāṃ ca nordhve adhaḥ prakṛtiḥ parā । ardhārdhe kramate māyā dvikhaṇḍā śivarūpiṇī ।। candrasūryātmanā dehaṃ pūrayetpravilāpayet । amṛtaṃ candrarūpeṇa dvidhā ṣoḍaśadhā punaḥ ।।
pivanti ca surāḥ sarve daśapañca parāḥ kalāḥ । amā śeṣaguhāntaḥsthāmāvāsyā viśvatarpiṇī ।। evaṃ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kṣīyante śaśinaḥ kramāt । āpyāyinyamṛtābrūpatādātmyātṣoḍaśī na tu ।।
tatra pañcadaśī yāsau tuṭiḥ prakṣīṇacandramāḥ । tadūrdhvagaṃ yattuṭyardhaṃ pakṣasaṃdhiḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ।। tasmādviśramatuṭyardhādāmāvasyaṃ purādalam । paraṃ prātipadaṃ cārdhamiti saṃdhiḥ sa kalpyate ।।
tatra prātipade tasmiṃstuṭyardhārdhe purādalam । āmāvasyaṃ tithicchedātkuryātsūryagrahaṃ viśat ।। tatrārkamaṇḍale līnaḥ śaśī sravati yanmadhu । taptatvāttatpibedindusahabhūḥ siṃhikāsutaḥ ।।
arkaḥ pramāṇaṃ somastu meyaṃ jñānakriyātmakau । rāhurmāyāpramātā syāttadācchādanakovidaḥ ।। tata eva tamorūpo vilāpayitumakṣamaḥ । tatsaṃghaṭṭādvayollāso mukhyo mātā vilāpakaḥ ।।
arkendurāhusaṃghaṭṭāt pramāṇaṃ vedyavedakau । advayena tatastena puṇya eṣa mahāgrahaḥ ।। amāvasyāṃ vināpyeṣa saṃghaṭṭaścenmahāgrahaḥ । yathārke meṣage rāhāvaśvinīsthe aśvinīdine ।।
āmāvāsyaṃ yadā tvardhaṃ līnaṃ prātipade dale । pratipacca viśuddhā syāttanmokṣo dūrage vidhau ।। grāsamokṣāntare snānadhyānahomajapādikam । laukikālaukikaṃ bhūyaḥphalaṃ syātpāralaukikam ।।
grāsyagrāsakatākṣobhaprakṣaye kṣaṇamāviśan । mokṣabhāgdhyānapūjādi kurvaṃścandrārkayorgrahe ।। tithiccheda ṛṇaṃ kāso vṛddhirniḥśvasanaṃ dhanam । ayatnajaṃ yatnajaṃ tu recanādatha rodhanāt ।।
evaṃ prāṇe viśati citsūrya induṃ sudhāmayam । ekaikadhyena bodhāṃśu kalayā paripūrayet ।। kramasaṃpūraṇāśāliśaśāṅkāmṛtasundarāḥ । tuṭyaḥ pañcadaśaitāḥ syustithayaḥ sitapakṣagāḥ ।।
antyāyāṃ pūrṇamastuṭyāṃ pūrvavatpakṣasandhitā । indugrahaśca pratipatsandhau pūrvapraveśataḥ ।। aihikaṃ grahaṇe cātra sādhakānāṃ mahāphalam । prāgvadanyadayaṃ māsaḥ prāṇacāre abda ucyate ।।
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsvaṅguleṣvarko hṛdayānmakarādiṣu । tiṣṭhanmāghāḍhikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ kuryāttaccottarāyaṇam ।। saṃkrāntitritaye vṛtte bhukte cāṣṭādaśāṅgule । meṣaṃ prāpte ravau puṇyaṃ viṣuvatpāralaukikam ।।
praveśe tu tulāsthe arke tadeva viṣuvadbhavet । iha siddhipradaṃ caitaddakṣiṇāyanagaṃ tataḥ ।। garbhatā prodbubhūṣiṣyadbhāvaścāthodbubhūṣutā । udbhaviṣyattvamudbhūtiprārambho apyudbhavasthitiḥ ।।
janma sattā pariṇatirvṛddhirhrāsaḥ kṣayaḥ kramāt । makarādīni tenātra kriyā sūte sadṛkphalam ।। āmutrike jhaṣaḥ kumbho mantrādeḥ pūrvasevane । catuṣkaṃ kila mīnādyamantikaṃ cottarottaram ।।
praveśe khalu tatraiva śāntipuṣṭyādisundaram । karma syādaihikaṃ tacca dūradūraphalaṃ kramāt ।। nirgame dinavṛddhiḥ syādviparīte viparyayaḥ । varṣe asmiṃstithayaḥ pañca pratyaṅgulamiti kramaḥ ।।
tatrāpyahorātravidhiriti sarvaṃ hi pūrvavat । prāṇīye varṣa etasminkārtikādiṣu dakṣataḥ ।। pitāmahāntaṃ rudrāḥ syurdvādaśāgre atra bhāvinaḥ । prāṇe varṣodayaḥ prokto dvādaśābdodayo adhunā ।।
kharasāstithya ekasminnekasminnaṅgule kramāt । dvādaśābdodaye te ca caitrādyā dvādaśoditāḥ ।। caitre mantroditiḥ so api tālunyukto adhunā punaḥ । hṛdi caitroditistena tatra mantrodayo api hi ।।
pratyaṅgulaṃ tithīnāṃ tu triśate parikalpite । sapañcāṃśāṅgule abdaḥ syātprāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdatā punaḥ ।। śatāni ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi caikaviṃśatirityayam । vibhāgaḥ prāṇagaḥ ṣaṣṭivarṣāhorātra ucyate ।।
praharāharniśāmāsaṛtvabdaraviṣaṣṭigaḥ । yaśchedastatra yaḥ sandhiḥ sa puṇyo dhyānapūjane ।। iti prāṇodaye yo ayaṃ kālaḥ śaktyekavigrahaḥ । viśvātmāntaḥsthitastasya bāhye rūpaṃ nirūpyate ।।
ṣaṭ prāṇāścaṣakasteṣāṃ ṣaṣṭirnālī ca tāstathā । tithistattriṃśatā māsaste dvādaśa tu vatsaraḥ ।। abdaṃ pitryastvahorātra udagdakṣiṇato ayanāt । pitṝṇāṃ yatsvamānena varṣaṃ taddivyamucyate ।।
ṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ ca triśataṃ varṣāṇāmatra mānuṣam । tacca dvādaśabhirhatvā māsasaṃkhyātra labhyate ।। tāṃ punastriṃśatā hatvāhorātrakalpanā vadet । hatvā tāṃ caikaviṃśatyā sahasraiḥ ṣaṭśatena ca ।।
prāṇasaṃkhyāṃ vadettatra ṣaṣṭyādyabdodayaṃ punaḥ । uktaṃ ca gurubhiḥ śrīmadrauravādisvavṛttiṣu ।। devānāṃ yadahorātraṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ sa hāyanaḥ । śatatrayeṇa ṣaṣṭyā ca nṝṇāṃ vibudhavatsaraḥ ।।
śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca tadeva matamīkṣyate । pitṝṇāṃ tadahorātramityupakramya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। evaṃ daivastvahorātra iti hyaikyopasaṃhṛtiḥ । tena ye guravaḥ śrīmatsvacchandoktidvayāditaḥ ।।
pitryaṃ varṣaṃ divyadinamūcurbhrāntā hi te mudhā । divyārkābdasahasrāṇi yugeṣu caturāditaḥ ।। ekaikahānyā tāvadbhiḥ śataisteṣvaṣṭa saṃdhayaḥ । caturyugaikasaptatyā manvantaste caturdaśa ।।
brahmaṇo ahastatra cendrāḥ kramādyānti caturdaśa । brahmāho ante kālavahnerjvālā yojanalakṣiṇī ।। dagdhvā lokatrayaṃ dhūmāttvanyatprasvāpayettrayam । nirayebhyaḥ purā kālavahnervyaktiryatastataḥ ।।
vibhuradhaḥsthito apīśa iti śrīrauravaṃ matam । brahmaniḥśvāsanirdhūte bhasmani svedavāriṇā ।। tadīyenāplutaṃ viśvaṃ tiṣṭhettāvanniśāgame । tasminniśāvadhau sarve pudgalāḥ sūkṣmadehagāḥ ।।
agnivegeritā loke jane syurlayakevalāḥ । kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakādyāstu krīḍanti mahadālaye ।। niśākṣaye punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ kurute tāmasāditaḥ । svakavarṣaśatānte asya kṣayastadvaiṣṇavaṃ dinam ।।
rātriśca tāvatītyevaṃ viṣṇurudraśatābhidhāḥ । kramātsvasvaśatānteṣu naśyantyatrāṇḍalopataḥ ।। abādyavyaktatattvānteṣvitthaṃ varṣaśataṃ kramāt । dinarātrivibhāgaḥ syāt svasvāyuḥśatamānataḥ ।।
brahmaṇaḥ pralayollāsasahasraistu rasāgnibhiḥ । avyaktastheṣu rudreṣu dinaṃ rātriśca tāvatī ।। tadā śrīkaṇṭha eva syātsākṣātsaṃhārakṛtprabhuḥ । sarve rudrāstathā mūle māyāgarbhādhikāriṇaḥ ।।
avyaktākhye hyāviriñcācchrīkaṇṭhena sahāsate । nivṛttādhaḥsthakarmā hi brahmā tatrādhare dhiyaḥ ।। na bhoktā jño adhikāre tu vṛtta eva śivībhavet । sa eṣo avāntaralayastatkṣaye sṛṣṭirucyate ।।
sāṃkhyavedādisaṃsiddhāñchrīkaṇṭhastadaharmukhe । sṛjatyeva punastena na samyaṅmuktirīdṛśī ।। pradhāne yadahorātraṃ tajjaṃ varṣaśataṃ vibhoḥ । śrīkaṇṭhasyāyuretacca dinaṃ kañcukavāsinām ।।
tatkramānniyatiḥ kālo rāgo vidyā kaletyamī । yāntyanyonyaṃ layaṃ teṣāmāyurgāhanikaṃ dinam ।। taddinaprakṣaye viśvaṃ māyāyāṃ pravilīyate । kṣīṇāyāṃ niśi tāvatyāṃ gahaneśaḥ sṛjetpunaḥ ।।
evamavyaktakālaṃ tu parārdhairdaśabhirjahi । māyāhastāvatī rātrirbhavetpralaya eṣa saḥ ।। māyākālaṃ parārdhānāṃ guṇayitvā śatena tu । aiśvaro divaso nādaḥ prāṇātmātra sṛjejjagat ।।
tāvatī caiśvarī rātriryatra prāṇaḥ praśāmyati । prāṇagarbhasthamapyatra viśvaṃ sauṣumnavartmanā ।। prāṇe brahmavile śānte saṃvidyāpyavaśiṣyate । aṃśāṃśikāto apyetasyāḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmataro layaḥ ।।
guṇayitvaiśvaraṃ kālaṃ parārdhānāṃ śatena tu । sādāśivaṃ dinaṃ rātrirmahāpralaya eva ca ।। sadāśivaḥ svakālānte bindvardhendunirodhikāḥ । ākramya nāde līyeta gṛhītvā sacarācaram ।।
nādo nādāntavṛttyā tu bhittvā brahmabilaṃ haṭhāt । śaktitattve layaṃ yāti nijakālaparikṣaye ।। etāvacchaktitattve tu vijñeyaṃ khalvaharniśam । śaktiḥ svakālavilaye vyāpinyāṃ līyate punaḥ ।।
vyāpinyā taddivārātraṃ līyate sāpyanāśrite । parārdhakoṭyā hatvāpi śaktikālamanāśrite ।। dinaṃ rātriśca tatkāle parārdhaguṇite api ca । so api yāti layaṃ sāmyasaṃjñe sāmanase pade ।।
sa kālaḥ sāmyasaṃjñaḥ syānnityo akalyaḥ kalātmakaḥ । yattatsāmanasaṃ rūpaṃ tatsāmyaṃ brahma viśvagam ।। ataḥ sāmanasātkālānnimeṣonmeṣamātrataḥ । tuṭyādikaṃ parārdhāntaṃ sūte saivātra niṣṭhitam ।।
daśaśatasahasramayutaṃ lakṣaniyutakoṭi sārbudaṃ vṛndam । kharvanikharve śaṃkhābjajaladhimadhyāntamatha parārdhaṃ ca ।। ityekasmātprabhṛti hi daśadhā daśadhā krameṇa kalayitvā । ekādiparārdhānteṣvaṣṭādaśasu sthitiṃ brūyāt ।।
catvāra ete pralayā mukhyāḥ sargāśca tatkalāḥ । bhūmūlanaiśaśaktisthāstadevāṇḍacatuṣṭayam ।। kālāgnirbhuvi saṃhartā māyānte kālatattvarāṭ । śrīkaṇṭho mūla ekatra sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ ।।
tallayo vāntarastasmādekaḥ sṛṣṭilayeśitā । śrīmānaghoraḥ śaktyante saṃhartā sṛṣṭikṛcca saḥ ।। tatsṛṣṭau sṛṣṭisaṃhārā niḥsaṃkhyā jagatāṃ yataḥ । antarbhūtāstataḥ śāktī mahāsṛṣṭirudāhṛtā ।।
laye brahmā harī rudraśatānyaṣṭakapañcakam । ityanyonyaṃ kramādyānti layaṃ māyāntake adhvani ।। māyātattvalaye tvete prayānti paramaṃ padam । māyordhve ye sitādhvasthāsteṣāṃ paraśive layaḥ ।।
tatrāpyaupādhikādbhedāllaye bhedaṃ pare viduḥ । evaṃ tāttveśvare varge līne sṛṣṭau punaḥ pare ।। tatsādhakāḥ śiveṣṭā vā tatsthānamadhiśerate । brāhmī nāma parasyaiva śaktistāṃ yatra pātayet ।।
sa brahmā viṣṇurudrādyā vaiṣṇavyāderataḥ kramāt । śaktimantaṃ vihāyānyaṃ śaktiḥ kiṃ yāti nedṛśam ।। chāditaprathitāśeṣa śaktirekaḥ śivastathā । evaṃ visṛṣṭipralayāḥ prāṇa ekatra niṣṭhitāḥ ।।
so api saṃvidi saṃvicca cinmātre jñeyavarjite । cinmātrameva devī ca sā parā parameśvarī ।। aṣṭātriṃśaṃ ca tattattvaṃ hṛdayaṃ tatparāparam । tena saṃvittvamevaitatspandamānaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।।
layodayā iti prāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdodayakīrtanam । icchāmātrapratiṣṭheyaṃ kriyāvaicitryacarcanā ।। kālaśaktistato bāhye naitasyā niyataṃ vapuḥ । svapnasvapne tathā svapne supte saṃkalpagocare ।।
samādhau viśvasaṃhārasṛṣṭikramavivecane । mito api kila kālāṃśo vitatatvena bhāsate ।। pramātrabhede bhede atha citro vitatimāpyasau । evaṃ prāṇe yathā kālaḥ kriyāvaicitryaśaktijaḥ ।।
tathāpāne api hṛdayānmūlapīṭhavisarpiṇi । mūlābhidhamahāpīṭhasaṅkocapravikāsayoḥ ।। brahmādyanāśritāntānāṃ cinute sṛṣṭisaṃhṛtī । śaśvadyadyapyapāno aya mitthaṃ vahati kiṃtvasau ।।
avedyayatno yatnena yogibhiḥ samupāsyate । hṛtkandānandasaṃkocavikāsadvādaśāntagāḥ ।। brahmādayo anāśritāntāḥ sevyante atra suyogibhiḥ । ete ca parameśānaśaktitvādviśvavartinaḥ ।।
dehamapyaśnuvānāstatkāraṇānīti kāmike । bālyayauvanavṛddhatvanidhaneṣu punarbhave ।। muktau ca dehe brahmādyāḥ ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānakāriṇaḥ । tasyānte tu parā devī yatra yukto na jāyate ।।
anena jñātamātreṇa dīkṣānugrahakṛdbhavet । samastakāraṇollāsapade suvidite yataḥ ।। akāraṇaṃ śivaṃ vindedyattadviśvasya kāraṇam । adhovaktraṃ tvidaṃ dvaitakalaṅkaikāntaśātanam ।।
kṣīyate tadupāsāyāṃ yenordhvādharaḍambaraḥ । atrāpānodaye prāgvatṣaṣṭyabdodayayojanām ।। yāvatkurvīta tuṭyāderyuktāṅgulavibhāgataḥ । evaṃ samāne api vidhiḥ sa hi hārdīṣu nāḍiṣu ।।
saṃcaransarvatodikkaṃ daśadhaiva vibhāvyate । daśa mukhyā mahānāḍīḥ pūrayanneṣa tadgatāḥ ।। nāḍyantaraśritā nāḍīḥ krāmandehe samasthitiḥ । aṣṭāsu digdaleṣveṣa krāmaṃstaddikpateḥ kramāt ।।
ceṣṭitānyanukurvāṇo raudraḥ saumyaśca bhāsate । sa eva nāḍītritaye vāmadakṣiṇamadhyage ।। indvarkāgnimaye mukhye caraṃstiṣṭhatyaharniśam । sārdhanālīdvayaṃ prāṇaśatāni nava yatsthitam ।।
tāvadvahannahorātraṃ caturviṃśatidhā caret । viṣuvadvāsare prātaḥ sāṃśāṃ nālīṃ sa madhyagaḥ ।। vāmetarodaksavyānyairyāvatsaṃkrāntipañcakam । evaṃ kṣīṇāsu pādonacaturdaśasu nāliṣu ।।
madhyāhne dakṣaviṣuvannavaprāṇaśatīṃ vahet । dakṣodaganyodagdakṣaiḥ punaḥ saṃkrāntipañcakam ।। navāsuśatamekaikaṃ tato viṣuvaduttaram । pañcake pañcake atīte saṃkrānterviṣuvadbahiḥ ।।
yadvattathāntaḥ saṅkrāntirnavaprāṇaśatāni sā । evaṃ rātrāvapītyevaṃ viṣuvaddivasātsamāt ।। ārabhyāharniśāvṛddhihrāsasaṅkrāntigo apyasau । rātryantadinapūrvāṃśau madhyāhno divasakṣayaḥ ।।
sa śarvaryudayo madhyamudakto viṣutedṛśī । vyāptau viṣeryato vṛttiḥ sāmyaṃ ca vyāptirucyate ।। tadarhati ca yaḥ kālo viṣuvattadihoditaḥ । viṣuvatprabhṛti hrāsavṛddhī ye dinarātrige ।।
tatkrameṇaiva saṃkrāntihrāsavṛddhī divāniśoḥ । itthaṃ samānamaruto varṣadvayavikalpanam ।। cāra ekatra nahyatra śvāsapraśvāsacarcanam । samāne api tuṭeḥ pūrvaṃ yāvatṣaṣṭyabdagocaram ।।
kālasaṃkhyā susūkṣmaikacāragā gaṇyate budhaiḥ । saṃdhyāpūrvāhṇamadhyāhnamadhyarātrādi yatkila ।। antaḥsaṃkrāntigaṃ grāhyaṃ tanmukhyaṃ tatphaloditeḥ । uktaḥ samānagaḥ kāla udāne tu nirūpyate ।।
prāṇavyāptau yaduktaṃ tadudāne apyatra kevalam । nāsāśaktyantayoḥ sthāne brahmarandhrordhvadhāmanī ।। tenodāne atra hṛdayānmūrdhanyadvādaśāntagam । tuṭyādiṣaṣṭivarṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ kālaṃ vicārayet ।।
vyāne tu viśvātmamaye vyāpake kramavarjite । sūkṣmasūkṣmocchaladrūpamātraḥ kālo vyavasthitaḥ ।। sṛṣṭiḥ pravilayaḥ sthemā saṃhāro anugraho yataḥ । kramātprāṇādike kāle taṃ taṃ tatrāśrayettataḥ ।।
prāṇacāre atra yo varṇapadamantrodayaḥ sthitaḥ । yatnajo ayatnajaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ sthūlaḥ sa kathyate ।। eko nādātmako varṇaḥ sarvavarṇāvibhāgavān । so anastamitarūpatvādanāhata ihoditaḥ ।।
sa tu bhairavasadbhāvo mātṛsadbhāva eṣa saḥ । parā saikākṣarā devī yatra līnaṃ carācaram ।। hrasvārṇatrayamekaikaṃ ravyaṅgulamathetarat । praveśa iti ṣaḍvarṇāḥ sūryendupathagāḥ kramāt ।।
ikārokārayorādisandhau saṃdhyakṣaradvayam । e o iti praveśe tu ai au iti dvayaṃ viduḥ ।। ṣaṇṭhārṇāni praveśe tu dvādaśāntalalāṭayoḥ । gale hṛdi ca bindvarṇavisargau paritaḥsthitau ।।
kādipañcakamādyasya varṇasyāntaḥ sadoditam । evaṃ sasthānavarṇānāmantaḥ sā sārṇasantatiḥ ।। hṛdyeṣa prāṇarūpastu sakāro jīvanātmakaḥ । binduḥ prakāśo hārṇaśca pūraṇātmatayā sthitaḥ ।।
uktaḥ paro ayamudayo varṇānāṃ sūkṣma ucyate । praveśe ṣoḍaśaunmukhye ravayaḥ ṣaṇṭhavarjitāḥ ।। tadevendvarkamatrānye varṇāḥ sūkṣmodayastvayam । kālo ardhamātraḥ kādīnāṃ trayastriṃśata ucyate ।।
mātrā hrasvāḥ pañca dīrghāṣṭakaṃ dvistriḥ plutaṃ tu lṝ । ekāśītimimāmardhamātrāṇāmāha no guruḥ ।। yadvaśādbhagavānekāśītikaṃ mantramabhyadhāt । ekāśītipadā devī śaktiḥ proktā śivātmikā ।।
śrīmātaṅge tathā dharmasaṃghātātmā śivo yataḥ । tathā tathā parāmarśaśakticakreśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। sthūlaikāśītipadajaparāmarśairvibhāvyate । tata eva parāmarśo yāvatyekaḥ samāpyate ।।
tāvattatpadamuktaṃ no suptiṅniyamayāntritam । ekāśītipadodāravimarśaktamabṛṃhitaḥ ।। sthūlopāyaḥ paropāyastveṣa mātrākṛto layaḥ । ardhamātrā nava nava syuścaturṣu caturṣu yat ।।
aṅguleṣviti ṣaṭtriṃśatyekāśītipadodayaḥ । aṅgule navabhāgena vibhakte navamāśakāḥ ।। vedā mātrārdhamanyattu dvicatuḥṣaṅguṇaṃ trayam । evamaṅgularandhrāṃśacatuṣkadvayagaṃ laghu ।।
dīrghaṃ plutaṃ kramāddvitriguṇamardhaṃ tato api hal । kṣakārastryardhamātrātmā mātrikaḥ satathāntarā ।। viśrāntāvardhamātrāsya tasmiṃstu kalite sati । aṅgulārdhe adribhāgena tvardhamātrā purā punaḥ ।।
kṣakāraḥ sarvasaṃyogagrahaṇātmā tu sarvagaḥ । sarvavarṇodayādyantasandhiṣūdayabhāgvibhuḥ ।। itthaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśake cāre varṇānāmudayaḥ phale । krūre saumye vilomena hādi yāvadapaścimam ।।
hṛdyakāro dvādaśānte hakārastadidaṃ viduḥ । ahamātmakamadvaitaṃ yaḥ prakāśātmaviśramaḥ ।। śivaśaktyavibhāgena mātraikāśītikā tviyam । dvāsaptatāvaṅguleṣu dviguṇatvena saṃsaret ।।
uktaḥ sūkṣmodayastraidhaṃ dvidhoktastu parodayaḥ । atha sthūlodayo arṇānāṃ bhaṇyate guruṇoditaḥ ।। ekaikamardhapraharaṃ dine vargāṣṭakodayaḥ । rātrau ca hrāsavṛddhyatra kecidāhurna ke api tu ।।
eṣa vargodayo rātrau divā cāpyardhayāmagaḥ । prāṇatrayodaśaśatī pañcāśadadhikā ca sā ।। adhyardhā kila saṃkrāntirvarge varge divāniśoḥ । tadaikye tūdayaścāraśatānāṃ saptaviṃśatiḥ ।।
nava vargāṃstu ye prāhusteṣāṃ prāṇaśatī svīn[viḥ] । satribhāgaiva saṃkrāntirvarge pratyekamucyate ।। aharniśaṃ tadaikye tu śatānāṃ śruticakṣuṣī । sthūlo vargodayaḥ so ayamathārṇodaya ucyate ।।
ekaikavarṇe prāṇānāṃ dviśataṃ ṣoḍaśādhikam । bahiścaṣakaṣaṭtriṃśaddina itthaṃ tathāniśi ।। śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tatra raudraṃ śāktamathottaram । yāmalasthitiyoge tu rudraśaktyavibhāgitā ।।
dinarātryavibhāge tu dṛgvahnyabdhyasucāraṇāḥ । sapañcamāṃśā nāḍī ca bahirvarṇodayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। iti pañcāśikā seyaṃ varṇānāṃ paricarcitā । ekonāṃ ye tu tāmāhustanmataṃ saṃpracakṣmahe ।।
vedāścārāḥ pañcamāṃśanyūnaṃ cārārdhamekaśaḥ । varṇe adhikaṃ taddviguṇamavibhāge divāniśoḥ ।। sthūlo varṇodayaḥ so ayaṃ purā sūkṣmo nigadyate ।। iti kālatattvamuditaṃ śāstramukhāgamanijānubhavasiddham ।।
atha paramarahasyo ayaṃ cakrāṇāṃ bhaṇyate abhyudayaḥ ।। ityayatnajamākhyātaṃ yatnajaṃ tu nigadyate । bījapiṇḍātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saṃvidaḥ spandanātmatām ।। vidadhatparasaṃvittāvupāya iti varṇitam ।
yathāraghaṭṭacakrāgraghaṭīyantraughavāhanam ।। ekānusaṃdhiyatnena citraṃ yantrodayaṃ bhajet । ekānusaṃdhānabalājjāte mantrodaye aniśam ।। tanmantradevatā yatnāttādātmyena prasīdati ।
khe rasaikākṣi nityotthe tadardhaṃ dvikapiṇḍake ।। trike sapta sahasrāṇi dviśatītyudayo mataḥ । catuṣke tu sahasrāṇi pañca caiva catuḥśatī ।। pañcārṇe abdhisahasrāṇi triśatī viṃśatistathā ।
ṣaṭke sahasratritayaṃ ṣaṭśatī codayo bhavet ।। saptake trisahasraṃ tu ṣaḍaśītyadhikaṃ smṛtam । śataistu saptaviṃśatyā varṇāṣṭakavikalpite ।। caturviṃśatiśatyā tu navārṇeṣūdayo bhavet ।
adhiṣaṣṭyekaviṃśatyā śatānāṃ daśavarṇake ।। ekānnaviṃśatiśataṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śivārṇake । aṣṭādaśa śatāni syurudayo dvādaśārṇake ।। trayodaśārṇe dvāṣaṣṭyā śatāni kila ṣoḍaśa ।
tricatvāriṃśatā pañcadaśeti bhuvanārṇake ।। caturdaśaśatī khābdhiḥ syātpañcadaśavarṇake । trayodaśaśatī sārdhā ṣoḍaśārṇe tu kathyate ।। śatadvādaśikā saptadaśārṇe saikasaptatiḥ ।
aṣṭādaśārṇe vijñeyā śatadvādaśikā budhaiḥ ।। caturviṃśatisaṃkhyāke cakre navaśatī bhavet । saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyāte tūdayo aṣṭaśatātmakaḥ ।। dvātriṃśake mahācakre ṣaṭśatī pañcasaptatiḥ ।
dvicaturviṃśake cakre sārdhāṃ śatacatuṣṭayīm ।। udayaṃ piṇḍayogajñaḥ piṇḍamantreṣu lakṣayet । catuṣpañcāśake cakre śatānāṃ tu catuṣṭayam ।। saptatriṃśatsahārdhena triśatyaṣṭāṣṭake bhavet ।
ardhamardhatribhāgaśca ṣaṭṣaṣṭirdviśatī bhavet ।। ekāśītipade cakre udayaḥ prāṇacāragaḥ । cakre tu ṣaṇṇavatyākhye sapādā dviśatī bhavet ।। aṣṭottaraśate cakre dviśatastūdayo bhavet ।
krameṇetthamidaṃ cakraṃ ṣaṭkṛtvo dviguṇaṃ yadā ।। tato api dviguṇe aṣṭāṃśasyārdhamadhyardhamekakam । tato api sūkṣmakuśalairardhārdhādiprakalpane ।। bhāgaṣoḍaśakasthityā sūkṣmaścāro abhilakṣyate ।
evaṃ prayatnasaṃruddhaprāṇacārasya yoginaḥ ।। krameṇa prāṇacārasya grāsa evopajāyate । prāṇagrāsakramāvāptakālasaṃkarṣaṇasthitiḥ ।। saṃvidekaiva pūrṇā syājjñānabhedavyapohanāt ।
tathā hi prāṇacārasya navasyānudaye sati ।। na kālabhedajanito jñānabhedaḥ prakalpate । saṃvedyabhedānna jñānaṃ bhinnaṃ śikharivṛttavat ।। kālastu bhedakastasya sa tu sūkṣmaḥ kṣaṇo mataḥ ।
saukṣmyasya cāvadhirjñānaṃ yāvattiṣṭhati sa kṣaṇaḥ ।। anyathā na sa nirvaktuṃ nipuṇairapi pāryate । jñānaṃ kiyadbhavettāvattadabhāvo na bhāsate ।। tadabhāvaśca no tāvadyāvattatrākṣavartmani ।
arthe vātmapradeśe vā na saṃyogavibhāgitā ।। sā cedudayate spandamayī tatprāṇagā dhruvam । bhavedeva tataḥ prāṇaspandābhāve na sā bhavet ।। tadabhāvānna vijñānābhāvaḥ saivaṃ tu saiva dhīḥ ।
na cāsau vastuto dīrghā kālabhedavyapohanāt ।। vastuto hyata eveyaṃ kālaṃ saṃvinna saṃspṛśet । ata ekaiva saṃvittirnānārūpe tathātathā ।। vindānā nirvikalpāpi vikalpo bhāvagocare ।
spandāntaraṃ na yāvattaduditaṃ tāvadeva saḥ ।। tāvāneko vikalpaḥ syādvividhaṃ vastu kalpayan । ye tvitthaṃ na vidusteṣāṃ vikalpo nopapadyate ।। sa hyeko na bhavetkaścit trijagatyāpi jātucit ।
śabdārūṣaṇayā jñānaṃ vikalpaḥ kila kathyate ।। sā ca syātkramikaivetthaṃ kiṃ kathaṃ ko vikalpayet । ghaṭa ityapi neyānsyādvikalpaḥ kā kathā sthitau ।। na vikalpaśca ko apyasti yo mātrāmātraniṣṭhitaḥ ।
na ca jñānasamūho asti teṣāmayugapatsthiteḥ ।। tenāstaṅgata evaiṣa vyavahāro vikalpajaḥ । tasmātspandāntaraṃ yāvannodiyāttāvadekakam ।। vijñānaṃ tadvikalpātmadharmakoṭīrapi spṛśet ।
ekāśītipadodāraśaktyāmarśātmakastataḥ ।। vikalpaḥ śivatādāyī pūrvameva nirūpitaḥ । yathā karṇau nartayāmītyevaṃ yatnāttathā bhavet ।। cakracāragatādyatnāttadvattaccakragaiva dhīḥ ।
japahomārcanādīnāṃ prāṇasāmyamato vidhiḥ ।। siddhāmate kuṇḍalinīśaktiḥ prāṇasamonmanā । uktaṃ ca yoginīkaule tadetatparameśinā ।। padamantrākṣare cakre vibhāgaṃ śaktitattvagam ।
padeṣu kṛtvā mantrajño japādau phalabhāgbhavet ।। dvitrisaptāṣṭasaṃkhyātaṃ lopayecchatikodayam । iti śaktisthitā mantrā vidyā vā cakranāyakāḥ ।। padapiṇḍasvarūpeṇa jñātvā yojyāḥ sadā priye ।
nityodaye mahātattve udayasthe sadāśive ।। ayuktāḥ śaktimārge tu na japtāścodayena ye । te na siddhyanti yatnena japtāḥ koṭiśatairapi ।। mālāmantreṣu sarveṣu mānaso japa ucyate ।
upāṃśurvā śaktyudayaṃ teṣāṃ na parikalpayet ।। padamantreṣu sarveṣu yāvattatpadaśaktigam । śakyate satataṃ yuktaistāvajjapyaṃ tu sādhakaiḥ ।। tāvatī teṣu vai saṃkhyā padeṣu padasaṃjñitā ।
tāvantamudayaṃ kṛtvā tripadoktyāditaḥ kramāt ।। dvādaśākhye dvādaśite cakre sārdhaṃ śataṃ bhavet । udayastaddhi sacatuścatvāriṃśacchataṃ bhavet ।। ṣoḍaśākhye dvādaśite dvānavatyadhike śate ।
cārārdhena samaṃ proktaṃ śataṃ dvādaśakādhikam ।। ṣoḍaśākhye ṣoḍaśite bhaveccaturaśītigaḥ । udayo dviśataṃ taddhi ṣaṭpañcāśatsamuttaram ।। cārāṣṭabhāgāṃstrīnatra kathayantyadhikānbudhāḥ ।
aṣṭāṣṭake dvādaśite pādārdhaṃ viṃśatiṃ vasūn ।। udayaḥ saptaśatikā sāṣṭā ṣaṣṭiryato hi saḥ । eṣa cakrodayaḥ proktaḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāvahaḥ ।। niruddhya mānasīrvṛttīścakre viśrāntimāgataḥ ।
vyutthāya yāvadviśrāmyettāvaccārodayo hyayam ।। pūrṇe samudaye tvatra praveśaikātmyanirgamāḥ । traya ityata evoktaḥ siddhau madhyodayo varaḥ ।। ādyantodayanirmuktā madhyamodayasaṃyutāḥ ।
mantravidyācakragaṇāḥ siddhibhājo bhavanti hi ।। mantracakrodayajñastu vidyācakrodayārthavit । kṣipraṃ siddhyediti proktaṃ śrīmaddviṃśatike trike ।। dvistriścaturvā mātrābhirvidyāṃ vā cakrameva vā ।
tattvodayayutaṃ nityaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ japetsadā ।। piṇḍākṣarapadairmantramekaikaṃ śaktitattvagam । bahvakṣarastu yo mantro vidyā vā cakrameva vā ।। śaktisthaṃ naiva taṃ tatra vibhāgastvoṃnamontagaḥ ।
asmiṃstattvodaye tasmādahorātrastriśastriśaḥ ।। vibhajyate vibhāgaśca punareva triśastriśaḥ । pūrvodaye tu viśramya dvitīyenollasedyadā ।। viśeccārdhardhikāyogāttadoktārdhodayo bhavet ।
yadā pūrṇodayātmā tu samaḥ kālastrike sphuret ।। praveśaviśrāntyullāse syātsvatryaṃśodayastadā । etyeṣa kālavibhavaḥ prāṇa eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। sa spade khe sa taccityāṃ tenāsyāṃ viśvaniṣṭhiatiḥ ।
ataḥ saṃvitpratiṣṭhānau yato viśvalayodayau ।। śaktyante adhvani tatspandāsaṃkhyātā vāstavī tataḥ । uktaṃ śrīmālinītantre gātre yatraiva kutracit ।। vikāra upajāyeta tattattvaṃ tattvamuttamam ।
prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ kālastadāviṣṭā ca yattanuḥ ।। dehe pratiṣṭhitasyāsya tato rūpaṃ nirūpyate । citspandaprāṇavṛttīnāmantyā yā sthūlatā suṣiḥ ।। sā nāḍīrūpatāmetya dehaṃ saṃtānayedimam ।
śrīsvacchande ata evoktaṃ yathā parṇaṃ svatantubhiḥ ।। vyāptaṃ tadvattanurdvāradvāribhāvena nāḍibhiḥ । pādāṅguṣṭhādikordhvasthabrahmakuṇḍalikāntagaḥ ।। kālaḥ samastaścaturaśītāvevāṅguleṣvitaḥ ।
dvādaśāntāvadhiṃ kiṃcitsūkṣmakālasthitiṃ viduḥ ।। ṣaṇṇavatyāmadhaḥ ṣaḍdvikramāccāṣṭottaraṃ śatam । atra madhyamasaṃcāriprāṇodayalayāntare ।। viśve sṛṣṭilayāste tu citrā vāyvantarakramāt ।
ityeṣa sūkṣmaparimarśanaśīlanīyaścakrodayo anubhavaśāstradṛśā mayoktaḥ ।। deśādhvano apyatha samāsavikāsayogātsaṃgīyate vidhirayaṃ śivaśāstradṛṣṭaḥ ।। vicārito ayaṃ kālādhvā kriyāśaktimayaḥ prabhoḥ । mūrtivaicitryajastajjo deśādhvātha nirūpyate ।।
adhvā samasta evāyaṃ cinmātre saṃpratiṣṭhitaḥ । yattatra nahi viśrāntaṃ tannabhaḥkusumāyate ।। saṃviddvāreṇa tatsṛṣṭe śūnye dhiyi marutsu ca । nāḍīcakrānucakreṣu barhirdehe adhvasaṃsthitiḥ ।।
tatrādhvaivaṃ nirūpyo ayaṃ yatastatprakriyākramam । anusaṃdadhadeva drāg yogī bhairavatāṃ vrajet ।। didṛkṣayaiva sarvārthān yadā vyāpyāvatiṣṭhate । tadā kiṃ bahunoktena ityuktaṃ spandaśāsane ।।
jñātvā samastamadhvānaṃ tadīśeṣu vilāpayet । tān dehaprāṇadhīcakre pūrvavad gālayetkramāt ।। tatsamastaṃ svasaṃvittau sā saṃvidbharitātmikā । upāsyamānā saṃsārasāgarapralayānalaḥ ।।
śrīmahīkṣottare caitānadhveśān gururabravīt । brahmānantātpradhānāntaṃ viṣṇuḥ puṃsaḥ kalāntagam ।। rudro granthau ca māyāyāmīśaḥ sādākhyagocare । anāśritaḥ śivastasmādvyāptā tadvyāpakaḥ paraḥ ।।
evaṃ śivatvamāpannamiti matvā nyarūpyata । na prakriyāparaṃ jñānamiti svacchandaśāsane ।। triśiraḥśāsane bodho mūlamadhyāgrakalpitaḥ । ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasaṃrambhaḥ smṛtirbhedavikalpanā ।।
avyāhatavibhāgo asmibhāvo mūlaṃ tu bodhagam । samastatattvabhāvo ayaṃ svātmanyevāvibhāgakaḥ ।। bodhamadhyaṃ bhavetkiṃcidādhārādheyalakṣaṇam । tattvabhedavibhāgena svabhāvasthitilakṣaṇam ।।
bodhāgraṃ tattu vidbodhaṃ nistaraṅgaṃ bṛhatsukham । saṃvidekātmatānītabhūtabhāvapurādikaḥ ।। avyavacchinnasaṃvittirbhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ । śrīdevyāyāmale coktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasundaram ।।
adhvānaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ dhyāyansadyaḥ śivamayo bhavet । yadyapyamuṣya nāthasya saṃvittyanatirekiṇaḥ ।। pūrṇasyordhvādimadhyāntavyavasthā nāsti vāstavī । tathāpi pratipattṝṇāṃ pratipādayitustathā ।।
svasvarūpānusāreṇa madhyāditvādikalpanāḥ । tataḥ pramātṛsaṃkalpaniyamāt pārthivaṃ viduḥ ।। tattvaṃ sarvāntarālasthaṃ yatsarvāvaraṇairvṛtam । tadatra pārthive tattve kathyate bhuvanasthitiḥ ।।
netā kaṭāharudrāṇāmanantaḥ kāmasevinām । potārūḍho jalasyāntarmadyapānavighūrṇitaḥ ।। sa devaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyāyan nāgaiśca parivāritaḥ । kālāgrerbhuvanaṃ cordhve koṭiyojanamucchritam ।।
lokānāṃ bhasmasādbhāvabhayānnordhva sa vīkṣate । sa ca vyāptāpi viśvasya yasmātpluṣyannimāṃ bhuvam ।। narakebhyaḥ purā vyaktastenāsau tadadho mataḥ । daśa koṭyo vibhorjvālā tadardha śūnyamūrdhvataḥ ।।
tadūrdhve narakādhīśāḥ kramādduḥkhaikavedanāḥ । śdho madhye tadūrdhve ca sthitā bhedāntarairvṛtāḥ ।। avīcikumbhīpākākhyarauravāsteṣvanukramāt । ekādaśaikādaśa ca daśetyantaḥ śarāgni tat ।।
pratyekameṣāmekonā koṭirucchritirantaram । lakṣamatra khavedāsyasaṃkhyānāmantarā sthitiḥ ।। kūṣmāṇḍa ūrdhve lakṣonakoṭisthānastadīśitā । śāstraviruddhācaraṇāt kṛṣṇaṃ ye karma vidadhate ।।
tatra bhīmairlokapuruṣaiḥ pīḍyante bhogaparyantam । ye sakṛdapi parameśaṃ śivamekāgreṇa cetasā śaraṇam ।। yānti na te narakayujaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ teṣāṃ sukhālpatādāyi । sahasranavakotsedhamekāntaramatha kramāt ।।
pātālāṣṭakamekaikamaṣṭame hāṭakaḥ prabhuḥ । pratilokaṃ niyuktātmā śrīkaṇṭho haṭhato bahūḥ ।। siddhīrdadātyasāvevaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane । vratino ye cikarmasthā niṣiddhācārakāriṇaḥ ।।
dīkṣitā api ye luptasamayā naca kurvate । prāyaścittāṃstathā tatsthā vāmācārasya dūṣakāḥ ।। devāgnidravyavṛttyaṃśajīvinaścottamasthitāḥ । adhaḥsthagāruḍādyanyamantrasevāparāyaṇāḥ ।।
te hāṭakavibhoragre kiṅkarā vividhātmakāḥ । te tu tatrāpi deveśaṃ bhaktyā cetparyupāsate ।। tadīśatattve līyante kramācca parame śive । anyathā ye tu vartante tadbhoganiratātmakāḥ ।।
te kālavahnisaṃtāpadīnākrandaparāyaṇāḥ । guṇatattve nilīyante tataḥ sṛṣṭimukhe punaḥ ।। pātyante mātṛbhirghorayātanaughapurassaram । adhamādhamadeheṣu nijakarmānurūpataḥ ।।
mānuṣānteṣu tatrāpi kecinmantravidaḥ kramāt । mucyante anye tu badhyante pūrvakṛtyānusārataḥ ।। ityeṣa gaṇavṛttānto nāmnā hulahulādinā । proktaṃ bhagavatā śrīmadānandādhikaśāsane ।।
pātālordhve sahasrāṇi viṃśatirbhūkaṭāhakaḥ । siddhātantre tu pātālapṛṣṭhe yakṣīsamāvṛtam ।। bhadrakālyāḥ puraṃ yatra tābhiḥ krīḍanti sādhakāḥ । tatastamastaptabhūmistataḥśūnyaṃ tato ahayaḥ ।।
etāni yātanāsthānaṃ gurumantrādidūṣiṇām । tato bhūmyūrdhva [madhya] to meruḥ sahasrāṇi sa ṣoḍaśa ।। magnastanmūlavistārastaddvayenordhvavistṛtiḥ । sahasrābdhivasūcchrāyo haimaḥ sarvāmarālayaḥ ।।
madhyordhvādhaḥ samudvṛttaśarāvacaturaśrakaḥ । bhairavīyaṃ ca talliṅgaṃ dharaṇī cāsya pīṭhikā ।। sarve devā nilīnā hi tatra tatpūjitaṃ sadā । madhye merusabhā dhātustadīśadiśi ketanam ।।
jyotiṣkaśikharaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śrīkaṇṭhāṃśaśca sa prabhuḥ । avaruhya sahasrāṇi manovatyāścaturdaśa ।। cakravāṭaścaturdikko meruratra tu lokapāḥ । amarāvatikendrasya pūrvasyāṃ dakṣiṇena tām ।।
atsaraḥsiddhasādhyāstāmuttareṇa vināyakāḥ । tejovatī svadiśyagneḥ purī tāṃ paścimena tu ।। viśvedevā viśvakarmā kramāttadanugāśca ye । yāmyāṃ saṃyamanī tāṃ tu paścimena kramāt sthitāḥ ।।
mātṛnandā svasaṃkhyātā rudrāstatsādhakāstathā । kṛṣṇāṅgārā nirṛtiśca tāṃ pūrveṇa piśācakāḥ ।। rakṣāṃsi siddhagandharvāstūttareṇottareṇa tām । vāruṇī śuddhavatyākhyā bhūtaugho dakṣiṇena tām ।।
uttareṇottareṇaināṃ vasuvidyādharāḥ kramāt । vāyorgandhavatī tasyā dakṣiṇe kinnarāḥ punaḥ ।। vīṇāsarasvatī devī nāradastumburustathā । mahodayendorguhyāḥ syuḥ paścime asyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
kuberaḥ karmadevāśca tathā tatsādhakā api । yaśasvinī maheśasya tasyāḥ paścimato hariḥ ।। dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇe brahmāśvinau dhanvantariḥ kramāt । mairave cakravāṭe asminnevaṃ mukhyāḥ puro aṣṭadhā ।।
antarālagatāstvanyāḥ punaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ । iṣṭāpūrtaratāḥ puṇye varṣeye bhārate narāḥ ।। te merugāḥ sakṛcchambhuṃ ye vārcanti yathocitam । meroḥ pradakṣiṇāpyodagdikṣu viṣkambhaparvatāḥ ।।
mandaro gandhamādaśca vipulo atha supārśvakaḥ । sitapītanīlaraktāste kramātpādaparvatāḥ ।। etairbhuvamavaṣṭabhya merustiṣṭhati niścalaḥ । caitrarathanandanākhye vaiśrājaṃ pitṛvanaṃ vanānyāhuḥ ।।
raktodamānasasitaṃ bhadraṃ caitaccatuṣṭayaṃ sarasām । vṛkṣāḥ kadambajambvaśvatthanyagrodhakāḥ kramaśaḥ ।। eṣu ca caturṣvacaleṣu trayaṃ trayaṃ kramaśa etadāmnātam । mervadho lavaṇābdhyantaṃ jambudvīpaḥ samantataḥ ।।
lakṣamātraḥ sa navadhā jāto maryādaparvataiḥ । niṣadho hemakūṭaśca himavāndakṣiṇe trayaḥ ।। lakṣaṃ sahasranavatistadaśītiriti kramāt । nīlaḥ śvetastriśṛṅgaśca tāvantaḥ savyataḥ punaḥ ।।
meroḥ ṣaḍete maryādācalāḥ pūrvāparāyatāḥ । pūrvato mālyavānpaścādgandhamādanasaṃjñitaḥ ।। savyottarāyatau tau tu catustriṃśatsahasrakau । aṣṭāvete tato apyanyau dvau dvau pūrvādiṣu kramāt ।।
jāṭharaḥ kūṭahimavadyātrajārudhiśṛṅgiṇaḥ । evaṃ sthito vibhāgo atra varṣasiddhyai nirūpyate ।। samantāccakravāṭādho anarkendu caturaśrakam । sahasranavavistīrṇamilākhyaṃ trimukhāyuṣam ।।
meroḥ paścimato gandhamādo yastasya paścime । ketumālaṃ kulādrīṇāṃ saptakena vibhūṣitam ।। meroḥ pūrva mālyavānyo bhadrāśvastasya pūrvataḥ । sahasradaśakāyustatsapañcakulaparvatam ।।
pūrvapaścimataḥ savyottarataśca kramādime । dvātriṃśacca catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi nirūpite ।। merorudak śṛṅgavānyastadbahiḥ kuruvarṣakam । cāpavannavasāhasramāyustatra trayodaśa ।।
kuruvarṣasyottare atha vāyavye abdhau kramāccharāḥ । daśa ceti sahasrāṇi dvīpau candro atha bhadrakaḥ ।। yau śvetaśṛṅgiṇau merorvāme madhye hiraṇmayam । tayornavakavistīrṇamāyuścārdhatrayodaśa ।।
tatra vai vāmataḥ śvetanīlayo ramyako antare । sahasranavavistīrṇamāyurdvādaśa tāni ca ।। merordakṣiṇato hemaniṣadhau yau tadantare । haryākhyaṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam ।।
tatraiva dakṣiṇe hemahimavaddvitayāntare । kainnaraṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam ।। tatraiva dakṣiṇe merorhimavānyasya dakṣiṇe । bhārataṃ navasāhasraṃ cāpavatkarmabhogabhūḥ ।।
ilāvṛtaṃ ketubhadraṃ kuruhairaṇyaramyakam । harikinnaravarṣe ca bhogabhūrna tu karmabhūḥ ।। atra bāhulyataḥ karmabhūbhāvo atrāpyakarmaṇām । paśūnāṃ karmasaṃskāraḥ syāttādṛgdṛḍhasaṃskṛteḥ ।।
saṃbhavantyapyasaṃskārā bhārate anyatra cāpi hi । dṛḍhaprāktanasaṃskārādīśecchātaḥ śubhāśubham ।। sthānāntare api karmāsti dṛṣṭaṃ tacca purātane । tatra tretā sadā kālo bhārate tu caturyugam ।।
bhārate navakhaṇḍaṃ ca sāmudreṇāmbhasātra ca । sthalaṃ pañcaśatī tadvajjalaṃ ceti vibhajyate ।। indraḥ kaśerustāmrābho nāgīyaḥ prāggabhastimān । saumyagāndharvavārāhāḥ kanyākhyaṃ cāsamudrataḥ ।।
kanyādvīpe ca navame dakṣiṇenābdhimadhyagāḥ । upadvīpāḥ ṣaṭ kulādrisaptakena vibhūṣite ।। aṅgayavamalayaśaṅkuḥ kumudavarāhau ca malayago agastya । tatraiva ca trikūṭe laṅkā ṣaḍamī hyupadvīpāḥ ।।
dvīpopadvīpagāḥ prāyo mlecchā nānāvidhā janāḥ । muktākāñcanaratnāḍhyā iti śrīruruśāsane ।। bhārate yatkṛtaṃ karma kṣapitaṃ vāpyavīcitaḥ । śivāntaṃ tena muktirvā kanyākhye tu viśeṣataḥ ।।
mahākālādikā rudrakoṭiratraiva bhārate । gaṅgādipañcaśatikā janma tenātra durlabham ।। anyavarṣeṣu paśuvad bhogātkarmātivāhanam । prāpyaṃ manorathātītamapi bhāratajanmanām ।।
nānāvarṇāśramācārasukhaduḥkhavicitratā । kanyādvīpe yatastena karmabhūḥ seyamuttamā ।। puṃsā sitāsitānyatra kurvatāṃ kila siddhyataḥ । parāparau svarnirayāviti rauravavārtike ।।
evaṃ meroradho jambūrabhito yaḥ sa vistarāt । syāt saptadaśadhā khaṇḍairnavabhistu samāsataḥ ।। manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyāsan sutā daśa tatastrayaḥ । prāvrajannatha jambvākhye rājā yo agnīdhranāmakaḥ ।।
tasyābhavannava sutāstato ayaṃ navakhaṇḍakaḥ । nābhiryo navamastasya naptā bharata ārṣabhiḥ ।। tasyāṣṭau tanayāḥ sākaṃ kanyayā navamoṃ aśakaḥ । bhuktaistairnavadhā tasmāllakṣayojanamātrakāt ।।
lakṣaikamātro lavaṇastadbāhye asya puro adrayaḥ । ṛṣabho dundubhirdhūmraḥ kaṅkadroṇendavo hyudak ।। varāhanandanāśokāḥ paścāt sahabalāhakau । dakṣiṇa cakramainākau vāḍavo antastayoḥ sthitaḥ ।।
abdherdakṣiṇataḥ khākṣisahasrātikramād giriḥ । vidyutvāṃstrisahasrocchridāyāmo atra phalāśinaḥ ।। maladigdhā dīrghakeśaśmaśravo gosadharmakāḥ । nagnāḥ saṃvatsarāśītijīvinastṛṇabhojinaḥ ।।
niryantrāṇi sadā tatra dvārāṇi bilasiddhaye । ityetad gurubhirgītaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane ।। itthaṃ ya eṣa lavaṇasamudraḥ pratipāditaḥ । tadbahiḥ ṣaḍamī dvīpāḥ pratyekaṃ svārṇavairvṛtāḥ ।।
kramadviguṇitāḥ ṣaḍbhirmanuputrairadhiṣṭhitāḥ । śākakuśakrauñcāḥ śalmaligomedhābjamiti ṣaḍdvīpāḥ । kṣīradadhisarpiraikṣavamadirāmadhurāmbukāḥ ṣaḍambudhayaḥ ।। medhātithirvapuṣmāñjyotiṣmāndyutimatā havī rājā ।
saṃvara iti śākādiṣu jambudvīpe nyarūpi cāgnīdhraḥ ।। girisaptakaparikalpitatāvatkhaṇḍāstu pañca śākādyāḥ । puṣkarasaṃjño dvidalo hariyamavaruṇendavo atra pūrvādau ।। tripañcāśacca lakṣāṇi dvikoṭyayutapañcakam ।
svādvarṇavāntaṃ mervardhādyojananāmiyaṃ pramā ।। saptamajaladherbāhye haimī bhūḥ koṭidaśakamatha lakṣam । ucchrityā vistārādayutaṃ loketarācalaḥ kathitaḥ ।। lokālokadigaṣṭaka saṃsthaṃ rudrāṣṭakaṃ salokeśam ।
kevalamityapi kecillokālokāntare ravirna bahiḥ ।। pitṛdevapathāvasyodagdakṣiṇagau svajātpare vīthyau । bhānoruttaradakṣiṇamayanadvayametadeva kathayanti ।। udayāstamayāvitthaṃ sūryasya paribhāvayet ।।
ardharātro amarāvatyāṃ yāmyāyāmastameva ca । madhyandinaṃ tadvāruṇyāṃ saumye sūryodayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। udayo yo amarāvatyāṃ so ardharātro yamālaye । ke astaṃ saumye ca madhyāhna itthaṃ sūryagatāgate ।।
pañcatriṃ śatkoṭisaṃkhyā lakṣāṇyekonaviṃśatiḥ । catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi dhvāntaṃ lokācalādbahiḥ ।। saptasāgaramānastu garbhodākhyaḥ samudrarāṭ । lokālokasya parato yadgarbhe nikhilaiva bhūḥ ।।
siddhātantre atra garbhābdhestīre kauśeyasaṃjñitam । maṇḍalaṃ garuḍastatra siddhapakṣasamāvṛtaḥ ।। krīḍantiṃ parvatāgre te nava cātra kulādrayaḥ । tata uṣṇodakāstriṃśannadyaḥpātālagāstataḥ ।।
caturdiṅnaimirodyānaṃ yoginīsevitaṃ sadā । tato merustato nāgā meghā hemāṇḍakaṃ tataḥ ।। brahmaṇo aṇḍakaṭāhena merorardhena koṭayaḥ । pañcāśadevaṃ daśasu dicu bhūrlokasaṃjñitam ।।
paśukhagamṛgatarumānuṣasarīsṛpaiḥ ṣaḍbhireṣa bhūrlokaḥ । vyāptaḥ piśācarakṣogandharvāṇāṃ sayakṣāṇām ।। vidyābhṛtāṃ ca kiṃ vā bahunā sarvasya bhūtasargasya । abhimānato yatheṣṭaṃ bhogasthānaṃ nivāsaśca ।।
bhuvarlokastathā tvārkāllakṣamekaṃ tadantare । daśa vāyupathāste ca pratyekamayutāntarāḥ ।। ādyo vāyupathastatra vitataḥ paricarcyate । pañcāśadyojanordhve syādṛtarddhirnāma mārutaḥ ।।
āpyāyakaḥ sa jantūnāṃ tataḥ prācetaso bhavet । pañcāśadyojanādūrdhva tasmādūrdhva śatena tu ।। senānīvāyuratraite mūkameghāstaḍinmucaḥ । ye mahyāḥ krośamātreṇa tiṣṭhanti jalavarṣiṇaḥ ।।
tebhya ūrdhva śatānmeghā bhekādiprāṇivarṣiṇaḥ । pañcāśadūrdhvamogho atra viṣavāripravarṣiṇaḥ ।। meghāḥ skandodbhavāścānye piśācā oghamārute । tataḥ pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ syurmeghā mārakasaṃjñakāḥ ।।
tatra sthāne mahādevajanmānaste vināyakāḥ । ye haranti kṛtaṃ karma narāṇāmakṛtātmanām ।। pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṅko vāyuratropalāmbudāḥ । vidyādharādhamāścātra vajrāṅke saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
ye vidyāpauruṣe ye ca śmaśānādiprasādhane । mṛtāstatsiddhisiddhāste vajrāṃke maruti sthitāḥ ।। pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṃkādvaidyuto aśanivarṣiṇaḥ । abdā apsarasaścātra ye ca puṇyakṛto narāḥ ।।
bhṛgau vahnau jale ye ca saṃgrāme cānivartinaḥ । gograhe vadhyamokṣe vā mṛtāste vaidyute sthitāḥ ।। vaidyutādraivatastāvāṃstatra puṣṭivahāmbudāḥ । ūrdhvaṃ ca rogāmbumucaḥ saṃvartāstadanantare ।।
rocanāñjanabhasmādisiddhāstatraiva raivate । krodhodakamucāṃ sthānaṃ viṣāvartaḥ sa mārutaḥ ।। pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ tatraiva durdinābdā hutāśajāḥ । vidyādharaviśeṣāśca tathā ye parameśvaram ।।
gāndharveṇa sadārcanti viṣāvarte atha te sthitāḥ । viṣāvartācchatādūrdhva durjayaḥ śvāsasaṃbhavaḥ ।। brahmaṇo atra sthitā meghāḥ pralaye vātakāriṇaḥ । puṣkarābdā vāyugamā gandharvāśca parāvahe ।।
jīmūtameghāstatsaṃjñāstathā vidyādharottamāḥ । ye ca rūpavratā lokā āvahe te pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। mahāvahe tvīśakṛtāḥ prajāhitakarāmbudāḥ । mahāparivahe meghāḥ kapālotthā maheśituḥ ।।
mahāparivahānto ayamṛtarddheḥ prāṅmarutpathaḥ । agnikanyā mātaraśca rudraśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। dvitīye tatpare siddhacāraṇā nijakarmajāḥ । turye devāyudhānyaṣṭau diggajāḥ pañcame punaḥ ।।
ṣaṣṭhe garutmānanyasmiṅgaṅgānyatra vṛṣo vibhuḥ । dakṣastu navame brahmaśaktyā samadhiti[ni]ṣṭhitaḥ ।। daśame vasavo rudrā ādityāśca marutpathe । navayojanasāhasro vigraho arkasya maṇḍalam ।।
triguṇaṃ jñānaśaktiḥ sā tapatyarkatayā prabhoḥ । svarlokastu bhuvarlokāddhruvāntaṃ paribhāṣyate ।। sūryāllakṣeṇa śītāṃśuḥ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya sā । candrāllakṣeṇa nākṣatraṃ tato lakṣadvayena tu ।।
pratyekaṃ bhaumataḥ sūryasutānte pañcakaṃ viduḥ । saurāllakṣeṇa saptarṣivargastasmāddhruvastathā ।। brahmaivāpararūpeṇa brahmasthāne dhruvo acalaḥ । medhībhūto vimānānāṃ sarveṣāmupari dhruvaḥ ।।
atra baddhāni sarvāṇyapyūhyante anilamaṇḍale । svassapta mārutaskandhā āmeghādyāḥ pradhānataḥ ।। itaśca kratuhotrādi kṛtvā jñānavivarjitāḥ । svaryānti tatkṣaye lokaṃ mānuṣyaṃ puṇyaśeṣataḥ ।।
evaṃ bhūmerdhruvāntaṃ syāllakṣāṇi daśa pañca ca । dve koṭī pañca cāśītirlakṣāṇi svargato mahān ।। mārkaṇḍādyā ṛṣimunisiddhāstatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ । nivartitādhikārāśca devā mahati saṃsthitāḥ ।।
mahāntarāle tatrānye tvadhikārabhujo janāḥ । aṣṭau koṭyo mahallokājjano atra kapilādayaḥ ।। tiṣṭhanti sādhyāstatraiva bahavaḥ sukhabhāginaḥ । janāttaporkakoṭyo atra sanakādyā mahādhiyaḥ ।।
prajāpatīnāṃ tatrādhikāro brahmātmajanmanām । brahmālayastu tapasaḥ satyaḥ ṣoḍaśa koṭayaḥ ।। tatra sthitaḥ sa svayambhūrviśvamāviṣkarotyadaḥ । satye vedāstathā cānye karmadhyānena bhāvitāḥ ।।
ānandaniṣṭhāstatrordhvekoṭirvairiñcamāsanam । brahmāsanātkoṭiyugmaṃ puraṃ viṣṇornirūpitam ।। dhyānapūjājapairviṣṇorbhaktā gacchanti tatpadam । vaiṣṇavātsaptakoṭībhirbhuvanaṃ parameśituḥ ।।
rudrasya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakarturbrahmāṇḍavartmani । dīkṣājñānavihīnā ye liṅgārādhanatatparāḥ ।। te yāntyaṇḍāntare raudraṃ puraṃ nādhaḥ kadācana । tatsthāḥ sarve śivaṃ yānti rudrāḥ śrīkaṇṭhadīkṣitāḥ ।।
adhikārakṣaye sākaṃ rudrakanyāgaṇena te । puraṃ puraṃ ca rudrordhvamuttarottaravṛddhitaḥ ।। brahmāṇḍādhaśca rudrordhva daṇḍapāṇeḥ puraṃ sa ca । śivecchayā dṛṇātyaṇḍaṃ mokṣamārga karoti ca ।।
śarvarudrau bhīmabhavāvugro devo mahānatha । īśāna iti bhūrlokāt sapta lokeśvarāḥ śivāḥ ।। sthūlairviśeṣairārabdhāḥ sapta lokāḥ pare punaḥ । sūkṣmairiti guruścaiva rurau samyaṅnyarūpayat ।।
ye brahmaṇādisarge svaśarīrānnirmitāḥ prabhūtākhyāḥ । sthūlāḥ pañca viśeṣāḥ saptāmī tanmayā lokāḥ ।। parato liṅgādhāraiḥ sūkṣmaistanmātrajairmahābhūtaiḥ । lokānāmāvaraṇairviṣṭabhya parasperaṇa gandhādyaiḥ ।।
kālāgnerdaṇḍapāṇyantamaṣṭānavatikoṭayaḥ । ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṭāho aṇḍe sa ghanaḥ koṭiyojanam ।। pañcāśatkoṭayaścordhvaṃ bhūpṛṣṭhādadharaṃ tathā । evaṃ koṭiśataṃ bhūḥ syāt sauvarṇastaṇḍulastataḥ ।।
śatarudrāvadhirhuphaṭ bhedayettattu duḥśamam । pratidikkaṃ daśa daśetyevaṃ rudraśataṃ bahiḥ ।। brahmāṇḍādhārakaṃ tacca svaprabhāveṇa sarvataḥ । aṇḍasvarūpaṃ gurubhiścoktaṃ śrīrauravādiṣu ।।
vyakterabhimukhībhūtaḥ pracyutaḥ śaktirūpataḥ । āvāpavānanirbhakto vastupiṇḍo aṇḍa ucyate ।। tamoleśānuviddhasya kapālaṃ sattvamuttaram । rajo anuviddhaṃ nirmṛṣṭaṃ sattvamasyādharaṃ tamaḥ ।।
vastupiṇḍa iti proktaṃ śivaśaktisamūhabhāk । aṇḍaḥ syāditi tadvyaktau saṃmukhībhāva ucyate ।। tathāpi śivamagnānāṃ śaktīnāmaṇḍatā bhavet । tadartha vākyamaparaṃ tā hi na cyutaśaktitaḥ ।।
tanvakṣādau mā prasāṅkṣīdaṇḍateti padāntaram । tanvakṣādiṣu naivāste kasyāpyāvāpanaṃ yataḥ ।। tanvakṣasamudāyatve kathamekatvamityataḥ । anirbhakta iti proktaṃ sājātyaparidarśakam ।।
vināpi vastupiṇḍākhyapadenaikaikaśo bhavet । tattveṣvaṇḍasvabhāvatvaṃ nanvevamapi kiṃ na tat ।। guṇatanmātrabhūtaughamaye tattve prasajyate । ucyate vastuśabdena tanvakṣabhuvanātmakam ।।
rūpamuktaṃ yatastena tatsamūho aṇḍa ucyate । bhavecca tatsamūhatvaṃ patyurviśvavapurbhṛtaḥ ।। tadartha bhedakānyanyānyupāttānīti darśitam । tāvanmātrāsvavasthāsu māyādhīne adhvamaṇḍale ।।
mā bhūdaṇḍatvamityāhuranye bhedakayojanam । itthamuktaviriñcāṇḍamṛto rudrāḥ śataṃ hi yat ।। teṣāṃ sve patayo rudrā ekādaśa mahārciṣaḥ । ananto atha kapālyāgniryamanairṛtakau balaḥ ।।
śīghro nidhīśo vidyeśaḥ śambhuḥ savīrabhadrakaḥ । madhu madhukṛtaḥ kadambaṃ kesarajālāni yadvadāvṛṇate ।। tadvatte śivarudrā brahmāṇḍamasaṃkhyaparivārāḥ । śarāṣṭaniyutaṃ koṭirityeṣāṃ sanniveśanam ।।
śrīkaṇṭhādhiṣṭhitāste ca sṛjanti saṃharanti ca । īśvaratvaṃ diviṣadāmiti rauravavārtike ।। siddhātantre tu hemāṇḍācchatakoṭerbahiḥ śatam । aṇḍānāṃ kramaśo dvidviguṇaṃ rūpyādiyojitam ।।
teṣu krameṇa brahmāṇaḥ saṃsyurdviguṇajīvitāḥ । kṣīyante kramaśaste ca tadante tattvamammayam ।। dharāto atra jalādi syāduttarottarataḥ kramāt । daśadhāhaṅkṛtāntaṃ dhīstasyāḥ syācchatadhā tataḥ ।।
sahasradhā vyaktamataḥ pauṃsnaṃ daśasahasradhā । niyatirlakṣadhā tasmāttasyāstu daśalakṣadhā ।। kalāntaṃ koṭidhā tasmānmāyā viddaśakoṭidhā । īśvaraḥ śatakoṭiḥ syāttasmātkoṭisahasradhā ।।
sādākhyaṃ vyaśnute tacca śaktirvṛndena saṃkhyayā । vyāpinī sarvamadhvānaṃ vyāpyadevī vyavasthitā ।। aprameyaṃ tataḥ śuddhaṃ śivatattvaṃ paraṃ viduḥ । jalādeḥ śivatattvāntaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ kenacicchivāt ।।
ṛte tataḥ śivajñānaṃ paramaṃ mokṣakāraṇam । tathā cāha mahādevaḥ śrīmatsvacchandaśāsane ।। nānyathā mokṣamāyāti paśurjñānaśatairapi । śivajñānaṃ na bhavati dīkṣāmaprāpya śāṅkarīm ।।
prāktanī pārameśī sā pauruṣeyī ca sā punaḥ । śatarudrordhvato bhadrakālyā nīlaprabhaṃ jayam ।। na yajñadānatapasā prāpyaṃ kālyāḥ puraṃ jayam । tadbhaktāstatra gacchanti tanmaṇḍalasudīkṣitāḥ ।।
nirbījadīkṣayā mokṣaṃ dadāti parameśvarī । vidyeśāvaraṇe dīkṣāṃ yāvatīṃ kurute nṛṇām ।। tāvatīṃ gatimāyānti bhuvane atra niveśitāḥ । tataḥ koṭyā vīrabhadro yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ ।।
vijayākhyaṃ puraṃ cāsya ye smaranto maheśvaram । jaleṣu maruṣu cāgnau śiraśchedena vā mṛtāḥ ।। te yānti bodhamaiśānaṃ vīrabhadraṃ mahādyutim । vairabhadrordhvataḥ koṭirviṣkambhādvistṛtaṃ tridhā ।।
rudrāṇḍaṃ sālilaṃ tvaṇḍaṃ śakracāpākṛti sthitam । ā vīrabhadrabhuvanādbhadrakālyālayāttathā ।। trayodaśabhiranyaiśca bhuvanairupaśobhitam । tato bhuvaḥ sahādreḥ pūrgandhatanmātradhāraṇāt ।।
mṛtā gacchanti tāṃ bhūmiṃ dharitryāḥ paramāṃ budhāḥ । abdheḥ puraṃ tatastvāpyaṃ rasatanmātradhāraṇāt ।। tataḥ śriyaḥ puraṃ rudrakrīḍāvataraṇeṣvatha । prayāgādau śrīgirau ca viśeṣānmaraṇena tat ।।
sārasvataṃ puraṃ tasmācchabdabrahmavidāṃ padam । rudrocitāstā mukhyatvādrudrebhyo anyāstathā sthitāḥ ।। pureṣu bahudhā gaṅgā devādau śrīḥ sarasvatī । lakulādyamareśāntā aṣṭāvapsu surādhipāḥ ।।
tatastu taijasaṃ tattvaṃ śivāgneratra saṃsthitiḥ । te cainaṃ vahnimāyānti vāhnīṃ ye dhāraṇāṃ śritāḥ ।। bhairavādiharīndvantaṃ taijase nāyakāṣṭakam । prāṇasya bhuvanaṃ vāyordaśadhā daśadhā tu tat ।।
dhyātvā tyaktvātha vā prāṇān kṛtvā tatraiva dhāraṇām । taṃ viśanti mahātmāno vāyubhūtāḥ khamūrtayaḥ ।। bhīmādigayaparyantamaṣṭakaṃ vāyutattvagam । khatattve bhuvanaṃ vyomnaḥ prāpyaṃ tadvyomadhāraṇāt ।।
vastrāpadāntaṃ sthāṇvādi vyomatattve surāṣṭakam । adīkṣitā ye bhūteṣu śivatattvābhimāninaḥ ।। jñānahīnā api prauḍhadhāraṇāste aṇḍato bahiḥ । dharābdhitejo anilakhapuragā dīkṣitāśca vā ।।
tāvatsaṃskārayogārthaṃ na paraṃ padamīhitum । tathāvidhāvatāreṣu mṛtāścāyataneṣu ye ।। tatpadaṃ te samāsādya kramādyānti śivātmatām । punaḥ punaridaṃ coktaṃ śrīmaddevyākhyayāmale ।।
śrīkāmikāyāṃ kaśmīravarṇane coktavānvibhuḥ । sureśvarīmahādhāmni ye mriyante ca tatpure ।। brāhmaṇādyāḥ saṅkarāntāḥ paśavaḥ sthāvarāntagāḥ । rudrajātaya evaite ityāha bhagavāñchivaḥ ।।
ākāśāvaraṇādūrdhvamahaṅkārādadhaḥ priye । tanmātrādimano antānāṃ purāṇi śivaśāsane ।। pañcavarṇayutaṃ gandhatanmātramaṇḍalaṃ mahat । ācchādya yojanānekakoṭibhiḥ sthitamantarā ।।
evaṃ rasādimātrāṇāṃ maṇḍalāni svavarṇata । śarvo bhavaḥ paśupatirīśo bhīma iti kramāt ।। tanmātreśā yadicchātaḥ śabdādyāḥ khādikāriṇaḥ । tataḥ sūryenduvedānāṃ maṇḍalāni vibhurmahān ।।
ugraścetyeṣu patayastebhyo arkendū sayājakau । ityaṣṭau tanavaḥ śaṃbhoryāḥ parāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। aparā brahmaṇo aṇḍe tā vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitāḥ । kalpe kalpe prasūyante dharādyāstābhya eva tu ।।
tato vāgādikarmākṣayuktaṃ karaṇamaṇḍalam । agnīndraviṣṇumitrāḥ sabrahmāṇasteṣu nāyakāḥ ।। prakāśamaṇḍalaṃ tasmācchrutaṃ buddhyakṣapañcakam । digvidyudarkavaruṇabhuvaḥ śrotrādidevatāḥ ।।
prakāśamaṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sthitaṃ pañcārthamaṇḍalam । manomaṇḍalametasmāt somenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yataḥ ।। bāhyadeveṣvadhiṣṭhātā sāmyaiśvaryasukhātmakaḥ । manodevastato divyaḥ somo vibhurudīritaḥ ।।
tato api sakalākṣāṇāṃ yonerbuddhyakṣajanmanaḥ । sthūlādicchagalāntāṣṭayuktaṃ cāhaṅkṛteḥ puram ।। buddhitattvaṃ tato devayonyaṣṭakapurādhipam । paiśācaprabhṛtibrāhmaparyantaṃ tacca kīrtitam ।।
etāni devayonīnāṃ sthānānyeva purāṇyataḥ । avatīryātmajanmānaṃ dhyāyantaḥ saṃbhavanti te ।। parameśaniyogācca codyamānāśca māyayā । niyāmitā niyatyā ca brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।
vyajyante tena sargādau nāmarūpairanekadhā । svāṃśanaiva mahātmāno na tyajanti svaketanam ।। uktaṃ ca śivatanāvidamadhikārapadasthitena guruṇā naḥ । aṣṭānāṃ devānāṃ śaktyāvirbhāvayonayo hyetāḥ ।।
tanubhogāḥ punareṣāmadhaḥ prabhūtātmakāḥ proktāḥ । catvāriṃśattulyopabhogadeśādhikāni bhuvanāni ।। sādhanabhedātkevalamaṣṭakapañcakatayoktāni । etāni bhaktiyogaprāṇatyāgādigamyāni ।।
teṣūmāpatireva prabhuḥ svatantrendriyo vikaraṇātmā । taratamayogena tato api devayonyaṣṭakaṃ lakṣyaṃ tu ।। lokānāmakṣāṇi ca viṣayaparicchittikaraṇāni । gandhādermahadantādekādhikyena jātamaiśvaryam ।।
aṇimādyātmakamasminpaiśācādye viriñcānte । jñātvaivaṃ śodhayedbuddhiṃ sārdhaṃ puryaṣṭakendriyaiḥ ।। krodheśāṣṭakamānīlaṃ saṃvartādyaṃ tato viduḥ । tejoṣṭakaṃ balādhyakṣaprabhṛtikrodhanāṣtakāt ।।
akṛtādi tato buddhau yogāṣṭakamudāhṛtam । svacchandaśāsane tattu mūle śrīpūrvaśāsane ।। yogāṣṭakapade yattu some śraikaṇṭhameva ca । tato māyāpuraṃ bhūyaḥ śrīkaṇṭhasya ca kathyate ।।
tena dvitīyaṃ bhuvanaṃ tayoḥ pratyekamucyate । tatra māyāpuraṃ devyā yayā viśvamadhiṣṭhitam ।। pratikalpaṃ nāmabhedairbhaṇyate sā maheśvarī । umāpateḥ puraṃ paścānmātṛbhiḥ parivāritam ।।
śrīkaṇṭha eva parayā mūrtyomāpatirucyate । brāhmyaiśī skandajā hārī vārāhyaindrī saviccikā [carcikā] ।। pītā śuklā pītanīle nīlā śuklāruṇā kramāt । agnīśasaumyayāmyāpyapūrvanairṛtagāstu tāḥ ।।
