aṃśena mānuṣe loke dhātrā tā hyavatāritāḥ । svacchandāstāḥ parāścānyāḥ pare vyomni vyavasthitāḥ ।। svacchandaṃ tā niṣevante saptadheyamumā yataḥ । umāpatipurasyordhva sthitaṃ mūrtyaṣṭakaṃ param ।।
śarvādikaṃ yasya sṛṣṭirdharādyā yājakāntataḥ । tābhya īśānamūrtiryā sā merau saṃpratiṣṭhitā ।। śrīkaṇṭhaḥ sphaṭikādrau sā vyāptā tanvaṣṭakairjagat । ye yogaṃ saguṇaṃ śambhoḥ saṃyatāḥ paryupāsate ।।
tanmaṇḍalaṃ vā dṛṣṭvaiva muktadvaitā hṛtatrayāḥ । guṇānāmādharauttaryācchuddhāśuddhatvasaṃsthiteḥ ।। tāratamyācca yogasya bhedātphalavicitratā । tato bhogaphalāvāptibhedādbhedo ayamucyate ।।
mūrtyaṣṭakopariṣṭāttu suśivā dvādaśoditāḥ । vāmādyekaśivāntāste kuṅkumābhāḥ sutejasaḥ ।। tadūrdhva vīrabhadrākhyo maṇḍalādhipatiḥ sthitaḥ । yatta [sta] tsāyujyamāpannaḥ sa tena saha modate ।।
tato apyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ bhavet । buddhitattvamidaṃ proktaṃ devayonyaṣṭakāditaḥ ।। mahādevāṣṭakānte tad yogāṣṭakamihoditam । tatra śraikaṇṭhamuktaṃ yat tasyaivomāpatistathā ।।
mūrtayaḥ suśivā vīro mahādevāṣṭakaṃ vapuḥ । upariṣṭāddhiyo adhaśca prakṛterguṇasaṃjñitam ।। tattvaṃ tatra tu saṃkṣubdhā guṇāḥ prasuvate dhiyam । na vaiṣamyamanāpannaṃ kāraṇaṃ kāryasūtaye ।।
guṇasāmyatmikā tena prakṛtiḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet । nanvevaṃ sāpi saṃkṣobhaṃ vinā tānviṣamānguṇān ।। kathaṃ suvīta tatrādye kṣobhe syādanavasthitiḥ । sāṃkhyasya doṣa evāyaṃ yadi vā tena te guṇāḥ ।।
avyaktamiṣṭāḥ sāmyaṃ tu saṅgamātraṃ na cetarat । asmākaṃ tu svatantreśatathecchākṣobhasaṃgatam ।। avyaktaṃ buddhitattvasya kāraṇaṃ kṣobhitā guṇāḥ । nanu tattveśvarecchāto yaḥ kṣobhaḥ prakṛteḥ purā ।।
tadeva buddhitattvaṃ syāt kimanyaiḥ kalpitairguṇaiḥ । naitatkāraṇatārūpaparāmarśāvarodhi yat ।। kṣobhāntaraṃ tataḥ kārya bījocchūnāṅkurādivat । kramāttamorajaḥsattve gurūṇāṃ paṅktayaḥ sthitāḥ ।।
tisro dvātriṃśadekātastriṃśadapyekaviṃśatiḥ । svajñanayogabalataḥ krīḍanto daiśikottamāḥ ।। trinetrāḥ pāśanirmuktāste atrānugrahakāriṇaḥ । buddheśca guṇaparyantamubhe saptādhike śate ।।
rudrāṇāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca mukhyato anye tadantare । yogāṣṭakaṃ guṇaskandhe proktaṃ śivatanau punaḥ ।। yonīratītya gauṇe skandhe syuryogadātāraḥ । akṛtakṛtavibhuviriñcā harirguhaḥ kramavaśāttato devī ।।
karaṇānyaṇimādiguṇāḥ kāryāṇi pratyayaprapañcaśca । avyaktādutpannā guṇāśca sattvādayo amīṣām ।। dharmajñānavirāgānaiśvaryaṃ tatphalāni vividhāni । yacchanti guṇebhyo amī puruṣebhyo yogadātāraḥ ।।
tebhyaḥ parato bhuvanaṃ sattvādiguṇāsanasya devasya । sakalajagadekamāturbhartuḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthasya ।। yenomāguhanīlabrahmaṛbhukṣakṛtākṛtādibhuvaneṣu । graharūpiṇyā śaktyā prābhvyādhiṣṭhāni bhūtāni ।।
upasaṃjihīrṣuriha yaścaturānanapaṅkajaṃ samāviśya । dagdhvā caturo lokāñjanalokānnirmiṇoti punaḥ ।। yasyecchātaḥ sattvādiguṇaśarīrā visṛjati rudrāṇī । anukalpo rudrāṇyā vedī tatrejyate anukalpena ।।
paśupatirindropendraviriñcairatha tadupalambhato devaiḥ । gandharvayakṣarākṣasapitṛmunibhiścitritāstathā yāgāḥ ।। guṇānāṃ yatparaṃ sāmyaṃ tadavyaktaṃ guṇordhvataḥ । krodheśacaṇḍasaṃvartā jyotiḥpiṅgalasūrakau ।।
pañcāntakaikavīrau ca śikhodaścāṣṭa tatra te । gahanaṃ puruṣanidhānaṃ prakṛtirmūlaṃ pradhānamavyaktam ।। guṇakāraṇamityete māyāprabhavasya paryāyāḥ । yāvantaḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sahajāgantukamalopadigdhacitaḥ ।।
te sarve atra vinihitā rudrāśca tadutthabhogabhujaḥ । mūḍhavivṛttavilīnaiḥ karaṇaiḥ kecittu vikaraṇakāḥ ।। akṛtādhiṣṭhānatayā kṛtyāśaktāni mūḍhāni । pratiniyataviṣayabhāñji sphuṭāni śāstre vivṛttāni ।।
bhagnāni mahāpralaye sṛṣṭau notpāditāni līnāni । icchādhīnāni punarvikaraṇasaṃjñāni kāryamapyevam ।। puṃstattve tuṣṭinavakaṃ siddhayo aṣṭau ca tatpuraḥ । tāvatya evāṇimādibhuvanāṣṭakameva ca ।।
atattve tattvabuddhyā yaḥ santoṣastuṣṭiratra sā । heye apyādeyadhīḥ siddhiḥ tathā coktaṃ hi kāpilaiḥ ।। ādhyātmikāścatasraḥ prakṛtyupādānakālabhāgyākhyāḥ । pañca viṣayoparamato arjanarakṣāsaṅgasaṃkṣayavighātaiḥ ।।
ūhaḥ śabdo adhyayanaṃ duḥkhavighātāstrayaḥ suhṛtprāptiḥ । dānaṃ ca siddhayo aṣṭau siddheḥ pūrvo aṅkuśastrividhaḥ ।। aṇimādyūrdhvatastisraḥ paṅktayo guruśiṣyagāḥ । tatrāpi triguṇacchāyāyogāt tritvamudāhṛtam ।।
nāḍīvidyāṣṭakaṃ cordhvaṃ paṅktīnāṃ syādiḍādikam । puṃsi nādamayī śaktiḥ prasarākhyā ca yatsthitā ।। na hyakartā pumānkartuḥ kāraṇatvaṃ ca saṃsthitam । akartaryapi vā puṃsi sahakāritayā sthite ।।
śeṣakāryātmataiṣṭavyānyathā satkāryahānitaḥ । tasmāttathāvidhe kārye yā śaktiḥ puruṣasya sā ।। tāvanti rūpāṇyādāya pūrṇatāmadhigacchati । nāḍyaṣṭakordhve kathitaṃ vigrahāṣṭakamucyate ।।
kāryaṃ heturduḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ ca vijñānasādhyakaraṇāni । sādhanamiti vigrahatāyugaṣṭakaṃ bhavati puṃstattve ।। bhuvanaṃ dehadharmāṇāṃ daśānāṃ vigrahāṣṭakāt । ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmākalkākrudho guroḥ ।।
śuśrūṣāśaucasantoṣā ṛjuteti daśoditāḥ । puṃstattva eva gandhāntaṃ sthitaṃ ṣoḍaśakaṃ punaḥ ।। ārabhya dehapāśākhyaṃ puraṃ buddhiguṇāstataḥ । tatraivāṣṭāvahaṃkārastridhā kāmādikāstathā ।।
pāśā āgantukagāṇeśavaidyeśvarabheditāḥ । trividhāste sthitāḥ puṃsi mokṣamārgoparodhakāḥ ।। yatkiṃcitparamādvaitasaṃvitsvātantryasundarāt । parācchivāduktarūpādanyattatpāśa ucyate ।।
tadevaṃ puṃstvamāpanne pūrṇe api parameśvare । tatsvarūpāparijñānaṃ citraṃ hi puruṣāstataḥ ।। uktānuktāstu ye pāśāḥ paratantroktalakṣaṇāḥ । te puṃsi sarve tāṃstatra śodhayanmucyate bhavāt ।।
puṃsa ūrdhva tu niyatistatrasthāḥ śaṃkarā daśa । hemābhāḥ susitāḥ kālatattve tu daśa te śivāḥ ।। koṭiḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ pratyekaṃ parivāriṇaḥ । rāge vīreśabhuvanaṃ gurvantevāsināṃ puram ।।
puraṃ cāśuddhavidyāyāṃ syācchaktinavakojjvalam । manonmanyantagāstāśca vāmādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। kalāyāṃ syānmahādevatrayasya puramuttamam । tato māyā tripuṭikā mukhyato anantakoṭibhiḥ ।।
ākrāntā sā bhagabilaiḥ proktaṃ śaivyāṃ tanau punaḥ । aṅguṣṭhamātraparyantaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ niśi ।। cakrāṣṭakādhipatyena tathā śrīmālinīmate । vāmādyāḥ puruṣādau ye proktāḥ śrīpūrvaśāsane ।।
te māyātattva evoktāstanau śaivyāmanantataḥ । kapālavratinaḥ svāṅgahotāraḥ kaṣṭatāpasāḥ ।। sarvābhayāḥ khaḍgadhārāvratāstattattvavedinaḥ । kramāttattattvamāyānti yatreśo ananta ucyate ।।
uktaṃ ca tasya parataḥ sthānamanantādhipasya devasya । sthitivilayasargakarturguhābhagadvārapālasya ।। dharmānaṇimādiguṇāñjñānāni tapaḥsukhāni yogāṃśca । māyābilātpradatte puṃsāṃ niṣkṛṣya niṣkṛṣya ।।
tacchaktīddhasvabalā guhādhikārāndhakāraguṇadīpāḥ । sarve anantapramukhā dīpyante śatabhavapramukhāntāḥ ।। so avyaktamadhiṣṭhāya prakaroti jaganniyogataḥ śambhoḥ । śuddhāśuddhasroto adhikārahetuḥ śivo yasmāt ।।
śivaguṇayoge tasmin mahati pade ye pratiṣṭhitāḥ prathamam । te anantāderjagataḥ sargasthitivilayakartāraḥ ।। māyābilamidamuktaṃ paratastu guhā jagadyoniḥ । utpattyā teṣvasyāḥ patiśaktikṣobhamanuvidhīyamāneṣu ।।
yonivivareṣu nānākāmasamṛddheṣu bhagasaṃjñā । kāmayate patirenāmicchānuvidhāyinīṃ yadā devīm ।। pratibhagamavyaktādyāḥ prajāstadāsyāḥ prajāyante । teṣāmatisūkṣmāṇāmetāvattvaṃ na varṇyate vidhiṣu ।।
avavarakāṇyekasminyadvatsāle bahūni baddhāni । yonibilānyekasmiṃstadvanmāyāśiraḥsāle ।। māyāpaṭalaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ kuḍyaiḥ pihitāḥ parasparamadṛśyāḥ । nivasanti tatra rudrāḥ sukhinaḥ pratibilamasaṃkhyātāḥ ।।
sthāne sāyujyagatāḥ sāmīpyagatāḥ pare salokasthāḥ । pratibhuvanamevamayaṃ nivāsināṃ gurubhiruddiṣṭaḥ ।। api sarvasiddhavācaḥ kṣīyerandīrghakālamudgīrṇāḥ । na punaryonyānantyāducyante srotasāṃ saṃkhyāḥ ।।
tasmānnirayādyekaṃ yatproktaṃ dvārapālaparyantam । srotastenānyānyapi tulyavidhānāni vedyāni ।। avyaktakale guhayā prakṛtikalābhyāṃ vikāra ātmīyaḥ । otaḥ proto vyāptaḥ kalitaḥ pūrṇaḥ parikṣiptaḥ ।।
madhye puṭatrayaṃ tasyā rudrāḥ ṣaḍadhare antare । eka ūrdhve ca pañceti dvādaśaite nirūpitāḥ ।। gahanāsādhyau hariharadaśeśvarau trikalagopatī ṣaḍime । madhye anantaḥ kṣemo dvijeśavidyeśaviśvaśivāḥ ।।
iti pañca teṣu pañcasu ṣaṭsu ca puṭageṣu tatparāvṛttyā । parivarttate sthitiḥ kila devo anantastu sarvathā madhye ।। ūrdhvādharagakapālakapuṭaṣaṭkayugena tatparāvṛttyā । madhyato aṣṭābhirdiksthairvyāpto granthirmataṅgaśāstroktaḥ ।।
śrīsāraśāsane punareṣā ṣaṭpuṭatayā vinirdiṣṭā । granthyākhyamidaṃ tattvaṃ māyākāryaṃ tato māyā ।। māyātattvaṃ vibhu kila gahanamarūpaṃ samastavilayapadam । tatra na bhuvanavibhāgo yukto granthāvasau tasmāt ।।
māyātattvādhipatiḥ so anantaḥ samuditānvicāryāṇūn । yugapatkṣobhayati niśāṃ sā sūte saṃpuṭairanantaiḥ svaiḥ ।। tena kalādidharāntaṃ yaduktamāvaraṇajālamakhilaṃ tat । niḥsaṃkhyaṃ ca vicitraṃ māyaivaikā tvabhinneyam ।।
uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca dharāvyaktātmakaṃ dvayam । asaṃkhyātaṃ niśāśaktisaṃjñaṃ tvekasvarūpakam ।। pāśāḥ puroktāḥ praṇavāḥ pañcamānāṣṭakaṃ muneḥ । kulaṃ yoniśca vāgīśī yasyāṃ jāto na jāyate ।।
dīkṣākāle adharādhvasthaśuddhau yaccādharādhvagam । anantasya samīpe tu tatsarvaṃ pariniṣṭhitam ।। sādhyo dātā damano dhyāno bhasmeti bindavaḥ pañca । pañcārthaguhyarudrāṅkuśahṛdayalakṣaṇaṃ ca savyūham ।।
ākarṣādarśau cetyaṣṭakametatpramāṇānām । aluptavibhavāḥ sarve māyātattvādhikāriṇaḥ ।। māyāmayaśarīrāste bhogaṃ svaṃ paribhuñjate । pralayānte hyanantena saṃhṛtāste tvaharmukhe ।।
anyānantaprasādena vibudhā api taṃ param । suptabuddhaṃ manyamānāḥ svatantrammanyatājaḍāḥ ।। svātmānameva jānanti hetuṃ māyāntarālagāḥ । ataḥ paraṃ sthitā māyā devī jantuvimohinī ।।
devadevasya sā śaktiratidurghaṭakāritā । nirvairaparipanthinyā tayā bhramitabuddhayaḥ ।। idaṃ tattvamidaṃ neti vivadantīha vādinaḥ । gurudevāgniśāstreṣu ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ ।।
satpathaṃ tānparityājya sotpathaṃ nayati dhruvam । asadyuktivicārajñāñchuṣkatarkāvalambinaḥ ।। bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hyamokṣe mokṣalipsayā । śivadīkṣāsinā cchinnā śivajñānāsinā tathā ।।
na prarohetpunarnānyo hetustacchedanaṃ prati । mahāmāyordhvataḥ śuddhā mahāvidyātha mātṛkā ।। vāgīśvarī ca tatrasthaṃ vāmādinavasatpuram । vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kalavikaraṇībalavikārike tathā ।।
mathanī damanī manonmanī ca tridṛśaḥ pītāḥ samastāstāḥ । saptakoṭyo mukhyamantrā vidyātattve atra saṃsthitāḥ ।। ekaikārbudalakṣāṃśāḥ padmākārapurā iha । vidyārājñyastriguṇyādyāḥ sapta saptārbudeśvarāḥ ।।
vidyātattvordhvamaiśaṃ tu tattvaṃ tatra kramordhvagam । śikhaṇḍyādyamanantāntaṃ purāṣṭakayutaṃ puram ।। śikhaṇḍī śrīgalo mūrtirekanetraikarudrakau । śivottamaḥ sūkṣmarudro ananto vidyeśvarāṣṭakam ।।
kramādūrdhvordhvasaṃsthānaṃ saptānāṃ nāyako vibhuḥ । ananta eva dhyeyaśca pūjyaścāpyuttarottaraḥ ।। mukhyamantreśvarāṇāṃ yat sārdhaṃ koṭitrayaṃ sthitam । tannāyakā ime tena vidyeśāścakravartinaḥ ।।
uktaṃ ca gurubhiritthaṃ śivatanvādyeṣu śāsaneṣvetat । bhagabilaśatakalitaguhāmūrdhāsanago aṣṭaśaktiyugdevaḥ ।। gahanādyaṃ nirayāntaṃ sṛjati ca rudrāṃśca viniyuṅkte । uddharati manonmanyā puṃsasteṣveva bhavati madhyasthaḥ ।।
te tenodastacitaḥ paratattvālocane abhiniviśante । sa punaradhaḥ pathavartiṣvadhikṛta evāṇuṣu śivena ।। avasitapativiniyogaḥ sārdhamanekātmamantrakoṭībhiḥ । nirvātyanantanāthastaddhāmāviśati sūkṣmarudrastu ।।
anugṛhyāṇumapūrvaṃ sthāpayati patiḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ sthāne । ityaṣṭau paripāṭyā yāvaddhāmāni yāti gururekaḥ ।। tāvadasaṃkhyātānāṃ jantūnāṃ nirvṛtiṃ kurute । te aṣṭāvapi śaktyaṣṭakayogāmalajalaruhāsanāsīnāḥ ।।
ālokayanti devaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ kāraṇaṃ paramam । taṃ bhagavantamanantaṃ dhyāyantaḥ svahṛdi kāraṇaṃ śāntam ।। saptānudhyāyantyapi mantrāṇāṃ koṭayaḥ śuddhāḥ । māyādiravīcyanto bhavastvanantādirucyate apyabhavaḥ ।।
śivaśuddhaguṇādhīkārāntaḥ so apyeṣa heyaśca । atrāpi yato dṛṣṭānugrāhyāṇāṃ niyojyatā śaivī ।। iṣṭā ca tannivṛttirhyabhavastvadhare na bhūyate yasmāt । patyurapasarpati yataḥ kāraṇatā kāryatā ca siddhebhyaḥ ।।
kañcukavacchivasiddhau tāvatibhavasaṃjñayātimadhyasthau । dharmajñānavirāgaiśyacatuṣṭayapuraṃ tu yat ।। rūpāvaraṇasaṃjñaṃ tattattve asminnaiśvare viduḥ । vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrīti bhuvanatrayaśobhitam ।।
sūkṣmāvaraṇamākhyātamīśatattve gurūttamaiḥ । aiśātsādāśivaṃ jñānakriyāyugalamaṇḍitam ।। śuddhāvaraṇamityāhuruktā śuddhāvṛteḥ param । vidyāvṛtistato bhāvābhāvaśaktidvayojjvalā ।।
śaktyāvṛtiḥ pramāṇākhyā tataḥ śāstre nirūpitā । śaktyāvṛtestu tejasvidhruveśābhyāmalaṅkṛtam ।। tejasvyāvaraṇaṃ vedapurā mānāvṛtistataḥ । mānāvṛteḥ suśuddhāvṛtpuratritayaśobhitā ।।
suśuddhāvaraṇādūrdhva śaivamekapuraṃ bhavet । śivāvṛterūrdhvamāhurmokṣāvaraṇasaṃjñitam ।। asyāṃ mokṣāvṛtau rudrā ekādaśa nirūpitāḥ । mokṣāvaraṇatastvekapuramāvaraṇaṃ dhruvam ।।
ūrdhve dhruvāvṛtericchāvaraṇaṃ tatra te śivāḥ । īśvarecchāgṛhāntasthāstatpuraṃ caikamucyate ।। icchāvṛteḥ prabuddhākhyaṃ digrudrāṣṭakacarcitam । prabuddhāvaraṇādūrdhva samayāvaraṇaṃ mahat ।।
bhuvanaiḥ pañcabhirgarbhīkṛtānantasamāvṛti । sāmayātsauśivaṃ tatra sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। tasminsadāśivo devastasya savyāpasavyayoḥ । jñānakriye parecchā tu śaktirutsaṅgagāminī ।।
sṛṣṭyādipañcakṛtyāni kurute sa tayecchayā । pañca brahmāṇyaṅgaṣaṭkaṃ sakalādyaṣṭakaṃ śivāḥ ।। daśāṣṭādaśa rudrāśca taireva suśivo vṛtaḥ । sadyo vāmāghorau puruṣeśau brahmapañcakaṃ hṛdayam ।।
mūrdhaśikhāvarmadṛgastramaṅgāni ṣaṭ prāhuḥ । sakalākalaśūnyaiḥ saha kalāḍhyakhamalaṅkṛte kṣapaṇamantyam ।। kaṇṭhyauṣṭhyamaṣṭamaṃ kila sakalāṣṭakametadāmnātam । oṃ kāraśivau dīpto hetvīśadaśeśakau suśivakālau ।।
sūkṣmasutejaḥśarvāḥ śivāḥ daśaite atra pūrvādeḥ । vijayo niḥśvāsaśca svāyambhuvo vahnivīrarauravakāḥ ।। mukuṭavisarenduvinduprodgītā lalitasiddharudrau ca । santānaśivau parakiraṇapārameśā iti smṛtā rudrāḥ ।।
sarveṣāmeteṣāṃ jñānāni viduḥ svatulyanāmāni । mantramunikoṭiparivṛta matha vibhuvāmādirudratacchaktiyutam ।। tārādiśaktijuṣṭaṃ suśivāsanamatisitakajamasaṃkhyadalam । yaḥ śaktirudravargaḥ parivāre viṣṭare ca suśivasya ।।
pratyekamasya nijanijaparivāre parārdhakoṭayo asaṃkhyāḥ । māyāmalanirmuktāḥ kevalamadhikāramātrasaṃrūḍhāḥ ।। suśivāvaraṇe rudrāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvaśaktisampūrṇāḥ । adhikārabandhavilaye śāntāḥ śivarūpiṇo punarbhavinaḥ ।।
ūrdhve bindvāvṛtirdīptā tatra tatra padmaṃ śaśiprabham । śāntyatītaḥ śivastatra tacchaktyutsaṅgabhūṣitaḥ ।। nivṛttyādikalāvargaparivārasamāvṛtaḥ । asaṃkhyarudratacchaktipurakoṭibhirāvṛtaḥ ।।
śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca layākhyaṃ tattvamuttamam । pāribhāṣikamityetannāmnā bindurihocyate ।। caturmūrtimayaṃ śubhraṃ yattatsakalaniṣkalam । tasminbhogaḥ samuddiṣṭa ityatredaṃ ca varṇitam ।।
nivṛttyādeḥ susūkṣmatvāddharādyārabdhadehatā । mātuḥ sphūrjanmahājñānalīnatvānna vibhāvyate ।। udrikta taijasatvena hemno bhūparamāṇavaḥ । yathā pṛthaṅna bhāntyevamūrdhvādhorudradehagāḥ ।।
bindūrdhve ardhenduretasya kalā jyotsnā ca tadvatī । kāntiḥ prabhā ca vimalā pañcaitā rodhikāstataḥ ।। rundhanī rodhanī roddhrī jñānabodhā tamopahā । etāḥ pañca kalāḥ prāhurnirodhinyāṃ gurūttamāh ।।
ardhamātraḥ smṛto bindurvyomarūpī catuṣkalaḥ । tadardhamardhacandrastadaṣṭāṃśena nirodhikā ।। hetūnbrahmādikān runddhe rodhikāṃ tāṃ tyajettataḥ । nirodhikāmimāṃ bhittvā sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ param ।।
pararūpeṇa yatrāste pañcamantramahātanuḥ । ityardhendunirodhyantabindvāvṛtyūrdhvato mahān ।। nādaḥ kiñjalkasadṛśo mahadbhiḥ puruṣairvṛtaḥ । catvāri bhuvanānyatra dikṣu madhye ca pañcamam ।।
indhikā dīpikā caiva rodhikā mocikordhvagā । madhye atra padmaṃ tatrordhvagāmī tacchaktibhirvṛtaḥ ।। nādordhvatastu sauṣumnaṃ tatra tacchaktibhṛtprabhuḥ । tadīśaḥ piṅgalelābhyāṃ vṛtaḥ savyāpasavyayoḥ ।।
yā prabhoraṅkagā devī suṣumnā śaśisaprabhā । grathito adhvā tayā sarva ūrdhvaścādhastanastathā ।। nādaḥsuṣumnādhārastu bhittvā viśvamidaṃ jagat । adhaḥśaktyā vinirgacchedūrdhvaśaktyā ca mūrdhataḥ ।।
nāḍyā brahmabile līnaḥ so avyaktadhvanirakṣaraḥ । nadansarveṣu bhūteṣu śivaśaktyā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। suṣumnordhve brahmabilasaṃjñayāvaraṇaṃ tridṛk । tatra brahmā sitaḥ śūlī pañcāsyaḥ śaśiśekharaḥ ।।
tasyotsaṅge parā devī brahmāṇī mokṣamārgagā । roddhrī dātrī ca mokṣasya tāṃ bhittvā cordhvakuṇḍalī ।। śaktiḥ suptāhisadṛśī sā viśvādhāra ucyate । tasyāṃ sūkṣmā susūkṣmā ca tathānye amṛtāmite ।।
madhyato vyāpinī tasyāṃ vyāpīśo vyāpinīdharaḥ । śaktitattvamidaṃ yasya prapañco ayaṃ dharāntakaḥ ।। śivatattvaṃ tatastatra caturdikkaṃ vyavasthitāḥ । vyāpī vyomātmako ananto anāthastacchaktibhāginaḥ ।।
madhye tvanāśritaṃ tatra devadevo hyanāśritaḥ । tacchaktyutsaṅgabhṛtsūryaśatakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।। śivatattvordhvataḥ śaktiḥ parā sā samanāhvayā । sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ sā kartṛbhūtā vyavasthitā ।।
bibhartyaṇḍānyanekāni śivena samadhiṣṭhitā । tadārūḍhaḥ śivaḥ kṛtyapañcakaṃ kurute prabhuḥ ।। samanā karaṇaṃ tasya hetukarturmahośituḥ । anāśritaṃ tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ heturucyate ।।
tayādhitiṣṭhati vibhuḥ kāraṇānāṃ tu pañcakam । anāśrito anāthamayamanantaṃ khavapuḥ sadā ।। sa vyāpinaṃ prerayati svaśaktyā karaṇena tu । karmarūpā sthitā māyā yadadhaḥ śaktikuṇḍalī ।।
nādabindvādikaṃ kāryamityādijagadudbhavaḥ । yatsadāśivaparyantaṃ pārthivādyaṃ ca śāsane ।। tatsarva prākṛtaṃ proktaṃ vināśotpattisaṃyutam । atha sakalabhuvanamānaṃ yanmahyaṃ nigaditaṃ nijairgurubhiḥ ।।
tadvakṣyate samāsādbuddhau yenāśu saṅkrāmet । aṇḍasyāntaranantaḥ kālaḥ kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakau brahmaharī ।। rudrāḥ śataṃ savīraṃ bahirnivṛttistu sāṣṭaśatabhuvanā syāt । jalatejaḥsamīranabho ahaṃkṛddhīmūlasaptake pratyekam ।।
aṣṭau ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanā tena pratiṣṭheti kalā kathitā । atra prāhuḥ śodhyānaṣṭau kecinnijāṣṭakādhipatīn ।। anye tu samastānāṃ śodhyatvaṃ varṇayanti bhuvanānām । śrībhūtirājamiśrā guravaḥ prāhuḥ punarbahī rudraśatam ।।
aṣṭāvantaḥ sākaṃ śarveṇetīdṛśī nivṛttiriyaṃ syāt । rudrāḥ kālī vīro dharābdhilakṣmyaḥ sarasvatī guhyam ।। ityaṣṭakaṃ jale anau vahnyatiguhyadvayaṃ maruti vāyoḥ । svapuraṃ gayādi khe ca vyoma pavitrāṣṭakaṃ ca bhuvanayugam ।।
abhimāne ahaṅkāracchagalādyaṣṭakamathāntarā nabho ahaṃkṛt । tanmātrārkenduśratipurāṣṭakaṃ buddhikarmadevānām ।। daśa tanmātrasamūhe bhuvanaṃ punarakṣavargavinipatite । manasaścetyabhimāne dvāviṃśatireva bhuvanānām ।।
dhiyi daivīnāmaṣṭau kruttejoyogasaṃjñakaṃ trayaṃ tadumā । tatpatiratha mūrtyaṣṭakasuśivadvādaśakavīrabhadrāḥ syuḥ ।। tadatha mahādevāṣṭakamiti buddhau saptadaśa saṃkhyā । guṇatattve paṅktitrayamiti ṣaṭpañcāśataṃ purāṇi viduḥ ।।
yadyapi guṇasāmyātmani mūle krodheśvarāṣṭakaṃ tathāpi dhiyi । tacchodhitamiti gaṇanāṃ na punaḥ prāptaṃ pratiṣṭhāyām ।। iti jalatattvānmūlaṃ tattvacaturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhāyām । ambādituṣṭivargastārādyāḥ siddhayo aṇimādigaṇaḥ ।।
guravo guruśiṣyā ṛṣivarga iḍādiśca vigrahāṣṭakayuk । gandhādivikārapuraṃ buddhiguṇāṣṭakamahaṃkriyā viṣayaguṇāḥ ।। kāmādisaptaviṃśakamāgantu tathā gaṇeśavidyeśamayau । iti pāśeṣu puratrayamitthaṃ puruṣe atra bhuvanaṣoḍaśakam ।।
niyatau śaṅkaradaśakaṃ kāle śivadaśakamiti puradvitayam । rāge suhṛṣṭabhuvanaṃ guruśiṣyapuraṃ ca vitkalāyugale ।। bhuvanaṃ bhuvanaṃ niśi puṭapuratrayaṃ vākpuraṃ pramāṇapuram । iti saptaviṃśatipurā vidyā puruṣāditattvasaptakayuk ।।
vāmeśarūpasūkṣmaṃ śuddhaṃ vidyātha śaktitejasvimitiḥ । suviśuddhiśivau mokṣa dhuveṣisaṃbuddhasamayasauśivasaṃjñāḥ ।। saptadaśapurā śāntā vidyeśasadāśivapuratritayayuktā । bindvardhendunirodhyaḥ parasauśivamindhikādipurasauṣumne ।।
paranādo brahmabilaṃ sūkṣmādiyutordhvakuṇḍalī śaktiḥ । vyāpivyomānantānāthānāśritapurāṇi pañca tataḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca paramamanāśritamatha samanābhuvanaṣoḍaśī yadi vā । bindvāvaraṇaṃ parasauśivaṃ ca pañcendhikādibhuvanāni ।।
sauṣumnaṃ brahmabilaṃ kuṇḍalinī vyāpipañcakaṃ samanā । iti ṣoḍaśabhuvaneyaṃ tattvayugaṃ śāntyatītā syāt ।। śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca kramo ayaṃ purapūgagaḥ । kālāgnirnarakāḥ khābdhiyutaṃ mukhyatayā śatam ।।
kūṣmāṇḍaḥ saptapātālī saptalokī maheśvaraḥ । ityaṇḍamadhyaṃ tadbāhye śataṃ rudrā iti sthitāḥ ।। sthānānāṃ dviśatī bhūmiḥ saptapañcāśatā yutā । pañcāṣṭakasya madhyāddvātriṃśadbhūtacatuṣṭaye ।।
tanmātreṣu ca pañca syurviśvedevāstato aṣṭakam । pañcamaṃ sendriye garve buddhau devāṣṭakaṃ guṇe ।। yogāṣṭakaṃ krodhasaṃjñaṃ mūle kāle sanaiyate । patadrugādyāścāṅguṣṭhamātrādyā rāgatattvagāḥ ।।
dvādaśaikaśivādyāḥ syurvidyāyāṃ kalane daśa । vāmādyāstriśatī seyaṃ triparvaṇyabdhirasyayuk ।। śaivāḥ kecidihānantāḥ śraikaṇṭhā iti saṃgrahaḥ । yatra yadā parabhogān bubhukṣate tatra yojanaṃ kāryam ।।
śodhanamatha taddhānau śeṣaṃ tvantargataṃ kāryam । ityāgamaṃ prathayituṃ darśitametadvikalpitaṃ tena ।। anye api bahuvikalpāḥ svadhiyācāryaiḥ samabhyūhyāḥ । śrīpūrvaśāsane punaraṣṭādaśādhikaṃ śataṃ kathitam ।।
tadiha pradhānamadhikaṃ saṃkṣepeṇocyate śodhyam । kālāgniḥ kūṣmāṇḍo narakeśo hāṭako atha bhūtalapaḥ ।। brahmā munilokeśo rudrāḥ pañcāntarālasthāḥ । adhare anantaḥ prācyāḥ kapālivahnyantanirṛtibalākhyāḥ ।।
laghunidhipatividyādhipaśambhūrdhvāntaṃ savīrabhadrapati । ekādaśabhirbāhye brahmāṇḍaṃ pañcabhistathāntarikaiḥ ।। iti ṣoḍaśapurametannivṛttikalayeha kalanīyam । lakulīśabhārabhūtī diṇḍyāṣāḍhī ca puṣkaranimeṣau ।।
prabhāsasureśāviti salile pratyātmakaṃ saparivāre । bhairavakedāramahākālā madhyāmrajalpākhyāḥ ।। śrīśailahariścandrāviti guhyāṣṭakamidaṃ mahasi । bhīmendrāṭṭahāsavimalakanakhalanākhalakurusthitigayākhyāḥ ।।
atiguhyāṣṭakametanmaruti ca satanmātrake ca sākṣe ca । sthāṇusuvarṇākhyau kila bhadro gokarṇako mahālayakaḥ ।। avimuktarudrakoṭī vastrāpada ityadaḥ pavitraṃ khe । sthūlasthūleśaśaṅkuśrutikālañjarāśca maṇḍalabhṛt ।।
mākoṭāṇḍadvitayacchagalāṇḍā aṣṭakaṃ hyahaṅkāre । anye ahaṅkārāntastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi cāpyāhuḥ ।। dhiyi yonyaṣṭakamuktaṃ prakṛtau yogāṣṭakaṃ kilākṛtaprabhṛti । iti saptāṣṭakabhuvanā pratiṣṭhitiḥ salilato hi mūlāntā ।।
nari vāmo bhīmograu bhaveśavīrāḥ pracaṇḍagaurīśau । ajasānantaikaśivau vidyāyāṃ krodhacaṇḍayugmaṃ syāt ।। saṃvarto jyotiratho kalāniyatyāṃ ca sūrapañcāntau । vīraśikhīśaśrīkaṇṭhasaṃjñametattrayaṃ ca kāle syāt ।।
samahātejā vāmo bhavodbhavaścaikapiṅgaleśānau । bhuvaneśapuraḥsarakāvaṅguṣṭha ime niśi sthitā hyaṣṭau ।। aṣṭāviṃśatibhuvanā vidyā puruṣānniśāntamiyam । hālāhalarudrakrudambikāghorikāḥ savāmāḥ syuḥ ।।
vidyāyāṃ vidyeśāstvaṣṭāvīśe sadāśive pañca । vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī śaktiḥ sakalā ca śontayam ।। aṣṭādaśa bhuvanā syāt śāntyatītā tvabhuvanaiva । iti deśādhvavibhāgaḥ kathitaḥ śrīśambhunā samādiṣṭaḥ ।।
atha tattvapravibhāgo vistarataḥ kathyate kramaprāptaḥ ।। yānyuktāni purāṇyamūni vividhaibhadairyadeṣvanvitaṃ rūpaṃ bhāti paraṃ prakāśaniviḍaṃ devaḥ sa ekaḥ śivaḥ । tatsvātantryarasātpunaḥ śivapadādbhede vibhāte paraṃ yadrūpaṃ bahudhānugāmi tadidaṃ tattvaṃ vibhoḥ śāsane ।। tathāhi kālasadanādvīrabhadrapurāntagam ।
dhṛtikāṭhinyagarimādyavabhāsāddharātmatā ।। evaṃ jalāditattveṣu vācyaṃ yāvatsadāśive । svasminkārye atha dharmaughe yadvāpi svasadṛgguṇe ।। āste sāmānyakalpena tananādvyāptṛbhāvataḥ ।
tattattvaṃ kramaśaḥ pṛthvīpradhānaṃ puṃśivādayaḥ ।। dehānāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca na prasaṅgastato bhavet । śrīmanmataṅgaśāstrādau taduktaṃ parameśinā ।। tatraiṣāṃ darśyate dṛṣṭaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate ।
kāryakāraṇabhāvo yaḥ śivecchāparikalpitaḥ ।। vastutaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ karteśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ । asvatantrasya kartṛtvaṃ nahi jātūpapadyate ।। svatantratā ca cinmātravapuṣaḥ parameśituḥ ।
svatantraṃ ca jaḍaṃ ceti tadanyonyaṃ virudhyate ।। jāḍyaṃ pramātṛtantratvaṃ svātmasiddhimapi prati । na kartṛtvādṛte cānyat kāraṇatvaṃ hi labhyate ।। tasminsati hi tadbhāva ityapekṣaikajīvitam ।
nirapekṣeṣu bhāveṣu svātmaniṣṭhatayā katham ।। sa pūrvamatha paścātsa iti cetpūrvapaścimau । svabhāve anatiriktau cetsama ityavaśiṣyate ।। bījamaṅkura ityasmin satattve hetutadvatoḥ ।
ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti bhavet kāryakāraṇatā na kim ।। bījamaṅkurapatrāditayā pariṇameta cet । atatsvabhāvavapuṣaḥ sa svabhāvo na yujyate ।। sa tatsvabhāva iti cet tarhi bījāṅkurā nije ।
tāvatyeva na viśrāntau tadanyātyantasaṃbhavāt ।। tataśca citrākāro asau tāvānkaścitprasajyate । astu cet na jaḍe anyonyaviruddhākārasaṃbhavaḥ ।। krameṇa citrākāro astu jaḍaḥ kiṃ nu viruddhyate ।
kramo akramo vā bhāvasya na svarūpādhiko bhavet ।। tathopalambhamātraṃ tau upalambhaśca kiṃ tathā । upalabdhāpi vijñānasvabhāvo yo asya so api hi ।। kramopalambharūpatvāt krameṇopalabheta cet ।
tasya tarhi kramaḥ ko asau tadanyānupalambhataḥ ।। svabhāva iti cennāsau svarūpādadhiko bhavet । svarūpānadhikasyāpi kramasya svasvabhāvataḥ ।। svātantryādbhāsanaṃ syāccet kimanyadbrūmahe vayam ।
itthaṃ śrīśiva evaikaḥ karteti paribhāṣyate ।। kartṛtvaṃ caitadetasya tathāmātrāvabhāsanam । tathāvabhāsanaṃ cāsti kāryakāraṇabhāvagam ।। yathā hi ghaṭasāhityaṃ paṭasyāpyavabhāsate ।
tathā ghaṭānantaratā kiṃ tu sā niyamojjhitā ।। ato yanniyamenaiva yasmādābhātyanantaram । tattasya kāraṇaṃ brūmaḥ sati rūpānvaye adhike ।। niyamaśca tathārūpabhāsanāmātrasārakaḥ ।
bījādaṅkura ityevaṃ bhāsanaṃ nahi sarvadā ।। yogīcchānantarodbhūtatathābhūtāṅkuro yataḥ । iṣṭe tathāvidhākāre niyamo bhāsate yataḥ ।। svapne ghaṭapaṭādīnāṃ hetutadvatsvabhāvatā ।
bhāsate niyamenaiva bādhāśūnyena tāvati ।। tato yāvati yādrūpyānniyamo bādhavarjitaḥ । bhāti tāvati tādrūpyāddṛḍhahetuphalātmatā ।। tathābhūte ca niyame hetutadvattvakāriṇi ।
vastutaścinmayasyaiva hetutā taddhi sarvagam ।। ata eva ghaṭodbhūtau sāmagrī heturucyate । sāmagrī ca samagrāṇāṃ yadyekaṃ neṣyate vapuḥ ।। hetubhedānna bhedaḥ syāt phale taccāsamañjasam ।
yadyasyānuvidhatte tāmanvayavyatirekitām ।। tattasya hetu cetso ayaṃ kuṇṭhatarko na naḥ priyaḥ । samagrāśca yathā daṇḍasūtracakrakarādayaḥ ।। dūrāśca bhāvinaścetthaṃ hetutveneti manmahe ।
yadi tatra bhavenmerurbhaviṣyanvāpi kaścana ।। na jāyeta ghaṭo nūnaṃ tatpratyūhavyapohitaḥ । yathā ca cakraṃ niyate deśe kāle ca hetutām ।। yāti karkisumervādyāstadvatsvasthāvadhi sthitāḥ ।
tathā ca teṣāṃ hetunāṃ saṃyojanaviyojane ।। niyate śiva evaikaḥ svatantraḥ kartṛtāmiyāt । kumbhakārasya yā saṃvit cakradaṇḍādiyojane ।। śiva eva hi sā yasmāt saṃvidaḥ kā viśiṣṭatā ।
kaumbhakārī tu saṃvittiravacchedāvabhāsanāt ।। bhinnakalpā yadi kṣepyā daṇḍacakrādimadhyataḥ । tasmādekaikanirmāṇe śivo viśvaikavigrahaḥ ।। karteti puṃsaḥ kartṛtvābhimāno api vibhoḥ kṛtiḥ ।
ata eva tathābhānaparamārthatayā sthiteḥ ।। kāryakāraṇabhāvasya loke śāstre ca citratā । māyāto avyaktakalayoriti rauravasaṃgrahe ।। śrīpūrve tu kalātattvādavyaktamiti kathyate ।
tata eva niśākhyānātkalībhūtādaliṅgakam ।। iti vyākhyāsmadukte asminsati nyāye atiniṣphalā । loke ca gomayātkīṭāt saṃkalpātsvapnataḥ smṛteḥ ।। yogīcchāto dravyamantraprabhāvādeśca vṛścikaḥ ।
anya eva sa cet kāmaṃ kutaścitsvaviśeṣataḥ ।। sa tu sarvatra tulyastatparāmarśaikyamasti tu । tata eva svarūpe api krame apyanyādṛśī sthitiḥ ।। śāstreṣu yujyate citrāt tathābhāvasvabhāvataḥ ।
puṃrāgavitkalākālamāyā jñānottare kramāt ।। niyatirnāsti vairiñce kalordhve niyatiḥ śratā । puṃrāgavittrayādūrdhvaṃ kalāniyatisaṃpuṭam ।। kālo māyeti kathitaḥ kramaḥ kiraṇaśāstragaḥ ।
pumānniyatyā kālaśca rāgavidyākalānvitaḥ ।। ityeṣa krama uddiṣṭo mātaṅge pārameśvare । kāryakāraṇabhāvīye tattve itthaṃ vyavasthite ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre kathitāṃ vacmaḥ kāraṇakalpanām ।
śivaḥ svatantradṛgrūpaḥ pañcaśaktisunirbharaḥ ।। svātantryabhāsitabhidā pañcadhā pravibhajyate । cidānandeṣaṇājñānakriyāṇāṃ susphuṭatvataḥ ।। śivaśaktisadeśānavidyākhyaṃ tattvapañcakam ।
ekaikatrāpi tattve asmin sarvaśaktisunirbhare ।। tattatprādhānyayogena sa sa bhedo nirūpyate । tathāhi svasvatantratvaparipūrṇatayā vibhuḥ ।। niḥsaṃkhyairbahubhī rūpairbhātyavacchedavarjanāt ।
śāṃbhavāḥ śaktijā mantramaheśā mantranāyakāh ।। mantrā iti viśuddhāḥ syuramī pañca gaṇāḥ kramāt । svasminsvasmin gaṇe bhāti yadyadrūpaṃ samanvayi ।। tadeṣu tattvamityuktaṃ kālāgnyāderdharādivat ।
tena yatprāhurākhyānasādṛśyena viḍambitāḥ ।। gurūpāsāṃ vinaivāttapustakābhīṣṭadṛṣṭayaḥ । brahmā nivṛttyadhipatiḥ pṛthaktattvaṃ na gaṇyate ।। sadāśivādyāstu pṛthag gaṇyanta iti ko nayaḥ ।
brahmaviṣṇuhareśānasuśivānāśritātmani ।। ṣaṭke kāraṇasaṃjñe ardhajaratīyamiyaṃ kutaḥ । iti tanmūlato dhvastaṃ gaṇitaṃ nahi kāraṇam ।। yathā pṛthivyadhipatirnṛpastattvāntaraṃ nahi ।
tathā tattatkaleśānaḥ pṛthak tattvāntaraṃ katham ।। tadevaṃ pañcakamidaṃ śuddho adhvā paribhāṣyate । tatra sākṣācchivecchaiva kartryābhāsitabhedikā ।। īśvarecchāvaśakṣubdhabhogalolikacidgaṇān ।
saṃvibhaktumaghoreśaḥ sṛjatīha sitetaram ।। aṇūnāṃ lolikā nāma niṣkarmā yābhilāṣitā । apūrṇaṃmanyatājñānaṃ malaṃ sāvacchidojjhitā ।। yogyatāmātramevaitadbhāvyavacchedasaṃgrahe ।
malastenāsya na pṛthaktattvabhāvo asti rāgavat ।। niravacchedakarmāṃśamātrāvacchedatastu sā । rāgaḥ puṃsi dhiyo dharmaḥ karmabhedavicitratā ।। apūrṇamanyatā ceyaṃ tathārūpāvabhāsanam ।
svatantrasya śivasyecchā ghaṭarūpo yathā ghaṭaḥ ।। svātmapracchādanecchaiva vastubhūtastathā malaḥ । yathaivāvyatiriktasya dharāderbhāvitātmatā ।। tathaivāsyeti śāstreṣu vyatiriktaḥ sthito malaḥ ।
vyatiriktaḥ svatantrastu na ko api śakaṭādivat ।। tatsadvitīyā sāśuddhiḥ śivamuktāṇugā na kim । malasya roddhrī kāpyasti śaktiḥ sa cāpyamuktagā ।। iti nyāyojjhito vādaḥ śraddhāmātraikakalpitaḥ ।
roddhrī śaktirjaḍasyāsau svayaṃ naiva pravartate ।। svayaṃ pravṛttau viśvaṃ syāttathā ceśanikā pramā । malasya roddhrīṃ tāṃ śaktimīśaścetsaṃyunakti tat ।। kīdṛśaṃ pratyaṇumiti praśne nāstyuttaraṃ vacaḥ ।
malaścāvaraṇaṃ tacca nāvāryasya viśeṣakam ।। upalambhaṃ vihantyetadghaṭasyeva paṭāvṛtiḥ । malenāvṛtarūpāṇāmaṇūnāṃ yatsatattvakam ।। śiva eva ca tatpaśyettasyaivāsau malo bhavet ।
vibhorjñānakriyāmātrasārasyāṇugaṇasya ca ।। tadabhāvo malo rūpadhvaṃsāyaiva prakalpate । dharmāddharmiṇi yo bhedaḥ samavāyena caikatā ।। na tadbhavadbhiruditaṃ kaṇabhojanaśiṣyavat ।
nāmūrtena na mūrtena prāvarītuṃ ca śakyate ।। jñānaṃ cākṣuṣaraśmīnāṃ tathābhāve saratyapi । sa eva ca malo mūrtaḥ kiṃ jñānena na vedyate ।। sarvageṇa tataḥ sarvaḥ sarvajñatvaṃ na kiṃ bhajet ।
yaśca dhvāntātprakāśasyāvṛtistatpratighātibhiḥ ।। mūrtānāṃ pratighastejo aṇūnāṃ nāmūrta īdṛśam । na ca cetanamātmānamasvatantro malaḥ kṣamaḥ ।। āvarītuṃ na cācyaṃ ca madyāvṛtinidarśanam ।
uktaṃ bhavadbhirevetthaṃ jaḍaḥ kartā nahi svayam ।। svatantrasyeśvarasyaitāḥ śaktayaḥ prerikāḥ kila । ataḥ karmavipākajñaprabhuśaktibaleritam ।। madyaṃ sūte madaṃ duḥkhasukhamohaphalātmakam ।
na ceśapreritaḥ puṃso mala āvṛṇuyādyataḥ ।। nirmale puṃsi neśasya prerakatvaṃ tathocitam । tulye nirmalabhāve ca prerayeyurna te katham ।। tamīśaṃ prati yuktaṃ yad bhūyasāṃ syātsadharmatā ।
tena svarūpasvātantryamātraṃ malavijṛmbhitam ।। nirṇītaṃ vitataṃ caitanmayānyatretyalaṃ punaḥ । malo abhilāṣaścājñānamavidyā lolikāprathā ।। bhavadoṣo anuplavaśca glāniḥ śoṣo vimūḍhatā ।
ahaṃmamātmatātaṅko māyāśaktirathāvṛtiḥ ।। doṣabījaṃ paśutvaṃ ca saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam । ityādyanvarthasaṃjñābhistatra tatraiṣa bhaṇyate ।। asmin sati bhavati bhavo duṣṭo bhedātmaneti bhavadoṣaḥ ।
mañcavadasmin duḥkhasroto aṇūn vahati yatplavastena ।। śeṣāstu sugamarūpāḥ śabdāstatrārthamūhayeducitam । saṃsārakāraṇaṃ karma saṃsārāṅkura ucyate ।। caturdaśavidhaṃ bhūtavaiciatryaṃ karmajaṃ yataḥ ।
ata eva sāṃkhyayogapāñcarātrādiśāsane ।। ahaṃmameti saṃtyāgo naiṣkarmyāyopadiśyate । niṣkarmā hi sthite mūlamale apyajñānanāmani ।। vaicitryakāraṇābhāvānnordhva sarati nāpyadhaḥ ।
kevalaṃ pārimityena śivābhedamasaṃspṛśan ।। vijñānakevalī proktaḥ śuddhacinmātrasaṃsthitaḥ । sa punaḥ śāṃbhavecchātaḥ śivābhedaṃ parāmṛśan ।। kramānmantreśatannetṛrūpo yāti śivātmatām ।
nanu kāraṇametasya karmaṇaścenmalaḥ katham ।। sa vijñānākalasyāpi na sūte karmasaṃtatim । maivaṃ sa hi malo jñānākale didhvaṃsiṣuḥ katham ।। hetuḥ syāddhvaṃsamānatvaṃ svātantryādeva codbhavet ।
didhvaṃsiṣudhvaṃsamānadhvastākhyāsu tisṛṣvatha ।। daśāsvantaḥ kṛtāvasthāntarāsu svakramasthiteḥ । vijñānākalamantreśatadīśāditvakalpanā ।। tataśca supte turye ca vakṣyate bahubhedatā ।
ataḥ pradhvaṃsanaunmukhyakhilībhūtasvaśaktikaḥ ।। karmaṇo hetutāmetu malaḥ kathamivocyatām । kiṃ ca karmāpi na malādyataḥ karma kriyātmakam ।। kriyā ca kartṛtārūpāt svātantryānna punarmalāt ।
yā tvasya karmaṇaścitraphaladatvena karmatā ।। prasiddhā sā na saṃkocaṃ vinātmani malaśca saḥ । vicitraṃ hi phalaṃ bhinnaṃ bhogyatvenābhimanyate ।। bhoktaryātmani teneyaṃ bhedarūpā vyavasthitiḥ ।
iti svakāryaprasave sahakāritvamāśrayan ।। sāmarthyavyañjakatvena karmaṇaḥ kāraṇaṃ malaḥ । nanvevaṃ karmasadbhāvānmalasyāpi sthiteḥ katham ।। vijñānākalatā tasya saṃkoco hyasti tādṛśaḥ ।
maivamadhvastasaṃkoco apyasau bhāvanayā dṛḍham ।। nāhaṃ karteti manvānaḥ karmasaṃskāramujjhati । phaliṣyatīdaṃ karmeti yā dṛḍhā vṛttirātmani ।। sa saṃskāraḥ phalāyeha na tu smaraṇakāraṇam ।
apradhvaste api saṃkoce nāhaṃ karteti bhāvanāt ।। na phalaṃ kṣīvamūḍhādeḥ prāyaścitte atha vā kṛte । yanmayādya tapastaptaṃ tadasmai syāditi sphuṭam ।। abhisaṃdhimataḥ karma na phaledabhisandhitaḥ ।
tathābhisaṃdhānākhyāṃ tu mānase karma saṃskriyām ।। phaloparaktāṃ vidadhatkalpate phalasampade । yastu tatrāpi dārḍhyena phalasaṃskāramujjhati ।। sa tatphalatyāgakṛtaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ phalamaśnute ।
anayā paripāṭyā yaḥ samastāṃ karmasaṃtatim ।। anahaṃyutayā projjhet sasaṃkoco api so akalaḥ । nanvitthaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcidātmīyamabhisaṃdhitaḥ ।। parasmai syānna vijñātaṃ bhavatā tāttvikaṃ vacaḥ ।
tasya bhoktustathā cetsyādabhisaṃdhiryathātmani ।। tadavaśyaṃ parasyāpi satastadduṣkṛtaṃ bhavet । parābhisaṃdhisaṃvittau svābhisaṃdhirdṛḍhībhavet ।। abhisaṃdhānavirahe tvasya no phalayogitā ।
na me duṣkṛtamityeṣā rūḍhistasyāphalāya sā ।। parābhisandhivicchede svātmanānabhisaṃhitau । dvayorapi phalaṃ na syānnāśahetuvyavasthiteḥ ।। sukhahetau sukhe cāsya sāmānyādabhisaṃdhitaḥ ।
nirviśeṣādapi nyāyyā dharmādiphalabhoktṛtā ।। duḥkhaṃ me duḥkhaheturvā stādityeṣa punarna tu । sāmānyo apyabhisaṃdhiḥ syāttadadharmasya nāgamaḥ ।। prakṛtaṃ brūmahe jñānākalasyoktacarasya yat ।
anahaṃyutayā sarvā vilīnāḥ karmasaṃskriyāḥ ।। tasmādasya na karmāsti kasyāpi sahakāritām । malaḥ karotu tenāyaṃ dhvaṃsamānatvamaśnute ।। apadhvastamalastvantaḥśivāveśavaśīkṛtaḥ ।
ahaṃbhāvaparo apyeti na karmādhīnavṛttitām ।। uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca tadetatparameśinā । malamajñānamicchanti saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam ।। dharmādharmātmakaṃ karma sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇam ।
lakṣayetsukhaduḥkhādi svaṃ kārya hetubhāvataḥ ।। nahi hetuḥ kadāpyāste vinā kārya nijaṃ kvacit । hetutā yogyataivāsau phalānantaryabhāvitā ।। pūrvakasya tu hetutvaṃ pāramparyeṇa kiṃ ca tat ।
lakṣyate sukhaduḥkhādyaiḥ samāne dṛṣṭakāraṇe ।। citrairhetvantaraṃ kiṃcittacca karmeha darśanāt । svāṅge prasādaraukṣyādi jāyamānaṃ svakarmaṇā ।। dṛṣṭamityanyadehasthaṃ kāraṇaṃ karma kalpyāte ।
ihāpyanyānyadehasthe sphuṭaṃ karmaphale yataḥ ।। kṛṣikarma madhau bhogaḥ śaradyanyā ca sā tanuḥ । anusaṃdhāturekasya saṃbhavastu yatastataḥ ।। tasyaiva tatphalaṃ citraṃ karma yasya purātanam ।
kṣīvo api rājā sūdaṃ cedādiśetprātarīdṛśam ।। bhojayetyanusaṃdhānādvinā prāpnoti tatphalam । itthaṃ janmāntaropāttakarmāpyadyānusaṃdhinā ।। vinā bhuṅkte phalaṃ hetustatra prācyā hyakampatā ।
ata eva kṛtaṃ karma karmaṇā tapasāpi vā ।। jñānena vā nirudhyeta phalapākeṣvanunmukham । ārabdhakāryaṃ dehe asmin yatpunaḥ karma tatkatham ।। ucchidyatāmantyadaśaṃ niroddhuṃ nahi śakyate ।
tatraiva dehe yattvanyadadyagaṃ vā purātanam ।। karma tajjñānadīkṣādyaiḥ śaṇḍhīkartuṃ prasahyate । tathā saṃskāradārḍhya hi phalāya dṛḍhatā punaḥ ।। yadā yadā vinaśyeta karmadhvastaṃ tadā tadā ।
ato mohaparādhīno yadyapyakṛta kiṃcana ।। tathāpi jñānakāle tatsarvameva pradahyate । uktaṃ ca śrīpare ahānādānaḥ sarvadṛgulvaṇaḥ ।। muhūrtānnirdahetsarva dehasthamakṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
dehasthamiti dehena saha tādātmyamāśritā ।। svācchandyātsaṃvidevoktā tatrasthaṃ karma dahyate । dehaikyavāsanātyāgāt sa ca viśvātmatāsthiteḥ ।। akālakalite vyāpinyabhinne yā hi saṃskriyā ।
saṃkoca eva sānena so api dehaikatāmayaḥ ।। etatkārmamalaṃ proktaṃ yena sākaṃ layākalāḥ । syurguhāgahanāntaḥsthāḥ suptā iva sarīsṛpāḥ ।। tataḥ prabuddhasaṃskārāste yathocitabhāginaḥ ।
brahmādisthāvarānte asmin saṃsranti punaḥ punaḥ ।। ye punaḥ karmasaṃskārahānyai prārabdhabhāvanāḥ । bhāvanāpariniṣpattimaprāpya pralayaṃ gatāḥ ।। mahāntaṃ te tathāntaḥsthabhāvanāpākasauṣṭhavāt ।
mantratvaṃ pratipadyante citrāccitraṃ ca karmataḥ ।। asya kārmamalasyeyanmāyāntādhvavisāriṇaḥ । pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ proktamajñānātmāṇavo malaḥ ।। kṣobho asya lolikākhyasya sahakāritayā sphuṭam ।
tiṣṭhāsāyogyataunmukhyamīśvarecchāvaśācca tat ।। na jaḍaścidadhiṣṭhānaṃ vinā kvāpi kṣamo yataḥ । aṇavo nāma naivānyatprakāśātmā maheśvaraḥ ।। cidacidrūpatābhāsī pudgalaḥ kṣetravitpaśuḥ ।
cidrūpatvācca sa vyāpī nirguṇo niṣkriyastataḥ ।। yogopāyepsako nityo mūrtivandhyaḥ prabhāṣyate । acittvādajñatā bhedo bhogyādbhoktrantarādatha ।। teṣāmaṇūnāṃ sa mala īśvarecchāvaśādbhṛśam ।
prabudhyate tathā coktaṃ śāstre śrīpūrvanāmani ।। īśvarecchāvaśādasya bhogecchā saṃprajāyate । bhogecchorupakārārthamādyo mantramaheśvaraḥ ।। māyāṃ vikṣobhya saṃsāraṃ nirmimīte vicitrakam ।
māyā ca nāma devasya śaktiravyatirekiṇī ।। bhedāvabhāsasvātantryaṃ tathāhi sa tayā kṛtaḥ । ādyo bhedāvabhāso yo vibhāgamanupeyivān ।। garbhīkṛtānantabhāvivibhāsā sā parā niśā ।
sā jaḍā bhedarūpatvāt kāryaṃ cāsyā jaḍaṃ yataḥ ।। vyāpinī viśvahetutvāt sūkṣmā kāryaikakalpanāt । śivaśaktyavinābhāvānnityaikā mūlakāraṇam ।। acetanamanekātma sarva kārya yathā ghaṭaḥ ।
pradhānaṃ ca tathā tasmāt kārya nātmā tu cetanaḥ ।। ata evādhvani proktā pūrvaṃ māyā dvidhā sthitā । yathā ca māyā devasya śaktirabhyeti bhedinam ।। tattvabhāvaṃ tathānyo api kalādistattvavistaraḥ ।
niruddhaśakteryā kiṃcitkartṛtodvalanātmikā ।। nāthasya śaktiḥ sādhastātpuṃsaḥ kṣeptrī kalocyate । evaṃ vidyādayo apyete dharāntāḥ paramārthataḥ ।। śivaśaktimayā eva proktanyāyānusārataḥ ।
tathāpi yatpṛthagbhānaṃ kalāderīśvarecchayā ।। tato jaḍatve kāryatve pṛthaktattvasthitau dhruvam । upādānaṃ smṛtā māyā kvacittatkāryameva ca ।। tathāvabhāsacitraṃ ca rūpamanyonyavarjitam ।
yadbhāti kila saṃkalpe tadasti ghaṭavadvahiḥ ।। khapuṣpādyastitāṃ brūmastato na vyabhicāritā । khapuṣpaṃ kāladiṅmātṛsāpekṣaṃ nāstiśabdataḥ ।। dharādivat tathātyantābhāvo apyevaṃ vivicyatām ।
yatsaṃkalpyaṃ tathā tasya bahirdeho asti cetanaḥ ।। caitravatsauśivāntaṃ tat sarva tādṛśadehavat । yasya deho yathā tasya tajjātīyaṃ puraṃ bahiḥ ।। ataḥ suśivaparyantā siddhā bhuvanapaddhatiḥ ।
ātmanām tatpuraṃ prāpyaṃ deśatvādanyadeśavat ।। ātmanāmadhvabhoktṛtvaṃ tato ayatnena siddhyati । sā māyā kṣobhamāpannā viśvaṃ sūte samantataḥ ।। daṇḍāhatevāmalakī phalāni kila yadyapi ।
tathāpi tu tathā citrapaurvāparyāvabhāsanāt ।। māyākārye api tattvaughe kāryakāraṇatā mithaḥ । sā yadyapyanyaśāstreṣu bahudhā dṛśyate sphuṭam ।। tathāpi mālinīśāstradṛśā tāṃ saṃpracakṣmahe ।
kalādivasudhāntaṃ yanmāyāntaḥ saṃpracakṣate ।। pratyātmabhinnamevaitat sukhaduḥkhādibhedataḥ । ekasyāmeva jagati bhogasādhanasaṃhatau ।। sukhādīnāṃ samaṃ vyakterbhogabhedaḥ kuto bhavet ।
na cāsau karmabhedena tasyaivānupapattitaḥ ।। tasmāt kalādiko vargo bhinna eva kadācana । aikyametīśvarecchāto nṛttagītādivādane ।। eṣāṃ kalāditattvānāṃ sarveṣāmapi bhāvinām ।
śuddhatvamasti teṣāṃ ye śaktipātapavitritāḥ ।। kalā hi śuddhā tattādṛk karmatvaṃ saṃprasūyate । mitamapyāśu yenāsmāt saṃsārādeṣa mucyate ।। rāgavidyākālayatiprakṛtyakṣārthasaṃcayaḥ ।
itthaṃ śuddha iti procya gururmānastutau vibhuḥ ।। evameṣā kalādīnāmutpattiḥ pravivicyate । māyātattvāt kalā jātā kiṃcitkartṛtvalakṣaṇā ।। māyā hi cinmayādbhedaṃ śivādvidadhatī paśoḥ ।
suṣuptatāmivādhatte tata eva hyadṛkkriyaḥ ।। kalā hi kiṃcitkartṛtvaṃ sūte svāliṅganādaṇoḥ । tasyāścāpyaṇunānyonyaṃ hyañjane sā prasūyate ।। sadyonirvāṇadīkṣotthapuṃviśleṣe hi sā satī ।
śliṣyantyapi ca no sūte tathāpi svaphalaṃ kvacit ।। ucchūnateva prathamā sūkṣmāṅkurakaleva ca । bījasyāmbvagnimṛtkambutuṣayogāt prasūtikṛt ।। kalā māyāṇusaṃyogajāpyeṣā nirvikārakam ।
nāṇuṃ kuryādupādānaṃ kiṃtu māyāṃ vikāriṇīm ।। malaścāvārako māyā bhāvopādānakāraṇam । karma syāt sahakāryeva sukhaduḥkhodbhavaṃ prati ।। ataḥ saṃcchannacaitanyasamudbalanakāryakṛt ।
kalaivānantanāthasya śaktyā saṃpreritā jaḍā ।। na ceśaśaktirevāsya caitanyaṃ balayiṣyati । tadupodbalitaṃ taddhi na kiṃcitkartṛtāṃ vrajet ।। seyaṃ kalā na karaṇaṃ mukhyaṃ vidyādikaṃ yathā ।
puṃsi kartari sā kartrī prayojakatayā yataḥ ।। alakṣyāntarayoritthaṃ yadā puṃskalayorbhavet । māyāgarbheśaśaktyāderantarajñānamāntaram ।। tadā māyāpuṃvivekaḥ sarvakarmakṣayādbhavet ।
vijñānākalatā māyādhastānno yātyadhaḥ pumān ।। dhīpuṃviveke vijñāte pradhānapuruṣāntare । api na kṣīṇakarmā syāt kalāyāṃ taddhi saṃbhavet ।। ataḥ sāṃkhyadṛśā siddhaḥ pradhānādho na saṃsaret ।
kalāpuṃsorviveke tu māyādho naiva gacchati ।। malādviviktamātmānaṃ paśyaṃstu śivatāṃ vrajet । sarvatra caiśvaraḥ śaktipāto atra sahakāraṇam ।। māyāgarbhādhikārīyo dvayorantye tu nirmalaḥ ।
seyaṃ kalā kāryabhedādanyaiva hyanumīyate ।। anyathaikaṃ bhavedviśvaṃ kāryāyetyanyanihnavaḥ । iti mataṅgaśāstrādau yā proktā sā kalā svayam ।। kiṃcidrūpatayākṣipya kartṛtvamiti bhaṅgitaḥ ।
kiṃcidrūpaviśiṣṭaṃ yat kartṛtvaṃ tatkathaṃ bhavet ।। ajñasyeti tataḥ sūte kiṃcijjñatvātmikāṃ vidam । buddhiṃ paśyati sā vidyā buddhidarpaṇacāriṇaḥ ।। sukhādīn pratyayān mohaprabhṛtīn kāryakāraṇe ।
karmajālaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ vivinakti nijātmanā ।। buddhistu guṇasaṃkīrṇā vivekena kathaṃ sukham । duḥkhaṃ mohātmakaṃ vāpi viṣayaṃ darśayedapi ।। svacchāyāṃ dhiyi saṃkrāmanbhāvaḥ saṃvedyatāṃ katham ।
tayā vinaiti sāpyanyatkaraṇaṃ puṃsi kartari ।। nanu cobhayataḥ śubhrādarśadaśīyadhīgatāt । puṃsprakāśādbhāti bhāvaḥ maivaṃ tatpratibimbanam ।। jaḍameva hi mukhyo atha puṃsprakāśo asya bhāsanam ।
bahiḥsthasyaiva tasyāstu buddheḥ kiṃkalpanā kṛtā ।। abhedabhūmireṣā ca bhedaśceha vicāryate । tasmādbuddhigato bhāvo vidyākaraṇagocaraḥ ।। bhāvānāṃ pratibimbaṃ ca vedyaṃ dhīkalpanā tataḥ ।
kiṃcittu kurute tasmānnūnamastyaparaṃ tu tat ।। rāgatattvamiti proktaṃ yattatraivoparañjakam । na cāvairāgyamātraṃ tattatrāpyāsaktivṛttitaḥ ।। viraktāvapi tṛptasya sūkṣmarāgavyavasthiteḥ ।
kālastuṭyādibhiścaitat kartṛtvaṃ kalayatyataḥ ।। kāryāvacchedi kartṛtvaṃ kālo avaśyaṃ kaliṣyati । niyatiryojanāṃ dhatte viśiṣṭe kāryamaṇḍale ।। vidyā rāgo atha niyatiḥ kālaścaitaccatuṣṭayam ।
kalākāryaṃ bhoktṛbhāve tiṣṭhadbhoktṛtvapūritam ।। māyā kalā rāgavidye kālo niyatireva ca । kañcukāni ṣaḍuktāni saṃvidastatsthitau paśuḥ ।। dehapuryaṣṭakādyeṣu vedyeṣu kila vedanam ।
etatṣaṭkasasaṃkocaṃ yadavedyamasāvaṇuḥ ।। uktaṃ śivatanuśāstre tadidaṃ bhaṅgyantareṇa punaḥ । āvaraṇaṃ sarvātmagamaśuddhiranyāpyananyarūpeva ।। śivadahanakiraṇajālairdāhyatvāt sā yato anyarūpaiva ।
anidaṃpūrvatayā yadrañjayati nijātmanā tato ananyā ।। sahajāśuddhimato aṇorīśaguhābhyāṃ hi kañcukastrividhaḥ । tasya dvitīyacitiriva svacchasya niyujyate kalā ślakṣṇā ।। anayā vidvasya paśorupabhogasamarthatā bhavati ।
vidyā cāsya kalātaḥ śaraṇāntardīpakaprabhevābhūt ।। sukhaduḥkhasaṃvidaṃ yā vivinakti paśorvibhāgena । rāgaśca kalātattvācchucivastrakaṣāyavat samutpannaḥ ।। tyaktuṃ vāñchati na yataḥ saṃsṛtisukhasaṃvidānandam ।
evamavidyāmalinaḥsamarthitastriguṇakañcukabalena ।। gahanopabhogagarbhe paśuravaśamadhomukhaḥ patati । etena malaḥ kathitaḥ kambukavadaṇoḥ kalādikaṃ tuṣavat ।। evaṃ kalākhyatattvasya kiṃcitkartṛtvalakṣaṇe ।
viśeṣabhāge kartṛtvaṃ carcitaṃ bhoktṛpūrvakam ।। viśeṣaṇatayā yo atra kiñcidbhāgastadotthitam । vedyamātraṃ sphuṭaṃ bhinnaṃ pradhānaṃ sūyate kalā ।। samameva hi bhogyaṃ ca bhoktāraṃ ca prasūyate ।
kalā bhedābhisaṃdhānādaviyuktaṃ parasparam ।। bhoktṛbhogyātmatā na syādviyogācca parasparam । vilīnāyāṃ ca tasyāṃ syānmāyāsyāpi na kiṃcana ।। nanu śrīmadrauravādau rāgavidyātmakaṃ dvayam ।
sūte kalā hi yugapattato avyaktamiti sthitiḥ ।। uktamatra vibhātyeṣa kramaḥ satyaṃ tathā hyalam । rajyamāno veda sarva vidaṃścāpyatra rajyate ।। tathāpi vastusatteyamihāsmābhirnirūpitā ।
tasyāṃ ca na kramaḥ ko api syādvā so api viparyayāt ।। tasmādvipratipattiṃ no kuryācchāstrodite vidhau । evaṃ saṃvedyamātraṃ yat sukhaduḥkhavimohataḥ ।। bhotsyate yattataḥ proktaṃ tatsāmyātmakamāditaḥ ।
sukhaṃ sattvaṃ prakāśatvāt prakāśo hlāda ucyate ।। duḥkhaṃ rajaḥ kriyātmatvād kriyā hi tadatatkramaḥ । mohastamo varaṇakaḥ prakāśābhāvayogataḥ ।। ta ete kṣobhamāpannā guṇāḥ kārya pratanvate ।
akṣubdhasya vijātīyaṃ na syāt kāryamadaḥ purā ।। uktameveti śāstre asmin guṇāṃstattvāntaraṃ viduḥ । bhuvanaṃ pṛthagevātra darśitaṃ guṇabhedataḥ ।। īśvarecchāvaśakṣubdhalolikaṃ puruṣaṃ prati ।
bhoktṛtvāya svatantreśaḥ prakṛtiṃ kṣobhayed bhṛśam ।। tena yaccodyate sāṃkhyaṃ muktāṇuṃ prati kiṃ na sā । sūte puṃso vikāritvāditi tannātra bādhakam ।। guṇebhyo buddhitattvaṃ tat sarvato nirmalaṃ tataḥ ।
puṃsprakāśaḥ sa vedyo atra pratibimbatvamārchati ।। viṣayapratibimbaṃ ca tasyāmakṣakṛtaṃ bahiḥ । ataddvāraṃ samutprekṣāpratibhādiṣu tādṛśī ।। vṛttirbodho bhavedbuddheḥ sā cāpyālambanaṃ dhruvam ।
ātmasaṃvitprakāśasya bodho asau tajjaḍo apyalam ।। buddherahaṃkṛt tādṛkṣe pratibimbitapuṃskṛteḥ । prakāśe vedyakaluṣe yadahaṃmananātmatā ।। tayā pañcavidhaścaiṣa vāyuḥ saṃrambharūpayā ।
prerito jīvanāya syādanyathā maraṇaṃ punaḥ ।। ata eva viśuddhātmasvātantryāhaṃsvabhāvataḥ । akṛtrimādidaṃ tvanyadityuktaṃ kṛtiśabdataḥ ।। ityayaṃ karaṇaskandho ahaṃkārasya nirūpitaḥ ।
tridhāsya prakṛtiskandhaḥ sāttvarājasatāmasaḥ ।। sattvapradhānāhaṃkārādbhoktraṃśasparśinaḥ sphuṭam । manobuddhyakṣaṣaṭkaṃ tu jātaṃ bhedastu kathyate ।। mano yatsarvaviṣayaṃ tenātra pravivakṣitam ।
sarvatanmātrakartṛtvaṃ viśeṣaṇamahaṃkṛteḥ ।। buddhyahaṃkṛnmanaḥ prāhurbodhasaṃrabhaṇaiṣaṇe । karaṇaṃ bāhyadevairyannaivāpyantarmukhaiḥ kṛtam ।। prāṇaśca nāntaḥkaraṇaṃ jaḍatvāt preraṇātmanaḥ ।
prayatnecchāvibodhāṃśahetutvāditi niścitam ।। avasāyo abhimānaśca kalpanā ceti na kriyā । ekarūpā tatastritvaṃ yuktamantaḥkṛtau sphuṭam ।। na ca buddhirasaṃvedyā karaṇatvānmano yathā ।
pradhānavadasaṃvedyabuddhivādastadujjhitaḥ ।। śabdatanmātrahetutvaviśiṣṭā yā tvahaṃkṛtiḥ । sā śrotre karaṇaṃ yāvadghrāṇe gandhatvabhoditā ।। bhautikatvamato apyastu niyamādviṣayeṣvalam ।
ahaṃ śṛṇomi paśyāmi jighrāmītyādisaṃvidi ।। ahaṃtānugamādāhaṃkārikatvaṃ sphuṭaṃ sthitam । karaṇatvamato yuktaṃ kartraśaspṛktvayogataḥ ।। karturvibhinnaṃ karaṇaṃ preryatvāt karaṇaṃ kutaḥ ।
karaṇāntaravāñchāyāṃ bhavettatrānavasthitiḥ ।। tasmāt svātantryayogena kartā svaṃ bhedayan vapuḥ । karmāśasparśinaṃ svāṃśaṃ karaṇīkurute svayam ।। karaṇīkṛtatatsvāṃśatanmayībhāvanāvaśāt ।
karaṇīkurute atyantavyatiriktaṃ kuṭhāravat ।। tenāśuddhaiva vidyāsya sāmānyaṃ karaṇaṃ purā । jñaptau kṛtau tu sāmānyaṃ kalā karaṇamucyate ।। nanu śrīmanmataṅgādau kalāyāḥ kartṛtoditā ।
tasyāṃ satyāṃ hi vidyādyāḥ karaṇatvārhatājuṣaḥ ।। ucyate kartṛtaivoktā karaṇatve prayojikā । tayā vinā tu nānyeṣāṃ karaṇānāṃ sthitiryataḥ ।। ato asāmānyakaraṇavargāt tatra pṛthak kṛtā ।
vidyāṃ vinā hi nānyeṣāṃ karaṇānāṃ nijā sthitiḥ ।। kalāṃ vinā na tasyāśca kartṛtve jñātṛtā yataḥ । kalāvidye tataḥ puṃso mukhyaṃ tatkaraṇaṃ viduḥ ।। ata eva vihīne api buddhikarmendriyaiḥ kvacit ।
andhe paṅgau rūpagatiprakāśo na na bhāsate ।। kiṃtu sāmānyakaraṇabalādvedye api tādṛśi । rūpasāmānya evāndhaḥ pratipattiṃ prapadyate ।। tata eva tvahaṃkārāt tanmātrasparśino adhikam ।
karmendriyāṇi vākpāṇipāyūpasthāṅghri jajñire ।। vacmyādade tyajāmyāśu visṛjāmi vrajāmi ca । iti yāhaṃkriyā kāryakṣamā karmendriyaṃ tu tat ।। tena cchinnakarasyāsti hastaḥ karmendriyātmakaḥ ।
tasya pradhānādhiṣṭhānaṃ paraṃ pañcāṅguliḥ karaḥ ।। mukhenāpi yadādānaṃ tatra yat karaṇaṃ sthitam । sa pāṇireva karaṇaṃ vinā kiṃ saṃbhavet kriyā ।। tathābhāve tu buddhyakṣairapi kiṃ syātprayojanam ।
darśanaṃ karaṇāpekṣaṃ kriyātvāditi cocyate ।। parairgamau tu karaṇaṃ neṣyate ceti vismayaḥ । gamanotkṣepaṇādīni mukhyaṃ karmopalambhanam ।। punarguṇaḥ kriyā tveṣā vaiyākaraṇadarśane ।
kriyā karaṇapūrveti vyāptyā karaṇapūrvakam ।। jñānaṃ nādānamityetat sphuṭamāndhyavijṛmbhitam । tasmāt karmendriyāṇyāhustvagvadvyāptṝṇi mukhyataḥ ।। tatsthāne vṛttimantīti mataṅge guravo mama ।
nanvanyānyapi karmāṇi santi bhūyāṃsi tatkṛte ।। karaṇānyapi vācyāni tathā cākṣeṣvaniṣṭhitiḥ । nanvetat kheṭapālādyairnirākāri na karmaṇām ।। yatsādhanaṃ tadakṣaṃ syāt kiṃtu kasyāpi karmaṇaḥ ।
etannāsmatkṛtapraśnatṛṣṇāsaṃtāpaśāntaye ।। nahyasvacchamitaprāyairjalaistṛpyanti barhiṇaḥ । ucyate śrīmatādiṣṭaṃ śaṃbhunātra mamottaram ।। svacchasaṃvedanodāravikalāprabalīkṛtam ।
iha karmānusaṃdhānabhedādekaṃ vibhidyate ।। tatrānusaṃdhiḥ pañcātmā pañca karmendriyāṇyataḥ । tyāgāyādānasaṃpattyai dvayāya dvitayaṃ vinā ।। svarūpaviśrāntikṛte caturdhā karma yadbahiḥ ।
pāyupāṇyaṅghrijananaṃ karaṇaṃ taccaturvidham ।। antaṃ prāṇāśrayaṃ yattu karmātra karaṇaṃ hi vāk । uktāḥ samāsataścaiṣāṃ citrāḥ kāryeṣu vṛttayaḥ ।। tadetadvyatiriktaṃ hi na karma kvāpi dṛśyate ।
tatkasyārthe prakalpyeyamindriyāṇāmaniṣṭhitiḥ ।। etatkartavyacakraṃ tadasāṃkaryeṇa kurvate । akṣāṇi sahavṛttyā tu buddhyante saṃkaraṃ jaḍāḥ ।। ukta indriyavargo ayamahaṃkārāt tu rājasāt ।
tamaḥpradhānāhaṃkārād bhoktraṃśacchādanātmanaḥ ।। bhūtādināmnastanmātrapañcakaṃ bhūtakāraṇam । manobuddhyakṣakarmākṣavargastanmātravargakaḥ ।। ityatra rājasāhaṃkṛdyogaḥ saṃśleṣako dvaye ।
anye tvāhurmano jātaṃ rājasāhaṃkṛteryataḥ ।। samastendriyasaṃcāracaturaṃ laghu vegavat । anye tu sāttvikāt svāntaṃ buddhikarmendriyāṇi tu ।। rājasādgrāhakagrāhyabhāgasparśīni manvate ।
kheṭapālāstu manyante karmendriyagaṇaḥ sphuṭam ।। rājasāhaṃkṛterjāto rajasaḥ karmatā yataḥ । śrīpūrvaśāstre tu mano rājasāt sāttvikātpunaḥ ।। indriyāṇi samastāni yuktaṃ caitadvibhāti naḥ ।
tathāhi bāhyavṛttīnāmakṣāṇāṃ vṛttibhāsane ।। ālocane śaktirantaryojane manasaḥ punaḥ । uktaṃ ca guruṇā kuryānmano anuvyavasāyi sat ।। taddvayālambanā mātṛvyāpārātmakriyā iti ।
tānmātrastu gaṇo dhvāntapradhānāyā ahaṃkṛteḥ ।। atrāvivādaḥ sarvasya grāhyopakrama eva hi । pṛthivyāṃ saurabhānyādivicitre gandhamaṇḍale ।। yatsāmānyaṃ hi gandhatvaṃ gandhatanmātranāma tat ।
vyāpakaṃ tata evoktaṃ sahetutvāttu na dhruvam ।। svakāraṇe tirobhūtirdhvaso yattena nādhruvam । evaṃ rasādiśabdāntatanmātreṣvapi yojanā ।। viśeṣāṇāṃ yato avaśyaṃ daśā prāgaviśeṣiṇī ।
kṣubhitaṃ śabdatanmātraṃ citrākārāḥ śratīrdadhat ।। nabhaḥ śabdo avakāśātmā vācyādhyāsasaho yataḥ । tadetatsparśatanmātrayogāt prakṣobhamāgatam ।। vāyutāmeti tenātra śabdasparśobhayātmatā ।
anye tvāhurdhvaniḥ khaikaguṇastadapi yujyate ।। yato vāyurnijaṃ rūpaṃ labhate na vināmbarāt । uttarottarabhūteṣu pūrvapūrvasthitiryataḥ ।। tata eva marudvyomnoraviyogo mithaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
śabdasparśau tu rūpeṇa samaṃ prakṣobhamāgatau ।। tejastattvaṃ tribhirdharmaiḥ prāhuḥ pūrvavadeva tat । taistribhiḥ sarasairāpaḥ sagandhairbhūriti kramaḥ ।। tatra pratyakṣataḥ siddho dharādiguṇasaṃcayaḥ ।
nahi gandhādidharmaughavyatiriktā vibhāti bhūḥ ।। yathā guṇaguṇidvaitavādināmekamapyadaḥ । citraṃ rūpaṃ paṭe bhāti kramāddharmāstathā bhuvi ।। yathā ca vistṛte vastre yugapadbhāti citratā ।
tathaiva yogināṃ dharmasāmastyenāvabhāti bhūḥ ।। gandhādiśabdaparyantacitrarūpā dharā tataḥ । upāyabhedādbhātyeṣā kramākramavibhāgataḥ ।। tata eva kramavyaktikṛto dhībheda ucyate ।
ṣaṣṭhīprayogo dhībhedādbhedyabhedakatā tathā ।। tena dharmātirikto atra dharmī nāma na kaścana । tatrānekaprakārāḥ syurgandharūparasāḥ kṣitau ।। saṃsparśaḥ pākajo anuṣṇāśītaḥ śabdo vicitrakaḥ ।
śauklyaṃ mādhuryaśītatve citrāḥ śabdāśca vāriṇi ।। śuklabhāsvaratoṣṇatvaṃ citrāḥ śabdāśca pāvake । apākajaścāśītoṣṇo dhvaniścitraśca mārute ।। varṇātmako dhvaniḥ śabdapratibimbānyathāmbare ।
yattu na sparśavaddharmaḥ śabda ityādi bhaṇyate ।। kāṇādaistatsvapratītiviruddhaṃ kena gṛhyatām । paṭahe dhvanirityeva bhātyabādhitameva yat ।। na ca hetutvamātreṇa tadādānatvavedanāt ।
śrotraṃ cāsmanmate ahaṃkṛtkāraṇaṃ tatra tatra tat ।। vṛttibhāgīti taddeśaṃ śabdaṃ gṛhṇātyalaṃ tathā । yastvāha śrotramākāśaṃ karṇasaṃyogabheditam ।। śabdajaḥ śabda āgatya śabdabuddhiṃ prasūyate ।
tasya mande api murajadhvanāvākarṇake sati ।। amutra śrutireṣeti dūre saṃvedanaṃ katham । nahi śabdajaśabdasya dūrādūraravoditeḥ ।। śrotrākāśagatasyāsti dūrādūrasvabhāvatā ।
na cāsau prathamaḥ śabdastāvadvyāpīti yujyate ।। tatrasthaiḥ saha tīvrātmā śrūyamāṇastvanena tu । kathaṃ śrūyeta mandaḥsannahi dharmāntarāśrayaḥ ।। etaccānyairapākāri bahudheti vṛthā punaḥ ।
nāyastaṃ patitāghātadāne ko hi na paṇḍitaḥ ।। amīṣāṃ tu dharādīnāṃ yāvāṃstattvagaṇaḥ purā । guṇādhikatayā tiṣṭhan vyāptā tāvān prakāśate ।। vyāpyavyāpakatā yaiṣā tattvānāṃ darśitā kila ।
sā guṇādhikyataḥ siddhā na hetutvānna lāghavāt ।। ahetunāpi rāgo hi vyāpto vidyādinā sphuṭam । tadvinā na bhavedyattadvyāptamityucyate yataḥ ।। na lāghavaṃ ca nāmāsti kiṃcidatra svadarśane ।
guṇādhikyādato jñeyā vyāpyavyāpakatā sphuṭā ।। yo hi yasmādguṇotkṛṣṭaḥ sa tasmādūrdhva ucyate । ūrdhvatā vyāptṛtā śrīmanmālinīvijaye sphuṭā ।। ataḥ śivatvātprabhṛti prakāśatāsvarūpamādāya nijātmani dhruvam ।
samastatattvāvalidharmasaṃcayairvibhāti bhūrvyāptṛtayā sthitairalam ।। evaṃ jalāderapi śaktitattvaparyantadhāmno vapurasti tādṛk । kiṃ tūttaraṃ śaktitayaiva tattvaṃ pūrva tu taddharmatayeti bhedaḥ ।। anuttaraprakriyāyāṃ vaitatyena pradarśitam ।
etat tasmāt tataḥ paśyedvistarārthī vivecakaḥ ।। iti tattvasyarūpasya kṛtaṃ samyak prakāśanam ।। ucyate trikaśāstrekarahasyaṃ tattvabhedanam ।। teṣāmamīṣāṃ tattvānāṃ svavargeṣvanugāminām ।
bhedāntaramapi proktaṃ śāstre atra śrītrikābhidhe ।। śaktimacchaktibhedena dharādyaṃ mūlapaścimam । bhidyate pañcadaśadhā svarūpeṇa sahānarāt ।। kalāntaṃ bhedayugghīnaṃ rudravatpralayākalaḥ ।
tadvanmāyā ca navadhā jñākalāḥ saptadhā punaḥ ।। mantrāstadīśāḥ pāñcadhye mantreśapatayastridhā । śivo na bhidyate svaikaprakāśaghanacinmayaḥ ।। śivo mantramaheśeśamantrā akalayukkalī ।
śaktimantaḥ sapta tathā śaktayastaccaturdaśa ।। svaṃ svarūpaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tadbhūḥ pañcadaśātmikā । tathāhi tisro devasya śaktayo varṇitāḥ purā ।। tā eva mātṛmāmeyatrairūpyeṇa vyavasthitāḥ ।
parāṃśo mātṛrūpo atra pramāṇāṃśaḥ parāparaḥ ।। meyo aparaḥ śaktimāṃśca śaktiḥ svaṃ rūpamityadaḥ । tatra svarūpaṃ bhūmeryatpṛthagjaḍamavasthitam ।। mātṛmānādyupadhibhirasaṃjātoparāgakam ।
sakalādiśivāntaistu mātṛbhirvedyatāsya yā ।। śaktimadbhiranudbhūtaśaktibhiḥ sapta tadbhidaḥ । sakalādiśivāntānāṃ śaktiṣūdrecitātmasu ।। vedyatājanitāḥ sapta bhedā iti caturdaśa ।
sakalasya pramāṇāṃśo yo asau vidyākalātmakaḥ ।। sāmānyātmā sa śaktitve gaṇito natu tadbhidaḥ । layākalasya mānāṃśaḥ sa eva paramasphuṭaḥ ।। jñānākalasya mānaṃ tu galadvidyākalāvṛti ।
aśuddhavidyākalanādhvaṃsasaṃskārasaṃgatā ।। prabubhutsuḥ śuddhavidyā santrāṇāṃ karaṇaṃ bhavet । prabuddhā śuddhavidyā tu tatsaṃskāreṇa saṃgatā ।। mānaṃ mantreśvarāṇāṃ syāttatsaṃskāravivarjitā ।
mānaṃ mantramaheśānāṃ karaṇaṃ śaktirucyate ।। svātantryamātrasadbhāvā yā tvicchā śaktiraiśvarī । śivasya saiva karaṇaṃ tayā vetti karoti ca ।। ā śivātsakalāntaṃ ye mātāraḥ sapta te dvidhā ।
nyagbhūtodriktaśaktitvāttadbhedo vedyabhedakaḥ ।। tathāhi vedyatā nāma bhāvasyaiva nijaṃ vapuḥ । caitreṇa vedyaṃ vedmīti kiṃhyatra pratibhāsatām ।। nanu caitrīyavijñānamātramatra prakāśate ।
vedyatākhyastu no dharmo bhāti bhāvasya nīlavat ।। vedyatā ca svabhāvena dharmo bhāvasya cettataḥ । sarvānpratyeva vedyaḥ syāddhaṭanīlādidharmavat ।। atha vedakasaṃvittibalādvedyatvadharmabhāk ।
bhāvastathāpi doṣo asau kuvindakṛtavastravat ।। vedyatākhyastu yo dharmaḥ so avedyaścetkhapuṣpavat । vedyaścedasti tatrāpi vedyetatyanavasthitiḥ ।। tato na kiṃcidvedyaṃ syānmūrchitaṃ tu jagadbhavet ।
nanu vijñātrupādhyaṃ śo paskṛtaṃ vapurucyatām ।। bhāvasyārthaprakāśātma yathā jñānamidaṃ tvasat । ekavijñātṛvedyatve na jñātrantaravedyatā ।। samastajñātṛvedyatve naikavijñātṛvedyatā ।
tasmānna vedyatā nāma bhāvadharmo asti kaścana ।। bhāvasya vedyatā saiva saṃvido yaḥ samudbhavaḥ । arthagrahaṇarūpaṃ hi yatra vijñānamātmani ।। samavaiti prakāśyo arthastaṃ pratyeṣaiva vedyatā ।
atra brūmaḥ padārthānāṃ na dharmo yadi vedyatā ।। avedyā eva te saṃsyurjñāne satyapi varṇite । yathāhi pṛthubudhnādirūpe kumbhasya satyapi ।। atadātmā paṭo naiti pṛthubudhnādirūpatām ।
tathā satyapi vijñāne vijñātṛsamavāyini ।। avedyadharmakā bhāvāḥ kathaṃ vedyatvamāpnuyuḥ । anarthaḥ sumahāṃścaiṣa dṛśyatāṃ vastu yatsvayam ।। prakāśātma na tatsaṃviccāprakāśā tadāśrayaḥ ।
aprakāśo manodīpacakṣurādi tathaiva tat ।। kiṃ tatprakāśatāṃ nāma supte jagati sarvataḥ । jñānasyārthaprakāśatvaṃ nanu rūpaṃ pradīpavat ।। apūrvamatra viditaṃ narīnṛtyāmahe tataḥ ।
arthaprakāśo jñānasya yadrūpaṃ tannirūpyatām ।। arthaḥ prakāśaścedrūpamartho vā jñānameva vā । athārthasya prakāśo yastadrūpamiti bhaṇyate ।। ṣaṣṭhī kartari cedukto doṣa eva duruddharaḥ ।
atha karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhyeṣā ṇyarthastatra hṛdi sthitaḥ ।। tathā cedaṃ darśayāmaḥ kiṃ prakāśaḥ prakāśate । aprakāśo api naivāsau tathāpi ca na kiṃcana ।। tarhi loke kathaṃ ṇyarthaḥ ucyate cetanasthitau ।
mukhyo ṇyarthasya viṣayo jaḍeṣu tvaupacārikaḥ ।। tathāhi gantuṃ śakto api caitro anyāyattatāṃ gateḥ । manvāna eva vaktyasmi gamitaḥ svāmineti hi ।। svāmyapyasya gatau śaktiṃ buddhvā svādhīnatāṃ sphuṭam ।
paśyannivṛttimāśaṃkya gamayāmīti bhāṣate ।। preryaprerakayorevaṃ maulikī ṇyarthasaṃgatiḥ । tadabhiprāyato anyo api loke vyavaharettathā ।। śaraṃ gamayatītyatra punarvegākhyasaṃskriyām ।
vidadhatprerakammanya upacāreṇa jāyate ।। vāyuradriṃ pātayatītyatra dvāvapi tau jaḍau । draṣṭṛbhiḥ prerakapreryavapuṣā parikalpitau ।। itthaṃ jaḍena saṃbandhe na mukhyā ṇyarthasaṃgatiḥ ।
āstāmanyatra vitatametadvistarato mayā ।। arthe prakāśanā seyamupacārastato bhavet । astu cedbhāsate tarhi sa eva patadadrivat ।। upacāre nimittena kenāpi kila bhūyate ।
vāyuḥ pātayatītyatra nimittaṃ tatkṛtā kriyā ।। girau yenaiṣa saṃyoganāśādbhraṃśaṃ prapadyate । iha tu jñānamarthasya na kiṃcitkarameva tat ।। upacāraḥ kathaṃ nāma bhavetso api hyavastusan ।
aprakāśita evārthaḥ prakāśatvopacārataḥ ।। tādṛgeva śiśuḥ kiṃ hi dahatyagnyupacārataḥ । śiśau vahnyupacāre yadbījaṃ taikṣṇyādi tacca sat ।। prakāśatvopacāre tu kiṃ bījaṃ yatra satyatā ।
siddhe hi cetane yukta upacāraḥ sa hi sphuṭam ।। adhyāropātmakaḥ so api pratisaṃdhānajīvitaḥ । na cādyāpi kimapyasti cetanaṃ jñānamapyadaḥ ।। aprakāśaṃ tadanyena tatprakāśe apyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
nanu pradīpo rūpasya prakāśaḥ kathamīdṛśam ।। atrāpi na vahantyetāḥ kiṃ nu yuktivikalpanāḥ । yādṛśā svena rūpeṇa dīpo rūpaṃ prakāśayet ।। tādṛśā svayamapyeṣa bhāti jñānaṃ tu no tathā ।
pradīpaścaiṣa bhāvānāṃ prakāśatvaṃ dadā[dhā]tyalam ।। anyathā na prakāśerannabhede cedṛśo vidhiḥ । tasmātprakāśa evāyaṃ pūrvoktaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ ।। yathā yathā prakāśeta tattadbhāvavapuḥ sphuṭam ।
evaṃ ca nīlatā nāma yathā kācitprakāśate ।। tadvaccakāsti vedyatvaṃ tacca bhāvāṃśapṛṣṭhagam । phalaṃ prakaṭatārthasya saṃvidveti dvayaṃ tataḥ ।। vipakṣato rakṣitaṃ ca saṃdhānaṃ cāpi tanmithaḥ ।
tathāhi nibhṛtaścauraścaitravedyamiti sphuṭam ।। buddhvā nādatta evāśu parīpsāvivaśo api san । seyaṃ paśyati māṃ netratribhāgeneti sādaram ।। svaṃ dehamamṛteneva siktaṃ paśyati kāmukaḥ ।
na caitajjñānasaṃvittimātraṃ bhāvāṃśapṛṣṭhagam ।। arthakriyākaraṃ taccenna dharmaḥ konvasau bhavet । yaccoktaṃ vedyatādharmā bhāvaḥ sarvānapi prati ।। syādityetatsvapakṣaghnaṃ duṣprayogāstravattava ।
asmākaṃ tu svaprakāśaśivatāmātravādinām ।। anyaṃ prati cakāstīti vaca eva na vidyate । sarvānprati ca tannīlaṃ sa ghaṭaśceti yadvacaḥ ।। tadapyaviditaprāyaṃ gṛhītaṃ mugdhabuddhibhiḥ ।
nahi kālāgnirudrīyakāyāvagatanīlimā ।। tava nīlaḥ kiṃ nu pīto maivaṃ bhūnnatu nīlakaḥ । na kaṃcitprati nīlo asau nīlo vā yaṃ prati sthitaḥ ।। taṃ pratyeva sa vedyaḥ syātsaṃkalpadvārako antataḥ ।
yathā cārthaprakāśātma jñānaṃ saṃgīryate tvayā ।। tathā tajjñātṛvedyatvaṃ bhāvīyaṃ rūpamucyatām । na ca jñātātra niyataḥ kaścijjñāne yathā tava ।। arthe jñātā yadā yo yastadvedyaṃ vapurucyatām ।
tattadvijñātṛvedyatvaṃ sarvānpratyeva bhāsatām ।। ityevaṃ codayanmanye vrajedbadhiradhuryatām । nahyanyaṃ prati vai kaṃcidbhāti sā vedyatā tathā ।। bhāvasya rūpamityukte keyamasthānavaidhurī ।
anena nītimārgeṇa nirmūlamapasāritā ।। anavasthā tathā hyanyairnīlādyaiḥ sadṛśī na sā । vedyatā kiṃtu dharmo asau yadyogātsarvadharmavān ।। dharmī vedyatvamabhyeti sa sattāsamavāyavat ।
brūṣe yathā hi kurute sattā satyasataḥ sataḥ ।। samavāyo api saṃśliṣṭaḥ śliṣṭānaśliṣṭatājuṣaḥ । antyo viśeṣo vyāvṛttirūpo vyāvṛttivarjitān ।। vyāvṛttān śvetimā śuklamaśuklaṃ gamanaṃ tathā ।
tadvannīlādidharmāṃśayukto dharmī svayaṃ sthitaḥ ।। avedyo vedyatārūpāddharmādvedyatvamāgataḥ । vedyatā bhāsamānā ca svayaṃ nīlādidharmavat ।। aprakāśā svaprakāśāddharmādeti prakāśatām ।
prakāśe khalu viśrāntiṃ viśvaṃ śrayati cettataḥ ।। nānyā kācidapekṣāsya kṛtakṛtyasya sarvataḥ । yathā ca śivanāthena svātantryādbhāsyate bhidā ।। nīlādivattathaivāyaṃ vedyatā dharma ucyate ।
evaṃ siddhaṃ hi vedyatvaṃ bhāvadharmo astu kā ghṛṇā ।। idaṃ tu cintyaṃ sakalaparyantoktapramātṛbhiḥ । vedyatvamekarūpaṃ syāccāturdaśyamataḥ kutaḥ ।। ucyate paripūrṇaṃ cedbhāvīyaṃ rūpamucyate ।
tadvibhurbhairavo devo bhagavāneva bhaṇyate ।। atha tannijamāhātmyakalpitoṃ aśāṃśikākramaḥ । sahyate kiṃ kṛtaṃ tarhi proktakalpanayānayā ।। ata eva yadā yena vapuṣā bhāti yadyathā ।
tadā tathā tattadrūpamityeṣopaniṣatparā ।। caitreṇa vedyaṃ jānāmi dvābhyāṃ bahubhirapyatha । mantreṇa tanmaheśena śivenodriktaśaktinā ।। anyādṛśena vetyevaṃ bhāvo bhāti yathā tathā ।
arthakriyādivaicitryamabhyetyaparisaṃkhyayā ।। tathā hyekāgrasakalasāmājikajanaḥ khalu । nṛttaṃ gītaṃ sudhāsārasāgaratvena manyate ।। tata evocyate mallanaṭaprekṣopadeśane ।
sarvapramātṛtādātmyaṃ pūrṇarūpānubhāvakam ।। tāvanmātrārthasaṃvittituṣṭāḥ pratyekaśo yadi । kaḥ saṃbhūya guṇasteṣāṃ pramātraikyaṃ bhavecca kim ।। yadā tu tattadvedyatvadharmasaṃdarbhagarbhitam ।
tadvastu śuṣkātprāgrūpādanyadyuktamidaṃ tadā ।। śāstre api tattadvedyatvaṃ viśiṣṭārthakriyākaram । bhūyasaiva tathāca śrīmālinīvijayottare ।। tathā ṣaḍvidhamadhvānamanenādhiṣṭhitaṃ smaret ।
adhiṣṭhānaṃ hi devena yadviśvasya pravedanam ।। tadīśavedyatvenetthaṃ jñātaṃ prakṛtakāryakṛt । evaṃ siddhaṃ vedyatākhyo dharmo bhāvasya bhāsate ।। tadanābhāsayoge tu svarūpamiti bhaṇyate ।
upādhiyogitāśaṅkāmapahastayato asphuṭam ।। svātmano yena vapuṣā bhātyarthastatsvakaṃ vapuḥ । jānāmi ghaṭamityatra vedyatānuparāgavān ।। ghaṭa eva svarūpeṇa bhāta ityapadiśyate ।
nanu tatra svayaṃvedyabhāvo mantrādyapekṣayā ।। api cāstyeva nanvastu natu sanpratibhāsate । avedyameva kālāgnivapurmeroḥ parā diśaḥ ।। mameti saṃvidi paraṃ śuddhaṃ vastu prakāśate ।
bhātatvādvedyamapi tanna vedyatvena bhāsanāt ।। avedyameva bhānaṃ hi tathā kamanuyuñjmahe । evaṃ pañcadaśātmeyaṃ dharā tadvajjalādayaḥ ।। avyaktāntā yato astyeṣāṃ sakalaṃ prati vedyatā ।
yattūcyate kalādyena dharāntena samanvitāḥ ।। sakalā iti tatkośaṣaṭkodrekopalakṣaṇam । udbhūtāśuddhacidrāgakalādirasakañcukāḥ ।। sakalālayasaṃjñāstu nyagbhūtākhilakañcukāḥ ।
jñānākalāstu dhvastaitatkañcukā iti nirṇayaḥ ।। tena pradhāne vedye api pumānudbhūtakañcukaḥ । pramātāstyeva sakalaḥ pāñcadaśyamataḥ sthitam ।। pāñcadaśyaṃ dharādhantarniviṣṭe sakale api ca ।
sakalāntaramastyeva prameye atrāpi mātṛ hi ।। sthūlāvṛtādisaṃkocatadanyavyāptṛtājuṣaḥ । pītādyāḥ sthirakampratvāccaturdaśa dharādiṣu ।। svarūpībhūtajaḍatāḥ prāṇadehapathe tataḥ ।
pramātṛtājuṣaḥ proktā dhāraṇā vijayottare ।। yadā tu meyatā puṃsaḥ kalāntasya prakalpyate । tadudbhūtaḥ kañcukāṃśo meyo nāsya pramātṛtā ।। ataḥ sakalasaṃjñasya pramātṛtvaṃ na vidyate ।
trayodaśatvaṃ tacchaktiśaktimaddvayavarjanāt ।। nyagbhūtakañcuko mātā yukta[yata]statra layākalaḥ । māyāniviṣṭo vijñānākalādyāḥ prāgvadeva tu ।। māyātattve jñeyarūpe kañcukanyagbhavo api yaḥ ।
so api meyaḥ kañcukaikyaṃ yato māyā susūkṣmikā ।। vijñānākala evātra tato mātāpakañcukaḥ । māyāniviṣṭe apyakale tathetyekādaśātmatā ।। vijñānakevale vedye kañcukadhvaṃsasusthite ।
udbubhūṣuprabodhānāṃ mantrāṇāmeva mātṛtā ।। te api mantrā yadā meyāstadā mātā tadīśvaraḥ । sa hyudbhavātpūrṇabodhastasminprāpte tu meyatām ।। udbhūtapūrṇarūpo asau mātā mantramaheśvaraḥ ।
tasminvijñeyatāṃ prāpte svaprakāśaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ ।। pramātā svakatādātmyabhāsitākhilavedyakaḥ । śivaḥ pramātā no meyo hyanyādhīnaprakāśatā ।। meyatā sā na tatrāsti svaprakāśo hyasau prabhuḥ ।
svaprakāśe atra kasmiṃścidanabhyupagate sati ।। aprakāśātprakāśatve hyanavasthā duruttarā । tataśca suptaṃ viśvaṃ syānna caivaṃ bhāsate hi tat ।। anyādhīnaprakāśaṃ hi tadbhātyanyastvasau śivaḥ ।
ityasya svaprakāśatve kimanyairyuktiḍambaraiḥ ।। mānānāṃ hi paro jīvaḥ sa evetyuktamāditaḥ । nanvasti svaprakāśe api śive vedyatvamīdṛśaḥ ।। upadeśo[śyo]padeṣṭṛtvavyavahāro anyathā katham ।
satyaṃ sa tu tathā sṛṣṭaḥ parameśena vedyatām ।। nīto mantramaheśādikakṣyāṃ samadhiśāyyate । tathābhūtaśca vedyo asau nānavacchinnasaṃvidaḥ ।। pūrṇasya vedyatā yuktā parasparavirodhataḥ ।
tathā vedyasvabhāve api vastuto na śivātmatām ।। ko api bhāvaḥ projjhatīti satyaṃ tadbhāvanā phalet । śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ śivaḥ sākṣānna bhidyate ।। sākṣātpadenāyamarthaḥ samastaḥ prasphuṭīkṛtaḥ ।
nanvekarūpatāyuktaḥ śivastadvaśato bhavet ।। trivedatāmantramahānāthe kātra vivāditā । maheśvareśamantrāṇāṃ tathā kevalinordvayoḥ ।। anantabhedataikaikaṃ sthitā sakalavatkila ।
tato layākale meye pramātāsti layākalaḥ ।। atastrayodaśatvaṃ syāditthaṃ naikādaśātmatā । vijñānākalavedyatve apyanyo jñānākalo bhavet ।। mātā tadekādaśatā syānnaiva tu navātmatā ।
evaṃ mantratadīśānāṃ mantreśāntarasaṃbhave ।। vedyatvānnava sapta syuḥ sapta pañca tu te katham । ucyate satyamastyeṣā kalanā kiṃtu susphuṭaḥ ।। yathātra sakale bhedo na tathā tvakalādike ।
anantāvāntaredṛkṣayonibhedavataḥ sphuṭam ।। caturdaśavidhasyāsya sakalasyāsti bheditā । layākale tu saṃskāramātrātsatyapyasau bhidā ।। akalena viśeṣāya sakalasyaiva yujyate ।
vijñānakevalādīnāṃ tāvatyapi na vai bhidā ।। śivasvācchandyamātraṃ tu bhedāyaiṣāṃ vijṛmbhate । ityāśayena saṃpaśyanviśeṣaṃ sakalādiha ।। layākalādau novāca trāyodaśyādikaṃ vibhuḥ ।
nanvastu vedyatā bhāvadharmaḥ kiṃtu layākalau ।। manvāte neha vai kiṃcittadapekṣā tvasau katham । śrūyatāṃ saṃvidaikātmyatattve asminsaṃvyavasthite ।। jaḍe api citirastyeva bhotsyamāne tu kā kathā ।
svabodhāvasare tāvadbhotsyate layakevalī ।। dvividhaśca prabodho asya mantratvāya bhavāya ca । bhāvanādibalādanyavaiṣṇavādinayoditāt ।। yathāsvamādharauttaryavicitrātsaṃskṛtastathā ।
līnaḥ prabuddho mantratvaṃ tadīśatvamathaiti vā ।। svātantryavarjitā ye tu balānmohavaśīkṛtāḥ । layākalātsvasaṃskārātprabuddhyante bhavāya te ।। jñānākalo api mantreśamaheśatvāya budhyate ।
mantrāditvāya vā jātu jātu saṃsṛtaye api vā ।। avatāro hi vijñāniyogibhāve asya bhidyate । uktaṃ ca bodhayāmāsa sa sisṛkṣurjagatprabhuḥ ।। vijñānakevalānaṣṭāviti śrīpūrvaśāsane ।
ataḥ prabhotsyamānatve yānayorbodhayogyatā ।। tadbalādvedyatāyogyabhāvenaivātra vedyatā । tathāhi gāḍhanidre api priye anāśaṅkitāgatām ।। māṃ drakṣyatīti nāṅgeṣu sveṣu mātyabhisārikā ।
evaṃ śivo api manute etasyaitatpravedyatām ।। yāsyatīti sṛjāmīti tadānīṃ yogyataiva sā । vedyatā tasya bhāvasya bhoktṛtā tāvatī ca sā ।। layākalasya citro hi bhogaḥ kena vikalpyate ।
yathā yathā hi samvittiḥ sa hi bhogaḥ sphuṭo asphuṭaḥ ।। smṛtiyogyo apyanyathā vā bhogyabhāvaṃ na tūjjhati । gāḍhanidrāvimūḍho api kāntāliṅgitavigrahaḥ ।। bhoktaiva bhaṇyate so api manute bhoktṛtāṃ purā ।
utprekṣāmātrahīno api kāṃcitkulavadhūṃ puraḥ ।। saṃbhokṣyamāṇāṃ dṛṣṭvaiva rabhasādyāti saṃmadam । tāmeva dṛṣṭvā ca tadā samānāśayabhāgapi ।। anyastathā na saṃvitte kamatropalabhāmahe ।
loke rūḍhamidaṃ dṛṣṭirasminkāraṇamantarā ।। prasīdatīva magneva nirvātīvetivādini । itthaṃ vistaratastattvabhedo ayaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। śaktiśaktimatāṃ bhedādanyonyaṃ tatkṛteṣvapi ।
bhedeṣvanyonyato bhedāttathā tattvāntaraiḥ saha ।। bhedopabhedagaṇanāṃ karvato nāvadhiḥ kvacit । tata eva vicitro ayaṃ bhuvanādividhiḥ sthitaḥ ।। pārthivatve api no sāmyaṃ rudravaiṣṇavalokayoḥ ।
kā kathānyatra tu bhavedbhoge vāpi svarūpake ।। sa ca no vistaraḥ sākṣācchakyo yadyapi bhāṣitum । tathāpi mārgamātreṇa kathyamāno vivicyatām ।। saptānāṃ mātṛśaktīnāmanyonyaṃ bhedane sati ।
rūpamekānnapañcāśatsvarūpaṃ cādhikaṃ tataḥ ।। sarvaṃ sarvātmakaṃ yasmāttasmātsakalamātari । layākalādiśaktīnāṃ saṃbhavo astyeva tattvataḥ ।। sa tvasphuṭo astu bhedāṃśaṃ dātuṃ tāvatprabhurbhavet ।
teṣāmapi ca bhedānāmanyonyaṃ bahubhedatā ।। mukhyānāṃ bhedabhedānāṃ jalādyairbhedane sati । mukhyabhedaprakāreṇa vidherānantyamucyate ।। sakalasya samudbhūtāścakṣurādisvaśaktayaḥ ।
nyagbhūtāśca pratanvanti bhedāntaramapi sphuṭam ।। evaṃ layākalādīnāṃ tatsaṃskārapadoditāt । pāṭavātprakṣayādvāpi bhedāntaramudīyate ।। nyakkṛtāṃ śaktimāsthāyāpyudāsīnatayā sthitim ।
anāviśyeva yadvetti tatrānyā vedyatā khalu ।। āviśyeva nimajjyeva vikāsyeva vighūrṇya ca । vidato vedyatānyaiva bhedo atrārthakriyocitaḥ ।। anyaśaktitirobhāve kasyāścitsusphuṭodaye ।
bhedāntaramapi jñeyaṃ vīṇāvādakadṛṣṭivat ।। tirobhāvodbhavau śakteḥ svaśaktyantarato anyataḥ । cetyamānādacetyādvā tanvāte bahubhedatām ।। evametaddharādīnāṃ tattvānāṃ yāvatī daśā ।
kācidasti ghaṭākhyāpi tatra saṃdarśitā bhidaḥ ।। atrāpi vedyatā nāma tādātmyaṃ vedakaiḥ saha । tataḥ sakalavedyo asau ghaṭaḥ sakala eva hi ।। yāvacchivaikavedyo asau śiva evāvabhāsate ।
tāvadekaśarīro hi bodho bhātyeva yāvatā ।। adhunātra samastasya dharātattvasya darśyate । sāmastya evābhihitaṃ pāñcadaśyaṃ puroditam ।। dharātattvāvibhedena yaḥ prakāśaḥ prakāśate ।
sa eva śivanātho atra pṛthivī brahma tanmatam ।। dharātattvagatāḥ siddhīrvitarītuṃ samudyatān । prerayanti śivecchāto ye te mantramaheśvarāḥ ।। preryamāṇāstu mantreśā mantrāstadvācakāḥ sphuṭam ।
dharātattvagataṃ yogamabhyasya śivavidyayā ।। na tu pāśavasāṃkhyīyavaiṣṇavādidvitādṛśā । aprāptadhruvadhāmāno vijñānākalatājuṣaḥ ।। tāvattattvopabhogena ye kalpānte layaṃ gatāḥ ।
sauṣuptāvasthayopetāste atra pralayakevalāḥ ।। sauṣupte tattvalīnatvaṃ sphuṭameva hi lakṣyate । anyathā niyatasvapnasaṃdṛṣṭirjāyate kutaḥ ।। sauṣuptamapi citraṃ ca svacchāsvacchādi bhāsate ।
asvāpsaṃ sukhamityādismṛtivaicitryadarśanāt ।। yadaiva sa kṣaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ nidrāyaiva prabuddhyate । tadaiva smṛtireṣeti nārthajajñānajā smṛtiḥ ।। tena mūḍhairyaducyeta prabuddhasyāntarāntarā ।
tūlikādisukhasparśasmṛtireṣeti tatkutaḥ ।। māhākarmasamullāsasaṃmiśritamalābilāḥ । dharādhirohiṇo jñeyāḥ sakalā iha pudgalāḥ ।। asyaiva saptakasya svasvavyāpāraprakalpane ।
prakṣobho yastadevoktaṃ śaktīnāṃ saptakaṃ sphuṭam ।। śivo hyacyutacidrūpastisrastacchaktayastu yāḥ । tāḥ svātantryavaśopāttagrahītrākāratāvaśāt ।। tridhā mantrāvasānāḥ syurudāsīnā iva sthitāḥ ।
grāhyākāroparāgāttu grahītrākāratāvaśāt ।। sakalāntāstu tāstisra icchājñānakriyā matāḥ । saptadhetthaṃ pramātṛtvaṃ tatkṣobho mānatā tathā ।। yattu grahītṛtārūpasaṃvitsaṃsparśavarjitam ।
śuddhaṃ jaḍaṃ tatsvarūpamitthaṃ viśvaṃ trikātmakam ।। evaṃ jalādyapi vadedbhedairbhinnaṃ mahāmatiḥ । anayā tu diśā prāyaḥ sarvabhedeṣu vidyate ।। bhedo mantramaheśānteṣveṣa pañcadaśātmakaḥ ।
tathāpi sphuṭatābhāvātsannapyeṣa na carcitaḥ ।। etacca sūtritaṃ dhātrā śrīpūrve yadbravīti hi । savyāpārādhipatvenetyādinā jāgradāditām ।। abhinne api śive antaḥsthasūkṣmabodhānusārataḥ ।
adhunā prāṇaśaktisthe tattvajāle vivicyate ।। bhedo ayaṃ pāñcadaśyādiryathā śrīśaṃbhurādiśat । samaste arthe atra nirgrāhye tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśa kṣaṇāḥ ।। ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule cāre sāṃśadvyaṅgulakalpitāḥ ।
tatrādyaḥ paramādvaito nirvibhāgarasātmakaḥ ।। dvitīyo grāhakollāsarūpaḥ prativibhāvyate । antyastu grāhyatādātmyātsvarūpībhāvamāgataḥ ।। pravibhāvyo na hi pṛthagupāntyo grāhakaḥ kṣaṇaḥ ।
tṛtīyaṃ kṣaṇamārabhya kṣaṇaṣaṭkaṃ tu yatsthitam ।। tannirvikalpaṃ prodgacchadvikalpācchādanātmakam । tadeva śivarūpaṃ hi paraśaktyātmakaṃ viduḥ ।। dvitīyaṃ madhyamaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ parāparapadātmakam ।
vikalparūḍhirapyeṣā kramātprasphuṭatāṃ gatā ।। ṣaṭke atra prathame devyastisraḥ pronmeṣavṛttitām । nimeṣavṛttitāṃ cāśu spṛśantyaḥ ṣaṭkatāṃ gatāḥ ।। evaṃ dvitīyaṣaṭke api kiṃ tvatra grāhyavartmanā ।
uparāgapadaṃ prāpya parāparatayā sthitāḥ ।। ādye atra ṣaṭke tā devyaḥ svātantryollāsamātrataḥ । jighṛkṣite apyupādhau syuḥ pararūpādavicyutāḥ ।। asti cātiśayaḥ kaścittāsāmapyuttarottaram ।
yo vivekadhanairdhīraiḥ sphuṭīkṛtyāpi darśyate ।। kecittvekāṃ tuṭiṃ grāhye caikāmapi grahītari । tādātmyena vinikṣipya saptakaṃ saptakaṃ viduḥ ।। tadasyāṃ sūkṣmasaṃvittau kalanāya samudyatāḥ ।
saṃvedayante yadrūpaṃ tatra kiṃ vāgvikatthanaiḥ ।। evaṃ dharādimūlāntaṃ prakriyā prāṇagāminī । guruparvakramātproktā bhede pañcadaśātmake ।। kramāttu bhedanyūnatve nyūnatā syāttuṭiṣvapi ।
tasyāṃ hrāso vikalpasya sphuṭatā cāvikalpinaḥ ।। yathā hi ciraduḥkhārtaḥ paścādāttasukhasthitiḥ । vismaratyeva tadduḥkhaṃ sukhaviśrāntivartmanā ।। tathā gatavikalpe api rūḍhāḥ saṃvedane janāḥ ।
vikalpaviśrāntibalāttāṃ sattāṃ nābhimanvate ।। vikalpanirhrāsavaśena yāti vikalpavandhyā paramārthasatyā । saṃvitsvarūpaprakaṭatvamitthaṃ tatrāvadhāne yatatāṃ subuddhiḥ ।। grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittau saṃbandhe sāvadhānatā ।
iyaṃ sā tatra tatroktā sarvakāmadughā yataḥ ।। evaṃ dvayaṃ dvayaṃ yāvannyūnībhavati bhedagam । tāvattuṭidvayaṃ yāti nyūnatāṃ kramaśaḥ sphuṭam ।। ata eva śivāveśe dvituṭiḥ parigīyate ।
ekā tu sā tuṭistatra pūrṇā śuddhaiva kevalam ।। dvitīyā śiva rūpaiva sarvajñānakriyātmikā । tasyāmavahito yogī kiṃ na vetti karoti vā ।। tathā coktaṃ kallaṭena śrīmatā tuṭipātagaḥ ।
lābhaḥ sarvajñakartṛtve tuṭeḥ pāto aparā tuṭiḥ ।। ādyāyāṃ tu tuṭau sarvaṃ sarvataḥ pūrṇamekatām । gataṃ kiṃ tatra vedyaṃ vā kāryaṃ vā vyapadeśabhāk ।। ato bhedasamullāsakalāṃ prāthamikīṃ budhāḥ ।
cinvanti pratibhāṃ devīṃ sarvajñatvādisiddhaye ।। saiva śaktiḥ śivasyoktā tṛtīyādituṭiṣvatha । mantrādi nāthatacchaktimantreśādyāḥ kramoditāḥ ।। tāsu saṃdadhataścittamavadhānaikadharmakam ।
tattatsiddhisamāveśaḥ svayamevopajāyate ।। ata eva yathā bhedabahutvaṃ dūratā tathā । saṃvittau tuṭibāhulyādakṣārthāsaṃnikarṣavat ।। yathā yathā hi nyūnatvaṃ tuṭīnāṃ hrāsato bhidaḥ ।
tathā tathātinaikaṭyaṃ saṃvidaḥ syācchivāvadhi ।। śivatattvamataḥ proktamantikaṃ sarvato amutaḥ । ata eva prayatno ayaṃ tatpraveśe na vidyate ।। yathā yathā hi dūratvaṃ yatnayogastathā tathā ।
bhāvanākaraṇādīnāṃ śive niravakāśatām ।। ata eva hi manyante saṃpradāyadhanā janāḥ । tathā hi dṛśyatāṃ loko ghaṭādervedane yathā ।। prayatnavānivābhāti tathā kiṃ sukhavedane ।
āntaratvamidaṃ prāhuḥ saṃvinnaikaṭyaśālitām ।। tāṃ ca cidrūpatonmeṣaṃ bāhyatvaṃ tannimeṣatām । bhavināṃ tvantiko apyevaṃ na bhātītyatidūratā ।। dūre api hyantikībhūte bhānaṃ syāttvatra tatkatham ।
na ca bījāṅkuralatādalapuṣpaphalādivat ।। kramikeyaṃ bhavetsaṃvitsūtastatra kilāṅkuraḥ । bījāllatā tvaṅkurānno bījādiha sarvataḥ ।। saṃvittattvaṃ bhāsamānaṃ paripūrṇaṃ hi sarvataḥ ।
sarvasya kāraṇaṃ proktaṃ sarvatraivoditaṃ yataḥ ।। tata eva ghaṭe apyeṣā prāṇavṛttiryadi sphuret । viśrāmyeccāśu tatraiva śivabīje layaṃ vrajet ।। na tu kramikatā kācicchivātmatve kadācana ।
anyanmantrādi nāthādi kāraṇaṃ tattu saṃnidheḥ ।। śivābhedācca kiṃ cātha dvaite naikaṭyavedanāt । anayā ca diśā sarva sarvadā pravivecayan ।। bhairavāyata eva drāk ciccakreśvaratāṃ gataḥ ।
sa itthaṃ prāṇago bhedaḥ khecarīcakragopitaḥ ।। mayā prakaṭitaḥ śrīmacchāmbhavājñānuvartinā । atraivādhvani vedyatvaṃ prāpte yā saṃvidudbhavet ।। tasyāḥ svakaṃ yadvaicitryaṃ tadavasthāpadābhidham ।
jāgratsvapnaḥ suṣuptaṃ ca turyaṃ ca tadatītakam ।। iti pañca padānyāhurekasminvedake sati । tatra yaiṣā dharātattvācchivāntā tattvapaddhatiḥ ।। tasyāmekaḥ pramātā cedavaśyaṃ jāgradādikam ।
taddarśyate śaṃbhunāthaprasādādviditaṃ mayā ।। yadadhiṣṭheyameveha nādhiṣṭhātṛ kadācana । saṃvedanagataṃ vedyaṃ tajjāgratsamudāhṛtam ।। caitramaitrādibhūtāni tattvāni ca dharāditaḥ ।
abhidhākaraṇībhūtāḥ śabdāḥ kiṃ cābhidhā pramā ।। pramātṛmeyatanmānapramārūpaṃ catuṣṭayam । viśvametadadhiṣṭheyaṃ yadā jāgrattadā smṛtam ।। tathā hi bhāsate yattannīlamantaḥ pravedane ।
saṃkalparūpe bāhyasya tadadhiṣṭhātṛ bodhakam ।। yattu bāhyatayā nīlaṃ cakāstyasya na vidyate । kathaṃcidapyadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvastajjāgraducyate ।। tatra caitre bhāsamāne yo dehāṃśaḥ sa kathyate ।
abuddho yastu mānāṃśaḥ sa buddho mitikārakaḥ ।। prabuddhaḥ suprabuddhaśca pramāmātreti ca kramaḥ । cāturvidhyaṃ hi piṇḍasthanāmni jāgrati kīrtitam ।। jāgradādi catuṣkaṃ hi pratyekamiha vidyate ।
jāgrajjāgradabuddhaṃ tajjāgratsvapnastu buddhatā ।। ityādi turyātītaṃ tu sarvagatvātpṛthakkutaḥ । uktaṃ ca piṇḍagaṃ jāgradabuddhaṃ buddhameva ca ।। prabuddhaṃ suprabuddhaṃ ca caturvidhamidaṃ smṛtam ।
meyabhūmiriyaṃ mukhyā jāgradākhyānyadantarā ।। bhūtatattvābhidhānānāṃ yoṃ aśo adhiṣṭheya ucyate । piṇḍasthamiti taṃ prāhuriti śrīmālinīmate ।। laukikī jāgradityeṣā saṃjñā piṇḍasthamityapi ।
yogināṃ yogasiddhyarthaṃ saṃjñeyaṃ paribhāṣyate ।। adhiṣṭheyasamāpattimadhyāsīnasya yoginaḥ । tādātmyaṃ kila piṇḍasthaṃ mitaṃ piṇḍaṃ hi piṇḍitam ।। prasaṃkhyānaikarūḍhānāṃ jñānināṃ tu taducyate ।
sarvatobhadramāpūrṇaṃ sarvato vedyasattayā ।। sarvasattāsamāpūrṇa viśvaṃ paśyedyato yataḥ । jñānī tatastataḥ saṃvittatvamasya prakāśate ।। lokayogaprasaṃkhyānatrairūpyavaśataḥ kila ।
nāmāni trīṇi bhaṇyante svapnādiṣvapyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। yattvadhiṣṭhānakaraṇabhāvamadhyāsya vartate । vedyaṃ satpūrvakathitaṃ bhūtatattvābhidhāmayam ।। tatsvapno mukhyato jñeyaṃ tacca vaikalpike pathi ।
vaikalpikapathārūḍhavedyasāmyāvabhāsanāt ।। lokarūḍho apyasau svapnaḥ sāmyaṃ cābāhyarūpatā । utprekṣāsvapnasaṃkalpasmṛtyunmādādidṛṣṭiṣu ।। vispaṣṭaṃ yadvedyajātaṃ jāgranmukhyatayaiva tat ।
yattu tatrāpyavispaṣṭaṃ spaṣṭādhiṣṭhātṛ bhāsate ।। vikalpāntaragaṃ vedyaṃ tatsvapnapadamucyate । tadaiva tasya vettyeva svayameva hyabāhyatām ।। pramātrantarasādhārabhāvahānyasthirātmate ।
tatrāpi cāturvidhyaṃ tat prāgdiśaiva prakalpayet ।। gatāgataṃ suvikṣiptaṃ saṃgataṃ susamāhitam । atrāpi pūrvavannāma laukikaṃ svapna ityadaḥ ।। bāhyābhimatabhāvānāṃ svāpo hyagrahaṇaṃ matam ।
sarvādhvanaḥ padaṃ prāṇaḥ saṃkalpo avagamātmakaḥ ।। padaṃ ca tatsamāpatti padasthaṃ yogino viduḥ । vedyasattāṃ bahirbhūtāmanapekṣyaiva sarvataḥ ।। vedye svātantryabhāg jñānaṃ svapnaṃ vyāptitayā bhajet ।
mānabhūmiriyaṃ mukhyā svapno hyāmarśanātmakaḥ ।। vedyacchāyo avabhāso hi meye adhiṣṭhānamucyate । yattvadhiṣṭhātṛbhūtādeḥ pūrvoktasya vapurdhruvam ।। bījaṃ viśvasya tattūṣṇīṃbhūtaṃ sauṣuptamucyate ।
anubhūtau vikalpe ca yo asau draṣṭā sa eva hi ।। na bhāvagrahaṇaṃ tena suṣṭhu suptatvamucyate । tatsāmyāllaukikīṃ nidrāṃ suṣuptaṃ manvate budhāḥ ।। bījabhāvo athāgrahaṇaṃ sāmyaṃ tūṣṇīṃsvabhāvatā ।
mukhyā mātṛdaśā seyaṃ suṣuptākhyā nigadyate ।। rūpakatvācca rūpaṃ tattādātmyaṃ yoginaḥ punaḥ । rūpasthaṃ tatsamāpattyaudāsīnyaṃ rūpiṇāṃ viduḥ ।। prasaṃkhyānavataḥ kāpi vedyasaṃkocanātra yat ।
nāsti tena mahāvyāptiriyaṃ tadanusārataḥ ।। udāsīnasya tasyāpi vedyaṃ yena caturvidham । bhūtādi tadupādhyutthamatra bhedacatuṣṭayam ।। uditaṃ vipulaṃ śāntaṃ suprasannamathāparam ।
yattu pramātmakaṃ rūpaṃ pramāturupari sthitam ।। pūrṇatāgamanaunmukhyamaudāsīnyātparicyutiḥ । tatturyamucyate śaktisamāveśo hyasau mataḥ ।। sā saṃvitsvaprakāśā tu kaiściduktā prameyataḥ ।
mānānmātuśca bhinnaiva tadarthaṃ tritayaṃ yataḥ ।। meyaṃ māne mātari tat so api tasyāṃ mitau sphuṭam । viśrāmyatīti saivaiṣā devī viśvaikajīvitam ।। rūpaṃ dṛśāhamityaṃśatrayamuttīrya vartate ।
dvāramātrāśritopāyā paśyāmītyanupāyikā ।। pramātṛtā svatantratvarūpā seyaṃ prakāśate । saṃvitturīyarūpaivaṃ prakāśātmā svayaṃ ca sā ।। tatsamāveśatādātmye mātṛtvaṃ bhavati sphuṭam ।
tatsamāveśoparāgānmānatvaṃ meyatā punaḥ ।। tatsamāveśanaikaṭyāttrayaṃ tattadanugrahāt । vedyādibhedagalanāduktā seyamanāmayā ।। mātrādyanugrahādā nātsavyāpāreti bhaṇyate ।
jāgradādyapi devasya śaktitvena vyavasthitam ।। aparaṃ parāparaṃ ca dvidhā tatsā parā tviyam । rūpakatvādudāsīnāccyuteyaṃ pūrṇatonmukhī ।। daśā tasyāṃ samāpattī rūpātītaṃ tu yoginaḥ ।
pūrṇataunmukhyayogitvādviśvaṃ paśyati tanmayaḥ ।। prasaṃkhyātā pracayatasteneyaṃ pracayo matā । naitasyāmaparā turyadaśā saṃbhāvyate kila ।। saṃvinna kila vedyā sā vittvenaiva hi bhāsate ।
jāgradādyāstu saṃbhāvyāstisro asyāḥ prāgdaśā yataḥ ।। tritayānugrahātseyaṃ tenoktā trikaśāsane । manonmanamanantaṃ ca sarvārthamiti bhedataḥ ।। yattu pūrṇānavacchinnavapurānandanirbharam ।
turyātītaṃ tu tatprāhustadeva paramaṃ padam ।। nātra yogasya sadbhāvo bhāvanāderabhāvataḥ । aprameye aparicchinne svatantre bhāvyatā kutaḥ ।। yogādyabhāvatastena nāmāsminnādiśadvibhuḥ ।
prasaṃkhyānabalāttvetadrūpaṃ pūrṇatvayogataḥ ।। anuttarādiha proktaṃ mahāpracayasaṃjñitam । pūrṇatvādeva bhedānāmasyāṃ saṃbhāvanā na hi ।। tannirāsāya naitasyāṃ bheda ukto viśeṣaṇam ।
satatoditamityetatsarvavyāpitvasūcakam ।। na hyeka eva bhavati bhedaḥ kvacana kaścana । turyātīte bheda ekaḥ satatodita ityayam ।। mūḍhavādastena siddhamavibheditvamasya tu ।
śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ padasthamaparaṃ viduḥ ।। mantrāstatpatayaḥ seśā rūpasthamiti kīrtyate । rūpātītaṃ parā śaktiḥ savyāpārāpyanāmayā ।। niṣprapañco nirābhāsaḥ śuddhaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ ।
sarvātītaḥ śivo jñeyo yaṃ viditvā vimucyate ।। iti śrīsumatiprajñācandrikāśāntatāmasaḥ । śrīśaṃbhunāthaḥ sadbhāvaṃ jāgradādau nyarūpayat ।। anye tu kathayantyeṣāṃ bhaṅgīmanyādṛśīṃ śritāḥ ।
yadrūpaṃ jāgradādīnāṃ tadidānīṃ nirūpyate ।। tatrākṣavṛttimāśritya bāhyākāragraho hi yaḥ । tajjāgratsphuṭamāsīnamanubandhi punaḥ punaḥ ।। ātmasaṃkalpanirmāṇaṃ svapno jāgradviparyayaḥ ।
layākalasya bhogo asau malakarmavaśānnatu ।। sthirībhavenniśābhāvātsuptaṃ saukhyādyavedane । jñānākalasya malataḥ kevalādbhogamātrataḥ ।। bhedavantaḥ svato abhinnāścikīrṣyante jaḍājaḍāḥ ।
turye tatra sthitā mantratannāthādhīśvarāstrayaḥ ।। yāvadbhairavabodhāntaḥpraveśanasahiṣṇavaḥ । bhāvā vigaladātmīyasārāḥ svayamabhedinaḥ ।। turyātītapade saṃsyuriti pañcadaśātmake ।
yasya yadyatsphuṭaṃ rūpaṃ tajjāgraditi manyatām ।। yadevāsthiramābhāti sapūrvaṃ svapna īdṛśaḥ । asphuṭaṃ tu yadābhāti suptaṃ tattatpuro api yat ।। trayasyāsyānusaṃdhistu yadvaśādupajāyate ।
sraksūtrakalpaṃ tatturyaṃ sarvabhedeṣu gṛhyatām ।। yattvadvaitabharollāsadrāvitāśeṣabhedakam । turyātītaṃ tu tatprāhuritthaṃ sarvatra yojayet ।। layākale tu svaṃ rūpaṃ jāgrattatpūrvavṛtti tu ।
svapnādīti kramaṃ sarvaṃ sarvatrānusaredbudhaḥ ।। ekatrāpi prabhau pūrṇe citturyātītamucyate । ānandasturyamicchaiva bījabhūmiḥ suṣuptatā ।। jñānaśaktiḥ svapna uktaḥ kriyāśaktistu jāgṛtiḥ ।
na caivamupacāraḥ syātsarvaṃ tatraiva vastutaḥ ।। na cenna kvāpi mukhyatvaṃ nopacāro api tatkvacit । etacchrīpūrvaśāstre ca sphuṭamuktaṃ maheśinā ।। tatra svarūpaṃ śaktiśca sakalaśceti tattrayam ।
iti jāgradavastheyaṃ bhede pañcadaśātmake ।। akalau svapnasauṣupte turyaṃ mantrādivargabhāk । turyātītaṃ śaktiśaṃbhū trayodaśābhidhe punaḥ ।। svarūpaṃ jāgradanyattu prāgvatpralayakevale ।
svaṃ jāgratsvapnasupte dve turyādyatra ca pūrvavat ।। vijñānākalabhede api svaṃ mantrā mantranāyakāḥ । tadīśāḥ śaktiśaṃbhvitthaṃ pañca syurjāgradādayaḥ ।। saptabhede tu mantrākhye svaṃ mantreśā maheśvarāḥ ।
śaktiḥ śaṃbhuśca pañcoktā avasthā jāgradādayaḥ ।। svarūpaṃ mantramāheśī śaktirmantramaheśvaraḥ । śaktiḥ śaṃbhurimāḥ pañca mantreśe pañcabhedake ।। svaṃ kriyā jñānamicchā ca śaṃbhuratra ca pañcamī ।
