maheśabhede trividhe jāgradādi nirūpitam ।। vyāpārādādhipatyācca taddhānyā prerakatvataḥ । icchānivṛtteḥ svasthatvācchiva eko api pañcadhā ।। ityeṣa darśito asmābhistattvādhvā vistarādatha ।
kalādhvā vakṣyate śrīmacchāṃbhavājñānusārataḥ ।। yathā pūrvoktabhuvanamadhye nijanijaṃ gaṇam । anuyatparato bhinnaṃ tattvaṃ nāmeti bhaṇyate ।। tathā teṣvapi tattveṣu svavarge anugamātmakam ।
vyāvṛttaṃ paravargācca kaleti śivaśāsane ।। kecidāhuḥ punaryāsau śaktirantaḥ susūkṣmikā । tattvānāṃ sā kaletyuktā dharaṇyāṃ dhārikā yathā ।। atra pakṣadvaye vastu na bhinnaṃ bhāsate yataḥ ।
anugāmi na sāmānyamiṣṭaṃ naiyāyikādivat ।। anye vadanti dīkṣādau sukhasaṃgrahaṇārthataḥ । śivena kalpito vargaḥ kaleti samayāśrayaḥ ।। kṛtaśca devadevena samayo aparamārthatām ।
na gacchatīti nāsatyo na cānyasamayodayaḥ ।। nivṛttiḥ pṛthivītattve pratiṣṭhāvyaktagocare । vidyā niśānte śāntā ca śaktyante aṇḍamidaṃ catuḥ ।। śāntātītā śive tattve kalātītaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ ।
nahyatra vargīkaraṇaṃ samayaḥ kalanāpi vā ।। yujyate sarvatodikkaṃ svātantryollāsadhāmani । svātantryāttu nijaṃ rūpaṃ boddhṛdharmādavicyutam ।। upadeśatadāveśaparamārthatvasiddhaye ।
bodhyatāmānayandevaḥ sphuṭameva vibhāvyate ।। yato ataḥ śivatattve api kalāsaṃgatirucyate । aṇḍaṃ ca nāma bhuvanavibhāgasthitikāraṇam ।। prāhurāvaraṇaṃ tacca śaktyantaṃ yāvadasti hi ।
yadyapi prāk śivākhye api tattve bhuvanapaddhatiḥ ।। uktā tathāpyapratighe nāsminnāvṛtisaṃbhavaḥ । nanvevaṃ dharaṇīṃ muktvā śaktau prakṛtimāyayoḥ ।। api cāpratighatve api kathamaṇḍasya saṃbhavaḥ ।
atrāsmadguravaḥ prāhuryatpṛthivyādipañcakam ।। pratyakṣamidamābhāti tato anyannāsti kiṃcana । meyatve sthūlasūkṣmatvānmānatve karaṇatvataḥ ।। kartṛtollāsataḥ kartṛbhāve sphuṭatayoditam ।
triṃśattattvaṃ vibhedātma tadabhedo niśā matā ।। kāryatvakaraṇatvādivibhāgagalane sati । vikāsotkasvatantratve śivāntaṃ pañcakaṃ jaguḥ ।। śrīmatkālottarādau ca kathitaṃ bhūyasā tathā ।
pañcaitāni tu tattvāni yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat ।। pañcamantratanau tena sadyojātādi bhaṇyate । īśānāntaṃ tatra tatra dharādigaganāntakam ।। śivatattvamataḥ śūnyātiśūnyaṃ syādanāśri[vṛ]tam ।
yattu sarvāvibhāgātma svatantraṃ bodhasundaram ।। saptatriṃśaṃ tu tatprāhustattvaṃ paraśivābhidham । tasyāpyuktanayādvedyabhāve atra parikalpite ।। yadāste hyanavacchinnaṃ tadaṣṭātriṃśamucyate ।
na cānavasthā hyevaṃ syāddṛśyatāṃ hi mahātmabhiḥ ।। yadvedyaṃ kiṃcidābhāti tatkṣaye yatprakāśate । tattattvamiti nirṇītaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaṃ hṛdi bhāsate ।। tatkiṃ na kiṃcidvā kiṃcidityākāṅkṣāvaśe vapuḥ ।
cidānandasvatantraikarūpaṃ taditi deśane ।। saptatriṃśaṃ samābhāti tatrākāṅkṣā ca nāparā । taccāpi klṛptavedyatvaṃ yatra bhāti sa cinmayaḥ ।। aṣṭātriṃśattamaḥ so api bhāvanāyopadiśyate ।
yadi nāma tataḥ saptatriṃśa eva punarbhavet ।। avibhāgasvatantratvacinmayatvādidharmatā । samaiva vedyīkaraṇaṃ kevalaṃ tvadhikaṃ yataḥ ।। dharāyāṃ guṇatattvānte māyānte kramaśaḥ sthitāḥ ।
gandho raso rūpamantaḥ sūkṣmabhāvakrameṇa tu ।। iti sthite naye śaktitattvānte apyasti saukṣmyabhāk । sparśaḥ ko api sadā yasmai yoginaḥ spṛhayālavaḥ ।। tatsparśānte tu saṃvittiḥ śuddhacidvyomarūpiṇī ।
yasyāṃ rūḍhaḥ samabhyeti svaprakāśātmikāṃ parām ।। ato vindurato nādo rūpamasmādato rasaḥ । ityuktaṃ kṣobhakatvena spande sparśastu no tathā ।। mataṃ caitanmaheśasya śrīpūrve yadabhāṣata ।
dhārikāpyāyinī boddhrī pavitrī cāvakāśadā ।। ebhiḥ śabdairvyavaharan nivṛttyādernijaṃ vapuḥ । pañcatattvavidhiḥ proktastritattvamadhunocyate ।। vijñānākalaparyantamātmā vidyeśvarāntakam ।
śeṣe śivastritattve syādekatattve śivaḥ param ।। imau bhedāvubhau tattvabhedamātrakṛtāviti । tattvādhvaivāyamitthaṃ ca na ṣaḍadhvasthiteḥ kṣatiḥ ।। prakṛt pumānyatiḥ kālo māyā vidyeśasauśivau ।
śivaśca navatattve api vidhau tattvādhvarūpatā ।। evamaṣṭādaśākhye api vidhau nyāyaṃ vadetsudhīḥ । yatra yatra hi bhogecchā tatprādhānyopayogataḥ ।। anyāntarbhāvanātaśca dīkṣānantavibhedabhāk ।
tena ṣaṭtriṃśato yāvadekatattvavidhirbhavet ।। tattvādhvaiva sa devena prokto vyāsasamāsataḥ । ekatattvavidhiścaiṣa suprabuddhaṃ guruṃ prati ।। śiṣyaṃ ca gatabhogāśamuditaḥ śaṃbhunā yataḥ ।
bhedaṃ visphārya visphārya śaktyā svacchandarūpayā ।। svātmanyabhinne bhagavānnityaṃ viśramayan sthitaḥ । itthaṃ tryātmādhvano bhedaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaparatvataḥ ।। meyabhāgagataḥ proktaḥ puratattvakalātmakaḥ ।
adhunā mātṛbhāgasthaṃ rūpaṃ tredhā nirūpyate ।। yatpramāṇātmakaṃ rūpamadhvano mātṛbhāgagam । padaṃ hyavagamātmatvasamāveśāttaducyate ।। tadeva ca padaṃ mantraḥ prakṣobhātpracyutaṃ yadā ।
guptabhāṣī yato mātā tūṣṇīṃbhūto vyavasthitaḥ ।। tathāpi na vimarśātma rūpaṃ tyajati tena saḥ । pramāṇātmavimarśātmā mānavatkṣobhabhāṅnatu ।। mantrāṇāṃ ca padānāṃ ca tenoktaṃ trikaśāsane ।
abhinnameva svaṃ rūpaṃ niḥspandakṣobhite param ।। audāsīnyaparityāge prakṣobhānavarohaṇe । varṇādhvā mātṛbhāge syāt pūrvaṃ yā kathitā pramā ।। sā tu pūrṇasvarūpatvādavibhāgamayī yataḥ ।
tata ekaikavarṇatvaṃ tattve tattve kṣamāditaḥ ।। kṛtvā śaive pare proktāḥ ṣoḍaśārṇā visargataḥ । tatra śaktiparispandastāvān prāk ca nirūpitaḥ ।। saṃkalayyocyate sarvamadhunā sukhasaṃvide ।
padamantravarṇamekaṃ puraṣoḍaśakaṃ dhareti ca nivṛttiḥ । tattvārṇamagninayanaṃ rasaśarapuramastramantrapadamanyā ।। munitattvārṇaṃ dvikapadamantraṃ vasvakṣibhuvanamaparakalā । agnyarṇatattvamekakapadamantraṃ sainyabhuvanamiti turyā ।।
ṣoḍaśa varṇāḥ padamantratattvamekaṃ ca śāntyatīteyam । abhinavaguptenāryātrayamuktaṃ saṃgrahāya śiṣyebhyaḥ ।। so ayaṃ samasta evādhvā bhairavābhedavṛttimān । tatsvātantryātsvatantratvamaśnuvāno avabhāsate ।।
tathāhi mātṛrūpastho mantrādhveti nirūpitaḥ । tathāhi cidvimarśena grastā vācyadaśā yadā ।। śivajñānakriyāyattamananatrāṇatatparā । aśeṣaśaktipaṭalīlīlālāmpaṭyapāṭavāt ।।
cyutā mānamayādrūpāt saṃvinmantrādhvatāṃ gatā । pramāṇarūpatāmetya prayātyadhvā padātmatām ।। tathā hi māturviśrāntirvarṇānsaṃghaṭya tānbahūn । saṃghaṭṭanaṃ ca kramikaṃ saṃjalpātmakameva tat ।।
vikalpasya svakaṃ rūpaṃ bhogāveśamayaṃ sphuṭam । ataḥ pramāṇatārūpaṃ padamasmadgururjagau ।। pramāṇarūpatāveśamaparityajya meyatām ।। gacchankalanayā yogādadhvā proktaḥ kalātmakaḥ ।
śuddhe prameyatāyoge sūkṣmasthūlatvabhāgini ।। tattvādhvabhuvanādhvatve krameṇānusaredguruḥ । prameyamānamātṝṇāṃ yadrūpamupari sthitam ।। pramātmātra sthito adhvāyaṃ varṇātmā dṛśyatāṃ kila ।
ucchalatsaṃvidāmātraviśrāntyāsvādayoginaḥ ।। sarvābhidhānasāmarthyādaniyantritaśaktayaḥ । sṛṣṭāḥ svātmasahotthe arthe dharāparyantabhāgini ।। āmṛśantaḥ svacidbhūmau tāvato arthānabhedataḥ ।
varṇaughāste pramārūpāṃ satyāṃ bibhrati saṃvidam ।। bālāstiryakpramātāro ye apyasaṃketabhāginaḥ । te apyakṛtrimasaṃskārasārāmenāṃ svasaṃvidam ।। bhinnabhinnāmupāśritya yānti citrāṃ pramātṛtām ।
asyā cākṛtrimānantavarṇasaṃvidi rūḍhatām ।। saṃketā yānti cette api yāntyasaṃketavṛttitām । anayā tu vinā sarve saṃketā bahuśaḥ kṛtāḥ ।। aviśrāntatayā kuryuranavasthāṃ duruttarām ।
bālo vyutpādyate yena tatra saṃketamārgaṇāt ।। aṅgulyādeśane apyasya nāvikalpā tathā matiḥ । vikalpaḥ śabdamūlaśca śabdaḥ saṃketajīvitaḥ ।। tenānanto hyamāyīyo yo varṇagrāma īdṛśaḥ ।
saṃvidvimarśasacivaḥ sadaiva sa hi jṛmbhate ।। yata eva ca māyīyā varṇāḥ sūtiṃ vitenire । ye ca māyīyavarṇeṣu vīryatvena nirūpitāḥ ।। saṃketanirapekṣāste prameti parigṛhyatām ।
tathā hi paravākyeṣu śruteṣvāvriyate nijā ।। pramā yasya jaḍo asau no tatrārthe abhyeti mātṛtām । śukavatsa paṭhatyeva paraṃ tatkramitaikabhāk ।। svātantryalābhataḥ svākyapramālābhe tu boddhṛtā ।
yasya hi svapramābodho vipakṣodbhedanigrahāt ।। vākyādivarṇapuñje sve sa pramātā vaśībhavet । yathā yathā cākṛtakaṃ tadrūpamatiricyate ।। tathā tathā camatkāratāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate ।
ādyāmāyīyavarṇāntarnimagne cottarottare ।। sakete pūrvapūrvāṃśamajjane pratibhābhidaḥ । ādyodrekamahattve api pratibhātmani niṣṭhitāḥ ।। dhruvaṃ kavitvavaktṛtvaśālitāṃ yānti sarvataḥ ।
yāvaddhāmani saṃketanikārakalanojjhite ।। viśrāntaścinmaye kiṃ kiṃ na vetti kurute na vā । ata eva hi vāksiddhau varṇānāṃ samupāsyatā ।। sarvajñatvādisiddhau vā kā siddhiryā na tanmayī ।
taduktaṃ varadena śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate ।। tena guptena guptāste śeṣā varṇāstviti sphuṭam । evaṃ māmātṛmānatvameyatvairyo avabhāsate ।। ṣaḍvidhaḥ svavapuḥśuddhau śuddhiṃ so adhvādhigacchati ।
ekena vapuṣā śuddhau tatraivānyaprakāratām ।। antarbhāvyācarecchuddhimanusaṃdhānavān guruḥ । anantarbhāvaśaktau tu sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tu śodhayet ।। tadviśuddhaṃ bījabhāvāt sūte nottarasaṃtatim ।
śodhanaṃ bahudhā tattadbhogaprāptyekatānatā ।। tadādhipatyaṃ tattyāgastacchivātmatvavedanam । tallīnatā tannirāsaḥ sarvaṃ caitatkramākramāt ।। ata eva ca te mantrāḥ śodhakāścitrarūpiṇaḥ ।
siddhāntavāmadakṣādau citrāṃ śuddhiṃ vitanvate ।। anuttaratrikānāmakramamantrāstu ye kila । te sarve sarvadāḥ kintu kasyācit kvāpi mukhyatā ।। ataḥ śodhakabhāvena śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite ।
parāparādimantrāṇāmadhvanyuktā vyavasthitiḥ ।। śodhakatvaṃ ca mālinyā devīnāṃ tritayasya ca । devatrayasya vaktrāṇāmaṅgānāmaṣṭakasya ca ।। kiṃ vātibahunā dvāravāstvādhāragurukrame ।
lokapāstravidhau mantrān muktvā sarvaṃ viśodhakam ।। yaccaitadadhvanaḥ proktaṃ śodhyatvaṃ śoddhṛtā ca yā । sā svātantryācchivābhede yuktetyuktaṃ ca śāsane ।। sarvametadvibhātyeva parameśitari dhruve ।
pratibimbasvarūpeṇa na tu bāhyatayā yataḥ ।। cidvyomnyeva śive tattaddehādimatirīdṛśī । bhinnā saṃsāriṇāṃ rajjau sarpasragvīcibuddhivat ।। yataḥ prāgdehamaraṇasiddhāntaḥ svapnagocaraḥ ।
dehāntarādirmaraṇe kīdṛgvā dehasaṃbhavaḥ ।। svapne api pratibhāmātrasāmānyaprathanābalāt । viśeṣāḥ pratibhāsante na bhāvyante api te yathā ।। śālagrāmopalāḥ keciccitrākṛtibhṛto yathā ।
tathā māyādibhūmyantalekhācitrahṛdaścitaḥ ।। nagarārṇavaśailādyāstadicchānuvidhāyinaḥ । na svayaṃ sadasanto no kāraṇākāraṇātmakāḥ ।। niyateścirarūḍhāyāḥ samucchedātpravartanāt ।
arūḍhāyāḥ svatantro ayaṃ sthitaścidvyomabhairavaḥ ।। ekacinmātrasaṃpūrṇabhairavābhedabhāgini । evamasmītyanāmarśo bhedako bhāvamaṇḍale ।। sarvapramāṇairno siddhaṃ svapne kartrantaraṃ yathā ।
svasaṃvidaḥ svasiddhāyāstathā sarvatra buddhyatām ।। cittacitrapurodyāne krīḍedevaṃ hi vetti yaḥ । ahameva sthito bhūtabhāvatattvapurairiti ।। evaṃ jāto mṛto asmīti janmamṛtyuvicitratāḥ ।
ajanmanyamṛtau bhānti cittabhittau svanirmitāḥ ।। parehasaṃvidāmātraṃ paralokehalokate । vastutaḥ saṃvido deśaḥ kālo vā naiva kiṃcana ।। abhaviṣyadayaṃ sargo mūrtaścenna tu cinmayaḥ ।
tadavekṣyata tanmadhyāt kenaiko api dharādharaḥ ।। bhūtatanmātravargāderādhārādheyatākrame । ante saṃvinmayī śaktiḥ śivarūpaiva dhāriṇī ।। tasmātpratītirevetthaṃ kartrī dhartrī ca sā śivaḥ ।
tato bhāvāstatra bhāvāḥ śaktirādhārikā tataḥ ।। sāṃkalpikaṃ nirādhāramapi naiva patatyadhaḥ । svādhāraśaktau viśrāntaṃ viśvamitthaṃ vimṛśyatām ।। asyā ghanāhamityādirūḍhireva dharāditā ।
yāvadante cidasmīti nirvṛttā bhairavātmatā ।। maṇāvindrāyudhe bhāsa iva nīlādayaḥ śive । paramārthata eṣāṃ tu nodayo na vyayaḥ kvacit ।। deśe kāle atra vā sṛṣṭirityetadasamañjasam ।
cidātmanā hi devena sṛṣṭirdikkālayorapi ।। jāgarābhimate sārdhahastatritayagocare । prahare ca pṛthak svapnāścitradikkālamāninaḥ ।। ata eva kṣaṇaṃ nāma na kiṃcidapi manmahe ।
kriyākṣaṇe vāpyekasmin bahvyaḥ saṃsyurdrutāḥ kriyāḥ ।। tena ye bhāvasaṃkocaṃ kṣaṇāntaṃ pratipedire । te nūnamenayā nāḍyā śūnyadṛṣṭyavalambinaḥ ।। tadya eṣa sato bhāvāñ śūnyīkartuṃ tathāsataḥ ।
sphuṭīkartuṃ svatantratvādīśaḥ so asmatprabhuḥ śivaḥ ।। taditthaṃ parameśāno viśvarūpaḥ pragīyate । na tu bhinnasya kasyāpi dharāderupapannatā ।। uktaṃ caitatpuraiveti na bhūyaḥ pravivicyate ।
bhūyobhiścāpi bāhyārthadūṣaṇaiḥ pravyaramyata ।। taditthameṣa nirṇītaḥ kalādervistaro adhvanaḥ ।। athādhvano asya prakṛta upayogaḥ prakāśyate ।। itthamadhvā samasto ayaṃ yathā saṃvidi saṃsthitaḥ ।
taddvārā śūnyadhīprāṇanāḍīcakratanuṣvatho ।। bahiśca liṅgamūrtyagnisthaṇḍilādiṣu sarvataḥ । tathā sthitaḥ samastaśca vyastaścaiṣa kramākramāt ।। āsaṃvittattvamābāhyaṃ yo ayamadhvā vyavasthitaḥ ।
tatra tatrocitaṃ rūpaṃ svaṃ svātantryeṇa bhāsayet ।। sarvaṃ sarvatra rūpaṃ ca tasyāpi na na bhāsate । nahyavaccheditāṃ kvāpi svapne api viṣahāmahe ।। evaṃ viśvādhvasaṃpūrṇaṃ kālavyāpāracitritam ।
deśakālamayaspandasadma dehaṃ vilokayet ।। tathā vilokyamāno asau viśvāntardevatāmayaḥ । dhyeyaḥ pūjyaśca tarpyaśca tadāviṣṭo vimucyate ।। itthaṃ ghaṭaṃ paṭaṃ liṅgaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pustakaṃ jalam ।
yadvā kiṃcitkvacitpaśyettatra tanmayatāṃ vrajet ।। tatrārpaṇaṃ hi vastūnāmabhedenārcanaṃ matam । tathā saṃpūrṇarūpatvānusaṃdhirdhyānamucyate ।। saṃpūrṇatvānusaṃdhānamakampaṃ dārḍhyamānayan ।
tathāntarjalpayogena vimṛśañjapabhājanam ।। tatrārpitānāṃ bhāvānāṃ svakabhedavilāpanam । kurvaṃstadraśmisadbhāvaṃ dadyāddhomakriyāparaḥ ।। tathaivaṃkurvataḥ sarvaṃ samabhāvena paśyataḥ ।
niṣkampatā vrataṃ śuddhaṃ sāmyaṃ nandiśikhoditam ।। tathārcanajapadhyānahomavratavidhikramāt । paripūrṇāṃ sthitiṃ prāhuḥ samādhiṃ guravaḥ purā ।। atra pūjājapādyeṣu bahirantardvayasthitau ।
dravyaughe na vidhiḥ ko api na kāpi pratiṣiddhatā ।। kalpanāśuddhisaṃdhyādernopayogo atra kaścana । uktaṃ śrītrikasūtre ca jāyate yajanaṃ prati ।। avidhijño vidhijñaścetyevamādi suvistaram ।
yadā yathā yena yatra svā samvittiḥ prasīdati ।। tadā tathā tena tatra tattadbhogyaṃ vidhiśca saḥ । laukikālaukikaṃ sarvaṃ tenātra viniyojayet ।। niṣkampatve sakampastu kampaṃ nirhrāsayedbalāt ।
yathā yenābhyupāyena kramādakramato api vā ।। vicikitsā galatyantastathāsau yatnavānbhavet । dhīkarmākṣagatā devīrniṣiddhaireva tarpayet ।। vīravrataṃ cābhinandediti bhargaśikhāvacaḥ ।
tathāhi śaṅkā mālinyaṃ glāniḥ saṃkoca ityadaḥ ।। saṃsārakārāgārāntaḥ sthūlasthūṇāghaṭāyate । mantrā varṇasvabhāvā ye dravyaṃ yatpāñcabhautikam ।। yaccidātma prāṇijātaṃ tatra kaḥ saṃkaraḥ katham ।
saṃkarābhāvataḥ keyaṃ śaṅkā tasyāmapi sphuṭam ।। na śaṅketa tathā śaṅkā vilīyetāvahelayā । śrīsarvācāravīrālīniśācarakramādiṣu ।। śāstreṣu vitataṃ caitattatra tatrocyate yataḥ ।
śaṅkayā jāyate glāniḥ śaṅkayā vighnabhājanam ।। uvācotpaladevaśca śrīmānasmadgurorguruḥ । sarvāśaṅkāśaniṃ mārgaṃ numo māheśvaraṃ tviti ।। anuttarapadāptaye tadidamāṇavaṃ darśitābhyupāyamativistarānnanu vidāṃkurudhvaṃ budhāḥ ।
athādhikṛtibhāhanaṃ ka iha vā kathaṃ vetyalaṃ vivecayitumucyate vividhaśaktipātakramaḥ ।। tatra kecidiha prāhuḥ śaktipāta imaṃ vidhim । taṃ pradarśya nirākṛtya svamataṃ darśayiṣyate ।। tatredaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ satsukhaduḥkhavimohabhāk ।
viṣamaṃ sattathābhūtaṃ samaṃ hetuṃ prakalpayet ।। so avyaktaṃ tacca sattvādinānārūpamacetanam । ghaṭādivatkāryamiti hetureko asya sā niśā ।। sā jaḍā kāryatādrūpyātkāryaṃ cāsyāṃ sadeva hi ।
kalādidharaṇīprāntaṃ jāḍyātsā sūtaye akṣamā ।। teneśaḥ kṣobhayedenāṃ kṣobho asyāḥ sūtiyogyatā । puṃsaḥ prati ca sā bhogyaṃ sūte anādīn pṛthagvidhān ।। puṃsaśca nirviśeṣatve muktāṇūn prati kiṃ na tat ।
nimittaṃ karmasaṃskāraḥ sa ca teṣu na vidyate ।। iti cetkarmasaṃskārābhāvasteṣāṃ kutaḥ kila । na bhogādanyakarmāṃśaprasaṅgo hi duratyayaḥ ।। yugapatkarmaṇāṃ bhogo naca yuktaḥ krameṇa hi ।
phaledyatkarma tatkasmātsvaṃ rūpaṃ saṃtyajetkvacit ।। jñānātkarmakṣayaścettatkuta īśvaracoditāt । dharmādyadi kutaḥ so api karmataścettaducyatām ।। nahi karmāsti tādṛkṣaṃ yena jñānaṃ pravartate ।
karmajatve ca tajjñānaṃ phalarāśau pateddhruvam ।। anyakarmaphalaṃ prācyaṃ karmarāśiṃ ca kiṃ dahet । īśasya dveṣarāgādiśūnyasyāpi kathaṃ kvacit ।। tathābhisaṃdhirnānyatra bhedahetorabhāvataḥ ।
nanvitthaṃ pradahejjñānaṃ karmajālāni karma hi ।। ajñānasahakārīdaṃ sūte svargādikaṃ phalam । ajñānaṃ jñānato naśyedanyakarmaphalādapi ।। upavāsādikaṃ cānyadduṣṭakarmaphalaṃ bhavet ।
niṣphalīkurute duṣṭaṃ karmetyaṅgīkṛtaṃ kila ।। ajñānamiti yatproktaṃ jñānābhāvaḥ sa cetsa kim । prāgabhāvo athavā dhvaṃsa ādye kiṃ sarvasaṃvidām ।। kasyāpi vātha jñānasya prācyaḥ pakṣastvasaṃbhavī ।
na kiṃcidyasya vijñānamudapādi tathāvidhaḥ ।। nāṇurasti bhave hyasminnanādau ko anvayaṃ kramaḥ । bhāvinaḥ prāgabhāvaśca jñānasyeti sthite sati ।। muktāṇorapi so astyeva janmataḥ prāgasau naca ।
jñānaṃ bhāvi vimukte asminniti ceccarcyatāmidam ।। kasmājjñānaṃ na bhāvyatra nanu dehādyajanmataḥ । tatkasmātkarmaṇaḥ kṣaiṇyāttatkuto ajñānahānitaḥ ।। ajñānasya kathaṃ hāniḥ prāgabhāve hi saṃvidaḥ ।
ajñānaṃ prāgabhāvo asau na bhāvyutpattyasaṃbhavāt ।। kasmānna bhāvi tajjñānaṃ nanu dehādyajanmataḥ । ityeṣa sarvapakṣaghno niśitaścakrakabhramaḥ ।। atha pradhvaṃsa evedamajñānaṃ tatsadā sthitam ।
muktāṇuṣviti teṣvastu māyākāryavijṛmbhitam ।। athājñānaṃ nahyabhāvo mithyājñānaṃ tu tanmatam । tadeva karmaṇāṃ svasminkartavye sahakāraṇam ।। vaktavyaṃ tarhi kiṃ karma yadā sūte svakaṃ phalam ।
tadaiva mithyājñānena satā hetutvamāpyate ।। atha yasminkṣaṇe karma kṛtaṃ tatra svarūpasat । mithyājñānaṃ yadi tatastādṛśātkamarṇaḥ phalam ।। prākpakṣe pralaye vṛtte prācyasṛṣṭipravartane ।
dehādyabhāvānno mithyājñānasya kvāpi saṃbhavaḥ ।। uttarasminpunaḥ pakṣe yadā yadyena yatra vā । kriyate karma tatsarvamajñānasacivaṃ tadā ।। avaśyamiti kasyāpi na karmaprakṣayo bhavet ।
yadyapi jñānavānbhūtvā vidhatte karma kiṃcana ।। viphalaṃ syāttu tatpūrvakarmarāśau tu kā gatiḥ । atha pralayakāle api citsvabhāvatvayogataḥ ।। aṇūnā saṃbhavatyeva jñānaṃ mithyeti tatkutaḥ ।
svabhāvāditi cenmukte śive vā kiṃ tathā nahi ।। yaccādarśanamākhyātaṃ nimittaṃ pariṇāmini । pradhāne taddhi saṃkīrṇavaivittayobhayayogataḥ ।। darśanāya pumarthaikayogyatāsacivaṃ dhiyaḥ ।
ārabhya sate dharaṇīparyantaṃ tatra yaccitaḥ ।। buddhivṛttyaviśiṣṭatvaṃ puṃsprayāśarprasādataḥ । prakāśanāddhiyo arthena saha bhogaḥ sa bhaṇyate ।। buddhirevāsmi vikṛtidharmikānyastu ko apyasau ।
madvilakṣaṇa ekātmetyevaṃ vaivi yasaṃvidi ।। pumarthasya kṛtatvena sahakāriviyogataḥ । taṃ pumāṃsaṃ prati naiva sūte kiṃtvanyameva hi ।। atra puṃso atha mūlasya dharmo adarśanatā dvayoḥ ।
athaveti vikalpo ayamāstāmetattu bhaṇyatām ।। bhogo vivekaparyanta iti yattatra ko avadhiḥ । vivekalābhe nikhilasūtidṛgyadi sāpi kim ।। sāmānyena viśeṣairvā prācye syādekajanmataḥ ।
uttare na kadācitsyādbhāvikālasya yogataḥ ।। kaiścideva viśeṣaiścetsarveṣāṃ yugapadbhavet । viveko anādisaṃyogātkā hyanyonyaṃ vicitratā ।। tasmātsāṃkhyadṛśāpīdamajñānaṃ naiva yujyate ।
ajñānena vinā bandhamokṣau naiva vyavasthayā ।। yujyete tacca kathitayuktibhirnopapadyate । bhāyākarmāṇudevecchāsadbhāve api sthite tataḥ ।। na bandhamokṣayoryogo bhedahetorasaṃbhavāt ।
tasmādajñānaśabdena jñatvakartṛtvadharmaṇām ।। cidaṇūnāmāvaraṇaṃ kiṃcidvācyaṃ vipaścitā । āvāraṇātmanā siddhaṃ tatsvarūpādabhedavat ।। bhede pramāṇābhāvācca tadekaṃ nikhilātmasu ।
tacca kasmātprasūtaṃ syānmāyātaścetkathaṃ nu sā ।। kvacideva suvītaitanna tu muktātmanītyayam । prācyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ syānnimittaṃ cenna labhyate ।। utpattyabhāvatastena nityaṃ naca vinaśyati ।
tata evaikatāyāṃ cānyātmasādhāraṇatvataḥ ।। na vāvastvarthakāritvānna cittatsaṃvṛtitvataḥ । na caitenātmanāṃ yogo hetumāṃstadasaṃbhavāt ।। tenaikaṃ vastu sannityaṃ nityasaṃbaddhamātmabhiḥ ।
jaḍaṃ malaṃ tadajñānaṃ saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam ।। tasya roddhrī yadā śaktirudāste śivaraśmibhiḥ । tadāṇuḥ spṛśyate spṛṣṭaḥ svake jñānakriye sphuṭe ।। samāviśedayaṃ sūryakānto arkeṇeva coditaḥ ।
roddhryāśca śaktermādhyasthyatāratamyavaśakramāat ।। vicitratvamataḥ prāhurabhivyaktau svasaṃvidaḥ । sa eṣa śaktipātākhyaḥ śāstreṣu paribhāṣyate ।। atrocyate malastāvaditthameṣa na yujyate ।
iti pūrvāhṇike proktaṃ punaruktau tu kiṃ phalam ।। malasya pākaḥ ko ayaṃ syānnāśaśceditarātmanām । sa eko mala ityukternairmalyamanuṣajyate ।। atha pratyātmaniyato anādiśca prāgabhāvavat ।
malo naśyettathāpyeṣa nāśo yadi sahetukaḥ ।। hetuḥ karmeśvarecchā vā karma tāvanna tādṛśam । īśvarecchā svatantrā ca kvacideva tathaiva kim ।। ahetuko asya nāśaścetprāgevaiṣa vinaśyatu ।
kṣaṇāntaraṃ sadṛk sūte iti cetsthirataiva sā ।। na ca nityasya bhāvasya hetvanāyattajanmanaḥ । nāśo dṛṣṭaḥ prāgabhāvastvavastviti tathāstu saḥ ।। athāsya pāko nāmaiṣa svaśaktipratibaddhatā ।
sarvānprati tathaiṣa syādruddhaśaktirviṣāgnivat ।। punarudbhūtaśaktau ca svakāryaṃ syādviṣāgnivat । muktā api na muktāḥ syuḥ śaktiṃ cāsya na manmahe ।। roddhrīti cetkasya nṛṇāṃ jñatvakartṛtvayoryadi ।
sadbhāvamātrādroddhṛtve śivamuktāṇvasaṃbhavaḥ ।। saṃnidhānātiriktaṃ ca na kiṃcitkurute malaḥ । ātmanā pariṇāmitvādanityatvaprasaṅgataḥ ।। jñatvakartṛtvamātraṃ ca pudgalā na tadāśrayāḥ ।
taccedāvāritaṃ hanta rūpanāśaḥ prasajyate ।। āvāraṇaṃ cādṛśyatvaṃ na ca tadvastuno anyatām । karoti ghaṭavajjñānaṃ nāvarītuṃ ca śakyate ।। jñānenāvaraṇīyena tadevāvaraṇaṃ katham ।
na jñāyate tathā ca syādāvṛtirnāmamātrataḥ ।। roddhryāśca śakteḥ kastasya pratibandhaka īśvaraḥ । yadyapekṣāvirahitastatra prāgdattamuttaram ।। karmasāmyamapekṣyātha tasyecchā saṃpravartate ।
tasyāpi rūpaṃ vaktavyaṃ samatā karmaṇāṃ hi kā ।। bhogaparyāyamāhātmyātkāle kvāpi phalaṃ prati । virodhātkarmaṇī ruddhe tiṣṭhataḥ sāmyamīdṛśam ।। taṃ ca kālāṃśakaṃ devaḥ sarvajño vīkṣya taṃ malam ।
runddhe lakṣyaḥ sa kālaśca sukhaduḥkhādivarjanaiḥ ।। naitatkramikasaṃśuddhavyāmiśrākārakarmabhiḥ । tathaiva deye svaphale keyamanyonyaroddhṛtā ।। rodhe tayośca jātyāyurapi na syādataḥ patet ।
deho bhogadayoreva nirodha iti cennanu ।। jātyāyuṣpradakarmāṃśasaṃnidhau yadi śaṃkaraḥ । malaṃ runddhe bhogadātuḥ karmaṇaḥ kiṃ bibheti saḥ ।। śataśo api hlādatāpaśūnyāṃ saṃcinvate daśām ।
na ca bhaktirasāveśamiti bhūmnā vilokitam ।। athāpi kālamāhātmyamapekṣya parameśvaraḥ । tathā karoti vaktavyaṃ kālo asau kīdṛśastviti ।। kiṃ cānādirayaṃ bhogaḥ karmānādi sapudgalam ।
tataśca bhogaparyāyakālaḥ sarvasya niḥsamaḥ ।। ādimattve hi kasyāpi vargādasmādbhavediyam । vaicitrī bhuktametena kalpametena tu dvayam ।। iyato bhogaparyāyātsyātsāmyaṃ karmaṇāmiti ।
anena nayabījena manye vaicitryakāraṇam ।। jagataḥ karma yatklaptaṃ tattathā nāvakalpate । anādimalasaṃcchannā aṇavo dṛkkriyātmanā ।। sarve tulyāḥ kathaṃ citrāṃ śritāḥ karmaparamparām ।
bhogalolikayā cetsā vicitreti kuto nanu ।। anādi karmasaṃskāravaicitryāditi cetpunaḥ । vācyaṃ tadeva vaicitryaṃ kuto niyatirāgayoḥ ।। mahimā cedayaṃ tau kiṃ nāsamañjasyabhāginau ।
īśvarecchānapekṣā tu bhedaheturna kalpate ।। athānāditvamātreṇa yuktihīnena sādhyate । vyavastheyamalaṃ tarhi malenāstu vṛthāmunā ।। tathāhi karma tāvanno yāvanmāyā na pudgale ।
vyāpriyeta na cāhetustadvṛttistanmito malaḥ ।। itthaṃ ca kalpite māyākārye karmaṇi hetutām । anādi karma cedgacchetkiṃ malasyopakalpanam ।। nanu mābhūnmalastarhi citrākāreṣu karmasu ।
santatyāvartamāneṣu vyavasthā na prakalpate ।। ādau madhye ca citratvātkarmaṇāṃ na yathā samaḥ । ātmākāro api ko apyeṣa bhāvikāle tathā bhavet ।। itthamucchinna evāyaṃ bandhamokṣādikaḥ kramaḥ ।
ajñānādbandhanaṃ mokṣo jñānāditi parīkṣitam ।। virodhe svaphale caite karmaṇī samaye kvacit । udāsāte yadi tataḥ karmaitatpratibudhyatām ।। śivaśaktinipātasya ko avakāśastu tāvatā ।
kvāpi kāle tayoretadaudāsīnyaṃ yadā tataḥ ।। kālāntare tayostadvadvirodhasyānivṛttitaḥ । ataśca na phaletānte tābhyāṃ karmāntaraṇi ca ।। ruddhāni prāptakālatvādgatābhyāmupabhogyatām ।
evaṃ sadaiva vārtāyāṃ dehapāte tathaiva ca ।। jāte vimokṣa ityāstāṃ śaktipātādikalpanā । athodāsīnatatkarmadvayayogakṣaṇāntare ।। karmāntaraṃ phalaṃ sūte tatkṣaṇe api tathā na kim ।
kṣaṇāntare atha te eva pratibandhavivarjite ।। phalataḥ pratibandhasya varjanaṃ kiṃkṛtaṃ tayoḥ । karmasāmyaṃ svarūpeṇa na ca tattāratamyabhāk ।। na śiveccheti tatkārye śaktipāte na tadbhavet ।
tirobhāvaśca nāmāyaṃ sa kasmādudbhavetpunaḥ ।। karmasāmyena yatkṛtyaṃ prāgevaitatkṛtaṃ kila । hetutve ceśvarecchāyā vācyaṃ pūrvavadeva tu ।। etenānye api ye apekṣyā īśecchāyāṃ prakalpitāḥ ।
dhvastāste api hi nityānyahetvahetvādidūṣaṇāt ।। vairāgyaṃ bhogavairasyaṃ dharmaḥ ko api vivekitā । satsaṅgaḥ parameśānapūjādyabhyāsanityatā ।। āpatprāptistannirīkṣā dehe kiṃcicca lakṣaṇam ।
śāstrasevā bhogasaṃghapūrṇatā jñānamaiśvaram ।। ityapekṣyaṃ yadīśasya dūṣyametacca pūrvavat । vyabhicāraśca sāmastyavyastatvābhyāṃ svarūpataḥ ।। anyonyānupraveśaścānupapattiśca bhūyasī ।
tasmānna manmahe ko ayaṃ śaktipātavidheḥ kramaḥ ।। itthaṃ bhrāntiviṣāveśamūrcchānirmokadāyinīm । śrīśaṃbhuvadanodgīrṇāṃ vacmyāgamamahauṣadhīm ।। devaḥ svatantraścidrūpaḥ prakāśātmā svabhāvataḥ ।
rūpapracchādanakrīḍāyogādaṇuranekakaḥ ।। sa svayaṃ kalpitākāravikalpātmakakarmabhiḥ । badhnātyātmānameveha svātantryāditi varṇitam ।। svātantryamahimaivāyaṃ devasya yadasau punaḥ ।
svaṃ rūpaṃ pariśuddhaṃ satspṛśatyapyaṇutāmayaḥ ।। na vācyaṃ tu kathaṃ nāma kasmiṃścitpuṃsyasau tathā । nahi nāma pumānkaścidyasminparyanuyujyate ।। deva eva tathāsau cet svarūpaṃ cāsya tādṛśam ।
tādṛkprathāsvabhāvasya svabhāve kānuyojyatā ।। āhāsmatparameṣṭhī ca śivadṛṣṭau gurūttamaḥ । pañcaprakārakṛtyoktiśivatvānnijakarmaṇe ।। pravṛttasya nimittānāmapareṣāṃ kva mārgaṇam ।
channasvarūpatābhāse puṃsi yadyādṛśaṃ phalam ।। tatrāṇoḥ sata evāsti svātantryaṃ karmatohi tat । īśvarasya ca yā svātmatirodhitsā nimittatām ।। sābhyeti karmamalayorato anādivyavasthitiḥ ।
tirodhiḥ pūrṇarūpasyāpūrṇatvaṃ tacca pūraṇam ।। prati bhinnena bhāvena spṛhāto lolikā malaḥ । viśuddhasvaprakāśātmaśivarūpatayā vinā ।। na kiṃcidyujyate tena heturatra maheśvaraḥ ।
itthaṃ sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsatraye māyāmapekṣate ।। kṛtyai malaṃ tathā karma śivecchaiveti susthitam । yattu kasmiṃścana śivaḥ svena rūpeṇa bhāsate ।। tatrāsya nāṇuge tāvadapekṣye malakarmaṇī ।
aṇusvarūpatāhānau tadgataṃ hetutāṃ katham ।। vrajenmāyānapekṣatvamata evopapādayet । tena śuddhaḥ svaprakāśaḥ śiva evātra kāraṇam ।। sa ca svācchandyamātreṇa tāratamyaprakāśakaḥ ।
kulajātivapuṣkarmavayonuṣṭhānasaṃpadaḥ ।। anapekṣya śive bhaktiḥ śaktipāto aphalārthinām । yā phalārthitayā bhaktiḥ sā karmādyamapekṣate ।। tato atra syātphale bhedo nāpavarge tvasau tathā ।
bhogāpavargadvitayābhisaṃdhāturapi sphuṭam ।। prāgbhāge apekṣate karma citratvānnottare punaḥ । anābhāsitarūpo api tadābhāsitayeva yat ।। sthitvā mantrādi saṃgṛhya tyajetso asya tirobhavaḥ ।
śrīsāraśāstre bhagavānvastvetatsamabhāṣata ।। dharmādharmātmakairbhāvairanekairveṣṭayetsvayam । asandehaṃ svamātmānamavīcyādiśivāntake ।। tadvacchaktisamūhena sa eva tu viveṣṭayet ।
svayaṃ badhnāti deveśaḥ svayaṃ caiva vimuñcati ।। svayaṃ bhoktā svayaṃ jñātā svayaṃ caivopalakṣayet । svayaṃ bhuktiśca muktiśca svayaṃ devī svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। svayamekākṣarā caiva yathoṣmā kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ ।
vastūktamatra svātantryātsvātmarūpaprakāśanam ।। śrīmanniśākule apyuktaṃ mithyābhāvitacetasaḥ । malamāyāvicāreṇa kliśyante svalpabuddhayaḥ ।। sphaṭikopalago reṇuḥ kiṃ tasya kurutāṃ priye ।
vyomnīva nīlaṃ hi malaṃ malaśaṃkāṃ tatastyajet ।। śrīmānvidyāguruścāha pramāṇastutidarśane । dharmādharmavyāptivināśāntarakāle śakteḥ pāto gāhanikairyaḥ pratipannaḥ ।। taṃ svecchātaḥ saṃgiramāṇāḥ stavakādyāḥ svātantryaṃ tattvayyanapekṣaṃ kathayeyuḥ ।
tāratamyaprakāśo yastīvramadhyamamandatāḥ ।। tā eva śaktipātasya pratyekaṃ traidhamāsthitāḥ । tīvratīvraḥ śaktipāto dehapātavaśātsvayam ।। mokṣapradastadaivānyakāle vā tāratamyataḥ ।
madhyatīvrātpunaḥ sarvamajñānaṃ vinivartate ।। svayameva yato vetti bandhamokṣatayātmatām । tatprātibhaṃ mahājñānaṃ śāstrācāryānapekṣi yat ।। pratibhācandrikāśāntadhvāntaścācāryacandramāḥ ।
tamastāpau hanti dṛśaṃ visphāryānandanirbharām ।। sa śiṣṭaḥ karmakartṛtvācchiṣyo anyaḥ karmabhāvataḥ । śiṣṭaḥ sarvatra ca smārtapadakālakulādiṣu ।। uktaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śāstrārthapratibhāpariniṣṭhitaḥ ।
yanmūlaṃ śāsanaṃ tena na riktaḥ ko api jantukaḥ ।। tatrāpi tāratamyotthamānantyaṃ dārḍhyakamprate । yuktiḥ śāstraṃ gururvādo abhyāsa ityādyapekṣate ।। kampamānaṃ hi vijñānaṃ svayameva punarvrajet ।
kasyāpi dārḍhyamanyasya yuktyādyaiḥ kevaletaraiḥ ।। yathā yathā parāpekṣātānavaṃ prātibhe bhavet । tathā tathā gururasau śreṣṭho vijñānapāragaḥ ।। anyataḥ śikṣitānantajñāno api pratibhābalāt ।
yadvetti tatra tatrāsya śivatā jyāyasī ca sā ।। na cāsya samayitvādikramo nāpyabhiṣecanam । na santānādi no vidyāvrataṃ prātibhavartmanaḥ ।। ādividvānmahādevastenaiṣo adhiṣṭhito yataḥ ।
saṃskārāstadadhiṣṭhānasiddhyai tattasya tu svataḥ ।। devībhirdīkṣitastena sabhaktiḥ śivaśāsane । dṛḍhatākampratābhedaiḥ so api svayamatha vratāt ।। tapojapādergurutaḥ svasaṃskāraṃ prakalpayet ।
yato vājasineyākhya uktaṃ siñcetsvayaṃ tanum ।। ityādyupakramaṃ yāvadante tatpariniṣṭhitam । abhiṣikto bhavedevaṃ na bāhyakalaśāmbubhiḥ ।। śrīsarvavīraśrībrahmayāmalādau ca tattathā ।
nirūpitaṃ maheśena kiyadvā likhyatāmidam ।। itthaṃ prātibhavijñānaṃ kiṃ kiṃ kasya na sādhayet । yatprātibhādvā sarvaṃ cetyūce śeṣamahāmuniḥ ।। anye tvāhurakāmasya prātibho gururīdṛśaḥ ।
sāmagrījanyatā kāmye tenārimansaṃskṛto guruḥ ।। niyatermahimā naiva phale sādhye nivartate । abhiṣiktaścīrṇavidyāvratastena phalapradaḥ ।। asadetaditi prāhurguravastattvadarśinaḥ ।
śrīsomānandakalyāṇabhavabhūtipurogamāḥ ।। tathāhi trīśikāśāstravivṛtau te abhyadhurbudhāḥ । sāṃsiddhikaṃ yadvijñānaṃ taccintāratnamucyate ।। tadabhāve tadarthaṃ tadāhṛtaṃ jñānamādṛtam ।
evaṃ yo veda tattvena tasya nirvāṇagāminī ।। dīkṣā bhavatyasandigdhā tilājyāhutivarjitā । adṛṣṭamaṇḍalo apyevaṃ yaḥ kaścidvetti tattvataḥ ।। sa siddhibhāgbhavennityaṃ sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ ।
avidhijño vidhānajño jāyate yajanaṃ prati ।। ityādibhistrīśikoktairvākyairmāheśvaraiḥ sphuṭam । jñānaṃ dīkṣādisaṃskārasatattvamiti varṇitam ।। jñānopāyastu dīkṣādikriyā jñānaviyoginām ।
ityetadadhunaivāstā svaprastāve bhaviṣyati ।। guruśāstrapramāṇāderapyupāyatvamaṃjasā । pratibhā paramevaiṣā sarvakāmadughā yataḥ ।। upāyayogakramato nirupāyamathākramam ।
yadrūpaṃ tatparaṃ tattvaṃ tatra tatra suniścitam ।। yastu prātibhabāhyātmasaṃskāradvayasundaraḥ । ukto ananyopakāryatvātsa sākṣādvarado guruḥ ।। svamuktimātre kasyāpi yāvadviśvavimocane ।
pratibhodeti khadyotaratnatārendusūryavat ।। tataḥ prātibhasaṃvittyai śāstramasmatkṛtaṃ tvidam । yo abhyasyetsa gururnaiva vastvarthā hi viḍambakāḥ ।। paropajīvitābuddhyā sarva itthaṃ na bhāsate ।
taduktyā na vinā vetti śaktipātasya māndyataḥ ।। sphuṭametacca śāstreṣu teṣu teṣu nirūpyate । kiraṇāyāṃ tathoktaṃ ca gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ ।। jñānayogyāstathā keciccaryāyogyāstathāpare ।
śrīmannandiśikhātantre vitatyaitannirūpitam ।। praśnottaramukheneti tadabhagnaṃ nirūpyate । anirdeśyaḥ śivastatra ko abhyupāyo nirūpyatām ।। iti praśne kṛte devyā śrīmāñchaṃbhurnyarūpayam ।
upāyo atra vivekaikaḥ sa hi heyaṃ vihāpayan ।। dadātyasya ca suśroṇi prātibhaṃ jñānamuttamam । yadā pratibhayā yuktastadā muktaśca mocayet ।। paraśaktinipātena dhvastamāyāmalaḥ pumān ।
nanu prāgdīkṣayā mokṣo adhunā tu prātibhātkatham ।। iti devyā kṛte praśne prāvartata vibhorvacaḥ । dīkṣayā mucyate jantuḥ prātibhena tathā priye ।। gurvāyattā tu sā dīkṣā badhyabandhanamokṣaṇe ।
prātibho asya svabhāvastu kevalībhāvasiddhidaḥ ।। kevalasya dhruvaṃ muktiḥ paratattvena sā nanu । nṛśaktiśivamuktaṃ hi tattvatrayamidaṃ tvayā ।। nā badhyo bandhane śaktiḥ karaṇaṃ kartṛtāṃ spṛśat ।
śivaḥ karteti tatproktaṃ sarvaṃ gurvāgamādaṇoḥ ।। punarvivekāduktaṃ taduttarottaramucyatām । kathaṃ vivekaḥ kiṃ vāsya devadeva vivicyate ।। ityukte parameśānyā jagādādiguruḥ śivaḥ ।
śivāditattvatritayaṃ tadāgamavaśādguroḥ ।। adhrottaragairvākyaiḥ siddhaṃ prātibhatāṃ vrajet । dīkṣāsicchinnapāśatvādbhāvanābhāvitasya hi ।। vikāsaṃ tattvamāyāti prātibhaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।
bhasmacchannāgnivatsphauṭyaṃ prātibhe gauravāgamāt ।। bījaṃ kāloptasaṃsiktaṃ yathā vardheta tattathā । yogayāgajapairuktairguruṇā prātibhaṃ sphuṭet ।। viveko atīndriyastveṣa yadāyāti vivecanam ।
paśupāśapatijñānaṃ svayaṃ nirbhāsate tadā ।। prātibhe tu samāyāte jñānamanyattu sendriyam । vāgakṣiśrutigamyaṃ cāpyanyāpekṣaṃ varānane ।। tattyajedbuddhimāsthāya pradīpaṃ tu yathā divā ।
prādurbhūtavivekasya syāccidindriyagocare ।। dūrācchrutyādivedhādivṛddhikrīḍāvicitritā । sarvabhāvavivekāttu sarvabhāvaparāṅmukhaḥ ।। krīḍāsu suviraktātmā śivabhāvaikabhāvitaḥ ।
māhātmyametatsuśroṇi prātibhasya vidhīyate ।। svacchāyādarśavatpaśyedbahirantargataṃ śivam । heyopādeyatattvajñastadā dhyāyennijāṃ citim ।। siddhijālaṃ hi kathitaṃ parapratyayakāraṇam ।
ihaiva siddhāḥ kāyānte mucyeranniti bhāvanāt ।। parabhāvanadārḍhyāttu jīvanmukto nigadyate । etatte prātibhe bhede lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। śāpānugrahakāryeṣu tathābhyāsena śaktayā ।
teṣūdāsīnatāyāṃ tu mucyate mocayetparān ।। bhūtendriyādiyogena baddho aṇuḥ saṃsareddhruvam । sa eva pratibhāyuktaḥ śaktitattvaṃ nigadyate ।। tatpātāveśato muktaḥ śiva eva bhavārṇavāt ।
nanvācāryātsendriyaṃ tajjñānamuktamatīndriyam ।। vivekajaṃ ca tadbuddhyā tatkathaṃ syānnirindriyam । iti pṛṣṭo abhyadhātsvāntadhiyorjāḍyaikavāsanāt ।। akṣatvaṃ pravivekena tacchittau bhāsakaḥ śivaḥ ।
saṃskāraḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ paratā parikīrtitā ।। manobuddhī na bhinne tu kasmiṃścitkāraṇāntare । viveke kāraṇe hyete prabhuśaktyupavṛṃhite ।। na manobuddhihīnastu jñānasyādhigamaḥ priye ।
parabhāvāttu tatsūkṣmaṃ śaktitattvaṃ nigadyate ।। vivekaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ śuddhabhāvānmahāśayaḥ । buddhitattvaṃ tu triguṇamuttamādhamamadhyamam ।। aṇimādigataṃ cāpi bandhakaṃ jaḍamindriyam ।
nanu prātibhato muktau dīkṣayā kiṃ śivādhvare ।। ūce ajñānā hi dīkṣāyāṃ bālavāliśayoṣitaḥ । pāśacchedādvimucyante prabuddhyante śivādhvare ।। tasmāddīkṣā bhavatyeṣu kāraṇatvena sundari ।
dīkṣayā pāśamokṣe tu śuddhabhāvādvivekajam ।। ityeṣa paṭhito granthaḥ svayaṃ ye boddhumakṣamāḥ । teṣāṃ śivoktisaṃvādādbodho dārḍhyaṃ vrajediti ।। śrīmanniśāṭane cātmaguruśāstravaśāttridhā ।
jñānaṃ mukhyaṃ svopalabdhi vikalpārṇavatāraṇam ।। mantrātmabhūtadravyāśadivyatattvādigocarā । śaṃkā vikalpamūlā hi śāmyetsvapratyayāditi ।। enamevārthamantaḥsthaṃ gṛhītvā mālinīmate ।
evamasyātmanaḥ kāle kasmiṃścidyogyatāvaśāt ।। śaivī saṃbadhyate śaktiḥ śāntā muktiphalapradā । tatsaṃbandhāttataḥ kaścittatkṣaṇādapavṛjyate ।। ityuktvā tīvratīvrākhyaviṣayaṃ bhāṣate punaḥ ।
ajñānena sahaikatvaṃ kasyacidvinivartate ।। rudraśaktisamāviṣṭaḥ sa yiyāsuḥ śivecchayā । bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati ।। tamārādhya tatastuṣṭāddīkṣāmāsādya śāṅkarīm ।
tatkṣaṇādvopabhogādvā dehapātācchivaṃ vrajet ।। asyārthā ātmanaḥ kācitkalanāmarśanātmikā । svaṃ rūpaṃ prati yā saiva ko api kāla ihoditaḥ ।। yogyatā śivatādātmyayogārhatvamihocyate ।
pūrvaṃ kiṃ na tathā kasmāttadaiveti na saṃgatam ।। tathābhāsanamujjhitvā na hi kālo asti kaścana । svātantryāttu tathābhāse kālaśaktirvijṛmbhatām ।। natu paryanuyuktyai sā śive tanmahimoditā ।
nanu śaivī mahāśaktiḥ saṃbaddhaivātmabhiḥ sthitā । satyaṃ sācchādanātmā tu śāntā tveṣā svarūpadṛk ।। kṣobho hi bheda evaikyaṃ praśamastanmayī tataḥ ।। tayā śāntyā tu saṃbaddhaḥ sthitaḥ śaktisvarūpabhāk ।
tyaktāṇubhāvo bhavati śivastacchaktidārḍhyataḥ ।। tatrāpi tāratamyādivaśācchīghracirāditaḥ । dehapāto bhavedasya yadvā kāṣṭhāditulyatā ।। samastavyavahāreṣu parācīnitacetanaḥ ।
tīvratīvramahāśaktisamāviṣṭaḥ sa sidhyati ।। evaṃ prāgviṣayo grantha iyānanyatra tu sphuṭam । granthāntaraṃ madhyatīvraśaktipātāṃśasūcakam ।। ajñānarūpatā puṃsi bodhaḥ saṃkocite hṛdi ।
saṃkoce vinivṛtte tu svasvabhāvaḥ prakāśate ।। rudraśaktisamāviṣṭa ityanenāsya varṇyate । cihnavargo ya ukto atra rudre bhaktiḥ suniścalā ।। mantrasiddhiḥ sarvatattvavaśitvaṃ kṛtyasaṃpadaḥ ।
kavitvaṃ sarvaśāstrārthaboddhṛtvamiti tatkramāt ।। svatāratamyayogātsyādeṣāṃ vyastasamastatā । tatrāpi bhuktau muktau ca prādhānyaṃ carcayedbudhaḥ ।। sa ityanto grantha eṣa dvitīyaviṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।
anyastu mandatīvrākhyaśaktipātavidhiṃ prati ।। mandatīvrācchaktibalādyiyāsāsyopajāyate । śivecchāvaśayogena sadguruṃ prati so api ca ।। atraiva lakṣitaḥ śāstre yaduktaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।
yaḥ punaḥ sarvatattvāni vettyetāni yathārthataḥ ।। sa gururmatsamaḥ prokto mantravīryaprakāśakaḥ । dṛṣṭāḥ saṃbhāvitāstena spṛṣṭāśca prītacetasā ।। narāḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyante saptajanmakṛtairapi ।
ye punardīkṣitāstena prāṇinaḥ śivacoditāḥ ।। te yatheṣṭaṃ phalaṃ prāpya padaṃ gacchantyanāmayam । kiṃ tattvaṃ tattvavedī ka ityāmarśanayogataḥ ।। pratibhānātsuḥṛtsaṅgādgurau jigamiṣurbhavet ।
evaṃ jigamiṣāyogādācāryaḥ prāpyate sa ca ।। tāratamyādiyogena saṃsiddhaḥ saṃskṛto api ca । prāgbhedabhāgī jhaṭiti kramātsāmastyatoṃśataḥ ।। ityādibhedabhinno hi gurorlābha ihoditaḥ ।
tasmāddīkṣāṃ sa labhate sadya eva śivapradām ।। jñānarūpāṃ yathā vetti sarvameva yathārthataḥ । jīvanmuktaḥ śivībhūtastadaivāsau nigadyate ।। dehasaṃbandhitāpyasya śivatāyai yataḥ sphuṭā ।
asyāṃ bhedo hi kathanātsaṅgamādavalokanāt ।। śāstrātsaṃkramaṇātsāmyacaryāsaṃdarśanāccaroḥ । mantramudrādimāhātmyātsamastavyastabhedataḥ ।। kriyayā vāntarākārarūpaprāṇapraveśataḥ ।
tadā ca dehasaṃstho api sa mukta iti bhaṇyate ।। uktaṃ ca śāstrayoḥ śrīmadratnamālāgamākhyayoḥ । yasminkāle tu guruṇā nirvikalpaṃ prakāśitam ।। tadaiva kila mukto asau yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam ।
prārabdhṛkarmasaṃbandhāddehasya sukhiduḥkhite ।। na viśaṅketa tacca śrīgamaśāstre nirūpitam । avidyopāsito deho hyanyajanmasamudbhuvā ।। karmaṇā tena bādhyante jñānino api kalevare ।
jātyāyurbhogadasyaikapraghaṭṭakatayā sthitiḥ ।। uktaikavacanāddhiśca yatastenetisaṃgatiḥ । abhyāsayuktisaṃkrāntivedhaghaṭṭanarodhataḥ ।। hutervā mantrasāmarthyātpāśacchedaprayogataḥ ।
sadyonirvāṇadāṃ kuryātsadyaḥprāṇaviyojikām ।। tatra tveṣo asti niyama āsanne maraṇakṣaṇe । tāṃ kuryānnānyathārabdhṛ karma yasmānna śuddhyati ।। uktaṃ ca pūrvamevaitanmaṃtrasāmarthyayogataḥ ।
prāṇairviyojito apyeṣa bhuṅkte śeṣaphalaṃ yataḥ ।। tajjanmaśeṣaṃ vividhamativāhya tataḥ sphuṭam । karmāntaranirodhena śīghramevāpavṛjyate ।। tasmātprāṇaharīṃ dīkṣāṃ nājñātvā maraṇakṣaṇam ।
vidadhyātparameśājñālaṅghanaikaphalā hi sā ।। ekastriko ayaṃ nirṇītaḥ śaktipāte apyathāparaḥ । tīvramadhye tu dīkṣāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ na tathā dṛḍhām ।। svātmano vetti śivatāṃ dehānte tu śivo bhavet ।
uktaṃ ca niśisaṃcārayogasaṃcāraśāstrayoḥ ।। vikalpāttu tanau sthitvā dahānte śivatāṃ vrajet । madhyamadhye śaktipāte śivalābhotsuko api san ।। bubhukṣuryatra yuktastadbhuktvā dehakṣaye śivaḥ ।
mandamadhye tu tatraiva tattve kvāpi niyojitaḥ ।। dehānte tattvagaṃ bhogaṃ bhuktvā paścācchivaṃ vrajet । tatrāpi tāratamyasya saṃbhavācciraśīghratā ।। bahvalpabhogayogaśca dehabhūmālpatākramaḥ ।
tīvramande madhyamande mandamande bubhukṣutā ।। kramānmukhyātimātreṇa vidhinaityantataḥ śivam । anye yiyāsurityādigranthaṃ prāggranthasaṃgatam ।। kurvanti madhyatīvrākhyaśaktisaṃpātagocaram ।
yadā pratibhayāviṣṭo apyeṣa saṃvādayojanām ।। icchanyiyāsurbhavati tadā nīyeta sadgurum । na sarvaḥ pratibhāviṣṭaḥ śaktyā nīyeta sadgurum ।। iti brūte yiyāsutvaṃ vaktavyaṃ nānyathā dhruvam ।
rudraśaktisamāviṣṭo nīyate sadguruṃ prati ।। tena prāptavivekotthajñānasaṃpūrṇamānasaḥ । dārḍhyasaṃvādarūḍhyāderyiyāsurbhavati sphuṭam ।। uktaṃ nandiśikhātantre prācyaṣaṭke maheśinā ।
abhilāṣaḥ śive deve paśūnāṃ bhavate tadā ।। yadā śaivābhimānena yuktā vai paramāṇavaḥ । tadaiva te vimuktāstu dīkṣitā guruṇā yataḥ ।। prāptimātrācca te siddhasādhyā iti hi gamyate ।
tamārādhyeti tu grantho mandatīvraikagocaraḥ ।। navadhā śaktipāto ayaṃ śaṃbhunāthena varṇitaḥ । idaṃ sāramiha jñeyaṃ paripūrṇacidātmanaḥ ।। prakāśaḥ paramaḥ śaktipāto avacchedavarjitaḥ ।
tathāvidho api bhogāṃśāvacchedenopalakṣitaḥ ।। aparaḥ śaktipāto asau paryante śivatāpradaḥ । ubhayatrāpi karmādermāyāntarvartino yataḥ ।। nāsti vyāpāra ityevaṃ nirapekṣaḥ sa sarvataḥ ।
tena māyāntarāle ye rudrā ye ca tadūrdhvataḥ ।। svādhikārakṣaye taistairbhairavībhūyate haṭhāt । ye māyayā hyanākrāntāste karmādyanapekṣiṇaḥ ।। śaktipātavaśādeva tāṃ tāṃ siddhimupāśritāḥ ।
nanu pūjājapadhyānaśaṃkarāsevanādibhiḥ ।। te mantrāditvamāpannāḥ kathaṃ karmānapekṣiṇaḥ । maivaṃ tathāvidhottīrṇaśivadhyānajapādiṣu ।। pravṛttireva prathamameṣāṃ kasmādvivicyatām ।
karmatatsāmyavairāgyamalapākādi dūṣitam ।। īśvarecchā nimittaṃ cecchaktipātaikahetutā । japādikā kriyāśaktirevetthaṃ natu karma tat ।। karma tallokarūḍhaṃ hi yadbhogamavaraṃ dadat ।
tirodhatte bhoktṛrūpaṃ saṃjñāyā tu na no bharaḥ ।। teṣāṃ bhogotkatā kasmāditi ceddattamuttaram । citrākāraprakāśo ayaṃ svatantraḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। svātantryāttu tirobhāvabandho bhoge asya bhoktṛtām ।
puṣṇansvaṃ rūpameva syānmalakarmādivarjitam ।। uktaṃ seyaṃ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya paśuvartinī । bandhayitrīti tatkarma kathyate rūpalopakṛt ।। jñātā sā ca kriyāśaktiḥ sadyaḥ siddhyupapādikā ।
avicchinnasvātmasaṃvitprathā siddhirihocyate ।। sā bhogamokṣasvātantryamahālakṣmīrihākṣayā । viṣṇvādirūpatā deve yā kācitsā nijātmanā ।। bhedayogavaśānmāyāpadamadhyavyavasthitā ।
tena tadrūpatāyogācchaktipātaḥ sthito api san ।। tāvantaṃ bhogamādhatte paryante śivatāṃ natu । yathā svātantryato rājāpyanugṛhṇāti kaṃcana ।। īśaśaktisamāveśāttathā viṣṇvādayo apyalam ।
māyāgarbhādhikārīyaśaktipātavaśāttataḥ ।। ko api pradhānapuruṣavivekī prakṛtergataḥ । utkṛṣṭāttata evāśu ko api buddhā vivekitām ।। kṣaṇātpuṃsaḥ kalāyāśca puṃmāyāntaravedakaḥ ।
kalāśrayasyāpyatyantaṃ karmaṇo vinivartanāt ।। jñānākalaḥ prāktanastu karmī tasyāśrayasthiteḥ । sa paraṃ prakṛterbudhne sṛṣṭiṃ nāyāti jātucit ।। māyādhare tu sṛjyetānanteśena pracodanāt ।
vijñānākalatāṃ prāptaḥ kevalādadhikārataḥ ।। malānmantratadīśādibhāvameti sadā śivāt । patyuḥ parasmādyastveṣa śaktipātaḥ sa vai malāt ।। ajñānākhyādviyokteti śivabhāvaprakāśakaḥ ।
nānyena śivabhāvo hi kenacitsaṃprakāśate ।। svacchandaśāstre tenoktaṃ vādināṃ tu śatatrayam । triṣaṣṭyabhyadhikaṃ bhrāntaṃ vaiṣṇavādyaṃ niśāntare ।। śivajñānaṃ kevalaṃ ca śivatāpattidāyakam ।
śivatāpattiparyantaḥ śaktipātaśca carcyate ।। anyathā kiṃ hi tatsyādyacchaivyā śaktyānadhiṣṭhitam । teneha vaiṣṇavādīnāṃ nādhikāraḥ kathaṃcana ।। te hi bhedaikavṛttitvādabhede dūravarjitāḥ ।
svātantryāttu maheśasya te api cecchivatonmukhāḥ ।। dviguṇā saṃskriyāstyeṣāṃ liṅgoddhṛtyātha dīkṣayā । duṣṭādhivāsavigame puṣpaiḥ kumbho adhivāsyate ।। dviguṇo asya sa saṃskāro netthaṃ śuddhe ghaṭe vidhiḥ ।
itthaṃ śrīśaktipāto ayaṃ nirapekṣa ihoditaḥ ।। anayaiva diśā neyaṃ mataṅgakiraṇādikam । granthagauravabhītyā tu tallikhitvā na yojitam ।। purāṇe api ca tasyaiva prasādādbhaktiriṣyate ।
yayā yānti parāṃ siddhiṃ tadbhāvagatamānasāḥ ।। evakāreṇa karmādisāpekṣatvaṃ niṣidhyate । prasādo nirmalībhāvastena saṃpūrṇarūpatā ।। ātmanā tena hi śivaḥ svayaṃ pūrṇaḥ prakāśate ।
śivībhāvamahāsiddhisparśavandhye tu kutracit ।। vaiṣṇavādau hi yā bhaktirnāsau kevalataḥ śivāt । śivo bhavati tatraiṣa kāraṇaṃ na tu kevalaḥ ।। nirmalaścāpi tu prāptāvacchitkarmādyapekṣakaḥ ।
yayā yānti parāṃ siddhimityasyedaṃ tu jīvitam ।। śrīmānutpaladevaścāpyasmākaṃ paramo guruḥ । śaktipātasamaye vicāraṇaṃ prāptamīśa na karoṣi karhicit ।। adya māṃ prati kimāgataṃ yataḥ svaprakāśanavidhau vilambase ।
karhicitprāptaśabdābhyāmanapekṣitvamūcivān ।। durlabhatvamarāgitvaṃ śaktipātavidhau vibhoḥ । aparārdhena tasyaiva śaktipātasya citratām ।। vyavadhānacirakṣiprabhedādyairupavarṇitaiḥ ।
śrīmatāpyaniruddhena śaktimunmīlinīṃ vibhoḥ ।। vyācakṣāṇena mātaṅge varṇitā nirapekṣatā । sthāvarānte api devasya svarūponmīlanātmikā ।। śaktiḥ patantī sāpekṣā na kvāpīti suvistarāt ।
evaṃ vicitre apyetasmiñchaktipāte sthite sati ।। tāratamyādibhirbhedaiḥ samayyādivicitratā । kaścidrudrāśatāmātrāpādanāttatprasādataḥ ।। śivatvaṃ kramaśo gacchet samayī yo nirūpyate ।
kaścicchuddhādhvabandhaḥ san putrakaḥ śīghramakramāt ।। bhogavyavadhinā ko api sādhakaściraśīghrataḥ । kaścitsaṃpūrṇakartavyaḥ kṛtyapañcakabhāgini ।। rūpe sthito guruḥ so api bhogamokṣādibhedabhāk ।
samayyādicatuṣkasya samāsavyāsayogataḥ ।। kramākramādibhirbhedaiḥ śaktipātasya citratā । kramikaḥ śaktipātaśca siddhānte vāmake tataḥ ।। dakṣe mate kule kaule ṣaḍardhe hṛdaye tataḥ ।
ullaṅghanavaśādvāpi jhaṭityakramameva vā ।। uktaṃ śrībhairavakule pañcadīkṣāsusaṃskṛtaḥ । gururullaṅghitādhaḥsthasrotā vai trikaśāstragaḥ ।। jñānācārādibhedena hyuttarādharatā vibhuḥ ।
śāstreṣvadīdṛśacchrīmatsarvācārahṛdādiṣu ।। vāmamārgābhiṣiktastu daiśikaḥ paratattvavit । tathāpi bhairave tantre punaḥ saṃskāramarhati ।। śaivavaimalasiddhāntā ārhatāḥ kārukāśca ye ।
sarve te paśavo jñeyā bhairave mātṛmaṇḍale ।। kulakālīvidhau coktaṃ vaiṣṇavānā viśeṣataḥ । bhasmaniṣṭhāprapannānāmityādau naiva yogyatā ।। svacchandaśāstre saṃkṣepāduktaṃ ca śrīmaheśinā ।
anyaśāstrarato yastu nāsau siddhiphalapradaḥ ।। samayyādikramāllabdhābhiṣeko hi gururmataḥ । sa ca śaktivaśāditthaṃ vaiṣṇavādiṣu ko anvayaḥ ।। chadmāpaśravaṇādyaistu tajjñānaṃ gṛhṇato bhavet ।
prāyaścittamatastādṛgadhikāryatra kiṃ bhavet ।। phalākāṅkṣāyutaḥ śiṣyastadekāyattasiddhikaḥ । dhruvaṃ pacyeta narake prāyaścittyupasevanāt ।। tirobhāvaprakāro ayaṃ yattādṛśi niyojitaḥ ।
gurau śivena tadbhaktiḥ śaktipāto asya nocyate ।। yadātu vaicitryavaśājjānīyāttasya tādṛśam । viparītapravṛttatvaṃ jñānaṃ tasmādupāharet ।। taṃ ca tyajetpāpavṛttiṃ bhavettu jñānatatparaḥ ।
yathā caurādgṛhītvārthaṃ taṃ nigṛhṇāti bhūpatiḥ ।। vaiṣṇavādestathā śaivaṃ jñānamāhṛtya sanmatiḥ । sa hi bhedaikavṛttitvaṃ śivajñāne śrute apyalam ।। nojjhatīti dṛḍhaṃ vāmādhiṣṭhitastatpaśūttamaḥ ।
śivenaiva tirobhāvya sthāpito niyaterbalāt ।। kathaṅkāraṃ patipadaṃ prayātu paratantritaḥ । svacchandaśāstre proktaṃ ca vaiṣṇavādiṣu ye ratāḥ ।। bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hyamokṣe mokṣalipsayā ।
vaiṣṇavādiḥ śaivaśāstraṃ melayannijaśāsane ।। dhruvaṃ saṃśayamāpanna ubhayabhraṣṭatāṃ vrajet । svadṛṣṭau paradṛṣṭau ca samayollaṅghanādasau ।। pratyavāyaṃ yato abhyeti carettannedṛśaṃ kramam ।
uktaṃ śrīmadgahvare ca parameśena tādṛśam ।। nānyaśāstrābhiyuktaṣu śivajñānaṃ prakāśate । tanna saiddhāntiko vāme nāsau dakṣe sa no mate ।। kulakaule trike nāsau pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ paratra tu ।
avacchinno anavacchedaṃ no vettyānantyasaṃsthitaḥ ।। sarvaṃsahastato adhaḥstha ūrdhvastho adhikṛto guruḥ । svātmīyādharasaṃsparśātprāṇayannadharāḥ kriyāḥ ।। saphalīkurute yattadūrdhvastho gururuttamaḥ ।
adhaḥsthadṛkstho apyetādṛggurusevī bhavetsa yaḥ ।। tādṛkśaktinipāteddho yo drāgūrdhvamimaṃ nayet । tattadgirinadīprāyāvacchinne kṣetrapīṭhake ।। uttarottaravijñāne nādhikāryadharo adharaḥ ।
uttarottaramācāryaṃ vidannapyadharo adharaḥ ।। kurvannadhikriyāṃ śāstralaṅghī nigrahabhājanam । śaktipātabalādeva jñānayogyavicitratā ।। śrautaṃ cintāmayaṃ dvyātma bhāvanāmayameva ca ।
jñānaṃ taduttaraṃ jyāyo yato mokṣaikakāraṇam ।। tattvebhya uddhṛtiṃ kvāpi yojanaṃ sakale akale । kathaṃ kuryādvinā jñānaṃ bhāvanāmayamuttamam ।। yogī tu prāptatattattvasiddhirapyuttame pade ।
sadāśivādye svabhyastajñānitvādeva yojakaḥ ।। adhareṣu ca tattveṣu yā siddhiryogajāsya sā । vimocanāyāṃ nopāyaḥ sthitāpi dhanadāravat ।। yastūtpannasamastādhvasiddhiḥ sahi sadāśivaḥ ।
sākṣādeṣa kathaṃ martyānmocayedgurutāṃ vrajan ।। tenoktaṃ mālinītantre vicārya jñānayogite । yataśca mokṣadaḥ proktaḥ svabhyastajñānavānbudhaiḥ ।। tasmātsvabhyastavijñānataivaikaṃ gurulakṣaṇam ।
vibhāgastveṣa me proktaḥ śaṃbhunāthena darśyate ।। mokṣajñānaparaḥ kuryādguruṃ svabhyastavedanam । anyaṃ tyajetprāptamapi tathācoktaṃ śivena tat ।। āmodārthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpātpuṣpāntaraṃ vrajet ।
vijñānārthī tathā śiṣyo gurorgurvantaraṃ vrajet ।। śaktihīnaṃ guruṃ prāpya mokṣajñāne kathaṃ śrayet । naṣṭamūle drume devi kutaḥ puṣpaphalādikam ।। uttarottaramutkarṣalakṣmīṃ paśyannapi sthitaḥ ।
adhame yaḥ pade tasmātko anyaḥ syāddaivadagdhakaḥ ।। yastu bhogaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca vāñchedvijñānameva ca । svabhyastajñāninaṃ yogasiddhaṃ sa gurumāśrayet ।। tadabhāve tu vijñānamokṣayorjñāninaṃ śrayet ।
bhuktyaṃśe yoginaṃ yastatphalaṃ dātuṃ bhavetkṣamaḥ ।। phaladānākṣame yoginyapāyaikopadeśini । varaṃ jñānī yo abhyupāyaṃ diśedapica mocayet ।। jñānī na pūrṇa evaiko yadi hyaṃśāṃśikākramāt ।
jñānānyādāya vijñānaṃ kurvītākhaṇḍamaṇḍalam ।। tenāsaṃkhyāngurūnkuryātpūraṇāya svasaṃvidaḥ । dhanyastu pūrṇavijñānaṃ jñānārthī labhate gurum ।। nānāgurvāgamasrotaḥpratibhāmātramiśritam ।
kṛtvā jñānārṇavaṃ svābhirvipruṅgiḥ plāvayenna kim ।। ā tapanānmoṭakāntaṃ yasya me asti gurukramaḥ । tasya me sarvaśiṣyasya nopadeśadaridratā ।। śrīmatā kallaṭenetthaṃ guruṇā tu nyarūpyata ।
ahamapyata evādhaḥśāstradṛṣṭikutūhalāt ।। tārkikaśrautabauddhārhadvaiṣṇavādīnnaseviṣi । lokādhyātmātimārgādikarmayogavidhānataḥ ।। saṃbodhotkarṣabāhulyātkramotkṛṣṭānvibhāvayet ।
śrīpūrvaśāstre praṣṭāro munayo nāradādayaḥ ।। prāgvaiṣṇavāḥ saugatāśca siddhāntādividastataḥ । kramāttrikārthavijñānacandrotsukitadṛṣṭayaḥ ।। tasmānna gurubhūyastve viśaṅketa kadācana ।
gurvantararate mūḍhe āgamāntarasevake ।। pratyavāyo ya āmnātaḥ sa itthamiti gṛhyatām । yo yatra śāstre adhikṛtaḥ sa tatra gururucyate ।। tatrānadhikṛto yastu tadgurvantaramucyate ।
yathā tanmaṇḍalāsīno maṇḍalāntarabhūpatim ।। svamaṇḍalajigīṣuḥ sansevamāno vinaśyati । tathottarottarajñānasiddhiprepsuḥ samāśrayan ।। adharādharamācāryaṃ vināśamadhigacchati ।
evamevordhvavartiṣṇorāgamātsiddhivāñchakaḥ ।। māyīyaśāstranirato vināśaṃ pratipadyate । uktaṃ ca śrīmadānande karma saṃśritya bhāvataḥ ।। jugupsate tattasmiṃśca viphale anyatsamāśrayet ।
dināddinaṃ hrasaṃstvevaṃ pacyate rauravādiṣu ।। yastūrdhvordhvapathaprepsuradharaṃ gurumāgamam । jihāsecchaktipātena sa dhanyaḥ pronmukhīkṛtaḥ ।। ata eveha śāstreṣu śaiveṣveva nirūpyate ।
śāstrāntarārthānāśvastānprati saṃskārako vidhiḥ ।। ataścāpyuttamaṃ śaivaṃ yo anyatra patitaḥ sahi । ihānugrāhya ūrdhvordhvaṃ netastu patitaḥ kvacit ।। ata eva hi sarvajñairbrahmaviṣṇvādibhirnije ।
na śāsane samāmnātaṃ liṅgoddhārādi kiṃcana ।। itthaṃ viṣṇvādayaḥ śaivaparamārthaikavedinaḥ । kāṃścitprati tathādikṣuste mohādvimatiṃ śritāḥ ।। tathāvidhāmeva matiṃ satyasaṃsparśanākṣamām ।
dṛṣṭvaiṣāṃ brahmaviṣṇvādyairbuddhairapi tathoditam ।। ityeṣa yuktyāgamataḥ śaktipāto vivecitaḥ । tirobhāvasvarūpaṃ tu kathyamānaṃ vivicyatām । svabhāvāt parameśāno niyatyaniyatikramam ।।
spṛśanprakāśate yena tataḥ svacchanda ucyate । niyatiṃ karmaphalayorāśrityaiṣa maheśvaraḥ ।। sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhārānvidhatte avāntarasthitīn । mahāsarge punaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārānantyaśālini ।।
ekaḥ sa devo viśvātmā niyatityāgataḥ prabhuḥ । avāntare yā ca sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiścātrāpyayantritam ।। nojjhatyeṣa vapustyaktaniyatiśca sthito atra tat । niyatyaiva yadā caiṣa svarūpācchādanakramāt ।।
bhuṅkte duḥkhavimohādi tadā karmaphalakramaḥ । tyaktvā tu niyamaṃ kārmaṃ duḥkhamohaparītatām ।। bibhāsayiṣurāste ayaṃ tirodhāne anapekṣakaḥ । yathā prakāśasvātantryāt pratibuddho apyabuddhavat ।।
āste tadvadanuttīrṇo apyuttīrṇa iva ceṣṭate । yathā ca buddhastāṃ mūḍhaceṣṭāṃ kurvannapi dviṣan ।। hṛdyāste mūḍha evaṃ hi prabuddhānāṃ viceṣṭitam । śrīvidyādhipatiścāha mānastotre tadīdṛśam ।।
ye yauṣmāke śāsanamārge kṛtadīkṣāḥ saṃgacchanto mohavaśādvipratipattim । nūnaṃ teṣā nāsti bhavadbhānuniyogaḥ saṅkocaḥ kiṃ sūryakaraistāmarasānām ।। jñātajñeyā dhātṛpadasthā api santo ye tvanmārgātkāpathagāste api na samyaka । prāyasteṣāṃ laiṅgikabuddhyādisamuttho mithyābodhaḥ sarpavasādīpajakalpaḥ ।।
yasmādviddhaṃ sūtakamukhyena nu tāmraṃ tadyadbhūyaḥ svāṃ prakṛtiṃ no samupeyāt । no taiḥ pītaṃ bhūtalasaṃsthairamṛtaṃ tadyeṣāṃ tṛṭkṣudduḥkhavibādhāḥ punarasmin ।। tataḥ prabuddhaceṣṭāsau mantracaryārcanādikā । dveṣeddhāntardahatyenaṃ dāhaḥ śaṅkaiva sā yataḥ ।।
na cāsya karmamahimā tādṛgyenetthamāsta saḥ । kiṃ hi tatkarma kasmādvā pūrveṇātra samo vidhiḥ ।। tasmātsā parameśecchā yayāyaṃ mohitastathā । anantakālasaṃvedyaduḥkhapātratvamīhate ।।
tatrāpi cecchāvaicitryādihāmutrobhayātmakaḥ । duḥkhasyāpi vibhedo asti ciraśaighryakṛtastathā ।। kālakāmāndhakādīnāṃ paulastyapuravāsinām । tathānyeṣāṃ tirobhāvastāvadduḥkho hyamutra ca ।।
anyo api ca tirobhāvaḥ samayollaṅghanātmakaḥ । yaduktaṃ parameśena śrīmadānandagahvare ।। samayollaṅghanāddevi kravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ । tatrāpi mandatīvrādibhedādbahuvidhaḥ kramaḥ ।।
svātantryācca maheśasya tirobhūto apyasau svayam । paradvāreṇa vābhyeti bhūyo anugrahamapyalam ।। bhūyo anugrahataḥ prāyaścittādyācaraṇe sati । anusāreṇa dīkṣādau kṛte syācchivatāmayaḥ ।।
tirobhūtaḥ paretāsurapi bandhusuhṛdgurūn । ālambya śaktipātena dīkṣādyairanugṛhyate ।। tatrāpi kālaśīghratvaciratvādivibhedatām । tathaiti śaktipāto asau yenāyāti śivātmatām ।।
itthaṃ sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsatirobhāvamanugrahaḥ । iti pañcasu kartṛtvaṃ śivatvaṃ saṃvidātmanaḥ ।। pañcakṛtyasvatantratvasaṃpūrṇasvātmamāninaḥ । yogino arcājapadhyānayogāḥ saṃsyuḥ sadoditāḥ ।।
aindrajālikavṛttānte na rajyeta kadācana । sādāśivo api yo bhogo bandhaḥ so apyucitātmanām ।। jñātṛtvameva śivatā svātantryaṃ tadihocyate । kulālavattu kartṛtvaṃ na mukhyaṃ tadadhiṣṭhiteḥ ।।
iti jñātvā grahītavyā naiva jātvapi khaṇḍanā । śivo ahaṃ cenmadicchānuvarti kiṃ na jagattviti ।। mamecchāmanuvartantāmityatrāhaṃvidi sphuret । śivo vā parameśāno dehādiratha nirmitaḥ ।।
śivasya tāvadastyetaddehastveṣa tathā tvayā । kṛtaḥ kānyā dehatāsya tatkiṃ syādvācyatāpadam ।। uktaṃ ca siddhasantānaśrīmadūrmimahākule । pavanabhramaṇaprāṇavikṣepādikṛtaśramāḥ ।।
kuhakādiṣu ye bhrāntāste bhrāntāḥ parame pade । sarvatra bahumānena yāpyutkrāntirvimuktaye ।। proktā sā sāraśāstreṣu bhogopāyatayoditā । yadi sarvagatā devo vadotkramya kva yāsyati ।।
athāsarvagatastarhi ghaṭatulyastadā bhavet । utkrāntividhiyogo ayamekadeśena kathyate ।। niraṃśe śivatattve tu kathamutkrāntisaṃgatiḥ । yathā dharādau vāyvante bhṛgvambvagnyupavāsakaiḥ ।।
ātmano yojanaṃ vyomni tadvadutkrāntivartanā । tasmānnotkramayejjīvaṃ paratattvasamīhayā ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre tūktaṃ yadutkrānterlakṣaṇaṃ na tat । muktyupāyatayā kiṃtu bhogahānyai tathaiṣaṇāt ।।
japadhyānādisaṃsiddhaḥ svātantryācchaktipātataḥ । bhogaṃ prati viraktaśceditthaṃ dehaṃ tyajediti ।। svacchandamṛtyorapi yad bhīṣmādeḥ śrūyate kila । bhogavairasyasaṃprāptau jīvitāntopasarpaṇam ।।
yogamantrāmṛtadravyavarādyaiḥ siddhibhāktanuḥ । hātuṃ nahyanyathā śakyā vinoktakramayogataḥ ।। uktaṃ ca mālinītantre parameśena tādṛśam । sarvamapyathavā bhogaṃ manyamāno virūpakam ।।
ityādi vadatā sarvairalakṣyāntaḥsatattvakam । evaṃ sṛṣṭyādikartavyasvasvātantryopadeśanam ।। yatsaiva mukhyadīkṣā syācchiṣyasya śivadāyinī । uktaṃ śrīniśicāre ca bhairavīyeṇa tejasā ।।
vyāptaṃ viśvaṃ prapaśyanti vikalpojjhitacetasaḥ । vikalpayuktacittastu piṇḍapātācchivaṃ vrajet ।। bāhyadīkṣādiyogena caryāsamayakalpanaiḥ । avikalpastathādyaiva jīvanmukto na saṃśayaḥ ।।
saṃsārajīrṇatarumūlakalāpakalpasaṃkalpasāntaratayā paramārthavahneḥ । syurvisphuliṅgakaṇikā api cettadante dedīpyate vimalabodhahutāśarāśiḥ ।। itthaṃ dīkṣopakramo ayaṃ darśitaḥ śāstrasaṃmataḥ । athaitadupayogāya yāgastāvannirūpyate ।
tatra dīkṣaiva bhoge ca muktau cāyātyupāyatām ।। svayaṃ saṃskārayogādvā tadaṅgaṃ tatpradarśyate । yo yatrābhilaṣedbhogān sa tatraiva niyojitaḥ ।। siddhibhāṅmantraśaktyeti śrīmatsvāyaṃbhuve vibhuḥ ।
yogyatāvaśato yatra vāsanā yasya tatra saḥ ।। yojyo na cyavate tasmāditi śrīmālinīmate । vadanbhogādyupāyatvaṃ dīkṣāyāḥ prāha no guruḥ ।। na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yoge asti śāṅkare ।
na ca yogādhikāritvamekamevānayā bhavet ।। api mantrādhikāritvaṃ muktiśca śivadīkṣayā । ityasminmālinīvākye sākṣānmokṣābhyupāyatā ।। dīkṣāyāḥ kathitā prācyagranthena punarucyate ।
pāramparyeṇa saṃskṛtyā mokṣabhogābhyupāyatā ।। yeṣāmadhyavasāyo asti na vidyāṃ pratyaśaktitaḥ । sukhopāyamidaṃ teṣāṃ vidhānamuditaṃ guroḥ ।। iti śrīmanmataṅgākhye hyuktā mokṣābhyupāyatā ।
samyagjñānasvabhāvā hi vidyā sākṣādvimocikā ।। uktaṃ tatraiva tattvānāṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvataḥ । heyādeyatvakathane vidyāpāda iti sphuṭam ।। tatrāśaktāstu ye teṣāṃ dīkṣācaryāsamādhayaḥ ।
te vidyāpūrvakā yasmāttasmājjñānyuttamottamaḥ ।। jñānaṃ ca śāstrāttaccāpi śrāvyo nādīkṣito yataḥ । ato asya saṃskriyāmātropayogo dīkṣayā kṛtaḥ ।। yatra tatrāstu guruṇā yojito asau phalaṃ punaḥ ।
svavijñānocitaṃ yāti jñānītyuktaṃ purā kila ।। yasya tvīśaprasādena divyā kācana yogyatā । guroḥ śiśośca tau naiva prati dīkṣopayogitā ।। jñānameva tadā dīkṣā śrītraiśikanirūpaṇāt ।
sarvaśāstrārthavettṛtvamakasmāccāsya jāyate ।। iti śrīmālinīnītyā yaḥ sāṃsiddhikasaṃvidaḥ । sa uttamādhikārī syājjñānavānhi gururmataḥ ।। ātmane vā parebhyo vā hitārthī cetayedidam ।
ityuktyā mālinīśāstre tatsarvaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam ।। jñānayogyāstathā keciccaryāyogyāstathāpare । dīkṣāyogyā yogayogyā iti śrīkairaṇe vidhau ।। tatroktalakṣaṇaḥ karmayogajñānaviśāradaḥ ।
uttarottaratābhūmyutkṛṣṭo gururudīritaḥ ।। sa ca prāguktaśaktyanyatamapātapavitritam । parīkṣya pṛṣṭvā vā śiṣyaṃ dīkṣākarma samācaret ।। uktaṃ svacchandaśāstre ca śiṣyaṃ pṛcchedguruḥ svayam ।
phalaṃ prārthayase yādṛktādṛksādhanamārabhe ।। vāsanābhedataḥ sādhyaprāptirmantrapracoditā । mantramudrādhvadravyāṇāṃ home sādhāraṇā sthitiḥ ।। vāsanābhedato bhinnaṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca guroḥ phalam ।
sādhako dvividhaḥ śaivadharmā lokojjhitasthitiḥ ।। lokadharmī phalākāṃkṣī śubhasthaścāśubhojjhitaḥ । dvidhā mumukṣurnirbījaḥ samayādivivarjitaḥ ।। bālabāliśavṛddhastrībhogabhugvyādhitādikaḥ ।
anyaḥ sabījo yasyetthaṃ dīkṣoktā śivaśāsane ।। vidvaddvandvasahānāṃ tu sabījā samayātmikā । dīkṣānugrāhikā pālyā viśeṣasamayāstu taiḥ ।। abhāvaṃ bhāvayetsamyakkarmaṇāṃ prācyabhāvinām ।
mumukṣornirapekṣasya prārabdhrekaṃ na śādhayet ।। sādhakasya tu bhūtyarthamitthameva viśodhayet । śivadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā lokadharmāpahāriṇī ।। adharmarūpiṇāmeva na śubhānāṃ tu śodhanam ।
lokadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā mantrārādhanavarjitā ।। prārabdhadehabhede tu bhuṅkte asāvaṇimādikam । bhuktvordhvaṃ yāti yatraiṣa yukto atha sakale akale ।। samayācārapāśaṃ tu nirbījāyāṃ viśodhayet ।
dīkṣāmātreṇa muktiḥ syādbhaktyā deve gurau sadā ।। sadyonirvāṇadā seyaṃ nirbījā yeti bhaṇyate । atītānāgatārabdhapāśatrayaviyojikā ।। dīkṣāvasāne śuddhasya dehatyāge paraṃ padam ।
dehatyāge sabījāyāṃ karmābhāvādvipadyate ।। samayācārapāśaṃ tu dīkṣitaḥ pālayetsadā । evaṃ pṛṣṭvā parijñāya vicārya ca guruḥ svayam ।। ucitāṃ saṃvidhitsustāṃ vāsanāṃ tādṛśīṃ śrayet ।
āyātaśaktipātasya dīkṣāṃ prati na daiśikaḥ ।। avajñāṃ vidadhīteti śaṃbhunājñā nirūpitā । svadhanena daridrasya kuryāddīkṣāṃ guruḥ svayam ।। api dūrvāmbubhiryadvā dīkṣāyai bhikṣate śiśuḥ ।
bhikṣopāttaṃ nijaṃ vātha dhanaṃ prāggurave śiśuḥ ।। dadyādyena viśuddhaṃ tadyāgayogyatvamaśnute । tatrādau śivatāpattisvātantryāveśa eva yaḥ ।। sa eva hi guruḥ kāryastato asau dīkṣaṇe kṣamaḥ ।
śivatāveśitā cāsya bahūpāyā pradarśitā ।। kramikā bāhyarūpā tu snānanyāsārcanādibhiḥ । bahvīṣu tāsu tāsveṣa kriyāsu śivatāṃ hṛdi ।। saṃdadhaddṛḍhamabhyeti śivabhāvaṃ prasannadhīḥ ।
śivībhūto yadyadicchettattatkartuṃ samīhate ।। śivābhimānitopāyo bāhyo heturna mokṣadaḥ । śivo ayaṃ śiva evāsmītyevamācāryaśiṣyayoḥ ।। hetutadvattayā dārḍhyābhimāno mocako hyaṇoḥ ।
nādhyātmena vinā bāhyaṃ nādhyātmaṃ bāhyavarjitam ।। siddhyejjñānakriyābhyāṃ taddvitīyaṃ saṃprakāśate । śrībrahmayāmale deva iti tena nyarūpayat ।। śrīmadānandaśāstre ca nāśuddhiḥ syādvipaścitaḥ ।
kintu snānaṃ suvastratvaṃ tuṣṭisaṃjananaṃ bhavet ।। tatra prasiddhadehādimātṛnirmalatākramāt । ayatnato antarantaḥ syānnairmalya snāyatāṃ tataḥ ।। snānaṃ ca devadevasya yanmūrtyaṣṭakamucyate ।
tatraivaṃ mantradīpte antarmaladāhe nimajjanam ।। tatreṣṭamantrahṛdayo gorajo antaḥ padatrayam । gatvāgatya bhajetsnānaṃ pārthivaṃ dhṛtidāyakam ।। astramantritamṛddhūtamalaḥ pañcāṅgamantritaiḥ ।
jalairmūrdhādipādāntaṃ kramādākṣālayettataḥ ।। nimajjetsāṅgamūlākhyaṃ japannā tanmayatvataḥ । utthāyāśeṣasajjyotirdevatāgarbhamambare ।। sūryaṃ jalena mālinyā tarpayedviśvatarpakam ।
devānpitṝnmunīnyakṣān rakṣāṃsyanyacca bhautikam ।। sarvaṃ saṃtarpayetprāṇo vīryātmā sa ca bhāskaraḥ । tato japetparāmekāṃ prāguktoccārayogataḥ ।। ā tanmayatvasaṃvitterjalasnānamidaṃ matam ।
agnyutthaṃ bhasma śastreṇa japtvā malanivarhaṇam ।। kavaktrahṛdguhyapade pañcāṅgairbhasma mantritam । bhasmamuṣṭiṃ sāṅgamūlajaptāṃ mūrdhni kṣipettataḥ ।। hastapādau jalenaiva prakṣālyācamanādikam ।
tarpaṇaṃ japa ityevaṃ bhasmasnānaṃ hi taijasam ।। gorajovatyanudrikte vāyau hlādini mantravāk । gatyāgatiprayoge vā vāyavyaṃ snānamācaret ।। amale gagane vyāpinyekāgrībhūtadṛṣṭikaḥ ।
smaranmantraṃ yadāsīta kānyā nirmalatā tataḥ ।। yadi vā nirmalādvyomnaḥ patatā vāriṇā tanum । sparśayenmantrajapayuṅ nābhasaṃ snānamīdṛśam ।। evaṃ somārkatejaḥsu śivabhāvena bhāvanāt ।
nimajjandhautamālinyaḥ kva vā yogyo na jāyate ।। ātmaiva parameśāno nirācāramahāhradaḥ । viśvaṃ nimajjya tatraiva tiṣṭhecchuddhaśca śodhakaḥ ।। iti snānāṣṭakaṃ śuddhāvuttarottaramuttamam ।
sarvatra paścāttaṃ mantramekībhūtamupāharet ।। ghṛtyāpyāyamalaploṣavīryavyāptimṛjisthitīḥ । abhedaṃ ca kramādeti snānāṣṭakaparo muniḥ ।। etā hyanugrahātmāno mūrtayo aṣṭau śivātmikāḥ ।
svarūpaśivarūpābhyāṃ dhyānāttattatphalapradāḥ ।। anena vidhinārcāyāṃ kandādhārādiyojanām । kurvanvyāsasamāsābhyāṃ dharādestatphalaṃ bhajet ।। tathāhi yogasaṃcāre mantrāḥ syurbhuvi pārthivāḥ ।
āpye āpyā yāvadamī śive śivamayā iti ।। śrīnirmaryādaśāstre api taditthaṃ sunirūpitam । dharādeśca viśeṣo asti vīrasādhakasaṃmataḥ ।। raṇareṇurvīrajalaṃ vīrabhasma mahāmarut ।
śmaśānāraṇyagaganaṃ candrārkau tadupāhitau ।। ātmā nirdhūtaniḥśeṣavikalpātaṅkasusthitaḥ । snānārcādāvityupāsyaṃ vīrāṇāṃ vigrahāṣṭakam ।। śrīmantriśirasi proktaṃ madyaśīdhusurādinā ।
susvādunā prasannena tanunā susugandhinā ।। kandalādigatenāntarbahiḥ saṃskārapañcakam । kṛtvā nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣya tāḍanāpyāyaguṇṭhanam ।। mantracakrasya tanmadhye pūjāṃ vipruṭpratarpaṇam ।
tenātmasekaḥ kalaśamudrayā cābhiṣecanam ।। devatātarpaṇaṃ dehaprāṇobhayapathāśritam । sarvatīrthatapoyajñadānādi phalamaśnute ।। madyasnāne sādhakendro mumukṣuḥ kevalībhavet ।
yataḥ śivamayaṃ madyaṃ sarve mantrāḥ śivodbhavāḥ ।। śivaśaktyorna bhedo asti śaktyutthāstu marīcayaḥ । tāsāmānandajanakaṃ madyaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ ।। prabuddhe saṃvidaḥ pūrṇe rūpe adhikṛtibhājanam ।
mantradhyānasamādhānabhedātsnānaṃ tu yanna tat ।। yuktaṃ snānaṃ yato nyāsakarmādau yogyatāvaham । asya snānāṣṭakasyāsti bāhyāntaratayā dvitā ।। āntaraṃ tadyathordhvendudhārāmṛtapariplavaḥ ।
yato randhrordhvagāḥ sārdhamaṅgulaṃ vyāpya saṃsthitāḥ ।। mūrtayo aṣṭāvapi proktāḥ pratyekaṃ dvādaśāntataḥ । eṣāmekatamaṃ snānaṃ kuryāddvitryādiśo apivā ।। iti snānavidhiḥ prokto bhairaveṇāmalīkṛtau ।
snānānantarakartavyamathedamupadiśyate ।। bhāvaṃ prasannamālocya vrajedyāgagṛhaṃ tataḥ । parvatāgranadītīraikaliṅgādi yaducyate ।। tadbāhyamiha tatsiddhiviśeṣāya na muktaye ।
ābhyantaraṃ nagāgrādi dehāntaḥ prāṇayojanam ।। sādhakānāmupāyaḥ syātsiddhaye natu muktaye । pīṭhasthānaṃ sadā yāgayogyaṃ śāstreṣu bhaṇyate ।। tacca bāhyāntarādrūpādbahirdehe ca susphuṭam ।
yataḥ śrīnaiśasañcāre parameśo nyarūpayat ।। tasyecchā pīṭhamādhāro yatrasthaṃ sacarācaram । agryaṃ tatkāmarūpaṃ syādbindunādadvayaṃ tataḥ ।। nādapīṭhaṃ pūrṇagirirdakṣiṇe vāmataḥ punaḥ ।
pīṭhamuḍḍayanaṃ bindurmukhyaṃ pīṭhatrayaṃ tvidam ।। jñeyaṃ saṃkalpanārūpamardhapīṭhamataḥ param । śāktaṃ kuṇḍalinī vedakalaṃ ca tryupapīṭhakam ।। devīkoṭṭojjayinyau dve tathā kulagiriḥ paraḥ ।
lālanaṃ baindavaṃ vyāptiriti saṃdohakatrayam ।। puṇḍravardhanavārendre tathaikāmramidaṃ bahiḥ । navadhā kathitaṃ pīṭhamantarbāhyakrameṇa tat ।। kṣetrāṣṭakaṃ kṣetravido hṛdambhojadalāṣṭakam ।
prayāgo varaṇā paścādaṭṭahāso jayantikā ।। vārāṇasī ca kāliṅgaṃ kulūtā lāhulā tathā । upakṣetrāṣṭakaṃ prāhurhṛtpadmāgradalāṣṭakam ।। virajairuḍikā hālā elā pūḥ kṣīrikā purī ।
māyākhyā marudeśaśca bāhyābhyantararūpataḥ ।। hṛtpadmadalasandhīnāmupasaṃdohakāṣṭatā । jālandharaṃ ca naipālaṃ kaśmīrā gargikā haraḥ ।। mlecchadigdvāravṛttiśca kurukṣetraṃ ca kheṭakam ।
dvipathaṃ dvayasaṃghaṭṭāttripathaṃ trayamelakāt ।। catuṣpathaṃ śaktimato layāttatraiva manvate । nāsāntatālurandhrāntametaddehe vyavasthitam ।। bhrūmadhyakaṇṭhahṛtsaṃjñaṃ madhyamaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।
nābhikandamahānandadhāma tatkaulikaṃ trayam ।। parvatāgraṃ nadītīramekaliṅgaṃ tadeva ca । kiṃ vātibahunā sarvaṃ saṃvittau prāṇagaṃ tataḥ ।। tato dehasthitaṃ tasmāddehāyatanago bhavet ।
bāhye tu tādṛśāntaḥsthayogamārgaviśāradāḥ ।। devyaḥ svabhāvājjāyante pīṭhaṃ tadvāhyamucyate । yathā svabhāvato mlecchā adharmapathavartinaḥ ।। tatra deśe niyatyetthaṃ jñānayogau sthitau kvacit ।
yathācātanmayo apyeti pāpitāṃ taiḥ samāgamāt ।। tathā pīṭhasthito apyeti jñānayogādipātratām । mukhyatvena śarīre antaḥ prāṇe saṃvidi paśyataḥ ।। viśvametatkimanyaiḥ syādbahirbhramaṇaḍambaraiḥ ।
ityevamantarbāhye ca tattaccakraphalārthinām ।। sthānabhedo vicitraśca sa śāstre saṃkhyayojjhitaḥ । śrīvīrāvalihṛdaye sapta sthānāni śaktikamalayugam ।। surapathacatuṣpathākhyaśmaśānamekāntaśūnyavṛkṣau ca ।
iti nirvacanaguṇasthityupacāradṛśā vibodha evoktaḥ ।। tadadhiṣṭhite ca cakre śārīre bahiratho bhavedyāgaḥ । muktaye tanna yāgasya sthānabhedaḥ prakalpyate ।। deśopāyā na sā yasmātsā hi bhāvaprasādataḥ ।
uktaṃ ca śrīniśācāre siddhisādhanakāṅkṣiṇām ।। sthānaṃ mumukṣuṇā tyājyaṃ sarpakañcukavattvidam । muktirna sthānajanitā yadā śrotrapathaṃ gatam ।। gurostattvaṃ tadā muktistaddārḍhyāya tu pūjanam ।
yatra yatra hṛdambhojaṃ vikāsaṃ pratipadyate ।। tatraiva dhāmni bāhye antaryāgaśrīḥ pratitiṣṭhati । nānyatragatyā mokṣo asti so ajñānagranthikartanāt ।। tacca saṃvidvikāsena śrīmadvīrāvalīpade ।
guravastu vimuktau vā siddhau vā vimalā matiḥ ।। heturityubhayatrāpi yāgauko yanmanoramam । niyatiprāṇatāyogātsāmagrītastu yadyapi ।। siddhayo bhāvavaimalyaṃ tathāpi nikhilottamam ।
vimalībhūtahṛdayo yattatra pratibimbayet ।। sādhyaṃ tadasya dārḍhyena saphalatvāya kalpate । uktaṃ śrīsāraśāstre ca nirvikalpo hi sidhyati ।। kliśyante savikalpāstu kalpokte api kṛte sati ।
tadākramya balaṃ mantrā ayamevodayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।। ityādibhiḥ spandavākyairetadeva nirūpitam । tasmātsiddhyai vimuktyai vā pūjājapasamādhiṣu ।। tatsthānaṃ yatra viśrāntisundaraṃ hṛdayaṃ bhavet ।
yāgaukaḥ prāpya śuddhātmā bahireva vyavasthitaḥ ।। nyāsaṃ sāmānyataḥ kuryādbahiryāgaprasiddhaye । mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vātha dvitayaṃ vā kramākramāt ।। sṛṣṭyapyayadvayaiḥ kuryādekaikaṃ saṃghaśo dviśaḥ ।
lalāṭavaktre dṛkkarṇanāsāgaṇḍaradauṣṭhage ।। dvaye dvaye śikhājihve visargāntāstu ṣoḍaśa । dakṣānyayoḥ skandhabāhukarāṅgulinakhe kacau ।। vargau ṭatau kramātkaṭyāmūrvādiṣu niyojayet ।
pavargaṃ pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhe jaṭhare hṛdyatho nava ।। tvagraktamāṃsasūtrāsthivasāśukrapurogamān । ityeṣa mātṛkānyāso mālinyāstu nirūpyate ।। na śikhā ṛ ṝ ḷ ḷḷ ca śiromālā tha mastakam ।
netrāṇi cordhve dho anye ī ghrāṇaṃ mudre ṇu ṇū śrutī ।। bakavarga i ā vaktradantajihvāgiri kramāt । vabhayāḥ kaṇṭhadakṣādiskandhayorbhujayorḍaḍhau ।। ṭho hastayorjhañau śākhā jraṭau śūlakapālake ।
pa hṛcchalau stanau kṣīramā sa jīvo visargayuk ।। prāṇo havarṇaḥ kathitaḥ ṣakṣāvudaranābhigau । maśāntā kaṭiguhyoruyugmagā jānunī tathā ।। eaikārau tatparau tu jaṅghe caraṇagau daphau ।
ityeṣā mālinī devī śaktimatkṣobhitā yataḥ ।। kṛtyāveśāttataḥ śāktī tanuḥ sā paramārthataḥ । anyonyaṃ bījayonīnāṃ kṣobhādvaisargikodayāt ।। kāṃ kāṃ siddhiṃ na vitaretkiṃ vā nyūnaṃ na pūrayet ।
yonibījārṇasāṃkaryaṃ bahudhā yadyapi sthitam ।। tathāpi nādiphānto ayaṃ kramo mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । phakārādisamuccārānnakārānte adhvamaṇḍalam ।। saṃhṛtya saṃvidyā pūrṇā sā śabdairvarṇyate katham ।
ataḥ śāstreṣu bahudhā kulaputtalikādibhiḥ ।। bhedairgītā hi mukhyeyaṃ nādiphānteti mālinī । śabdarāśerbhairavasya yānucchūnatayāntarī ।। sā māteva bhaviṣyattvāttenāsau mātṛkoditā ।
mālinī mālitā rudrairdhārikā siddhimokṣayoḥ ।। phaleṣu puṣpitā pūjyā saṃhāradhvaniṣaṭpadī । saṃhāradānādānādiśaktiyuktā yato ralau ।। ekatvena smarantīti śaṃbhunātho nirūcivān ।
śabdarāśirmālinī ca śivaśaktyātmakaṃ tvidam ।। ekaikatrāpi pūrṇatvācchivaśaktisvabhāvatā । tena bhraṣṭe vidhau vīrye svarūpe vānayā param ।। mantrā nyastāḥ punarnyāsātpūryante tatphalapradāḥ ।
uktaṃ śrīpūrvatantre ca viśeṣavidhihīnite ।। nyasyecchāktaśarīrārthaṃ bhinnayoni tu mālinīm । viśeṣaṇamidaṃ hetau hetvarthaśca nirūpitaḥ ।। yatheṣṭaphalasiddhyai cetyatraivedamabhāṣata ।
sāñjanā api ye mantrā gāruḍādyā na te param ।। mālinyā pūritāḥ sidhdyai balādeva tu muktaye । tasmātphalepsurapyanya mantraṃ nyasyātra mālinīm ।। nyasyejjaptvāpica japedayatnādapavṛktaye ।
ityevaṃ mātṛkāṃ nyasyenmālinīṃ vā kramāddvayam ।। siddhimuktyanusārādvā varṇānvā yugapaddvayoḥ । akṣahrīṃ naphahrīmetau piṇḍau saṃghāvihānayoḥ ।। vācakau nyāsa etābhyāṃ kṛte nyāse athavaikakaḥ ।
eṣa cāṅgatanubrahmayukto vā tadviparyayaḥ ।। sāmudāyikavinyāse pṛthak piṇḍāvimau kramāt । akramādathavā nyasyedekamevātha yojayet ।। kriyayā siddhikāmo yaḥ sa kriyāṃ bhūyasīṃ caret ।
anīpsurapi yastasmai bhūyase svaphalāya sā ।। yastu dhyānajapābhyāsaiḥ siddhīpsuḥ sa kriyāṃ param । saṃskṛtyai svecchayā kuryāt prāṅnayenātha bhūyasīm ।। mumukṣuratha tasmai vā yathābhīṣṭaṃ samācaret ।
śivatāpattirevārtho hyeṣāṃ nyāsādikarmaṇām ।। evaṃ nyāsaṃ vidhāyārghapātre vidhimupācaret । uktanītyaiva tatpaścāt pūjayennyastavācakaiḥ ।। yataḥ samastabhāvānāṃ śivātsiddhimayādatho ।
pūrṇādavyatirekitvaṃ kārakāṇāmihārcayā ।। samastaṃ kārakavrātaṃ śivābhinnaṃ pradarśitam । pūjodāharaṇe sarvaṃ vyaśnute gamanādyapi ।। yathāhi vāhakaṭakabhramasvātantryamāgataḥ ।
aśvaḥ saṃgrāmarūḍho api tāṃ śikṣāṃ nātivartate ।। tathārcanakriyābhyāsaśivībhāvitakārakaḥ । gacchaṃstiṣṭhannapi dvaitaṃ kārakāṇāṃ vyapojjhati ।। tathaikyābhyāsaniṣṭhasyākramādviśvamidaṃ haṭhāt ।
saṃpūrṇaśivatākṣobhanarīnartadiva sphuret ।। uvāca pūjanastotre hyasmākaṃ paramo guruḥ । aho svādurasaḥ ko api śivapūjāmayotsavaḥ ।। ṣaṭtriṃśato api tattvānāṃ kṣobho yatrollasatyalam ।
tadetādṛkpūrṇaśivaviśvāveśāya ye arcanam ।। kurvanti te śivā eva tānpūrṇānprati kiṃ phalam । vināpi jñānayogābhyāṃ kriyā nyāsārcanādikā ।। itthamaikyasamāpattidānātparaphalapradā ।
sādhakasyāpi tatsadvipradamantraikatāṃ gatam ।। viśvaṃ vrajadavighnatvaṃ svāṃ siddhiṃ śīghramāvahet । uktaṃ ca parameśena na vidhirnārcanakramaḥ ।। kevalaṃ smaraṇātsiddhirvāñchiteti matādiṣu ।
tadevaṃ tanmayībhāvadāyinyarcākriyā yataḥ ।। samastakārakaikātmyaṃ tenāsyāḥ paramaṃ vapuḥ । yaṣṭrādhārasya tādātmyaṃ sthānaśuddhividhikramāt ।। yaṣṭṛyājyatadādhārakaraṇādānasaṃpradāḥ ।
nyāsakrameṇa śivatātādātmyamadhiśerate ।। arghapātramapādānaṃ tasmādādīyate yataḥ । yacca tatsthaṃ jalādyetatkaraṇaṃ śodhane arcane ।। arghapātrāmbuvipruḍbhiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ hi śudhyati ।
śivārkakarasaṃsparśātkānyā śuddhirbhaviṣyati ।। ūce śrīpūrvaśāstre tadarghapātravidhau vibhuḥ । na cāsaṃśodhitaṃ vastu kiṃcidapyupakalpayet ।। tena śuddhaṃ tu sarvaṃ yadaśuddhamapi tacchuci ।
aśuddhatā ca vijñeyā paśutacchāsanāśayāt ।। svatādavasthyātpūrvasmādathavāpyupakalpitāt । tena yadyadihāsannaṃ saṃvidaścidanugrahāt ।। kiyato api tadatyantaṃ yogyaṃ yāge atra jīvavat ।
anena nayayogena yadāsattividūrate ।। saṃvideti tadā tatra yogyāyogyatvamādiśet । vīrāṇāmata eveha mithaḥ svapratimāmṛtam ।। tattadyāgavidhāviṣṭaṃ gurubhirbhāvitātmabhiḥ ।
unmajjayati nirmagnāṃ saṃvidaṃ yattu suṣṭhu tat ।। arcāyai yogyamānando yasmādunmagnatā citaḥ । tenācidrūpadehādiprādhānyavinimajjakam ।। ānandajananaṃ pūjāyogyaṃ hṛdayahāri yat ।
ataḥ kulakramottīrṇatrikasāramatādiṣu ।। madyakādambarīśīdhudravyādermahimā param । lokasthitiṃ racayituṃ madyādeḥ paśuśāsane ।। proktā hyaśuddhistatraiva tasya kvāpi viśuddhatā ।
pañcagavye pavitratvaṃ somacarṇanapātrayoḥ ।। vidhiścāvabhṛthasnānaṃ haste kṛṣṇaviṣāṇitā । na patnyā ca vinā yāgaḥ sarvadaivatatulyatā ।। surāhutirbrahmasatre vapāntrahṛdayāhutiḥ ।
pāśaveṣvapi śāstreṣu tadadarśi maheśinā ।। ghorāndhyahaimananiśāmadhyagāciradīptivat । bhakṣyo haṃso na bhakṣyo asāviti ripratipattiṣu ।। smārtīṣu vijayatyeko yaḥ śivābhedaśuddhikaḥ ।
ajñatvavedādarśitvarāgadveṣādayo hyamī ।। munīnāṃ vacasi svasminprāmāṇyonmūlanakṣamāḥ । vede api yadabhakṣyaṃ tadbhakṣyamityupadiśyate ।। na vidhipratiṣedhākhyadharmayorekamāspadam ।
atha tatra na tadbhakṣyaṃ tadā tena tathā tataḥ ।। evaṃ viṣayabhedānno śivokterbādhikā śrutiḥ । kvacidviṣayatulyatvādbādhyabādhakatā yadi ।। tadbādhyā śrutireveti prāgevaitannirūpitam ।
prakṛtaṃ brūmahe kṛtvā nyāsaṃ dehārghapātrayoḥ ।। sāmānyamarghapātrāmbhovipruḍbhiḥ prokṣya cākhilam । yāgopakaraṇaṃ paścādbāhyayāgaṃ samācaret ।। prabhāmaṇḍalake khe vā suliptāyāṃ ca vā bhuvi ।
triśūlārkavṛṣāndikasthā mātaraḥ kṣetrapaṃ yajet ।। yoginīśca pṛthaṅmantrairoṃnamonāmayojitaiḥ । ekoccāreṇa vā bāhyaparivāretiśabditāḥ ।। tāro nāma caturthyantaṃ namaścetyarcane manuḥ ।
evaṃ bahiḥ pūjayitvā dvāraṃ prokṣya prapūjayet ।। triśiraḥśāsanādau ca sa dṛṣṭo vidhirucyate । gaṇeśalakṣmyau dvārordhve dakṣe vāme tayoḥ punaḥ ।। madhye vāgīśvarīṃ diṇḍimahodarayugaṃ tathā ।
kramātsvadakṣavāmasthaṃ tathaitena krameṇa ca ।। ekaikaṃ pūjayetsamyaṅ nandikālau trimārgagām । kālindīṃ chāgameṣāsyau svadakṣāddvāḥsthaśākhayoḥ ।। adhodehalyananteśādhāraśaktīśca pūjayet ।
dvāramadhye sarasvatyā mahāstraṃ pūjayedamī ।। padmādhāragatāḥ sarve apyuditā vighnanāśakāḥ । pūjane pūrvavanmantro dīpakadvayakalpitaḥ ।। arghapuṣpasamālambhadhūpanaivedyavandanaiḥ ।
pūjāṃ kuryādihārghaścāpyuttamadravyayojitaḥ ।। ekoccāreṇa vā kuryāddvāḥsthadaivatapūjanam । rahasyapūjāṃ cetkuryāttadbāhyaparivārakam ।। dvāḥsthāṃśca pūjayedantardevāgre kalpanākramāt ।
kṣiptvāstrajaptaṃ kusumaṃ jvaladveśmani vghnanut ।। praviśya śivaraśmīddhadṛśā veśmāvalokayet । diśo astreṇa ca badhnīyācchādayedvarmaṇākhilāḥ ।। tatrottarāśābhimukho mumukṣustādṛśāya vā ।
viśettathā hyaghorāgniḥ pāśānpluṣyati bandhakān ।। yadyapyasti na diṅnāma kācitpūrvāparādikā । pratyayo hi na tasyāḥ syādekasyā anupāhiteḥ ।। upādhiḥ pūrvatādiṣṭa iti cettatkṛtaṃ diśā ।
upādhimātraṃ tu tathā vaicitryāya kathaṃ bhavet ।। tasmātsaṃvitprakāśo ayaṃ mūrtyābhāsanabhāgataḥ । pūrvādidigvibhāgākhyavaicitryollekhadurmadaḥ ।। tatra yadyatprakāśena sadā svīkaraṇe kṣamam ।
tadevordhvaṃ prakāśātma sparśāyogyamadhaḥ punaḥ ।। kiṃcitprakāśatā madhyaṃ tato vai diksamudbhavaḥ । kiṃcitprakāśayogyasya saṃmukhaṃ prasaratpuraḥ ।। parāṅmukhaṃ tu tatpaścāditi digdvayamāgatam ।
prakāśaḥ saṃmukhaṃ vastu gṛhītvodriktaraśmikaḥ ।। yatra tiṣṭhoddakṣiṇaṃ tatprakāśasyānukūlyataḥ । dakṣiṇasya puraḥsaṃsthaṃ vāmamityupadiśyate ।। tatprakāśitameyendusparśasaumyaṃ tadeva hi ।
evamāśācatuṣke asminmadhyaviśrāntiyogataḥ ।। catuṣkamanyattenāṣṭau diśastattadadhiṣṭhitāḥ । evaṃ prakāśamātre asminvarade parame śive ।। digvibhāgaḥ sthito loke śāstre apica tathocyate ।
kramātsadāśivādhīśaḥ pañcamantratanuryataḥ ।। īśanraghoravāmākhyasadyo adhobhedato diśaḥ । īśa ūrdhvaṃ prakāśatvātpūrvaṃ vaktraṃ prasāri yat ।। puruṣo dakṣiṇācaṇḍo vāmā vāmastu saumyakaḥ ।
parāṅmukhatayā sadyaḥ paścimā paribhāṣyate ।। pātālavaktramadharamaprakāśatayā sthiteḥ । khamarudvahnijalabhūkhāni vaktrāṇyamuṣya hi ।। mukhyatvena khamevordhvaṃ prakāśamayamucyate ।
tadeva mukhyato adhastādaprakāśaṃ yataḥ sphuṭam ।। madhye tu yatprakāśaṃ tanna prakāśyaṃ na cetarat । prakāśatvāddiśyamānamato asmindikcatuṣṭayam ।। pañcamantratanurnātha itthaṃ viśvadigīśvaraḥ ।
tato apīśastathā rudro viṣṇurbrahmā tathā sthitaḥ ।। ūrdhvābhivyaktyayogyatvādviṣṇordhātuśca pañcamam । na vaktraṃ tau bhedamayau sṛṣṭisthitiprabhū yataḥ ।। digvibhāgastu tajjo asti vadanānāṃ catuṣṭayāt ।
pañcamasya yujitve tau parityaktanijātmakau ।। tato brahmāṇḍamadhye api jñānaśaktirvibho raviḥ । diśāṃ vibhāgaṃ kurute prakāśaghanavṛttimān ।। tathāhi viṣuvadyoge yataḥ pūrvaṃ pradṛśyate ।
tatpūrva yatra tacchāyā tatpaścimamudāhṛtam ।। tasmiñjigamiṣorasya yatsavyaṃ tattu dakṣiṇam । tatraiṣa caṇḍatejobhirbhāti jājvalyamānavat ।। tatpurovarti vāmaṃ tu tadbhāsā khacitaṃ manāk ।
tata eva hi somyaṃ tannacāpi hyaprakāśakam ।। yatrāsāvastamabhyeti tatpaścimamiti sthitiḥ । tatraiva paścime yeṣāṃ prākprakāśāvalokanam ।। tadeva pūrvameteṣāṃ yathādhvani nirūpitam ।
sā sā dikca tathā tasya phaladāpi viparyaye ।। vicitre phalasaṃpattiḥ prakāśādhīnikā yataḥ । itthaṃ sūryāśrayā diksyātsā vicitrāpi tādṛśī ।। adhiṣṭhitā maheśena citratadrūpadhāriṇā ।
kiṃ vātibahunā yo asau yaṣṭā tatsaṃmukhāditaḥ ।। diśo api pravibhajyante prāksavyottarapaścimāḥ । svānusārakṛtaṃ taṃ ca digvibhāgaṃ sadā śivaḥ ।। adhitiṣṭhatyarkamiva sa vicitravapuryataḥ ।
svotthā api diśaḥ sveśāḥ śakrādyā hyadhiśerate ।। te hi prakāśaśaktyaṃśāḥ prakāśānuvidhāyinaḥ । prakāśasya yadaiśvaryaṃ sa indro yattu tanmahaḥ ।। so agniryantṛtvabhīmatve yamo rakṣastadūnimā ।
prakāśyaṃ varuṇastacca cāñcalyādvāyurucyate ।। bhāvasañcayayogena vitteśastatkṣaye vibhuḥ । adṛṣṭavigraho ananto brahmordhve vṛṃhako vibhuḥ ।। prakāśasyaiva śaktyaṃśā lokapāstena kīrtitāḥ ।
itthaṃ svādhīnarūpāpi diksaurī tūpadiśyate ।। tatra sarvo hi niṣkampaṃ prakāśatvaṃ prapadyate । sarvago apyanilo yadvadvyajanenopavījitaḥ ।। prabuddhaḥ svāṃ kriyāṃ kuryāddharmanirṇodanādikām ।
tadvatsarvagatāḥ sarvā aindyādyāḥ śaktayaḥ sphuṭam ।। sādhakāśvāsasaṃbuddhāstattatsveṣṭaphalapradāḥ । evaṃ saurī digīśānabrahmaviṣṇvīśasauśivaiḥ ।। adhiṣṭhitā samāśvāsadārḍhyāttattatphalapradā ।
sādhako yacca vā kṣetraṃ maṇḍalaṃ veśma vā bhajet ।। sthitastadanusāreṇa madhyībhavati śaṃkaraḥ । sa hi sarvamadhiṣṭhātā mādhyasthyeneti tasya yaḥ ।। sauraḥ prakāśastatpūrvamitthaṃ syāddigvyavasthitiḥ ।
tanmadhyasthitanāthasya grahītuṃ dakṣiṇaṃ mahaḥ ।। udaṅmukhaḥ syāt pāścātyaṃ grahītuṃ pūrvatomukhaḥ । upaviśya nijasthāne dehaśuddhiṃ samācaret ।। aṅguṣṭhāgrātkālavahnijvālābhāsvaramutthitam ।
astraṃ dhyātvā tacchikhābhirbahirantardahettanum ।। dāhaśca dhvaṃsa evokto dhvaṃsakaṃ mantrasaṃjñitam । tejastathābhilāpākhyasvavikalparasombhitam ।। tena mantrāgninā dāho dehe puryaṣṭake tathā ।
dehapuryaṣṭakāhantāvidhvaṃsādeva jāyate ।। nahi sadbhāvamātreṇa deho asāvanyadehavat । ahantāyāṃ hi dehatvaṃ sā dhvastā taddaheddhruvam ।। taddehasaṃskārabharo bhasmatvenātha yaḥ sthitaḥ ।
taṃ varmavāyunādhūya tiṣṭhecchuddhacidātmani ।। tasmindhruve nistaraṅge samāpattimupāgataḥ । saṃvidaḥ sṛṣṭidharmitvādādyāmeti taraṅgitām ।। saiva mūrtiriti khyātā tārasadbinduhātmikā ।
tato navātmadevena nyāsastattvodayātmakaḥ ।। aṅgavaktrāṇi tasyaiva svasthāneṣu niyojayet । atha mātṛkayā prāgvattattattvasphuṭatātmakaḥ ।। tritattvanyāsatā cāsya pṛṣṭhe kakṣyātrayāgate ।
tato aghorāṣṭakanyāsaḥ śirastaccaraṇātmakam ।। tato api śivasadbhāvanyāsaḥ svāṃgasya saṃyutaḥ । ittha kṛte pañcake asminyattanmukhyatayā bhavet ।। upāsyamarcyaṃ tatsāṅgaṃ ṣaṣṭhe nyāse niyojayet ।
tenātra nyāsayogyo asau bhagavānratiśekharaḥ ।। ūrdhve nyāsyo navākhyasya mukhyatve anyonyadhāmatā । evaṃ bhairavasadbhāvanāthe mukhyatayā yadi ।। upāsyatā tattatsthāna prāṅnyāsyo ratiśekharaḥ ।
itthaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre me saṃpradāyaṃ nyarūpayat ।। śaṃbhunātho nyāsavidhau devo hi kathamanyathā । nyāsa vivarjyate amuṣminnaṅgānyapyasya santi hi ।। mūrtiḥ sṛṣṭistritattvaṃ cetyaṣṭau mūrtyaṅgasaṃyutāḥ ।
śivaḥ sāṅgaśca vijñeyo nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhā prakīrtitaḥ ।। asyopari tataḥ śāktaṃ nyāsaṃ kuryācca ṣaḍvidham । parāparāṃ savaktrāṃ prāktataḥ prāgiti mālinīm ।। paścātparāditritayaṃ śikhāhṛtpādagaṃ kramāt ।
tataḥ kavaktrakaṇṭheṣu hṛnnābhīguhya ūrutaḥ ।। jānupāde apyaghoryādyaṃ tato vidyāṅgapañcakam । tatastvāvāhayecchaktiṃ mātṛsadbhāvarūpiṇīm ।। yogeśvarīṃ parāṃ pūrṇāṃ kālasaṃkarṣiṇīṃ dhruvām ।
aṅgavaktraparīvāraśaktidvādaśakādhikām ।। sādhyānuṣṭhānabhedena nyāsakāle smaredguruḥ । paraiva devītritayamadhye yābhedinī sthitā ।। sānavacchedacinmātrasadbhāveyaṃ prakīrtitā ।
sāraśāstre yāmale ca devyāstena prakīrtitaḥ ।। mūrtiḥ savaktrā śaktiśca śaktitrayamathāṣṭakam । pañcāṅgāni parā śaktirnyāsaḥ śākto api ṣaḍvidhaḥ ।। yāmalo ayaṃ mahānyāsaḥ siddhimuktiphalapradaḥ ।
muktyekārthī punaḥ pūrvaṃ śāktaṃ nyāsaṃ samācaret ।। guravastvāhuritthaṃ yannyāsadvayamudāhṛtam । mumukṣuṇā tu pādādi tatkāryaṃ saṃhṛtikramāt ।। yāvantaḥ kīrtitā bhedāḥ śaṃbhuśaktyaṇuvācakāḥ ।
tāvatsvapyeṣu mantreṣu nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhaiva kīrtitaḥ ।। kiṃtvāvāhyastu yo mantraḥ sa tatrāṅgasamanvitaḥ । ṣaṣṭhaḥ syāditi sarvatra ṣoḍhaivāyamudāhṛtaḥ ।। mudrāpradarśanaṃ paścātkāyena manasā girā ।
pañcāvasthā jāgradādyāḥ ṣaṣṭhyanuttaranāmikā ।। ṣaṭkāraṇaṣaḍātmatvātṣaṭtriṃśattattvayojanam । evaṃ ṣoḍhāmahānyāse kṛte viśvamidaṃ haṭhāt ।। dehe tādātmyamāpannaṃ śuddhāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ prakāśayet ।
mūrtinyāsātsamārabhya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prasṛtātra sā ।। abhedamānīya kṛtā śuddhā nyāsabalakramāt । tena ye acodayanmūḍhāḥ pāśadāhavidhūnane ।। kṛte śānte śive rūḍhaḥ punaḥ kimavarohati ।
iti te dūrato dhvastāḥ paramārthaṃ hi śāṃbhavam ।। na vidusta svasaṃvittisphurattāsāravarjitāḥ । na khalveṣa śivaḥ śānto nāma kaścidvibhedavān ।। sarvetarādhvavyāvṛtto ghaṭatulyo asti kutracit ।
mahāprakāśarūpā hi yeyaṃ saṃvidvijṛmbhate ।। sa śivaḥ śivataivāsya vaiśvarūpyāvabhāsitā । tathābhāsanayogo ataḥ svarasenāsya jṛmbhate ।। bhāsyamāno atra cābhedaḥ svātmano bheda eva ca ।
bhede vijṛmbhite māyā māyāmāturvijṛmbhate ।। abhede jṛmbhate asyaiva māyāmātuḥ śivātmatā । māyāpramātā tadrūpavikalpābhyāsapāṭavāt ।। śiva eva tadabhyāsaphalaṃ nyāsādi kīrtitam ।
yathāhi duṣṭakarmāsmītyevaṃ bhāvayatastathā ।। tathā śivo ahaṃ nānyo asmītyevaṃ bhāvayatastathā । etadevocyate dārḍhyaṃ vimarśahṛdayaṅgamam ।। śivaikātmyavikalpaughadvārikā nirvikalpatā ।
anyathā tasya śuddhasya vimarśaprāṇavartinaḥ ।। kathaṃ nāmāvimṛṣṭaṃ syādrūpaṃ bhāsanadharmaṇaḥ । tenātidurghaṭaghaṭāsvatantrecchāvaśādayam ।। bhānapi prāṇabuddhyādiḥ svaṃ tathā na vikalpayet ।
pratyutātisvatantrātmaviparītasvadharmatām ।। vināśyanīśāyattatvarūpāṃ niścitya majjati । tataḥ saṃsārabhāgīyatathāniścayaśātinīm ।। nityādiniścayadvārāmavikalpāṃ sthitiṃ śrayet ।
ye tu tīvratamodriktaśaktinirmalatājuṣaḥ ।। na te dīkṣāmanunyāsakāriṇaśceti varṇitam । evaṃ viśvaśarīraḥ sanviśvātmatvaṃ gataḥ sphuṭam ।। nyāsamātrāt tathābhūtaṃ dehaṃ puṣpādinārcayet ।
pṛthaṅmantrairvistareṇa saṃkṣepānmūlamantrataḥ ।। dhūpanaivedyatṛptyādyaistathā vyāsasamāsataḥ । saṃsāravāmācāratvātsarvaṃ vāmakareṇa tu ।। kuryāttarpaṇayogaṃ ca daiśikastadanāmayā ।
vāmaśabdena guhyaṃ śrīmataṅgādāvapīritam ।। vāmācāraparo mantrī yāgaṃ kuryāditi sphuṭam । śrīmadbhargaśikhāśāstre tathā śrīgamaśāsane ।। sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam ।
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitamanāmātarpaṇātpriye ।। śrīmannandiśikhāyāṃ ca śrīmadānandaśāsane । taduktaṃ srukca pūrṇāyāṃ sruvaśvājyāhutau bhavet ।। śeṣaṃ vāmakareṇaiva pūjāhomajapādikam ।
evamānandasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvaunmukhyavivarjitam ।। yāgena dehaṃ miṣpādya bhāvayeta śivātmakam । galite viṣayaunmukhye pārimitye vilāpite ।। dehe kimavaśiṣyeta śivānandarasādṛte ।
śivānandarasāpūrṇaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśattattvanirbharam ।। dehaṃ divāniśaṃ paśyannarcayansyācchivātmakaḥ । viśvātmadehaviśrāntitṛptastalliṅganiṣṭhitaḥ ।। bāhyaṃ liṅgavratakṣetracaryādi nahi vāñchati ।
tāvanmātrāttvaviśrānteḥ saṃvidaḥ kathitāḥ kriyāḥ ।। uttarā bāhyayāgāntāḥ sādhyā tvatra śivātmatā । tato arghapātraṃ kartavyaṃ śivābhedamayaṃ param ।। ānandarasasaṃpūrṇaṃ viśvadaivatatarpaṇam ।
yathaiva dehe dāhādipūjāntaṃ tadvadeva hi ।। arghapātre api kartavyaṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ । kāni dravyāṇi yāgāya ko nvargha iti noditam ।। siddhikāmasya tatsiddhau sādhanaiva hi kāraṇam ।
