muktikāmasya no kiṃcinniṣiddhaṃ vihitaṃ ca no ।। yadeva hṛdyaṃ tadyogyaṃ śivasaṃvidabhedane । kṛtvārghapātraṃ tadvipruṭprokṣitaṃ kusumādikam ।। kṛtvā ca tena svātmānaṃ pūjayetparamaṃ śivam ।
arghapātrārcanādattapuṣpasaṃkīrṇatābhayāt ।। nārghapātre atra kusumaṃ kuryāddevārcanākṛte । arghapātre tadamṛtībhūtamambveva pūjitam ।। mantrāṇāṃ tṛptaye yāgadravyaśuddhyai ca kevalam ।
evaṃ dehaṃ pūjayitvā prāṇadhīśūnyavigrahān ।। anyonyatanmayībhūtān pūjayecchivatādṛśe । tatra prāṇāśraye nayāse buddhyā viracite sati ।। śūnyādhiṣṭhānataḥ sarvamekayatnena pūjyate ।
nyasyedādhāraśaktiṃ tu nābhyadhaścaturaṅgulām ।। dharāṃ surodaṃ tejaśca meyapārapratiṣṭhiteḥ । potarūpaṃ marutkandasvabhāvaṃ viśvasūtraṇāt ।। pratyekamaṅgulaṃ nyasyeccatuṣkaṃ vyomagarbhakam ।
īṣatsamantādamalamidamāmalasārakam ।। tato daṇḍamanantākhyaṃ kalpayellambikāvadhi । tanmātrādikalāntaṃ tadūrdhve granthirniśātmakaḥ ।। tatra māyāmaye granthau dharmādharmādyamaṣṭakam ।
vahniprāgādi māyā hi tatsūtirvibhavastu dhīḥ ।। māyāgrantherūrdhvabhūmau triśūlādhaścatuṣkikām । śuddhavidyātmikāṃ dhyāyecchadanadvayasaṃyutām ।। tacca tattvaṃ sthitaṃ bhāvyaṃ lambikābrahmarandhrayoḥ ।
prakāśayogo hyatraivaṃ dṛkśrotrarasanādikaḥ ।। dakṣānyāvartato nyasyecchaktīnāṃ navakadvayam । vidyāpadme atra taccoktamapi prāgdarśyate punaḥ ।। vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kalabalavikarike balamathanī ।
bhūtadamanī ca manonmanikā śāntā śakracāparuciratra syāt ।। vibhvī jñaptikṛtīcchā vāgīśī jvālinī tathā vāmā । jyeṣṭhā raudrītyetāḥ prāgdalataḥ kāladahanavatsarvāḥ ।। dalakesaramadhyeṣu sūryendudahanatrayam ।
nijādhipairbrahmaviṣṇuharaiścādhiṣṭhitaṃ smaret ।। māyottīrṇaṃ hi yadrūpaṃ brahmādīnāṃ puroditam । āsanaṃ tvetadeva syānnatu māyāñjanāñjitam ।। rudrordhve ceśvaraṃ devaṃ tadūrdhve ca sadāśivam ।
nyasyetsa ca mahāpreta iti śāstreṣu bhaṇyate ।। samastatattvavyāptṛtvānmahāpretaḥ prabodhataḥ । prakarṣagamanāccaiṣa līno yannādharaṃ vrajet ।। vidyāvidyeśinaḥ sarve hyuttarottaratāṃ gatāḥ ।
sadāśivībhūya tataḥ paraṃ śivamupāśritāḥ ।। ataḥ sadāśivo nityamūrdhvadṛgbhāsvarātmakaḥ । kṛśo meyatvadaurbalyātpreto aṭṭahasanāditaḥ ।। tasya nābhyutthitaṃ mūrdharandhratrayavinirgatam ।
nādāntātma smarecchaktivyāpinīsamanojjvalam ।। arātrayaṃ dviṣaṭkāntaṃ tatrāpyaunmanasaṃ trayam । paṅkajānāṃ sitaṃ saptatriṃśadātmedamāsanam ।। atra sarvāṇi tattvāni bhedaprāṇāni yattataḥ ।
āsanatvena bhinnaṃ hi saṃvido viṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। etānyeva tu tattvāni līnāni parabhairave । tādātmyenātha sṛṣṭāni bhidevārcyatvayojane ।। śrīmadbhairavabodhaikyalābhasvātantryavanti tu ।
etānyeva tu tattvāni pūjakatvaṃ prayāntyalam ।। pūjakaḥ paratattvātmā pūjyaṃ tattvaṃ parāparam । sṛṣṭatvādaparaṃ tattvajālamāsanatāspadam ।। vidyākalāntaṃ siddhānte vāmadakṣiṇaśāstrayoḥ ।
sadāśivāntaṃ samanāparyantaṃ matayāmale ।। unmanāntamihākhyātamityetatparamāsanam । arcayitvāsanaṃ pūjyā gurupaṅktistu bhāvivat ।। tatrāsane purā mūrtibhūtāṃ sārdhākṣarāṃ dvayīm ।
nyasyedvyāptṛtayetyuktaṃ siddhayogīśvarīmate ।। sadāśivaṃ mahāpretaṃ mūrtiṃ sārdhākṣarāṃ yajet । paratvena parāmūrdhve gandhapuṣpādibhistviti ।। vidyāmūrtimathātmākhyāṃ dvitīyāṃ parikalpayet ।
madhye bhairavasadbhāvaṃ dakṣiṇe ratiśekharam ।। navātmānaṃ vāmatastaddevīvadbhairavatrayam । madhye parāṃ pūrṇacandrapratimāṃ dakṣiṇe punaḥ ।। parāparāṃ raktavarṇāṃ kiṃcidagrāṃ na bhīṣaṇām ।
aparāṃ vāmaśṛṅge tu bhīṣaṇāṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalām ।। prāgvaddvidhātra ṣoḍhaiva nyāso dehe yathā kṛtaḥ । tataḥ sāṃkalpikaṃ yuktaṃ vapurāsāṃ vicintayet ।। kṛtyabhedānusāreṇa dvicatuḥṣaḍbhujādikam ।
kapālaśūlakhaṭvāṅgavarābhayaghaṭādikam ।। vāmadakṣiṇasaṃsthānacitratvātparikalpayet । vastuto viśvarūpāstā devyo bodhātmikā yataḥ ।। anavacchinnacinmātrasārāḥ syurapavṛktaye ।
sarvaṃ tato aṅgavaktrādi lokapālāstrapaścimam ।। madhye devyabhidhā pūjyā trayaṃ bhavati pūjitam । tato madhyagatāttasmādbodharāśeḥ sadaivatāt ।। aṅgādi niḥsṛtaṃ pūjyaṃ visphuliṅgātmakaṃ pṛthak ।
madhyagā kila yā devī saiva sadbhāvarūpiṇī ।। kālasaṃkarṣiṇī ghorā śāntā miśrā ca sarvataḥ । siddhātantre ca saikārṇā parā devīti kīrtitā ।। parā tu mātṛkā devī mālinī madhyagoditā ।
madhye nyasyetsūryaruciṃ sarvākṣaramayīṃ parām ।। tasyāḥ śikhāgre tvaikārṇāṃ tasyāścāṅgādikaṃ tviti । tato viśvaṃ viniṣkrāntaṃ pūjitaṃ dakṣiṇottare ।। syādeva pūjitaṃ tena sakṛnmadhye prapūjayet ।
śrīdevyāyāmale coktaṃ yāge ḍāmarasaṃjñite ।। nāsāgre trividhaṃ kālaṃ kālasaṃkarṣiṇī sadā । mukhasthā śvāsaniḥśvāsakalanī hṛdi karṣati ।। pūrakaiḥ kumbhakairdhatte grasate recakena tu ।
kālaṃ saṃgrasate sarvaṃ recakenotthitā kṣaṇāt ।। icchāśaktiḥ parā nāmnā śaktitritayabodhinī । yājyā karṣati yatsarvaṃ kālādhāraprabhañjanam ।। iha kila dṛkkarmecchāḥ śiva uktāstāstu vedyakhaṇḍanake ।
sthūle sūkṣme kramaśaḥ sakalapralayākalau bhavataḥ ।। śuddhā eva tu suptā jñānākalatāṃ gatāḥ prabuddhāstu । pravibhinnakatipayātmakavedyavido mantra ucyante ।। bhinne tvakhile vedye mantreśāstanmaheśāstu ।
bhinnābhinne tadiyān suśivānto adhvoditaḥ prete ।। tā eva galati bhedaprasare kramaśo vikāsamāyāntyaḥ । anyonyāsaṃkīrṇāstvarātrayaṃ galitabhedikāstu tataḥ ।। padmatrayyaunmanasī tadidaṃ syādāsanatvena ।
tā evānyonyātmakabhedāvacchedanājihāsutayā ।। kila śaktitadvadādiprabhidā pūjyatvamāyātāḥ । bhedagalanādyakoṭerārabhya yato nijaṃ nijaṃ rūpam ।। bibhrati tāstu tritvaṃ tāsāṃ sphuṭameva lakṣyeta ।
saṃbhāvyavedyakāluṣyayogato anyonyalabdhasaṃkarataḥ ।। prāk prasphuṭaṃ tribhāvaṃ nāgacchannatra tu tathā na । anyonyātmakabhedāvacchedanakalanasaṃgrasiṣṇutayā । svātantryamātrasārā saṃvitsā kālakarṣiṇī kathitā ।।
saiva ca bhūyaḥ svasmātsaṃkarṣati kālamiha bahiṣkurute । saṃkarṣiṇīti kathitā mātṛṣveteṣu sadbhāvaḥ ।। tattvaṃ sattā prāptirmātṛṣu meyo anayā saṃśca । viśvajananīṣu śaktiṣu paramārtho hi svatantratāmātram ।।
eṣaṇavidikriyātmakametatpūjyaṃ yato anavacchinnam । yasminsarvāvacchedadiśo api syuḥ samākṣiptāḥ ।। avikalpamiha na yāti hi pūjyatvaṃ naca vikalpa ekatra । bahavo dharmāstasmād yo dharmastāvato dharmān ।।
ākṣipati tatra rūḍhaḥ sarvotkṛṣṭo adharasthitāstvanye । iti bhairavaparapūjātattvaṃ śrīḍāmare mahāyāge ।। svayameva suprasannaḥ śrīmān śaṃbhurmamādikṣat । bāhyayāge tu padmānāṃ tritaye api prapūjayet ।।
astrāntaṃ parivāraughamiti no daiśikāgamaḥ । agnīśarakṣovāyvantadikṣu vidyāṅgapañcakam ।। śaktyaṅgāni śivāṅgāni tathaivātra punardvaye । astraṃ nyasyeccaturdikkaṃ madhye locanasaṃjñakam ।।
patrāṣṭake aṣṭakayugamaghorādeḥ svayāmalam । tathā dvādaśakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ catuṣkaṃ miśritaṃ dviśaḥ ।। sarvaśo dviguṇādītthamāvṛtitvena pūjayet । lokapālāṃstataḥ sāstrānsvadikṣu daśasu kramāt ।।
itthaṃ triśūlaparyantadevītādātmyavṛttitaḥ । tiṣṭhannatrārpayanviśvaṃ tarpayeddevatāgaṇam ।। tato japaṃ prakurvīta pratimantraṃ dvipañcadhā । ekaikasya tryātmakatvādabhedāccāpi sarvaśaḥ ।।
nābhihṛtkaṇṭhatālūrdhvakuṇḍe jvalanavatsmaran । mantracakraṃ tatra viśvaṃ jvahvansaṃpādayeddhutim ।। dīkṣākarmaṇi kartavye dīkṣāṃ yenādhvanā guruḥ । cikīrṣurdeha evādau bhūyastaṃ mukhyato arpayet ।।
dvādaśāntamidaṃ prāgraṃ triśūlaṃ mūlataḥ smaran । devīcakrāgragaṃ tyaktakramaḥ khecaratāṃ vrajet ।। mūlādhārāddviṣaṭkāntavyomāgrāpūraṇātmikā । khecarīyaṃ khasaṃcārasthitibhyāṃ khāmṛtāśanāt ।।
amuṣmācchāmbhavācchūlāddhrāsayeccaturaṅgulam । śākte tato apyāṇave tattriśūlatritayaṃ sthitam ।। tattriśūlatrayordhvordhvadevīcakrārpitātmakaḥ । kiṃ kiṃ na jāyate kiṃ vā na vetti na karoti vā ।।
ekaikāmathavā devīṃ mantraṃ vā padmagaṃ yajet । yāmalaikyāṅgavaktrādisadasattāvikalpataḥ ।। itthaṃ prāṇādvyomapadaparyantaṃ cetanaṃ nijam । śivībhāvyārcanāyogāttato bāhyaṃ vidhiṃ caret ।।
bahiryāgasya mukhyatve siddhyādiparikalpite । antaryāgaḥ saṃskriyāyai hyanyathārcayitā paśuḥ ।। yastu siddhyādivimukhaḥ sa bahiryajati prabhum । antarmahāyāgarūḍhyai tayaivāsau kṛtārthakaḥ ।।
kṛtvāntaryāgamādāya dhānyādyastreṇa mantritam । dikṣu kṣipedvighnanude saṃhṛtyaiśīṃ diśaṃ nayet ।। nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ ca tāḍanāpyāyane tathā । viguṇṭhanaṃ ca saṃskārāḥ sādhārāstriśiromate ।।
gomūtragomayadadhikṣīrājyaṃ mantrayenmukhaiḥ । ūrdhvāntairaṅgaṣaṭkena kuśāmbvetena cokṣayet ।। bhūmiṃ śeṣaṃ ca śiṣyārthaṃ sthāpayetpañcagavyakam । pañca gavyāni yatrāsminkuśāmbuni taducyate ।।
pañcagavyaṃ jalaṃ śāstre bāhyāśuddhivimardakam । laukikyāmaviśuddhau hi mṛditāyāmathāntarīm ।। aśuddhiṃ dagdhumāstheyaṃ mantrādi yadalaukikam । phādināntāṃ smareddevīṃ pṛthivyādiśivāntagām ।।
puṣpāñjaliṃ kṣipenmadhye dhūpagandhāsavādi ca । tathaiva dadyādyāgaukomadhye tenāśu vigraham ।। samastaṃ devatācakramadhiṣṭhātṛ prakalpyate । anantanāle dharmādipatre sadvaidyakarṇike ।।
ṣaḍutthe gandhapuṣpādyairgaṇeśaṃ hyaiśagaṃ yajet । atthitaṃ vighnasaṃśāntyai pūjayitvā visarjayet ।। । ।
। tataḥ kumbhaṃ parāmodidravadravyaprapūritam ।। pūjitaṃ carcitaṃ mūlamanunā mantrayecchatam । asinā karkarīṃ pūrvamastrayāgo na cetkṛtaḥ ।।
tamaiśānyāṃ yajetkumbhaṃ vāmasthakalaśānvitam । tataḥ sauradigāśrityā sāstrāṃllokeśvarānyajet ।। gandhapuṣpopahārādyairvidhinā mantrapūrvakam । tataḥ śiṣyo asikalaśīhasto dhārāṃ prapātayan ।।
guruṇā kumbhahastenānuvrajyo vadatā tvidam । bho bhoḥ śakra tvayā svasyāṃ diśi vighnapraśāntaye ।। sāvadhānena karmāntaṃ bhavitavyaṃ śivājñayā । tryakṣare nirṛtiprāye nāmni bhoḥśabdamekakam ।।
apāsayedyato mantraśchandobaddho ayamīritaḥ । tata aiśyāṃ diśi sthāpyaḥ sa kumbho vikiropari ।। dakṣiṇe cāstravārdhānī sthāpyā kumbhasya sāṃpratam । kumbhasthāmbusamāpattivṛṃhitaṃ mantravṛndakam ।।
tejomātrātmanā dhyātaṃ sarvamāpyāyayedvidhim । ataḥ kumbhe mantragaṇaṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūjayedguruḥ ।। pūrveṇa vidhināstraṃ ca karkaryāṃ vighnanudyajet । madhyegṛhaṃ tato gandhamaṇḍale pūjayedguruḥ ।।
trikaṃ yāmalataikyābhyāmekaṃ vā mantradaivatam । agnikāryavidhānāya tataḥ kuṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ।। śuddhamantrādisaṃjalpasaṃkalpotthamapūrvakam । śivasya yā kriyāśaktistatkuṇḍamiti bhāvanāt ।।
paramaḥ khalu saṃskāro vināpyanyaiḥ kriyākramaiḥ । evaṃ dehe sthaṇḍile vā liṅge pātre jale anale ।। puṣpādiṣu śiśau mukhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ śivatādṛśe । uktaṃ śrīyogasaṃcāre tathāhi parameśinā ।।
caturdaśavidhe bhūte puṣpe dhūpe nivedane । dīpe jape tathā home sarvatraivātra caṇḍikā ।। juhoti japati preddhe pūjayedvihasedvrajet । āhāre maithune saiva dehasthā karmakāriṇī ।।
tādṛśīṃ ye tu no rūḍhāṃ saṃvittimadhiśerate । akramāttatprasiddhyarthaṃ kramiko vidhirucyate ।। ahaṃ śivo mantramayaḥ saṃkalpā me tadātmakāḥ । tajjaṃ ca kuṇḍavahnyādi śivātmeti sphuṭaṃ smaret ।।
ata eva hi tatrāpi dārḍhyādārḍhyāvalokanāt । kriyamāṇe kṛte vāpi saṃskriyālpetarāpivā ।। yathāhi kaścitpratibhādaridro abhyāsapāṭavāt । vākyaṃ gṛhṇāti ko apyādau tathātrāpyavabudhyatām ।।
ullekhasekakuṭṭanalepacaturmārgamakṣavṛtiparikalanam । staraparidhiviṣṭarasthitisaṃskārā daśāstrataḥ kuṇḍagatāḥ ।। madhyagrahaṇaṃ darbhadvayena kuśasaṃvṛtiśca bhittīnām । prāṅmukharekhātritayordhvarekhikāḥ kuśasamāvṛtiśca bahiḥ ।।
śastalatāścaturaśraṃ daśalokeśārcanāsanavidhiśca । sadmāsādanamastrāgnitejasā rakṣaṇaṃ ca kuṇḍasya ।। bhūmeḥ śivāgnidhṛtyai śaktirvighnāpasāraṇaṃ cārthāḥ । tatastu pūjite kuṇḍe kriyāśaktitayā sphuṭam ।।
mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vāpi nyasyetsaṃkalparūpiṇīm । saṃkalpadevyā yatsṛṣṭidhāma tryaśraṃ kriyātmakam ।। jñānaśukrakaṇaṃ tatra triḥ prakṣobhya vinikṣipet । icchātaḥ kṣubhitaṃ jñānaṃ vimarśātmakriyāpade ।।
rūḍhaṃ jñatvādipañcāṅgavispaṣṭaṃ jājvalītyalam । tenāṅgapañcakaireva hutiṃ dadyātsakṛtsakṛt ।। janmādyakhilasaṃskāraśuddho agnistāvatā bhavet । pañcāṅgameva pṛthvyādirūpaṃ kaṭhinatādikāḥ ।।
śaktīrdadhadvahnigatāḥ kuryādgarbhādikāḥ kriyāḥ । tato akhilādhvasaddevīcakragarbhāṃ parāparām ।। smaranpūrṇāhutivaśātpūrayedagnisaṃskriyāḥ । tathā mantreśayuksatyasaṃkalpamahasā jvalan ।।
vahnistacchivasaṃkalpatādātmyācchivatātmakaḥ । ityetatsaṃskriyātattvaṃ śrīśaṃbhurme nyarūpayat ।। mayāpi darśitaṃ śuddhabuddhayaḥ praviviñcatām । tenātra ye codayanti yathā bālasya saṃskriyā ।।
bahnau vahnestathānyatretyanavasthaiva saṃskṛteḥ । te nirutthānavihatā naye asmingurudarśane ।। jāte agnau saṃskṛte śaive śabdarāśiṃ ca mālinīm । pitarau pūjayitvā svaṃ śuddhaṃ dhāma visarjayet ।।
śuddhāgnerbhāgamādāya carvarthaṃ sthāpayetpṛthak । athavāgneḥ śikhāṃ vāmaprāṇenādāya hṛjjuṣā ।। cidagninaikyamānīya kṣipeddakṣeṇa saṃskṛtām । śiva ityabhimānena dṛḍhena hi vilokanam ।।
sarvasya saṃskriyā tattvaṃ tattasmai yadyato amalam । navāhutīratho dadyānnavātmasahitena tu ।। śivāgnaye tārapūrvaṃ svāhāntaṃ saṃskriyā bhavet । śivacaitanyasāmānyavyoparūpe anale tataḥ ।।
prāgvadādhāramādheyaṃ devīcakraṃ ca yojayet । sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca saṃpaśyedadhovaktrau kramādguruḥ ।। śivaśaktitayābhyarcyau tathetthaṃ saṃskriyānayoḥ । tattvasaṃdarśanānnānyatsaṃskārasyāsti jīvitam ।।
iti vaktuṃ sruvādīśaḥ śrīpūrve na samaskarot । tatastilairmṛgīṃ madhyānāmāṅguṣṭhavaśādguruḥ ।। kṛtvā mūlaṃ tarpayet śatenājyasruvaistathā । aṅgavaktraṃ ṣaḍaṃśena śeṣāṃścāpi daśāṃśataḥ ।।
sahasrādikahomo api tṛptyai vittānusārataḥ । sati vitte api lobhādigrasto bāhyapradhānatām ।। prathayaṃścidguṇībhāvācchaktipātaṃ na vindati । uktaṃ svacchandatantre taddīkṣito api na mokṣabhāk ।।
nanu yattasya dīkṣāyāṃ kṛtaṃ karmāsya kiṃ phalam । tatrāhurgamaśāstrajñā vāmāśaktimayāstadā ।। mantrā badhnanti taṃ samyagbhavakārāmahāgṛhe । yā tvanugrāhikā śaktisteṣāṃ sā gurudīpitā ।।
śodhayeta svaśāstrasthaniṣkāmollaṅghanakriyām । tata ūrdhvādharanyāsādanyonyaunmukhyasundaram ।। sruksruvaṃ śivaśaktyātmādāyājyāmṛtapūritam । samacittaprāṇatanuraikātmyavidhiyogataḥ ।।
vāmaṃ srugdaṇḍagaṃ hastaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sopayāmakam । kaṇṭhādhogaṃ vinikṣipya dṛḍhamāpīḍya yatnavān ।। adhaḥ kuryātsrucaṃ prāṇamūrdhvordhvaṃ saṃniyojayan । yāvaddviṣaṭkaparyante bodhāgnau candracakrataḥ ।।
srugagrātparamaṃ hlādi patedamṛtamuttamam । tāvadvahnau mantramukhe vauṣaḍantāṃ hutiṃ kṣipet ।। ya ūrdhve kila saṃbodhaḥ kuṇḍe sa pratibimbitaḥ । vahniḥ prāṇaḥ sruksruvau ca snehaḥ saṃkalpacidrasaḥ ।।
itthaṃ jñātvāditaḥ kuṇḍasruksruvājyamanūnbhṛśam । dvādaśāntavibodhāgnau ruddhvā pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet ।। yathā yathā hi gaganamutpatetkalahaṃsakaḥ । jale binbaṃ bruḍatyasya tathetyatrāpyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।
svābhāvikaṃ sthiraṃ caiva dravaṃ dīptaṃ calaṃ nabhaḥ । māyā bindustathaivātmā nādaḥ śaktiḥ śivastathā ।। itthaṃ vyāpyavyāpakato vibhedyābhyantarāntam । tadadhaḥsthāni pṛthvyādimūlāntāni tathā pumān ।।
avidyārāganiyatikālamāyākalāstathā । aṇurvidyā tadīśeśau sādākhyaṃ śaktikuṇḍalī ।। vyāpinī samanaunmanyaṃ tato anāmani yojayet । recakastho madhyanāḍīsandhividgururityadaḥ ।।
proktaṃ traiśirase tantre parayojanavarṇane । tataḥ prāksthāpitānyastamantrasaṃskṛtavahninā ।। caruḥ sādhyo athavā śiṣyairhomena samakālakaḥ । carau ca vīradravyāṇi laukikānyathavecchayā ।।
carusiddhau samastāśca kriyā hṛnmantrayogataḥ । tataścaruṃ samādāya gururājyena pūritām ।। srucaṃ sruvaṃ vā kṛtvaiva bhuktimuktyanusārataḥ । devānāmatha śaktīnāṃ yantrāṇāṃ tu trayaṃ trayam ।।
saptamaṃ mātṛsadbhāvaṃ kramādekaikaśaḥ paṭhan । svā ityamṛtavarṇena vahnau hutvājyaśeṣakam ।। carau hetyagnirūpeṇa juhuyāttatpunaḥ punaḥ । bhojyabhojakacarvagnyoritthamekānusandhitaḥ ।।
svāhāpratyavamarśātsyātsamantrādadvayaṃ param । eṣa saṃpātasaṃskāraścarorbhoktā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। bhogyasya paramaṃ sāraṃ bhogyaṃ narnarti yatnataḥ । samamekānusandhānātpātato bhoktṛbhogyayoḥ ।।
anyo anyatra ca saṃpātātsaṃgamāccetthamucyate । sthaṇḍile kubhbhakarkaryorbhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ nivedayet ।। bhāgenāgnau mantratṛptirdvayaṃ śiṣyātmanoratha । itthaṃ vihitakartavyo vijñāpyeśaṃ tadīritaḥ ।।
śaktipātakramācchiṣyānsaṃskartuṃ niḥsaredbahiḥ । tatraiṣāṃ pañcagavyaṃ ca caruṃ daśanamārjanam ।। tasya pātaḥ śubhaḥ prācīsaumyaiśāpyordhvadiggataḥ । aśubho anyatra tatrāstrahomo apyaṣṭaśataṃ bhavet ।।
netramantritasadvastrabaddhanetrānacañcalān । ananyahṛdayībhūtānbalāditthaṃ nirodhataḥ ।। muktāratnādikusumasaṃpūrṇāñjalikānguruḥ । praveśya sthaṇḍilopāgra upaveśyaiva jānubhiḥ ।।
prakṣepayedañjaliṃ taṃ taiḥ śiṣyairbhāvitātmabhiḥ । añjali punarāpūrya teṣāṃ lāghavataḥ paṭam ।। dṛśornivārayetso api śiṣyo jhaṭiti paśyati । jhaṭityālokite māntraprabhāvollāsite sthale ।।
tadāveśavaśācchiṣyastanmayatvaṃ prapadyate । yathā hi raktahṛdayastāṃstānkāntāguṇānsvayam ।। paśyatyevaṃ śaktipātasaṃskṛto mantrasannidhim । cakṣurādīndriyāṇāṃ hi sahakāriṇi tādṛśe ।।
satyatyantamadṛṣṭe prāgapi jāyeta yogyatā । kṛtaprajñā hi vinyastamantraṃ dehaṃ jalaṃ sthalam ।। pratimādi ca paśyanto viduḥ saṃnidhyasaṃnidhī । nyastamantrāṃśusubhagātkiṃcidbhūtādimudritāḥ ।।
trasyantīveti tattaccidakṣaistatsahakāribhiḥ । tataḥ sa dakṣiṇe haste dīptaṃ sarvādhvapūritam ।। mantracakraṃ yajedvāmapāṇinā pāśadāhakam । taṃ śiṣyasya karaṃ mūrdhni dehanyastādhvasaṃtateḥ ।।
nyasyetkrameṇa sarvāṃṅgaṃ tenaivāsya ca saṃspṛśet । uktaṃ dīkṣottare caitajjvālāsaṃpātaśobhinā ।। dattena śivahastena samayī sa vidhīyate । sāyujyamīśvare tattve jīvato adhītiyogyatā ।।
śrīdevyāthāmale tūktamaṣṭārāntastriśūlake । cakre bhairavasannābhāvaghorādyaṣṭakārake ।। bāhyāpare parānemau madhyaśūlaparāpare । jvālākule aruṇe bhrāmyanmātṛpraṇavabhīṣaṇe ।।
cintite tu bahirhaste saṃdṛṣṭe samayī bhavet । pāśastobhādyastu sadya uccikramiṣurasya tam ।। prāṇairviyojakaṃ mūrdhni kṣipetsaṃpūjya tadbahiḥ । anena śivahastena samayī bhavati sphuṭam ।।
tasyaiva bhāvividhivattattvapāśaviyojane । putrakatvaṃ sa ca pare tattve yojyastu daiśikaiḥ ।। sa eva mantrajātijño japahomāditattvavit । nirvāṇakalaśenādau tata īśvarasaṃjñinā ।।
abhiṣiktaḥ sādhakaḥ syādbhogānte asya pare layaḥ । etairguṇaiḥ samāyukto dīkṣitaḥ śivaśāsane ।। catuṣpātsaṃhitābhijñastantrāṣṭādaśatatparaḥ । daśatantrātimārgajña ācāryaḥ sa vidhīyate ।।
pṛthivīmāditaḥ kṛtvā nirvāṇānte asya yojanām । abhiṣekavidhau kuryādācāryasya gurūttamaḥ ।। etairvākyairidaṃ coktaṃ samayī rājaputravat । sarvatraivādhikārī syātputrakādipadatraye ।।
putrako daiśikatve tu tulyayojaniko bhavet । adhikārī sa na punaḥ sādhane bhinnayojane ।। etattantre samayyādikramādāptottarakriyaḥ । ācāryo na punarbauddhavaiṣṇavādiḥ kadācana ।।
evaṃ prasaṅgānnirṇītaṃ prakṛtaṃ tu nirūpyate । śivahastavidhiṃ kṛtvā tena saṃpluṣṭapāśakam ।। śiṣyaṃ vidhāya viśrāntiparyantaṃ dhyānayogataḥ । tataḥ kumbhe astrakalaśe vahnau svātmani taṃ śiśum ।।
praṇāmaṃ kārayetpaścādbhūtamātṛbaliṃ kṣipet । tataḥ śaṃkaramabhyarcya śayyāmastrābhimantritām ।। kṛtvāsyāṃ śiṣyamāropya nyastamantraṃ vidhāya ca । śiṣyahṛccakraviśrāntiṃ kṛtvā taddvādaśāntagaḥ ।।
bhavetkṣīṇakalājālaḥ svaradvādaśakodayāt । tataḥ praveśapracitakalāṣoḍaśakojjvalaḥ ।। saṃpūrṇasvātmaciccandro viśrāmyeddhṛdaye śiśoḥ । svayaṃ vyutthānaparyantaṃ dvādaśāntaṃ tato vrajet ।।
punarviśecca hṛccakramitthaṃ nidrāvidhikramaḥ । āyātanidraḥ śiṣyo asau nirmalau śaśibhāskarau ।। hṛccakre pratisaṃdhatte balātpūrṇakṛśātmakau । haṭhanirmalacandrārkaprakāśaḥ satyamīkṣate ।।
svapnaṃ bhāviśubhānyatvasphuṭībhāvanakovidam । uktaṃ ca pūrṇāṃ ca kṛśāṃ dhyātvā dvādaśagocare ।। praviśya hṛdaye dhyāye tsuptaḥ svācchandyamāpnuyāt । āyātanidre ca śiśau gururabhyarcya śaṅkaram ।।
caruṃ bhuñjīta sasakhā tato adyāddantadhāvanam । svapyācca mantraraśmīddhahṛccakrārpitamānasaḥ ।। prātarguruḥ kṛtāśeṣanityo abhyarcitaśaṃkaraḥ । śiṣyātmanoḥ svapnadṛṣṭāvarthau vitte balābalāt ।।
svadṛṣṭaṃ balavannānyatsaṃbodhodrekayogataḥ । bodhasāmye punaḥ svapnasāmyaṃ syādguruśiṣyayoḥ ।। devāgnigurutatpūjākāraṇopaskarādikam । hṛdyā strī madyapānaṃ cāpyāmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam ।।
raktapānaṃ śiraśchedo raktaviṇmūtralepanam । parvatāśvagajaprāyahṛdyayugyādhirohaṇam ।। yatprītyai syādapi prāyastattacchubhamudāhṛtam । taṃ khyāpayettuṣṭivṛddhyai hlādo hi paramaṃ phalam ।।
ato anyadaśubhaṃ tatra homo aṣṭaśatako astrataḥ । aśubhaṃ nāśubhamiti śiṣyebhyo kathayedguruḥ ।। rūḍhāṃ hi śaṅkāṃ vicchettuṃ yatnaḥ saṃghaṭate mahān । yeṣāṃ tu śaṅkāvilayasteṣāṃ svapnavaśotthitam ।।
śubhāśubhaṃ na kiṃcitsyāt syuścetthaṃ citratāvaśāt । sphuṭaṃ paśyati sattvātmā rājaso liṅgamātrataḥ ।। na kiṃcittāmasastasya sukhaduḥkhācchubhāśubham । nanvatra tāmaso nāma kathaṃ yogyo vidhau bhavet ।।
maiva mā vigrahaṃ kaścitkvacitkasyāpi vai guṇaḥ । sarvasāttvikaceṣṭo api bhojane yadi tāmasaḥ ।। kiṃ tataḥ so adhamaḥ kivāpyutkṛṣṭastadviparyayaḥ । āyātaśaktipāto api dīkṣito api guṇasthiteḥ ।।
vicitrātmā bhavedeva mukhye tvarthe samāhitaḥ । tato guruḥ śiśormantrapūrvakaṃ devatārcanam ।। deśayetsa ca tatkuryātsaṃskuryāttaṃ tato guruḥ । hṛdādicakraṣaṭkasthānbrahmādīn ṣaṭ samāhitaḥ ।।
spṛśecchiśoḥ prāṇavṛttyā pratyekaṃ cāṣṭa saṃskriyāḥ । hṛdayādidviṣaṭkāntaṃ bodhasparśapavitritaḥ ।। āhārabījabhāvādidoṣadhvaṃsādbhaveddvijaḥ । vasuvedākhyasaṃskārapūrṇa itthaṃ dvijaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmanto jātakarma ca । nāma niṣkrāmaṇaṃ cānnapraśaścūḍā tathāṣṭamī ।। vratabandhaiṣṭike maujjībhautike saumikaṃ kramāt । godānamiti vedendusaṃskriyā brahmacaryataḥ ।।
pratyudvāhaḥ pañcadaśaḥ sapta pākamakhāstvataḥ । aṣṭakāḥ pārvaṇī śrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāgrāyaṇīdvayam ।। caitrī cāśvayujī paścāt saptaiva tu havirmakhāḥ । ādheyamagnihotraṃ ca paurṇamāsaḥ sadarśakaḥ ।।
cāturmāsyaṃ paśūdbandhaḥ sautrāmaṇyā saha tvamī । agniṣṭomo atipūrvo atha sokyyaḥ ṣoḍaśivājapau ।। āptoryāmātirātrau ca saptaitāḥ somasaṃsthitāḥ । hiraṇyapādādimakhaḥ sahasreṇa samāvṛtaḥ ।।
aṣṭatriṃśastvaśvamedho gārhasthyamiyatā bhavet । vānasthyapārivrājye ca catvāriṃśadamī matāḥ ।। dayā kṣamānasūyā ca śuddhiḥ satkṛtimaṅgale । akārpaṇyāspṛhe cātmaguṇāṣṭakamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
mekhalā daṇḍamajinatryāyuṣe vahnyupāsanam । saṃdhyā bhikṣeti saṃskārāḥ sapta sapta vratāni ca ।। bhauteśapāśupatye dve gāṇeśaṃ gāṇapatyakam । unmattakāsidhārākhyaghṛteśāni caturdaśa ।।
ete tu vratabandhasya saṃskārā aṅginaḥ smṛtāḥ । pārivrājyasya garbhe syādantyeṣṭiriti saṃskṛtaḥ ।। dvijo bhavettato yogyo rudrāṃśāpādanāya saḥ । etānprāṇakrameṇaiva saṃskārānyojayedguruḥ ।।
athavāhutiyogena tilādyairmantrapūrvakaiḥ । praṇavo hṛdayaṃ nāma śodhayāmyagnivallabhā ।। evaṃ krameṇa mūrdhādyairaṅgairatatpunaḥ punaḥ । yataściddharma evāsau śāntyādyātmā dvijanmatā ।।
tena rudratayā saṃvittatkrameṇaiva jāyate । yathā hemādidhātūnāṃ pāke kramavaśādbhavet ।। rajatādi tathā saṃvitsaṃskāre dvijatāntare । yonirna kāraṇaṃ tatra śāntātmā dvija ucyate ।।
muninā mokṣadharmādāvetacca pravivecitam । mukuṭādiṣu śāstreṣu devenāpi nirūpitam ।। saṃvido dehasaṃbhedātsadṛśātsadṛśodayāt । bhūmābhiprāyataḥ smārte dvijanmā dvijayoḥ sutaḥ ।।
antyajātīyadhīvādijananījanmalābhataḥ । utkṛṣṭacittā ṛṣayaḥ kiṃ brāhmaṇyena bhājanam ।। ata evārthasattattvadeśinyasminna diśyate । rahasyaśāstre jātyādisamācāro hi śāmbhave ।।
pāśavāni tu śāstrāṇi vāmaśaktyātmakānyalam । sṛṣṭyāṃcisiddhaye śaṃbhoḥ śaṅkātatphalakḷptaye ।। āpāditadvijatvasya dvādaśānte nijaikyataḥ । sparśamātrānna viśrāntyā jhaṭityevāvarohataḥ ।।
rudrāṃśāpādanaṃ yena samayī saṃskṛto bhavet । adhītau śravaṇe nityaṃ pūjāyāṃ gurusevane ।। samayyadhikṛto anyatra guruṇā vibhumarcayet । tamāpāditarudrāṃśaṃ samayān śrāvayedguruḥ ।।
aṣṭāṣṭakātmakāndevyāyāmalādau nirūpitān । avādo akaraṇaṃ gūḍhiḥ pūjā tarpaṇabhāvane ।। hananaṃ mohanaṃ ceti samayāṣṭakamaṣṭadhā । svabhāvaṃ mantratantrāṇāṃ samayācāramelakam ।।
asatpralāpaṃ paruṣamanṛtaṃ nāṣṭadhā vadet । aphalaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ hiṃsāṃ paradārābhimarśanam ।। garvaṃ dambhaṃ bhūtaviṣavyādhitantraṃ nacācaret । svaṃ mantramakṣasūtraṃ ca vidyāṃ jñānasvarūpakam ।।
samācārānguṇānkleśānsiddhiliṅgāni gūhayet । guruṃ śāstraṃ devavahnī jñānavṛddhāṃstriyo vratam ।। guruvargaṃ yathāśaktyā pūjayedaṣṭakaṃ tvidam । dīnānkliṣṭānpitṝnkṣetrapālānprāṇigaṇān khagān ।।
śmāśānikaṃ bhūtagaṇaṃ dehadevīśca tarpayet । śivaṃ śaktiṃ tathātmānaṃ mudrāṃ mantrasvarūpakam ।। saṃsārabhuktimuktīśca guruvaktrāttu bhāvayet । rāgaṃ dveṣamasūyāṃ ca saṃkocerṣyābhimānitāḥ ।।
samayapratibhettṝṃstadanācārāṃśca ghātayet । paśumārgasthitānkrūrāndveṣiṇaḥ piśunāñjaḍān ।। rājñaścānucarānpāpānvighnakartṝṃśca mohayet । śākinyaḥ pūjanīyāśca tāścetthaṃ śrīgamoditāḥ ।।
sāhasaṃ dviguṇaṃ yāsāṃ kāmaścaiva caturguṇaḥ । lobhaścāṣṭaguṇastāsāṃ śaṅkyaṃ śākinya ityalam ।। kulāmnāyasthitā vīradravyabāhyāstu ye na taiḥ । paśubhiḥ saha vastavyamiti śrīmādhave kule ।।
devatācakragurvagniśāstraṃ sāmyātsadārcayet । aniveditametebhyo na kiṃcidapi bhakṣayet ।। etaddravyaṃ nāpaharedguruvargaṃ prapūjayet । sa ca tadbhrātṛbhāryātukprāyo vidyākṛto bhavet ।।
na yonisaṃbandhakṛto laukikaḥ sa paśuryataḥ । tasyābhiṣvaṅgabhūmistu gurvārādhanasiddhaye ।। arcyo na svamahimnā tu tadvargo guruvatpunaḥ । gurornindāṃ na kurvīta tasyai hetuṃ nacācaret ।।
naca tāṃ śṛṇuyānnainaṃ kopayennāgrato asya ca । vinājñayā prakurvīta kiṃcittatsevanādṛte ।। laukikālaukikaṃ kṛtyaṃ krodhaṃ krīḍāṃ tapo japam । gurūpabhuktaṃ yatkiṃcicchayyāvastrāsanādikam ।।
nopabhuñjīta tatpadbhyāṃ na spṛśetkiṃtu vandayet । śrīmattraiśirase apyuktaṃ kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ ।। araṇye kāṣṭhavattiṣṭhedasidhārāvrato api san । niyamastho yamastho api tatpadaṃ nāśnute param ।।
gurvārādhanasaktastu manasā karmaṇā girā । prāpnoti gurutastuṣṭāt pūrṇaṃ śreyo mahādbhutam ।। himapātairyathā bhūmiśchāditā sā samantataḥ । mārutaśleṣasaṃyogādaśmavattiṣṭhate sadā ।।
yamādau niścale tadvadbhāva ekastu gṛhyate । gurostvārādhitātpūrṇaṃ prasarajjñānamāpyate ।। sarvato avasthitaṃ cittvaṃ jñeyasthaṃ yasya tatkathā । sadya eva nayedūrdhvaṃ tasmādārādhayedgurum ।।
śrīsāre apyasya saṃbhāṣātpātakaṃ naśyati kṣaṇāt । tasmātparīkṣya yatnena śāstroktyā jñānalakṣaṇaiḥ ।। śāstrācāreṇa varteta tena saṅgaṃ tathā kuru । snehājjātu vadejjñānaṃ lobhānna hriyate hi saḥ ।।
tena tuṣṭena tṛpyanti devāḥ pitara evaca । uttīrya narakādyānti sadyaḥ śivapuraṃ mahat ।। bhuṅkte tiṣṭhedyatra gṛhe vrajecchivapuraṃ tu saḥ । iti jñātvā sadā pitrye śrāddhe svaṃ gurumarcayet ।।
bhuñjīta sa svayaṃ cānyānādiśettatkṛte guruḥ । yo dīkṣitastu śrāddhādau svatantraṃ vidhimācaret ।। tasya tanniṣphalaṃ sarvaṃ samayena ca laṅghyate । saiddhāntikārpitaṃ caṇḍīyogyaṃ dravyaṃ vivarjayet ।।
śākinīvācakaṃ śabdaṃ na kadācitsamuccaret । striyaḥ pūjyā virūpāstu vṛddhāḥ śilpopajīvikāḥ ।। antyā vikāritāṅgyaśca veśyāḥ svacchandaceṣṭitāḥ । tathāca śrīgame proktaṃ pūjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
nirācārāḥ sarvabhakṣyā dharmādharmavivarjitāḥ । svacchandagāḥ palāśinyo lampaṭā devatā iva ।। veśyāḥ pūjyāstadgṛhaṃ ca prayāgo atra yajetkramam । strīṣu tannācaretkicidyena tābhyo jugupsate ।।
ato na nagnāstāḥ paśyennacāpi prakaṭastanīḥ । vṛddhāyāḥ saṃsthitāyā vā na jugupseta mudrikām ।। vaikṛtyaṃ tatra saurūpyaṃ melakaṃ na prakāśayet । devamūrtiṃ śūnyatanuṃ pūjayettripathādiṣu ।।
sarvaparvasu sāmānyaviśeṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ । pūjā guroranadhyāyo melake lobhavarjanam ।। na jugupseta madyādi vīradravyaṃ kadācana । na nindedatha vandeta nityaṃ tajjoṣiṇastathā ।।
upadeśāya na doṣā hṛdayaṃ cenna vidviṣet । vijātīyavikalpāṃśotpuṃsanāya yateta ca ।। guroḥ śāstrasya devīnāṃ nāma mantre yatastataḥ । arcāto anyatra noccāryamāhūtaṃ tarpayettataḥ ।।
āgatasya ca mantrasya na kuryāttarpaṇaṃ yadi । haratyardhaśarīraṃ tadityūce bhagavānyataḥ ।। śrīmadūrmau ca devīnāṃ vīrāṇāṃ ceṣṭitaṃ na vai । prathayenna jugupseta vadennādravyapāṇikaḥ ।।
śrīpūrvaṃ nāma vaktavyaṃ gurordravyakareṇa ca । gurvādīnāṃ na laṅghyā ca chāyā na tairthikaiḥ saha ।। jalpaṃ kurvansvaśāstrārthaṃ vadennāpica sūcayet । nityādviśeṣapūjāṃ ca kuryānnaimittike vidhau ।।
tato api madhye varṣasya tato api hi pavitrake । anyastamantro nāsīta sevyaṃ śāstrāntaraṃ ca no ।। aprarūḍhaṃ hi vijñānaṃ kampetetarabhāvanāt । gṛhopaskaraṇāstrāṇi davatāyāgayogataḥ ।।
arcyānīti na padbhyāṃ vai spṛśennāpi vilaṅghyet । guruvarge gṛhāyāte viśeṣaṃ kaṃcidācaret ।। dīkṣitānāṃ na nindādi kuryādvidveṣapūrvakam । upadeśāya no doṣaḥ sa hyavidveṣapūrvakaḥ ।।
na vaṣṇavādikādhaḥsthadṛṣṭibhiḥ saṃvasedalam । sahabhojanaśayyādyarnaiṣāṃ prakaṭayetsthitim ।। uktaṃ śrīṃmādhavakule śāsanāntarasaṃsthitān । vedoktiṃ vaiṣṇavoktiṃ ca tairuktaṃ varjayetsadā ।।
akulīneṣu saṃparkāttatkulātpatanādbhayam । ekapātre kulāmnāye tasmāttānparivarjayet ।। pramādācca kṛte sakhye goṣṭhyāṃ cakraṃ tu pūjayet । śrīmadūrmau ca kathitamāgamāntarasevake ।।
gurvantararate mūḍhe devadravyopajīvake । śaktihiṃsākare duṣṭe saṃparkaṃ naiva kārayet ।। na vikalpena dīkṣādau vrajedāyatanādikam । uktāsthāśithilatve yannimittaṃ naiva taccaret ।।
śāsanasthānpurājātyā na paśyennāpyudīrayet । naca vyavaharetsarvāñchivābhedena kevalam ।। sadvidyaiḥ sākamāsīta jñānadīptyai yateta ca । nāsaṃskṛtāṃ vrajettajjaṃ viphalatvaṃ nacānayet ।।
melakārdhaniśācaryā janavarjaṃ ca tannahi । māṃsādidāhagandhaṃ ca jighreddevīpriyo hyasau ।। gurvājñāṃ pālayansarvaṃ tyajenmantramayo bhavet । śāstrapūjājapadhyānavivekatadupakriyāḥ ।।
akurvanniṣphalāṃ naiva ceṣṭeta trividhāṃ kriyām । mantratantrairna vādaṃ ca kuryānno bhakṣayedviṣam ।। samayānāṃ vilope ca guruṃ pṛcchedasannidhau । tadvargaṃ nijasantānamanyaṃ tasyāpyasaṃnidhau ।।
tenoktamanutiṣṭhecca nirvikalpaṃ prayatnataḥ । yataḥ śāstrādisaṃbodhatanmayīkṛtamānasaḥ ।। śiva eva gururnāsya vāgasatyā viniḥsaret । śivasya svātmasaṃskṛtyai prahvībhāvo guroḥ punaḥ ।।
hlādāyetyubhayārthāya tattuṣṭiḥ phaladā śiśoḥ । gurvāyattaikasiddhirhisamayyapi vibodhabhāk ।। tadbodhabahumānena vidyādgurutamaṃ gurum । ataḥ saṃprāpya vijñānaṃ yo gurau bāhyamānavān ।।
nāsau vijñānaviśvasto nāsatyaṃ bhraṣṭa eva saḥ । jñānānāśvastacittaṃ taṃ vacomātreṇa śāstritam ।। bhaktaṃ ca nārcayejjātu hṛdā vijñānadūṣakam । tādṛk ca na guruḥ kāryastaṃ kṛtvāpi parityajet ।।
mukhyabuddhyā na saṃpaśyedvaiṣṇavādigatāngurūn । tathāca śrīmadūrmyākhye guroruktaṃ viśeṣaṇam ।। gurvājñā prāṇasaṃdehe nopekṣyā no vikalpyate । kauladīkṣā kaulaśāstraṃ tattvajñānaṃ prakāśitam ।।
yenāsau gururityukto hyanye vai nāmadhāriṇaḥ । śrīmadānandaśāstre ca tathaivoktaṃ viśeṣaṇam ।। yasmāddīkṣā mantraśāstraṃ tattvajñānaṃ sa vai guruḥ । tiṣṭhedavyaktaliṅgaśca na liṅgaṃ dhārayet kvacit ।।
na liṅgibhiḥ samaṃ kaiścitkuryādācāramelanam । kevalaṃ liṅginaḥ pālyā na bībhatsyā virūpakāḥ ।। śrīmadrātrikule coktaṃ mokṣaḥ śaṅkāpahānitaḥ । aśuddhavāsasnayaiṣā mokṣavārtāpi durlabhā ।।
na likhenmantrahṛdayaṃ śrīmanmāloditaṃ kila । tadaṅgāduddharenmantraṃ natu lekhe vilekhayet ।। atattve abhiniveśaṃ ca na kuryātpakṣapātataḥ । jātividyākulācāradehadeśaguṇārthajān ।।
grahāngrahānivāṣṭau drāktyajedgahvararśitān । tathā śrīniśicārādau hayatvenopadarśitān ।। brāhmaṇo ahaṃ mayā vedaśāstroktādaparaṃ katham । anuṣṭheyamayaṃ jātigrahaḥ paranirodhakaḥ ।।
evamanye apyudāhāryāḥ kulagahvaravartmanā । atatsvabhāve tādrūpyaṃ darśayannavaśe api yaḥ ।। svarūpācchādakaḥ so atra graho graha ivoditaḥ । saṃvitsvabhāve no jātiprabhṛtiḥ kāpi kalpanā ।।
rūpaṃ sā tvasvarūpeṇa tadrūpaṃ chādayatyalam । yā kācitkalpanā saṃvittattvasyākhaṇḍitātmanaḥ ।। saṃkocakāriṇī sarvaḥ sa grahastāṃ parityajet । śrīmadānandaśāstre ca kathitaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।।
nirapekṣaḥ prabhurvāmo na śuddhyā tatra kāraṇam । devītṛptirmakhe raktamāṃsairno śaucayojanāt ।। dvijāntyajaiḥ samaṃ kāryā carcānte api marīcayaḥ । avikārakṛtastena vikalpānnirayo bhavet ।।
sarvadevamayaḥ kāyaḥ sarvaprāṇiṣviti sphuṭam । śrīmadbhirnakuleśādyairapyetatsunirūpitam ।। śarīramevāyatanaṃ nānyadāyatanaṃ vrajet । tīrthamekaṃ smarenmantramanyatīrthāni varjayet ।।
vidhimenaṃ sukhaṃ jñātvā vidhijālaṃ parityajet । samādhirniścayaṃ muktvā na cānyenopalabhyate ।। iti matvā vidhānajñaḥ saṃmohaṃ parivarjayet । mantrasya hṛdayaṃ muktvā na cānyatparamaṃ kvacit ।।
iti matvā vidhānajño mantrajālaṃ parityajet । naivedyaṃ prāśayennadyāstaccheṣaṃ ca jale kṣipet ।। tairbhukte na bhaveddoṣo jalajaiḥ pūrvadīkṣitaiḥ । avayaśpālanīyatvātparattvena saṃgamāt ।।
jñānaprāptyabhyupāyatvātsamayāste prakīrtitāḥ । evaṃ saṃśrāvya samayāndevaṃ saṃpūjya daiśikaḥ ।। visarjayetsvacidvyomni śānte mūrtivilāpanāt । yadi putrakadīkṣāsya na kāryā samanantaram ।।
tadābhiṣiñcetsāstreṇa śivakumbhena taṃ śiśum । ātmānaṃ ca tato yasmājjalamūrtirmaheśvaraḥ ।। mantrayuṅnikhilāpyāyī kāryaṃ tadabhiṣecanam । iti samayadīkṣaṇamidaṃ prakāśitaṃ vistarācca saṃkṣepāt ।।
atha putrakatvasiddhyai nirūpyate śivanirūpito atra vidhiḥ । yadā tu samayasthasya putrakatve niyojanam । gurutve sādhakatve vā kartumicchati daiśikaḥ ।। tadādhivāsaṃ kṛtvāhni dvitīye maṇḍalaṃ likhet ।
sāmudāyikayāge atha tathānyatra yathoditam ।। ṣaḍaṣṭataddviguṇitacaturviṃśatisaṃkhyayā । cakrapañcakamākhyātaṃ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite ।। dvātriṃśattaddviguṇitaṃ śrīmattraiśirase mate ।
asaṃkhyacakrasaṃbandhaḥ śrīsiddhādau nirūpitaḥ ।। tasmādyathātathā yāgaṃ yāvaccakreṇa saṃmitam । pūjayedyena tenātra triśūlatrayamālikhet ।। triśūlatritaye devītrayaṃ paryāyavṛttitaḥ ।
madhyasavyānyabhedena pūrṇaṃ saṃpūjitaṃ bhavet ।। vartanā maṇḍalasyāgre saṃkṣepādupadekṣyate । ālikhya maṇḍalaṃ gandhavastreṇaivāsya mārjanam ।। kṛtvā snāto guruḥ prāgvanmaṇḍalāgre atra devatāḥ ।
bāhyagāḥ pūjayeddvāradeśe ca dvāradevatāḥ ।। maṇḍalasya purobhāge tadaiśānadiśaḥ kramāt । āgneyyantaṃ gaṇeśādīn kṣetrapāntānprapūjayet ।। gaṇapatiguruparamākhyāḥ parameṣṭhī pūrvasiddhavākkṣetrapatiḥ ।
iti saptakamākhyātaṃ gurupaṅktividhau prapūjyamasmadgurubhiḥ ।। tata ājñāṃ gṛhītvā tu puṣpadhūpādipūjitam । pūjyamādhāraśaktyādi śūlamūlātprabhṛtyalam ।। śivāntaṃ sitapadmānte triśūlānāṃ traye kramāt ।
madhyaśūle madhyagaḥ syātsadbhāvaḥ parayā saha ।। vāme cāparayā sākaṃ navātmā dakṣagaṃ param । triśūle dakṣiṇe madhyaśṛṅgastho ratiśekharaḥ ।। syātparāparayā sākaṃ dakṣe bhairavasatpare ।
vāme triśūle madhyastho navātmāparayā saha ।। syātpare parayā sākaṃ vāmāre saṃśca bhairavaḥ । itthaṃ sarvagatatve śrīparādevyāḥ sthite sati ।। yāgo bhavetsusaṃpūrṇastadadhiṣṭhānamātrataḥ ।
ekaśūle apyato yāge cintayettadadhiṣṭhitam ।। avidhijño vidhānajña ityevaṃ trīśikoditam । tato madhye tathā dakṣe vāme śṛṅge ca sarvataḥ ।। lokapālāstraparyantamekātmatvena pūjayet ।
paratvena ca sarvāsāṃ devatānāṃ prapūjayet ।। śrīmantaṃ mātṛsadbhāvabhaṭṭārakamanāmayam । tato api bhogayāgena vidyāṅgaṃ bhairavāṣṭakam ।। yāmalaṃ cakradevīśca svasthāne pūjayedbahiḥ ।
lokapālānastrayutāngandhapuṣpāsavādibhiḥ ।। pūjayetparayā bhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ । tataḥ kumbhāstrakalaśīmaṇḍalasthānalātmanām ।। pañcānāmanusandhānaṃ kuryādadvayabhāvanāt ।
ye tu tāmadvayavyāptiṃ na vindanti śivātmikām ।। mantranāḍīprayogeṇa te viśantyadvaye pathi । svadakṣiṇena niḥsṛtya maṇḍalasthasya vāmataḥ ।। praviśyānyena niḥsṛtya kumbhasthe karkarīgate ।
vahnisthe ca krameṇetthaṃ yāvatsvasminsvavāmataḥ ।। mūlānusandhānabalātprāṇatantūmbhane sati । itthamaikyasphurattātmā vyāptisaṃvitprakāśate ।। tato viśeṣapūjāṃ ca kuryādadvayabhāvitām ।
yacchivādvayapīyūṣasaṃsiktaṃ paramaṃ hi tat ।। tenārghapuṣpagandhāderāsavasya paśoratha । yā śivādvayatādṛṣṭiḥ sā śuddhiḥ paramīkṛtiḥ ।। nivedayedvibhoragre jīvāndhātūṃstadutthitān ।
siddhānasiddhānvyāmiśrānyadvā kiṃciccarācaram ।। dṛṣṭaprokṣitasaṃdraṣṭṛprālabdhopāttayojitaḥ । nirvāpito vīrapaśuḥ so aṣṭadhottaratottamaḥ ।। yathottaraṃ na dātavyamayogyebhyaḥ kadācana ।
śivopayuktaṃ hi havirna sarvo bhoktumarhati ।। yastu dīkṣāvihīno api śivecchāvidhicoditaḥ । bhaktyāśnāti sa saṃpūrṇaḥ samayī syātsubhāvitaḥ ।। dṛṣṭo avalokitaścaiva kiraṇeddhadṛgarpaṇāt ।
prokṣitaḥ kevalaṃ hyarghapātravipruḍbhirukṣitaḥ ।। saṃdraṣṭā darśitāśeṣasamyakpūjitamaṇḍalaḥ । prālabdha uktatritayasaṃskṛtaḥ so api dhūnayet ।। kampeta prasravetstabdhaḥ pralīno vā yathottaram ।
upātto yāgasānnidhye śamitaḥ śastramārutaiḥ ।। yojitaḥ kāraṇatyāgakrameṇa śivayojanāt । nirvāpitaḥ kṛtābhyāsaguruprāṇamanorpaṇāt ।। dakṣiṇenāgninā saumyakalājālavilāpanāt ।
tathāhyādau paraṃ rūpamekībhāvena saṃśrayet ।। tasmādāgneyacāreṇa jvālāmālāmucāviśet । paśorvāmena candrāṃśujālaṃ tāpena gālayet ।। nābhicakre atha viśrāmyetprāṇaraśmigaṇaiḥ saha ।
paro bhūtvā svaśaktyātra jīvaṃ jīvena veṣṭayet ।। svacitsūryeṇa saṃtāpya drāvayet kalāṃ kalām । tato drutaṃ kalājālaṃ prāpayyaikatvamātmani ।। samastatattvasaṃpūrṇamāpyāyanavidhāyinam ।
unmūlayeta saṃrambhātkarmabaddhamamuṃ rasāt ।। tata unmūlanodveṣṭayogādvāmaṃ paribhraman । kuṇḍalyamṛtasaṃpūrṇasvakaprāṇaprasevakaḥ ।। vāmāvartakramopāttahṛtpadmāmṛtakesaraḥ ।
hṛtkarṇikārūḍhilābhādojodhātuṃ vilāpitam ।। śuddhasomātmakaṃ sāramīṣallohitapītalam । ādāya karihastāgrasadṛśe prāṇavigrahe ।। niḥsṛtya jhaṭiti svātmavāmamārgeṇa saṃviśet ।
āpyāyayannapānākhyacandracakrahṛdambuje ।। sthitaṃ taddevatācakraṃ tena sāreṇa tarpayet । anena vidhinā sarvānrasaraktādikāṃstathā ।। dhātūnsamāharetsaṃghakramādekaikaśo athavā ।
kevalaṃ tvathavāgnīnduravisaṃghaṭṭamadhyagam ।। jyotīrūpamatha prāṇaśaktyākhyaṃ jīvamāharet । jīvaṃ samarasīkuryāddevīcakreṇa bhāvanāt ।। tadeva tarpaṇaṃ mukhyaṃ bhogyabhoktrātmataiva sā ।
agnisaṃpuṭaphullārṇatryaśrakālātmako mahān ।। piṇḍo raktādisāraughacālanākarṣaṇādiṣu । itthaṃ viśrāntiyogena ghaṭikārdhakrame sati ।। āvṛttiśatayogena paśornirvāpaṇaṃ bhavet ।
kṛtvā katipayaṃ kālaṃ tatrābhyāsamananyadhīḥ ।। yathā cintāmaṇau proktaṃ tena rūpeṇa yogavit । niḥśaṅkaḥ siddhimāpnoti gopyaṃ tatprāṇavatsphuṭam ।। parokṣe api paśāvevaṃ vidhiḥ syādyojanaṃ prati ।
praveśito yāgabhuvi hatastatraiva sādhitaḥ ।। cakrajuṣṭaśca tatraiva sa vīrapaśurucyate । yastvanyatrāpi nihataḥ sāmastyenāṃśato apivā ।। devāya vinivedyeta sa vai bāhyapaśurmataḥ ।
rājyaṃ lābho atha tatsthairyaṃ śive bhaktistadātmatā ।। śivajñānaṃ mantralokaprāptistatparivāratā । tatsāyujyaṃ paśoḥ sāmyādbāhyādervīradharmaṇaḥ ।। puṣpādayo api tallābhabhāginaḥ śivapūjayā ।
ekopāyena deveśo viśvānugrahaṇātmakaḥ ।। yāgenaivānugṛhṇāti kiṃ kiṃ yanna carācaram । tenāvīro api śaṅkādiyuktaḥ kāruṇiko apica ।। na hiṃsābuddhimādadhyātpaśukarmaṇi jātucit ।
paśormahopakāro ayaṃ tadātve apyapriyaṃ bhavet ।। vyādhicchedauṣadhatapoyojanātra nidarśanam । śrīmanmṛtyuñjaye proktaṃ pāśacchede kṛte paśoḥ ।। malatrayaviyogena śarīraṃ na prarohati ।
dharmādharmaughavicchedāccharīraṃ cyacate kila ।। tenaitanmāraṇaṃ noktaṃ dīkṣeyaṃ citrarūpiṇī । rūḍhapāśasya yaḥ prāṇairviyogo māraṇaṃ hi tat ।। iyaṃ tu yojanaiva syātpaśordevāya tarpaṇe ।
tasmāddevoktimāśritya paśūndadyādbahūniti ।। niveditaḥ punaḥprāptadeho bhūyoniveditaḥ । ṣaṭkṛtva itthaṃ yaḥ so atra ṣaḍjanmā paśuruttamaḥ ।। yathā pākakramācchuddhaṃ hema tadvatsa kīrtitaḥ ।
kāṃ siddhiṃ naiva vitaretsvayaṃ kiṃvā na mucyate ।। uktaṃ tvānandaśāstre yo mantrasaṃskāravāṃstyajet । samayānkutsayeddevīrdadyānmantrānvinā nayāt ।। dīkṣāmantrādikaṃ prāpya tyajetputrādimohitaḥ ।
tato manuṣyatāmetya punarevaṃ karotyapi ।। itthamekādisaptāntajanmāsau dvividho dvipāt । catuṣpādvā paśurdevīcarukārthaṃ prajāyate ।। dātrarpito asau taddvārā yāti sāyujyataḥ śivam ।
iti saṃbhāvya citraṃ tatpaśūnāṃ praviceṣṭitam ।। bhogyīcikīrṣitaṃ naiva kuryādanyatra taṃ paśum । nāpi naiṣa bhavedyogya iti buddhvāpasārayet ।। taṃ paśuṃ kiṃtu kāṅkṣā cedviśeṣe taṃ tu ḍhaukayet ।
tāvatastānpaśūndadyāttathācoktaṃ maheśinā ।। paśorvapāmedasī ca gālite vahnimadhyataḥ । arpayecchakticakrāya paramaṃ tarpaṇaṃ matam ।। hṛdantramuṇḍāṃsayakṛtpradhānaṃ vinivedayet ।
karṇikākuṇḍalīmajjaparśu mukhyataraṃ ca vā ।। tato agnau tarpaṇaṃ kuryānmantracakrasya daiśikaḥ । tannivedya ca devāya tato vijñāpayetprabhum ।। gurutvena tvayaivāhamājñātaḥ parameśvara ।
sākṣātsvapnopadeśādyairjapairgurumukhena vā ।। anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śivaśaktipracoditāḥ । tadete tadvidhāḥ prāptāstvamebhyaḥ kurvanugraham ।। samāveśaya māṃ svātmaraśmibhiryadahaṃ śivaḥ ।
evaṃ bhavatviti tataḥ śivoktimabhinandayet ।। śivābhinnamathātmānaṃ pañcakṛtyakaraṃ smaret । svātmanaḥ karaṇaṃ mantrānmūrtiṃ cānujighṛkṣayā ।। tato baddhvā sitoṣṇīṣaṃ hastayorarcayetkramāt ।
anyonyaṃ pāśadāhāya śuddhatattvavisṛṣṭaye ।। tejorūpeṇa mantrāṃśca śivahaste samarcayet । garbhāvaraṇagānaṅgaparivārāsanojjhitān ।। ātmānaṃ bhāvayetpaścādekakaṃ jalacandravat ।
kṛtyopādhivaśādbhinnaṃ ṣoḍhābhinnaṃ tu vastutaḥ ।। maṇḍalastho ahamevāyaṃ sākṣī cākhilakarmaṇām । śuddhā hi draṣṭṛtā śambhormaṇḍale kalpitā mayā ।। homādhikaraṇatvena vahnāvahamavasthitaḥ ।
yadātmateddhā mantrāḥ syuḥ pāśaploṣavidhāvalam ।। sāmānyatejorūpāntarāhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥ । tarpitāḥ śrāvitāścāṇornādhikāraṃ pratanvate ।। ā yāgāntamahaṃ kumbhe saṃsthito vighnaśāntaye ।
sāmānyarūpatā yena viśeṣāpyāyakāriṇī ।। śiṣyadehe ca tatpāśaśithilatvaprasiddhaye । sa hi svecchāvaśātpāśānvidhunvanniva vartate ।। sākṣātsvadehasaṃstho ahaṃ kartānugrahakarmaṇām ।
jñānakriyāsvatantratvāddīkṣākarmaṇi peśalaḥ ।। bhinnakāryākṛtivrātendriyacakrānusandhimān । eko yathāhaṃ vahnyādiṣaḍrūpo asmi tathā sphuṭam ।। evamālocya yenaiṣo adhvanā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati ।
anusaṃhitaye śiṣyavarjaṃ pañcasu taṃ yajet ।। anusandhibalānte ca samāsavyāsabhedataḥ । kuryādatyantamabhyastamanyāntarbhāvapūritam ।। tato api cintayā bhūyo anusandadhyācchivātmatām ।
ahameva paraṃ tattvaṃ naca paddhaṭavat kvacit ।। mahāprakāśastattena mayi sarvamidaṃ jagat । naca tatkenacidbāhyapratibimbavadarpitam ।। kartāhamasya tannānyādhīnaṃ ca madadhiṣṭhitam ।
itthaṃbhūtamahāvyāptisaṃvedanapavitritaḥ ।। matsamatvaṃ gato janturmukta ityabhidhīyate । tāpanirgharṣasekādipāramparyeṇa vahnitām ।। yathāyogolako yāti gururevaṃ śivātmatām ।
tataḥ puraḥsthitaṃ yadvā purobhāvitavigraham ।। parokṣadīkṣaṇe yadvā darbhādyaiḥ kalpite mṛte । śiṣye vīkṣyārcya puṣpādyairnyasedadhvānamasya tam ।। yenādhvanā mukhyatayā dīkṣāmicchati daiśikaḥ ।
taṃ dehe nyasya tatrāntarbhāvyamanyaditi sthitiḥ ।। śodhyādhvani ca vinyaste tatraiva pariśodhakam । nyasedyathepsitaṃ mantraṃ śodhyaucityānusārataḥ ।। kvacicchodhyaṃ tvavinyasya śodhakanyāsamātrataḥ ।
svayaṃ śuddhyati saṃśodhyaṃ śodhakasya prabhāvataḥ ।। aparaṃ parāparaṃ ca paraṃ ca vidhimicchayā । tadyojanānusāreṇa śritvā nyāsaḥ ṣaḍadhvanaḥ ।। lalāṭāntaṃ vedavasau randhrāntaṃ rasarandhrake ।
vasukhendau dvādaśāntamityeṣa trividho vidhiḥ ।। krameṇa kathyate dṛṣṭaḥ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite । tatra tattveṣu vinyāso gulphānte caturaṅgule ।। dharā jalādimūlāntaṃ pratyekaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ kramāt ।
rasaśrutyaṅgulaṃ nābherūrdhvamitthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule ।। puṃsaḥ kalāntaṃ ṣaṭtattvīṃ pratyekaṃ tryaṅgule kṣipet । aṣṭādaśāṅgulaṃ tvevaṃ kaṇṭhakūpāvasānakam ।। sadāśivāntaṃ māyādicatuṣkaṃ caturaṅgule ।
pratyekamityabdhivasusaṃkhyamālikadeśataḥ ।। śivatattvaṃ tataḥ paścāttejorūpamanākulam । sarveṣāṃ vyāpakatvena sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret ।। jalāddhyantaṃ sārdhayugmaṃ mūlaṃ tryaṅgulamityataḥ ।
dvādaśāṅgulatādhikyādvidhireṣa parāparaḥ ।। jalāddhyantaṃ tryaṅgule cedavyaktaṃ tu catuṣṭaye । taccaturviṃśatyādhikyātparo apyaṣṭaśate vidhiḥ ।। trividhonmānakaṃ vyaktaṃ vasudigbhyo ravikṣayāt ।
mayatantre tathācoktaṃ tattatsvaphalavāñchayā ।। navapañcacatustryekatattvanyāse svayaṃ dhiyā । nyāsaṃ prakalpayettāvattattvāntarbhāvacintanāt ।। kalāpañcakavedāṇḍanyāso anenaiva lakṣitaḥ ।
uktaṃ ca triśirastantre svādhārasthaṃ yathāsthitam ।। dvādaśāṅgulamutthānaṃ dehātītaṃ samaṃ tataḥ । dvāsaptatirdaśa dve ca dehasthaṃ śiraso antataḥ ।। pādādārabhya suśroṇi anāhatapadāvadhi ।
dehātīte api viśrāntyā saṃvitteḥ kalpanāvaśāt ।। dehatvamiti tasmātsyādutthānaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam । iti nirṇetumatraitaduktamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।। puranyāso atha gulphāntaṃ bhūḥ purāṇyatra ṣoḍaśa ।
tasmādekāṅgulavyāptyā pratyekaṃ lakulāditaḥ ।। dviraṇḍāntaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ tu cchagalāṇḍamathābdhiṣu । devayogāṣṭake dve hi pratyekāṅgulapādataḥ ।। iti pradhānaparyantaṃ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadaṅgulam ।
ṣaṭpañcāśatpurāṇītthaṃ prāgdharāyāṃ tu ṣoḍaśa ।। tato apyardhāṅgulavyāptyā ṣaṭpurāṇyaṅgulatraye । catvāri yugma ekasminnekaṃ ca puramaṅgule ।। sarāge puṃspurāṇīśasaṃkhyānītthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule ।
krodheśapuramekasmindvaye cāṇḍamiyaṃ ca vit ।। saṃvartajyotiṣorevaṃ kalātattvagayoḥ kramāt । śūrapañcāntapurayorniyatau caikayugmatā ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre taccoktaṃ parameśena śaṃbhunā ।
uttarādikramādadvyekabhedo vidyādike traye ।। asāratvātkramasyādau niyatiḥ parataḥ kalā । athavānyonyasaṃjñābhyāṃ tattvayorvyapadeśyatā ।। ekavīraśikheśaśrīkaṇṭhāḥ kāle trayastraye ।
kālasya pūrvaṃ vinyāso niyaterabhidhīyate ।। athavānyonyasaṃjñābhirvyapadeśo hi dṛśyate । evaṃ pumādiṣaṭtattvī vinyastāṣṭādaśāṅgule ।। tato apyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ māyātattvasthamaṣṭakam ।
pratyekamardhāṅgulataḥ syādaṅgulacatuṣṭaye ।। itthaṃ dvyakṣṇi purāṇyaṣṭāviṃśatiḥ puruṣānniśi । puratrayaṃ dvayostryaṃśanyūnāṅgulamiti kramāt ।। dvayordvayaṃ pañcapurī vaidyīye caturaṅgule ।
tata aiśapurāṇyaṣṭau catuṣke ardhāṅgulakramāt ।। tatastrīṇi dvaye dve ca dvayoritthaṃ catuṣṭaye । sādāśivaṃ pañcakaṃ syāditthaṃ vasvekakaṃ ravau ।। ṣoḍaśakaṃ rasaviśikhaṃ vasudvikaṃ vasuśaśīti puravargāḥ ।
vedā rasābdhi yugmākṣi ca ravayastatra cāṅgulāḥ kramaśaḥ ।। aṣṭādaśādhikaśataṃ purāṇi dehe atra caturaśītimite । vinyastāni taditthaṃ śeṣe tu vyāpakaṃ śivaṃ tattvam ।। iti vidhiraparaḥ kathitaḥ parāparākhyo rasaśrutisthāne ।
aṣṭaśaraṃ saṃkhyānaṃ khamunikṛtaṃ tatpare vidhau jñeyam ।। lakulāderyogāṣṭakaparyantasyātra bhuvanapūgasya । adhikīkuryādgaṇanāvaśena bhāgaṃ vidhidvaye kramaśaḥ ।। aparādividhitraitādatha nyāsaḥ padādhvanaḥ ।
pūrvaṃ daśapadī coktā svatantrā nyasyate yadā ।। tayaiva dīkṣā kāryā cettadeyaṃ nyāsakalpanā । tattvādimukhyatāyogāddīkṣāyāṃ tu padāvalī ।। tattattvādyanusāreṇa tatrāntarbhāvyate tathā ।
svapradhānatvayoge tu dīkṣāyāṃ padapaddhatim ।। nyasyetkrameṇa tattvādivadanānavalokinīm । caturṣvaṣṭāsu cāṣṭāsu daśasvatha daśasvatha ।। daśasvatho pañcadaśasvatha vedaśarenduṣu ।
dharāpadānnavapadīṃ mātṛkāmālinīgatām ।। yojayedvyāptṛ daśamaṃ padaṃ tu śivasaṃjñitam । dharāpadaṃ varjayitvā pañca yāni padāni tu ।। vidhidvayaṃ syānnikṣipya dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān ।
mantrādhvano apyeṣa eva vidhirvinyāsayojane ।। vyāptimātraṃ hi bhidyetetyuktaṃ prāgeva tattathā । varṇādhvano atha vinyāsaḥ kathyate atra vidhitraye ।। ekaṃ caturṣu pratyekaṃ dvayoraṅgulayoḥ kramāt ।
trayoviṃśativarṇī syāt ṣaḍvarṇyekaikaśastriṣu ।। pratyekamatha catvāraścaturṣviti vilomataḥ । mālinīmātṛkārṇāḥ syurvyāptṛ śaivaṃ rasendutaḥ ।। varjayitvādyavarṇaṃ tu tattvavatsyādravīnnavīn ।
tāṃ trayoviṃśatau varṇeṣvapyanyatsyādvidhidvayam ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre tenādau tattveṣūktaṃ vidhitrayam । atidiṣṭaṃ tu tadbhinnābhinnavarṇadvaye samam ।। dvividho api hi varṇānāṃ ṣaḍvidho bheda ucyate ।
tattvamārgavidhānena jñātavyaḥ paramārthataḥ ।। upadeśātideśābhyāṃ yaduktaṃ tatpadādiṣu । bhūyo atidiṣṭaṃ tatraiva śāstre asmaddhṛdayeśvare ।। padamantrakalādīnāṃ pūrvasūtrānusārataḥ ।
tritayatvaṃ prakurvīta tattvavarṇoktavartmanā ।। uktaṃ tatpadamantreṣu kalāsvatha nirūpyate । caturṣu rasavede dvāviṃśatau dvādaśasvatha ।। nivṛttyādyāścatasraḥ syurvyāptrī syācchāntyatītikā ।
dvitīyasyāṃ kalāyāṃ tu dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān ।। kramātkṣiptvā vidhidvaitaṃ parāparaparātmakam । caturaṇḍavidhistvādiśabdeneha pragṛhyate ।। kalācatuṣkavattena tasminvācyaṃ vidhitrayam ।
evaṃ ṣaḍvidhamadhvānaṃ śodhyaśiṣyatanau purā ।। nyasyaikatamamukhyatvānnyasyecchodhakasaṃmatam । adhvanyāsanamantraughaḥ śodhako hyeka āditaḥ ।। śabdarāśirmālinī ca samastavyastato dvidhā ।
ekavīratayā yadvā ṣaṭkaṃ yāmalayogataḥ ।। pañcavaktrī śaktitadvadbhedātṣoḍhā punardvidhā । ekākiyāmalatvenetyevaṃ sā dvādaśātmikā ।। ṣaḍaṅgī sakalānyatvāddvividhā vaktravatpunaḥ ।
dvādaśatvena guṇitā caturviṃśatibhedikā ।। aghorādyaṣṭake dve ca tṛtīyaṃ yāmalodayāt । mātṛsadbhāvamantraśca kevalaḥ śruticakragaḥ ।। ekadvitricaturbhedāttrayodaśabhidātmakaḥ ।
ekavīratayā so ayaṃ caturdaśatayā sthitaḥ ।। anāmasaṃhṛtisthairyasṛṣṭicakraṃ caturvidham । devatābhirnijābhistanmātṛsadbhāvavṛṃhitam ।। itthaṃ śodhakavargo ayaṃ mantrāṇāṃ saptatiḥ smṛtā ।
ṣaḍardhaśāstreṣu śrīmatsāraśāstre ca kathyate ।। aghorādyaṣṭakeneha śodhanīyaṃ vipaścitā । athavaikākṣarāmantrairathavā mātṛkākramāt ।। bhairavīyahṛdā vāpi khecarīhṛdayena vā ।
bhairaveṇa mahādevi tvatha vaktrāṅgapañcakaiḥ ।। yena yena hi mantreṇa tantre asminnudbhavaḥ kṛtaḥ । tenaiva dīkṣayenmantrī ityājñā pārameśvarī ।। evaṃ śodhakabhedena saptatiḥ kīrtitā bhidaḥ ।
śodhyanyāsaṃ vinā mantrairetairdīkṣā yadā bhavet ।। tadā saptatidhā jñeyā jananādivivarjitā । śodhyabhedo atha vaktavyaḥ saṃkṣepātso api kathyate ।। ekatripañcaṣaṭtriṃśadbhedāttāttvaścaturvidhaḥ ।
pañcaikabhedāccādhvānastathaivāṇḍacatuṣṭayam ।। evaṃ daśavidhaṃ śodhyaṃ triṃśaddhā tadvidhitrayāt । śodhyaśodhakabhedena śatāni tvekaviṃśatiḥ ।। atrāpi nyāsayogena śodhye adhvani tathākṛteḥ ।
śataikaviṃśatibhidā jananādyujjhitā bhavet ।। jananādimayī tāvatyevaṃ śatadṛśi śrutiḥ । syātsaptatyadhikā sāpi dravyavijñānabhedataḥ ।। dvidheti pañcāśītiḥ syācchatānyadhikakhābdhikā ।
bhogamokṣānusandhānāddvividhā sā prakīrtitā ।। aśubhasyaiva saṃśuddhyā śubhasyāpyatha śodhanāt । dvidhā bhogaḥ śubhe śuddhiḥ kālatrayavibhedini ।। ekadvisāmastyavaśātsaptadhetyaṣṭadhā bhujiḥ ।
guruśiṣyakramātso api dvidhetyevaṃ vibhidyate ।। pratyakṣadīkṣaṇe yasmāddvayorekānusandhitaḥ । tādṛgdīkṣāphalaṃ pūrṇaṃ visaṃvāde tu viplavaḥ ।। parokṣamṛtadīkṣādau gururevānusandhimān ।
kriyājñānamahimnā taṃ śiṣyaṃ dhāmnīpsite nayet ।। avibhinne kriyājñāne karmaśuddhau tathaiva te । anusandhiḥ punarbhinnaḥ karma yasmāttadātmakam ।। śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca vāsanābhedataḥ phalam ।
śiṣyāṇāṃ ca guroścoktamabhinne api kriyādike ।। bhogasya śodhakācchodhyādanusandheśca tādṛśāt । vaicitryamasti bhedasya vaicitryaprāṇatā yataḥ ।। tathāhi vaktrairyasyādhvā śuddhastaireva yojitaḥ ।
bhoktumiṣṭe kvacittattve sa bhoktā tadbalānvitaḥ ।। śubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ cātra sadbhāve bhogacitratā । tādṛgeva bhavetkarmaśuddhau tvanyaiva citratā ।। bhogaśca sadya utkrāntyā dehenaivātha saṃgataḥ ।
tadaivābhyāsato vāpi dehānte vetyasau catuḥ ।। prāktanāṣṭabhidā yogāddvātriṃśadbheda ucyate । mokṣa eko api bījasya samayākhyasya tādṛśam ।। bālādikaṃ jñātaśīghramaraṇaṃ śaktivarjitam ।
vṛddhaṃ voddiśya śaktaṃ vā śodhanāśodhanāddvidhā ।। sadya utkrāntitastraidhaṃ sā cāsannamṛtau guroḥ । kāryetyājñā maheśasya śrīmadgahvarabhāṣitā ।। dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam ।
utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet ।। pañcatriṃśadamī bhedā gurorvā guruśiṣyayoḥ । uktadvaividhyakalanātsaptatiḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। etairbhedaiḥ puroktāṃstānbhedāndīkṣāgatānguruḥ ।
hatvā vadetprasaṃkhyānaṃ svabhyastajñānasiddhaye ।। pañcāśītiśatī yā catvāriṃśatsamuttarā kathitā । tāṃ saptatyā bhittvā dīkṣābhedānsvayaṃ kalayet ।। pañcakamiha lakṣāṇāṃ ca saptanavatiḥ sahasraparisaṃkhyā ।
aṣṭau śatāni dīkṣābhedo ayaṃ mālinītantre ।। saptatidhā śoddhṛgaṇastriṃśaddhā śodhya ekatattvādiḥ । sāṇḍaḥ ṣaḍadhvarūpastathetikartavyatā caturbhedā ।। dravyajñānamayī sā jananādivivarjitātha tadyuktā ।
pañcatriṃśaddhā punareṣā bhogāpavargasandhānāt ।। yasmāddvātriṃśaddhā bhogaḥ śubhaśuddhyaśuddhikālabhidā । mokṣastredhā dviguṇā saptatiritikāryatābhedāḥ ।। śodhanaśodhyavibhedāditikartavyatvabhedataścaiṣā ।
dīkṣā bahudhā bhinnā śodhyavihīnā tu saptatidhā ।। mantrāṇāṃ sakaletarasāṅganiraṅgādibhedasaṃkalanāt । śyodhyasya ca tattvādeḥ pañcadaśādyuktabhedaparigaṇanāt ।। bhedānāṃ parigaṇanā na śakyate kartumityasaṃkīrṇāḥ ।
bhedāḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ punaranye bhūyastvakāriṇo bahudhā ।। śodhakaśodhyādīnāṃ dvitrādivibhedasadbhāvāt । bhoge sādhye yadyadbahu kartavyaṃ tadāśrayenmatimān ।। kāraṇabhūyastvaṃ kila phalabhūyastvāya kiṃ citram ।
apavarge natu bhedastenāsminvāsanādṛḍhatvajuṣā ।। alpāpyāśrayaṇīyā kriyātha vijñānamātre vā । abhinavaguptaguruḥ punarāha hi sati vittadeśakālādau ।। apavarge api hi vistīrṇakarmavijñānasaṃgrahaḥ kāryaḥ ।
cidvṛttervaicitryāccāñcalye api krameṇa sandhānāt ।। tasmiṃstasminvastuni rūḍhiravaśyaṃ śivātmikā bhavati । tattvamidametadātmakametasmātproddhṛto mayā śiṣyaḥ ।। itthaṃ kramasaṃvittau mūḍho api śivātmako bhavati ।
kramikatathāvidhaśivatānugrahasubhagaṃ ca daiśikaṃ paśyan ।। śiśurapi tadabhedadṛśā bhaktibalāccābhyupaiti śivabhāvam । yadyapi vikalpavṛtterapi mokṣaṃ dīkṣayaiva dehānte ।। śāstre provāca vibhustathāpi dṛḍhavāsanā yuktā ।
mokṣe apyasti viśeṣaḥ kriyālpabhūyastvajaḥ salokādiḥ ।। iti kecittadayuktaṃ sa vicitro bhoga eva kathitaḥ syāt । saṃskāraśeṣavartanajīvitamadhye asya samayalopādyam ।। nāyāti vighnajālaṃ kriyābahutvaṃ mumukṣostat ।
yasmāt sabījadīkṣāsaṃskṛtapuruṣasya samayalopādye ।। bhukte bhogānmokṣo naivaṃ nirbījadīkṣāyām । iti kecinmanyante yuktaṃ taccāpi yatsmṛtaṃ śāstre ।। samayollaṅghanāddevi kravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ ।।
tasmāduruśiṣyamatau śivabhāvanirūḍhivitaraṇasamartham । kramikaṃ tattvoddharaṇādi karma mokṣe api yuktamativitatam ।। yastu sadā bhāvanayā svabhyastajñānavānguruḥ sa śiśoḥ । apavargāya yathecchaṃ yaṃ kaṃcidupāyamanutiṣṭhet ।।
evaṃ śiṣyatanau śodhyaṃ nyasyādhvānaṃ yathepsitam । śodhakaṃ mantramupari nyasyettattvānusārataḥ ।। dvayormātṛkayostattvasthityā varṇakramaḥ purā । kathitastaṃ tathā nyasyettattattattvaviśuddhaye ।।
varṇādhvā yadyapi proktaḥ śodhyaḥ pāśātmakastu saḥ । māyīyaḥ śodhakastvanyaḥ śivātmā paravāṅmayaḥ ।। uvāca sadyojyotiśca vṛttau svāyambhuvasya tat । bāḍhameko hi pāśātmā śabdo anyaśca śivātmakaḥ ।।
tasmāttasyaiva varṇasya yuktā śodhakaśodhyatā । śrīpūrvaśāstre cāpyuktaṃ te tairāliṅgitā iti ।। sadyojātādivaktrāṇi hṛdādyaṅgāni pañca ca । ṣaṭkṛtvo nyasya ṣaṭtriṃśannyāsaṃ kuryāddharāditaḥ ।।
parāparāyā vailomyāddharāyāṃ syātpadatrayam । tato jalādahaṅkāre pañcāṣṭakasamāśrayāt ।। padāni pañca dhīmūlapuṃrāgākhye traye trayam । ekaṃ tvaśuddhavitkāladvaye caikaṃ niyāmake ।।
kalāmāyādvaye caikaṃ padamuktamiha kramāt । vidyeśvarasadāśaktiśiveṣu padapañcakam ।। ekonaviṃśatiḥ seyaṃ padānāṃ syātparāparā । sārdhaṃ caikaṃ caikaṃ sārdhaṃ dve dve śaśī dṛgatha yugmam ।।
trāṇi dṛgabdhiścandraḥ śrutiḥ śaśī pañca vidhumahaścandrāḥ । ekānnaviṃśatau syādakṣarasaṃkhyā padeṣviyaṃ devyāḥ ।। haldvayayutavasucitraguparisaṃkhyātasvavarṇāyāḥ । mūlāntaṃ sārdhavarṇaṃ syānmāyāntaṃ varṇamekakam ।।
śaktyantamekamaparānyāse vidhirudīritaḥ । māyāntaṃ haltataḥ śaktiparyante svara ucyate ।। niṣkale śivatattve vai paro nyāsaḥ paroditaḥ । parāparāpadānyeva hyaghoryādyaṣṭakadvaye ।।
mantrāstadanusāreṇa tattveṣvetaddvayaṃ kṣipet । piṇḍākṣarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ varṇasaṃkhyā vibhedataḥ ।। avyaktāntaṃ svare nyasyā śeṣaṃ śeṣeṣu yojayet । bījāni sarvatattveṣu vyāptṛtvena prakalpayet ।।
piṇḍānāṃ bījavannyāsamanye tu pratipedire । akṛte vātha śodhyasya nyāse vastubalāt sthiteḥ ।। śodhakanyāsamātreṇa sarvaṃ śodhyaṃ viśudhyati । śrīmanmṛtyuñjayādau ca kathitaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।।
adhunā nyāsamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiḥ prajāyate । dehaśuddhyarthamapyetattulyametena vastutaḥ ।। anyaprakaraṇoktaṃ yadyuktaṃ prakaraṇāntare । jñāpakatvena sākṣādvā tatkiṃ nānyatra gṛhyate ।।
mālinīmātṛkāṅgasya nyāso yo arcāvidhau purā । proktaḥ kevalasaṃśoddhṛmantranyāse sa eva tu ।। tripadī dvayordvayoḥ syātpratyekamathāṣṭasu śrutipadāni । dikcandracandrarasaraviśaraśaradṛgdṛṅmṛgāṅkaśaśigaṇane ।।
aṅgulamāne devyā aṣṭādaśa vaibhavena padamanyat । aparaṃ mānamidaṃ syāt kevalaśodhakamanunyāse ।। turyapadātpadaṣaṭke mānadvitayaṃ parāparaparākhyam । dvādaśakaṃ dvādaśakaṃ tattvopari pūrvavattvanyat ।।
kevalaśodhakamantranyāsābhiprāyato mahādevaḥ । tattvakramoditamapi nyāsaṃ punarāha tadviruddhamapi ।। niṣkale padamekārṇaṃ yāvattrīṇi tu pārthive । ityādinā tattvagatakramanyāsa udīritaḥ ।।
punaśca mālinītantre vargavidyāvibhedataḥ । dvidhā padānītyuktvākhyannyāsamanyādṛśaṃ vibhuḥ ।। ekaikaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ jñeyaṃ tatra pūrvaṃ padatrayam । aṣṭāṅgulāni catvāri daśāṅgulamataḥ param ।।
dvyaṅgule dve pade cānye ṣaḍaṅgulamataḥ param । dvādaśāṅgulamanyacca dve anye pañcāṅgule pṛthak ।। padadvayaṃ catuṣparva tathānye dve dviparvaṇī । evaṃ parāparādevyāḥ svatantro nyāsa ucyate ।।
vidyādvayaṃ śiṣyatanau vyāptṛtvenaiva yojayet । iti darśayituṃ nāsya pṛthaṅnyāsaṃ nyarūpayat ।। evaṃ śodhakamantrasya nyāse tadraśmiyogataḥ । pāśajālaṃ vilīyeta taddhyānabalato guroḥ ।।
śodhyatattve samastānāṃ yonīnāṃ tulyakālataḥ । jananādbhogataḥ karmakṣaye syādapavṛktatā ।। dehaistāvadbhirasyāṇościtraṃ bhokturapi sphuṭam । mano anusandhirno viśvasaṃyogapravibhāgavat ।।
niyatyā manaso dehamātre vṛttistataḥ param । nānusandhā yataḥ saikasvāntayuktākṣakalpitā ।। pradeśavṛtti ca jñānamātmanastatra tatra tat । bhogyajñānaṃ nānyadeheṣvanusandhānamarhati ।।
yadā tu manasastasya dehavṛtterapi dhruvam । yogamantrakriyādeḥ syādvaimalyaṃ tadvidā tadā ।। yathāmalaṃ mano dūrasthitamapyāśu paśyati । tathā pratyayadīkṣāyāṃ tattadbhuvanadarśanam ।।
jananādiviyuktāṃ tu yadā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati । tadāsmāduddharāmīti yuktamūhaprakalpanam ।। yadā śodhyaṃ vinā śoddhṛnyāsastatrāpi mantrataḥ । jananādikramaṃ kuryāttattvasaṃśleṣavarjitam ।।
ekākiśoddhṛnyāse ca jananādivivarjane । tacchoddhṛsaṃpuṭaṃ nāma kevalaṃ parikalpayet ।। dravyayogena dīkṣāyāṃ tilājyākṣatataṇḍulam । tattanmantreṇa juhuyājjanmayogaviyogayoḥ ।।
yadā vijñānadīkṣāṃ tu kuryācchiṣyaṃ tadā bhṛśam । tanmantrasaṃjalpabalāt paśyedā cāvikalpakāt ।। vikalpaḥ kila saṃjalpamayo yatsa vimarśakaḥ । mantrātmāsau vimarśaśca śuddho apāśavatātmakaḥ ।।
nityaścānādivaradaśivābhedopakalpitaḥ । tadyogāddaiśikasyāpi vikalpaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet ।। śrīsāraśāstre tadidaṃ parameśena bhāṣitam । arthasya pratipattiryā grāhyagrāhakarūpiṇī ।।
sā eva mantraśaktistu vitatā mantrasantatau । parāmarśasvabhāvetthaṃ mantraśaktirudāhṛtā ।। parāmarśo dvidhā śuddhāśuddhatvānmantrabhedakaḥ । uktaṃ śrīpauṣkare anye ca brahmaviṣṇvādayo aṇḍagāḥ ।।
prādhānikāḥ sāñjanāste sāttvarājasatāmasāḥ । tairaśuddhaparāmarśāttanmayībhāvito guruḥ ।। vaiṣṇavādiḥ paśuḥ prokto na yogyaḥ patiśāsane । ye mantrāḥ śuddhamārgasthāḥ śivabhaṭṭārakādayaḥ ।।
śrīmanmataṅgādidṛśā tanmayo hi guruḥ śivaḥ । nanu svatantrasaṃjalpayogādastu vimarśitā ।। prākkutaḥ sa vimarśāccetkutaḥ so api nirūpaṇe । ādyastathāvikalpatvapradaḥ syādupadeṣṭṛtaḥ ।।
yaḥ saṃkrānto abhijalpaḥ syāttasyāpyanyopadeṣṭṛtaḥ । pūrvapūrvakramāditthaṃ ya evādiguroḥ purā ।। saṃjalpo hyabhisaṃkrāntaḥ so adyāpyastīti gṛhyatām । yastathāvidhasaṃjalpabalātko api svatantrakaḥ ।।
vimarśaḥ kalpyate so api tadātmaiva suniścitaḥ । ghaṭakumbha itītthaṃ vā yadi bhedo nirūpyate ।। so apyanyakalpanādāyī hyanādṛtyaḥ prayatnataḥ । paṇāyate karotīti vikalpasyocitau sphuṭam ।।
karapāṇyabhijalpau tau saṃkīryetāṃ kathaṃ kila । śabdācchabdāntare tena vyutpattirvyavadhānataḥ ।। vyavahārāttu sā sākṣāccitropākhyāvimarśinī । tadvimarśodayaḥ prācyasvavimarśamayaḥ sphuret ।।
yāvadbālasya saṃvittirakṛtrimavimarśane । tena tanmantraśabdārthaviśeṣotthaṃ vikalpanam ।। śabdāntarotthādbhedena paśyatā mantra ādṛtaḥ । yaccāpi bījapiṇḍāderuktaṃ prāgbodharūpakam ।।
tattasyaiva kuto anyasya tatkasmādanyakalpanā । etadarthaṃ guroryatnāllakṣaṇe tatra tatra tat ।। lakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ hyeṣa mantratantraviśāradaḥ । tena mantrārthasaṃbodhe mantravārtikamādarāt ।।
ūhāpohaprayogaṃ vā sarvathā gururācaret । mantrārthavidabhāve tu sarvathā mantratanmayam ।। guruṃ kuryāt tadabhyāsāttatsaṃkalpamayo hyasau । tatsamānābhisaṃjalpo yadā mantrārthabhāvanāt ।।
gurorbhavettadā sarvasāmye ko bheda ucyatām । aṃśenāpyatha vaiṣamye na tato arthakriyā hi sā ।। gomayātkīṭataḥ kīṭa ityevaṃ nyāyato yadā । saṃjalpāntarato apyarthakriyāṃ tāmeva paśyati ।।
tadaiṣa satyasaṃjalpaḥ śiva eveti kathyate । sa yadvakti tadeva syānmantro bhogāpavargadaḥ ।। naiṣo abhinavaguptasya pakṣo mantrārpitātmanaḥ । yo arthakriyāmāha bhinnāṃ kīṭayorapi tādṛśoḥ ।।
mantrārpitamanāḥ kiṃcidvadanyattu viṣaṃ haret । tanmantra eva śabdaḥ sa paraṃ tatra ghaṭādivat ।। kāntāsaṃbhogasaṃjalpasundaraḥ kāmukaḥ sadā । tatsaṃskṛto apyanyadeṣa kurvansvātmani tṛpyati ।।
tathā tanmantrasaṃjalpabhāvito anyadapi bruvan । anicchurapi tadrūpastathā kāryakaro dhruvam ।। vikalpayannapyekārthaṃ yato anyadapi paśyati । viṣāpahārimantrādītyuktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāsane ।।
yadi vā viṣanāśe api hetubhedādvicitratā । dhātvāpyāyādikānantakāryabhedādbhaviṣyati ।। tadevaṃ mantrasaṃjalpavikalpābhyāsayogataḥ । bhāvyavastusphuṭībhāvaḥ saṃjalpahrāsayogataḥ ।।
vastveva bhāvayatyeṣa na saṃjalpamimaṃ punaḥ । gṛhṇāti bhāsanopāyaṃ bhāte tatra tu tena kim ।। evaṃ saṃjalpanirhrāse suparisphuṭatātmakam । akṛttrimavimarśātma sphuredvastvavikalpakam ।।
nirvikalpā ca sā saṃvidyadyathā paśyati sphuṭam । tattathaiva tathātmatvādvastuno api bahiḥsthiteḥ ।। viśeṣatastvamāyīyaśivatābhedaśālinaḥ । mokṣe abhyupāyaḥ saṃjalpo bandhamokṣau tataḥ kila ।।
vikalpe api guroḥ samyagabhinnaśivatājuṣaḥ । avikalpakaparyantapratīkṣā nopayujyate ।। tadvimarśasvabhāvā hi sā vācyā mantradevatā । mahāsaṃvitsamāsannetyuktaṃ śrīgamaśāsane ।।
nikaṭasthā yathā rājñāmanyeṣāṃ sādhayantyalam । siddhiṃ rājopagāṃ śīghramevaṃ mantrādayaḥ parām ।। uktābhiprāyagarbhaṃ taduktaṃ śrīmālinīmate । mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kasmādityukte munibhiḥ kila ।।
yogamekatvamicchanti vastuno anyena vastunā । tadvastu jñeyamityuktaṃ heyatvādiprasiddhaye ।। tatprasiddhyai śivenoktaṃ jñānaṃ yadupavarṇitam । sabījayogasaṃsiddhyai mantralakṣaṇamapyalam ।।
na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yoge asti śāṅkare । kriyājñānavibhedena sā ca dvedhā nigadyate ।। dvividhā sā prakartavyā tena caitadudāhṛtam । naca yogādhikāritvamekamevānayā bhavet ।।
api mantrādhikāritvaṃ muktiśca śivadīkṣayā । anenaitadapi proktaṃ yogī tattvaikyasiddhaye ।। mantramevāśrayenmūlaṃ nirvikalpāntamādṛtaḥ । mantrābhyāsena bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vāpi prasādhayan ।।
tatrādhikāritālabdhyai dīkṣāṃ gṛhṇīta daiśikāt । tena mantrajñānayogabalādyadyatprasādhayet ।। tatsyādasyānyatattve api yuktasya guruṇā śiśoḥ । dīkṣā hyasyopayujyeta saṃskriyāyāṃ sa saṃskṛtaḥ ।।
svabalenaiva bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vā labhate budhaḥ । tena vijñānayogādibalī prāk samayī bhavan ।। putrako vā na tāvānsyādapitu svabalocitaḥ । yastu vijñānayogādivandhyaḥ so andho yathā pathi ।।
daiśikāyatta eva syādbhoge muktau ca sarvathā । dīkṣā ca kevalā jñānaṃ vināpi nijamāntaram ।। mocikaiveti kathitaṃ yuktyā cāgamataḥ purā । yastu dīkṣākṛtāmevāpekṣya yojanikāṃ śiśuḥ ।।
sphuṭībhūtyai taducitaṃ jñānaṃ yogamathāśritaḥ । so api yatraiva yuktaḥ syāttanmayatvaṃ prapadyate ।। gurudīkṣāmantraśāstrādhīnasarvasthitistataḥ । duṣṭānāmeva sarveṣāṃ bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyatām ।।
karmaṇāṃ śodhanaṃ kāryaṃ bubhukṣorna śubhātmanām । yaḥ punarlaukikaṃ bhogaṃ rājyasvargādikaṃ śiśuḥ ।। tyaktvā lokottaraṃ bhogamīpsustasya śubheṣvapi । tatra dravyamayīṃ dīkṣāṃ kurvannājyatilādikaiḥ ।।
karmāsya śodhayāmīti juhuyāddaiśikottamaḥ । jñānamayyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ tadviśuddhyati sandhitaḥ ।। guroḥ svasaṃvidrūḍhasya balāttatprakṣayo bhavet । yadāsyāśubhakarmāṇi śuddhāni syustadā śubham ।।
svatāratamyāśrayaṇādadhvamadhye prasūtidam । śubhapākakramopāttaphalabhogasamāptitaḥ ।। yatraiṣa yojitastatstho bhāvikarmakṣaye kṛte । bhāvināṃ cādyadehasthadehāntaravibhedinām ।।
aśubhāṃśaviśuddhau syādbhogasyaivānupakṣayaḥ । bhuñjānasyāsya satataṃ bhogānmāyālayāntataḥ ।। na duḥkhaphaladaṃ dehādyadhvamadhye api kiṃcana । tato māyālaye bhuktasamastasukhabhogakaḥ ।।
niṣkale sakale vaiti layaṃ yojanikābalāt । iti prameyaṃ kathitaṃ dīkṣā kāle guroryathā ।। atha bhairavatādātmyadāyinīṃ prakriyāṃ bruve । evaṃ maṇḍalakumbhāgniśiṣyasvātmasu pañcasu ।।
gṛhītvā vyāptimaikyena nyasyādhvānaṃ ca śiṣyagam । karmamāyāṇumalinatrayaṃ bāhau gale tathā ।। śikhāyāṃ ca kṣipetsūtragranthiyogena daiśikaḥ । tasyātadrūpatābhānaṃ malo granthiḥ sa kīrtyate ।।
itipratītidārḍhyārthaṃ bahirgranthyupakalpanam । bāhū karmāspadaṃ viṣṇurmāyātmā galasaṃśritaḥ ।। adhovahā śikhāṇutvaṃ tenetthaṃ kalpanā kṛtā । naraśaktiśivākhyasya trayasya bahubhedatām ।।
vaktuṃ tristriguṇaṃ sūtraṃ granthaye parikalpayet । tejojalānnatritayaṃ tredhā pratyekamapyadaḥ ।। śrutyante ke apyataḥ śuklakṛṣṇaraktaṃ prapedire । tato agnau tarpitāśeṣamantre cidvyomamātrake ।।
sāmānyarūpe tattvānāṃ kramācchuddhiṃ samācaret । tatra svamantrayogena dharāmāvāhayetpurā ।। iṣṭvā puṣpādibhiḥ sarpistilādyairatha tarpayet । tattattvavyāpikāṃ paścānmāyātattvādhidevatām ।।
māyāśaktiṃ svamantreṇāvāhyābhyarcya pratarpayet । āvāhane mātṛkārṇaṃ mālinyarṇaṃ ca pūjane ।। kuryāditi guruḥ prāha svarūpāpyāyanadvayāt । tāro varṇo atha saṃbuddhipadaṃ tvāmityataḥ param ।।
uttamaikayutaṃ karmapadaṃ dīpakamapyataḥ । tabhyaṃ nāma caturthyantaṃ tato apyucitadīpakam ।। ityūhamantrayogena tattatkarma pravartayet । āvāhanānantaraṃ hi karma sarvaṃ nigadyate ।।
āvāhanaṃ ca saṃbodhaḥ svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ । bhāvasyāhaṃmayasvātmatādātmyāveśyamānatā ।। śāktī bhūmiśca saivoktā yasyāṃ mukhyāsti pūjyatā । abhātatvādabhedācca nahyasau nṛśivātmanoḥ ।।
jaḍābhāseṣu tattveṣu saṃvitsthityai tato guruḥ । āvāhanavibhaktiṃ prāk kṛtvā turyavibhaktitaḥ ।। namaskārāntatāyogātpūrṇāṃ sattāṃ prakalpayet । tataḥ pūrṇasvabhāvatvaṃ tadrūpodrekayogataḥ ।।
dhyeyodreko bhaveddhyātṛprahvībhāvavaśādyataḥ । āvāhyeṣṭvā pratarpyeti śrīsvacchande nirūpitam ।। anenaiva pathāneyamityasmadguravo jaguḥ । paratvena tu yatpūjyaṃ tatsvatantracidātmakam ।।
anavacchitprakāśatvānna prakāśyaṃ tu kutracit । tasya hyetatprapūjyatvadhyeyatvādi yadullaset ।। tasyaiva tatsvatantratvaṃ yātidurghaṭakāritā । saṃbodharūpe tattasmin kathaṃ saṃbodhanā bhavet ।।
prakāśanāyāṃ na syātprakāśasya prakāśatā । saṃbodhanavibhaktyaiva vinā karmādiśaktitām ।। svātantryāttaṃ darśayituṃ tatrohamimamācaret । devamāvāhayāmīti tato devāya dīpakam ।।
prāgyuktyā pūrṇatādāyi namaḥsvāhādikaṃ bhavet । nutiḥ pūrṇatvamagnīndusaṃghaṭṭāpyāyatā param ।। āpyāyakaṃ ca procchālaṃ vauṣaḍādi pradīpayet । tatra bāhye api tādātmyaprasiddhaṃ karma codyate ।।
yadi karmapadaṃ tanno gururabhyūhayetkvacit । anābhāsitatadvastubhāsanāya niyujyate ।। mantraḥ kiṃ tena tatra syātsphuṭaṃ yatrāvabhāsi tat । tena prokṣaṇasaṃsekajapādividhiṣu dhruvam ।।
tatkarmābhyūhanaṃ kuryātpratyuta vyavadhātṛtām । bahistathātmatābhāve kāryaṃ karmapadohanam ।। tṛptāvāhutihutabhukpāśaploṣacchidādiṣu । yatroddiṣṭe vidhau paścāttadanantaiḥ kriyātmakaiḥ ।।
aṃśaiḥ sādhyaṃ na tatroho dīkṣaṇādividhiṣviva । tataḥ śiṣyasya tattattvasthāne astreṇa pratāḍanam ।। kṛtvātha śivahastena hṛdayaṃ parimarśayet । tataḥ svanāḍīmārgeṇa hṛdayaṃ prāpya vai śiśoḥ ।।
śiṣyātmanā sahaikatvaṃ gatvādāya ca taṃ hṛdā । puṭitaṃ haṃsarūpākhyaṃ tatra saṃhāramudrayā ।। kuryādātmīyahṛdayasthitamapyavabhāsakam । śiṣyadehasya tejobhī raśmimātrāviyogataḥ ।।
svabandhasthānacalanāt svatantrasthānalābhataḥ । svakarmāparatantratvātsarvatrotpattimarhati ।। tenātmahṛdayānītaṃ prākkṛtvā pudgalaṃ tataḥ । māyāyāṃ taddharātattvaśarīrāṇyasya saṃsṛjet ।।
tatrāsya garbhādhānaṃ ca yuktaṃ puṃsavanādibhiḥ । garbhaniṣkrāmaparyantairekāṃ kurvīta saṃskriyām ।। jananaṃ bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ militvaikātha saṃskriyā । tato asya teṣu bhogeṣu kuryāttanmayatāṃ layam ।।
tatastattattvapāśānāṃ vicchedaṃ samupācaret । saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣke asminnaparāṃ ca parāparām ।। mantrāṇāṃ pañcadaśakaṃ parāṃ vā yojayetkramāt । pivanyādyaṣṭakaṃ śastrādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ parā tathā ।।
iti pañcadaśaite syuḥ kramāllīnatvasaṃskṛtau । aparāmantramuktvā prāgamukātmana ityatha ।। garbhādhānaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca । svāhāntamuccarandadyādāhutitritayaṃ guruḥ ।।
paraṃ parāparāmantramamukātmana ityatha । jātasya bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ karomyatha parāparām ।। ante svāheti proccārya vitarettisra āhutīḥ । uccārya pivanīmantramamukātmana ityatha ।।
bhoge layaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca । svāhāntamāhutīstisro dadyādājyatilādibhiḥ ।। eṣa eva vamanyādau vidhiḥ pañcadaśāntake । pūrvaṃ parātmakaṃ mantramamukātmana ityatha ।।
pāśācchedaṃ karomīti parāmantraḥ punastataḥ । huṃ svāhā phaṭ samuccārya dadyāttisro apyathāhutīḥ ।। saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣke asminye mantrāḥ kathitā mayā । teṣu karmapadātpūrvaṃ dharātattvapadaṃ vadet ।।
tato dharātattvapatimāmantryeṣṭvā pratarpya ca । śivābhimānasaṃrabdho gururevaṃ samādiśet ।। tattveśvara tvayā nāsya putrakasya śivājñayā । pratibandhaḥ prakartavyo yātuḥ padamanāmayam ।।
tato yadi samīheta dharātattvāntarālagam । pṛthak śodhayituṃ mantrī bhuvanādyadhvapañcakam ।। aparāmantrataḥ prāgvattisrastisrastadāhutīḥ । dadyātpuraṃ śodhayāmītyūhayuktaṃ prasannadhīḥ ।।
evaṃ kalāmantrapadavarṇeṣvapi vicakṣaṇaḥ । tisrastisro hutīrdadyāt pṛthak sāmastyato apivā ।। tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā parayā vauṣaḍantayā । aparāmantrataḥ śiṣyamuddhṛtyātmahṛdaṃ nayet ।।
yadā tvekena śuddhena tadantarbhāvacintanāt । na pṛthak śodhayettattvanāthasaṃśravaṇātparam ।। tadā pūrṇāṃ vitīryāṇumutkṣipyātmani yojayet । tātsthyātmasaṃsthyayogāya tayaivāparayāhutīḥ ।।
sakarmapadayā dadyāditi kecittu manvate । anye tu guravaḥ prāhurbhāvanāmayamīdṛśam ।। nātra bāhyāhutirdeyā daiśikasya pṛthak punaḥ । dadyādvā yadi no doṣaḥ syādupāyaḥ sa bhāvane ।।
evaṃ prāktanatātsthyātmasaṃsthatve yojayedguruḥ । tataḥ śiṣyahṛdaṃ neyaḥ sa ātmā tāvato adhvanaḥ ।। śuddhastaddārḍhyasiddhyai ca pūrṇā syātparayā punaḥ । mahāpāśupataṃ pūrvaṃ vilomasya viśuddhaye ।।
juhomi punarastreṇa vauṣaḍanta iti kṣipet । punaḥ pūrṇāṃ tato māyāmabhyarcyātha visarjayet ।। dharātattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ sajjalena śuddharūpiṇā । bhāvayenmiśritaṃ vāri śuddhiyogyaṃ tato bhavet ।।
tathā tattatpurātattvamiśraṇāduttarottaram । sarvā śivībhavettattvāvalī śuddhānyathā pṛthak ।। pṛthaktvaṃ ca malo māyābhidhānastasya saṃbhave । karmakṣaye api no muktirbhavedvidyeśvarādivat ।।
tato api jalatattvasya vahnau vyomni cidātmake । āhvānādyakhilaṃ yāvattejasyasya vimaśraṇam ।। evaṃ kramātkalātattve śuddhe pāśaṃ bhujāśritam । chindyātkalā hi sā kiṃcitkartṛtvonmīlanātmikā ।।
karmākhyamalajṛmbhātmā taṃ ca granthiṃ srugagragam । pūrṇāhutyā samaṃ vahnimantratejasi nirdahet ।। mantro hi viśvarūpaḥ sannupāśrayavaśāttathā । vyaktarūpastato vahnau pāśaploṣavidhāyakaḥ ।।
pluṣṭo līnasvabhāvo asau pāśastaṃ prati śambhuvat । parameśamahātejaḥśeṣamātratvamaśnute ।। karmapāśe atra hotavye pūrṇayāsya śubhāśubham । aśubhaṃ vā bhavadbhūtaṃ bhāvi vātha samastakam ।।
dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ vinikṣipet । evaṃ māyāntasaṃśuddhau kaṇṭhapāśaṃ ca homayet ।। pūrṇasya tasya māyākhyaṃ pāśabhedaprathātmakam । dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ kṣipedguruḥ ।।
nirbījā yadi kāryā tu tadātraivāparāṃ kṣipet । pūrṇāṃ samayapāśākhyabījadāhapadānvitām ।। gurau deve tathā śāstre bhaktiḥ kāryāsya nahyasau । samayaḥ śaktipātasya svabhāvo hyeṣa no pṛthak ।।
māyānte śuddhimāyāte vāgīśī yā purābhavat । māyā śaktimayī saiva vidyāśaktitvamaśnute ।। tacchuddhavidyāmāhūya vidyāśaktiṃ niyojayet । evaṃ krameṇa saṃśuddhe sadāśivapade apyalam ।।
śikhāṃ granthiyutāṃ chittvā malamāṇavakaṃ dahet । yato adhikārabhogākhyau dvau pāśau tu sadāśive ।। ityuktyāṇavapāśo atra māyīyastu niśāvadhiḥ । śiṣyo yathocitaṃ snāyādācāmeddaiśikaḥ svayam ।।
āṇavākhye vinirdagdhe hyadhovāhiśikhāmale । tataḥ prāguktasakalaprameyaṃ paricintayan ।। śiṣyadehādimātmīyadehaprāṇādiyojitam । kṛtvātmadehaprāṇāderviśvamantaranusmaret ।।
uktaprakriyayā caivaṃ dṛḍhabuddhirananyadhīḥ । prāṇasthaṃ deśakālādhvayugaṃ prāṇaṃ ca śaktigam ।। tāṃ ca saṃvidgatāṃ śuddhāṃ saṃvidaṃ śivarūpiṇīm । śiṣyasaṃvidabhinnāṃ ca mantravahnyādyabhedinīm ।।
dhyāyan prāgvatprayogeṇa śivaṃ sakalaniṣkalam । dvyātmakaṃ vā kṣipetpūrṇāṃ praśāntakaraṇena tu ।। uktaṃ traiśirase tantre sarvasaṃpūraṇātmakam । mūlādudayagatyā tu śivenduparisaṃplutam ।।
janmāntamadhyakuharamūlasrotaḥsamutthitam । śivārkaraśmibhistīvraiḥ kṣubdhaṃ jñānāmṛtaṃ tu yat ।। tena saṃtarpayetsamyak praśāntakaraṇena tu । śūnyadhāmābjamadhyasthaprabhākiraṇabhāsvaraḥ ।।
ādheyādhāraniḥspandabodhaśāstraparigrahaḥ । janmādheyaprapañcaikasphoṭasaṃghaṭṭaghaṭṭanaḥ ।। mūlasthānātsamārabhya kṛtvā someśamantagam । khamivātiṣṭhate yāvatpraśāntaṃ tāvaducyate ।।
uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca srucamāpūrya sarpiṣā । kṛtvā śiṣyaṃ tathātmasthaṃ mūlamantramanusmaran ।। śivaṃ śaktiṃ tathātmānaṃ śiṣyaṃ sarpistathānalam । ekīkurvañchanairgaccheddvādaśāntamananyadhīḥ ।।
tatra kumbhakamāsthāya dhyāyansakalaniṣkalam । tiṣṭhettāvadanudvigno yāvadājyakṣayo bhvet ।। evaṃ yuktaḥ pare tattve guruṇā śivamūrtinā । na bhūyaḥ paśutāmeti dagdhamāyānibandhanaḥ ।।
dehapāte punaḥ prepsedyadi tattveṣu kutracit । bhogān samastavyastatvabhedairante paraṃ padam ।। tadā tattattvabhūmau tu tatsaṃkhyāyāmananyadhīḥ । punaryojanikāṃ kuryātpūrṇāhutyantareṇa tu ।।
muktipradā bhogamokṣapradā vā yā prakīrtitā । dīkṣā sā syātsabījatvanirbījātmatayā dvidhā ।। bāle nirjñātamaraṇe tvaśakte vā jarādibhiḥ । kāryā nirbījikā dīkṣā śaktipātabalodaye ।।
nirbījāyāṃ sāmayāṃstu pāśānapi viśodhayet । kṛtanirbījadīkṣastu devāgnigurubhaktibhāk ।। iyataiva śivaṃ yāyāt sadyo bhogān vibhujya vā । śrīmaddīkṣottare coktaṃ cāre ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule ।।
tattvānyāpādamūrdhāntaṃ bhuvanāni tyajetkramāt । tuṭimātraṃ niṣkalaṃ tadadehaṃ tadahaṃparam ।। śaktyā tatra kṣipāmyenamiti dhyāyaṃstu dīkṣayet । sabījāyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ samayānna viśodhayet ।।
viśeṣastvayametasyāṃ yāvajjīvaṃ śiśorguruḥ । śeṣavṛttyai śuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ kurvīta pūrṇayā ।। abhinnācchivasaṃbodhajaladheryugapatsphurat । pūrṇāṃ kṣipaṃstattvajālaṃ dhyāyedbhārūpakaṃ sṛtam ।।
viśuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ vā kuryātkumbhābhiṣecanāt । tathā dhyānabalādeva yadvā pūrṇābhiṣecanaiḥ ।। pṛthivī sthirarūpāsya śivarūpeṇa bhāvitā । sthirīkaroti tāmeva bhāvanāmiti śuddhyati ।।
jalamāpyāyayatyenāṃ tejo bhāsvaratāṃ nayet । marudānandasaṃsparśaṃ vyoma vaitatyamāvahet ।। evaṃ tanmātravargo api śivatāmaya iṣyate । parānandamahāvyāptiraśeṣamalavicyutiḥ ।।
śive gantṛtvamādānamupādeyaśivastutiḥ । śivāmodabharāsvādadarśanasparśanānyalam ।। tadākarṇanamityevamindriyāṇāṃ viśuddhatā । saṃkalpādhyavasāmānāḥ prakāśo raktisaṃsthitī ।।
śivātmatvena yatseyaṃ śuddhatā mānasādike । niyamo rañjanaṃ kartṛbhāvaḥ kalanayā saha ।। vedanaṃ heyavastvaṃśaviṣaye suptakalpatā । itthaṃ śivaikyarūḍhasya ṣaṭkañcukagaṇo apyayam ।।
śuddha eva pumān prāptaśivabhāvo viśuddhyati । vidyeśādiṣu tattveṣu naiva kācidaśuddhatā ।। ityevaṃ śuddhatattvānāṃ sṛṣṭyā śiṣyo api tanmayaḥ । bhaveddhyetatsūcitaṃ śrīmālinīvijayottare ।।
bandhamokṣāvubhāvetāvindriyāṇi jagurbudhāḥ । nigṛhītāni bandhāya vimuktāni vimuktaye ।। etāni vyāpake bhāve yadā syurmanasā saha । muktāni kvāpi viṣaye rodhādbandhāya tāni tu ।।
ityevaṃ dvividho bhāvaḥ śuddhāśuddhaprabhedataḥ । indriyāṇāṃ samākhyātaḥ siddhayogīśvare mate ।। śrīmān vidyāgurustvāha pramāṇastutidarśane । samastamantrairdīkṣāyāṃ niyamastveṣa kathyate ।।
māyāntaśuddhau sarvāḥ syuḥ kriyā hyaparayā sadā । dvyātmayā sakalānte tu niṣkale parayaiva tu ।। īśānte ca pivanyādi sakalānte aṅgapañcakam । ityevaṃvidhimālocya karma kuryādgurūttamaḥ ।।
purādhvani hutīnāṃ yā saṃkhyeyaṃ tattvavarṇayoḥ । tāmeva dviguṇīkuryātpadādhvani caturguṇām ।। kramānmantrakalāmārge dviguṇā dviguṇā kramāt । yāvattritattvasaṃśuddhau syādviṃśatiguṇā tataḥ ।।
pratikarma bhavetṣaṣṭirāhutīnāṃ tritattvake । ekatattve śataṃ prāhurāhutīnāṃ tu sāṣṭakam ।। vilomakarmaṇā sākaṃ yāḥ pūrṇāhutayaḥ smṛtāḥ । tāsāṃ sarvādhvasaṃśuddhau saṃkhyānyatvaṃ na kiṃcana ।।
ityeṣā kathitā dīkṣā jananādisamanvitā ।। atha saṃkṣiptadīkṣeyaṃ śivatāpattidocyate । na rajo nādhivāso atra na bhūkṣetraparigrahaḥ । yatra tatra pradeśe tu pūjayitvā guruḥ śivam ।।
adhvānaṃ manasā dhyātvā dīkṣayettattvapāragaḥ । jananādivihīnāṃ tu yena yenādhvanā guruḥ ।। kuryātsa ekatattvāntāṃ śivabhāvaikabhāvitaḥ । parāmantrastato asyeti tattvaṃ saṃśodhayāmyatha ।।
svāheti pratitattvaṃ syācchuddhe pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet । evaṃ mantrāntaraiḥ kuryātsamastairathavoktavat ।। parāsaṃpuṭitaṃ nāma svāhāntaṃ prathamāntakam । śataṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭaṃ vā tena śaktyaiva homayet ।।
tataḥ pūrṇeti saṃśodhyahīnamuttamamīdṛśam । dīkṣākarmoditaṃ tatra tatra śāstre maheśinā ।। pratyekaṃ mātṛkāyugmavarṇaistattvāni śodhayet । yadi vā piṇḍamantreṇa sarvamantreṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।
yathā yathā ca svabhyastajñānastanmayatātmakaḥ । gurustathā tathā kuryāt saṃkṣiptaṃ karma nānyathā ।। śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ saṃkṣipte api hi bhāvayet । vyāptiṃ sarvādhvasāmānyāṃ kiṃtu yāge na vistaraḥ ।।
atanmayībhūtamiti vikṣiptaṃ karma sandadhat । kramāttādātmyametīti vikṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret ।। saṃkṣipto vidhirukto ayaṃ kṛpayā yaḥ śivoditaḥ । dīkṣottare kairaṇe ca tatra tatrāpi śāsane ।।
atha sadyaḥsamutkrāntipradā dīkṣā nirūpyate । tatkṣaṇāccopabhogādvā dehapāte śivaṃ vrajet । ityuktyā mālinīśāstre sūcitāsau maheśinā ।। dehapāte samīpasthe śaktipātasphuṭatvataḥ ।
āsādya śāṃkarīṃ dīkṣāṃ tasmāddīkṣākṣaṇātparam ।। śivaṃ vrajedityartho atra pūrvāparavivecanāt । vyākhyātaḥ śrīmatāsmākaṃ guruṇā śambhumūrtinā ।। yadā hyāsannamaraṇe śaktipātaḥ prajāyate ।
tatra mande atha gurvādisevayāyuḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet ।। athavā bandhumitrādidvārā sāsya vibhoḥ patet । pūrvaṃ vā samayī naiva parāṃ dīkṣāmavāptavān ।। āptadīkṣo api vā prāṇāñjihāsuḥ kleśavarjitam ।
antyāngurustadā kuryātsadya utkrāntidīkṣaṇam ।। natvapakvamale nāpi śeṣakārmikavigrahe । kuryādutkramaṇaṃ śrīmadgahvare ca nirūpitam ।। dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam ।
utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet ।। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve kāmacāravidhānataḥ । pūrvoktamarthajātaṃ śrīśambhunātra nirūpitam ।। vidhiṃ pūrvoditaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā samayaśuddhitaḥ ।
kṣurikāmasya vinyasyejjvalantīṃ marmakartarīm ।। kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ nyāsaṃ kālānalasamaprabham । saṃhṛtikramataḥ sārdhaṃ sṛkchindiyugalena tu ।। āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ kṛtvā sarvamarmapratāpanīm ।
pūrayedvāyunā dehamaṅguṣṭhānmastakāntakam ।। tamutkṛṣya tato aṅguṣṭhādūrdhvāntaṃ vakṣyamāṇayā । kṛntenmarmāṇi randhrāntāt kālarātryā visarjayet ।। anena kramayogena yojito hutivarjitaḥ ।
samayyapyeti tāṃ dīkṣāmiti śrīmālinīmate ।। ṣoḍaśādhāraṣaṭcakralakṣyatrayakhapañcakāt । kvacidanyataratrātha prāguktapaśukarmavat ।। praviśya mūlaṃ kandādeśchindannaikyavibhāvanāt ।
pūrṇāhutiprayogeṇa sveṣṭe dhāmni niyojayet ।। jñānatriśūlaṃ saṃdīptaṃ dīptacakratrayojjvalam । cintayitvāmunā tasya vedanaṃ bodhanaṃ bhramam ।। dīpanaṃ tāḍanaṃ todaṃ calanaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।
kandādicakragaṃ kuryādviśeṣeṇa hṛdambuje ।। dvādaśānte tataḥ kṛtvā binduyugmagate kṣipet । nirlakṣye vā pare dhāmni saṃyuktaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। na tasya kuryātsaṃskāraṃ kaṃcidityāha gahvare ।
devaḥ kimasya pūrṇasya śrāddhādyairiti bhāvitaḥ ।। śrīmaddīkṣottare tveṣa vidhirvahnipuṭīkṛtaḥ । haṃsaḥ pumānadhastasya rudrabindusamanvitaḥ ।। śiṣyadehe niyojyaitadanudvagnaḥ śataṃ japet ।
utkramyordhvanimeṣeṇa śiṣya itthaṃ paraṃ vrajet ।। eṣa eva vidhiḥ śrīmatsiddhayogīśvarīmate । iyamutkrāmaṇī dīkṣā kartavyā yogino guroḥ ।। anabhyastaprāṇacāraḥ kathamenāṃ kariṣyati ।
vakṣyamāṇāṃ brahmavidyāṃ sakalāṃ niṣkalombhitām ।। karṇe asya vā paṭhedbhūyo bhūyo vāpyatha pāṭhayet । svayaṃ ca karma kurvīta tattvaśuddhyādikaṃ guruḥ ।। mantrakriyābalātpūrṇāhutyetthaṃ yojayetpare ।
yogābhyāsamakṛtvāpi sadya utkrāntidāṃ guruḥ ।। jñānamantrakriyādhyānabalātkartuṃ bhavetprabhuḥ । anayotkramyate śiṣyo balādevaikakaṃ kṣaṇam ।। kālasyollaṅghya bhogo hi kṣaṇiko asyāstu kiṃ tataḥ ।
sadya utkrāntidā cānyā yasyāṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ tadā ।। dadyādyadāsya prāṇāḥ syurdhruvaṃ niṣkramaṇecchavaḥ । vināpi kriyayā bhāvibrahmavidyābalādguruḥ ।। karṇajāpaprayogeṇa tattvakañcukajālataḥ ।
niḥsārayanyathābhīṣṭe sakale niṣkale dvaye ।। tattve vā yatra kutrāpi yojayetpudgalaṃ kramāt । samayī putrako vāpi paṭhedvidyāmimāṃ tathā ।। tatpāṭhāttu samayyuktāṃ rudrāṃśāpattimaśnute ।
etau jape cādhyayane yasmādadhikṛtāvubhau ।। nādhyāpanopadeśe vā sa eṣo adhyayanādṛte । paṭhatostvanayorvastusvabhāvāttasya sā gatiḥ ।। yathā niṣiddhabhūtādikarmā mantraṃ smaransvayam ।
āviṣṭe api kvacinnaiti lopaṃ kartṛtvavarjanāt ।। yathā ca vācayañśāstraṃ samayī śūnyaveśmani । na lupyate tadantaḥsthaprāṇivargopakārataḥ ।। tathā svayaṃ paṭhanneṣa vidyāṃ vastusvabhāvataḥ ।
tasminmukte na lupyeta yato kiṃcitkaro atra saḥ ।। nanu cādīkṣitāgre sa noccarecchāstrapaddhatim ।। hanta kuḍyāgrato apyasya niṣedhastvatha kathyate । paryudāsena yaḥ śrotumavadhārayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।।
sa evātra niṣiddho no kuḍyakīṭapatatriṇaḥ । tarhi pāṣāṇatulyo asau vilīnendriyavṛttikaḥ ।। tasyāgre paṭhatastasya niṣedhollaṅghanā katham । sa tu vastusvabhāvena galitākṣo api budhyate ।।
akṣānapekṣayaivāntaścicchaktyā svaprakāśayā । prāgdehaṃ kila tityakṣurnottaraṃ cādhitaṣṭhivān ।। madhye prabodhakabalāt pratibudhyet pudgalaḥ । mantrāḥ śabdamayāḥ śuddhavimarśātmatayā svayam ।।
arthātmanā cāvabhāntastadarthapratibodhakāḥ । tenāsya galitākṣasya prabodho jāyate svayam ।। svacitsamānajātīyamantrāmarśanasaṃnidheḥ । yathā hyalpajavo vāyuḥ sajātīyavimiśritaḥ ।।
javī tathātmā saṃsuptāmarśo apyevaṃ prabudhyate । prabuddhaḥ sa ca saṃjāto na cādīkṣita ucyate ।। dīkṣā hi nāma saṃskāro na tvanyatso asti cāsya hi । ata eva nijaṃ śāstraṃ paṭhati kvāpi sāmaye ।।
tacchrutvā ko api dhanyaścenmucyate nāsya sā kṣatiḥ । śāstranindāṃ maiṣa kārṣīddvayoḥ pātityadāyinīm ।। ityevaṃparametannādīkṣitāgre paṭhediti । yathā ca samayī kāṣṭhe loṣṭe vā mantrayojanām ।।
kurvaṃstasmiṃścalatyeti na lopaṃ tadvadatra hi । yato asya pratyayaprāptiprepsoḥ samayinastathā ।। pravṛttasya svabhāvena tasminmukte na vai kṣatiḥ । sādhakastu sadā sādhye phale niyatiyantraṇāt ।।
makṣikāśrutamantro api prāyaścittaucitīṃ caret । itthaṃ sadyaḥsamutkrāntiryoktā tāmājñayā guroḥ ।। samayyādirapi proktakāle proktārthasiddhaye । svayaṃ kuryātsamabhyastaprāṇacāragamāgamaḥ ।।
akṛtādhikṛtirvāpi guruḥ samayaśuddhaye । adhastanapadāvastho natu jñāneddhacetanaḥ ।। itīyaṃ sadya utkrāntiḥ sūcitā mālinīmate । svayaṃ vā guruṇā vātha kāryatvena maheśinā ।।
sarvaṃ bhogaṃ virūpaṃ tu matvā dehaṃ tyajedyadi । tadā tena krameṇāśu yojitaḥ samayī śivaḥ ।। ukteyaṃ sadya utkrāntiryā gopyā prāṇavadbudhaiḥ ।। atha dīkṣāṃ bruve mūḍhajanāśvāsapradāyinīm ।।
trikoṇe vahnisadane vahnivarṇojjvale abhitaḥ । vāyavyapuranirdhūte kare savye sujājvale ।। bījaṃ kiṃcidgṛhītvaitattathaiva hṛdayāntare । kare ca dahyamānaṃ saccintayettajjapaikayuk ।।
vahnidīpitaphaṭkāradhoraṇīdāhapīḍitam । bījaṃ nirbījatāmeti svasūtikaraṇākṣamam ।। taptaṃ naitatprarohāya tenaiva pratyayena tu । malamāyākhyakarmāṇi mantradhyānakriyābalāt ।।
dagdhāni na svakāryāya nirbījapratyayaṃ tvimam । sa śrīmānsuprasanno me śaṃbhunātho nyarūpayat ।। bījasyāpyatra kāryā ca yojanā kṛpayā guroḥ । yato dīkṣā sudīptatvātsthāvarāṇyapi mocayet ।।
yo gururjapahomārcādhyānasiddhatvamātmani । jñātvā dīkṣāṃ carettasya dīkṣā sapratyayā smṛtā ।। avadhūte nirācāre tattvajñe natvayaṃ vidhiḥ । sācāraiḥ kriyate dīkṣā yā dṛṣṭapratyayānvitā ।।
nirācāreṇa dīkṣāyāṃ pratyayastu na gadyate । jñānaṃ svapratyayaṃ yasmānna phalāntaramarhati ।। dhyānādi tu phalātsādhyamiti siddhāmatoditam । tulāśuddhiparīkṣāṃ vā kuryātpratyayayoginīm ।।
yathā śrītantrasadbhāve kathitā parameśinā । śrīpūrvaśāstre apyeṣā ca sūcitā parameśinā ।। ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nidrā ghūrṇiśca pañcamī । ityevaṃvadatā śaktitāratamyābhidhāyinā ।।
udbhavo laghubhāvena dehagrahatirohiteḥ । deho hi pārthivo mukhyastadā mukhyatvamujjhati ।। bhāvilāghavamantreṇa śiṣyaṃ dhyātvā samutplutam । karmāṇi tatrāśeṣāṇi pūrvoktānyācaredguruḥ ।।
uktā seyaṃ tulāśuddhidīkṣā pratyayadāyinī । parokṣasaṃsthitasyātha dīkṣākarma nigadyate ।। bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati । ityasminmālinīvākye pratiḥ sāṃmukhyāvācakaḥ ।।
