sāṃmukhyaṃ cāsya śiṣyasya tatkṛpāspadatātmakam । tamārādhyeti vacanaṃ kṛpāhetūpalakṣaṇam ।। tatsaṃbandhāttataḥ kaścittatkṣaṇādapavṛjyate । ityasyāyamapi hyartho mālinīvākyasanmaṇeḥ ।।
tatkṣaṇāditi nāsyāsti yiyāsādikṣaṇāntaram । kiṃtvevameva karuṇānighnastaṃ gururuddharet ।। gurusevākṣīṇatanordīkṣāmaprāpya pañcatām । gatasyātha svayaṃ mṛtyukṣaṇoditatathāruceḥ ।।
athavādharatantrādidīkṣāsaṃskārabhāginaḥ । prāptasāmayikasyātha parāṃ dīkṣāmavindataḥ ।। ḍimbāhatasya yogeśībhakṣitasyābhicārataḥ । mṛtasya guruṇā yantratantrādinihatasya vā ।।
bhraṣṭasvasamayasyātha dīkṣāṃ prāptavato apyalam । bandhubhāryāsuhṛtputragāḍhābhyarthanayogataḥ ।। svayaṃ tadviṣayotpannakaruṇābalato api vā । vijñātatanmukhāyātaśaktipātāṃśadharmaṇaḥ ।।
gururdīkṣāṃ mṛtoddhārīṃ kurvīta śivadāyinīm । śrīmṛtyuñjayasiddhādau taduktaṃ parameśinā ।। adīkṣite nṛpatyādāvalase patite mṛte । bālāturastrīvṛddhe ca mṛtoddhāraṃ prakalpayet ।।
vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pūrvamuktaḥ sa tu saṃkṣipta iṣyate । gurvādipūjārahito bāhye bhogāya sā yataḥ ।। adhivāsacarukṣetraṃ śayyāmaṇḍalakalpane । nopayogyatra tacchiṣyasaṃskriyāsvapnadṛṣṭaye ।।
mantrasaṃnidhisaṃtṛptiyogāyātra tu maṇḍalam । bhūyodine ca devārcā sākṣānnāsyopakāri tat ।। kriyopakaraṇasthānamaṇḍalākṛtimantrataḥ । dhyānayogaikatadbhaktijñānatanmayabhāvataḥ ।।
tatpraviṣṭasya kasyāpi śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā । ekādaśaite kathitāḥ saṃnidhānāya hetavaḥ ।। uttarottaramutkṛṣṭāstathā vyāmiśraṇāvaśāt । kriyātibhūyasī puṣpādyuttamaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।।
ekaliṅgādi ca sthānaṃ yatrātmā saṃprasīdati । maṇḍalaṃ tritriśūlābjacakraṃ yanmantramaṇḍale ।। anāhūte api dṛṣṭaṃ satsamayitvaprasādhanam । taduktaṃ mālinītantre siddhaṃ samayamaṇḍalam ।।
yena saṃdṛṣṭamātreti siddhamātrapadadvayāt । ākṛtirdīptarūpā yā mantrastadvatsudīptikaḥ ।। śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭamato neha kathitaṃ vistarātpunaḥ । kṛtvā maṇḍalamabhyarcya tatra devaṃ kuśairatha ।।
gomayenākṛtiṃ kuryācchiṣyavattāṃ nidhāpayet । tatastasyāṃ śodhyamekamadhvānaṃ vyāptibhāvanāt ।। prakṛtyantaṃ vinikṣipya punarenaṃ vidhiṃ caret । mahājālaprayogeṇa sarvasmādadhvamadhyataḥ ।।
cittamākṛṣya tatrasthaṃ kuryāttadvidhirucyate । mūlādhārādudetya prasṛtasuvitatānantanāḍyadhvadaṇḍaṃ vīryeṇākramya nāsāgaganaparigataṃ vikṣipan vyāptumīṣṭe । yāvaddhūmābhirāmapracitataraśikhājālakenādhvacakraṃ saṃchādyābhīṣṭajīvānayanamiti mahājālanāmā prayogaḥ ।। etenācchādanīyaṃ vrajati paravaśaṃ saṃmukhīnatvamādau pañcādānīyate cetsakalamatha tato apyadhvamadhyādyatheṣṭam ।
ākṛṣṭāvuddhṛtau vā mṛtajanaviṣaye karṣaṇīye atha jīve yogaḥ śrīśaṃbhunāthāgamaparigamito jālanāmā mayoktaḥ ।। ciravighaṭite senāyugmeyathāmilite punarhayagajanaraṃ svāṃ svāṃ jātiṃ rasādabhidhāvati । karaṇapavanairnāḍīcakraistathaiva samāgatairnijanijarasādekībhāvyaṃ svajālavaśīkṛtaiḥ ।। mahājālasamākṛṣṭo jīvo vijñānaśālinā ।
svaḥpretatiryaṅnirayāṃstadaivaiṣa vimuñcati ।। tajjñānamantrayogāptaḥ puruṣaścaiṣa kṛtrimam । yogīva sādhyahṛdayāttadā tādātmyamujjhati ।। sthāvarādidaśāścitrāstatsalokasamīpatāḥ ।
tyajecceti na citraṃ sa evaṃ yaḥ karmaṇāpi vā ।। adhikāriśarīratvānmānuṣye tu śarīragaḥ । na tadā mucyate dehāddehānte tu śivaṃ vrajet ।। tasmindehe tu kāpyasya jāyate śāṅkarī parā ।
bhaktirūhācca vijñānādācāryādvāpyasevitāt ।। taddehasaṃsthito apyeṣa jīvo jālabalādimam । dārbhādidehaṃ vyāpnoti svādhiṣṭhityāpyacetayan ।। yogamantrakriyājñānabhūyobalavaśātpunaḥ ।
manuṣyadehamapyeṣa tadaivāśu vimuñcati ।। suptakalpo apyadeho api yo jīvaḥ so api jālataḥ । ākṛṣṭo dārbhamāyāti dehaṃ phalamayaṃ ca vā ।। jātīphalādi yatkiṃcittena vā dehakalpanā ।
antarbahirdvayaucityāttadatrotkṛṣṭamucyate ।। tato jālakramānītaḥ sa jīvaḥ suptavatsthitaḥ । manoviśiṣṭadehādisāmagrīprāptyabhāvataḥ ।। na spandate na jānāti na vakti na kilecchati ।
tādṛśasyaiva saṃskārān sarvān prāgvatprakalpayet ।। nirbījadīkṣāyogena sarvaṃ kṛtvā puroditam । vidhiṃ yojanikāṃ pūrṇāhutyā sākaṃ kṣipecca tam ।। dārbhādidehe mantrāgnāvarpite pūrṇayā saha ।
muktapāśaḥ śivaṃ yāti punarāvṛttivarjitaḥ ।। sapratyayā tviyaṃ yatra spandate darbhajā tanuḥ । tatra prāṇamanomantrārpaṇayogāttathā bhavet ।। sābhyāsasya tadapyuktaṃ balāśvāsi na tatkṛte ।
mṛtoddhāroditaireva yathāsaṃbhūti hetubhiḥ ।। jīvatparokṣadīkṣāpi kāryā nirbījikā tu sā । tasyāṃ darbhākṛtiprāyakalpane jālayogataḥ ।। saṃkalpamātreṇākarṣo jīvasya mṛtibhītitaḥ ।
śiṣṭaṃ prāgvatkuśādyutthākāraviploṣavarjitam ।। pārimityādanaiśvaryātsādhye niyatiyantraṇāt । jālākṛṣṭirvinābhyāsaṃ rāgadveṣānna jāyate ।। parokṣa evātulyābhirdīkṣābhiryadi dīkṣitaḥ ।
tatrottaraṃ syādbalavatsaṃskārāya tvadhastanam ।। bhuktiyojanikāyāṃ tu bhūyobhirgurubhistathā । kṛtāyāṃ bhogavaicitryaṃ hetuvaicitryayogataḥ ।। parokṣadīkṣaṇe māyottīrṇe bhogāya yojayet ।
bhogānīpsā durlabhā hi satī vā bhogahānaye ।। uktaṃ hi svānyasaṃvittyoḥ svasaṃvidbalavattarā । bādhakatve bādhikāsau sāmyaudāsīnyayostathā ।। śrīmān dharmaśivo apyāha pārokṣyāṃ karmapaddhatau ।
parokṣadīkṣaṇe samyak pūrṇāhutividhau yadi ।। agniściṭiciṭāśabdaṃ sadhūmaṃ pratimuñcati । dhatte nīlāmbudacchāyāṃ muhurjvalati śāmyati ।। vistaro ghorarūpaśca mahīṃ dhāvati cāpyadhaḥ ।
dhvāṃkṣādyaśravyaśabdo vā tadā taṃ lakṣayedguruḥ ।। brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpaistatsaṅgaiścopapātakaiḥ । tadā tasya na kartavyā dīkṣāsminnakṛte vidhau ।। navātmā phaṭpuṭāntaḥsthaḥ punaḥ pañcaphaḍanvitaḥ ।
amukasyeti pāpāni dahāmyanu phaḍaṣṭakam ।। iti sāhasriko homaḥ kartavyastilataṇḍulaiḥ । ante pūrṇā ca dātavyā tato asmai dīkṣayā guruḥ ।। parayojanaparyantaṃ kuryāttattvaviśodhanam ।
pratyakṣe api sthitasyāṇoḥ pāpino bhagavanmayīm ।। śaktiṃ prāptavato jyeṣṭhāmevameva vidhiṃ caret । yadi vā daiśikaḥ samyaṅ na dīptastasya tatpurā ।। prāyaścittaistathā dānaiḥ prāṇāyāmaiśca śodhanam ।
kṛtvā vidhimimāṃ cāpi dīkṣāṃ kuryādaśaṅkitaḥ ।। sarvathā vartamāno api tattvavinmocayetpaśūn । icchayaiva śivaḥ sākṣāttasmāttaṃ pūjayetsadā ।। śāṭhyaṃ tatra na kāryaṃ ca tatkṛtvādho vrajecchiśuḥ ।
na punaḥ kīrtayettasya pāpaṃ kīrtayitā vrajet ।। nirayaṃ varjayettasmāditi dīkṣottare vidhiḥ । eṣā parokṣadīkṣā dvidhoditā jīvaditarabhedena ।। liṅgoddhārākhyāmatha vacmaḥ śivaśāsanaikanirdiṣṭām ।।
uktaṃ śrīmālinītantre kila pārthivadhāraṇām । uktvā yo yojito yatra sa tasmānna nivartate ।। yogyatāvaśasaṃjātā yasya yatraiva śāsanā । sa tatraiva niyoktavyo dīkṣākāle tatastvasau ।।
phalaṃ sarvaṃ samāsādya śive yukto apavṛjyate । ayukto apyūrdhvasaṃśuddhiṃ saṃprāpya bhuvaneśataḥ ।। śuddhaḥ śivatvamāyāti dagdhasaṃsārabandhanaḥ । uktvā puṃdhāraṇāṃ coktametadvaidāntikaṃ mayā ।।
kapilāya purā proktaṃ prathame paṭale tathā । anena kramayogena saṃprāptaḥ paramaṃ padam ।। na bhūyaḥ paśutāmeti śuddhe svātmani tiṣṭhati । ato hi dhvanyate artho ayaṃ śivatattvādhareṣvapi ।।
tattveṣu yojitasyāsti punaruddharaṇīyatā । samastaśāstrakathitavastuvaiviktyadāyinaḥ ।। śivāgamasya sarvebhyo apyāgamebhyo viśiṣṭatā । śivajñānena ca vinā bhūyo api paśutodbhavaḥ ।।
kramaśca śaktisaṃpāto malahāniryiyāsutā । dīkṣā bodho heyahānirupādeyalayātmatā ।। bhogyatvapāśavatyāgaḥ patikartṛtvasaṃkṣayaḥ । svātmasthitiścetyevaṃ hi darśanāntarasaṃsthiteḥ ।।
proktamuddharaṇīyatvaṃ śivaśaktīritasya hi । atha vaiṣṇavabauddhāditantrāntādharavartinām ।। yadā śivārkaraśmyoghairvikāsi hṛdayāmbujam । liṅgoddhṛtistadā pūrvaṃ dīkṣākarma tataḥ param ।।
prāgliṅgāntarasaṃstho api dīkṣātaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet । tatropavāsya taṃ cānyadine sādhāramantrataḥ ।। sthaṇḍile pūjayitveśaṃ śrāvayettasya vartanīm । eṣa prāgabhavalliṅgī coditastvadhunā tvayā ।।
prasannena tadetasmai kuru samyaganugraham । svaliṅgatyāgaśaṅkotthaṃ prāyaścittaṃ ca māsya bhūt ।। acirāttvanmayībhūya bhogaṃ mokṣaṃ prapadyatām । evamastvityathājñāṃ ca gṛhīrvā vratamasya tat ।।
apāsyāmbhasi nikṣipya snapayedanurūpataḥ । snātaṃ saṃprokṣayedarghapātrāmbhobhiranantaram ।। pañcagavyaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ tatastasmai samarpayet । tatastaṃ baddhanetraṃ ca praveśya praṇipātayet ।।
praṇavo mātṛkā māyā vyomavyāpī ṣaḍakṣaraḥ । bahurūpo atha netrākhyaḥ sapta sādhāraṇā amī ।। teṣāṃ madhyādekatamaṃ mantramasmai samarpayet । so apyahorātramevainaṃ japedalpabhugapyabhuk ।।
mantramasmai samarpyātha sādhāravidhisaṃskṛte । vahnau tarpitatanmantre vrataśuddhiṃ samācaret ।। pūjitenaiva mantreṇa kṛtvā nāmāsya saṃpuṭam । prāyaścittaṃ śodhayāmi phaṭsvāhetyūhayogataḥ ।।
śataṃ sahasraṃ vā hutvā punaḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ tathā । prayogādvauṣaḍantāṃ ca kṣiptvāhūya vrateśvaram ।। tāro vrateśvarāyeti namaścetyenamarcayet । śrāvayecca tvayā nāsya kāryaṃ kiṃcicchivājñayā ।।
tato vrateśvarastarpyaḥ svāhāntena tataśca saḥ । kṣamayitvā visṛjyaḥ syāttato agneśca visarjanam ।। tacchrāvaṇaṃ ca devāya kṣamasveti visarjanam । tatastṛtīyadivase prāgvatsarvo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
adhivāsādikaḥ sveṣṭadīkṣākarmāvasānakaḥ । prāgliṅgināṃ mokṣadīkṣā sādhikāravivarjitā ।। sādhakācāryatāmārge na yogyāste punarbhuvaḥ । punarbhuvo api jñāneddhā bhavanti gurutāspadam ।।
mokṣāyaiva na bhogāya bhogāyāpyabhyupāyataḥ । ityuktavānsvapaddhatyāmīśānaśivadaiśikaḥ ।। śrīdevyā yāmalīyoktitattvasamyakpravedakaḥ । gurvantasyāpyadhodṛṣṭiśāyinaḥ saṃskriyāmimām ।।
kṛtvā rahasyaṃ kathayennānyathā kāmike kila । anyatantrābhiṣikte api rahasyaṃ na prakāśayet ।। svatantrastho api gurvanto gurumajñamupāśritaḥ । tatra paścādanāśvastastatrāpi vidhimācaret ।।
ajñācāryamukhāyātaṃ nirvīryaṃ mantrameṣa yat । japtavānsa guruścātra nādhikāryuktadūṣaṇāt ।। tato asya śuddhiṃ prākkṛtvā tato dīkṣāṃ samācaret । adhodarśanasaṃsthena guruṇā dīkṣitaḥ purā ।।
tīvraśaktivaśātpaścādyadā gacchetsa sadgurum । tadāpyasya śiśorevaṃ śuddhiṃ kṛtvā sa sadguruḥ ।। dīkṣādikarma nikhilaṃ kuryāduktavidhānataḥ । prāpto api sadgururyogyabhāvamasya na vetti cet ।।
vijñānadāne tacchiṣyo yogyatāṃ darśayennijām । sarvathā tvabruvanneṣa bruvāṇo vā viparyayam ।। ajño vastuta eveti tattyaktvetthaṃ vidhiṃ caret । na tirobhāvaśaṅkātra kartavyā buddhiśālinā ।।
adhaḥspṛktvaṃ tirobhūtirnordhvopāyavivecanam । siddhānte dīkṣitāstantre daśāṣṭādaśabhedini ।। bhairavīye catuḥṣaṣṭau tānpaśūndīkṣayettrike । siddhavīrāvalīsāre bhairavīye kule api ca ।।
pañcadīkṣākramopāttā dīkṣānuttarasaṃjñitā । tena sarvo adharastho api liṅgoddhṛtyānugṛhyate ।। yo api hṛtsthamaheśānacodanātaḥ suvistṛtam । śāstrajñānaṃ samanvicchetso api yāyādbahūngurūn ।।
taddīkṣāścāpi gṛhṇīyādabhiṣecanapaścimāḥ । jñānopodbalikāstā hi tattajjñānavatā kṛtāḥ ।। uktaṃ ca śrīmate śāstre tatra tatra ca bhūyasā । āmodārthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpātpuṣpāntaraṃ vrajet ।।
vijñānārthī tathā śiṣyo gurorgurvantaraṃ tviti । gurūṇāṃ bhūyasāṃ madhye yato vijñānamuttamam ।। prāptaṃ so asya gururdīkṣā nātra mukhyā hi saṃvidi । sarvajñānanidhānaṃ tu guruṃ saṃprāpya susthitaḥ ।।
tamevārādhayeddhīmāṃstattajjijñāsanonmukhaḥ । iti dīkṣāvidhiḥ prokto liṅgoddharaṇapaścimaḥ ।। athābhiṣekasya vidhiḥ kathyate pārameśvaraḥ ।। yaiṣā putrakadīkṣoktā gurusādhakayorapi ।
saivādhikāriṇī bhogyatattvayuktimatī kramāt ।। svabhyastajñāninaṃ santaṃ bubhūṣumatha bhāvinam । yogyaṃ jñātvā svādhikāraṃ gurustasmai samarpayet ।। yo naivaṃ veda naivāsāvabhiṣikto api daiśikaḥ ।
samayyādikrameṇeti śrīmatkāmika ucyate ।। yo na vedādhvasandhānaṃ ṣoḍhā bāhyāntarasthitam । sa gururmocayenneti siddhayogīśvarīmate ।। sarvalakṣaṇahīno api jñānavān gururiṣyate ।
jñānaprādhānyamevoktamiti śrīkacabhārgave ।। padavākyapramāṇajñaḥ śivabhaktyekatatparaḥ । samastaśivaśāstrārthaboddhā kāruṇiko guruḥ ।। na svayaṃbhūstasya coktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ parameśinā ।
abhakto jīvitadhiyā kurvannīśānadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। paścātmanā svayaṃbhūṣṇurnādhikārī sa kutracit । bhasmāṅkuro vratisuto duḥśīlātanayastathā ।। kuṇḍo golaśca te duṣṭā uktaṃ devyākhyayāmale ।
punarbhūścānyaliṅgo yaḥ punaḥ śaive pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre na tveṣa niyamaḥ ko api coditaḥ । yathārthatattvasaṃghajñastathā śiṣye prakāśakaḥ ।। yaḥ punaḥ sarvatattvāni vettītyādi ca lakṣaṇam ।
yogacāre ca yadyatra tantre coditamācaret ।। tathaiva siddhaye seyamājñeti kila varṇitam । yastu karmitayācāryastatra kāṇādivarjanam ।। yataḥ kārakasāmagryātkarmaṇo nādhikaḥ kvacit ।
devyā yāmalaśāstre ca kāñcyādiparivarjanam ।। taddṛṣṭadoṣātkrodhādeḥ samyakjñātaryasau kutaḥ । guravastu svayaṃbhvādi varjyaṃ yadyāmalādiṣu ।। karmyabhiprāyataḥ sarvaṃ taditi vyācacakṣire ।
ato deśakulācāradehalakṣaṇakalpanām ।। anādṛtyaiva saṃpūrṇajñānaṃ kuryādgururgurum । prāgvatsaṃpūjya hutvā ca śrāvayitvā cikīrṣitam ।। tato abhiṣiñcettaṃ śiṣyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā tataḥ sakṛt ।
tanmantrarasatoyena pūrvoktavidhinā guruḥ ।। vibhavena suvistīrṇaṃ tatastasmai vadetsvakam । sarvaṃ kartavyasāraṃ yacchāstrāṇāṃ paramaṃ rahaḥ ।। anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śivaśaktipracoditāḥ ।
uktaṃ jñānottare caitadbrāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ ।। napuṃsakāḥ striyaḥ śūdrā ye cānye api tadarthinaḥ । te dīkṣāyāṃ na mīmāṃsyā jñānakāle vicārayet ।। jñānamūlo guruḥ proktaḥ saptasatrīṃ pravartayet ।
dīkṣā vyākhyā kṛpā maitrī śāstracintā śivaikatā ।। annādidānamityetatpālayetsaptasatrakam । abhiṣekavidhau cāsmai karaṇīkhaṭikādikam ।। sarvopakaraṇavrātamarpaṇīyaṃ vipaścite ।
so abhiṣikto guruṃ paścāddakṣiṇābhiḥ prapūjayet ।। jñānahīno guruḥ karmī svādhikāraṃ samarpya no । dīkṣādyadhikṛtiṃ kuryādvinā tasyājñayā punaḥ ।। ityevaṃ śrāvayetso api namaskṛtyābhinandayet ।
tataḥ prabhṛtyasau pūrvo gurustyaktādhikārakaḥ ।। yathecchaṃ vicaredvyākhyādīkṣādau yantraṇojjhitaḥ । kurvanna bādhyate yasmāddīpāddīpavadīdṛśaḥ ।। santāno nādhikārasya cyavo akurvanna bādhyate ।
prāk ca kurvanvihanyeta siddhātantre taducyate ।। yathārthamupadeśaṃ tu kurvannācārya ucyate । na cāvajñā kriyākāle saṃsāroddharaṇaṃ prati ।। na dīkṣeta guruḥ śiṣyaṃ tattvayuktastu garvataḥ ।
yo asya syānnarake vāsa iha ca vyādhito bhavet ।। prāptābhiṣekaḥ sa guruḥ ṣaṇmāsānmantrapaddhatim । sarvāṃ tantroditāṃ dhyāyejjapeccātanmayatvataḥ ।। yadaiva tanmayībhūtastadā vīryamupāgataḥ ।
chindyātpāśāṃstato yatnaṃ kuryāttanmayatāsthitau ।। hṛccakrādutthitā sūkṣmā śaśisphaṭikasaṃnibhā । lekhākārā nādarūpā praśāntā cakrapaṅktigā ।। dvādaśānte nirūḍhā sā sauṣumne tripathāntare ।
tatra hṛccakramāpūrya japenmantraṃ jvalatprabham ।। cakṣurlomādirandhraughavahajjvālaurvasaṃnibham । yāvacchāntaśikhākīrṇaṃ viśvājyapravilāpakam ।। tadājyadhārāsaṃtṛptamānābhikuharāntaram ।
evaṃ mantrā mokṣadāḥ syurdīptā buddhāḥ sunirmalāḥ ।। mūlakandanabhonābhihṛtkaṇṭhālikatālugam । ardhendurodhikānādatadantavyāpiśaktigam ।। samanonmanaśuddhātmaparacakrasamāśritam ।
yatra yatra japeccakre samastavyastabhedanāt ।। tatra tatra mahāmantra iti devyākhyayāmale । vidyāvratamidaṃ proktaṃ mantravīryaprasiddhaye ।। tacca tādātmyameveti yaduktaṃ spandaśāsane ।
tadākramya balaṃ mantrāḥ sarvajñabalaśālinaḥ ।। pravartante adhikārāya karaṇānīva dehinām । kṛtavidyāvrataḥ paścāddīkṣāvyākhyādi sarvataḥ ।। kuryādyogyeṣu śiṣyeṣu nāyogyeṣu kadācana ।
rahasye yojayedvipraṃ parīkṣya viparītataḥ ।। ācārācchaktimapyeva nānyathetyūrmiśāsane । nityādyalpālpakaṃ kuryādyaduktaṃ brahmayāmale ।। cīrṇavidyāvrataḥ sarvaṃ manasā vā smaretpriye ।
dehasaṃbandhasaṃchannasārvajñyo dambhabhājanam ।। avidandīkṣamāṇo api na duṣyeddaiśikaḥ kvacit । jñātvā tvayogyatāṃ nainaṃ dīkṣeta pratyavāyitām ।। buddhvā jñāne śāstrasiddhigurutvādau ca taṃ punaḥ ।
bhūya eva parīkṣeta tattadaucityaśālinam ।। tatra tatra niyuñjīta natu jātu viparyayāt । nanu tadvastvayogyasya tatrecchā jāyate kutaḥ ।। tadīśādhiṣṭhitecchaiva yogyatāmasya sūcayet ।
satyaṃ kāpi prabuddhāsāvicchā rūḍhiṃ na gacchati ।। vidyudvatpāpaśīlasya yathā pāpāpavarjane । rūḍhyarūḍhī tadicchāyā api śaṃbhuprasādataḥ ।। aprarūḍhatathecchākastata eva na bhājanam ।
yaḥ samyagjñānamādāya guruviśvāsavarjitaḥ ।। lokaṃ viplāvayennāsmiñjñāte vijñānamarpayet । ajñāte api punarjñāte vijñānaharaṇaṃ caret ।। punaḥpunaryadā jñāto viśvāsaparivarjitaḥ ।
tadā tamagrato dhyāyetsphurantaṃ candrasūryavat ।। tato nijahṛdambhojabodhāmbarataloditām । svarbhānumalināṃ dhyāyedvāmāṃ śaktiṃ vimohanīm ।। vāmācārakrameṇaināṃ niḥsṛtāṃ sādhyagāminīm ।
cintayitvā tayā grastaprakāśaṃ taṃ vicintayet ।। anena kramayogena mūḍhabuddherdurātmanaḥ । vijñānamantravidyādyāḥ prakurvantyapakāritām ।। nanu vijñānamātmasthaṃ kathaṃ hartuṃ kṣamaṃ bhavet ।
ato vijñānaharaṇaṃ kathaṃ śrīpūrva ucyate ।। ucyate nāsya śiṣyasya vijñānaṃ rūḍhimāgatam । tathātve haraṇaṃ kasmātpūrṇayogyatvaśālinaḥ ।। kiṃtveṣa vāmayā śaktyā mūḍho gāḍhaṃ vibhoḥ kṛtaḥ ।
svabhāvādeva tenāsya vidyādyamapakārakam ।। guruḥ punaḥ śivābhinnaḥ sanyaḥ pañcavidhāṃ kṛtim । kuryādyadi tataḥ pūrṇamadhikāritvamasya tat ।। ato yathā śuddhatattvasṛṣṭisthityormalātyaye ।
yojanānugrahe kāryacatuṣke adhikṛto guruḥ ।। śivābhedena tatkuryāttadvatpañcamamapyayam । tirobhāvābhidhaṃ kṛtyaṃ tathāsau śivatātmakaḥ ।। ata eva śive śāstre jñāne cāśvāsabhājanam ।
gurormūḍhatayā kopadhāmāpi na tirohitaḥ ।। gururhi kupito yasya sa tirohita ucyate । saṃsārī satu devo hi gururna ca mṛṣāvidaḥ ।। tata eva ca śāstrādidūṣako yadyapi krudhā ।
na dahyate asau guruṇā tathāpyeṣa tirohitaḥ ।। asmadgurvāgamastveṣa tirobhūte svayaṃ śiśau । na kupyenna śapeddhīmān sa hyanugrāhakaḥ sadā ।। īśecchācoditaḥ pāśaṃ yadi kaṇṭhe nipīḍayet ।
kimācāryeṇa tatrāsya kāryā syātsahakāritā ।। śivābhinno api hi gururanugrahamayīṃ vibhoḥ । mukhyāṃ śaktimupāsīno anugṛhṇīyātsa sarvathā ।। svātantryamātrajñaptyai tu kathitaṃ śāstra īdṛśam ।
na kāryaṃ patatāṃ hastālambaḥ sahyo na pātanam ।। ata eva svatantratvādicchāyāḥ punarunmukham । prāyaścittairviśodhyainaṃ dīkṣeta kṛpayā guruḥ ।। ūrdhvadṛṣṭau prapannaḥ sannanāśvastastataḥ param ।
adhaḥśāstraṃ prapadyāpi na śreyaḥpātratāmiyāt ।। adhodṛṣṭau prapannastu tadanāśvastamānasaḥ । ūrdhvaśāsanabhāk pāpaṃ taccojjhecca śivībhavet ।। rājñe druhyannamātyāṅgabhūto api hi vihanyate ।
viparyayastu netyevamūrdhvāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ samāśrayet ।। śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ yāvattenaiva noddhṛtaḥ । atra hyartho ayametāvatpūrvoktajñānavṛṃhitaḥ ।। gurustāvatsa evātra tacchabdenāvamṛśyate ।
tādṛksvabhyastavijñānabhājordhvapadaśālinā ।। anuddhṛtasya na śreya etadanyagurūddhṛteḥ । ata evāmbujanmārkadṛṣṭānto atra nirūpitaḥ ।। trijagajjyotiṣo hyanyattejo anyacca niśākṛtaḥ ।
jñānamanyattrikaguroranyattvadharavartinām ।। ata eva purābhūtagurvabhāvo yadā tadā । tadanyaṃ lakṣaṇopetamāśrayetpunarunmukhaḥ ।। sati tasmiṃstūnmukhaḥ sankasmājjahyādyadi sphuṭam ।
syādanyatarago doṣo yo adhikārāpaghātakaḥ ।। doṣaśceha na lokastho doṣatvena nirūpyate । ajñānakhyāpanāyuktakhyāpanātmā tvasau mataḥ ।। śiṣyasyāpi tathābhūtajñānānāśvastarūpatā ।
mukhyo doṣastadanye hi doṣāstatprabhavā yataḥ ।। na dhvastavyādhikaḥ ko hi bhiṣajaṃ bahu manyate । asūyurnūnamadhvastavyādhiḥ svasthāyate balāt ।। evaṃ jñānasamāśvastaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na gurave caret ।
no cennūnamaviśvasto viśvasta iva tiṣṭhati ।। ajñānādaya evaite doṣā na laukikā guroḥ । iti khyāpayituṃ proktaṃ mālinīvijayottare ।। na tasyānveṣayedvṛttaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham ।
sa eva tadvijānāti yuktaṃ cāyuktameva vā ।। akāryeṣu yadā saktaḥ prāṇadravyāpahāriṣu । tadā nivāraṇīyo asau praṇatena vipaścitā ।। viśeṣaṇamakāryāṇāmuktābhiprāyameva yat ।
tenātivāryamāṇo api yadyasau na nivartate ।। tadānyatra kvacidgatvā śivamevānucintayet । na hyasya sa gurutve syāddoṣo yenoṣare kṛṣim ।। kuryādvrajenniśāyāṃ vā sa tvarthaprāṇahārakaḥ ।
tadīyāpriyabhīrustu paraṃ tādṛśamācaret ।। yatastadapriyaṃ naiṣa śṛṇuyāditi bhāṣitam । śrīmātaṅge taduktaṃ ca nādhītaṃ bhūmabhītitaḥ ।। yaccaitaduktametāvatkartavyamiti taddhruvam ।
tīvraśaktigṛhītānāṃ svayameva hṛdi sphuret ।। upadeśastvayaṃ mandamadhyaśakternijāṃ kramāt । śaktiṃ jvalayituṃ proktaḥ sā hyevaṃ jājvalītyalam ।। dṛḍhānurāgasubhagasaṃrambhābhogabhāginaḥ ।
svollāsi smarasarvasyaṃ dārḍhyāyānyatra dṛśyate ।। nanveṣa kasmāddṛṣṭāntaḥ kimetenāśubhaṃ kṛtam । citspandaḥ sarvago bhinnādupādheḥ sa tathā tathā ।। bhavetko api tirobhūtaḥ punarunmukhito api san ।
vināpi daiśikātprāgvatsvayameva vimucyate ।। prakārastveṣa nātroktaḥ śaktipātabalādgataḥ । asaṃbhāvyatayā cātra dṛḍhakopaprasādavat ।। ityeṣa yo guroḥ prokto vidhistaṃ pālayedguruḥ ।
anyathā na śivaṃ yāyācchrīmatsāre ca varṇitam ।। anyāyaṃ ye prakurvanti śāstrārthaṃ varjayantyalam । te ardhanārīśapuragā guravaḥ samayacyutāḥ ।। anyatrāpyadhikāraṃ ca neyādvidyeśatāṃ vrajet ।
anyatra samayatyāgātkravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ ।। iyattatratyatātparyaṃ siddhāntagururunnayaḥ । bhavetpiśācavidyeśaḥ śuddha eva tu tāntrikaḥ ।। ṣaḍardhadaiśikaścārdhanārīśabhuvanasthitiḥ ।
eṣā karmapradhānānāṃ gurūṇāṃ gatirucyate ।। jñānināṃ caiṣa no bandha iti sarvatra varṇitam । sādhakasyābhiṣeke api sarvo ayaṃ kathyate vidhiḥ ।। adhikārārpaṇaṃ nātra naca vidyāvrataṃ kila ।
sādhyamantrārpaṇaṃ tvatra svopayogikriyākrame ।। samaste apyupadeśaḥ syānnijopakaraṇārpaṇam । abhiṣekavidhirnirūpitaḥ parameśena yathā nirūpitaḥ ।। atha śāmbhavaśāsanoditāṃ sarahasyāṃ śṛṇutāntyasaṃskriyām ।।
sarveṣāmadharasthānāṃ gurvantānāmapi sphuṭam । śaktipātātpurāproktātkuryādantyeṣṭidīkṣaṇam ।। ūrdhvaśāsanagānāṃ ca samayopahatātmanām । antyeṣṭidīkṣā kartavyā guruṇā tattvavedinā ।।
samayācāradoṣeṣu pramādātskhalitasya hi । antyeṣṭidīkṣā kāryeti śrīdīkṣottaraśāsane ।। yatkiṃcitkathitaṃ pūrvaṃ mṛtoddhārābhidhe vidhau । pratimāyāṃ tadevātra sarvaṃ śavatanau caret ।।
śrīsiddhātantrakathito vidhireṣa nirūpyate । antimaṃ yadbhavetpūrvaṃ tatkṛtvāntimamādimam ।। saṃhṛtyaikaikamiṣṭiryā sāntyeṣṭirdvitayī matā । pūjādhyānajapāpluṣṭasamaye natu sādhake ।।
piṇḍapātādayaṃ muktaḥ khecaro vā bhavetpriye । ācārye tattvasaṃpanne yatra tatra mṛte sati ।। antyeṣṭirnaiva vidyeta śuddhacetasyamūrdhani । mantrayogādibhirye ca māritā narake tu te ।।
kāryā teṣāmihāntyeṣṭirguruṇātikṛpālunā । na maṇḍalādikaṃ tvatra bhavecchamāśānike vidhau ।। kecittadapi kartavyamūcire pretasadmani । pūjayitvā vibhuṃ sarvaṃ nyāsaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।।
saṃhārakramayogena caraṇānmūrdhapaścimam । tathaiva bodhayedenaṃ kriyājñānasamādhibhiḥ ।। bindunā rodhayettattvaṃ śaktibījena vedhayet । ghaṭṭayennādadeśe tu triśūlena tu tāḍayet ।।
suṣumnāntargatenaiva visargeṇa punaḥ punaḥ । tāḍayeta kalāḥ sarvāḥ kampate asau tataḥ paśuḥ ।। utkṣipedvāmahastaṃ vā tatastaṃ yojayetpare । pratyayena vinā mokṣo hyaśraddheyo vimohitaiḥ ।।
tadarthametaduditaṃ natu mokṣopayogyadaḥ । ityūce parameśaḥ śrīkulagahvaraśāsane ।। sādhyo anumeyo mokṣādiḥ pratyayairyadatīndriyaḥ । dīkṣottare ca puryaṣṭavargārpaṇamihoditam ।।
tadvidhiḥ śrutipatre abje madhye devaṃ sadāśivam । īśarudraharibrahmacatuṣkaṃ prāgdigāditaḥ ।। pūjayitvā śrutisparśau rasaṃ gandhaṃ vapurdvayam । dhyahaṃkṛtī manaśceti brahmādiṣvarpayetkramāt ।।
eteṣāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā śatahomena daiśikaḥ । eṣā sāṃnyāsikī dīkṣā puryaṣṭakaviśodhanī ।। puryaṣṭakasyābhāve ca na svarganarakādayaḥ । tathā kṛtvā na kartavyaṃ laukikaṃ kiṃcanāpi hi ।।
uktaṃ śrīmādhavakule śāsanastho mṛteṣvapi । piṇḍapātodakāsrvādi laukikaṃ parivarjayet ।। śivaṃ saṃpūjya cakrārcāṃ yathāśakti samācaret । kramāttridaśamatriṃśatriṃśavatsaravāsare ।।
ityukto antyeṣṭiyāgo ayaṃ parameśvarabhāṣitaḥ ।। atha śrāddhavidhiḥ śrīmatṣaḍardhokto nigadyate ।। siddhātantre sūcito asau mūrtiyāganirūpaṇe । antyeṣṭyā suviśuddhānāmaśuddhānāṃ ca tadvidhiḥ ।।
tryahe turye ahni daśame māsi māsyādyavatsare । varṣe varṣe sarvakālaṃ kāryastatsvaiḥ sa pūrvavat ।। tatra prāgvadyajeddevaṃ homayedanale tathā । tato naivedyameva prāggṛhītvā hastagocare ।।
gururannamayīṃ śaktiṃ vṛṃhikāṃ vīryarūpiṇīm । dhyātvā tayā samāviṣṭaṃ taṃ sādhyaṃ cintayetsudhīḥ ।। tato asya yaḥ pāśavoṃ aśo bhogyarūpastamarpayet । bhoktaryekātmabhāvena śiṣya itthaṃ śivībhavet ।।
bhogyatānyā tanurdeha iti pāśātmakā matāḥ । śrāddhe mṛtoddhṛtāvantayāge teṣāṃ śivīkṛtiḥ ।। ekenaiva vidhānena yadyapi syātkṛtārthatā । tathāpi tanmayībhāvasiddhyai sarvaṃ vidhiṃ caret ।।
bubhukṣostu kriyābhyāsabhūmānau phalabhūmani । hetu tato mṛtoddhāraśrāddhādyasmai samācaret ।। tattvajñānārkavidhvastadhvāntasya tu na ko apyayam । antyeṣṭiśrāddhavidhyādirupayogī kadācana ।।
teṣāṃ tu guru tadvargavargyasabrahmacāriṇām । tatsantānajuṣāmaikyadinaṃ parvadinaṃ bhavet ।। yadāhi bodhasyodrekastadā parvāha pūraṇāt । janmaikyadivasau tena parvaṇī bodhasiddhitaḥ ।।
putrako api yadā kasmaicana syādupakārakaḥ । tadā mātuḥ pituḥ śaktervāmadakṣāntarālagāḥ ।। nāḍīḥ pravāhayeddevāyārpayeta niveditam । śrīmadbharuṇatantre ca tacchivena nirūpitam ।।
tadvāhakālāpekṣā ca kāryā tadrūpasiddhaye । svācchandyenātha tatsiddhiṃ vidhinā bhāvinā caret ।। yasya kasyāpi vā śrāddhe gurudevāgnitarpaṇam । sacakreṣṭi bhavecchrauto natu syātpāśavo vidhiḥ ।।
śrīmaukuṭe tathā coktaṃ śivaśāstre sthito api yaḥ । pratyeti vaidike bhagnaghaṇṭāvanna sa kiṃcana ।। tathoktadevapūjādicakrayāgāntakarmaṇā । rudratvametyasau janturbhogāndivyānsamaśnute ।।
atha vacmaḥ sphuṭaṃ śrīmatsiddhaye nāḍicāraṇam । yā vāhayitumiṣyeta nāḍī tāmeva bhāvayet ।। bhāvanātanmayībhāve sā nāḍī vahati sphuṭam । yadvā vāhayituṃ yeṣṭā tadaṅgaṃ tena pāṇinā ।।
āpīḍya kukṣiṃ namayetsā vahennāḍikā kṣaṇāt । evaṃ śrāddhamukhenāpi bhogamokṣobhayasthitim ।। kuryāditi śivenoktaṃ tatra tatra kṛpālunā । śaktipātodaye jantoryenopāyena daiśikaḥ ।।
karotyuddharaṇaṃ tattannirvāṇāyāsya kalpate । uddhartā devadevo hi sa cācintyaprabhāvakaḥ ।। upāyaṃ gurudīkṣādidvāramātreṇa saṃśrayet । uktaṃ śrīmanmataṅgākhye munipraśnādanantaram ।।
muktirvivekāttattvānāṃ dīkṣāto yogato yadi । caryāmātrātkathaṃ sā syādityataḥ samamuttaram ।। prahasyoce vibhuḥ kasmādbhrāntiste parameśituḥ । sarvānugrāhakatvaṃ hi saṃsiddhaṃ dṛśyatāṃ kila ।।
prāptamṛtyorviṣavyādhiśastrādi kila kāraṇam । alpaṃ vā bahu vā tadvadanudhyā muktikāraṇam ।। muktyarthamupacaryante bāhyaliṅgānyamūni tu । iti jñātvā na sandeha itthaṃ kāryo vipaścitā ।।
iyataiva kathaṃ muktiriti bhaktiṃ parāṃ śrayet । uktaḥ śrāddhavidhirbhrāntigarātaṅkavimardanaḥ ।। athocyate śeṣavṛttirjīvatāmupayoginī ।। dīkṣā bahuprakāreyaṃ śrāddhāntā yā prakīrtitā ।
sā saṃskriyāyai mokṣāya bhogāyāpi dvayāya vā ।। tatra saṃskārasiddhyai yā dīkṣā sākṣānna mocanī । anusaṃdhivaśādyā ca sākṣānmoktrī sabījikā ।। tayobhayyā dīkṣitā ye teṣāmājīvavartanam ।
vaktavyaṃ putrakādīnāṃ tanmayatvaprasiddhaye ।। bubhukṣorvā mumukṣorvā svasaṃvidguruśāstrataḥ । pramāṇādyā saṃskriyāyai dīkṣā hi guruṇā kṛtā ।। tataḥ sa saṃskṛtaṃ yogyaṃ jñātvātmānaṃ svaśāsane ।
taduktavastvanuṣṭhānaṃ bhuktyai muktyai ca sevate ।। ācāryapratyayādeva yo api syādbhuktimuktibhāk । tatpratyūhodayadhvastyai brūyāttasyāpi vartanam ।। svasaṃvidgurusaṃvittyostulyapratyayabhāgapi ।
śeṣavṛttyā samādeśyastadvighnādipraśāntaye ।। yaḥ sarvathā parāpekṣāmujjhitvā tu sthito nijāt । pratyayādyo api cācāryapratyayādeva kevalāt ।। tau sāṃsiddhikanirbījau ko vadeccheṣavṛttaye ।
kramāttanmayatopāyagurvarcanaratau tu tau ।। tatraiṣāṃ śeṣavṛttyarthaṃ nityanaimittike dhruve । kāmyavarjaṃ yataḥ kāmāścitrāścitrābhyupāyakāḥ ।। tatra nityo vidhiḥ sandhyānuṣṭhānaṃ devatāvraje ।
gurvagniśāstrasahite pūjā bhūtadayetyayam ।। naimittikastu sarveṣāṃ parvaṇāṃ pūjanaṃ japaḥ । viśeṣavaśataḥ kiṃca pavitrakavidhikramaḥ ।। ācāryasya ca dīkṣeyaṃ bahubhedā vivecitā ।
vyākhyādikaṃ ca tattasyādhikaṃ naimittikaṃ dhruvam ।। tatrādau śiśave vrūyādgururnityavidhiṃ sphuṭam । tadyogyatāṃ samālokya vitatāvitatātmanām ।। mukhyetarādimantrāṇāṃ vīryavyāptyādiyogyatām ।
dṛṣṭvā śiṣye tamevāsmai mūlamantraṃ samarpayet ।। tacchāstradīkṣito hyeṣa niryantrācāraśaṅkitaḥ । na mukhye yogya ityanyasevātaḥ syāttu yogyatā ।। sādhakasya bubhukṣostu sādhakībhāvino apivā ।
puṣpapātavaśātsiddho mantro arpyaḥ sādhyasiddhaye ।। vitate guṇabhūte vā vidhau diṣṭe punarguruḥ । jñātvāsmai yogyatāṃ sāraṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret ।। tatraiṣa niyamo yadyanmāntraṃ rūpaṃ na tadguruḥ ।
likhitvā prathayecchiṣye viśeṣādūrdhvaśāsane ।। mantrā varṇātmakāste ca parāmarśātmakāḥ saca । gurusaṃvidabhinnaśvetsaṃkrāmetsā tataḥ śiśau ।। lipisthitastu yo mantro nirvīryaḥ so atra kalpitaḥ ।
saṃketabalato nāsya pustakātprathate mahaḥ ।। pustakādhītavidyāścetyuktaṃ siddhāmate tataḥ । ye tu pustakalabdhe api mantre vīryaṃ prajānate ।। te bhairavīyasaṃskārāḥ proktāḥ sāṃsiddhikā iti ।
iti jñātvā guruḥ samyak paramānandaghūrṇitaḥ ।। tādṛśe tādṛśe dhāmni pūjayitvā vidhiṃ caret । yathānyaśiṣyānuṣṭhānaṃ nānyaśiṣyeṇa budhyate ।। tathā kuryādgururguptihānirdoṣavatī yataḥ ।
devīnāṃ tritayaṃ śuddhaṃ yadvā yāmalayogataḥ ।। devīmekāmatho śuddhāṃ vadedvā yāmalātmikām । tatra mantraṃ sphuṭaṃ vaktrādguruṇopāṃśu coditam ।। avadhāryā pravṛttestamabhyasyenmanasā svayam ।
tataḥ suśikṣitāṃ sthānadehāntaḥśodhanatrayīm ।। nyāsaṃ dhyānaṃ japaṃ mudrāṃ pūjāṃ kuryātprayatnataḥ । tatra prabhāte saṃbudhya sveṣṭāṃ prāgdevatāṃ smaret ।। kṛtāvaśyakakartavyaḥ śuddho bhūtvā tato gṛham ।
āśrityottaradigvaktraḥ sthānadehāntaratraye ।। śuddhiṃ vidhāya mantrāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ niveśanam । mudrāpradarśanaṃ dhyānaṃ bhedābhedasvarūpataḥ ।। dehāsudhīvyomabhūṣu manasā tatra cārcanam ।
japaṃ cātra yathāśakti devāyaitannivedanam ।। tanmayībhāvasiddhyarthaṃ pratisandhyaṃ samācaret । anye tu prāgudakpaścāddaśadikṣu catuṣṭayīm ।। sandhyānāmāhuretacca tāntrikīyaṃ na no matam ।
yāsau kālādhikāre prāk sandhyā proktā catuṣṭayī ।। tāmevāntaḥ samādhāya sāndhyaṃ vidhimupācaret । sandhyācatuṣṭayīkṛtyamekasyāmathavā śiśuḥ ।। kuryātsvādhyāyavijñānagurukṛtyāditatparaḥ ।
sandhyādhyānoditānantatanmayībhāvayuktitaḥ ।। tatsaṃskāravaśātsarvaṃ kālaṃ syāttanmayo hyasau । tato yatheṣṭakāle asau pūjāṃ puṣpāsavādibhiḥ ।। sthaṇḍilādau śiśuḥ kuryādvibhavādyanurūpataḥ ।
suśuddhaḥ sanvidhiṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvāntarajapāntakam ।। arghapātraṃ purā yadvadvidhāya sveṣṭamantrataḥ । tena sthaṇḍilapuṣpādi sarvaṃ saṃprokṣayedbudhaḥ ।। tatastatraiva saṃkalpya dvārāsanagurukramam ।
pūjayecchivatāviṣṭaḥ svadehārcāpuraḥsaram ।। tatastatsthaṇḍilaṃ vīdhravyomasphaṭikanirmalam । bodhātmakaṃ samālokya tatra svaṃ devatāgaṇam ।। pratibimbatayā paśyedbimbatvena ca bodhataḥ ।
etadāvāhanaṃ mukhyaṃ vyajanānmarutāmiva ।। sarvago api marudyadvadvyajanenopajīvitaḥ । arthakṛtsarvagaṃ mantracakraṃ rūḍhestathā bhavet ।। catuṣkapañcāśikayā tadetattattvamucyate ।
śrīnirmaryādaśāstre ca tadetadvibhunoditam ।। devaḥ sarvagato deva nirmaryādaḥ kathaṃ śivaḥ । āvāhyate kṣamyate vetyevaṃpṛṣṭo abravīdvibhuḥ ।। vāsanāvāhyate devi vāsanā ca visṛjyate ।
paramārthena devasya nāvāhanavisarjane ।। āvāhito mayā devaḥ sthaṇḍile ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ । pūjitaḥ stuta ityevaṃ hṛṣṭvā devaṃ visarjayet ।। prāṇināmaprabuddhānāṃ santoṣajananāya vai ।
āvāhanādikaṃ teṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ kathamanyathā ।। kālena tu vijānanti pravṛttāḥ patiśāsane । anukrameṇa devasya prāptiṃ bhuvanapūrvikām ।। jñānadīpadyutidhvastasamastājñānasañcayāḥ ।
kuto vānīyate devaḥ kutra vā nīyate api saḥ ।। sthūlasūkṣmādibhedena sa hi sarvatra saṃsthitaḥ । āvāhite mantragaṇe puṣpāsavanivedanaiḥ ।। dhūpaiśca tarpaṇaṃ kāryaṃ śraddhābhaktibalocitaiḥ ।
dīptānāṃ śaktinādādimantrāṇāmāsavaiḥ palaiḥ ।। raktaiḥ prāk tarpaṇa paścāt puṣpadhūpādivistaraiḥ । āgatasya tu mantrasya na kuryāttarpaṇaṃ yadi ।। haratyardhaśarīraṃ sa ityuktaṃ kila śambhunā ।
yadyadevāsya manasi vikāsitvaṃ prayacchati ।। tenaiva kuryātpūjāṃ sa iti śambhorviniścayaḥ । sādhakānāṃ bubhukṣūṇāṃ vidhirniyatiyantritaḥ ।। mumukṣūṇāṃ tattvavidāṃ sa eva tu nirargalaḥ ।
kārye viśeṣamādhitsurviśiṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ spṛśet ।। raktakarpāsatūlecchustulyatadbījapuñjavat । santi bhoge viśeṣāśca vicitrāḥ kāraṇeritāḥ ।। deśakālānusandhānaguṇadravyakriyādibhiḥ ।
svalpā kriyā bhūyasī vā hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ ।। bāhyaiḥ saṃkalpajairvāpi kārakaiḥ parikalpitā । mumukṣorna viśeṣāya naiḥśreyasavidhiṃ prati ।। nahi brahmaṇi śaṃsanti bāhulyālpatvadurdaśāḥ ।
citaḥ svātantryasāratvāt tasyānandaghanatvataḥ ।। kriyā syāttanmayībhūtyai hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ । śivābhedabharādbhāvavargaḥ ścyotati yaṃ rasam ।। tameva parame dhāmni pūjanāyārpayedbudhaḥ ।
stotreṣu bahudhā caitanmayā proktaṃ nijāhnike ।। adhiśayya pāramārthikabhāvaprasaraprakāśamullasati । yā paramāmṛtadṛk tvāṃ tayārcayante rahasyavidaḥ ।। kṛtvādhāradharāṃ camatkṛtirasaprokṣākṣaṇakṣālitāmāttairmānasataḥ svabhāvakusumaiḥ svāmodasandohibhiḥ ।
ānandāmṛtanirbharasvahṛdayānarghārghapātrakramāt tvāṃ devyā saha dehadevasadane devārcaye aharniśam ।। nānāsvādarasāmimāṃ trijagatīṃ hṛccakrayantrārpitāmūrdhvādhyastavivekagauravabharānniṣpīḍya niḥṣyanditam । yatsaṃvitparamāmṛtaṃ mṛtijarājanmāpahaṃ jṛmbhate tena tvāṃ haviṣā pareṇa parame saṃtarpaye aharniśam ।। iti ślokatrayopāttamarthamantarvibhāvayan ।
yena kenāpi bhāvena tarpayeddevatāgaṇam ।। mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścānmanasā vāpi yogataḥ । vacasā mantrayogena vapuṣā saṃniveśataḥ ।। kṛtvā japaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ devatāyai samarpayet ।
taccoktaṃ kartṛtātattvanirūpaṇavidhau purā ।। tato visarjanaṃ kāryaṃ bodhaikātmyaprayogataḥ । kṛtvā vā vahnigāṃ mantratṛptiṃ proktavidhānataḥ ।। dvārapīṭhaguruvrātasamarpitanivedanāt ।
ṛte anyatsvayamaśnīyādagādhe ambhasyatha kṣipet ।। prāṇino jalajāḥ pūrvadīkṣitāḥ śambhunā svayam । vidhinā bhāvinā śrīmanmīnanāthāvatāriṇā ।। mārjāramūṣikādyairyadadīkṣaiścāpi bhakṣitam ।
tacchaṅkātaṅkadānena vyādhaye narakāya ca ।। atastattvavidā dhvastaśaṅkātaṅko api paṇḍitaḥ । prakaṭaṃ nedṛśaṃ kuryāllokānugrahavāñchayā ।। śrīmanmatamahāśāstre taduktaṃ vibhunā svayam ।
svayaṃ tu śaṅkāsaṅkocaniṣkāsanaparāyaṇaḥ ।। bhavettathā yathānyeṣāṃ śaṅkā no manasi sphuret । mārjayitvā tataḥ snānaṃ puṣpeṇātha prapūjayet ।। puṣpādi sarvaṃ tatsthaṃ tadagādhāmbhasi nikṣipet ।
uktaḥ sthaṇḍilayāgo ayaṃ nityakarmaṇi śambhunā ।। athocyate liṅgapūjā sūcitā mālinīmate ।। eteṣāmūrdhvaśāstroktamantrāṇāṃ na pratiṣṭhitam । bahiṣkuryāttato hyete rahasyatvena siddhidāḥ ।।
svavīryānandamāhātmyapraveśavaśaśālinīm । ye siddhiṃ dadate teṣāṃ bāhyatvaṃ rūpavicyutiḥ ।। kiṃca coktaṃ samāveśapūrṇo bhoktrātmakaḥ śivaḥ । bhogalāmpaṭyabhāgbhogavicchede nigrahātmakaḥ ।।
śāntatvanyakkriyodbhūtajighatsāvṛṃhitaṃ vapuḥ । svayaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yena so asyābhoge vinaśyati ।। uktaṃ jñānottarāyāṃ ca tadetatparameśinā । śivo yāgapriyo yasmādviśeṣānmātṛmadhyagaḥ ।।
tasmādrahasyaśāstreṣu ye mantrāstānbudho bahiḥ । na pratiṣṭhāpayejjātu viśeṣādvyaktarūpiṇaḥ ।। ata eva mṛtasyārthe pratiṣṭhānyatra yoditā । sātra śāstreṣu no kāryā kāryā sādhāraṇī punaḥ ।।
ā tanmayatvasaṃsiddherā cābhīṣṭaphalodayāt । putrakaḥ sādhako vyaktamavyaktaṃ vā samāśrayet ।। putrakairgururabhyarthyaḥ sādhakastu svayaṃ vidan । yadi tatsthāpayenno cettenāpyarthyo gururbhavet ।।
guruścātra nirodhākhye kāla itthaṃ vibhau vadet । jīvatyasminphalāntaṃ tvaṃ tiṣṭherjīvāvadhīti vā ।। liṅgaṃ ca bāṇaliṅgaṃ vā ratnajaṃ vātha mauktikam । pauṣpamānnamatho vāstraṃ gandhadravyakṛtaṃ ca vā ।।
natu pāṣāṇajaṃ liṅgaṃ śilpyutthaṃ parikalpayet । dhātūtthaṃ ca suvarṇotthavarjamanyadvivarjayet ।। na cātra liṅgamānādi kvacidapyupayujyate । udāravīryairmantrairyadbhāsitaṃ phaladaṃ hi tat ।।
tasyāpi sthaṇḍilādyuktavidhinā śuddhimācaret । mantrārpaṇaṃ tathaiva syānnirodhastūktayuktitaḥ ।। agnau ca tarpaṇaṃ bhūriviśeṣāddakṣiṇā guroḥ । dīnāditṛptirvibhavādyāga ityadhiko vidhiḥ ।।
sarveṣvavyaktaliṅgeṣu pradhānaṃ syādakalpitam । tathā ca tatra tatroktaṃ lakṣaṇe pārameśvare ।। sūtre pātre dhvaje vastre svayambhūbāṇapūjite । nadīprasravaṇotthe ca nāhvānaṃ nāpi kalpanā ।।
pīṭhaprasādamantrāṃśavelādiniyamo naca । vyaktaṃ vā citrapustādau devadārusuvarṇajam ।। atha dīkṣitasacchilpikṛtaṃ sthāpayate guruḥ । athavā lakṣaṇopetamūrdhatatkarparāśritam ।।
paṅkticakrakaśūlābjavidhinā tūramāśrayet । tallakṣaṇaṃ bruve śrīmatpicuśāstre nirūpitam ।। tūre yogaḥ sadā śastaḥ siddhido doṣavarjite । jālakairjarjarai randhrairdantairūnādhikai rujā ।।
yukte ca tūre hāniḥ syāt taddhīne yāga uttamaḥ । kāmya eva bhavettūramiti kecitprapedire ।। guravastu vidhau kāmye yatnāddoṣāṃstyajediti । vyācakṣate picuproktaṃ na nitye karmaṇītyadaḥ ।।
śrīsiddhātantra uktaṃ ca tūralakṣaṇamuttamam । ekādikacatuṣkhaṇḍe gomukhe pūrṇacandrake ।। padmagorocanāmuktānīrasphaṭikasaṃnibhe । ekādipañcasadrandhravidyārekhānvite śubhe ।।
na rūkṣavakraśakaladīrghanimnasabinduke । ślakṣṇayā vajrasūcyātra sphuṭaṃ devīgaṇānvitam ।। sarvaṃ samālikhetpūjyaṃ sarvāvayavasundaram । etadevānusartavyamarghapātre api lakṣaṇam ।।
śrībrahmayāmale apyuktaṃ pātraṃ gomukhamuttamam । gajakūrmatalaṃ kumbhavṛttaśaktikajākṛti ।। akṣasūtramatho kuryāttatraivābhyarcayetkramam । vīradhātujalodbhūtamuktāratnasuvarṇajam ।।
akṣasūtraṃ kramotkṛṣṭaṃ raudrākṣaṃ vā viśeṣataḥ । śataṃ tithyuttaraṃ yadvā sāṣṭaṃ yadvā tadardhakam ।। tadardhaṃ vātha pañcāśadyuktaṃ tatparikalpayet । vaktrāṇi pañca citspandajñānecchākṛtisaṃgateḥ ।।
pañcadhādyantagaṃ caikyamityupāntyākṣago vidhiḥ । śaktitadvatprabhedena tatra dvairūpyamucyate ।। tato dviguṇamāne tu dvirūpaṃ nyāsamācaret । tato api dviguṇe sṛṣṭisaṃhṛtidvitayena tam ।।
mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vātha nyasyetkhaśarasaṃmite । uttame tu dvayīṃ nyasyennyasya pūrvaṃ pracoditān ।। dīkṣāyāṃ mukhyato mantrāṃstānpañcadaśa daiśikaḥ । yadi vā tattvabhuvanakalāmantrapadārṇajaiḥ ।।
saṃkhyābhedaiḥ kṛte sūtre taṃ taṃ nyāsaṃ guruścaret । kṛtvākṣasūtraṃ tasyāpi sarvaṃ sthaṇḍilavadbhavet ।। pūjitena ca tenaiva japaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ । vidhiruktastvayaṃ śrīmanmālinīvijayottare ।।
cakravadbhramayannetadyadvakti sa japo bhavet । yadīkṣate juhotyetadbodhāgnau saṃpraveśanāt ।। athavārghamahāpātraṃ kuryāttaccottaraṃ param । nārikelamatho bailvaṃ sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ ca vā ।।
tasyāpyeṣa vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pratiṣṭhādau prakīrtitaḥ । tanniṣkamparasaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kṛtvāsminpūjayetkramam ।। adhomukhaṃ sadā sthāpyaṃ pūjitaṃ pūjane punaḥ । tatpātramunmukhaṃ tacca riktaṃ kuryānna tādṛśam ।।
pūjānte tadrasāpūrṇamātmānaṃ pravidhāya tat । adhomukhaṃ ca saṃpūjya sthāpayet vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। khaṅgaṃ kṛpāṇikāṃ yadvā kartarīṃ makuraṃ ca vā । vimalaṃ tattathā kuryācchrīmatkālīmukhoditam ।।
śrībhairavakule apyuktaṃ kulaparvaprapūjane । sthaṇḍile agnau paṭe liṅge pātre padme atha maṇḍale ।। mūrtau ghaṭe astrasaṃghāte dhaṭe sūtre atha pūjayet । svena svenopacāreṇa saṅkaraṃ varjayediti ।।
yathāpsu śāntaye mantrāstadvadastrādiṣu dhruvam । śatrucchedādikartāraḥ kāmyo ataḥ saṅkarojjhitaḥ ।। akāmasya tu te tattatsthānopādhivaśāddhruvam । pāśakartanasaṃśuddhatattvāpyāyādikāriṇaḥ ।।
athavā pustakaṃ tādṛgrahaḥśāstrakramombhitam । suśuddhaṃ dīkṣitakṛtaṃ tatrāpyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। itthaṃ svayaṃpratiṣṭheṣu yāvadyāvatsthitirbhavet । vibhavaistarpaṇaṃ śuddhistāvadvicchedavarjanam ।।
ata eva yadā bhūridinaṃ maṇḍalakalpanam । tadā dine dine kuryādvibhavaistarpaṇaṃ bahu ।। pratiṣṭhāyāṃ ca sarvatra guruḥ pūrvoditaṃ param । satattvamanusandhāya saṃnidhiṃ sphuṭamācaret ।।
siddhe tu tanmayībhāve phale putrakasādhakaiḥ । anyasmai taddvayādanyatarasmai tatsamarpyate ।। tasyāpyeṣa vidhiḥ sarvastadalābhe tu sarvathā । agādhe ambhasi tatkṣepyaṃ kṣamayitvā visṛjya ca ।।
ityeṣa svapratiṣṭhānavidhiḥ śivanirūpitaḥ । parapratiṣṭhite liṅge bāṇīye atha svayaṃbhuvi ।। sarvamāsanapakṣe prāṅnyasya saṃpūjayetkramam । śuddhāśuddhādhvajāḥ sarve mantrāḥ sarvaḥ śivāntakaḥ ।।
adhvā cehāsane proktastatsarvatrārcayedidam । āvāhanavisṛṣṭī tu tatra prāgvatsamācaret ।। uktaṃ tantre apyaghoreśe svacchande vibhunā tathā । athavā pratyahaṃ proktamānārdhārdhaniyogataḥ ।।
kṛtveṣṭaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tatra samastaṃ kramamarcayet । bahuprakārabhinnasya liṅgasyārcā nirūpitā ।। iti nityavidhiḥ prokto naimittikamathocyate ।। niyataṃ bhāvi yannityaṃ tadityasminvidhau sthite ।
mukhyatvaṃ tanmayībhūtiḥ sarvaṃ naimittikaṃ tataḥ ।। dinādikalpanotthe tu naiyatye sarvanityatā । dinamāsarkṣavarṣādinaiyatyāducyate tadā ।। aśaṅkitavyāvaśyantāsattākaṃ jātucidbhavam ।
pramātraniyataṃ prāhurnaimittikamidaṃ budhāḥ ।। sandhyādi parvasaṃpūjā pavitrakamidaṃ sadā । nityaṃ niyatarūpatvātsarvasmin śāsanāśrite ।। jñānaśāstragurubhrātṛtadvargaprāptayastathā ।
tajjanmasaṃskriyābhedāḥ svajanmotsavasaṃgatiḥ ।। śrāddhaṃ vipatpratīkāraḥ pramodo adbhutadarśanam । yoginīmelakaḥ svāṃśasantānādyaiśca melanam ।। śāstravyākhyāpurāmadhyāvasānāni kramodayaḥ ।
devatādarśanaṃ svāpnamājñā samayaniṣkṛtiḥ ।। iti naimittikaṃ śrīmattantrasāre nirūpitam । trayoviṃśatibhedena viśeṣārcānibandhanam ।। tatra parvavidhiṃ brūmo dvidhā parva kulākulam ।
kulāṣṭakakṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ proktaṃ śrīyogasaṃcare ।। abdhīndu munirityetanmāheśyā brahmasantateḥ । pratipatpañcadaśyau dve kaumāryā rasavahniyuk ।। abdhirakṣīndu vaiṣṇavyā aindryāstvastraṃ trayodaśī ।
vārāhyā randhrarudrau dve caṇḍyā vasvakṣiyugmakam ।। dve dve tithī tu sarvāsāṃ yogeśyā daśamī punaḥ । tasyā apyaṣṭamī yasmāddvitithiḥ sā prakīrtitā ।। anyāścākulaparvāpi vaiparītyena lakṣitam ।
kulaparveti tadbrūmo yathoktaṃ bhairave kule ।। haiḍare trikasadbhāve trikakālīkulādike । yo ayaṃ prāṇāśritaḥ pūrvaṃ kālaḥ proktaḥ suvistarāt ।। sa cakrabhedasaṃcāre kāṃcit sūte svasaṃvidam ।
svasaṃvitpūrṇatālābhasamayaḥ parva bhaṇyate ।। parva pūraṇa ityeva yadvā pṝ pūraṇārthakaḥ । parvaśabdo niruktaśca parva tatpūraṇāditi ।। haiḍare atra ca śabdo ayaṃ dvidhā nāntetaraḥ śrutaḥ ।
taccakracāraniṣṇātā ye kecit pūrṇasaṃvidaḥ ।। tanmelakasamāyuktāste tatpūjāparāḥ sadā । yo apyatanmaya eṣo api tatkāle svakramārcanāt ।। tadyoginīsiddhasaṅghamelakāt tanmayībhavet ।
yathā prekṣaṇake tattaddraṣṭṛsaṃvidabheditām ।। kramoditāṃ sadya eva labhate tatpraveśanāt । yogābhyāsakramopāttāṃ tathā pūrṇāṃ svasaṃvidam ।। labhante sadya evaitatsaṃvidaikyapraveśanāt ।
tatkālaṃ cāpi saṃvitteḥ pūrṇatvāt kāmadogdhṛtā ।। tena tattatphalaṃ tatra kāle saṃpūjayācirāt । yathā ciropāttadhanaḥ kurvannutsavamādarāt ।। atithiṃ so anugṛhṇāti tatkālābhijñamāgatam ।
tathā suphalasaṃsiddhyai yoginīsiddhanāyakāḥ ।। yatnavanto api tatkālābhijñaṃ tamanugṛhṇate । uktaṃ ca tatra teneha kule sāmānyatetyalam ।। yasya yaddhṛdaye devi vartate daiśikājñayā ।
mantro yogaḥ kramaścaiva pūjanāt siddhido bhavet ।। kulācāreṇa deveśi pūjyaṃ siddhivimuktaye । ye parvasveṣu deveśi tarpaṇaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।। gurūṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca na kurvanti pramādataḥ ।
durācārā hi te duṣṭāḥ paśutulyā varānane ।। abhāvānnityapūjāyā avaśyaṃ hyeṣu pūjayet । aṭanaṃ jñānaśaktyādilābhārthaṃ yatprakīrtitam ।। śaktiyāgaśca yaḥ prokto vaśyākarṣaṇamāraṇam ।
tatsarvaṃ parvadivaseṣvayatnenaiva siddhyati ।। tatsāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ ṣoḍhā parva nirūpitam । māsasyādyaṃ pañcamaṃ ca śrīdinaṃ paribhāṣyate ।। utkṛṣṭatvāt parvadinaṃ śrīpūrvatvena bhāṣyate ।
samayo hyeṣa yadguptaṃ tannānupapadaṃ vadet ।। turyāṣṭamānyabhuvanacaramāṇi dvayorapi । pakṣayoriha sāmānyasāmānyaṃ parva kīrtitam ।। yadeteṣu dineṣveva bhaviṣyadgrahabhātmakaḥ ।
ubhayātmā viśeṣaḥ syāttatsāmānyaviśeṣatā ।। sā caikādaśadhaikasminnekasminvibhunoditā । sajātīyā tu sotkṛṣṭetyevaṃ śambhurnyarūpayat ।। kṛṣṇayugaṃ vahnisitaṃ śrutikṛṣṇaṃ vahnisitamiti pakṣāḥ ।
arkendujīvacandrā budhayugmendvarkakaviguruvidhu syāt ।। paraphalguścaitramaghe tiṣyaḥ prākphalgukarṇaśatabhiṣajaḥ । mūlaprājāpatye viśākhikā śravaṇasaṃjñayā bhāni ।। randhre tithyarkapare vasurandhre śaśivṛṣāṅkarasarandhrayugam ।
prathamaniśāmadhyaniśe madhyāhnaśarā dinodayo madhyadinam ।। prathamaniśeti ca samayo mārgaśiraḥprabhṛtimāseṣu । kanyāntyajātha veśyā rāgavatī tattvavedinī dūtī ।। vyāsasamāsāt kramaśaḥ pūjyāścakre anuyāgākhye ।
sarvatra ca parvadine kuryādanuyāgacakramatiśayataḥ ।। guptāguptavidhānādiyāgacaryākrameṇa sampūrṇam । anuyāgaḥ kila mukhyaḥ sarvasminneva karmaviniyoge ।। anuyāgakālalābhe tasmātprayateta tatparamaḥ ।
bhagrahasamayaviśeṣo nāśvayuje ko api tena tadvarjam ।। velābhagrahakalanā kathitaikādaśasu māseṣu । phālgunamāse śuklaṃ yatproktaṃ dvādaśīdinaṃ parva ।। agratithivedhayogo mukhyatamo asau viśeṣo atra ।
divasaniśe kila kṛtvā tribhāgaśaḥ prathamamadhyamāparavibhāgaḥ ।। pūjākālastatra tribhāgite mukhyatamaḥ kālaḥ । yadi saṃghaṭeta velā mukhyatamā bhagrahau tathā cakram ।। tadyāga ādiyāgastatkāmyaṃ pūjayaiva parvasu siddhyet ।
dinavelābhagrahakalpanena tatrāpi saumyaraudratvam ।। jñātvā sādhakamukhyastattatkāryaṃ tadā tadā kuryāt । ukto yo arcākālastaṃ cedullaṅghya bhagrahatithiḥ syāt ।। tamanādṛtya viśeṣaṃ pradhānayetsāmayamiti kecit ।
neti tvasmadguravo viśeṣarūpā hi tithiriha na velā ।। saṃvedyarūpaśaśadharabhāgaḥ saṃvedakārkakaranikaraiḥ । yāvānyāvati pūrṇaḥ sā hi tithirbhagrahaiḥ sphuṭībhavati ।। tasmānmukhyātra tithiḥ sā ca viśeṣyā graharkṣayogena ।
velātra na pradhānaṃ yuktaṃ caitattathāhi parameśaḥ ।। śrītrikabhairavakulaśāstreṣūce na parvadivaseṣu । velāyogaṃ kaṃcana tithibhagrahayogato hyanyam ।। tithistu pūjyā pradhānarūpatvāt ।
śvetābhāve kṛṣṇacchāgālambhaṃ hi kathayanti ।। yatpunarūrmiprabhṛtini śāstre veloditāpi tatkāmyam । mukhyatayoddiśya vidhiṃ tathāca tatra pauṣaparvadine ।। kṛtvārcanamardhaniśi dhyātvā japtvā bahirgatasya yathā ।
ādeśaḥ phalati tathā māghe cakrādvacaḥ phalati ।। acirādabhīṣṭasiddhiḥ pañcasu maitrī dhanaṃ ca melāpaḥ । cakrasthāne krodhāt pāṣāṇasphoṭanena ripunāśaḥ ।। siddhādeśaprāptirmārgāntaṃ kathyate vibhunā ।
bhagrahayogābhāve velāṃ tu titheravaśyamīkṣeta ।। sā hi tathā sphuṭarūpā titheḥ svabhāvodayaṃ dadyāt । bhagrahatithivelāṃśānuyāyi sarvāṅgasundaraṃ tu dinam ।। yadi labhyeta tadāsminviśeṣatamapūjanaṃ racayet ।
naca kāmyameva kevalametatparivarjane yataḥ kathitaḥ ।। samayavilopaḥ śrīmadbhairavakula ūrmiśāstre ca । duṣṭā hi durācārāḥ paśutulyāḥ parva ye na viduḥ ।। naca kāmyasyākaraṇe syājjātu pratyavāyitvam ।
tatrānuyāgasiddhyarthaṃ cakrayāgo nirūpyate ।। mūrtiyāga iti prokto yaḥ śrīyogīśvarīmate । nityaṃ naimittikaṃ karma yadatroktaṃ maheśinā ।। sarvatra cakrayāgo atra mukhyaḥ kāmye viśeṣataḥ ।
jñānī yogī ca puruṣaḥ strī vāsminmūrtisaṃjñake ।। yoge prayatnato yojyastaddhi pātramanuttaram । tatsaṃparkātpūrṇatā syāditi traiśirasādiṣu ।। tena sarvaṃ hutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
jñānine yogine vāpi yo dadāti karoti vā ।। dīkṣottare api ca proktamannaṃ brahmā raso hariḥ । bhoktā śiva iti jñānī śvapacānapyathoddhareat ।। sarvatattvamayo bhūtvā yadi bhuṅkte sa sādhakaḥ ।
tena bhojitamātreṇa sakṛtkoṭistu bhojitā ।। atha tattvavidetasminyadi bhuñjīta tat priye । parisaṃkhyā na vidyeta tadāha bhagavāñchivaḥ ।। bhojyaṃ māyātmakaṃ sarvaṃ śivo bhoktā sa cāpyaham ।
evaṃ yo vai vijānāti daiśikastattvapāragaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamāyāntaṃ krīḍantyoṣadhayo gṛhe । nivṛttamadyaivāsmābhiḥ saṃsāragahanārṇavāt ।। yadasya vaktraṃ saṃprāptā yāsyāmaḥ paramaṃ padam ।
anye apānabhujo hyūrdhve prāṇo apānastvadhomukhaḥ ।। tasminbhoktari deveśi dātuḥ kulaśatānyapi । āśveva parimucyante narakādyātanārṇavāt ।। śrīmanniśāṭane apyuktaṃ kathanānveṣaṇādapi ।
śrotrābhyantarasaṃprāpte guruvaktrādvinirgate ।। muktastadaiva kāle tu yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam । surāpaḥ steyahārī ca brahmahā gurutalpagaḥ ।। antyajo vā dvijo vātha bālo vṛddho yuvāpi vā ।
paryantavāsī yo jñānī deśasyāpi pavitrakaḥ ।। tatra saṃnihito devaḥ sadevīkaḥ sakiṅkaraḥ । tasmātprādhānyataḥ kṛtvā guruṃ jñānaviśāradam ।। mūrtiyāgaṃ carettasya vidhiryogīśvarīmate ।
pavitrārohaṇe śrāddhe tathā parvadineṣvalam ।। sūryacandroparāgādau laukikeṣvapi parvasu । utsave ca vivāhādau viprāṇāṃ yajñakarmaṇi ।। dīkṣāyāṃ ca pratiṣṭhāyāṃ samayānāṃ viśodhane ।
kāmanārthaṃ ca kartavyo mūrtiyāgaḥ sa pañcadhā ।। kevalo yāmalo miśraścakrayugvīrasaṅkaraḥ । kevalaḥ kevalaireva gurubhirmiśritaḥ punaḥ ।। sādhakādyaiḥ sapatnīkairyāmalaḥ sa dvidhā punaḥ ।
patnīyogāt krayānītaveśyāsaṃyogato athavā ।। cakriṇyādyāśca vakṣyante śaktiyogādyathocitāḥ । tatsaṃyogāccakrayukto yāgaḥ sarvaphalapradaḥ ।। sarvaistu sahito yāgo vīrasaṅkara ucyate ।
madhye gururbhavetteṣāṃ guruvargastadāvṛtiḥ ।। tisra āvṛtayo bāhye samayyantā yathākramam । paṅktikrameṇa vā sarve madhye teṣāṃ guruḥ sadā ।। tadā tadgandhadhūpasraksamālambhanavāsasā ।
pūjyaṃ cakrānusāreṇa tattaccakramidaṃ tviti ।। ekārake yathā cakre ekavīravidhiṃ smaret । dvyare yāmalamanyatra trikamevaṃ ṣaḍasrake ।। ṣaḍyoginīḥ saptakaṃ ca saptāre aṣṭāṣṭake ca vā ।
anyadvā tādṛśaṃ tatra cakre tādṛksvarūpiṇi ।। tataḥ pātre alisaṃpūrṇe pūrvaṃ cakraṃ yajetsudhīḥ । ādhārayukte nādhārarahitaṃ tarpaṇaṃ kvacit ।। ādhāreṇa vinā bhraṃśo naca tuṣyanti raśmayaḥ ।
pretarūpaṃ bhavetpātraṃ śāktāmṛtamathāsavaḥ ।। bhoktrī tatra tu yā śaktiḥ sa śambhuḥ parameśvaraḥ । aṇuśaktiśivātmetthaṃ dhyātvā saṃmilitaṃ trayam ।। tatastu tarpaṇaṃ kāryamāvṛterāvṛteḥ kramāt ।
pratisaṃcarayogena punarantaḥ praveśayet ।। yāvadgurvantikaṃ taddhi pūrṇaṃ bhramaṇamucyate । tatrādau devatāstarpyāstato vīrā iti kramaḥ ।। vīraśca vīraśaktiścetyevamasmadgurukramaḥ ।
tato avadaṃśānvividhān māṃsamatsyādisaṃyutān ।। agre tatra pravikiret tṛptyantaṃ sādhakottamaḥ । pātrābhāve punarbhadraṃ vellitāśuktimeva ca ।। pātre kurvīta matimāniti siddhāmate kramaḥ ।
dakṣahastena bhadraṃ syādvellitā śuktirucyate ।। dakṣahastasya kurvīta vāmopari kanīyasīm । tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayogena dakṣādho vāmakāṅgulīḥ ।। niḥsandhibandhau dvāvitthaṃ vellitā śuktirucyate ।
ye tatra pānakāle tu bindavo yānti medinīm ।। taistuṣyanti hi vetālaguhyakādyā gabhastayaḥ । dhārayā bhairavastuṣyet karapānaṃ paraṃ tataḥ ।। praveśo atra na dātavyaḥ pūrvameva hi kasyacit ।
pramādāttu praviṣṭasya vicāraṃ naiva carcayet ।। evaṃ kṛtvā kramādyāgamante dakṣiṇayā yutam । samālambhanatāmbūlavastrādyaṃ vitaredbudhaḥ ।। rūpakārdhāt paraṃ hīnāṃ na dadyāddakṣiṇāṃ sudhīḥ ।
samayibhyaḥ kramāddvidviguṇā gurvantakaṃ bhavet ।। eṣa syānmūrtiyāgastu sarvayāgapradhānakaḥ । kāmye tu saṃvidhau saptakṛtvaḥ kāryastathāvidhaḥ ।। jānanti prathamaṃ gehaṃ tatastasya samarthatām ।
balābalaṃ tataḥ paścādvismayante atra mātaraḥ ।। tato api saṃnidhīyante prīyante varadāstataḥ । devīnāmatha nāthasya parivārayujo apyalam ।। vallabho mūrtiyāgo ayamataḥ kāryo vipaścitā ।
rāktau gupte gṛhe vīrāḥ śaktayo anyonyamapyalam ।। asaṃketayujo yojyā devatāśabdakīrtanāt । alābhe mūrticakrasya kumārīreva pūjayet ।। kāmyārthe tu na tāṃ vyaṅgāṃ stanapuṣpavatīṃ tathā ।
pratipacchrutisaṃjñe ca caturthī cottarātraye ।। haste ca pañcamī ṣaṣṭhī pūrvāsvatha punarvasau । saptamī tatparā pitrye rohiṇyāṃ navamī tathā ।। mūle tu dvādaśī brāhme bhūtāśvinyāṃ ca pūrṇimā ।
dhaniṣṭhāyāmamāvasyā so ayamekādaśātmakaḥ ।। arkāditrayaśukrānyatamayukto apyahargaṇaḥ । yogaparveti vikhyāto rātrau vā dina eva vā ।। yogaparvaṇi kartavyo mūrtiyāgastu sarvathā ।
yaḥ sarvānyogaparvākhyān vāsarān pūjayetsudhīḥ ।। mūrtiyāgena so api syāt samayī maṇḍalaṃ vinā । ityeṣa mūrtiyāgaḥ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate ।। athocyate śivenoktaḥ pavitrakavidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ ।
śrīratnamālātriśiraḥśāstrayoḥ sūcitaḥ punaḥ ।। śrīsiddhāṭanasadbhāvamālinīsāraśāsane । tatra prādhānyataḥ śrīmanmālokto vidhirucyate ।। kṣīrābdhimathanodbhūtaviṣanidrāvimūrcchitaḥ ।
nāgarājaḥ svabhuvane meghakāle sma nāvasat ।। kevalaṃ tu pavitro ayaṃ vāyubhakṣaḥ samāḥ śatam । divyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ nāthaṃ bhairavaṃ paryapūjayat ।। vyajijñapacca taṃ tuṣṭaṃ nāthaṃ varṣāsvahaṃ nije ।
pātāle nāsituṃ śaktaḥ so apyenaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। nāgaṃ nijajaṭājūṭapīṭhagaṃ paryakalpayat । tataḥ samastadevaughairdhārito asau svamūrdhani ।। mahatāṃ mahitānāṃ hi nādbhuta viśvapūjyatā ।
tasmānmaheśiturmūrdhni devatānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। ātmanaśca pavitraṃ taṃ kuryādyāgapuraḥsaram । daśa koṭyo na pūjānāṃ pavitrārohaṇe samāḥ ।। vṛthā dīkṣā vṛthā jñānaṃ gurvārādhanameva ca ।
vinā pavitrādyenaitaddharennāgaḥ śivājñayā ।। tasmātsarvaprayatnena sa kāryaḥ kulavedibhiḥ । āṣāḍhaśuklānmithunakarkaṭasthe ravau vidhiḥ ।। kartavyaḥ so anirodhena yāvatsā tulapūrṇimā ।
tulopalakṣitasyāntyaṃ kārtikasya dinaṃ matam ।। kulaśabdaṃ paṭhanto anye vyākhyābhedaṃ prakurvate । nityātantravidaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kārtikāccaramaṃ dinam ।। kulasya nityācakrasya pūrṇatvaṃ yatra tanmatam ।
māghaśuklāntyadivasaḥ kulaparveti tanmatam ।। pūrṇatvaṃ tatra candrasya sā tithiḥ kulapūrṇimā । dakṣiṇottaragaḥ kālaḥ kulākulatayoditaḥ ।। kulasya tasya carame dine pūrṇatvamucyate ।
dakṣiṇāyanaṣaṇmāsakartavyatvamato vidhau ।। pavitrake prakāśatvasiddhyai kṛṣṇasya vartmanaḥ । tadetadbahuśāstroktaṃ rūpaṃ devo nyarūpayat ।। ekenaiva padena śrīratnamālākulāgame ।
tadatra samaye sarvavidhisaṃpūraṇātmakaḥ ।। pavitrakavidhiḥ kāryaḥ śuklapakṣe tu sarvathā । pūraṇaṃ śaktiyogena śaktyātma ca sitaṃ dalam ।। dakṣiṇāyanasājātyāt tena tadvidhirucyate ।
ekadvitricatuḥpañcaṣaḍlataikatamaṃ mahat ।। hemaratnāṅkitagranthi kuryānmuktāpavitrakam । sauvarṇasūtraṃ triguṇaṃ saikagranthiśataṃ gurau ।। pare gurau tu tryadhikamadhyabdhi parameṣṭhini ।
prāksiddhācāryayogeśa viṣaye tu rasādhikam ।। aṣṭādhikaṃ śivasyoktaṃ citraratnaprapūritam । vidyāpīṭhākṣasūtrādau guruvacchivavat punaḥ ।। vaṭuke kanakābhāve raupyaṃ tu parikalpayet ।
pāṭṭasūtramatha kṣaumaṃ kārpāsaṃ tritritānitam ।। tasmānnavaguṇāt sūtrāttriguṇādikramāt kuru । caṇḍāṃśuguṇaparyantaṃ tato api triguṇaṃ ca vā ।। tenāṣṭādaśatantūtthamadhamaṃ madhyamaṃ punaḥ ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ tasmāt triguṇaṃ tūttamaṃ matam ।। granthayastattvasaṃkhyātāḥ ṣaḍadhvakalanāvaśāt । yadvā vyāsasamāsābhyāṃ citrāḥ sadgandhapūritāḥ ।। viśeṣavidhinā pūrvaṃ pūjayitvārpayettataḥ ।
pavitrakaṃ samastādhvaparipūrṇatvabhāvanāt ।। gurvātmanorjānunābhikaṇṭhamūrdhāntagaṃ ca vā । tato mahotsavaḥ kāryo gurupūjāpuraḥsaraḥ ।। tarpyāḥ śāsanagāḥ sarve dakṣiṇāvastrabhojanaiḥ ।
mahotsavaḥ prakartavyo gītanṛttātmako mahān ।। cāturmāsyaṃ saptadinaṃ tridinaṃ vāpyalābhataḥ । tadante kṣamayeddevaṃ maṇḍalādi visarjayet ।। vahniṃ ca paścātkartavyaścakrayāgaḥ puroditaḥ ।
māse māse caturmāse varṣe vāpi pavitrakam ।। sarvathaiva prakartavyaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram । vittābhāve punaḥ kāryaṃ kāśairapi kuśombhitaiḥ ।। sati vitte punaḥ śāṭhyaṃ vyādhaye narakāya ca ।
nityapūjāsu pūrṇatvaṃ parvapūjāprapūraṇāt ।। tatrāpi paripūrṇatvaṃ pavitrakasamarcanāt । pavitrakavilope tu prāyaścittaṃ japetsudhīḥ ।। suśuddhaḥ sanpunaḥ kuryādityājñā parameśituḥ ।
atha triśirasi prokto likhyate tadvidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ ।। triprameyasya śaivasya pañcapañcātmakasya vā । daśāṣṭādaśabhedasya ṣaṭsrotasa ihocyate ।। ye narāḥ samayabhraṣṭā guruśāstrādidūṣakāḥ ।
nityanaimittikādyanyaparvasandhivivarjitāḥ ।। akāmāt kāmato vāpi sūkṣmapāpapravartinaḥ । teṣāṃ praśamanārthāya pavitraṃ kriyate śive ।। śrāvaṇādau kārtikānte śuklapakṣe śubhaprade ।
natu duḥkhaprade kṛṣṇe kartṛrāṣṭranṛpādiṣu ।। pāṭṭasūtraṃ tu kauśeyaṃ kārpāsaṃ kṣaumameva ca । cāturāśramikāṇāṃ tu subhruvā kartitokṣitam ।। tridhā tu triguṇīkṛtya mānasaṃkhyāṃ tu kārayet ।
aṣṭottaraṃ tantuśataṃ tadardhaṃ vā tadardhakam ।। hrāsastu pūrvasaṃkhyāyā daśabhirdaśabhiḥ kramāt । navabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ saptaviṃśatyā vā śivāditaḥ ।। yādṛśastantuvinyāso granthīnkuryāttu tāvataḥ ।
catuḥsamaviliptāṃstānathavā kuṅkumena tu ।। vyakte jānutaṭāntaṃ syālliṅge pīṭhāvasānakam । arcāsu śobhanaṃ mūrghni tritattvaparikalpanāt ।। dvādaśagranthiśaktīnāṃ brahmavaktrārciṣāmapi ।
vidyāpīṭhe cale liṅge sthaṇḍile ca gurorgaṇe ।। ghaṇṭāyāṃ sruksruve śiṣyaliṅgiṣu dvāratoraṇe । svadehe vahnipīṭhe ca yathāśobhaṃ tadiṣyate ।। prāsāde yāgagehe ca kārayennavaraṅgikam ।
vidyāpīṭhe tu khaśarāḥ pratimāliṅgapīṭhagam ।। vasuvedaṃ ca ghaṇṭāyāṃ śarākṣyaṣṭādaśa sruve । vedākṣi sruci ṣaṭtriṃśat prāsāde maṇḍape raviḥ ।। rasendu snānagehe abdhinetre dhyānagṛhe gurau ।
sapta sādhakagāḥ pañca putrake sapta sāmaye ।। catvāro athānyaśāstrasthe śiṣye pañcakamucyate । liṅgināṃ kevalo granthistoraṇe daśa kalpayet ।। dvāreṣvaṣṭau granthayaḥ syuḥ kṛtvetthaṃ tu pavitrakam ।
pūjayitvā mantrajālaṃ tatsthatvātmasthate tataḥ ।। pavitrakāṇāṃ saṃpādya kuryātsaṃpātasaṃskriyām । tataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ dhyāyedbhairavaṃ chidrasākṣiṇam ।। dattvā pūrṇāhutiṃ devi praṇamenmantrabhairavam ।
oṃ samastakriyādoṣapūraṇeśa vrataṃ prati ।। yatkiṃcidakṛtaṃ duṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ vā mātṛnandana । tatsarvaṃ mama deveśa tvatprasādātpraṇaśyatu ।। sarvathā raśmicakreśa namastubhyaṃ prasīda me ।
anena dadyāddevāya nimantraṇapavitrakam ।। yoginīkṣetramātṝṇāṃ baliṃ dadyāttato guruḥ । pañcagavyaṃ caruṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ śiṣyaiḥ samantataḥ ।। ācārya nidrāṃ kurvīta prātarutthāya cāhnikam ।
tato vidhiṃ pūjayitvā pavitrāṇi samāharet ।। dantakāṣṭhaṃ mṛcca dhātrī samṛddhātrī sahāmbunā । catuḥsamaṃ ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ bhasma pañcasu yojayet ।। prāgdakṣapaścimordhvasthavāmavaktreṣu vai kramāt ।
pañcaitāni pavitrāṇi sthāpayecceśagocare ।। kuśedhma pañcagavyaṃ ca śarvāgre viniyojayet । vāmāmṛtādisaṃyuktaṃ naivedyaṃ trividhaṃ tataḥ ।। dadyādasṛk tathā madyaṃ pānāni vividhāni ca ।
tato homo mahākṣmājamāṃsaistilayutairatho ।। tilairghṛtayutairyadvā taṇḍulairatha dhānyakaiḥ । śarkarākhaṇḍasaṃyuktapañcāmṛtapariplutaiḥ ।। mūlaṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭoktaṃ triśaktau brahmavaktrakam ।
arciṣāṃ tu śataṃ sāṣṭaṃ tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet ।। tato añjalau pavitraṃ tu gṛhītvā prapaṭhedidam । akāmādathavā kāmādyanmayā na kṛtaṃ vibho ।। tadacchidraṃ mamāstvīśa pavitreṇa tavājñayā ।
mūlamantraḥ pūrayeti kriyāniyamamityatha ।। vauṣaḍantaṃ pavitraṃ ca dadyādbindvavasānakam । nādāntaṃ samanāntaṃ cāpyunmanāntaṃ kramāttrayam ।। evaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ dadyādanulomena bhautikaḥ ।
naiṣṭhikastu vilomena pavitrakacatuṣṭayam ।। yatkiñcidvividhaṃ vastracchatrālaṅkaraṇādikam । tannivedyaṃ dīpamālāḥ suvarṇatilabhājanam ।। vastrayugmayutaṃ sarvasampūraṇanimittataḥ ।
bhojanīyāḥ pūjanīyāḥ śivabhaktāstu śaktitaḥ ।। catustridvyekamāsādidinaikāntaṃ mahotsavam । kuryāttato na vrajeyuranyasthānaṃ kadācana ।। tatastu daiśikaḥ pūjyo gāmasmai kṣīriṇīṃ navām ।
dadyātsuvarṇaratnādirupyavastravibhūṣitām ।। vadedguruśca saṃpūrṇo vidhistava bhavatviti । vaktavyaṃ devadevasya punarāgamanāya ca ।। tato visarjanaṃ kāryaṃ guptamābharaṇādikam ।
naivedyaṃ gururādāya yāgārthe tanniyojayet ।। caturṇāmapi sāmānyaṃ pavitrakamiti smṛtam । nāsmādvrataṃ paraṃ kiñcit kā vāsya stutirucyate ।। śeṣaṃ tvagādhe vāryoghe kṣipenna sthāpayetsthiram ।
atha naimittikavidhiryaḥ purāsūtrito mayā ।। sa bhaṇyate tatra kāryā devasyārcā viśeṣataḥ । cakrayāgaśca kartavyaḥ pūrvoktavidhinā budhaiḥ ।। tatra yadyannijābhīṣṭabhogamokṣopakārakam ।
pāramparyeṇa sākṣādvā bhaveccidacidātmakam ।। tatpūjyaṃ tadupāyāśca pūjyāstanmayatāptaye । tadupāyo api saṃpūjyo mūrtikālakriyādikaḥ ।। upeyasūtisāmarthyamupāyatvaṃ tadarcanāt ।
tadrūpatanmayībhāvādupeyaṃ śīghramāpnuyāt ।। yathā yathā ca naikaṭyamupāyeṣu tathā tathā । avaśyaṃbhāvi kāryatvaṃ viśeṣāccārcanādike ।। jñānasya kasyacitprāptirbhogamokṣopakāriṇaḥ ।
yadā tanmukhyamevoktaṃ naimittikadinaṃ budhaiḥ ।। tadupāyaḥ śāstramatra vaktāpyaupayiko guruḥ । tadvidyo api gurubhrātā saṃvādājjñānadāyakaḥ ।। guroḥ patnī tathā bhrātā putra ityādiko gaṇaḥ ।
na yonisaṃbandhavaśādvidyāsaṃbandhajastu saḥ ।। vīryāruṇaparīṇāmadehāhantāpratiṣṭhitāḥ । dehopakārasantānā jñāteye pariniṣṭhitāḥ ।। tathāca smṛtiśāstreṣu santaterdāyahāritā ।
yuktaiva tāvānsa hyukto bhedāddūrāntikatvataḥ ।। ye tu tyaktaśarīrāsthā bodhāhambhāvabhāginaḥ । bodhopakārasantānadvayātte bandhutājuṣaḥ ।। tatretthaṃ prāgyadā paśyecchaktyunmīlitadṛkkriyaḥ ।
dehastāvadayaṃ pūrvapūrvopādānanirmitaḥ ।। ātmā vikārarahitaḥ śāśvatatvādahetukaḥ । svātantryāt punarātmīyādayaṃ channa iva sthitaḥ ।। punaśca prakaṭībhūya bhairavībhāvabhājanam ।
tatrāsya prakaṭībhāve bhuktimuktyātmake bhṛśam ।। ya upāyaḥ samucito jñānasantāna eṣa saḥ । kramasphuṭībhavattādṛksadṛśajñānadhārayā ।। galadvijātīyatayā prāpyaṃ śīghraṃ hi labhyate ।
evaṃ cānādisaṃsārocitavijñānasantateḥ ।। dhvaṃse lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ santānāntaratāṃ śrayet । asaṃsārocitodāratathāvijñānasantateḥ ।। kāraṇaṃ mukhyamādyaṃ tadguruvijñānamātmagam ।
atyantaṃ svaviśeṣāṇāṃ tatrārpaṇavaśāt sphuṭam ।। upādānaṃ hi tadyuktaṃ dehabhede hi satyapi । dehasantatigau bhedābhedau vijñānasantateḥ ।। na tathātvāya yogīcchāviṣṭaśāvaśarīravat ।
yoginaḥ paradehādijīvattāpādane nijam ।। dehamatyajato nānājñānopādānatā na kim । tena vijñānasantānaprādhānyādyaunasantateḥ ।। anyonyaṃ gurusantāno yaḥ śivajñānaniṣṭhitaḥ ।
itthaṃ sthite trayaṃ mukhyaṃ kāraṇaṃ sahakāri ca ।। ekakāraṇakāryaṃ ca vastvityeṣa gurorgaṇaḥ । guruḥ kāraṇamatroktaṃ tatpatnī sahakāriṇī ।। yato niḥśaktikasyāsya na yāge adhikṛtirbhavet ।
antaḥsthodārasaṃvittiśakterbāhyāṃ vināpi tām ।। sāmarthyaṃ yogino yadvadvināpi sahakāriṇam । ekajanyā bhrātaraḥ syustatsadṛgyastu ko api saḥ ।। punaḥ paramparāyogādguruvargo api bhaṇyate ।
mukhya eṣa tu santānaḥ pūjyo mānyaśca sarvadā ।। gurvādīnāṃ ca sambhūtau dīkṣāyāṃ prāyaṇe api ca । yadahastaddhi vijñānopāyadehādikāraṇam ।। evaṃ svajanmadivaso vijñānopāya ucyate ।
tādṛgbhogāpavargādihetordehasya kāraṇam ।। dīkṣādikaśca saṃskāraḥ svātmano yatra cāhni tat । bhavejjanmadinaṃ mukhyaṃ jñānasantānajanmataḥ ।। svakaṃ mṛtidinaṃ yattu tadanyeṣāṃ bhaviṣyati ।
naimittikaṃ mṛto yasmācchivābhinnastadā bhavet ।। tatra prasaṅgānmaraṇasvarūpaṃ brūmahe sphuṭam । vyāpako api śivaḥ svecchākḷptasaṅkocamudraṇāt ।। vicitraphalakarmaughavaśāttattaccharīrabhāk ।
śarīrabhāktvaṃ caitāvadyattadgarbhasthadehagaḥ ।। saṃvitteḥ śūnyarūḍhāyāḥ prathamaḥ prāṇanodayaḥ । garbhasthadehanirmāṇe tasyaiveśvaratā punaḥ ।। asaṅkocasya tanvādikartā teneśa ucyate ।
sa vāyvātmā dṛḍhe tasmindehayantre cidātmanā ।। preryamāṇo vicarati bhastrāyantragavāyuvat । ataḥ prāggāḍhasaṃsuptotthitavatsa prabuddhyate ।। kramāddehena sākaṃ ca prāṇanā syādbalīyasī ।
tatrāpi karmaniyatibalātsā prāṇanākṣatām ।। gṛhṇāti śūnyasuṣirasaṃvitsparśādhikatvataḥ । evaṃ krameṇa saṃpuṣṭadehaprāṇabalo bhṛśam ।। bhogānkarmakṛtānbhuṅkte yonyayonijadehagaḥ ।
uktaṃ ca gahvarābhikhye śāstre śītāṃśumaulinā ।। yathā gṛhaṃ viniṣpādya gṛhī samadhitiṣṭhati । tathā dehī tanuṃ kṛtvā kriyādiguṇavarjitaḥ ।। kiñcitsphuraṇamātraḥ prāgniṣkalaḥ so api śabdyate ।
sphuṭendriyāditattvastu sakalātmeti bhaṇyate ।। ityādi śrīgahvaroktaṃ tata eva paṭhedbahu । kṣaye tu karmaṇāṃ teṣāṃ dehayantre anyathāgate ।। prāṇayantraṃ vighaṭate dehaḥ syātkuḍyavattataḥ ।
nāḍīcakreṣu saṅkocavikāsau viparītataḥ ।। bhaṅgaḥ śoṣaḥ klidirvātaśleṣmāgnyapacayoccayaiḥ । ityevamādi yatkiñcit prāksaṃsthānopamardakam ।। dehayantre vighaṭanaṃ tadevoktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।
tasminvighaṭite yantre sā saṃvitprāṇanātmatām ।। gṛhṇāti yonije anyatra vā dehe karmacitrite । sa dehaḥ pratibudhyeta prasuptotthitavattadā ।। tasyāpi bhogataddhānimṛtayaḥ prāgvadeva hi ।
visṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārā ete karmabalādyataḥ ।। ato niyatikālādivaicitryānuvidhāyinaḥ । anugrahastu yaḥ so ayaṃ svasvarūpe vikasvare ।। jñaptyātmeti kathaṃ karmaniyatyādi pratīkṣate ।
karmakālaniyatyādi yataḥ saṅkocajīvitam ।। saṅkocahānirūpe asminkathaṃ heturanugrahe । anugrahaśca kramikastīvraśceti vibhidyate ।। prāk caiṣa vistarātprokta iti kiṃ punaruktibhiḥ ।
tena dīkṣāśivajñānadagdhasaṅkocabandhanaḥ ।। dehānte śiva eveti nāsya dehāntarasthitiḥ । ye api tattvāvatīrṇānāṃ śaṃkarājñānuvartinām ।। svayambhūmunidevarṣimanujādibhuvāṃ gṛhe ।
mṛtāste tatpuraṃ prāpya pureśairdīkṣitāḥ kramāt ।। martye avatīrya vā no vā śivaṃ yāntyapunarbhavāḥ । tatra svayambhuvo dvedhā ke apyanugrahatatparāḥ ।। ke api svakṛtyāyātāṃśasthānamātropasevinaḥ ।
ye anugrahārthamājñaptāsteṣu yo mriyate naraḥ ।। so anugrahaṃ sphuṭaṃ yāti vinā martyāvatārataḥ । yastu svakāryaṃ kurvāṇastatsthānaṃ nāṃśatastyajet ।। yathā gaurī tapasyantī kaśmīreṣu guhāgatā ।
tatraiva vā yathā dhyānoḍḍāre naraharirvibhuḥ ।। vitastāṃ nayato daityāṃstrāsayandṛpta utthitaḥ । sāligrāme yathā viṣṇuḥ śivo vā svopabhoginaḥ ।। tapasyantau badaryāṃ ca naranārāyaṇau tathā ।
ityevamādayo devāḥ svakṛtyāṃśasthitāstathā ।। ārādhitāḥ svocitaṃ tacchīghraṃ vidadhate phalam । svakṛtyāṃśasthitānāṃ ca dhāmni ye antaṃ vrajanti te ।। tatra bhogāṃstathā bhuktvā martyeṣvavatarantyapi ।
martyāvatīrṇāste tattadaṃśakāstanmayāḥ punaḥ ।। taddīkṣājñānacaryādikramādyānti śivātmatām । sthāvarādyāstiryagantāḥ paśavo asmindvaye mṛtāḥ ।। svakarmasaṃskriyāvedhāttalloke citratājuṣaḥ ।
puṃsāṃ ca paśumātrāṇāṃ sālokyamavivekataḥ ।। avivekastadviśeṣānunmeṣānmauḍhyatastathā । sthāvarādyāstathābhāvamuttarottaratāṃ ca vā ।। prapadyante na te sākṣādrudratāṃ tāṃ kramātpunaḥ ।
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇe nānātarukulākule ।। ityetadāgameṣūktaṃ tata eva pure pure । kṣetramānaṃ bruve śrīmatsarvajñānādiṣūditam ।। liṅgāddhastaśataṃ kṣetramācāryasthāpite sati ।
svayambhūte sahasraṃ tu tadardhamṛṣiyojite ।। tattvavitsthāpite liṅge svayambhūsadṛśaṃ phalam । atattvavidyadācāryo liṅgaṃ sthāpayate tadā ।। punarvidhirbhaveddoṣo hyanyathobhayadūṣakaḥ ।
ahamanyaḥ parātmānyaḥ śivo anya iti cenmatiḥ ।। na mocayenna muktaśca sarvamātmamayaṃ yataḥ । tasmāttattvavidā yadyatsthāpitaṃ liṅgamuttamam ।। tadevāyatanatvena saṃśrayedbhuktimuktaye ।
uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ jñātvā kālamupasthitam ।। mokṣārthī na bhayaṃ gacchettyajeddehamaśaṅkitaḥ । tīrthāyatanapuṇyeṣu kālaṃ vā vañcayetpriye ।। ayogināmayaṃ panthā yogī yogena vañcayet ।
vañcane tvasamarthaḥ san kṣetramāyatanaṃ vrajet ।। tīrthe samāśrayāttasya vañcanaṃ tu vijāyate । anena ca dharādyeṣu tattveṣvabhyāsayogataḥ ।। tāvatsiddhijuṣo apyuktā muktyai kṣetropayogitā ।
samyagjñānini vṛttāntaḥ purastāttūpadekṣyate ।। paśūnāmeṣa vṛttānto ye tu tattattvadīkṣitāḥ । te tadīśasamīpatvaṃ yānti svaucityayogataḥ ।। yogyatāvaśasaṃjātā yasya yatraiva vāsanā ।
sa tatraiva niyoktavyaḥ pureśāccordhvaśuddhibhāk ।। iti śrīpūrvakathitaṃ śrīmatsvāyambhuve apica । yo yatrābhilaṣedbhogānsa tatraiva niyojitaḥ ।। siddhibhāṅmantrasāmarthyādityādyanyatra varṇitam ।
ye tu tattattvavijñānamantracaryādivartinaḥ ।। mṛtāste tatra tadrudrasayuktvaṃ yānti kovidāḥ । teṣāṃ sayuktvaṃ yātānāmapi saṃskārato nijāt ।। tathā tathā vicitraḥ syādavatārastadaṃśataḥ ।
siddhāntādau purāṇeṣu tathāca śrūyate bahu ।। tulye rudrāvatāratve citratvaṃ karmabhogayoḥ । anekaśaktikhacitaṃ yato bhāvasya yadvapuḥ ।। śaktibhyo arthāntaraṃ naiṣa tatsamūhādṛte bhavet ।
tena śaktisamūhākhyāt tasmādrudrādyadaṃśataḥ ।। kṛtyaṃ taducitaṃ siddhyet soṃ aśo avatarati sphuṭam । ye cādharaprāptadīkṣāstadāsthānujjhitāḥ pare ।। tattve mṛtāḥ kāṣṭhavatte adhare apyutkarṣabhāginaḥ ।
ye tūjjhitatadutkarṣāste taduttarabhāginaḥ ।। ye apyūrdhvatattvadīkṣāste vinā tāvadvivekataḥ । prāptādharāntā api taddīkṣāphalasubhāginaḥ ।। atyaktāsthā hi te tatra dīkṣāyāmapi śāstritāt ।
vinā vivekādāsthāṃ te śritā lokaprasiddhitaḥ ।। paśumātrasya sālokyaṃ sāmīpyaṃ dīkṣitasya tu । tatparasya tu sāyujyamityuktaṃ parameśinā ।। yastūrdhvaśāstragastatra tyaktāsthaḥ saṃśayena saḥ ।
vrajannāyatanaṃ naiva phalaṃ kiñcitsamaśnute ।। uktaṃ tadviṣayaṃ caitaddevadevena yadvṛthā । dīkṣā jñānaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ tasyetyādi savistaram ।। yastu tāvadayogyo api tathāste sa śivālaye ।
paścādāsthānibandhena tāvadeva phalaṃ bhajet ।। nadīnagahradaprāyaṃ yacca puṇyaṃ na tanmṛtau । utkṛṣṭaṃ tanmṛtānāṃ tu svargabhogopabhogitā ।। ye punaḥ prāptavijñānavivekā maraṇāntike ।
adharāyataneṣvāsthāṃ śritāste atra tirohitāḥ ।। tajjñānadūṣaṇoktaṃ yatteṣāṃ syātkila pātakam । tattatpureśadīkṣādikramānnaśyediti sthitiḥ ।। dīkṣāyatanavijñānadūṣiṇo ye tu cetasā ।
ācaranti ca tatte atra sarve nirayagāminaḥ ।। jñānāyatanadīkṣādāvāsthābandhaparicyutiḥ । vyāpāravyāhṛtairjñeyā tānyapi dvividhāni ca ।। yāni jātucidapyeva svāsthye nodamiṣanpunaḥ ।
asvāsthye dhātudoṣotthānyeva tadbhogamātrakam ।। dhātudoṣācca saṃsārasaṃskārāste prabodhitāḥ । chidragā api bhūyiṣṭhajñānadagdhā na rohiṇaḥ ।। ye tu kaivalyabhāgīyāḥ svāsthye anunmiṣitāḥ sadā ।
asvāsthye conmiṣantyete saṃskārāḥ śaktipātataḥ ।। yataḥ sāṃsārikāḥ pūrvagāḍhābhyāsopasaṃskṛtāḥ । ityūce bhujagādhīśastacchidreṣviti sūtrataḥ ।। ye tu kaivalyabhāgīyāḥ pratyayāste na jātucit ।
abhyastāḥ saṃsṛterbhāvāttenaite śaktipātataḥ ।। vyāpāravyāhṛtaistena dhātudoṣaprakopitaiḥ । aprāptaniścayāmarśaiḥ suptamattopamānakaiḥ ।। viparītairapi jñānadīkṣāgurvādidūṣakaiḥ ।
tirobhāvo na vijñeyo hṛdaye rūḍhyabhāvataḥ ।। ata eva prabuddho api karmotthānbhogarūpiṇaḥ । yamakiṅkarasarpādipratyayāndehago bhajet ।। naitāvatā na mukto asau mṛtirbhogo hi janmavat ।
sthitivacca tato duḥkhasukhābhyāṃ maraṇaṃ dvidhā ।। ato yathā prabuddhasya sukhaduḥkhavicitratāḥ । sthitau na ghnanti muktatvaṃ maraṇe api tathaiva tāḥ ।। ye punaryoginaste api yasmiṃstattve subhāvitāḥ ।
cittaṃ niveśayantyeva tattattvaṃ yāntyaśaṅkitāḥ ।। śrīsvacchande tataḥ proktaṃ gandhadhāraṇayā mṛtāḥ । ityādi mālinīśāstre dhāraṇānāṃ tathā phalam ।। eteṣāṃ maraṇābhikhyo bhogo nāsti tu ye tanum ।
dhāraṇābhistyajantyāśu paradehapraveśavat ।। etāvānmṛtibhogo hi marmacchinmūḍhatākṣagā । dhvāntābilatvaṃ manasi taccaiteṣu na vidyate ।। tathāhi mānasaṃ yatnaṃ tāvatsamadhitiṣṭhati ।
ahaṃrūḍhyā pare dehe yāvatsyādbuddhisaṃcaraḥ ।। prāṇacakraṃ tadāyattamapi saṃcarate pathā । tenaivātaḥ prabuddhyeta paradehe akṣacakrakam ।। makṣikā makṣikārājaṃ yathotthitamanūtthitāḥ ।
sthitaṃ cānuviśantyevaṃ cittaṃ sarvākṣavṛttayaḥ ।। ato asya paradehādisaṃcāre nāsti melanam । akṣāṇāṃ madhyagaṃ sūkṣmaṃ syādetaddehavatpunaḥ ।। evaṃ paraśarīrādicāriṇāmiva yoginām ।
tattattattvaśarīrāntaścāriṇāṃ nāsti mūḍhatā ।। te cāpi dvividhā jñeyā laukikā dīkṣitāstathā । pūrve śivāḥ syuḥ kramaśaḥ pare tadbhogamātrataḥ ।। dīkṣāpyūrdhvādharānekabhedayojanikāvaśāt ।
bhidyamānā yogināṃ syādvicitraphaladāyinī ।। ye tu vijñāninaste atra dvedhā kampretaratvataḥ । tatra ye kampravijñānāste dehānted śivāḥ sphuṭam ।। yato vijñānameteṣāmutpannaṃ naca susphuṭam ।
vikalpāntarayogena nacāpyunmūlitātmakam ।। ato dehe pramādottho vikalpo dehapātataḥ । naśyedavaśyaṃ taccāpi budhyate jñānamuttamam ।। saṃskārakalpanātiṣṭhadadhvastīkṛtamantarā ।
prāptapākaṃ saṃvarīturapāye bhāsate hi tat ।। ye tu svabhyastavijñānamayāḥ śivamayāḥ sadā । jīvanmuktā hi te naiṣāṃ mṛtau kāpi vicāraṇā ।। yathāhi jīvanmuktānāṃ sthitau nāsti vicāraṇā ।
sukhiduḥkhivimūḍhatve, mṛtāvapi tathā na sā ।। śrīratnamālāśāstre taduvāca parameśvaraḥ । svaśāstre cāpyahīśāno viśvādhāradhurandharaḥ ।। rathyāntare mūtrapurīṣamadhye caṇḍālagehe niraye śmaśāne ।
sacintako vā gatacintako vā jñānī vimokṣaṃ labhate api cānte ।। apiceti dhvanirjīvanmuktatāmasya bhāṣate । sacintācintakatvoktiretāvatsaṃbhavasthitim ।। tīrthe śvapacagṛhe vā naṣṭasmṛtirapi parityajeddeham ।
jñānasamakālamuktaḥ kaivalyaṃ yāti hataśokaḥ ।। anantakārikā caiṣā prāhedaṃ bandhakaṃ kila । sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ cāsya śaṅkyaṃ taccāsya no bhavet ।। apiśabdādaluptasmṛtyā vā saṃbhāvyate kila ।
mṛtirnaṣṭasmṛtereva mṛteḥ prāk sāstu kiṃ tayā ।। liṅca saṃbhāvanāyāṃ syādiyatsaṃbhāvyate kila । saca kāladhvaniḥ prāha mṛtermuktāvahetutām ।। kaivalyamiti cāśaṅkāpadaṃ yāpyabhavattanuḥ ।
bhedapradatvenaiṣāpi dhvastā tena viśokatā ।। paradehādisaṃbandho yathā nāsya vibhedakaḥ । tathā svadehasaṃbandho jīvanmuktasya yadyapi ।। ataśca na viśeṣo asya viśvākṛtinirākṛteḥ ।
śivābhinnasya dehe vā tadabhāve api vā kila ।। tathāpi prācyatadbhedasaṃskārāśaṅkanasthiteḥ । adhunoktaṃ kevalatvaṃ yadvā mātrantarāśrayāt ।। tānyenaṃ na vidurbhinnaṃ taiḥ sa mukto abhidhīyate ।
śrīmattraiśirase apyuktaṃ sūryendupuṭavarjite ।। jugupsābhāvabhaṅgasthe sarvataḥ stambhavatsthite । sarvavyāpattirahite pramāṇapratyayātige ।। tasminbodhāntare līnaḥ karmakartāpyanañjanaḥ ।
pradhānaṃ ghaṭa ākāśa ātmā maṣṭe ghaṭe api kham ।। na naśyettadvadevāsāvātmā śivamayo bhavet । svatantro avasthito jñānī prasaretsarvavastuṣu ।। tasya bhāvo nacābhāvaḥ saṃsthānaṃ naca kalpanā ।
etadevāntarāgūrya gururgītāsvabhāṣata ।। yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaranbhāvaṃ tyajatyante kalevaram । taṃ tamevaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।। tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu māmanusmara yudhya ca ।
yadā sattve vivṛddhe tu pralīnastvūrdhvagastadā ।। kramādrajastamolīnaḥ karmayonivimūḍhagaḥ । tatrendriyāṇāṃ saṃmohaśvāsāyāsaparītatā ।। ityādimṛtibhogo ayaṃ dehe na tyajanaṃ tanoḥ ।
yastvasau kṣaṇa evaikaścaramaḥ prāṇanātmakaḥ ।। yadanantaramevaiṣa dehaḥ syātkāṣṭhakuḍyavat । sā dehatyāgakālāṃśakalā dehaviyoginī ।। tata eva hi taddehasukhaduḥkhādikojjhitā ।
tasyāṃ yadeva smarati prāksaṃskāraprabodhataḥ ।। adṛṣṭābhyāsabhūyastvaśaktipātādihetukāt । tadeva rūpamabhyeti sukhiduḥkhivimūḍhakam ।। yadvā niḥsukhaduḥkhādi yadi vānandarūpakam ।
kasmādeti tadevaiṣa yataḥ smarati saṃvidi ।। prāk prasphuredyadadhikaṃ deho asau cidadhiṣṭhiteḥ । yadeva prāgadhiṣṭhānaṃ citā tādātmyavṛttitaḥ ।। saivātra līnatā proktā sattve rajasi tāmase ।
nīlapītādike jñeye yataḥ prākkalpitāṃ tanum ।। adhiṣṭhāyaiva saṃvittiradhiṣṭhānaṃ karotyalam । ato adhiṣṭheyamātrasya śarīratve api kuḍyataḥ ।। dehasyāsti viśeṣo yatsarvādhiṣṭheyapūrvatā ।
tādātmyavṛttiranyeṣāṃ tanna satyapi vedyate ।। vedyānāṃ kintu dehasya nityāvyabhicaritvataḥ । sā ca tasyaiva dehasya pūrvamṛtyantajanmanā ।। smṛtyā prācyānubhavanakṛtasaṃskāracitrayā ।
yuktyānayāsmatsantānaguruṇā kallaṭena yat ।। dehāviśeṣe prāṇākhyadārḍhyaṃ heturudīritam । tadyuktamanyathā prāṇadārḍhye ko heturekataḥ ।। dehatvasyāviśeṣe apītyeṣa praśno na śāmyati ।
smaranniti śatā hetau tadrūpaṃ pratipadyate ।। prāk smaryate yato dehaḥ prākcitādhiṣṭhitaḥ sphuran । ataḥ smaraṇamantyaṃ yattadasarvajñamātṛṣu ।। na jātu gocaro yasmāddehāntaraviniścayaḥ ।
yattu bandhupriyāputrapānādismaraṇaṃ sphuṭam ।। na taddehāntarāsaṅgi na tadantyaṃ yato bhavet । kasyāpi tu śarīrānte vāsanā yā prabhotsyate ।। dehasattve tadaucityājjāyetānubhavaḥ sphuṭaḥ ।
yathā purāṇe kathitaṃ mṛgapotakatṛṣṇayā ।। muniḥ ko api mṛgībhāvamabhyuvāhādhivāsitaḥ । tatra so anubhavo heturna janmāntarasūtaye ।। tasyaitadvāsanā hetuḥ kākatālīyavat sa tu ।
nanu kasmāttadevaiṣa smarati ityāha yatsadā ।। tadbhāvabhāvitastena tadevaiṣa smaratyalam । evamasmi bhaviṣyāmītyeṣa tadbhāva ucyate ।। bhaviṣyato hi bhavanaṃ bhāvyate na sataḥ kvacit ।
kramātsphuṭatvakaraṇaṃ bhāvanaṃ parikīrtyate ।। sphuṭasya cānubhavanaṃ na bhāvanamidaṃ sphuṭam । tadaharjātabālasya paśoḥ kīṭasya vā taroḥ ।। mūḍhatve api tadānīṃ prāgbhāvanā hyabhavatsphuṭā ।
sā tanmūḍhaśarīrānte saṃskārapratibodhanāt ।। smṛtidvāreṇa taddehavaicitryaphaladāyinī । deśādivyavadhāne api vāsanānāmudīritāt ।। ānantaryaikarūpatvātsmṛtisaṃskārayorataḥ ।
tathānubhavanārūḍhyā sphuṭasyāpi tu bhāvitā ।। bhāvyamānā na kiṃ sūte tatsantānasadṛgvapuḥ । tattādṛktādṛśairbandhuputramitrādibhiḥ saha ।। bhāsate api pare loke svapnavadvāsanākramāt ।
nanu mātrantarairbandhuputrādyaistattathā na kim ।। vedyate ka idaṃ prāha sa tāvadveda vedyatām । vyāpāravyāhṛtivrātavedye mātrantaravraje ।। svapne nāsti sa ityeṣā vākpramāṇavivarjitā ।
ya evaite tu dṛśyante jāgratyete mayekṣitāḥ ।। svapna ityastu mithyaitattatpramātṛvacobalāt । yānapaśyamahaṃ svapne pramātṝṃste na kecana ।। na śocanti na cekṣante māmityatrāsti kā pramā ।
yataḥ sarvānumānānāṃ svasaṃvedananiṣṭhitau ।। pramātrantarasadbhāvaḥ saṃvinniṣṭho na tadgataḥ । ghaṭāderastitā saṃvinniṣṭhitā natu tadgatā ।। tadvanmātrantare apyeṣā saṃvinniṣṭhā na tadgatā ।
tena sthitamidaṃ yadyadbhāvyate tattadeva hi ।। dehānte budhyate no cet syādanyādṛkprabodhanam । tathāhyantyakṣaṇe brahmavidyākarṇanasaṃskṛtaḥ ।। mucyate janturityuktaṃ prāksaṃskārabalatvataḥ ।
nipātābhyāmantaśabdātsmaraṇācchaturantyataḥ ।। pādācca nikhilādardhaślokācca samanantarāt । līnaśabdācca sarvaṃ taduktamarthasatattvakam ।। ajñātvaitattu sarve api kuśakāśāvalambinaḥ ।
yattadorvyatyayaṃ kecitkecidanyādṛśaṃ kramam ।। bhinnakramau nipātau ca tyajatīti ca saptamīm । vyācakṣate tacca sarvaṃ nopayogyuktayojane ।। naca taddarśitaṃ mithyā svāntasammohadāyakam ।
taditthaṃprāyaṇasyaitattattvaṃ śrīśambhunāthataḥ ।। adhigamyoditaṃ tena mṛtyorbhītirvinaśyati । viditamṛtisatattvāḥ saṃvidambhonidhānādacalahṛdayavīryākarṣaniṣpīḍanottham । amṛtamiti nigīrṇe kālakūṭe atra devā yadi pivatha tadānīṃ niścitaṃ vaḥ śivatvam ।।
utsavo api hi yaḥ kaścillaukikaḥ so api saṃmadam । saṃvidabdhitaraṅgābhaṃ sūte tadapi parvavat ।। etena ca vipaddhvaṃsapramodādiṣu parvatā । vyākhyātā tena tatrāpi viśeṣāddevatārcanam ।।
purakṣobhādyadbhutaṃ yattatsvātantrye svasaṃvidaḥ । dārḍhyadāyīti tallābhadine vaiśeṣikārcanam ।। yoginīmelako dvedhā haṭhataḥ priyatastathā । prācye cchidrāṇi saṃrakṣetkāmacāritvamuttare ।।
sa ca dvayo api mantroddhṛtprasaṅge darśayiṣyate । yoginīmelakāccaiṣo avaśyaṃ jñānaṃ prapadyate ।। tena tatparva tadvacca svasantānādimelanam । saṃvitsarvātmikā dehabhedādyā saṅkucettu sā ।।
melake anyonyasaṅghaṭṭapratibimbādvikasvarā । ucchalannijaraśmyoghaḥ saṃvitsu pratibimbitaḥ ।। bahudarpaṇavaddīptaḥ sarvāyetāpyayatnataḥ । ata eva gītagītaprabhṛtau bahuparṣadi ।।
yaḥ sarvatanmayībhāve hlādo natvekakasya saḥ । ānandanirbharā saṃvitpratyekaṃ sā tathaikatām ।। nṛttādau viṣaye prāptā pūrṇānandatvamaśnute । īrṣyāsūyādisaṅkocakāraṇābhāvato atra sā ।।
vikasvarā niṣpratighaṃ saṃvidānandayoginī । atanmaye tu kasmiṃścittatrasthe pratihanyate ।। sthapuṭasparśavatsaṃvidvijātīyatayā sthite । ataścakrārcanādyeṣu vijātīyamatanmayam ।।
naiva praveśayetsaṃvitsaṅkocananibandhanam । yāvantyeva śarīrāṇi svāṅgavatsyuḥ sunirbharām ।। ekāṃ saṃvidamāviśya cakre tāvanti pūjayet । praviṣṭaścetpramādena saṅkocaṃ na vrajettataḥ ।।
prastutaṃ svasamācāraṃ tena sākaṃ samācaret । sa tvanugrahaśaktyā cedviddhastattanmayībhavet ।। vāmāviddhastu tannindetpaścāttaṃ ghātayedapi । śrīmatpicumate coktamādau yatnena rakṣayet ।।
praveśaṃ saṃpaviṣṭasya na vicāraṃ tu kārayet । lokācārasthito yastu praviṣṭe tādṛśe tu saḥ ।। akṛtvā taṃ samācāraṃ punaścakraṃ prapūjayet । atha vacmi guroḥ śāstravyākhyākramamudāhṛtam ।।
devyāyāmalaśāstrādau tuhinābhīśumaulinā । kalpavittatsamūhajñaḥ śāstravitsaṃhitārthavit ।। sarvaśāstrārthavicceti gururbhinno apadiśyate । yo yatra śāstre svabhyastajñāno vyākhyāṃ carettu saḥ ।।
nānyathā tadabhāvaścetsarvathā so apyathācaret । śrībhairavakule coktaṃ kalpādijñatvamīdṛśam ।। gurorlakṣaṇametāvatsaṃpūrṇajñānataiva yā । tatrāpi yāsya cidvṛttikarmibhit sāpyavāntarā ।।
devyāyāmala uktaṃ taddvāpañcāśāhva āhnike । deva eva gurutvena tiṣṭhāsurdaśadhā bhavet ।। ucchuṣmaśavaracaṇḍagumataṅgaghorāntakograhalahalakāḥ । krodhī huluhulurete daśa guravaḥ śivamayāḥ pūrve ।।
te svāṃśacittavṛttikrameṇa pauruṣaśarīramāsthāya । anyonyabhinnasaṃvitkriyā api jñānaparipūrṇāḥ ।। sarve alimāṃsanidhuvanadīkṣārcanaśāstrasevane niratāḥ । abhimānaśamakrodhakṣamādiravāntaro bhedaḥ ।।
itthaṃ vijñāya sadā śiṣyaḥ sampūrṇaśāstraboddhāram । vyākhyāyai gurumabhyarthayeta pūjāpuraḥsaraṃ matimān ।। so api svaśāsanīye paraśiṣye apivāpi tādṛśaṃ śāstram । śrotuṃ yogye kuryādvyākhyānaṃ vaiṣṇavādyadhare ।।
karuṇārasaparipūrṇo guruḥ punarmarmadhāmaparivarjam । adhame api hi vyākuryātsambhāvya hi śaktipātavaicitryam ।। liptāyāṃ bhuvi pīṭhe caturasre paṅkajatrayaṃ kajage । kuryādvidyāpīṭhaṃ syādrasavahnyaṅgulaṃ tvetat ।।
madhye vāgīśānīṃ dakṣottarayorgurūngaṇeśaṃ ca । adhare kaje ca kalpeśvaraṃ prapūjyārghapuṣpatarpaṇakaiḥ ।। sāmānyavidhiniyuktārghapātrayogena cakramatha samyak । santarpya vyākhyānaṃ kuryātsambandhapūrvakaṃ matimān ।।
sūtrapadavākyapaṭalagranthakramayojanena sambandhāt । avyāhatapūrvāparamupavṛhya nayeta vākyāni ।। maṇḍūkaplavasiṃhāvalokanādyairyathāyathaṃ nyāyaiḥ । avihatapūrvāparakaṃ śāstrārthaṃ yojayedasaṅkīrṇam ।।
tantrāvartanabādhaprasaṅgatarkādibhiśca sannyāyaiḥ । vastu vadedvākyajño vastvantarato viviktatāṃ vidadhat ।। yadyadvyāhṛtipadavīmāyāti tadeva dṛḍhatarairnyāyaiḥ । balavatkuryāddūṣyaṃ yadyapyagre bhaviṣyatsyāt ।।
dṛḍharacitapūrvapakṣaproddharaṇapathena vastu yadvācyam । śiṣyamatāvārohati tadāśu saṃśayaviparyayairvikalam ।। bhāṣā nyāyo vādo layaḥ kramo yadyadeti śiṣyasya । sambodhopāyatvaṃ tathaiva gururāśrayedvyākhyām ।।
vācyaṃ vastu samāpya pratarpaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ bhaveccakre । punaraparaṃ vastu vadetpaṭalādūrdhvaṃ tu no jalpet ।। vyākhyānte kṣamayitvā visṛjya sarvaṃ kṣipedagādhajale । śāstrādimadhyanidhane viśeṣataḥ pūjanaṃ kuryāt ।।
viśeṣapūjanaṃ kuryātsamayebhyaśca niṣkṛtau । avikalpamaterna syuḥ prāyaścittāni yadyapi ।। tathāpyatattvavidvargānugrahāya tathā caret । śrīpicau ca smṛtereva pāpaghnatve kathaṃ vibho ।।
prāyaścittavidhiḥ prokta iti devyā pracodite । satyaṃ smaraṇameveha sakṛjjaptaṃ vimocayet ।। sarvasmātkarmaṇo jālātsmṛtitattvakalāvidaḥ । tathāpi sthitirakṣārthaṃ kartavyaścodito vidhiḥ ।।
atattvavedino ye hi caryāmātraikaniṣṭhitāḥ । teṣāṃ dolāyite citte jñānahāniḥ prajāyate ।। tasmādvikalparahitaḥ saṃvṛtyuparato yadi । śāstracaryāsadāyattaiḥ saṅkaraṃ tadvivarjayet ।।
saṅkaraṃ vā samanvicchetprāyaścittaṃ samācaret । yathā teṣāṃ na śāstrārthe dolārūḍhā matirbhavet ।। yatsvayaṃ śivahastākhye vidhau saṃcoditaṃ purā । śataṃ japtvāsya cāstrasya mucyate strīvadhādṛte ।।
śaktināśānmahādoṣo narakaṃ śāśvataṃ priye । iti śrīratnamālāyāṃ samayollaṅghane kṛte ।। kulajānāṃ samākhyātā niṣkṛtirduṣṭakartarī । śrīpūrve samayānāṃ tu śodhanāyoditaṃ yathā ।।
mālinī mātṛkā vāpi japyā lakṣatrayāntakam । pratiṣṭhitasya pūrāderdarśane anadhikāriṇā ।। prāyaścittaṃ prakartavyamiti śrībrahmayāmale । brahmaghno gurutalpastho vīradravyaharastathā ।।
devadravyahṛdākāraprahartā liṅgabhedakaḥ । nityādilopakṛdbhraṣṭasvakamātrāparicchadaḥ ।। śaktivyaṅgatvakṛdyogijñānihantā vilopakaḥ । naimittikānāṃ lakṣādikramāddvidviguṇaṃ japet ।।
vratena kenacidyukto mitabhugbrahmacaryavān । dūtīparigrahe anyatra gataścetkāmamohitaḥ ।। lakṣajāpaṃ tataḥ kuryādityuktaṃ brahmayāmale । dīkṣābhiṣekanaimittavidhyante gurupūjanam ।।
aparedyuḥ sadā kāryaṃ siddhayogīśvarīmate । pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaḥ kavistrikasatattvavit ।। sa guruḥ sarvadā grāhyastyaktvānyaṃ tatsthitaṃ tvapi । maṇḍale svastikaṃ kṛtvā tatra haimādikāsanam ।।
kṛtvārcayeta tatrasthamadhvānaṃ sakalāntakam । tato vijñapayedbhaktyā tadadhiṣṭhitaye gurum ।। sa tatra pūjyaḥ svairmantraiḥ puṣpadhūpārghavistaraiḥ । samālambhanasadvastrairnaivedyaistarpaṇaiḥ kramāt ।।
āśāntaṃ pūjayitvainaṃ dakṣiṇābhiryajecchiśuḥ । sarvasvamasmai saṃdadyādātmānamapi bhāvitaḥ ।। atoṣayitvā tu guruṃ dakṣiṇābhiḥ samantataḥ । tattvajño apyṛṇabandhena tena yātyadhikāritām ।।
gurupūjāmakurvāṇaḥ śataṃ janmāni jāyate । adhikārī tato muktiṃ yātīti skandayāmale ।। tasmādavaśyaṃ dātavyā gurave dakṣiṇā punaḥ । pūrvaṃ hi yāgāṅgatayā proktaṃ tattuṣṭaye tvidam ।।
tajjuṣṭamatha tasyājñāṃ prāpyāśnīyātsvayaṃ śiśuḥ । tataḥ prapūjayeccakraṃ yathāvibhavasambhavam ।। akṛtvā guruyāgaṃ tu kṛtamapyakṛtaṃ yataḥ । tasmātprayatnataḥ kāryo guruyāgo yathābalam ।।
atatrastho api hi guruḥ pūjyaḥ saṃkalpya pūrvavat । taddravyaṃ devatākṛtye kuryādbhaktajaneṣvatha ।। parvapavitraprabhṛtiprabhedi naimittikaṃ tvidaṃ karma । atha samucitādhikāriṇa uddiśya rahasya ucyate atra vidhiḥ ।
atha sarvāpyupāseyaṃ kulaprakriyayocyate ।। tathā dhārādhirūḍheṣu guruśiṣyeṣu yocitā । uktaṃ ca parameśena sāratvaṃ kramapūjane ।। siddhakramaniyuktasya māsenaikena yadbhavet ।
na tadvarṣasahasraiḥ syānmantraughairvividhairiti ।। kulaṃ ca parameśasya śaktiḥ sāmarthyamūrdhvatā । svātantryamojo vīryaṃ ca piṇḍaḥ saṃviccharīrakam ।। tathātvena samastāni bhāvajātāni paśyataḥ ।
dhvastaśaṅkāsamūhasya yāgastādṛśa eva saḥ ।। tādṛgrūpanirūḍhyarthaṃ manovākkāyavartmanā । yadyatsamācaredvīraḥ kulayāgaḥ sa sa smṛtaḥ ।। bahiḥ śaktau yāmale ca dehe prāṇapathe matau ।
