iti ṣoḍhā kulejyā syātpratibhedaṃ vibhedinī ।। snānamaṇḍalakuṇḍādi ṣoḍhānyāsādi yanna tat । kiñcidatropayujyeta kṛtaṃ vā khaṇḍanāya no ।। ṣaṇmaṇḍalavinirmuktaṃ sarvāvaraṇavarjitam ।
jñānajñeyamayaṃ kaulaṃ proktaṃ traiśirase mate ।। atra yāge ca yaddravyaṃ niṣiddhaṃ śāstrasantatau । tadeva yojayeddhīmānvāmāmṛtapariplutam ।। śrībrahmayāmale apyuktaṃ surā śivaraso bahiḥ ।
tāṃ vinā bhuktimuktī no piṣṭakṣaudraguḍaistu sā ।। strīnapuṃsakapuṃrūpā tu pūrvāparabhogadā । drākṣotthaṃ tu paraṃ tejo bhairavaṃ kalpanojjhitam ।। etatsvayaṃ rasaḥ śuddhaḥ prakāśānandacinmayaḥ ।
devatānāṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ tasmādetatpivetsadā ।। śrīmatkramarahasye ca nyarūpi parameśinā । arghapātraṃ yāgadhāma dīpa ityucyate trayam ।। rahasyaṃ kaulike yāge tatrārghaḥ śaktisaṃgamāt ।
bhūvastrakāyapīṭhākhyaṃ dhāma cotkarṣabhāk kramāt ।। dīpā ghṛtotthā gāvo hi bhūcaryo devatāḥ smṛtāḥ । iti jñātvā traye amuṣminyatnavānkauliko bhavet ।। tenārghapātraprādhānyaṃ jñātvā dravyāṇi śambhunā ।
yānyuktānyaviśaṅko atra bhavecchaṅkā hi dūṣikā ।। yāgauko gandhadhūpāḍhyaṃ praviśya prāgudaṅmukhaḥ । parayā vā atha mālinyā vilomāccānulomataḥ ।। dāhāpyāyamayīṃ śuddhiṃ dīptasaumyavibhedataḥ ।
krameṇa kuryādathavā mātṛsadbhāvamantrataḥ ।। dīkṣāṃ cetpracikīrṣustacchodhyādhvanyāsakalpanam । tataḥ saṃśodhyavastūni śaktyaivāmṛtatāṃ nayet ।। parāsampuṭagā yadvā mātṛsampuṭagāpyatho ।
kevalā mālinī yadvā tāḥ samasteṣu karmasu ।। nandahetuphalairdravyairarghapātraṃ prapūrayet । tatroktamantratādātmyādbhairavātmatvamānayet ।। tena nirbharamātmānaṃ bahiścakrānucakragam ।
vipruḍbhirūrdhvādharayorantaḥ pītyā ca tarpayet ।। tathā pūrṇasvaraśmyoghaḥ procchaladvṛttitāvaśāt । bahistādṛśamātmānaṃ didṛkṣurbahirarcayet ।। arkāṅgule atha taddvitriguṇe raktapaṭe śubhe ।
vyomni sindūrasubhage rājavarttabhṛte athavā ।। nārikelātmake kādye madyapūrṇe atha bhājane । yadvā samudite rūpe maṇḍalasthe ca tadṛśi ।। yāgaṃ kurvīta matimāṃstatrāyaṃ krama ucyate ।
diśyudīcyāṃ rudrakoṇādvāyavyantaṃ gaṇeśvaram ।। vaṭukaṃ trīn gurūnsiddhānyoginīḥ pīṭhamarcayet । prācyāṃ diśi gaṇeśādha ārabhyābhyarcayettataḥ ।। siddhacakraṃ dikcatuṣke gaṇeśādhastanāntakam ।
khagendraḥ sahavijjāmba illā ī ambayā saha ।। vaktaṣṭirvimalo anantamekhalāmbāyutaḥ purā । śaktyā maṅgalayā kūrma illā ī ambayā saha ।। jaitro yāmye hyavijitastathā sānandamekhalaḥ ।
kāmamaṅgalayā meṣaḥ kullā ī ambayā saha ।। vindhyo ajito apyajarayā saha mekhalayā pare । macchandaḥ kuṅkuṇāmbā ca ṣaḍyugmaṃ sādhikārakam ।। saumye marutta īśāntaṃ dvitīyā paṅktirīdṛśī ।
amaravaradevacitrālivindhyaguḍikā iti kramātṣaḍamī ।। sillā ī eruṇayā tathā kumārī ca bodhā ī । samahālacchī cāparamekhalayā śaktayaḥ ṣaḍimāḥ ।। ete hi sādhikārāḥ pūjyā yeṣāmiyaṃ bahuvibhedā ।
santatiranavacchinnā citrā śiṣyapraśiṣyamayī ।। ānandāvalibodhiprabhupādāntātha yogiśabdāntā । etā ovallyaḥ syurmudrāṣaṭkaṃ kramāttvetat ।। dakṣāṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhikāntamatha sā kanīyasī vāmāt ।
dvidaśāntordhvagakuṇḍalibaindavahṛnnābhikandamiti chu mmāḥ ।। śavarāḍabillapaṭṭillāḥ karabillāmbiśarabillāḥ । aḍabīḍombīdakṣiṇabillāḥ kumbhārikākṣarākhyāca ।। devīkoṭṭakulādritripurīkāmākhyamaṭṭahāsaśca ।
dakṣiṇapīṭhaṃ caitatṣaṭkaṃ gharapallipīṭhagaṃ kramaśaḥ ।। iti saṅketābhijño bhramate pīṭheṣu yadi sa siddhīpsuḥ । acirāllabhate tattatprāpyaṃ yadyoginīvadanāt ।। bhaṭṭendravalkalāhīndragajendrāḥ samahīdharāḥ ।
ūrdhvaretasa ete ṣaḍadhikārapadojjhitāḥ ।। adhikāro hi vīryasya prasaraḥ kulavartmani । tadaprasarayogena te proktā ūrdhvaretasaḥ ।। anyāśca gurutatpatnyaḥ śrīmatkālīkuloditāḥ ।
anāttadehāḥ krīḍanti taistairdehairaśaṅkitāḥ ।। prabodhitatathecchākaistajje kaulaṃ prakāśate । tathārūpatayā tatra gurutvaṃ paribhāṣitam ।। te viśeṣānna saṃpūjyāḥ smartavyā eva kevalam ।
tato abhyantarato vāyuvahnyormātṛkayā saha ।। mālinī kramaśaḥ pūjyā tato antarmantracakrakam । mantrasiddhaprāṇasaṃvitkaraṇātmani yā kule ।। cakrātmake citiḥ prabhvī proktā seha kuleśvarī ।
sā madhye śrīparā devī mātṛsadbhāvarūpiṇī ।। pūjyātha tatsamāropādaparātha parāparā । ekavīrā ca sā pūjyā yadivā sakuleśvarā ।। prasarecchaktirucchūnā sollāso bhairavaḥ punaḥ ।
saṅghaṭṭānandaviśrāntyā yugmamitthaṃ prapūjayet ।। mahāprakāśarūpāyāḥ saṃvido visphuliṅgavat । yo raśmyoghastamevātra pūjayeddevatāgaṇam ।। antardvādaśakaṃ pūjyaṃ tato aṣṭāṣṭākameva ca ।
catuṣkaṃ vā yathecchaṃ vā kā saṅkhyā kila raśmiṣu ।। māheśī vairiñcī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī caturdikkam । aindrī yāmyā muṇḍā yogeśīrīśatastu koṇeṣu ।। pavanāntamaghorādikamaṣṭakamasminnathāṣṭake kramaśaḥ ।
saṅghaṭṭānandadṛśā sampūjyaṃ yāmalībhūtam ।। aṣṭāṣṭake api hi vidhau nānānāmaprapañcite bahudhā । vidhireṣa eva vihitastatsaṃkhyā dīpamālā syāt ।। śrīratnamālāśāstre tu varṇasaṃkhyāḥ pradīpakāḥ ।
varṇāṃśca mukhyapūjyāyā vidyāyā gaṇayetsudhīḥ ।। pīṭhakṣetrādibhiḥ sākaṃ kuryādvā kulapūjanam । yathā śrīmādhavakule parameśena bhāṣitam ।। sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhārānāmakramacatuṣṭayam ।
pīṭhaśmaśānasahitaṃ pūjayedbhogamokṣayoḥ ।। ātmano vāthavā śakteścakrasyātha smaredimam । nyasyatvena vidhiṃ dehe pīṭhākhye pārameśvaram ।। aṭṭahāsaṃ śikhāsthāne caritraṃ ca karandhrake ।
śrutyoḥ kaulagiriṃ nāsārandhrayośca jayantikām ।। bhruvorujjayinīṃ vaktre prayāgaṃ hṛdaye punaḥ । vārāṇasīṃ skandhayuge śrīpīṭhaṃ virajaṃ gale ।। eḍābhīmudare hālāṃ nābhau kande tu gośrutim ।
upasthe marukośaṃ ca nagaraṃ pauṇḍravardhanam ।। elāpuraṃ purastīraṃ sakthyūrvordakṣiṇāditaḥ । kuḍyākeśīṃ ca sopānaṃ māyāpūkṣīrake tathā ।। jānujaṅghe gulphayugme tvāmrātanṛpasadmanī ।
pādādhāre tu vairiñcīṃ kālāgnyavadhidārikām ।। nāhamasmi nacānyo asti kevalāḥ śaktayastvaham । ityevaṃvāsanāṃ kuryātsarvadā smṛtimātrataḥ ।। na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ nopavāso vidhīyate ।
grāmyadharmarataḥ siddhyetsarvadā smaraṇena hi ।। mātaṅgakṛṣṇasaunikakārmukacārmikavikoṣidhātuvibhedāḥ । mātsyikacākrikadayitāsteṣāṃ patnyo navātra navayāge ।। saṅgamavaruṇākulagiryaṭṭahāsajayantīcaritrakāmrakakoṭṭam ।
haimapuraṃ navamaṃ syānmadhye tāsāṃ ca cakriṇī mukhyā ।। bījaṃ sā pīḍayate rasaśalkavibhāgato atra kuṇḍalinī । adhyuṣṭapīṭhanetrī kandasthā viśvato bhramati ।। iṣṭvā cakrodayaṃ tvitthaṃ madhye pūjyā kuleśvarī ।
saṅkarṣiṇī tadantānte saṃhārāpyāyakāriṇī ।। ekavīrā cakrayuktā cakrayāmalagāpi vā । īśendrāgniyamakravyātkavāyūdakṣu hāsataḥ ।। trikaṃ trikaṃ yajedetadbhāvisvatrikasaṃyutam ।
hṛtkuṇḍalī bhruvormadhyametadeva kramāttrayam ।। śmaśānāni kramātkṣetrabhavaṃ sadyoginīgaṇam । vasvaṅgulonnatānūrdhvavartulān kṣāmamadhyakān ।। raktavartīñśrutidṛśo dīpānkurvīta sarpiṣā ।
yatkiñcidathavā madhye svānuṣṭhānaṃ prapūjayet ।। advaitameva na dvaitamityājñā parameśituḥ । siddhāntavaiṣṇavādyuktā mantrā malayutāstataḥ ।। tāvattejo asahiṣṇutvānnirjīvāḥ syurihādvaye ।
kalaśaṃ netrabandhādi maṇḍalaṃ sruksruvānalam ।। hitvātra siddhiḥ sanmadye pātre madhye kṛśāṃ yajet । ahorātramimaṃ yāgaṃ kurvataścāpare ahani ।। vīrabhojye kṛte avaśyaṃ mantrāḥ siddhyantyayatnataḥ ।
pīṭhastotraṃ paṭhedatra yāge bhāgyāvahāhvaye ।। mūrtīrevāthavā yugmarūpā vīrasvarūpiṇīḥ । avadhūtā nirācārāḥ pūjayetkramaśo budhaḥ ।। eka evātha kauleśaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvāpi tāvatīḥ ।
śaktīryāmalayogena tarpayedviśvarūpavat ।। kramo nāma na kaścitsyātprakāśamayasaṃvidi । cidabhāvo hi nāstyeva tenākālaṃ tu tarpaṇam ।। atra krame bhedataroḥ samūlamunmūlanādāsanapakṣacarcā ।
pṛthaṅna yuktā parameśvaro hi svaśaktidhāmnīva viśaṃśramīti ।। tato japaḥ prakartavyastrilakṣādivibhedataḥ । uktaṃ śrīyogasañcāre sa ca citrasvarūpakaḥ ।। udaye saṅgame śāntau trilakṣo japa ucyate ।
āsye gamāgame sūtre haṃsākhye śaivayugmake ।। pañcalakṣā ime proktā daśāṃśaṃ homamācaret । netre gamāgame vaktre haṃse caivākṣasūtrake ।। śivaśaktisamāyoge ṣaḍlakṣo japa ucyate ।
netre gamāgame karṇe haṃse vaktre ca bhāmini ।। haste ca yugmake caiva japaḥ saptavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ । netre gamāgame karṇāvāsyaṃ guhyaṃ ca guhyakam ।। śatāreṣu ca madhyasthaṃ sahasrāreṣu bhāmini ।
japa eṣa rudralakṣo homo apyatra daśāṃśataḥ ।। netre gamāgame karṇau mukhaṃ brahmabilāntaram । stanau hastau ca pādau ca guhyacakre dvirabhyaset ।। yatra yatra gataṃ cakṣuryatra yatra gataṃ manaḥ ।
haṃsastatra dvirabhyasyo vikāsākuñcanātmakaḥ ।। sa ātmā mātṛkā devī śivo dehavyavasthitaḥ । anyaḥ so anyo ahamityevaṃ vikalpaṃ nācaredyataḥ ।। yo vilpayate tasya siddhimuktī sudūrataḥ ।
atha ṣoḍaśalakṣādiprāṇacāre puroktavat ।। śuddhāśuddhavikalpānāṃ tyāga ekānta ucyate । tatrasthaḥ svayamevaiṣa juhoti ca japatyapi ।। japaḥ sañjalpavṛttiśca nādāmarśasvarūpiṇī ।
tadāmṛṣṭasya cidvahnau layo homaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। āmarśaśca purā prokto devīdvādaśakātmakaḥ । dve antye saṃvidau tatra layarūpāhutikriyā ।। daśānyāstadupāyāyetyevaṃ home daśāṃśatām ।
śrīśambhunātha ādikṣattrikārthāmbhodhicandramāḥ ।। sākaṃ bāhyasthayā śaktyā yadā tveṣa samarcayet । tadāyaṃ parameśokto rahasyo bhaṇyate vidhiḥ ।। uktaṃ śrīyogasañcāre brahmacarye sthitiṃ bhajet ।
ānando brahma paramaṃ tacca dehe tridhā sthitam ।। upakāri dvayaṃ tatra phalamanyattadātmakam । oṣṭhyāntyatritayāsevī brahmacārī sa ucyate ।। tadvarjitā ye paśava ānandaparivarjitāḥ ।
ānandakṛttrimāhārāstadvarjaṃ cakrayājakāḥ ।। dvaye api niraye yānti raurave bhīṣaṇe tviti । śakterlakṣaṇametāvattadvato hyavibheditā ।। tādṛśīṃ tena tāṃ kuryānnatu varṇādyapekṣaṇam ।
laukikālaukikadvyātmasaṅgāttādātmyato adhikāt ।। kāryahetusahotthā sā tridhoktā śāsane guroḥ । sākṣātparamparāyogāttattulyeti tridhā punaḥ ।। śrīsarvācārahṛdaye tadetadupasaṃhṛtam ।
ṣaḍetāḥ śaktayaḥ proktā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ ।। dvābhyāṃ tu sṛṣṭisaṃhārau tasmānmelakamuttamam । tāmāhṛtya mitho abhyarcya tarpayitvā parasparam ।। antaraṅgakrameṇaiva mukhyacakrasya pūjanam ।
yadevānandasandohi saṃvido hyantaraṅgakam ।। tatpradhānaṃ bhaveccakramanucakramato aparam । vikāsāttṛptitaḥ pāśotkartanātkṛtiśaktitaḥ ।। cakraṃ kaseścakeḥ kṛtyā karoteśca kiloditam ।
yāgaśca tarpaṇaṃ bāhye vikāsastacca kīrtyate ।। cakrānucakrāntaragācchaktimatparikalpitāt । prāṇagādapyathānandasyandino abhyavahārataḥ ।। gandhadhūpasragādeśca bāhyāducchalanaṃ citaḥ ।
itthaṃ svocitavastvaṃśairanucakreṣu tarpaṇam ।। kurvīyātāmihānyonyaṃ mukhyacakraikatākṛte । uktaṃ ca triśirastantre vimalāsanagocaraḥ ।। akṣaṣaṭkasya madhye tu rudrasthānaṃ samāviśet ।
nijanijabhogābhogapravikāsinijasvarūpaparimarśe ।। kramaśo anucakradevyaḥ saṃviccakraṃ hi madhyamaṃ yānti । svasthatanoraparasya tu tā dehādhiṣṭhitaṃ vihāya yataḥ ।। āsata iti tadahaṃyurno pūrṇo nāpi cocchalati ।
anucakradevatātmakamarīciparipūraṇādhigatavīryam ।। tacchaktiśaktimadyugamanyonyasamunmukhaṃ bhavati । tadyugalamūrdhvadhāmapraveśasaṃsparśajātasaṅkṣobham ।। kṣubhnātyanucakrāṇyapi tāni tadā tanmayāni na pṛthaktu ।
itthaṃ yāmalametadgalitabhidāsaṃkathaṃ yadeva syāt ।। kramatāratamyayogātsaiva hi saṃvidvisargasaṅghaṭṭaḥ । taddhruvadhāmānuttaramubhayātmakajagadudārasānandam ।। no śāntaṃ nāpyuditaṃ śāntoditasūtikāraṇaṃ paraṃ kaulam ।
anavacchinnapadepsustāṃ saṃvidamātmasātsadā kuryāt ।। anavacchinnaṃ paramārthato hi rūpaṃ cito devyāḥ । īdṛktādṛkprāyapraśamodayabhāvavilayaparikathayā ।। anavacchinnaṃ dhāma praviśedvaisargikaṃ subhagaḥ ।
śāntoditātmakaṃ dvayamatha yugapadudeti śaktiśaktimatoḥ ।। rūpamuditaṃ parasparadhāmagataṃ śāntamātmagatameva । ubhayamapi vastutaḥ kila yāmalamiti tathoditaṃ śāntam ।। śaktistadvaducitāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ puṣṇāti no tadvān ।
śāntoditātmakobhayarūpaparāmarśasāmyayoge api ।। pravikasvaramadhyapadā śaktiḥ śāstre tataḥ kathitā । tasyāmeva kulārthaṃ samyak saṃcārayedgurustena ।। taddvāreṇa ca kathitakrameṇa saṃcārayeta nṛṣu ।
svaśarīrādhikasadbhāvabhāvitāmiti tataḥ prāha ।। śrīmatkallaṭanāthaḥ proktasamastārthalabdhaye vākyam । tanmukhyacakramuktaṃ maheśinā yoginīvaktram ।। tatraiṣa sampradāyastasmātsaṃprāpyate jñānam ।
tadidamalekhyaṃ bhaṇitaṃ vaktrādvaktrasthamuktayuktyā ca ।। vaktraṃ pradhānacakraṃ svā saṃvillikhyatāṃ ca katham । atha sṛṣṭe dvitaye asmin śāntoditadhāmni ye anusaṃdadhate ।। prācyāṃ visargasattāmanavacchidi te pade rūḍhāḥ ।
ye siddhimāptukāmāste abhyuditaṃ rūpamāhareyuratho ।। tenaiva pūjayeyuḥ saṃvinnaikaṭyaśuddhatamavapuṣā । tadapica mitho hi vaktrātpradhānato vaktragaṃ yato bhaṇitam ।। ajarāmarapadadānapravaṇaṃ kulasaṃjñitaṃ paramam ।
ye apyaprāptavibodhāste abhyuditotphullayāgasaṃrūḍhāḥ ।। tatparikalpitacakrasthadevatāḥ prāpnuvanti vijñānam । te tatra śakticakre tenaivānandarasamayena bahiḥ ।। dikṣu catasṛṣu proktakrameṇa gaṇanāthataḥ prabhṛti sarvam ।
saṃpūjya madhyamapade kuleśayugmaṃ tvarātraye devīḥ ।। bāhye pratyaramatha kila catuṣkamiti raśmicakramarkāram । aṣṭakamaṣṭāṣṭakamatha vividhaṃ saṃpūjayetkrameṇa muniḥ ।। nijadehagate dhāmani tathaiva pūjyaṃ samabhyasyet ।
yattacchāntaṃ rūpaṃ tenābhyastena hṛdayasaṃvittyā ।। śāntaṃ śivapadameti hi galitataraṅgārṇavaprakhyam । tacchāntapadādhyāsāccakrastho devatāgaṇaḥ sarvaḥ ।। tiṣṭhatyuparatavṛttiḥ śūnyālambī nirānandaḥ ।
yo apyanucakradṛgādisvarūpabhāk so api yattadāyattaḥ ।। tenānande magnastiṣṭhatyānandasākāṅkṣaḥ । paratatsvarūpasaṅghaṭṭamantareṇaiṣa karaṇaraśmigaṇaḥ ।। āste hi niḥsvarūpaḥ svarūpalābhāya conmukhitaḥ ।
raṇaraṇakarasānnijarasabharitabahirbhāvacarvaṇavaśena ।। viśrāntidhāma kiñcillabdhvā svātmanyathārpayate । tannijaviṣayārpaṇataḥ pūrṇasamucchalitasaṃvidāsāraḥ ।। anucakradevatāgaṇaparipūraṇajātavīryavikṣobhaḥ ।
cakreśvaro api pūrvoktayuktitaḥ procchaledrabhasāt ।। trividho visarga itthaṃ saṅghaṭṭaḥ proditastathā śāntaḥ । visṛjati yato vicitraḥ sargo vigataśca yatra sarga iti ।। śrītattvarakṣaṇe śrīnigame triśiromate ca tatproktam ।
kuṇḍaṃ śaktiḥ śivo liṅgaṃ melakaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। dvābhyāṃ sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtistadvisargastrividho game । srotodvayasya niṣṭhāntamūrdhvādhaścakrabodhanam ।। viśrāmaṃ ca samāveśaṃ suṣīṇāṃ marutāṃ tathā ।
gatabhedaṃ ca yantrāṇāṃ sandhīnāṃ marmaṇāmapi ।। dvāsaptatipade dehe sahasrāre ca nityaśaḥ । gatyāgatyantarā vittī saṅghaṭṭayati yacchivaḥ ।। tatprayatnātsadā tiṣṭhetsaṅghaṭṭe bhairave pade ।
ubhayostannirākārabhāvasaṃprāptilakṣaṇam ।। mātrāvibhāgarahitaṃ susphuṭārthaprakāśakam । abhyasyedbhāvasaṃvittiṃ sarvabhāvanivartanāt ।। sūryasomau tu saṃrudhya layavikṣepamārgataḥ ।
evaṃ trividhavimarśāveśasamāpattidhāmni ya udeti ।। saṃvitparimarśātmā dhvanistadeveha mantravīryaṃ syāt । tatraivoditatādṛśaphalalābhasamutsukaḥ svakaṃ mantram ।। anusandhāya sadā cedāste mantrodayaṃ sa vai vetti ।
atraiva japaṃ kuryādanucakraikatvasaṃvidāgamane ।। yugapallakṣavibhedaprapañcitaṃ nādavṛttyaiva । śrīyogasañcare apica mudreyaṃ yoginīpriyā paramā ।। koṇatrayāntarāśritanityonmukhamaṇḍalacchade kamale ।
satatāviyutaṃ nālaṃ ṣoḍaśadalakamalakalitasanmūlam ।। madhyasthanālagumphitasarojayugaghaṭṭanakramādagnau । madhyasthapūrṇasundaraśaśadharadinakarakalaughasaṅghaṭṭāt ।। tridalāruṇavīryakalāsaṅgānmadhye aṅkuraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ ।
iti śaśadharavāsarapaticitragusaṃghaṭṭamudrayā jhaṭiti ।। sṛṣṭyādikramamantaḥ kurvaṃsturye sthitiṃ labhate । etatkhecaramudrāveśe anyonyasya śaktiśaktimatoḥ ।। pānopabhogalīlāhāsādiṣu yo bhavedvimarśamayaḥ ।
avyaktadhvanirāvasphoṭaśrutinādanādāntaiḥ ।। avyucchinnānāhatarūpaistanmantravīryaṃ syāt । iti cakrāṣṭakarūḍhaḥ sahajaṃ japamācaran pare dhāmni ।। yadbhairavāṣṭakapadaṃ tallabhate aṣṭakakalābhinnam ।
gamanāgamane avasitau karṇe nayane dviliṅgasaṃparke ।। tatsaṃmelanayoge dehāntākhye ca yāmale cakre । kucamadhyahṛdayadeśādoṣṭhāntaṃ kaṇṭhagaṃ yadavyaktam ।। taccakradvayamadhyagamākarṇya kṣobhavigamasamaye yat ।
nirvānti tatra caivaṃ yo aṣṭavidho nādabhairavaḥ paramaḥ ।। jyotirdhvanisamirakṛtaḥ sā māntrī vyāptirucyate paramā । sakalākaleśaśūnyaṃ kalāḍhyakhamale tathā kṣapaṇakaṃ ca ।। antaḥsthaṃ kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyaṃ candrādvyāptistathonmanānteyam ।
evaṃ karmaṇi karmaṇi yatra kvāpi smaran vyāptim ।। satatamalepo jīvanmuktaḥ parabhairavībhavati । tādṛṅmelakakalikākalitatanuḥ ko api yo bhavedgarbhe ।। uktaḥ sa yoginībhūḥ svayameva jñānabhājanaṃ rudraḥ ।
śrīvīrāvaliśāstre bālo api ca garbhago hi śivarūpaḥ ।। ādīyate yataḥ sāraṃ tasya mukhyasya caiṣa yat । mukhyaśca yāgastenāyamādiyāga iti smṛtaḥ ।। tatra tatra ca śāstre asya svarūpaṃ stutavān vibhuḥ ।
śrīvīrāvalihārdeśakhamatārṇavavartiṣu ।। śrīsiddhotphullamaryādāhīnacaryākulādiṣu । yugmasyāsya prasādena vratayogavivarjitaḥ ।। sarvadā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ādiyāgaikatatparaḥ ।
śaktidehe nije nyasyedvidyāṃ kūṭamanukramāt ।। dhyātvā candranibhaṃ padmamātmānaṃ bhāskaradyutim । vidyāmantrātmakaṃ pīṭhadvayamatraiva melayet ।। na paṭhyate rahasyatvātspaṣṭaiḥ śabdairmayā punaḥ ।
kutūhalī tūktaśāstrasaṃpāṭhādeva lakṣayet ।। yadbhajante sadā sarve yadvān devaśca devatā । taccakraṃ paramaṃ devīyāgādau saṃnidhāpakam ।। deha eva paraṃ liṅgaṃ sarvatattvātmakaṃ śivam ।
devatācakrasaṃjuṣṭaṃ pūjādhāma taduttamam ।। tadeva maṇḍalaṃ mukhyaṃ tritriśūlābjacakrakham । tatraiva devatācakraṃ bahirantaḥ sadā yajet ।। svasvamantraparāmarśapūrvaṃ tajjanmabhī rasaiḥ ।
ānandabahulaiḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravidhinā spṛśet ।। tatsparśarabhasodbuddhasaṃviccakraṃ tadīśvaraḥ । labhate paramaṃ dhāma tarpitāśeṣadaivataḥ ।। anuyāgoktavidhinā dravyairhṛdayahāribhiḥ ।
tathaiva svasvakāmarśayogādantaḥ pratarpayet ।। kṛtvādhāradharāṃ camatkṛtirasaprokṣākṣaṇakṣālitāmāttairmānasataḥ svabhāvakusumaiḥ svāmodasandohibhiḥ । ānandāmṛtanirbharasvahṛdayānarghārghapātrakramāt tvāṃ devyā saha dehadevasadane devārcaye aharniśam ।। śrīvīrāvalyamaryādaprabhṛtau śāstrasañcaye ।
sa eṣa paramo yāgaḥ stutaḥ śītāṃśumaulinā ।। athavā prāṇavṛttisthaṃ samastaṃ devatāgaṇam । paśyetpūrvoktayuktyaiva tatraivābhyarcayedguruḥ ।। prāṇāśritānāṃ devīnāṃ brahmanāsādibhedibhiḥ ।
karandhrairviśatāpānacāndracakreṇa tarpaṇam ।। evaṃ prāṇakrameṇaiva tarpayeddevatāgaṇam । acirāttatprasādena jñānasiddhīrathāśnute ।। saṃvinmātrasthitaṃ devīcakraṃ vā saṃvidarpaṇāt ।
viśvābhogaprayogeṇa tarpaṇīyaṃ vipaścitā ।। yatra sarve layaṃ yānti dahyante tattvasañcayāḥ । tāṃ citiṃ paśya kāyasthāṃ kālānalasamaprabhām ।। śūnyarūpe śmaśāne asmin yoginīsiddhasevite ।
krīḍāsthāne mahāraudre sarvāstamitavigrahe ।। svaraśmimaṇḍalākīrṇe dhvaṃsitadhvāntasantatau । sarvairvikalpairnirmukte ānandapadakevale ।। asaṃkhyacitisaṃpūrṇe śmaśāne citibhīṣaṇe ।
samastadevatādhāre praviṣṭaḥ ko na siddhyati ।। śrīmadvīrāvalīśāstre itthaṃ provāca bhairavī । itthaṃ yāgaṃ vidhāyādau tādṛśaucityabhāginam ।। lakṣaikīyaṃ svaśiṣyaṃ taṃ dīkṣayettādṛśi krame ।
rudraśaktyā tu taṃ prokṣya devābhyāśe niveśayet ।। bhujau tasya samālokya rudraśaktyā pradīpayet । tayaivāsyārpayetpuṣpaṃ karayorgandhadigdhayoḥ ।। nirālambau tu tau tasya sthāpayitvā vicintayet ।
rudraśaktyākṛṣyamāṇau dīptayāṅkuśarūpayā ।। tataḥ sa svayamādāya vastraṃ baddhadṛśirbhavet । svayaṃ ca pātayetpuṣpaṃ tatpātāllakṣayetkulam ।। tato asya mukhamuddhāṭya pādayoḥ praṇipātayet ।
hastayormūrdhni cāpyasya devīcakraṃ samarcayet ।। ākarṣyākarṣakatvena preryaprerakabhāvataḥ । uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ nābhiṃ daṇḍena saṃpuṭam ।। vāmabhūṣaṇajaṅghābhyāṃ nitambenāpyalaṅkṛtam ।
śiṣyahaste puṣpabhṛte codanāstraṃ tu yojayet ।। yāvatsa stobhamāyātaḥ svayaṃ patati mūrdhani । śivahastaḥ svayaṃ so ayaṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaḥ ।। anenaiva prayogeṇa carukaṃ grāhayedguruḥ ।
śiṣyeṇa dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca tatpātaḥ prāgvadeva tu ।। karastobho netrapaṭagrahāt prabhṛti yaḥ kila । dantakāṣṭhasamādānaparyantastatra lakṣayet ।। tīvramandādibhedena śaktipātaṃ tathāvidham ।
ityeṣa samayī proktaḥ śrīpūrve karakampataḥ ।। samayī tu karastobhāditi śrībhogahastake । carveva vā gururdadyādvāmāmṛtapariplutam ।। niḥśaṅkaṃ grahaṇācchaktigotro māyojjhito bhavet ।
sakampastvādadānaḥ syāt samayī vācanādiṣu ।। kālāntare adhvasaṃśuddhyā pālanātsamayasthiteḥ । siddhipātramiti śrīmadānandeśvara ucyate ।। yadā tu putrakaṃ kuryāttadā dīkṣāṃ samācaret ।
uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ nādiphāntāṃ jvalatprabhām ।। nyasyecchikhāntaṃ patati tenātredṛk kramo bhavet । prokṣitasya śiśornyastaproktaśodhyādhvapaddhateḥ ।। ṛjudehajuṣaḥ śaktiṃ pādānmūrdhāntamāgatām ।
pāśāndahantīṃ saṃdīptāṃ cintayettanmayo guruḥ ।। upaviśya tatastasya mūlaśodhyāt prabhṛtyalam । antaśodhyāvasānāntāṃ dahantīṃ cintayetkramāt ।। evaṃ sarvāṇi śodhyāni tattvādīni puroktavat ।
dagdhvā līnāṃ śive dhyāyenniṣkale sakale athavā ।। yoginā yojitā mārge sajātīyasya poṣaṇam । kurute nirdahatyantadbhinnajātikadambakam ।। anayā śodhyamānasya śiśostīvrādibhedataḥ ।
śaktipātāccitivyomaprāṇanāntarbahistanūḥ ।। āviśantī rudraśaktiḥ kramātsūte phalaṃ tvidam । ānandamudbhavaṃ kampaṃ nidrāṃ ghūrṇiṃ ca dehagām ।। evaṃ stobhitapāśasya yojitasyātmanaḥ śive ।
śeṣabhogāya kurvīta sṛṣṭiṃ saṃśuddhatattvagām ।। athavā kasyacinnaivamāveśastaddahedimam । bahirantaścoktaśaktyā pateditthaṃ sa bhūtale ।। yasya tvevamapi syānna tamatropalavattyajet ।
atha sapratyayāṃ dīkṣāṃ vakṣye tuṣṭena dhīmatā ।। śaṃbhunāthenopadiṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭāṃ sadbhāvaśāsane । sudhāgnimaruto mandaparakālāgnivāyavaḥ ।। vahnisaudhāsukūṭāgnivāyuḥ sarve saṣaṣṭhakāḥ ।
etatpiṇḍatrayaṃ stobhakāri pratyekamucyate ।। śaktibījaṃ smṛtaṃ yacca nyasyetsārvāṅgikaṃ tu tat । hṛccakre nyasyate mantro dvādaśasvarabhūṣitaḥ ।। japākusumasaṃkāśaṃ caitanyaṃ tasya madhyataḥ ।
vāyunā preritaṃ cakraṃ vahninā paridīpitam ।। taddhyāyecca japenmantraṃ nāmāntaritayogataḥ । nimeṣārdhāttu śiṣyasya bhavetstobho na saṃśayaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ prekṣate devi tattve tattve niyojitaḥ ।
yāvatprāptaḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ tadā tveṣa na paśyati ।। anena kramayogena sarvādhvānaṃ sa paśyati । athavā sarvaśāstrāṇyapyudgrāhayati tatkṣaṇāt ।। pṛthaktattvavidhau dīkṣāṃ yogyatāvaśavartinaḥ ।
tattvābhyāsavidhānena siddhayogī samācaret ।। iti saṃdīkṣitasyāsya mumukṣoḥ śeṣavartane । kulakrameṣṭirādeśyā pañcāvasthāsamanvitā ।। jāgradādiṣu saṃvittiryathā syādanapāyinī ।
kulayāgastathādeśyo yoginīmukhasaṃsthitaḥ ।। sarvaṃ jāgrati kartavyaṃ svapne pratyekamantragam । nivārya supte mūlākhyaḥ svaśaktiparibṛṃhitaḥ ।। turye tvekaiva dūtyākhyā tadatīte kuleśitā ।
svaśaktiparipūrṇānāmitthaṃ pūjā pravartate ।। piṇḍasthādi ca pūrvoktaṃ sarvātītāvasānakam । avasthāpañcakaṃ proktabhedaṃ tasmai nirūpayet ।। sādhakasya bubhukṣostu samyagyogābhiṣecanam ।
tatreṣṭvā vibhavairdevaṃ hemādimayamavraṇam ।। dīpāṣṭakaṃ raktavartisarpiṣāpūrya bodhayet । kulāṣṭakena tatpūjyaṃ śaṅkhe cāpi kuleśvarau ।। ānandāmṛtasaṃpūrṇe śivahastoktavartmanā ।
tenābhiṣiñcettaṃ paścāt sa kuryānmantrasādhanam ।। ācāryasyābhiṣeko ayamadhikārānvitaḥ sa tu । kuryātpiṣṭādibhiścāsya catuṣṣaṣṭiṃ pradīpakān ।। aṣṭāṣṭakena pūjyāste madhye prāgvat kuleśvarau ।
śivahastoktayuktyaiva gurumapyabhiṣecayet ।। abhiṣiktāvimāvevaṃ sarvayogigaṇena tu । viditau bhavatastatra gururmokṣaprado bhavet ।। tātparyamasya pādasya sa siddhīḥ saṃprayacchati ।
gururyaḥ sādhakaḥ prāksyādanyo mokṣaṃ dadātyalam ।। anayoḥ kathayejjñānaṃ trividhaṃ sarvamapyalam । svakīyājñāṃ ca vitaret svakriyākaraṇaṃ prati ।। ṣaṭkaṃ kāraṇasaṃjñaṃ yattathā yaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ ।
sākaṃ bhairavanāthena tadaṣṭakamudāhṛtam ।। pratyekaṃ tasya sārvātmyaṃ paśyaṃstāṃ vṛttimātmagām । cakṣurādau saṃkramayedyatra yatrendriye guruḥ ।। sa eva pūrṇaiḥ kalaśairabhiṣekaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ।
vinā bāhyairapītyuktaṃ śrīvīrāvalibhairave ।। sadya eva tu bhogepsoryogātsiddhatamo guruḥ । kuryātsadyastathābhīṣṭaphaladaṃ vedhadīkṣaṇam ।। vedhadīkṣā ca bahudhā tatra tatra nirūpitā ।
sā cābhyāsavatā kāryā yenordhvordhvapraveśataḥ ।। śiṣyasya cakrasaṃbhedapratyayo jāyate dhruvaḥ । yenāṇimādikā siddhiḥ śrīmālāyāṃ ca coditā ।। ūrdhvacakradaśālābhe piśācāveśa eva sā ।
mantranādabinduśaktibhujaṅgamaparātmikā ।। ṣoḍhā śrīgahvare vedhadīkṣoktā parameśinā । jvālākulaṃ svaśāstroktaṃ cakramaṣṭārakādikam ।। dhyātvā tenāsya hṛccakravedhanānmantravedhanam ।
ākāraṃ navadhā dehe nyasya saṃkramayettataḥ ।। nyāsayogena śiṣyāya dīpyamānaṃ mahārciṣam । pāśastobhāttatastasya paratattve tu yojanam ।। iti dīkṣottare dṛṣṭo vidhirme śaṃbhunoditaḥ ।
nādoccāreṇa nādākhyaḥ sṛṣṭikramaniyogataḥ ।। nādena vedhayeccittaṃ nādavedha udīritaḥ । bindusthānagataṃ cittaṃ bhrūmadhyapathasaṃsthitam ।। hṛllakṣye vā maheśāni binduṃ jvālākulaprabham ।
tena saṃbodhayetsādhyaṃ bindvākhyo ayaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।। śāktaṃ śaktimaduccārādgandhoccāreṇa sundari । śṛṅgāṭakāsanasthaṃ tu kuṭilaṃ kuṇḍalākṛtim ।। anuccāreṇa coccārya vedhayennikhilaṃ jagat ।
evaṃ bhramaravedhena śāktavedha udāhṛtaḥ ।। sā caiva paramā śaktirānandapravikāsinī । janmasthānātparaṃ yāti phaṇapañcakabhūṣitā ।। kalāstattvāni nandādyā vyomāni ca kulāni ca ।
brahmādikāraṇānyakṣāṇyeva sā pañcakātmikā ।। evaṃ pañcaprakārā sā brahmasthānavinirgatā । brahmasthāne viśantī tu taḍillīnā virājate ।। praviṣṭā vedhayetkāyamātmānaṃ pratibhedayet ।
evaṃ bhujaṅgavedhastu kathito bhairavāgame ।। tāvadbhāvayate cittaṃ yāvaccittaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam । kṣīṇe citte sureśāni parānanda udāhṛtaḥ ।। nendriyāṇi na vai prāṇā nāntaḥkaraṇagocaraḥ ।
na mano nāpi mantavyaṃ na mantā na manikriyā ।। sarvabhāvaparikṣīṇaḥ paravedha udāhṛtaḥ । manuśaktibhuvanarūpajñāpiṇḍasthānanāḍiparabhedāt ।। navadhā kalayantyanye vedaṃ guravo rahasyavidaḥ ।
māyāgarbhāgnivarṇaughayukte tryaśriṇi maṇḍale ।। dhyātvā jvālākarālena tena granthīn vibhedayet । puṣpairhanyādyojayecca pare mantrābhidho vidhiḥ ।। nāḍyāviśyānyatarayā caitanyaṃ kandadhāmani ।
piṇḍīkṛtya paribhramya pañcāṣṭaśikhayā haṭhāt ।। śaktiśūlāgragamitaṃ kvāpi cakre niyojayet । śaktyeti śākto vedho ayaṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaḥ ।। ādhārānnirgatayā śikhayā jyotsnāvadātayā rabhasāt ।
aṅguṣṭhamūlapīṭhakrameṇa śiṣyasya līnayā vyomni ।। dehaṃ svacchīkṛtya kṣādīnāntān smaranpuroktapuryoghān । nijamaṇḍalanirdhyānātpratibimbayate bhuvanavedhaḥ ।। bhrūmadhyoditabaindavadhāmāntaḥ kāṃcidākṛtiṃ rucirām ।
tādātmyena dhyāyecchiṣyaṃ paścācca tanmayīkuryāt ।। iti rūpavedha uktaḥ sā cehākṛtirupaiti dṛśyatvam । ante tatsāyujyaṃ śiṣyaścāyāti tanmayībhūtaḥ ।। vijñānamaṣṭadhā yaddhrāṇādikabuddhisaṃjñakaraṇāntaḥ ।
tat svasvanāḍisūtrakrameṇa saṃcārayecchiṣye ।। abhimānadārḍhyabandhakrameṇa vijñānasaṃjñako vedhaḥ । hṛdayavyomani sadyo divyajñānārkasamudayaṃ dhatte ।। piṇḍaḥ paraḥ kalātmā sūkṣmaḥ puryaṣṭako bahiḥ sthūlaḥ ।
chāyātmā sa parāṅmukha ādarśādau ca saṃmukho jñeyaḥ ।। iti yaḥ piṇḍavibhedastaṃ rabhasāduttarottare śamayet । tattadnalane kramaśaḥ paramapadaṃ piṇḍavedhena ।। yadyaddehe cakraṃ tatra śiśoretya viśramaṃ kramaśaḥ ।
ujjvalayettaccakraṃ sthānākhyastatphalaprado vedhaḥ ।। nāḍyaḥ pradhānabhūtāstisro anyāstadgatāstvasaṃkhyeyāḥ । ekīkārastābhirnāḍīvedho atra tatphalakṛt ।। abhilaṣitanāḍivāho mukhyābhiścakṣurādiniṣṭhābhiḥ ।
adbodhaprāptiḥ syānnāḍīvedhe vicitrabahurūpā ।। lāṅgūlākṛtibalavat svanāḍisaṃvoṣṭitāmaparanāḍīm । āsphoṭya siddhamapi bhuvi pātayati haṭhānmahāyogī ।। paravedhaṃ samasteṣu cakreṣvadvaitamāmṛśan ।
paraṃ śivaṃ prakurvīta śivatāpattido guruḥ ।। śrīmadvīrāvalikule tathā cetthaṃ nirūpitam । abhedyaṃ sarvathā jñeyaṃ madhyaṃ jñātvā na lipyate ।। tadvibhāgakrame siddhaḥ sa gururmocayet paśūn ।
guroragre viśecchiṣyo vaktraṃ vaktre tu vedhayet ।। rūpaṃ rūpe tu viṣayairyāvatsamarasībhavet । citte samarasībhūte dvayoraunmanasī sthitiḥ ।। ubhayośconmanogatyā tatkāle dīkṣito bhavet ।
śaśibhāskarasaṃyoge jīvastanmayatāṃ vrajet ।। atra brahmādayo devā muktaye mokṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ । nirudhya raśmicakraṃ svaṃ bhogamokṣāvubhāvapi ।। grasate yadi taddīkṣā śārvīyaṃ parikīrtitā ।
sa eṣa mokṣaḥ kathito niḥspandaḥ sarvajantuṣu ।। agnīṣomakalāghātasaṅghātāt spandanaṃ haret । bāhyaṃ prāṇaṃ bāhyagataṃ timirākārayogataḥ ।। niryātaṃ romakūpaistu bhramantaṃ sarvakāraṇaiḥ ।
madhyaṃ nirlakṣyamāsthāya bhramayedvisṛjettataḥ ।। saṃghaṭṭotpāṭayogena vedhayedgranthipañcakam । saṃghaṭṭavṛttiyugalaṃ madhyadhāma vicintayet ।। nātmavyomabahirmantradehasaṃdhānamācaret ।
dīkṣeyaṃ sarvajantūnāṃ śivatāpattidāyikā ।। dīkṣānte dīpakān paktvā samastaiḥ sādhakaiḥ saha । caruḥ prāśyaḥ kulācāryairmahāpātakanāśanaḥ ।। iti śrīratnamālāyāmūnādhikavidhistu yaḥ ।
sa eva pātakaṃ tasya praśamo ayaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।। pare ahani guroḥ kāryo yāgastena vinā yataḥ । na vidhiḥ pūrṇatāṃ yāti kuryādyatnena taṃ tataḥ ।। yena yena gurustuṣyettattadasmai nivedayet ।
cakracaryāntarāle asyā vidhiḥ saṃcāra ucyāte ।। alipātraṃ susaṃpūrṇaṃ vīrendrakarasaṃsthitam । avalokya paraṃ brahma tatpivedājñayā guroḥ ।। tarpayitvā tu bhūtāni gurave vinivedayet ।
kṛtvā bhuvi guruṃ natvādāya saṃtarpya khecarīḥ ।। svaṃ mantraṃ tacca vanditvā dūtīṃ gaṇaptiṃ gurūn । kṣetrapaṃ vīrasaṅghātaṃ gurvādikramaśastataḥ ।। vīraspṛṣṭaṃ svayaṃ dravyaṃ pivennaivānyathā kvacit ।
parabrahmaṇyavettāro agamāgamavivarjitāḥ ।। lobhamohamadakrodharāgamāyājuṣaśca ye । taiḥ sākaṃ na ca kartavyametacchreyorthinātmani ।। yāgādau yāgamadhye ca yāgānte gurupūjane ।
naimittikeṣu prokteṣu śiṣyaḥ kuryādimaṃ vidhim ।। iti rahasyavidhiḥ paricarcito gurumukhānubhavaiḥ suparisphuṭaḥ । atha yathocitamantrakadambakaṃ trikakulakramayogi nirūpyate । tāvadvimarśānārūḍhadhiyāṃ tātsiddhaye kramāt ।।
pratibuddhā hi te mantrā vimarśaikasvabhāvakāḥ । svatantrasyaiva ciddhāmnaḥ svātantryāt kartṛtāmayāḥ ।। yamāviśanti cācāryaṃ taṃ tādātmyanirūḍhitaḥ । svatantrīkurvate yānti karaṇānyapi kartṛtām ।।
ādhāraśaktau hrīṃ pṛthvīprabhṛtau tu catuṣṭaye । kṣlāṃ kṣvīṃ vaṃ kṣamiti prāhuḥ kramādvarṇacatuṣṭayam ।। haṃ nāle yaṃ tathā raṃ laṃ vaṃ dharmādicatuṣṭaye । ṛṃ ṝṃ ḷṃ ḷḷṃ catuṣke ca viparītakramādbhavet ।।
oṃ auṃ hastrayamityetadvidyāmāyākalātraye । anusvāravisargau ca vidyeśeśvaratattvayoḥ ।। kādibhāntāḥ kesareṣu prāṇo aṣṭasvarasaṃyutaḥ । sabinduko daleṣvaṣṭasvatha svaṃ nāma dīpitam ।।
śaktīnāṃ navakasya syācchaṣasā maṇḍalatraye । sabindukāḥ kṣmaṃ prete jraṃ śūlaśṛṅgeṣu kalpayet ।। pṛthagāsanapūjāyāṃ kramānmantrā ime smṛtāḥ । saṃkṣepapūjane tu prāgādyamantyaṃ ca bījakam ।।
ādāyādhāraśaktyādiśūlaśṛṅgāntamarcayet । agnimārutapṛthvyambusaṣaṣṭhasvarabindukam ।। ratiśekharamantro asya vaktrāṅgaṃ hrasvadīrghakaiḥ । agniprāṇāgnisaṃhārakālendrāmbusamīraṇāḥ ।।
saṣaṣṭhasvarabirndvadhacandrādyāḥ syurnavātmanaḥ । bindunādādikā vyāptiḥ śrīmattraiśirase mate ।। kṣepākrānticidudbodhadīpanasthāpanānyatha । tatsaṃvittistadāpattiriti saṃjñābhiśabditā ।।
etāvatī mahāvyāptirmūrtitvenātra kīrtitā । pariṇāmastallayaśca namaskāraḥ sa ucyate ।। eṣa tryarṇojjhito adhastāddīrghaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairyutaḥ । ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛdādīni vaktrāṇyasya ca kalpayet ।।
kṣayaravalabījaistu dīptairbinduvibhūṣitaiḥ । jhakārasaṃhṛtiprāṇāḥ saṣaṣṭhasvarabindukāḥ ।। eṣa bhairavasadmāvaścandrārdhādivibhūṣitaḥ । mātṛkāmālinīmantrau prāgeva samudāhṛtau ।।
oṃkāro atha caturthyantā saṃjñā natiriti kramāt । gaṇeśādiṣu mantraḥ syādbījaṃ yeṣu na coditam ।। nāmādyakṣaramākārabinducandrādidīpitam । sarveṣāmeva bījānāṃ taccaturdaśaṣaṣṭhayuk ।।
āmantritānyaghoryāditritayasya kramoditaiḥ । bījairvisargiṇī māyā huṃ hakāro visargavān ।। punardevītrayasyāpi kramādāmantraṇatrayam । dvitīyasminpade akāra ekārasyeha ca smṛtaḥ ।।
tataḥ śaktidvayāmantro luptaṃ tatrāntyamakṣaram । he agnivarṇāvubhau pañcasvarayuktau parau pṛthak ।। akārayuktāvastraṃ huṃ ha visargī punaḥ śaraḥ । tāreṇa saha vasvagnivarṇārdhārṇadvayādhikā ।।
eṣā parāparādevyā vidyā śrītrikaśāsane । pañcaṣaṭpañcavedākṣivahninetrākṣaraṃ padam ।। aghoryādau saptake syāt pivanyāḥ pariśiṣṭakam । pratyekavarṇago apyuktaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate ।।
devatācakravinyāsaḥ sa bahutvānna lipyate । māyā visargiṇī huṃ phaṭ ceti mantro aparātmakaḥ ।। parāyāstūktasadvyāptirjīvaḥ sahacaturdaśaḥ । sānekabhedā triśiraḥśāstre proktā maheśinā ।।
svarūpato vibhinnāpi racanānekasaṅkulā । jīvaḥ prāṇastha evātra prāṇo vā jīvasaṃsthitaḥ ।। ādhārādheyabhāvena avinābhāvayogataḥ । haṃsaṃ cāmṛtamadhyasthaṃ kālarudravibheditam ।।
bhuvaneśaśiroyuktamanaṅgadvayayojitam । dīptāddīptataraṃ jñeyaṃ ṣaṭcakrakramayojitam ।। prāṇaṃ daṇḍāsanasthaṃ tu guhyaśaktīcchayā yutam । pareyaṃ vācikoddiṣṭā mahājñānasvarūpataḥ ।।
sphuṭaṃ bhairavahṛjjñānamidaṃ tvekākṣaraṃ param । amṛtaṃ kevalaṃ khasthaṃ yadvā sāvitrikāyutam ।। śūnyadvayasamopetaṃ parāyā hṛdayaṃ param । yugmayāge prasiddhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ tattvavedibhiḥ ।।
anye apyekākṣarā ye tu ekavīravidhānataḥ । guptā guptatarāste tu aṃgābhijanavarjitāḥ ।। yaṣṭavyāḥ sādhakendraistu kulasthāḥ siddhidāyakāḥ । kulakramavidhānena sūkṣmavijñānayogataḥ ।।
anuṣṭheyāḥ sadā devi striyā vā puruṣeṇa vā । sakāro dīrghaṣaṭkena yukto aṅgānyānanāni tu ।। syāt sa eva paraṃ hrasvapañcasvarakhasaṃyutaḥ । oṃkāraiḥ pañcabhirmantro vidyāṅgahṛdayaṃ bhavet ।।
praṇavaścāmṛte tejomālini svāhayā saha । ekādaśākṣaraṃ brahmaśirastanmālinīmate ।। vedavedani hūṃ phaṭca praṇavādiyutā śikhā । vajriṇe vajradharāya svāhetyoṃkārapūrvakam ।।
ekādaśākṣaraṃ varma puruṣṭutamiti smṛtam । tāro dvijihvaḥ khaśarasvarayugjīva eva ca ।। netrametatprakāśātma sarvasādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam । tāraḥ ślīṃ paśu huṃ phat ca tadastraṃ rasavarṇakam ।।
laraṭakṣavayairdīrghaiḥ samayuktaiḥ sabindukaiḥ । indrādayastadastrāṇi hrasvairviṣṇuprajāpatī ।। smṛtau turyadvitīyābhyāṃ hrasvābhyāṃ padmacakrake । namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ ca jātayaḥ ।।
aṅgeṣu kramaśaḥ ṣaṭsu karmasvatha tadātmikāḥ । jape home tathāpyāye samuccāṭe atha śāntike ।। abhicāre ca mantrāṇāṃ namaskārādijātayaḥ । akṣiṣaṇmunivargebhyo dvitīyāḥ saha bindunā ।।
yonyarṇena ca mātṝṇāṃ sadmāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī । ādyojjhito vāpyantena varjito vātha saṃmataḥ ।। jīvaḥ prāṇapuṭāntaḥsthaḥ kālānalasamadyutiḥ । atidīptastu vāmāṃghrirbhūṣito mūrdhni bindunā ।।
dakṣajānugataścāyaṃ sarvamātṛgaṇārcitaḥ । anena prāṇitāḥ sarve dadate vāñchitaṃ phalam ।। sadbhāvaḥ paramo hyeṣa mātṝṇāṃ bhairavasya ca । tasmādenaṃ japenmantrī ya icchetsiddhimuttamām ।।
rudraśaktisamāveśo nityamatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ । yasmādeṣā parā śaktirbhedenānyena kīrtitā ।। yāvatyaḥ siddhayastantre tāḥ sarvāḥ kurute tviyam । aṅgavaktrāṇi cāpyasyāḥ prāgvatsvaraniyogataḥ ।।
daṇḍo jīvastriśūlaṃ ca dakṣāṅgulyaparastanau । nābhikaṇṭhau marudrudrau visargaḥ satriśūlakaḥ ।। sarvayoginicakrāṇāmadhipo ayamudāhṛtaḥ । asyāpyuccāraṇādeva saṃvittiḥ syātpuroditā ।।
mahācaṇḍeti tu yogeśvaṛ ityaṣṭavarṇakam । navārṇeyaṃ guptatarā sadbhāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī ।। śrīḍāmare mahāyāge parātparataroditā । sudhācchedakaṣaṇṭhādyairbījaṃ chedakamasvaram ।।
adhyardhārṇā kālarātriḥ kṣurikā mālinīmate । śatāvartanayā hyasyā jāyate mūrdhni vedanā ।। evaṃ pratyayamālocya mṛtyujiddhyānamāśrayet । naināṃ samuccareddevi ya iccheddīrghajīvitam ।।
dvirdaṇḍāgnī śūlanabhaḥprāṇāśchettranalau tathā । kūṭāgnī savisargāśca pañcāpyete atha pañcasu ।। vyomasviti śivenoktaṃ tantrasadbhāvaśāsane । chedinī kṣurikeyaṃ syādyayā yojayate pare ।।
bindvindvanalakūṭāgnimarutṣaṣṭhasvarairyutam । āpādatalamūrdhāntaṃ smaredastramidaṃ jvalat ।। kuñcanaṃ cāṅgulīnāṃ tu kartavyaṃ codanaṃ tataḥ । jānvādiparacakrāntaṃ cakrāccakraṃ tu kuñcayet ।।
kathitaṃ sarahasyaṃ tu sadyonirvāṇakaṃ param । athocyate brahmavidyā sadyaḥpratyayadāyinī ।। śivaḥ śrībhūtirājo yāmasmabhyaṃ pratyapādayat । sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ maraṇe samupasthite ।।
yayā paṭhitayotkramya jīvo yāti nirañjanam । yā jñānino api saṃpūrṇakṛtyasyāpi śrutā satī ।। prāṇādicchedajāṃ mṛtyuvyathāṃ sadyo vyapohati । yāmākarṇya mahāmohavivaśo api kramādgataḥ ।।
prabodhaṃ vaktṛsāṃmukhyamabhyeti rabhasātsvayam । paramapadāttvamihāgāḥ sanātanastvaṃ jahīhi dehāntam ।। pādāṅguṣṭhādi vibho nibandhanaṃ bandhanaṃ hyugram । āryāvākyamidaṃ pūrvaṃ bhuvanākhyaiḥ padairbhavet ।।
gulphānte jānugataṃ jatrusthaṃ bandhanaṃ tathā meḍhre । jahihi puramagryamadhyaṃ hṛtpadmāttvaṃ samuttiṣṭha ।। etāvadbhiḥ padairetadāryāvākyaṃ dvitīyakam । haṃsa hayagrīva vibho sadāśivastvaṃ paro asi jīvākhyaḥ ।।
ravisomavahnisaṅghadṛbindudeho hahaha samutkrāma । tṛtīyamāryāvākyaṃ prāksaṃkhyairekādhikaiḥ padaiḥ ।। haṃsamahāmantramayaḥ sanātanastvaṃ śubhāśubhāpekṣī । maṇḍalamadhyaniviṣṭaḥ śaktimahāsetukāraṇamahārthaḥ ।।
kamalobhayaviniviṣṭaḥ prabodhamāyāhi devatādeha । āryāvākyamidaṃ sārdhaṃ rudrasaṃkhyapaderitam ।। niḥśvāse tvapaśabdasya sthāne astyupa iti dhvaniḥ । ajñānāttvaṃ baddhaḥ prabodhitottiṣṭha devāde ।।
etatpañcamamāryārdhavākyaṃ syātsaptabhiḥ padaiḥ । vraja tālusāhvayāntaṃ hyauḍambaraghaṭṭitaṃ mahādvāram ।। prāpya prayāhi haṃho haṃho vā vāmadevapadam । āryyāvākyamidaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ syāccaturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ ।।
granthīśvara paramātman śānta mahātālurandhramāsādya । utkrama he deheśvara nirañjanaṃ śivapadaṃ prayāhyāśu ।। āryāvākyaṃ saptamaṃ syāttaccaturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ । prabhañjanastvamityevaṃ pāṭho niḥśvāsaśāsane ।।
ākramya madhyamārgaṃ prāṇāpānau samāhṛtya । dharmādharmau tyaktvā nārāyaṇa yāhi śāntāntam ।। āryāvākyamidaṃ proktamaṣṭamaṃ navabhiḥ padaiḥ । he brahman he viṣṇo he rudra śivo asi vāsudevastvam ।।
agnīṣomasanātanamṛtpiṇḍaṃ jahihi he mahākāśa । etadbhuvanasaṃkhyātairāryyāvākyaṃ prakīrtitam ।। sanātma tripiṇḍamiti mahākośamiti sthitam । padatrayaṃ tu niḥśvāsamukuṭottarakādiṣu ।।
aṅguṣṭhamātramamalamāvaraṇaṃ jahihi he mahāsūkṣma । āryyāvākyamidaṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ padairdaśamamucyate ।। alaṃ dviriti sūkṣmaṃ cetyevaṃ śrīmukuṭottare । puruṣastvaṃ prakṛtimayairbaddho ahaṅkāratantunā bandhaiḥ ।।
abhavābhava nityodita paramātmaṃstyaja sarāgamadhvānam । etattrayodaśapadaṃ syādāryāvākyamuttamam ।। hrīṃhūṃmantraśarīramavilambamāśu tvamehi dehāntam । āryārdhavākyametatsyād dvādaśaṃ ṣaṭpadaṃ param ।।
tadidaṃ guṇabhūtamayaṃ tyaja sva ṣoṭkośikaṃ piṇḍam । syāt trayodaśamāryārdhaṃ padaiḥ saptabhirīdṛśam ।। mā dehaṃ bhūtamayaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ śāśvataṃ mahādeham । āryārdhavākyaṃ tāvadbhiḥ padairetaccaturdaśam ।।
maṇḍalamamalamanantaṃ tridhā sthitaṃ gaccha bhittvaitat । āryārdhavākyamaṣṭābhiḥ padaiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tvidam ।। sakaleyaṃ brahmavidyā syātpañcadaśabhiḥ sphuṭaiḥ । vākyaiḥ pañcākṣaraistvasyā niṣkalā parikīrtyate ।।
prativākyaṃ yayādyantayojitā paripaṭhyate । tāro māyā vedakalo mātṛtāro navātmakaḥ ।। iti pañcākṣarāṇi syuḥ proktavyāptyanusārataḥ । binduprāṇāmṛtajalaṃ marutṣaṣṭhasvarānvitam ।।
etena śaktyuccārasthabījenālabhyate paśuḥ । kṛtadīkṣāvidhiḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaghno api viśuddhyati ।। laghutvena tulāśuddhiḥ sadyaḥpratyayakāriṇī । tāraḥ śamarayaiḥ piṇḍo natiśca caturarṇakam ।।
śākinīstobhanaṃ marma hṛdayaṃ jīvitaṃ tvidam । ṣaṣṭhaprāṇatrikūṭordhvabāhuśūlākhyabindubhiḥ ।। anackanāsādhovaktracandrakhaṇḍaiśca maṇḍitam । hṛdayaṃ bhairavākhyaṃ tu sarvasaṃhārakārakam ।।
agnimaṇḍalamadhyasthabhairavānalatāpitāḥ । vaśamāyānti śākinyaḥ sthānametena ceddahet ।। visarjayettāḥ prathamamanyathā cchidrayanti tāḥ । hrīṃ klīṃ vleṃ kleṃ ebhirvarṇairdvādaśasvarabhūṣitaiḥ ।।
priyamelāpanaṃ nāma hṛdayaṃ sampuṭaṃ japet । pratyekamathavā dvābhyāṃ sarvairvā vidhiruttamaḥ ।। tulāmelakayogaḥ śrītantrasadbhāvaśāsane । ya uktaḥ śambhunāthena sa mayā darśitaḥ kramāt ।।
atha vittavihīnānāṃ prapannānāṃ ca tattvataḥ । deśakālādidoṣeṇa na tathādhyavasāyinām ।। prakartavyā yathā dīkṣā śrīsantatyāgamoditā । kathyate hāṭakeśānapātālādhipacoditā ।।
śrīnātha ārya bhagavannetattritayaṃ hi kanda ādhāre । varuṇo macchando bhagavatta iti trayamidaṃ hṛdaye ।। dharmādivargasaṃjñāścatvāraḥ kaṇṭhadeśagāḥ pūjyāḥ । hrīṃśrīṃpūrvāḥ sarve sambodhajuṣaśca pādaśabdāntāḥ ।।
mūrdhatale vidyātrayamuktaṃ bhāvyatha mano abhiyogena । kusumairānandairvā bhāvanayā vāpi kevalayā ।। guruṇā tattvavidā kila śiṣyo yadi mokṣamātrakṛtahṛdayaḥ । mokṣaikadānacaturā dīkṣā seyaṃ paropaniṣaduktā ।।
etaddīkṣādīkṣita etadvidyātrayaṃ smaran hṛdaye । bāhyārcādi vinaiva hi vrajati paraṃ dhāma dehānte ।। praṇavo māyā bindurvarṇatrayamāditaḥ kuryāt । padapañcakasya saṃbodhanayuktasyāgnidayitānte ।।
siddhasādhani tatpūrvaṃ śabdabrahmasvarūpiṇi । samastabandhaśabdena sahitaṃ ca nikṛntani ।। bodhani śivasadbhāvajananyāmantritaṃ ca tat । pañcāṣṭarandhratryaṣṭārṇakrameṇa padapañcakam ।।
khapañcārṇā parabrahmavidyeyaṃ mokṣadā śivā । anuttarecche ghāntaśca satrayodaśasusvaraḥ ।। asya varṇatrayasyānte tvantaḥsthānāṃ catuṣṭayam । vargādyaśvau tryasrabinduyuk pānto arṇatrayādataḥ ।।
mahāhāṭakaśabdādyamīśvarītyarṇasaptakam । āmantritaṃ kṣamasveti tryarṇaṃ pāpāntakāriṇi ।। ṣaḍarṇaṃ pāpaśabdādivimohanipadaṃ tataḥ । pāpaṃ hana dhuna dvirdvirdaśārṇaṃ padamīdṛśam ।।
pañcamyantaṃ ṣaḍarṇaṃ syādrudraśaktivaśāditi । tata ekākṣaraṃ yattadvisargabrahma kīrtitam ।। tadanackatakāreṇa sahaikībhāvataḥ paṭhet । randhrābdhivarṇā vidyeyaṃ dīkṣāvidyeti kīrtitā ।।
māyārṇañca pare brahme caturvidye padatrayam । aṣṭārṇamatha pañcārṇaṃ yogadhāriṇisaṃjñitam ।। ātmāntarātmaparamātmarūpaṃ ca padatrayam । ekārāntaṃ bodhanasthaṃ daśārṇaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
rudraśaktīti vedārṇaṃ syādrudradayite atha me । pāpaṃ dahadahetyeṣā dvādaśārṇā catuṣpadī ।। saumye sadāśive yugmaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ bindviṣusāvahā । sārdhavarṇacatuṣkaṃ tadityeṣā samayāpahā ।।
vidyā sārdhārṇakhaśarasaṃkhyā sā pārameśvarī । etadvidyātrayaṃ śrīmadbhūtirājo nyarūpayat ।। yaḥ sākṣādabhajacchrīmāñśrīkaṇṭho mānuṣīṃ tanum । atra vīryaṃ puraivoktaṃ sarvatrānusaredguruḥ ।।
arthabījapraveśāntaruccārādyanusārataḥ । nahi tatkiṃcanāpyasti yatpurā na nirūpitam ।। niṣphalā punaruktistu nāsmabhyaṃ jātu rocate । ityevaṃ mantravidyādisvarūpamupavarṇitam ।।
atha maṇḍalasadbhāvaḥ saṃkṣepeṇābhidhīyate । sādhayitvā diśaṃ pūrvāṃ sūtramāsphālayetsamam ।। tadardhayitvā madhyaprākpratīcīṣvaṅkayetpunaḥ । tato apyardhatadardhārdhamānataḥ pūrvapaścimau ।।
aṅkayettāvatā dadyāt sūtreṇa bhramayugmakam । matsyasandhidvayaṃ tvevaṃ dakṣiṇottarayorbhavet ।। tanmadhye pātayetsūtraṃ dakṣiṇottarasiddhaye । yadi vā prākparāktulyasūtreṇottaradakṣiṇe ।।
aṅkayedaparādaṅkāt pūrvādapi tathaiva te । matsyamadhye kṣipetsūtramāyataṃ dakṣiṇottare ।। matakṣetrārdhamānena madhyāddikṣvaṅkayettataḥ । sūtrābhyāṃ digdvayotthābhyāṃ matsyaḥ syātpratikoṇagaḥ ।।
matsyeṣu vedāḥ sūtrāṇītyevaṃ syāccaturasrakam । ekasmātprabhṛti proktaṃ śatāntaṃ maṇḍalaṃ yataḥ ।। siddhātantre maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ tatpīṭha ucyate । yattanmadhyagataṃ mukhyaṃ maṇḍalānāṃ trayaṃ smṛtam ।।
madhyaśūlaṃ tritriśūlaṃ navaśūlamiti sphuṭam । tatra śūlavidhānaṃ yaduktaṃ bhedairanantakaiḥ ।। tadyoni maṇḍalaṃ brūmaḥ sadbhāvakramadarśitam । vedāśrite caturhaste tribhāgaṃ sarvatastyajet ।।
bhāgaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sarvaṃ tattatkṣetraṃ vibhājayet । brahmasūtradvayasyātha madhyaṃ brahmapadaṃ sphuṭam ।। kṛtvāvadhiṃ tato lakṣyaṃ caturthaṃ sūtramāditaḥ । tatastiryagvrajet sūtraṃ caturthaṃ tadanantare ।।
koṣṭhe cendudvayaṃ kuryādbahirbhāgārdhabhāgataḥ । tayorlagnaṃ brahmasūtrāttṛtīye marmaṇi sthitam ।। koṣṭhakārdhe aparaṃ ceti yugmamantarmukhaṃ bhavet । brahmasūtrāddvitīyasmin haste marmaṇi niścalam ।।
kṛtvā pūrṇenduyugalaṃ vartayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ । brahmasūtragatāt ṣaṣṭhāt tiryagbhāgāttṛtīyake ।। kṛtvārdhakoṣṭhake sūtraṃ pūrṇacandrāgralambitam । bhramayedunmukhaṃ khaṇḍacandrayugvahnibhāgagam ।।
tiryagbhāgadvayaṃ tyaktvā khaṇḍendoḥ paścimāttataḥ । koṇaṃ yāvattathā syācca kuryāt khaṇḍaṃ bhramadvayam ।। sutīkṣṇakuṭilāgraṃ tadekaṃ śṛṅgaṃ prajāyate । dvitīyasminnapi proktaḥ śṛṅga eṣa vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ ।।
madhyaśṛṅge atha kartavye tṛtīye ūrdhvakoṣṭhake । caturthārdhe ca candrārdhadvayamantarmukhaṃ bhavet ।। tacca pūrṇendumekaṃ prāgvartitaṃ prāpnuyādyathā । anyonyagranthiyogena baddhāratvaṃ prajāyate ।।
evaṃ dvitīyapārśve asya khaṇḍendudvayavartanāt । madhyābhyāṃ gaṇḍikā śliṣṭā parābhyāmagrato nayet ।। sūtraṃ pārśvadvaye yena tīkṣṇaṃ syānmadhyaśṛṅgagam । pārśvadvayādhare paścādbrahmasūtraṃ dvitīyakam ।।
avadhānena saṃgrāhyamācāryeṇohavedinā । bhavetpaścānmukho mantrī tasmiṃśca brahmasūtrake ।। madhyaśṛṅgaṃ varjayitvā sarvaḥ pūrvodito vidhiḥ । tato yadunmukhaṃ khaṇḍacandrayugmaṃ puroditam ।।
tato dvayena kartavyā gaṇḍikāntaḥsusaṃgatā । dvayenāgragasūtrābhyāṃ madhyaśṛṅgadvayaṃ bhavet ।। adho bhāgavivṛddhyāsya padmaṃ vṛttacatuṣṭayam । tataścakraṃ ṣoḍaśāraṃ dvādaśāraṃ dvidhātha tat ।।
madhye kuleśvarīsthānaṃ vyoma vā tilakaṃ ca vā । padmaṃ vātha ṣaḍaraṃ vā viyaddvādaśakaṃ ca vā ।। tritriśūle atra saptāre śliṣṭamātreṇa madhyataḥ । padmānāmatha cakrāṇāṃ vyomnāṃ vā saptakaṃ bhavet ।।
miśritaṃ vātha saṃkīrṇaṃ samāsavyāsabhedataḥ । tataḥ kṣetrārdhamānena kṣetraṃ tatrādhikaṃ kṣipet ।। tatra daṇḍaḥ smṛto bhāgaḥ ṣaḍarāmalasārakaḥ । sutīkṣṇāgraḥ suraktābhaḥ kṣaṇādāveśakārakaḥ ।।
yā sā kuṇḍalinī devī taraṅgākhyā mahormiṇī । sā ṣaḍaśreṇa kandākhye sthitā ṣaḍdevatātmikā ।। aṣṭabhāgaiśca vistīrṇo dīrghaścāpi tadardhataḥ । tato dvārāṇi kāryāṇi citravartanayā kramāt ।।
vedāśrāyatarūpāṇi yadivā vṛttamātrataḥ । spaṣṭaśṛṅgamatho kuryādyadivā vaiparītyataḥ ।। unmukhaṃ candrayugmaṃ vā bhaṅktvā kuryāccatuṣṭayam । kuṭilo madhyataḥ spaṣṭo adhomukhaḥ pārśvagaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
uttāno ardho asamaḥ pūrṇaḥ śliṣṭo granthigatastathā । candrasyetthaṃ dvādaśadhā vartanā bhramabhedinī ।। antarbahirmukhatvena sā punardvividhā matā । tadbhedānmaṇḍalānāṃ syādasaṅkhyo bhedavistaraḥ ।।
pīṭhavīthībahiarbhūmikaṇṭhakarṇakapolataḥ । śobhopaśobhāsaṃbhedādguṇarekhāvikalpataḥ ।। svastikadvitayādyaṣṭatayāparyantabhedataḥ । bhāvābhāvavikalpena maṇḍalānāmanantatā ।।
tato rajāṃsi deyāni yathāśobhānusārataḥ । sindūraṃ rājavartaṃ ca khaṭikā ca sitottamā ।। uttamāni rajāṃsīha devatātrayayogataḥ । parā candrasamaprakhyā raktā devī parāparā ।।
aparā sā parā kālī bhīṣaṇā caṇḍayoginī । dṛṣṭvaitanmaṇḍalaṃ devyaḥ sarvā nṛtyanti sarvadā ।। anarcite apyadīkṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dīkṣyeta mātṛbhiḥ । kiṃvātibahunoktena tritriśūlārasaptakāḥ ।।
śūlayāgāḥ ṣaṭ sahasrāṇyevaṃ sārdhaśatadvayam । yā sā devī parā śaktiḥ prāṇavāhā vyavasthitā ।। viśvāntaḥ kuṇḍalākārā sā sākṣādatra vartitā । tattvāni tattvadevyaśca viśvamasminpratiṣṭhitam ।।
atrordhve tantumātreṇa tisraḥ śūlāragāḥ sthitāḥ । āsanatvena cecchādyā bhogamokṣaprasādhikāḥ ।। tāstu mokṣaikakāmasya śūlārāviddhamadhyakāḥ । tasmādenaṃ mahāyāgaṃ mahāvibhavavistaraiḥ ।।
pūjayedbhūtikāmo vā mokṣakāmo apivā budhaḥ । asya darśanamātreṇa bhūtavetālaguhyakāḥ ।। palāyante daśa diśaḥ śivaḥ sākṣātprasīdati । mandaśaktibalāviddho apyetanmaṇḍalapūjanāt ।।
satataṃ māsaṣaṭkena trikajñānaṃ samaśnute । yatprāpya heyopādeyaṃ svayameva vicārya saḥ ।। dehānte syādbhairavātmā siddhikāmo atha siddhyati । maṇḍalasyāsya yo vyāptiṃ devatānyāsameva ca ।।
vartanāṃ ca vijānāti sa gurustrikaśāsane । tasya pādarajo mūrdhni dhāryaṃ śivasamīhinā ।। atra sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsān kramāt trīnapi pūjayet । turyaṃ tu madhyato yadvā sarveṣu paripūrakam ।।
catustriśūlaṃ vā guptadaṇḍaṃ yāgaṃ samācaret । tatra tat pūjayetsamyak sphuṭaṃ kramacatuṣṭayam ।। ityetatkathitaṃ gupte ṣaḍardhahṛdaye pare । ṣaṭke proktaṃ sūcitaṃ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate ।।
agrataḥ sūtrayitvā tu maṇḍalaṃ sarvakāmadam । mahāśūlasamopetaṃ padmacakrādibhūṣitam ।। dvāre dvāre likhecchūlaṃ varjayitvā tu paścimam । koṇeṣvapica vā kāryaṃ mahāśūlaṃ drumānvitam ।।
amṛtāmbhobhavārīṇāṃ śūlāgre tu trikaṃ trikam । śūla itthaṃ prakartavyamaṣṭadhā tat tridhāpivā ।। evaṃ saṃsūcitaṃ divyaṃ khecarīṇāṃ puraṃ tviti । sthānāntare api kathitaṃ śrīsiddhātantraśāsane ।।
kajaṃ madhye tadardhena śūlaśṛṅgāṇi tāni tu । śūlāṅkaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kalpyaṃ kamalāṅkaṃ ca pūraṇe ।। atha śūlābjavinyāsaḥ śrīpūrve triśiromate । siddhātantre trikakule devyāyāmalamālayoḥ ।।
yathoktaḥ sāraśāstre ca tantrasadbhāvaguhyayoḥ । tathā pradarśyate spaṣṭaṃ yadyapyuktakramādgataḥ ।। vedāśrite trihaste prāk pūrvamardha vibhājayet । hastārdhaṃ sarvatastyaktvā pūrvodagyāmyadiggatam ।।
tryaṅgulaiḥ koṣṭhakairūrdhvaistiryak cāṣṭadvidhātmakaiḥ । dvau dvau bhāgau parityajya punardakṣiṇasaumyagau ।। brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayorjīvāccaturthāt pūrvatastathā । bhāgārdhabhāgamānaṃ tu khaṇḍacandradvayaṃ dvayam ।।
tayorantastṛtīye tu dakṣiṇottarapārśvayoḥ । jīve khaṇḍenduyugalaṃ kuryādantarbhramādbudhaḥ ।। tayoraparamarmasthaṃ khaṇḍendudvayakoṭigam । bahirmukhaṃ bhramaṃ kuryāt khaṇḍacandradvayaṃ dvayam ।।
tadvadbrahmaṇi kurvīta bhāgabhāgārdhasaṃmitam । tato dvitīyabhāgānte brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayordvayoḥ ।। dve rekhe pūrvage neye bhāgatryaṃśaśame budhaiḥ । ekārdhendūrdhvakoṭisthaṃ brahmasūtrāgrasaṅgatam ।।
sūtradvayaṃ prakurvīta madhyaśṛṅgaprasiddhaye । tadagrapārśvayorjīvāt sūtramekāntare dhṛtam ।। ādidvitīyakhaṇḍendukoṇāt koṇāntamānayet । tayorevāparājjīvāt prathamārdhendukoṇataḥ ।।
tadvadeva nayetsūtraṃ śṛṅgadvitayasiddhaye । kṣetrārdhe cāpare daṇḍo dvikaraśchannapañcakaḥ ।। ṣaḍvistṛtaṃ caturdīrghaṃ tadadho amalasārakam । vedāṅgulaṃ ca tadadho mūlaṃ tīkṣṇāgramiṣyate ।।
ādikṣetrasya kurvīta dikṣu dvāracatuṣṭayam । hastāyāmaṃ tadardhaṃ vā vistārādapi tatsamam ।। dviguṇaṃ bāhyataḥ kuryāttataḥ padmaṃ yathā śṛṇu । ekaikabhāgamānāni kuryādvṛttāni vedavat ।।
dikṣvaṣṭau punarapyaṣṭau jīvasūtrāṇi ṣoḍaśa । dvayordvayoḥ punarmadhye tatsaṃkhyātāni pātayet ।। eṣāṃ tṛtīyavṛttasthaṃ pārśvajīvasamaṃ bhramam । etadantaṃ prakurvīta tato jīvāgramānayet ।।
yatraiva kutracitsaṅgastatsaṃbandhe sthirīkṛte । tatra kṛtvā nayenmantrī patrāgrāṇāṃ prasiddhaye ।। ekaikasmindale kuryātkesarāṇāṃ trayaṃ trayam । dviguṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ tadvacchṛṅgakajatrayam ।।
karṇikā pītavarṇena mūlamadhyāgrabhedataḥ । sitaṃ raktaṃ tathā pītaṃ kāryaṃ kesarajālakam ।। dalāni śuklavarṇāni prativāraṇayā saha । pīṭhaṃ tadvaccatuṣkoṇaṃ karṇikārdhasamaṃ bahiḥ ।।
sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaistatpādān vahnitaḥ kramāt । caturbhirapi śṛṅgāṇi tribhirmaṇḍalamiṣyate ।। daṇḍaḥ syānnīlaraktena pītamāmalasārakam । raktaṃ śūlaṃ prakurvīta yattatpūrvaṃ prakalpitam ।।
paścāddvārasya pūrveṇa tyaktvāṅgulacatuṣṭayam । dvāraṃ vedāśri vṛttaṃ vā saṃkīrṇaṃ vā vicitritam ।। ekadvitripuraṃ tulyaṃ sāmudgamathavobhayam । kapolakaṇṭhaśobhopaśobhādibahucitritam ।।
vicitrākārasaṃsthānaṃ vallīsūkṣmagṛhānvitam । śrīdevyāyāmale tūktaṃ kṣetre vedāśrite sati ।। ardhaṃ dvādaśadhā kṛtvā tiryagūrdhvaṃ ca tiryajam । bhāgamekaṃ svapārśvordhvaṃ guruḥ samavatārayet ।।
madhyasthaṃ taṃ tribhāgaṃ ca tadante bhramayedubhau । bhāgamekaṃ parityajya tanmadhye bhramayetpunaḥ ।। tṛtīyāṃśordhvato bhrāmyamūrdhvāṃśaṃ yāvadantataḥ । caturthāṃśāttadūrdhvaṃ tu ūrdhvādho yojayetpunaḥ ।।
tanmānādūrdhvamābhrāmya caturthena niyojayet । ūrdhvādyojayate sūtraṃ brahmasūtrāvadhi kramāt ।। kramādvaipulyataḥ kṛtvā aṃśaṃ vai hrāsayet punaḥ । ardhabhāgapramāṇastu daṇḍo dviguṇa iṣyate ।।
bhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ gṛhītvā tu ubhayoratha gocarāt । bhrāmyaṃ pippalavat patraṃ vartanaiṣā tvadho bhavet ।। ṣoḍaśāṃśe likhetpadmaṃ dvādaśāṅgulalopanāt । tadūrdhvaṃ madhyabhāge tu vārijanma samālikhet ।।
madhyaśṛṅgāvasāne tu tṛtīyaṃ vilikhettataḥ । savyāsavye tathaiveha kaṭisthābje samālikhet ।। karṇikā pītalā raktapītaśuklaṃ ca kesaram । dalāni padmabāhyasthā śuklā ca prativāraṇī ।।
śūlaṃ kṛṣṇena rajasā brahmarekhā sitā punaḥ । śūlāgraṃ jvālayā yuktaṃ śūladaṇḍastu pītalaḥ ।। śūlamadhye ca yatpadmaṃ tatreśaṃ pūjayetsadā । asyordhve tu parāṃ dakṣe anyāṃ vāme cāparāṃ budhaḥ ।।
yā sā kālāntakā devī parātītā vyavasthitā । grasate śūlacakraṃ sā tvicchāmātreṇa sarvadā ।। śāntirūpā kalā hyeṣā vidyārūpā parā bhavet । aparā tu pratiṣṭhā syānnivṛttistu parāparā ।।
bhairavaṃ daṇḍa ūrdhvasthaṃ rūpaṃ sādāśivātmakam । catasraḥ śaktayastvasya sthūlāḥ sūkṣmāstvanekadhā ।। eṣa yāgaḥ samākhyāto ḍāmarākhyastriśaktikaḥ । atha traiśirase śūlābjavidhirdṛṣṭo abhilikhyate ।।
vāmāmṛtādibhirmukhyaiḥ pavitraiḥ sumanoramaiḥ । bhūmiṃ rajāṃsi karaṇīṃ khaṭikāṃ mūlato arcayet ।। caturaśre caturhaste madhye śūlaṃ karatrayam । caṇḍo dvihasta ūrdhvādhaḥpīṭhayugvipulastvasau ।।
vasvaṅgulaḥ prakartavyaḥ sūtratrayasamanvitaḥ । dvādaśāṅgulamānena daṇḍamūle tu pīṭhikā ।। dairghyāttūcchrāyāccordhve ca caturaṅgulamānataḥ । ūrdhve apyucchrāyato vedāṅgulā dairghyāddaśāṅgulā ।।
śūlamūlagataṃ pīṭhīmadhyaṃ khābdhisamāṅgulam । kṛtvā daṇḍaṃ triśūlaṃ tu tribhirbhāgaiḥ samantataḥ ।। aṣṭāṅgulapramāṇaiḥ syāddhastamātraṃ samantataḥ । śūlāgraṃ śūlamadhyaṃ tacchūlamūlaṃ tu tadbhavet ।।
vedī madhye prakartavyā ubhayośca ṣaḍaṅgulam । dvādaśāṅguladīrghā tu ubhayoḥ pārśvayostathā ।। caturaṅgulamucchrāyānmūle vedīṃ prakalpayet । ubhayoḥ pārśvayoścaivamardhacandrākṛtiṃ tathā ।।
bhrāmayet khaṭikāsūtraṃ kaṭiṃ kuryāddviraṅgulām । vaipulyāddairghyato devi caturaṅgulamānataḥ ।। yādṛśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge vāme tadvatprakalpayet । madhye śūlāgravaipulyādaṅgulaśca adhordhvataḥ ।।
caturaṅgulamānena vaipulyāttu ṣaḍaṅgulā । ucchrāyāttu tataḥ kāryā gaṇḍikā tu svarūpataḥ ।। pīṭhordhve tu prakartavyaṃ śūlamūlaṃ tu suvrate । śūlāgramaṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ sutīkṣṇaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgulam ।।
arāmadhyaṃ prakartavyamarādhastu ṣaḍaṅgulam । caturaṅgulanimnaṃ tu madhyaṃ tu parikalpayet ।। pūrvāparaṃ tadeveha madhye śūlaṃ tu tadbahiḥ । kārayeta tribhiḥ sūtrairekaikaṃ vartayeta ca ।।
kajatrayaṃ tu śūlāgraṃ vedāṃśairdvādaśāṅgulam । kramāddakṣānyamadhyeṣu tryaṣṭadvādaśapatrakam ।। cakratrayaṃ vātapuraṃ padmamaṣṭāṅgulārakam । vidyābhikhyaṃ śūlamūle rajaḥ paścātprapātayet ।।
triśūlaṃ daṇḍaparyantaṃ rājavartena pūrayet । sūtratrayasya pṛṣṭhe tu śuklaṃ cārātrayaṃ bhavet ।। śuklena rajasā śūlamūle vidyāmbujaṃ bhavet । raktaṃ raktāsitaṃ śuklaṃ kramādūrdhvāmbujatrayam ।।
śuklena vyomarekhā syāt sā sthaulyādaṅgulaṃ bahiḥ । tāṃ tyaktvā vedikā kāryā hastamātraṃ pramāṇātaḥ ।। vaipulyatriguṇaṃ dairghyāt prākāraṃ caturaśrakam । samantato atha dikṣu syurdvārāṇi karamātrataḥ ।।
tridhā vibhajya kramaśo dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ । kaṇṭhaṃ kapolaṃ śobhāṃ tu upaśobhāṃ tadantataḥ ।। prākāraṃ caturaśraṃ tu sabhūrekhāsamanvitam । sitaraktapītakṛṣṇai rajobhiḥ kārayettataḥ ।।
raktai rajobhirmadhyaṃ tu yathāśobhaṃ tu pūrayet । asyā vyāptau purā coktaṃ tatraivānusarecca tat ।। arātrayavibhāgastu praveśo nirgamo bhramaḥ । anāhatapadavyāptiḥ kuṇḍalyā udayaḥ paraḥ ।।
hṛdi sthāne gatā devyastriśūlasya sumadhyame । nābhisthaḥ śūladaṇḍastu śūlamūlaṃ hṛdi sthitam ।। śaktisthānagataṃ prāntaṃ prānte cakratrayaṃ smaret । utkṣipyotkṣipya kalayā dehamadhyasvarūpataḥ ।।
śūladaṇḍāntamadhyasthaśūlamadhyāntagocaram । praviśenmūlamadhyāntaṃ prāntānte śaktiveśmani ।। aspandakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ekadā spandavartanam । mūlamānandamāpīḍya śaktitrayapadaṃ viśet ।।
tatra pūjyaṃ prayatnena jāyante sarvasiddhayaḥ । samastādhvasamāyogāt ṣoḍhādhvavyāptibhāvataḥ ।। samastamantracakrādyairevamādiprayatnataḥ । ṣaṭtriṃśattattvaracitaṃ triśūlaṃ paribhāvayet ।।
viṣuvatsthena vinyāso mantrāṇāṃ maṇḍalottame । kāryo asmin pūjite yatra sarveśvarapadaṃ bhajet ।। svastikenātha kartavyaṃ yuktaṃ tasyocyate vidhiḥ । nāḍikāḥ sthāpayetpūrvaṃ muhūrtaṃ parimāṇataḥ ।।
śakravāruṇadiksthāśca yāmyasaumyagatāstathā । ekonatriṃśadvaṃśāḥ syurṛjutiryaggatāstathā ।। aṣṭau marmaśatānyekacatvāriṃśacca jāyate । vaṃśairviṣayasaṃkhyaiśca padmaṃ yugmendumaṇḍalam ।।
rasasaṃkhyairbhavetpīṭhaṃ svastikaṃ sarvakāmadam । vasusaṃkhyairdvāravīthāvevaṃ bhāgaparikramaḥ ।। randhravipraśarāgnīṃśca lupyedbāhyāntaraṃ kramāt । marmāṇi ca caturdikṣu madhyāddvāreṣu sundari ।।
vahnibhūtamunivyomabāhyagarbhe purīṣu ca । lopayeccaiva marmāṇi antarnāḍivivarjitān ।। dvāraprākārakoṇeṣu netrānalaśarānṛtūn । nāḍayo brahmavaṃśasya lopyā netrādrasasthitāḥ ।।
vahnernetrānalau lopyau vedānnetrayugaṃ rasāt । netraṃ saumyagataṃ lopyaṃ pūrvādvedānalau rasāt ।। lokasthā nāḍikā hitvā netrādvedāgnayaḥ kramāt । śarairvahnigataṃ caiva yugaṃ netrāgnayo rasāt ।।
netrāt pūrvagatāccaiva sumerurdvārasaṃjñitaḥ । svastikā ca purī ramyā caturdikṣu sthitāvubhau ।। marmaṇāṃ ca śate dve ca ṛṣibhirguṇitā diśaḥ । netrādikāṃśca saṃmārjya mārgamadhyāt suśobhane ।।
ṛṣitrayakṛte madhye viṣayaiḥ karṇikā bhavet । netrīkṛtānvasūn patraṃ netraṃ sakṛdvibhājitam ।। vahniṃ vasugataṃ kṛtvā śaśāṅkasthāṃśca lopayet । vahnīṣuṛṣimadhyācca lopyaṃ pīṭhendukāvadhi ।।
brahmaṇo netraviṣayānnetrādvedānalau haret । sāgare netrakaṃ lopyaṃ nāḍayaḥ pūrvadiggatāḥ ।। bhūtanetragatānmūrdhnā netrāddvivahnidṛktrikāt । saumyagāt pīṭhakoṇeṣu lopayeta caturṣvapi ।।
dalāni kāryāṇi sitaiḥ kesaraṃ raktapītalaiḥ । karṇikā kanakaprakhyā pallavāntāśca lohitāḥ ।। vyomarekhā tu susitā vartulābjāntanīlabhāḥ । pīṭhaṃ rekhātrayopetaṃ sitalohitapītalam ।।
svastikāśca caturvarṇā agnerīśānagocarāḥ । vīthī vidrumasaṃkāśā svadikṣvastrāṇi bāhyataḥ ।। indranīlanibhaṃ vajraṃ śaktiṃ padmamaṇiprabhām । daṇḍaṃ hāṭakasaṃkāśaṃ vaktraṃ tasyātilohitam ।।
nīladyutisamaṃ khaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ vatsakasaprabham । dhvajaṃ puṣpaphalopetaṃ pañcaraṅgaiśca śobhitam ।। gadā hemanibhātyugrā nānāratnavibhūṣitā । śūlaṃ nīlāmbujasamaṃ jvaladvahnyugraśekharam ।।
tasyopari sitaṃ padmamīṣatpītāruṇaprabham । cakraṃ hemanibhaṃ dīptamarā vaiḍūryasaṃnibhāḥ ।। arāmadhyaṃ supītaṃ ca bāhyaṃ jvālāruṇaṃ bhavet । mandiraṃ devadevasya sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
śrīsiddhāyāṃ śūlavidhiḥ prāk kṣetre caturaśrite । hastamātraṃ tridhā sūryānnavakhaṇḍaṃ yathā bhavet ।। madhye śūlaṃ ca tatretthaṃ madhyabhāgaṃ tridhā bhajet । navabhiḥ koṣṭhakairyuktaṃ tato ayaṃ vidhirucyate ।।
madhyabhāgatrayaṃ tyaktvā madhye bhāgadvayasya tu । adhastādbhrāmayetsūtraṃ śaśāṅkaśakalākṛti ।। ubhayato bhrāmayettatra yathāgre hākṛtirbhavet । koṭyāṃ tatra kṛtaṃ sūtraṃ nayedrekhāṃ tu pūrvikām ।।
aparadvārapūrveṇa tyaktvāṅgulacatuṣṭayam । rekhāṃ vināśayetprājño yathā śūlākṛtirbhavet ।। śūlāgre tvardhahastena tyaktvā padmāni kārayet । adhaḥ śṛṅgatrayaṃ hastamadhye padmaṃ sakarṇikam ।।
mukhāgre dhārayetsūtraṃ tribhirhastaistu pātayet । madhye cordhvaṃ tataḥ kuryādadhastādaṅguladvayam ।। rekhādvayaṃ pātayeta yathā śūlaṃ bhavatyapi । adhobhāgādibhiścordhvaṃ tatra rekhā prapadyate ।।
samīkṛtya tataḥ sūtre ūrdhve dve evameva tu । madhyaṃ padmaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ śūlādhastādyaśasvini ।। ityeṣa maṇḍalavidhiḥ kathitaḥ saṃkṣepayogato mahāgurubhiḥ । atha kathaye mudrāṇāṃ gurvāgamagītamatra vidhim ।
mudrā ca pratibimbātmā śrīmaddevyākhyayāmale । uktā bimbodayaśrutyā vācyadvayavivecanāt ।। bimbātsamudayo yasyā ityuktā pratibimbatā । vimbasya yasyā udaya ityuktā tadupāyatā ।।
mudaṃ svarūpalābhākhyaṃ dehadvāreṇa cātmanām । rātyarpayati yattena mudrā śāstreṣu varṇitā ।। tatra pradhānabhūtā śrīkhecarī devatātmikā । niṣkalatvena vikhyātā sākalyena triśūlinī ।।
karaṅkiṇī krodhanā ca bhairavī lelihānikā । mahāpretā yogamudrā jvālinī kṣobhiṇī dhruvā ।। ityevaṃbahubhedeyaṃ śrīkhecaryeva gīyate । anyāstadaṅgabhūtāstu padmādyā mālinīmate ।।
tāsāṃ bahutvāmukhyatvayogābhyāṃ neha varṇanam । śrīkhecarīsamāviṣṭo yadyatsthānaṃ samāśrayet ।। devīsaṃnidhaye tatsyādalaṃ kiṃ ḍambarairvṛthā । kāmye karmaṇi tāśca syurmukhyāḥ kasyāpi jātucit ।।
mudrā caturvidhā kāyakaravākcittabhedataḥ ।। tatra pūrṇena rūpeṇa khecarīmeva varṇaye । baddhvā padmāsanaṃ yogī nābhāvakṣeśvaraṃ kṣipet ।। daṇḍākāraṃ tu taṃ tāvannayedyāvatkakhatrayam ।
nigṛhya tatra tattūrṇaṃ prerayet khatrayeṇa tu ।। etāṃ baddhvā khe gatiḥ syāditi śrīpūrvaśāsane । dhvanijyotirmarudyuktaṃ cittaṃ viśramya copari ।। anenābhyāsayogena śivaṃ bhittvā paraṃ vrajet ।
jatrvadhastātkarau kṛtvā vāmapādaṃ ca dakṣiṇe ।। vidāryāsyaṃ kaniṣṭhābhyāṃ madhyamābhyāṃ tu nāsikām । anāme kuñcayetprājño bhrūbhaṅgaṃ tarjanīdvayam ।। jihvāṃ ca cālayenmantrī hāhākāraṃ ca kārayet ।
triśūlena prayogeṇa brahmarandhramupasthitaḥ ।। padaṃ santyajya tanmātraṃ sadyastyajati medinīm । śūnyāśūnyalaye kṛtvā ekadaṇḍe anilānalau ।। śaktitritayasambaddhe adhiṣṭhātṛtridaivate ।
triśūlaṃ tadvijānīyādyena vyomotpatedbudhaḥ ।। ākāśabhāvaṃ santyajya sattāmātramupasthitaḥ । śūlaṃ samarasaṃ kṛtvā rase rasa iva sthitaḥ ।। ekadaṇḍaṃ sa vijñāya triśūlaṃ khacaraṃ priye ।
baddhvā tu khecarīṃ mudrāṃ dhyātvātmānaṃ ca bhairavam ।। khecarīcakrasaṃjuṣṭaṃ sadyastyajati medinīm । tyaktāṃśako nirācāro niḥśaṅko lokavarjitaḥ ।। avadhūto nirācāro nāhamasmīti bhāvayam ।
mantraikaniṣṭhaḥ saṃpaśyan dehasthāḥ sarvadevatāḥ ।। hlādodvegāsmitākruṣṭanidrāmaithunamatsare । rūpādau vā kartṛkarmakaraṇeṣu ca sarvaśaḥ ।। nāhamasmīti manvāna ekībhūtaṃ vicintayan ।
karṇākṣimukhanāsādicakrasthaṃ devatāgaṇam ।। grahītāraṃ sadā paśyan khecaryā siddhyati sphuṭam । vidyāśaṅkī malāśaṅkī śāstraśaṅkī na siddhyati ।। śivo raviḥ śivo vahniḥ paktṛtvātsa purohitaḥ ।
tatrasthā devatāḥ sarvā dyotayantyo akhilaṃ jagat ।। kaniṣṭhayā vidāryāsyaṃ tarjanībhyāṃ bhruvau tathā । anāme madhyame vaktre jihvayā tālukaṃ spṛśet ।। eṣā karaṅkiṇī devī jvālinīṃ śṛṇu sāṃpratam ।
hanurlalāṭagau hastau prasāryāṅgulitaḥ sphuṭau ।। cālayedvāyuvegena kṛtvāntarbhrukuṭīṃ budhaḥ । vidāryāsyaṃ sajihvaṃ ca hāhākāraṃ tu kārayet ।। eṣā jvālinyagnicakre tayā cāṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।
japedyadi tataḥ siddhyettrailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। paradeheṣu cātmānaṃ paraṃ cātmaśarīrataḥ । paśyeccarantaṃ hānādādgamāgamapadasthitam ।। navacchidragataṃ caikaṃ nadantaṃ vyāpakaṃ dhruvam ।
anayā hi khacārī śrīyogasañcāra ucyate ।। kulakuṇḍalikāṃ baddhvā aṇorantaravedinīm । vāmo yo ayaṃ jagatyasmiṃstasya saṃharaṇodyatām ।। svasthāne nirvṛtiṃ labdhvā jñānāmṛtarasātmakam ।
vrajetkandapadaṃ madhye rāvaṃ kṛtvā hyarāvakam ।। yāvajjīvaṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ piṇḍādhāraṃ ca kāmikam । tatra tāṃ bodhayitvā tu gatiṃ buddhvā kramāgatām ।। cakrobhayanibaddhāṃ tu śākhāprāntāvalambinīm ।
mūlasthānādyathā devi tamogranthiṃ vidārayet ।। vajrākhyāṃ jñānajenaiva tathā śākhobhayāntataḥ । koṇamadhyaviniṣkrāntaṃ liṅgamūlaṃ vibhedayet ।। tatra saṅghaṭṭitaṃ cakrayugmamaikyena bhāsate ।
vaiparītyāttu nikṣipya dvidhābhāvaṃ vrajatyataḥ ।। ūrvādyaṅguṣṭhakālāgniparyante sā vinikṣipet । gamāgamanasañcāre caretsā liṅgaliṅginī ।। tatra tatpadasaṃyogādunmīlanavidhāyinī ।
yo jānāti sa siddhyettu rasādānavisargayoḥ ।। sasaṅgamamidaṃ sthānamūrmiṇyunmīlanaṃ param । eṣa kramastato anyo api vyutkramaḥ khecarī parā ।। yonyādhāreti vikhyātā śūlamūleti śabdyate ।
varṇāstatra layaṃ yānti hyavarṇe varṇarūpiṇi ।। nādiphāntaṃ samuccārya kauleśaṃ dehasaṃnibham । ākramya prathamaṃ cakraṃ khe yantre pādapīḍitam ।। nādaṃ vai śaktisadgarbhaṃ sadgarbhātkaulinīpadam ।
bījapañcakacāreṇa śūlabhedakrameṇa tu ।। hṛcchūlagranthibhedaiścidrudraśaktiṃ prabodhayet । vāyucakrāntanilayaṃ bindvākhyaṃ nābhimaṇḍalam ।। āgacchellambikāsthānaṃ sūtradvādaśanirgatam ।
candracakravilomena praviśedbhūtapañjare ।। bhūyastu kurute līlāṃ māyāpañjaravartinīm । punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtiśca khecaryā kriyate budhaiḥ ।। śrīmadvīrāvalīyoga eṣa syātkhecarīvidhiḥ ।
cumbākāreṇa vaktreṇa yattattvaṃ śrūyate param ।। grasamānamidaṃ viśvaṃ candrārkapuṭasaṃpuṭe । tenaiva syātkhagāmīti śrīmatkāmika ucyate ।। bhavānmuktvā drāvayanti pāśānmudrā hi śaktayaḥ ।
mukhyāsāṃ khecarī sā ca tridhoccāreṇa vācikī ।। triśiromudgaro devi kāyikī paripaṭhyate । nāsāṃ netradvayaṃ cāpi hṛtstanadvayameva ca ।। vṛṣaṇadvayaliṅgaṃ ca prāpya kāyaṃ gatā tviyam ।
bhavasthānābhavasthānamuccāreṇāvadhārayet ।। mānasīyamitastvanyāḥ padmādyā aṣṭa mudrikāḥ । mātṛvyūhakule tāḥ syurasyāstu parivāragāḥ ।। śarīraṃ tu samastaṃ yatkūṭākṣarasamākṛti ।
eṣā mudrā mahāmudrā bhairavasyeti gahvare ।। sūpaviṣṭaḥ padmake tu hastāgrāṅguliraśmibhiḥ । parāṅmukhairjhaṭityudyadraśmibhiḥ pṛṣṭhasaṃsthitaiḥ ।। antaḥsthitiḥ khecarīyaṃ saṃkocākhyā śaśāṅkinī ।
tasmādeva samuttambya bāhū caivāvakuñcitau ।। samyagvyomasu saṃsthānādvyomākhyā khecarī matā । muṣṭidvitayasaṅghaṭṭāddhṛdi sā hṛdayāhvāyā ।। śāntākhyā sā hastayugmamūrdhvādhaḥ sthitamudgatam ।
samadṛṣṭyāvalokyaṃ ca bahiryojitapāṇikam ।। eṣaiva śaktimudrā cedadhodhāvitapāṇikā । daśānāmaṅgulīnāṃ tu muṣṭibandhādanantaram ।। drākkṣepātkhecarī devī pañcakuṇḍalinī matā ।
saṃhāramudrā caiṣaiva yadyūrdhvaṃ kṣipyate kila ।। utkrāmaṇī jhagityeva paśūnāṃ pāśakartarī । śvabhre sudūre jhaṭiti svātmānaṃ pātayanniva ।। sāhasānupraveśena kuñcitaṃ hastayugmakam ।
adhovīkṣaṇaśīlaṃ ca samyagdṛṣṭisamanvitam ।। vīrabhairavasaṃjñeyaṃ khecarī bodhavardhinī । aṣṭadhetthaṃ varṇitā śrībhargāṣṭakaśikhākule ।। evaṃ nānāvidhānbhedānāśrityaikaiva yā sthitā ।
śrīkhecarī tayāviṣṭaḥ paraṃ bījaṃ prapadyate ।। ekaṃ sṛṣṭimayaṃ bījaṃ yadvīryaṃ sarvamantragam । ekā mudrā khecarī ca mudraughaḥ prāṇito yayā ।। tadevaṃ khecarīcakrarūḍhau yadrūpamullaset ।
tadeva mudrā mantavyā śeṣaḥ syāddehavikriyā ।। yāgādau tanmadhye tadavasitau jñānayogaparimarśe । vighnapraśame pāśacchede mudrāvidheḥ samayaḥ ।। bodhāveśaḥ sannidhiraikyena visarjanaṃ svarūpagatiḥ ।
śaṅkādalanaṃ cakrodayadīptiriti kramātkṛtyam ।। iti mudrāvidhiḥ proktaḥ sugūḍho yaḥ phalapradaḥ । athāvasarasaṃprāpta ekīkāro nigadyate । yaduktaṃ cakrabhedena sārdhaṃ pūjyamiti trikam ।
tatraiṣa cakrabhedānāmekīkāro diśānayā ।। viśvā tadīśā hāraudrī vīranetryambikā tathā । gurvīti ṣaḍare devyaḥ śrīsiddhāvīradarśitāḥ ।। māheśī brāhmaṇī skāndī vaiṣṇavyaindrī yamātmikā ।
cāmuṇḍā caiva yogīśītyaṣṭāghoryādayo athavā ।। agninirṛtivāyvīśamātṛbhirdvādaśānvitāḥ । nandā bhadrā jayā kālī karālī vikṛtānanā ।। kroṣṭukī bhīmamudrā ca vāyuvegā hayānanā ।
gambhīrā ghoṣaṇī ceti caturviṃśatyare vidhiḥ ।। siddhirvṛddhirdyutirlakṣmīrmedhā kāntiḥ sudhā dhṛtiḥ । dīptiḥ puṣṭirmatiḥ kīrtiḥ susthitiḥ sugatiḥ smṛtiḥ ।। suprabhā ṣoḍaśī ceti śrīkaṇṭhādikaśaktayaḥ ।
baliśca balinandaśca daśagrīvo haro hayaḥ ।। mādhavaḥ ṣaḍare cakre dvādaśāre tvamī smṛtāḥ । dakṣaścaṇḍo haraḥ śauṇḍī pramatho bhīmamanmathau ।। śakuniḥ sumatirnando gopālaśca pitāmahaḥ ।
śrīkaṇṭho anantasūkṣmau ca trimūrtiḥ śaṃbareśvaraḥ ।। arghīśo bhārabhūtiśca sthitiḥ sthāṇurharastathā । jhaṇṭhibhautikasadyojānugrahakrūrasainikāḥ ।। dvyaṣṭau yadvāmṛtastena yuktāḥ pūrṇābhataddravāḥ ।
oghormisyandanāṅgāśca vapurudgāravaktrakāḥ ।। tanusecanamūrtīśāḥ sarvāmṛtadharo aparaḥ । śrīpāṭhācchaktayaścaitāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ ।। saṃvartalakulibhṛgusitabakakhaṅgipinākibhujagabalikālāḥ ।
dviśchagalāṇḍau śikhiśoṇameṣamīnatridaṇḍi sāṣāḍhi ।। devīkāntatadardhau dārukahalisomanāthaśarmāṇaḥ । jayavijayajayantājitasujayajayarudrakīrtanāvahakāḥ ।। tanmūrtyutsāhadavardhanāśca balasubalabhadradāvahakāḥ ।
tadvāndātā ceśo nandanasamabhadratanmūrtiḥ ।। śivadasumanaḥspṛhaṇakā durgo bhadrākhyakālaśca । ceto anugakauśikakālaviśvasuśivāstathāparaḥ kopaḥ ।। śrutyagnyare syurete strīpāṭhācchaktayastvetāḥ ।
juṃkāro athāgnipatnīti ṣaḍare ṣaṇṭhavarjitāḥ ।। dvādaśāre tatsahitāḥ ṣoḍaśāre svarāḥ kramāt । halastaddviguṇe aṣṭāre yādyaṃ hāntaṃ tu tattrike ।। dvātriṃśadarake sāntaṃ binduḥ sarveṣu mūrdhani ।
evamanyānbahūṃścakrabhedānasmātprakalpayet ।। eka eva cidātmaiṣa viśvāmarśanasārakaḥ । śaktistadvānato mātā śabdarāśiḥ prakīrtitau ।। tayoreva vibhāge tu śaktitadvatprakalpane ।
śabdarāśirmālinī ca kṣobhātma vapurīdṛśam ।। tathāntaḥsthaparāmarśabhedane vastutastrikam । anuttarecchonmeṣākhyaṃ yato viśvaṃ vimarśanam ।। ānandeśormiyoge tu tatṣaṭkaṃ samudāhṛtam ।
antaḥsthoṣmasamāyogāttadaṣṭakamudāhṛtam ।। tadāmṛtacatuṣkonabhāve dvādaśakaṃ bhavet । tadyoge ṣoḍaśākhyaṃ syādevaṃ yāvadasaṃkhyatā ।। viśvamekaparāmarśasahatvātprabhṛti sphuṭam ।
aṃśāṃśikāparāmarśān paryante sahate yataḥ ।। ataḥ pañcāśadaikātmyaṃ svaravyaktivirūpatā । vargāṣṭakaṃ varṇabheda ekāśītikalodayaḥ ।। iti pradarśitaṃ pūrvam ardhamātrāsahatvataḥ ।
svarārdhamapyasti yataḥ svaritasyārdhamātrakam ।। tasyādita udāttaṃ tatkathitaṃ padavedinā । itthaṃ saṃvidiyaṃ yājyasvarūpāmarśarūpiṇī ।। abhinnaṃ saṃvidaścaitaccakrāṇāṃ cakravālakam ।
svāmyāvaraṇabhedena bahudhā tatprayojayet ।। parāparā parā cānyā sṛṣṭisthititirodhayaḥ । mātṛsadbhāvarūpā tu turyā viśrāntirucyate ।। tacca prakāśaṃ vaktrasthaṃ sūcitaṃ tu pade pade ।
turye viśrāntirādheyā mātṛsadbhāvasāriṇi ।। tathāsya viśvamābhāti svātmatanmayatāṃ gatam । ityeṣa śāstrārthasyokta ekīkāro gurūditaḥ ।। ucyate atha svasvarūpapraveśaḥ kramasaṅgataḥ ।
yadetadbahudhā proktamāṇavaṃ śivatāptaye । tatrāntarantarāviśya viśrāmyetsavidhe pade ।। tato apyāṇavasaṃtyāgācchāktīṃ bhūmimupāśrayet । tato api śāmbhavīmevaṃ tāratamyakramātsphuṭam ।।
itthaṃ kramoditavibodhamahāmarīcisaṃpūritaprasarabhairavabhāvabhāgī । ante abhyupāyanirapekṣatayaiva nityaṃ svātmānamāviśati garbhitaviśvarūpam ।। kathito ayaṃ svasvarūpapraveśaḥ parameṣṭhinā । athocyate samastānāṃ śāstrāṇāmiha melanam ।
iha tāvatsama sto ayaṃ vyavahāraḥ purātanaḥ ।। prasiddhimanusandhāya saiva cāgama ucyate । anvayavyatirekau hi prasiddherupajīvakau ।। svāyattatve tayorvyaktipūge kiṃ syāttayorgatiḥ ।
pratyakṣamapi netrātmadīpārthādiviśeṣajam ।। apekṣate tatra mūle prasiddhiṃ tāṃ tathātmikām । abhitaḥsaṃvṛte jāta ekākī kṣudhitaḥ śiśuḥ ।। kiṃ karotu kimādattāṃ kena paśyatu kiṃ vrajet ।
nanu vastuśatākīrṇe sthāne apyasya yadeva hi ।। paśyato jighrato vāpi spṛśataḥ saṃprasīdati । cetastadevādāya drāk so anvayavyatirekabhāk ।। hanta cetaḥprasādo api yo asāvarthaviśeṣagaḥ ।
so api prāgvāsanārūpavimarśaparikalpitaḥ ।। na pratyakṣānumānādibāhyamānaprasādajaḥ । prāgvāsanopajīvyetat pratibhāmātrameva na ।। na mṛdabhyavahārecchā puṃso bālasya jāyate ।
prāgvāsanopajīvī cedvimarśaḥ sā ca vāsanā ।। prācyā cedāgatā seyaṃ prasiddhiḥ paurvakālikī । naca cetaḥprasattyaiva sarvo vyavahṛtikramaḥ ।। mūlaṃ prasiddhistanmānaṃ sarvatraiveti gṛhyatām ।
pūrvapūrvopajīvitvamārgaṇe sā kvacitsvayam ।। sarvajñarūpe hyekasminniḥśaṅkaṃ bhāsata purā । vyavahāro hi naikatra samastaḥ ko api mātari ।। tenāsarvajñapūrvatvamātreṇaiṣā na siddhyati ।
bahusarvajñapūrvatve na mānaṃ cāsti kiṃcana ।। bhogāpavargataddhetuprasiddhiśataśobhitaḥ । tadvimarśasvabhāvo asau bhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। tataścāṃśāṃśikāyogātsā prasiddhiḥ paramparām ।
śāstraṃ vāśritya vitatā lokānsaṃvyavahārayet ।। tayaivāśaiśavātsarve vyavahāradharājuṣaḥ । santaḥ samupajīvanti śaivamevādyamāgamam ।। apūrṇāstu pare tena na mokṣaphalabhāginaḥ ।
upajīvanti yāvattu tāvattatphalabhāginaḥ ।। bālyāpāye api yadbhoktumannameṣa pravartate । tatprasiddhyaiva nādhyakṣānnānumānādasambhavāt ।। naca kāpyatra doṣāśāśaṅkāyāśca nivṛttitaḥ ।
prasiddhiścāvigānotthā pratītiḥ śabdanātmikā ।। mātuḥ svabhāvo yattasyāṃ śaṅkate naiṣa jātucit । svakṛtatvavaśādeva sarvavitsa hi śaṅkaraḥ ।। yāvattu śivatā nāsya tāvatsvātmānusāriṇīm ।
tāvatīmeva tāmeṣa prasiddhiṃ nābhiśaṅkate ।। anyasyāmabhiśaṅkī syādbhūyastāṃ bahu manyate । evaṃ bhāviśivatvo amūṃ prasiddhiṃ manyate dhruvam ।। eka evāgamaścāyaṃ vibhunā sarvadarśinā ।
darśito yaḥ pravṛtte ca nivṛtte ca pathi sthitaḥ ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu pūrṇāpūrṇādibhedataḥ । vicitreṣu phaleṣveka upāyaḥ śāmbhavāgamaḥ ।। tasminviṣayavaiviktyādvicitraphaladāyini ।
citropāyopadeśo api na virodhāvaho bhavet ।। laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ sāṅkhyaṃ yogādi pāñcarātrakam । bauddhārhatanyāyaśāstraṃ padārthakramatantraṇam ।। siddhāntatantraśāktādi sarvaṃ brahmodbhavaṃ yataḥ ।
śrīsvacchandādiṣu proktaṃ sadyojātādibhedataḥ ।। yathaikatrāpi vedādau tattadāśramagāminaḥ । saṃskārāntaramatrāpi tathā liṅgoddhṛtādikam ।। yathāca tatra pūrvasminnāśrame nottarāśramāt ।
phalameti tathā pāñcarātrādau na śivātmatām ।। eka evāgamastasmāttatra laukikaśāstrataḥ । prabhṛtyāvaiṣṇavādbauddhācchaivātsarvaṃ hi niṣṭhitam ।। tasya yattat paraṃ prāpyaṃ dhāma tat trikaśabditam ।
sarvāvibhedānucchedāt tadeva kulamucyate ।। yathordhvādharatābhāksu dehāṅgeṣu vibhediṣu । ekaṃ prāṇitamevaṃ syāt trikaṃ sarveṣu śāstrataḥ ।। śrīmatkālīkule coktaṃ pañcasrotovivarjitam ।
daśāṣṭādaśabhedasya sārametatprakīrtitam ।। puṣpe gandhastile tailaṃ dehe jīvo jale amṛtam । yathā tathaiva śāstrāṇāṃ kulamantaḥ pratiṣṭhitam ।। tadeka evāgamo ayaṃ citraścitre adhikāriṇi ।
tathaiva sā prasiddhirhi svayūthyaparayūthyagā ।। sāṃkhyaṃ yogaṃ pāñcarātraṃ vedāṃścaiva na nindayet । yataḥ śivodbhavāḥ sarva iti svacchandaśāsane ।। ekasmādāgamāccaite khaṇḍakhaṇḍā vyapoddhṛtāḥ ।
loke syurāgamāstaiśca jano bhrāmyati mohitaḥ ।। anekāgamapakṣe api vācyā viṣayabheditā । avaśyamūrdhvādharatāsthityā prāmāṇyasiddhaye ।। anyathā naiva kasyāpi prāmāṇyaṃ siddhyati dhruvam ।
nityatvamavisaṃvāda iti no mānakāraṇam ।। asminnaṃśe apyamuṣyaiva prāmāṇyaṃ syāttathoditeḥ । anyathāvyākṛtau kḷptāvasatyatve prarocane ।। atiprasaṅga sarvasyāpyāgamasyāpabādhakaḥ ।
avaśyopetya ityasminmāna āgamanāmani ।। avaśyopetyamevaitacchāstraniṣṭhānirūpaṇam । pradhāne aṅge kṛto yatnaḥ phalavānvastuto yataḥ ।। ato asmin yatnavān ko api bhavecchaṃbhupracoditaḥ ।
tatra tatra ca śāstreṣu nyarūpyata maheśinā ।। etāvatyadhikārī yaḥ sa durlabha iti sphuṭam । itthaṃ śrīśambhunāthena mamoktaṃ śāstramelanam ।। āyātiratha śāstrasya kathyate avasarāgatā ।
śrīsiddhādivinirdiṣṭā gurubhiśca nirūpitā । bhairavo bhairavī devī svacchando lākulo aṇurāṭ ।। gahaneśo abjajaḥ śakro guruḥ koṭyapakarṣataḥ । navabhiḥ kramaśo adhītaṃ navakoṭipravistaram ।।
etaistato guruḥ koṭimātrāt pādaṃ vitīrṇavān । dakṣādibhya ubhau pādau saṃvartādibhya eva ca ।। pādaṃ ca vāmanādibhyaḥ pādārdhaṃ bhārgavāya ca । pādapādaṃ tu balaye pādapādastu yo aparaḥ ।।
siṃhāyārdhaṃ tataḥ śiṣṭāddvau bhāgau vinatābhuve । pādaṃ vāsukināgāya khaṇḍāḥ saptadaśa tvamī ।। svargādardhaṃ rāvaṇo atha jahre rāmo ardhamapyataḥ । vibhīṣaṇamukhādāpa guruśiṣyavidhikramāt ।।
khaṇḍairekānnaviṃśatyā vibhaktaṃ tadabhūttataḥ । khaṇḍaṃ khaṇḍaṃ cāṣṭakhaṇḍaṃ proktapādādibhedataḥ ।। pādo mūloddhārāvuttaravṛhaduttare tathā kalpaḥ । sāṃhitakalpaskandāvanuttaraṃ vyāpakaṃ tridhā tisraḥ ।।
devyo atra nirūpyante kramaśo vistāriṇaiva rūpeṇa । navame pade tu gaṇanā na kāciduktā vyavacchidāhīne ।। rāmācca lakṣmaṇastasmāt siddhāstebhyo api dānavāḥ । guhyakāśca tatastebhyo yogino nṛvarāstataḥ ।।
teṣāṃ krameṇa tanmadhye bhraṣṭaṃ kālāntarādyadā । tadā śrīkaṇṭhanāthājñāvaśāt siddhā avātaram ।। tryambakāmardakābhikhyaśrīnāthā advaye dvaye । dvayādvaye ca nipuṇāḥ krameṇa śivaśāsane ।।
ādyasya cānvayo jajñe dvitīyo duhitṛkramāt । sa cārdhatryambakābhikhyaḥ saṃtānaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। ataścārdhacatasro atra maṭhikāḥ saṃtatikramāt । śiṣyapraśiṣyairvistīrṇāḥ śataśākhaṃ vyavasthitaiḥ ।।
adhyuṣṭasaṃtatisrotaḥsārabhūtarasāhṛtim । vidhāya tantrāloko ayaṃ syandate sakalānrasān ।। uktāyātirupādeyabhāvo nirṇīyate adhunā । uktanītyaiva sarvatra vyavahāre pravartite ।
prasiddhāvupajīvyāyāmavaśyagrāhya āgamaḥ ।। yathā laukikadṛṣṭyānyaphalabhāk tatprasiddhitaḥ । samyagvyavaharaṃstadvacchivabhāk tatprasiddhitaḥ ।। tadavaśyagrahītavye śāstre svāṃśopadeśini ।
manākphale abhyupādeyatamaṃ tadviparītakam ।। yathā khageśvarībhāvaniḥśaṅkatvādviṣaṃ vrajet । kṣayaṃ karmasthitistadvadaśaṅkādbhairavatvataḥ ।। yadārṣe pātahetūktaṃ tadasminvāmaśāsane ।
āśusiddhyai yataḥ sarvamārṣaṃ māyodarasthitam ।। tacca yatsarvasarvajñadṛṣṭaṃ taccāpi kiṃ bhavet । yadaśeṣopadeśena sūyate anuttaraṃ phalam ।। yathādharādharaproktavastutattvānuvādataḥ ।
uttaraṃ kathitaṃ saṃvitsiddhaṃ taddhi tathā bhavet ।। yaduktādhikasaṃvittisiddhavastunirūpaṇāt । apūrṇasarvavitproktirjñāyate adharaśāsane ।। ūrdhvaśāsanavastvaṃśe dṛṣṭvāpica samujjhite ।
adhaḥ śāstreṣu māyātvaṃ lakṣyate sargarakṣaṇāt ।। śrīmadānandaśāstrādau proktaṃ ca parameśinā । ṛṣivākyaṃ bahukleśamadhruvālpaphalaṃ mitam ।। naiva pramāṇayedvidvān śaivamevāgamaṃ śrayet ।
tadārṣe pātahetūktaṃ tadasmin vāmaśāsane ।। āśusiddhyai yataḥ sarvamārṣaṃ māyodarasthitam । yathā khageśvarībhāvaniḥśaṅkatvādviṣaṃ vrajet ।। kṣayaṃ karmasthitistadvadaśaṅkādbhairavatvataḥ ।
ajñatvānupadeṣṭṛtvasaṃdaṣṭe adharaśāsane ।। etadviparyayādgrāhyamavaśyaṃ śivaśāsanam । dvāvāptau tatra ca śrīmacchrīkaṇṭhalakuleśvarau ।। dvipravāhamidaṃ śāstraṃ mamyaṅniḥśreyasapradam ।
prācyasya tu yathābhīṣṭabhogadatvamapi sthitam ।। tacca pañcavidhaṃ proktaṃ śaktivaicitryacitritam । pañcasrota iti proktaṃ śrīmacchrīkaṇṭhaśāsanam ।। daśāṣṭādaśadhā srotaḥpañcakaṃ yattato apyalam ।
utkṛṣṭaṃ bhairavābhikhyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭivibheditam ।। śrīmadānandaśāstrādau proktaṃ bhagavatā kila । samūhaḥ pīṭhametacca dvidhā dakṣiṇavāmataḥ ।। mantro vidyeti tasmācca mudrāmaṇḍalagaṃ dvayam ।
mananatrāṇadaṃ yattu mantrākhyaṃ tatra vidyayā ।। upodbalanamāpyāyaḥ sā hi vedyārthabhāsinī । mantrapratikṛtirmudrā tadāpyāyanakārakam ।। maṇḍalaṃ sāramuktaṃ hi maṇḍaśrutyā śivāhvayam ।
evamanyonyasaṃbhedavṛtti pīṭhacatuṣṭayam ।। yatastasmādbhavetsarvaṃ pīṭhe pīṭhe api vastutaḥ । pradhānatvāttasya tasya vastuno bhinnatā punaḥ ।। kathitā sādhakendrāṇāṃ tattadvastuprasiddhaye ।
pratyekaṃ taccaturdhaivaṃ maṇḍalaṃ mudrikā tathā ।। mantro vidyeti ca pīṭhamutkṛṣṭaṃ cottarottam । vidyāpīṭhapradhānaṃ ca siddhayogīśvarīmatam ।। tasyāpi paramaṃ sāraṃ mālinīvijayottaram ।
uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāmetacca parameśinā ।। aśeṣatantrasāraṃ tu vāmadakṣiṇamāśritam । ekatra militaṃ kaulaṃ śrīṣaḍardhakaśāsane ।। siddhānte karma bahulaṃ malamāyādirūṣitam ।
dakṣiṇaṃ raudrakarmāḍhyaṃ vāmaṃ siddhisamākulam ।। svalpapuṇyaṃ bahukleśaṃ svapratītivivarjitam । mokṣavidyāvihīnaṃ ca vinayaṃ tyaja dūrataḥ ।। yasminkāle ca guruṇā nirvikalpaṃ prakāśitam ।
muktastenaiva kālena yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam ।। mayaitatsrotasāṃ rūpamanuttarapadāddhruvāt । ārabhya vistareṇoktaṃ mālinīślokavārtike ।। jijñāsustata evedamavadhārayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।
vayaṃ tūktānuvacanamaphalaṃ nādriyāmahe ।। itthaṃ dadadanāyāsājjīvanmuktimahāphalam । yathepsitamahābhogadātṛtvena vyavasthitam ।। ṣaḍardhasāraṃ sacchāstramupādeyamidaṃ sphuṭam ।
ṣaṭtriṃśatā tattvabalena sūtā yadyapyanantā bhuvanāvalīyam । brahmāṇḍamatyantamanoharaṃ tu vaicitryavarjaṃ nahi ramyabhāvaḥ ।। bhūrādisaptapurapūrṇatame api tasmin manye dvitīyabhuvanaṃ bhavanaṃ sukhasya । kvānyatra citragatisūryaśaśāṅkaśobhirātrindivaprasarabhogavibhāgabhūṣā ।।
tatrāpica tridivabhogamahārghavarṣadvīpāntarādadhikameva kumārikāhvam । yatrādharādharapadātparamaṃ śivāntamāroḍhumapyadhikṛtiḥ kṛtināmanarghā ।। prākkarmabhogipaśutocitabhogabhājā kiṃ janmanā nanu sukhaikapade api dhāmni । sarvo hi bhāvini paraṃ paritoṣameti saṃbhāvite natu nimeṣiṇi vartamāne ।।
kanyāhvaye api bhuvane atra paraṃ mahīyān deśaḥ sa yatra kila śāstravarāṇi cakṣuḥ । jātyandhasadmani na janma na ko abhinindedbhinnāñjanāyitaravipramukhaprakāśe ।। niḥśeṣaśāstrasadanaṃ kila madhyadeśastasminnajāyata guṇābhyadhiko dvijanmā । ko apyatrigupta iti nāmaniruktagotraḥ śāstrābdhicarvaṇakalodyadagastyagotraḥ ।।
tamatha lalitādityo rājā nijaṃ puramānayat praṇayarabhasāt kaśmīrākhyaṃ himālayamūrdhagam । adhivasati yadgaurīkāntaḥ karairvijayādibhiryugapadakhilaṃ bhogāsāraṃ rasāt paricarcitum ।। sthāne sthāne munibhirakhilaiścakrire yannivāsā yaccādhyāste pratipadamidaṃ sa svayaṃ candracūḍaḥ । tanmanye ahaṃ samabhilaṣitāśeṣasiddhernasiddhyai kaśmīrebhyaḥ paramatha puraṃ pūrṇavṛtterna tuṣṭyai ।।
yatra svayaṃ śāradacandraśubhrā śrīśāradeti prathitā janeṣu । śāṇḍilyasevārasasuprasannā sarvaṃ janaṃ svairvibhavairyunakti ।। nāraṅgāruṇakānti pāṇḍuvikacadballāvadātacchavi prodbhinnāmalamātuluṅgakanakacchāyābhirāmaprabham । kerīkuntalakandalīpratikṛtiśyāmaprabhābhāsvaraṃ yasmiñśakticatuṣṭayojjvalamalaṃ madyaṃ mahābhairavam ।।
trinayanamahākopajvālāvilīna iha sthito madanaviśikhavrāto madyacchalena vijṛmbhate । kathamitarathā rāgaṃ mohaṃ madaṃ madanajvaraṃ vidadhadaniśaṃ kāmātaṅkairvaśīkurute jagat ।। yatkāntānāṃ praṇayavacasi prauḍhimānaṃ vidatte yannirvighnaṃ nidhuvanavidhau sādhvasaṃ saṃdhunoti । yasmin viśvāḥ kalitarucayo devatāścakracaryastanmārdvīkaṃ sapadi tanute yatra bhogāpabargau ।।
udyadgaurāṅkuravikasitaiḥ śyāmaraktaiḥ palāśairantargāḍhāruṇarucilasatkesarālīvicitraiḥ । ākīrṇā bhūḥ pratipadamasau yatra kāśmīrapuṣpaiḥ samyagdevītritayayajanodyānamāviṣkaroti ।। sarvo lokaḥ kaviratha budho yatra śūro api vāgmī candroddyotā masṛṇagatayaḥ pauranāryaśca yatra । yatrāṅgārojjvalavikasitānantasauṣumṇamārgagrastārkendurgaganavimalo yoginīnāṃ ca vargaḥ ।।
śrīmatparaṃ pravaranāma puraṃ ca tatra yannirmame pravarasena iti kṣitīśaḥ । yaḥ svapratiṣṭhitamaheśvarapūjanānte vyomotpatannudasṛjatkila dhūpaghaṇṭām ।। āndolanoditamanoharavīranādaiḥ sā cāsya tatsucaritaṃ prathayāṃbabhūva । sadvṛttasāragurutaijasamūrtayo hi tyaktā api prabhuguṇānadhikaṃ dhvananti ।।
saṃpūrṇacandravimaladyutivīrakāntāgāḍhāṅgarāgaghanakuṅkumapiñjaraśrīḥ । proddhūtavetasalatāsitacāmaraughairājyābhiṣekamaniśaṃ dadatī smarasya ।। rodhaḥpratiṣṭhitamaheśvarasiddhaliṅgasvāyaṃbhuvārcanavilepanagandhapuṣpaiḥ । āvarjyamānatanuvīcinimajjanaughavidhvastapāpmamunisiddhamanuṣyavandyā ।।
bhogāpavargaparipūraṇakalpavallī bhogaikadānarasikāṃ surasiddhasindhum । nyakkurvatī harapinākakalāvatīrṇā yadbhūṣayatyavirataṃ taṭinī vitastā ।। tasmin kuverapuracārisiṃtāṃśumaulisāṃmukhyadarśanavirūḍhapavitrabhāve । vaitastarodhasi nivāsamamuṣya cakre rājā dvijasya parikalpitabhūrisaṃpat ।।
tasyānvaye mahati ko api varāhaguptanāmā babhūva bhagavān svayamantakāle । gīrvāṇasindhulaharīkalitāgramūrdhā yasyākarot paramanugrahamāgraheṇa ।। tasyātmajaścukhalaketi jane prasiddhaścandrāvadātadhiṣaṇo narasiṃhaguptaḥ । yaṃ sarvaśāstrarasamajjanaśubhracittaṃ māheśvarī paramalaṃkurute sma bhaktiḥ ।।
tāruṇyasāgarataraṅgabharānapohya vairāgyapotamadhiruhya dṛḍhaṃ haṭhena । yo bhaktirohaṇamavāpya maheśacintāratnairalaṃ dalayati sma bhavāpadastāḥ ।। tasyātmajo abhinavagupta iti prasiddhaḥ śrīcandracūḍacaraṇābjaparāgapūtaḥ । mātā vyayūyujadamuṃ kila bālya eva daivaṃ hi bhāviparikarmaṇi saṃskaroti ।।
mātā paraṃ bandhuriti pravādaḥ snoho atigāḍhīkurute hi pāśān । tanmūlabandhe galite kilāsya manye sthitā jīvata eva muktiḥ ।। pitrā sa śabdagahane kṛtasaṃpraveśastarkārṇavormipṛṣatāmalapūtacittaḥ । sāhityasāndrarasabhogaparo maheśabhaktyā svayaṃgrahaṇadurmadayā gṛhītaḥ ।।
sa tanmayībhūya na lokavartanīmajīgaṇat kāmapi kevalaṃ punaḥ । tadīyasaṃbhogavivṛddhaye purā karoti dāsyaṃ guruveśmasu svayam ।। ānandasaṃtatimahārṇavakarṇadhāraḥ saddaiśikairakavarātmajavāmanāthaḥ । śrīnāthasaṃtatimahāmbaragharmakāntiḥ śrībhūtirājatanayaḥ svapitṛprasādaḥ ।।
traiyambakaprasarasāgaraśāyisomānandātmajotpalajalakṣmaṇaguptanāthaḥ । turyākhyasaṃtatimahodadhipūrṇacandraḥ śrīsomataḥ sakalavitkila śaṃbhunāthaḥ ।। śrīcandraśarmabhavabhaktivilāsayogānandābhinandaśivaśaktivicitranāthāḥ । anye api dharmaśivavāmanakodbhaṭaśrībhūteśabhāskaramukhapramukhā mahāntaḥ ।।
ete sevārasaviracitānugrahāḥ śāstrasārapauḍhādeśaprakaṭasubhagaṃ svādhikāraṃ kilāsmai । yat saṃprāduryadapi ca janānnaikṣatākṣetrabhūtān svātmārāmastadayamaniśaṃ tattvasevāraso abhūt ।। so anugrahītumatha śāṃbhavabhaktibhājaṃ svaṃ bhrātaramakhilaśāstravimarśapūrṇam । yāvanmanaḥ praṇidadhāti manorathākhyaṃ tāvajjanaḥ katipayastamupāsasāda ।।
śrīśaurisaṃjñatanayaḥ kila karṇanāmā yo yauvane viditaśāṃbhavatattvasāraḥ । dehaṃ tyajan prathayati sma janasya satyaṃ yogacyutaṃ prati mahāmunikṛṣṇavākyam ।। tadbālamitramatha mantrisutaḥ prasiddhaḥ śrīmandra ityakhilasāraguṇābhirāmaḥ । lakṣmīsarasvati samaṃ yamalaṃcakāra sāpatnakaṃ tirayate subhagaprabhāvaḥ ।।
anye pitṛvyatanayāḥ śivaśaktiśubhrāḥ kṣemotpalābhinavacakrakapadmaguptāḥ । ye saṃpadaṃ tṛṇamamaṃsata śaṃbhusevāsaṃpūritaṃ svahṛdayaṃ hṛdi bhāvayantaḥ ।। ṣaḍardhaśāstreṣu samastameva yenādhijagme vidhimaṇḍalādi । sa rāmagupto guruśaṃbhuśāstrasevāvidhivyagrasamagramārgaḥ ।।
anyo api kaścana janaḥ śivaśaktipātasaṃpreraṇāparavaśasvakaśaktisārthaḥ । abhyarthanāvimukhabhāvamaśikṣitena tenāpyanugrahapadaṃ kṛta eṣa vargaḥ ।। ācāryamabhyarthayate sma gāḍhaṃ saṃpūrṇatantrādhigamāya samyak । jāyeta daivānugṛhītabuddheḥ saṃpatprabandhaikarasaiva saṃpat ।।
so apyabhyupāgamadabhīpsitamasya yadvā svātodyameva hi ninartiṣato avatīrṇam । so anugrahapravaṇa eva hi sadgurūṇāmājñāvaśena śubhasūtimahāṅkureṇa ।। vikṣiptabhāvaparihāramatho cikīrṣan mandraḥ svake puravare sthitimasya vavre । ābālagopamapi yatra maheśvarasya dāsyaṃ janaścarati pīṭhanivāsakalpe ।।
tasyābhavat kila pitṛvyavadhūrvidhātrā yā nirmame galitasaṃsṛticitracintā । śītāṃśumaulicaraṇābjaparāgamātrabhūṣāvidhirvihitavatsalikocitākhyā ।। mūrtā kṣameva karuṇeva gṛhītadehā dhāreva vigrahavatī śubhaśīlatāyāḥ । vairāgyasāraparipākadaśeva pūrṇā tattvārtharatnarucirasthitirohaṇorvī ।।
bhrātāpi tasyāḥ śaśiśubhramaulerbhaktyā paraṃ pāvitacittavṛttiḥ । sa śaurirātteśvaramantribhāvastatyāja yo bhūpatimantribhāvam ।। tasya snuṣā karṇavadhūrvidhūtasaṃsāravṛttiḥ sutamekameva । yāsūta yogeśvaridattasaṃjñaṃ nāmānurūpasphuradarthatattvam ।।
yāmagrage vayasi bhartṛviyogadīnāmanvagrahīt trinayanaḥ svayameva bhaktyā । bhāviprabhāvarabhaseṣu janeṣvanarthaḥ satyaṃ samākṛṣati so arthaparamparāṇām ।। bhaktyullasatpulakatāṃ sphuṭamaṅgabhūṣāṃ śrīśaṃbhunāthanatimeva lalāṭikāṃ ca । śaivaśrutiṃ śravaṇabhūṣaṇamapyavāpya saubhāgyamabhyadhikamudvahati sma yāntaḥ ।।
ambābhidhānā kila sā guruṃ taṃ svaṃ bhrātaraṃ śaṃbhudṛśābhyapaśyat । bhāviprabhāvojjvalabhavyabuddhiḥ sato avajānāti na bandhubuddhyā ।। bhrātā tadīyo abhinavaśca nāmnā na kevalaṃ saccaritairapi svaiḥ । pītena vijñānarasena yasya tatraiva tṛṣṇā vavṛdhe nikāmam ।।
so anyaśca śāṃbhavamarīcicayapraṇaśyatsaṃkocahārdanalinīghaṭitojjvalaśrīḥ । taṃ lumpakaḥ paricacāra samudyameṣu sādhuḥ samāvahati hanta karāvalambam ।। itthaṃ gṛhe vatsalikāvitīrṇe sthitaḥ samādhāya matiṃ bahūni । pūrvaśrutānyākalayan svabuddhyā śāstrāṇi tebhyaḥ samavāpa sāram ।।
sa tannibandhaṃ vidadhe mahārthaṃ yuktyāgamodīritatantratattvam । ālokamāsādya yadīyameṣa lokaḥ sukhaṃ saṃcaritā kriyāsu ।। santo anugṛhṇīta kṛtiṃ tadīyāṃ hṛhṇīta pūrvaṃ vidhireṣa tāvat । tato api gṛhṇātu bhavanmatiṃ sā sadyo anugṛhṇātu ca tattvadṛṣṭyā ।।
idamabhinavaguptaprombhitaṃ śāstrasāraṃ śiva niśamaya tāvat sarvataḥśrotratantraḥ । tava kila nutireṣā sā hi tvadrūpacarcetyabhinavaparituṣṭo lokamātmīkuruṣva ।।
